	saśastro 'nuttarīyaś ca muktakeśaḥ sasādhanaḥ |

	vāmahastena ca sragvī vadan daṇḍam avāpnuyāt ||

ato 'nevaṃbhūto vaded ity abhiprāyaḥ | tatas tadvacanaṃ sarvaṃ phalakādau lekhako likhet | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	rāgādīnāṃ yadaikena kopitaḥ karaṇe vadet |

	tad om iti likhet sarvam arthinaḥ phalakādiṣu ||

karaṇe rājādisaṃnidhāv ity arthaḥ | tac ca likhitaṃ janmāntare mayāsmai dhanaṃ dattaṃ tad asau na prayacchatītivad vicārāyogyaṃ yadi na syāt tadā tat pratyarthyānayanāya mudrāpradānādikaṃ kuryāt | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	evaṃ pṛṣṭaḥ sa yad brūyāt tat sabhyair brāhmaṇaiḥ saha |

	vimṛśya kāryaṃ nyāyyaṃ ced āhvānārtham ataḥ param ||

	mudrāṃ vā nikṣipet tasmin puruṣaṃ vā samādiśet ||

tasminn āvedake | puruṣaḥ sādhyapālaḥ | nyāyyaṃ yogyam | āhvānārtham abhiyuktasyeti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	yasyābhiyogaṃ kurute tathyenāśaṅkayātha vā |

	tam evānāyayed rājā mudrayā puruṣeṇa vā ||

uttaradāne tasyaivādhikārād ity abhiprāyaḥ | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	adhikāro 'bhiyuktasya netarasyāsty asaṃgateḥ | iti |

itarasyānabhiyuktasya tasmin vivāde saṃbandhābhāvān nāsty uttaradāne 'dhikāra ity arthaḥ | ata itarasyottaravāditvam, na svataḥ, kiṃ tu abhiyuktena prativāditvakaraṇāt | prāḍvivāke vā svakāryakaraṇatvena samarpaṇād arthinā vā svarucyā prativāditvāṅgīkārāt | nānyathā, tad āha sa eva |

	itaro 'py abhiyuktena pratirodhīkṛto mataḥ |

	samarpito 'rthinā yo 'nyaḥ paro dharmādhikāriṇi |

	prativādī sa vijñeyaḥ pratipannaś ca yaḥ svayam ||

ayam arthaḥ | itaro vivādāsaṃbaddho 'pi abhiyuktena pratirodhīkṛtaḥ prativādīkṛtaḥ manvādīnām uttaravāditvena saṃmataḥ | tathā anyo dvitīyaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ, yaḥ paro vivādāsaṃbandhī dharmādhikāriṇi prāḍvivāke 'bhiyuktena samarpitaḥ arthinā vā svayam eva yaḥ pratipannaḥ prativāditvenāṅgīkṛta iti | etac cānadhikāriṇaḥ prativāditvam akalyādyadhikāriviṣaye veditavyam | tatrādhikāriṇaḥ sākṣāt kartṛtvasya duṣkaratvāt | ata eva bṛhaspatiḥ |

	apragalbhajaḍonmattavṛddhastrībālarogiṇām |

	pūrvottaraṃ vaded bandhuḥ niyukto 'nyo 'tha vā naraḥ ||

ata eva ca teṣām ahvānapratiṣedho hārītādibhiḥ smaryate |

	akalyabālasthaviraviṣamasthakriyākulān |

	kāryātipātivyasaninṛpakāryotsavākulān |

	mattonmattapramattārtabhṛtyān nāhvāpayen nṛpaḥ ||

akalyo vyādhitaḥ | viṣamastha utpannasaṅkaṭaḥ | kriyākulaḥ nityanaimittikakarmakaraṇavyagraḥ | yasya tv āgacchato gurutarakāryahāniḥ sa kāryātipātī | vyasanam iṣṭaviyogādijaṃ duḥkham, tadvān vyasanī | matto duttūrādimadanīyadravyeṇa (?) skhalitabuddhiḥ | unmatto grahapittādibhiḥ | pramattaḥ sarvatrāvadhānahīnaḥ | ārto viṣādinā duḥkhitaḥ | bhṛtyagrahaṇam asvatantrastrīṇām apy upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	dharmotsukān abhyudaye rogiṇo 'tha jaḍān api |

	asvasthamattonmattārtastriyo nāhnāpayen (?) nṛpaḥ ||

striyo 'tra paratantrā vivakṣitāḥ | āha sa eva |

	na hīnapakṣāṃ yuvatiṃ kule jātāṃ prasūtikām |

	sarvavarṇottamāṃ kanyāṃ tāḥ jñātiprabhukāḥ smṛtāḥ ||

	tadadhīnakuṭumbinyaḥ svairiṇyo gaṇikāś ca yāḥ |

	niṣkulā yāś ca patitās tāsām āhnānam iṣyate || iti |

hīnapakṣā mandakulā, yuvatīti tasyā eva viśeṣaṇam | kule jātā satkule jātā, sarvavarṇottamā vādyapekṣayottamavarṇā | tāḥ pūrvoktāḥ pañca jñātiprabhukāḥ paratantāḥ | netarāḥ | tena tadadhīnakuṭumbinyādīnām āhvānaṃ manvādyabhīṣṭam ity arthaḥ | nārado 'pi keṣucid āhvānaṃ pratiṣedhati |

	nirveṣṭukāmo rogārto yiyakṣur vyasane sthitaḥ |

	abhiyuktas tathānyena rājakāryodyatas tathā ||

	gavāṃ pracāre gopālāḥ sasyārambhe kṛṣīvalāḥ |

	śilpinaś cāpi tatkāla āyudhīyāś ca vigrahe ||

	aprāptavyavahāraś ca dūto dānonmukho vratī |

	viṣamasthāś ca nāsedhyāḥ na ca tān āhvayen nṛpaḥ ||

nirveṣṭukāmo vivāhābhimukhaḥ | vyāso 'pi |

	rogī yiyakṣur unmatto dharmārthī vyasanī vratī |

	dānomukho nābhiyojyo nāsedhyo nāhavayec ca tam || iti |

ato 'kalyādiviṣaya eva pratinidhividhānaṃ vyavatiṣṭhata iti sthitam | yadā tv akalyādiprahitapratinidhinā na kāryaniṣpattiḥ tadākalyādīnām apy āhvānaṃ kāryam | tathā ca hārītaḥ |

	deśaṃ kālaṃ ca vijñāya kāryāṇāṃ ca balābalam |

	akalyādīn api śanair yānair āhvāpayen nṛpaḥ || iti |

yadā tu gurutarakāryeṣv abhiyogaḥ tadābhiyuktasyaivāhvānam āvaśyakam, tatra pratinidhiniṣedhāt | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	brahmahatyāsurāpānasteyagurvaṅganāgame |

	anyeṣv asabhyavādeṣu prativādī na dīyate ||

asabhyavādān api sa evāha |

	manuṣyamāraṇe steye paradārābhimarśane |

	abhakṣyabhakṣaṇe caiva kanyāharaṇadūṣaṇe ||

	pāruṣye kūṭakaraṇe nṛpadrohe tathaiva ca |

	prativādī na dāpyaḥ syād arthipratyarthinor api ||

vādiprativādinoḥ pratinidhiḥ prativādī, sa sarvathā gurukāryeṣv evamādiṣu na grāhyaḥ | ata eva hārītaḥ |

	jñātvābhiyogaṃ ye 'pi syur vane pravrajitādayaḥ |

	tān apy āhvapayed rājā gurukāryeṣv akopayan ||

atrākopayann iti vadan prākṛtajane niṣṭhuragirāpy āhvānaṃ kāryam iti jñāpayati | spaṣṭīkṛtaṃ caivad vyāsena |

	utpādayati yo hiṃsāṃ deyaṃ vā na prayacchati |

	yācamānāya dauḥśīlyād ākṛṣyo 'sau nṛpājñayā ||

yas tu nṛpājñayāpi nāgacchati tasya daṇḍam āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	āhūto yas tu nāgacchet darpād bandhubalānvitaḥ |

	abhiyogānurūpeṇa tasya daṇḍaṃ prakalpayet ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	āhūtas tv avamanyeta yaḥ śakto rājaśāsanam |

	tasya kuryān nṛpo daṇḍaṃ vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā ||

	hīne karmaṇi pañcāśat madhyame dviśatāvaraḥ |

	gurukāryeṣu daṇḍyaḥ syān nityaṃ pañcasatāvaraḥ ||

paṇānāṃ saṃkhyeyam |

	kalpito yasya yo daṇḍas tv aparādhasya yatnataḥ |

	paṇānāṃ grahaṇaṃ tu syāt tanmūlyaṃ vātha rājani ||

iti tenaivābhidhānāt | paṇaparimāṇam uttaratra vakṣyamāṇam anusaṃdheyam | sakta iti vacanād āpadādiviṣaye na daṇḍaprakalpanam, kiṃ tu tannivṛttau punar āhvānaṃ kāryam | ata eva vyāsaḥ |

	parānīkahate deśe durbhikṣe vyādhipīḍite |

	kurvīta punar āhvānaṃ daṇḍaṃ na parikalpayet ||

hārīto 'pi |

	rājikaṃ daivikaṃ kāryam abhiyuktasya tattvataḥ |

	sthāne vāpy antarāle vā yāty evaṃ tu na doṣabhāk ||

tattvataḥ paramārthataḥ | aparamārthaṃ ced daṇḍayitvā paścān nyāyena vartayet | tathā ca sa eva |

	pratiṣṭhāpyaṃ tu yatnena so 'nyathā daṇḍabhāg bhavet |

	daṇḍayitvā punaḥ paścād rājā nyāye pravartayet ||

evaṃ yena kenāpy upāyena nītam abhiyuktam abhiyoktrā saha sabhāyāḥ purato 'nyatra vāpekṣitasthāne sthāpayet | tathā ca pitāmahaḥ |

	sabhāyāh purataḥ sthāpyo 'bhiyogī vādināṃ tathā |

	īpsate 'nyatra vā sthāne pramāṇaṃ so 'nyathā na tu ||

yatra sthite duṣṭalakṣaṇapracchādanam aśakyaṃ tatrāvasthāpya ity arthaḥ | tato rājñā pṛṣṭo 'bhiyogī svopayogivṛttāntam āvedayet | abhiyoktṛkṛtāvedanamātrato bhūtānveṣaṇānupapatteḥ | ata eva bhūtānveṣaṇavidhāv uktaṃ manunā |

	svaravarṇeṅgitākāraiś cakṣuṣā bhāṣitena ca || iti |

chalavyavahāre 'pi pūrvapakṣalekhanād arvāk chalavāditvāvadhāraṇāyābhiyuktasya vṛttāntas tanmukhenāvagantavyaḥ | dvayoś chalavāditve niścite paścācchalānusāreṇa darśanavidhiḥ | tasmād abhiyuktasyāpi vṛttāntāvedanam astīty avagantavyam | vivādinoḥ chalitvaniścayānantaraṃ yājñavalkyaḥ |

	ubhayoḥ pratibhūr grāhyaḥ samarthaḥ kāryanirnaye ||

sādhitadhanadaṇḍadhanyor anāyāsena prāptiḥ kāryanirṇayaḥ, tatkaraṇasamarthaḥ pratibhūr arthipratyarthinor dvayor api grāhyo vyavahāradraṣṭety arthaḥ | atra varjanīyān aha kātyāyanaḥ |

	na svāmī na ca vai śatruḥ svāminādhikṛtas tathā |

	niruddho daṇḍitaś caiva saṃśayasthāś ca na kvacit ||

	naiva rikthī na riktaś ca na caivātyantavāsinaḥ |

	rājakāryaniyuktaś ca ye ca pravrajitā narāḥ ||

	nāśakto dhanine dātuṃ daṇḍaṃ rājñe ca tatsamam |

	nāvijñāto grahītavyaḥ pratibhūtvakriyāṃ prati ||

saṃśayasthāḥ abhiśastāḥ | atyantavāsinaḥ naiṣṭhikabrahmacāriṇaḥ | tatsamaṃ vivādāspadībhūtadravyasamam | vihitadaṇḍopalakṣaṇārtham etat | yadi vādī vivādapratibhuvaṃ dātum asamarthaḥ tadāpi tenaivoktam |

	atha cet pratibhūr nāsti vādayogyasya vādinaḥ |

	sa rakṣito dinasyānte dadyād dūtāya vetanam ||

dūtāya sādhyapālāya | tathā parityājitagṛhītadravya eva vivādī nyāye pravartya ity āha sa eva |

	gṛhītagrahaṇo nyāye na pravartyo mahībhṛtā |

	tasya vā tatsamarpyaṃ syāt sthāpayed vā parasya tat || iti |

parasya madhyasthasya, samīpa iti śeṣaḥ | tathābhiyoktrādīnām uktikramo 'pi tenaivoktaḥ |

	tatrābhiyoktā prāk brūyād abhiyuktas tv anantaram |

	tayor ante sadasyās tu prāḍvivākas tataḥ param ||

prāg brūyāt pratijñāṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	ājñālekhyau paṭṭake śāsane vā ādhau patre vikraye vā kraye vā |

	rājñe kuryāt pūrvam āvedanaṃ yaḥ tasya jñeyaḥ pūrvavādo vidhijñaiḥ ||

vivāde sarvatrābhiyoktur eva pratijñāvāditvam ity arthaḥ | atrāpavādam āha sa eva |

	yasya vābhyadhikā pīḍā kāryaṃ vā hy adhikaṃ bhavet |

	tasyārthivādo dātavyo na yaḥ pūrvaṃ nivedayet ||

arthavādaḥ pūrvapakṣaḥ | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	yasya syād adhikā pīḍā kāryaṃ vāpy adhikaṃ bhavet |

	pūrvapakṣo bhavet tasya na yaḥ pūrvaṃ nivedayet ||

evaṃvidhaviṣaye arthipratyarthibhāvasya vaiparītyaṃ parīkṣakaiḥ kāryam ity arthaḥ | yatrobhayor api parasparam arthitvaṃ pratyarthitvaṃ ca sādhyabhedāt yugapad bhavati tatrotkṛṣṭajāteḥ bahupīḍasya vā arthivādaḥ pūrvaṃ draṣṭavyaḥ | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	ahaṃpūrvikayā tāvad arthipratyarthinau yadā |

	vādo varṇānupūrvyeṇa grāhyaḥ pīḍām avekṣya vā ||

samānavarṇatve pīḍāpekṣayā grāhyaḥ | anekavādiyugmānāṃ yugapadupasthāne tu darśanakramam āha manuḥ |

	arthānarthāv ubhau buddhvā dharmādharmau ca kevalau |

	varṇakrameṇa sarvāṇi paśyet kāryāṇi kāryiṇām ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ darśanopakramaḥ **

**atha pratijñāpādaḥ**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	upasthite tatas tasmin vādī pakṣaṃ prakalpayet || iti |

samīpasthe pratyarthini pakṣaṃ lekhayed ity arthaḥ | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	pratyarthino 'grato lekhyaṃ yathāveditam arthinā || iti |

yathāveditam iti yat sādhyam āveditaṃ tad eva lekhyam, na sādhyāntaram iti pratipādanārtham, na punar yāvad āveditaṃ tāvad eva lekhyam iti | yato 'nāveditasyāpi vatsarādiviśeṣasyedānīṃ lekhanaṃ kāryam iti sa evāha |

	samāmāsatadardhāharnāmajātyādicihnitam || iti |

samā saṃvatsaraḥ | sa ca dhanaprayogādikālīno lekhanīyaḥ | māsādir api tatkālīna eva | ādiśabdasaṃgṛhītāni viśeṣaṇāni kātyāyanena darśitāni |

	niveśya kālaṃ varṣaṃ ca māsaṃ pakṣaṃ tithiṃ tathā |

	velāṃ pradeśaṃ viṣayaṃ sthānaṃ jātyākṛtī vayaḥ ||

	sādhyadravyapramāṇaṃ ca saṃkhyāṃ nāma tathātmanaḥ |

	rājñāṃ ca kramaśo nāma nivāsaṃ sādhyanāma ca ||

	kramāt pitṝṇāṃ nāmāni pīḍām āhartṛdāyakau |

	kṣamāliṅgāni cānyāni pakṣaṃ saṃkīrtya kalpayet || iti |

kālo dhanaprayogādikālaḥ vartamānena rājñopalakṣitaḥ | varṣaṃ devavarṣam ityādi | velā bhujyādikriyopalakṣitaḥ kālaḥ | pradeśaḥ sādhyakṣetrādeḥ sthalaviśeṣaḥ | viṣayo 'ntarvedyādideśaḥ | sthānaṃ vivādāspadasya gṛhāder grāmādiḥ | ākṛtiḥ avayavasaṃsthānaviśeṣaḥ | vayas tāruṇyādi | pramāṇaṃ parimāṇaṃ daṇḍatulāprasthādikam | ātmano 'rthinaḥ | rājñāṃ kṣetrādibhuktikālīnānām | nivāso vāsasthānaṃ gṛhagoṣṭhādi | pitaro 'rthipratyarthinor janakādayaḥ | pīḍā pratibhuvā dhanikena kṛtā | āhartā pratigrahādyāgamakartā | dāyako dātā | kṣamāliṅgāni ātmīyadhanādeḥ paropabhogāsahananimittāni | anyāni pradarśitebhyo 'dhikāny api vṛddhyāgamādīni | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	niravadyaṃ sapratijñaṃ pramāṇāgamasaṃyutam |

	dravyasaṃkhyodayaṃ pīḍāṃ kṣamāliṅgaṃ ca lekhayet ||

tathā lakṣaṇāntarāṇy api sa evāha |

	alpākṣaraḥ prabhūtārtho niḥsaṃdigdhas tv anākulaḥ |

	yukto virodhikaraṇair virodhipratiṣedhakaḥ ||

	evam ādiguṇān samyag ālocya ca suniścitaḥ |

	pakṣaḥ kṛtaḥ samādeyaḥ pakṣābhāsas tato 'nyathā || iti |

saṃgrahakāro 'pi |

	arthavad dharmasaṃyuktaṃ paripūrṇam anākulam |

	sādhyavad vācakapadaṃ prakṛtārthānubandhi ca ||

	prasiddham aviruddhaṃ ca niścitaṃ sādhanakṣamam |

	saṃkṣiptaṃ nikhilārthaṃ ca deśakālāvirodhi ca ||

	varṣartumāsapakṣāhovelādeśapradeśavat |

	sthānāvasathasādhyākhyājātyākāravayoyutam ||

	sādhyapramāṇasaṃkhyāvad ātmapratyarthināmavat |

	parātmapūrvajān ekarājanāmabhir aṅkitam ||

	kṣamāliṅgātmapīḍāvat kathitāhartṛdayakam |

	yad āvedayate rājñe tad bhāṣety abhidhīyate || iti |

arthavat prayojanavat | dharmasaṃyuktam alpākṣaratvaprabhūtārthavattvādiguṇānvitam | paripūrṇam adhyāhārānapekṣam | anākulam asaṃdigdhākṣarakam | sādhyavat siṣādhayiṣitārthāhīnam | vācakapadaṃ gauṇalākṣaṇikarahitam | prakṛtārthānubandhi prāgāveditārthāvirodhi | prasiddhaṃ lokaprasiddhavastuviṣayam | aviruddhaṃ purarāṣṭraprāḍvivākanṛpādyaviruddham | tathā pūrvāparāviruddhaṃ pratyakādipramāṇāviruddhaṃ vyāvahārikadharmāviruddhaṃ ca | niścitam arthantaraśaṅkārahitam | sādhanakṣamaṃ sādhanārham | saṃkṣiptaṃ anativistṛtam | nikhilārtham anavaśeṣitavaktavyam | deśakālāvirodhi madhyadeśīyaṃ kramukakṣetram, śaratkālīnam āmraphalasahasram apahṛtam ity evamādirahitam | parātmapūrvajānekarājanāmabhir aṅkitam, paraḥ prativādī | ātmā vādī | pūrvajāḥ tayoḥ pitrādayaḥ | aneke rājāno bhuktikālīnāḥ | teṣāṃ nāmāni parātmapūrvajānekarājanāmāni, taiś cihnitam | śiṣṭam uktārtham | arthavattvādīni desakālāvirodhitvāntāny arthipratyarthināmasahitāni sarvavyavahārabhāṣopayogīni | tena taiḥ sarvatra bhāṣāyām avaśyaṃ bhavitavyam | tair vinā kvacid api sādhyasiddheḥ sukhena kartum aśakyatvāt | varṣādīni punar viśeṣaṇāni sarvāṇi na sarvatropayogīni, katipayair vināpi tatra tatra sādhyasiddhisaṃbhavāt | ato yatra yeṣām upayogas tatraiva teṣāṃ niveśanaṃ kāryam, netaratrāpi, prayojanābhāvāt | tatra varṣādikālānāṃ vṛddhimaddhanadvaiguṇyādivivāde pratigrahakrayādhyādīnāṃ paurvāparyavivāde copayogaḥ | deśapradeśasthānānāṃ tathā parātmapūrvajānekarājanāmadheyānām āhartṛdāyakakathanasya ca sthāvaravivādeṣūpayogaḥ | sādhyākhyājātyākāravayasāṃ cauryāsvāmivikrayādāv arthavivāde 'py upayogaḥ | pramāṇasaṃkhyayor meyatulimagaṇimādidravyavivāde cauryavivāde copayogaḥ | kṣamāliṅgānām upekṣitasthānādivivādeṣūpayogaḥ | ātmapīḍāyāḥ ṛṇikalagnakavivādādāv upayoga ity eṣā dik | evaṃ cārthavattvādibhiḥ saha varṣādīnāṃ yathopayogaṃ kvacit kvacin niveśanam iti mantavyam | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	deśaś caiva tathā sthānaṃ saṃniveśas tathaiva ca |

	jātiḥ saṃjñā nivāsaś ca pramāṇaṃ kṣetranāma ca ||

	pitṛpaitāmahaś caiva pūrvarājānukīrtanam |

	sthāvareṣu vivādeṣu daśaitāni niveśayet || iti |

teṣāṃ tatropayogād ity abhiprāyaḥ | hārīto 'pi |

	āsanaṃ śayanaṃ yānaṃ tāmraṃ kāṃsyam ayomayam |

	dhānyam aśmamayaṃ vastraṃ dvipadaṃ ca catuṣpadam ||

	maṇimuktāpravālāni hīrakaṃ rūpyakāñcanam |

	yadi dravyasamūhaḥ syāt saṃkhyā kāryā tathaiva ca ||

	yasmin deśe ca yad dravyaṃ yena mānena mīyate |

	tena tasmin yathā saṃkhyā kartavyā vyavahāribhiḥ || iti |

hīrakaṃ vajram, tena mānena mitvā saṃkhyā kartavyety āha | evaṃ ca yatra yad upayujyate tatra tadabhāve sādyasiddheḥ kartum aśakyatvād anādeya evopayogivihīnaḥ pakṣaḥ | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	deśakālavihīnas ca dravyasaṃkhyāvivarjitaḥ |

	kriyāpramāṇahīnaś ca pakṣo nādeya iṣyate ||

kriyāpramāṇaṃ sādhyaparimāṇam | tathā prayojanavatvādilakṣaṇahīno 'pi pakṣo heya eva |

	aprasiddhaṃ nirābādhaṃ nirarthaṃ niṣprayojanam |

	asādhyaṃ vā viruddhaṃ vā pakṣaṃ rājā vivarjayet ||

tatrāprasiddho bṛhaspatinā nirūpitaḥ |

	na kenacit kṛto yas tu so 'prasiddha udāhṛtaḥ | iti |

atrodāharaṇaṃ phalasahasrakṛtaṃ sthālaṃ gṛhītam iti | nirābādho nirupadravaḥ, yathā asmadbhavanasthapradīpaprabhayā svagṛhe vyavaharatīti | nirarthaniṣprayojanau bṛhaspatinā darśitau |

	svalpāparādhaḥ svalpārtho nirarthaka iti smṛtaḥ |

	kāryabādhavihīnas tu vijñeyo niṣprayojanaḥ ||

tatra nirarthaksyodāharaṇam: aham anena sasmitaṃ nirīkṣitaḥ, māmakī lākṣānenāpahṛteti vā | niṣprayojanasya tu yathā: yajñadatto 'smadgṛhasamīpe ślāghamānaḥ paṭhatīti | prakārāntareṇāpy etau tenaiva darśitau |

	kusīdādyaiḥ padair hīno vyavahāro nirarthakaḥ |

	vākpāruṣyādibhiś caiva vijñeyo niṣprayojanaḥ ||

ṛṇādānādyaṣṭādaśapadānantarbhūto nirarthakaḥ | vākpāruṣyādibhiḥ sādhyasiddhyanupayuktaiḥ sahitaḥ pakṣo niṣprayojana ity arthaḥ | asādhyaviruddhāv api tenaiva darśitau |

	mamānena pradātavyaṃ śaśaśṛṅgakṛtaṃ dhanuḥ |

	asaṃbhāvyam asādhyaṃ taṃ pakṣaṃ āhur manīṣiṇaḥ ||

	yasminn āvedite pakṣe prāḍvivāke ca rājani |

	pure rāṣṭre virodhaḥ syād viruddaḥ so 'bhidhīyate || iti |

nārado 'pi bhāṣādoṣān darsayati |

	anyārtham arthahīnaṃ ca pramāṇāgamavarjitam |

	lekhyahīnādhikaṃ bhraṣṭaṃ bhāṣādoṣā udāhṛtāḥ ||

svayamam eva vyācaṣṭe 

	arthe sādhāraṇe py eko vādyarthe vāniyuktakaḥ |

	lekhayed yas tu bhāṣāyām anyārthāṃ tāṃ vidur budhāḥ ||

eka eva gaṇī gaṇasya kāryam ekasya vā kāryam aniyukto 'saṃbandhī vā lekhayed yasyāṃ bhāṣāyām ity arthaḥ |

	brahmahāyam iti jñeyo dveṣān mohād vadet tu yaḥ |

	sādhyaṃ ca mocayet tatra dravyahīnāṃ tu tāṃ viduḥ ||

uktaṃ sādhyavādinā yasyāṃ tyajyate sā ca bhāṣārthahīnety arthaḥ |

	gaṇime tulime meye tathā kṣetragṛhādike |

	yatra saṃkhyā na nirdiṣṭā sā pramāṇavivarjitā ||

	vidyayā prāptam ādhyāptaṃ labdhaṃ krītaṃ kramāgatam |

	na tv evaṃ likhyate yatra sā bhāṣā syād anāgamā ||

	samā māsas tathā pakṣas tithir vāras tathaiva ca |

	yatraitāni na likhyante lekhyahīnāṃ tu tāṃ viduḥ ||

	lekhayitvā tu yo bhāṣām nirdiṣṭe tathottare |

	uddiśet sākṣiṇaṃ pūrvam adhikāṃ tāṃ vinirdiśet ||

	yatra syād ubhayaṃ sarvaṃ nirdiṣṭaṃ pūrvavādinā |

	saṃdigdham iva likhyeta bhraṣṭāṃ bhāṣāṃ tu tāṃ viduḥ || iti |

yatra pakṣadvayam akhilaṃ pratijñāvādinaiva nirdiṣṭaṃ syād ity arthaḥ | tathānyān api pakṣān anādeyān āha sa eva |

	bhinnakramo vyutkramārthaḥ prakīrṇārtho nirarthakaḥ |

	atītakālo dviṣṭhaś (?) ca pakṣo 'nādeya iṣyate ||

tatra bhinnakramas tenaiva vyākhyātaḥ |

	yathāsthānaniveśena naiva pakṣārthakalpanā |

	śasyate na sa pakṣas tu bhinnakrama udāhṛtaḥ ||

vyastākṣarasaṃsthāno bhinnakrama ity arthaḥ | vyutkramārtho vyavahitānvayenārthabodhakaḥ | prakīrṇārthaḥ saṃkalitārthaḥ | nirarthakādīn sa evācaṣṭe |

	mūlam arthaṃ parityajya tadguṇo yatra likhyate |

	nirarthakaḥ sa vai pakṣo bhūtasādhanavarjitaḥ ||

	bhūtakālam atikrāntaṃ dravyaṃ yatra vilikhyate |

	atītakālaḥ pakṣo 'sau pramāṇe saty api smṛtaḥ ||

	yasmin pakṣe dvidhā sādhyaṃ bhinnakālavimarśanam |

	vimṛśyate kriyābhedāt sa pakṣo dviṣṭha ucyate || iti ||

bhūtasādhanaṃ mūlabhūtadhanasādhanam | bhūtakālo 'vadhibhūtaḥ kālaḥ | kriyābhedāt pramāṇabhedāt | tathāparān api pakṣābhāsān āha sa eva |

	anyākṣaraniveśena anyarthagamanena ca |

	ākulaṃ tu bhavel lekhyaṃ kriyā caivākulā bhavet ||

	upekṣā yatra sādhyasya viṃśatir daśa vā samāḥ |

	śaktenāpi kṛtā vāde tasya pakṣo mṛṣā bhavet ||

	sāhasaṃ saha sādhyena nirdiṣṭaṃ yatra lekhayet |

	uktikramavihīnatvāt so 'pi pakṣo na siddhyati || 

kriyā sādhyam, sādhanaṃ pramāṇam | hārīto 'pi |

	prakrāntasādhano 'rthas tu dvidhā yasmin niveśyate |

	svasādhyād vā vibhinno vā so 'pi pakṣo mṛṣā bhavet ||

prakrāntaḥ sādhayitum upakrānto 'rtho dvidhā dviprakāreṇa dādhyatayātha vāveditāt sādhyād vidhāntareṇa tadvirodhitayā vā yatra pakṣe niveśyate so 'pi pakṣābhāsa ity arthaḥ | bhṛgur api |

	utsṛṣṭaṃ yatra hīnena kalpyaṃ vāpy ekam ekataḥ |

	tatra pakṣo na sādhyaḥ syāc chāstraśiṣṭavivarjitaḥ ||

	viruddhaś cāviruddhas ca dvāv apy arthau niveśitau |

	ekasmin yatra dṛśyete taṃ pakṣaṃ dūratas tyajet ||

hīnena hīnavādinā | pitāmaho 'pi |

	parasparaviruddhāni yaḥ padāni niveśayet |

	viruddhapadasaṃkīrṇā bhāṣā tasya na siddhyati ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	nyāyasthaṃ necchate kartuṃ anyāyyaṃ vā karoty ayam |

	na lekhayati yas tv evaṃ tasya pakṣo na siddhyati ||

nyāyāgataṃ madīyaṃ dhanaṃ gṛhītvā na dadatītivat pratiṣedharūpeṇa vā madīyaṃ kṣetrādikam apaharatītivad vidhirūpeṇa vā na lekhayatīty arthaḥ | tathā |

	purarāṣṭraviruddhaś ca yaś ca rājñā vivarjitaḥ |

	anekapadasaṃkīrṇaḥ pūrvapakṣo na siddhyati ||

purarāṣṭrācāraviruddho rājatyaktaśulkaśālādiviṣayaḥ sarvadhā na siddhyati | ṛṇādānādyanekapadasaṃkīrṇas tu kriyābhedād yaugapadyena na siddhyatīty arthaḥ | yat punas tenoktam |

	bahupratijñaṃ yat kāryaṃ vyavahāre suniścitam |

	kāmaṃ tad api gṛhṇīyād rājā tattvabubhutsayā ||

iti, tad anekapadasaṃkīrṇasya kalabhedenopādeyatvapratipādanārtham, atha vā ṛṇādānādyekapadāntargatānekajātīyānāṃ hiraṇyavastrapaśudhānyānām ekajātīyānāṃ saṃkhyāparimāṇadeśakālavṛddhyādibhedena gṛhītānāṃ yathāvṛttakathanārthaṃ bhedena pratijñāya punas tat sarvaṃ pratideyam ity ekakāryatayopasaṃhṛtaṃ grāhyam ity evaṃ pratipādanārtham, ato na prācīnavacanena virodhaḥ | tathā |

	āgamaḥ paribhogaś ca vyucchittiḥ prārthanā tathā |

	etac catuṣṭayaṃ prāhuḥ bhāṣādoṣāś tv akāraṇāḥ ||

āgamo dhanāgamananimittaṃ pratigrahādiḥ | paribhogo yatheṣṭaviniyogānivṛttiḥ | vyutcchittiḥ deśaviplavādinā bhogavicchittiḥ | prārthanā yuktibhir bhogāgamakīrtanam | etad āgamādicatuṣṭayaṃ bhāṣāguṇā iti prāhuḥ | ye punar āgamādayaḥ akāraṇāḥ vinā niveśakāraṇaṃ bhāṣāyāṃ niviṣṭās te bhāṣādoṣā iti prāhur ity arthaḥ | ato 'trākāṅkṣitasyāpāvaḥ kāryo 'nākāṅkṣitasya voddhāraḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	adhikān bhedayed arthān nyūnāṃś ca pratipūrayet |

	bhūmau niveśayed tāvat yāvad artho na niścitaḥ ||

chedayed uddhared ity arthaḥ | bhūmāv ity upalakṣaṇārthaḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	pūrvapakaṣaṃ svabhāvoktaṃ prāḍvivāko 'bhlekhayet |

	pāṇḍulekhena phalake tataḥ patre viśodhitam ||

svabhāvoktaṃ bhayādyupādhirāhityenoktam | viśodhitam anyūnānatiriktam aprasiddhatvādidūṣaṇarahitaṃ ca | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	pratijñādoṣanirmuktaṃ sādhyatatkāraṇānvitam |

	niścitaṃ lokasiddhaṃ ca pakṣaṃ pakṣavido viduḥ |

lokasiddhaṃ vyāvahārikadharmāviruddham ity arthaḥ, lokaprasiddham ity evaṃvidhārthasya pratijñādoṣanirmuktam ity anenaivārthād uktatvāt | ata eva manuḥ |

	sabhyā bhāṣā na bhavati yady api syāt pratiṣṭhitā |

	bahiś ced bhāṣyate dharmāt niyatād vyāvahārikāt ||

sarvadoṣarahitāpi bhāṣā vyāvahārikadharmaviruddhā cet sabhāsadbhir na grāhyety arthaḥ | evam uktalakṣaṇaḥ pakṣaś caturvidha ity āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	śaṅkābhiyogas tathyaṃ ca labdhe 'rtha 'bhyarthanaṃ tathā |

	vṛtte vāde punar nyāyaḥ pakṣo jñeyaś caturvidhaḥ ||

atra nāradaḥ |

	śodhayet pūrvavādaṃ tu yāvan nottaradarsanam |

	avaṣṭabdhasyottareṇa nivṛttaṃ śodhanaṃ bhavet ||

na cātra śaṅkhavelānyāyenottaradānayogyakālātīte śodhananivṛttir iti śaṅkanīyam | yata āha sa eva |

	bhāṣāyā uttaraṃ yāvat pratyarthī na niviśayet |

	arthī tu lekhayet tāvad yāvad vastu vivakṣitam || iti ||

kecin nirdiṣṭe 'py uttare śodhanam icchanti tad anavasthāprasaṅgāt pūrvoktavacanavirodhāc ca heyam | ata eva saṅgrahakāraḥ |

	bhāṣānyūnātirikteṣu samyak sūtraṇakāribhiḥ |

	punaḥ pratisamādhāya śṛṇuyād uttaraṃ tataḥ ||

	yasmāt pratyarthinārabdha uttare 'rthiprabhāṣitam |

	upayogy api nādeyaṃ tasyāvasaravarjanāt ||

ārabdhe datta ity arthaḥ | dīyamāne 'py uttare pratisamādhānasyeṣṭatvāt tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	mohād vā yadi vā śāṭhyādyannoktaṃ pūrvavādinā |

	uttarāntargataṃ vāpi tadgrāhyam ubhayor api ||

uttarāntargatam uttare kathyamāne 'pi vādinā procyamānam ity arthaḥ | ubhayoḥ arthipratyarthinoḥ | pratyarthinas tu kriyāpāda uttaraḥ | yadā pūrvapakṣam aśodhayitvaiva sabhyair uttaraṃ gṛhītam, tadā sabhyadaṇḍanaṃ kṛtvā pratijñāpūrvakaṃ kāryaṃ draṣṭavyam | yadā tv arthī sapadi pratijñāṃ kartum asamarthaḥ tadā bṛhaspatir āha |

	abhiyoktāpragalbhatvāt vaktuṃ notsahate yadā |

	tasya kālaḥ pradātavyaḥ kāryaśaktyanurūpataḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ pratijñāpādaḥ **

**athottarapādaḥ** 

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	viniścite pūrvapakṣe grāhyāgrāhyaviśeṣite |

	pratijñārthe sthirībhūte lekhayed uttaraṃ tataḥ ||

vādinā niścitasyāpi pakṣasya punaḥ prāḍvivākādibhir vicārya kṛte sthairye tatas tatpakṣasyottaraṃ prativādī lekhayed ity arthaḥ | nārado 'pi |

	yadā tv evaṃvidhaḥ pakṣaḥ kalpitaḥ pūrvavādinā |

	dadyāt tatpakṣasaṃbandhaṃ prativādī tadottaram ||

evaṃvidha ity asyārtho hārītena vivṛtaḥ |

	svalpavarṇo 'rthabahulaḥ pratijñādoṣavarjitaḥ |

	sākṣimān kāraṇopeto niravadyaḥ suniscitaḥ ||

	īdṛśaḥ pūrvapakṣas tu likhito yatra vādinā |

	dadyāt tatpakṣasaṃbaddhaṃ prativādī tadottaram ||

sākṣimān prāḍvivākādipratyavekṣaṇavān | yadā tv anīdṛśas tadā na dadyād ity arthasiddhaṃ spaṣṭayituṃ pakṣābhāsam ekam udāhṛtya tasyottaraṃ na deyam ity āha sa eva |

	sādhāraṇī ca yā bhūmir yac ca dravyaṃ gaṇāśritam |

	ekasya prārthayānasya na vaded uttaraṃ budhaḥ || iti |

ataḥ parīkṣitapūrvapakṣasyaiva prativādinā uttaraṃ lekhyam ityāha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	śrutārthasyottaraṃ lekhyaṃ pūrvāvedakasaṃnidhau || iti |

śrutabhāṣārthasya pratyarthina ity akṣarārthaḥ | saṃgrahakāro 'pi |

	ananyārtham ahīnārthaṃ nyāyāgamasamanvitam |

	anyūnānadhikādṛṣṭam ananyākṣarasaṃbhavam ||

	bhāṣāyām it patreṣū likhitāyām anantaram |

	pratyarthinaḥ śrutārthasya kalo 'yaṃ dātum uttaram || iti |

ananyārtham ityādilakṣaṇajātaṃ yathā bhavati tathā bhāṣāyāṃ likhitāyām ity arthaḥ | ayaṃ ca kālaniyamo gavādivivādeṣv eva | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	gobhūhiraṇyastrīsteyapāruṣyātyayikeṣu ca |

	sāhaseṣv abhiśāpe ca sadya eva vivādayet ||

abhiśāpaḥ pāpābhiśaṃsanam | tasya pāruṣyabhedatve 'py ādarārthaṃ punar vacanam | ātyayikaṃ kātyāyanenoktam |

	vyapaiti gauravaṃ yatra vināśas tyāga eva vā |

	kālaṃ tatra na kurvīta kāryam ātyayikaṃ hi tat ||

tathānyeṣv api kāryeṣu sadya evottaraṃ kāryam ity āha sa eva |

	dhenāv anaḍuhi kṣetre strīṣu prajanane tathā |

	nyāse yācitake datte tathaiva krayavikraye ||

	kanyāyā dūṣaṇe steye kalahe sāhase nidhau |

	upadhau kauṭasākṣye ca sadya eva vivādayet ||

upadhiḥ bhayādivaśād abhyupagamaḥ | yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	sāhasasteyapāruṣyago'bhiśāpātyaye striyāṃ |

	vivādayet sadya eva kālo 'nyatrecchayā smṛtaḥ ||

anyatra ṛṇādānādāv ity arthaḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	gahanatvād vivādānām asāmarthyāt smṛter api |

	ṛṇādiṣu haret kālaṃ kāmaṃ tattvabubhutsayā ||

ṛṇādiṣu ṛṇādānādivivādapadeṣv ity arthaḥ | ata eva pitāmahaḥ |

	ṛṇopanidhinikṣepadānasaṃbhūyakarmaṇām |

	samaye dāyabhāge ca kālaḥ kāryaḥ prayatnataḥ ||

evamādiṣv api kāladānaṃ vismṛtyādikāraṇataḥ pratyarthinaḥ kālārthitva eva | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	śrutvā lekhyagataṃ tv arthaṃ pratyarthī kāraṇād yadi |

	kālaṃ vivāde yācet tasya deyo na saṃśayaḥ ||

sadyaḥkṛteṣu kāryeṣu smṛtisaṃbhavāt sadya eva vivāha ity āha sa eva |

	sadyaḥ kṛteṣu kāryeṣu sadya eva vivādayet |

	kālātīteṣu vā kālaṃ dadyāt pratyarthine prabhuḥ ||

pratyarthina ity upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	matir notsahate yasya vivāde vaktum icchataḥ |

	dātavya eva kālaḥ syād arthipratyarthinor api ||

dātavyas ca kālaḥ kiyān ity apekṣite sa evāha |

	sadya ekāhapañcāhau tryahaṃ vā gurulāghavāt |

	labhen māsaṃ tripakṣaṃ vā saptāhaṃ vā ṛṇādiṣu ||

gautamo 'pi "saṃvatsaraṃ pratīkṣeta" iti | atra vyavasthām āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	kālaṃ śaktaṃ viditvā tu kāryāṇāṃ ca balābalam |

	alpaṃ vā bahu vā kālaṃ dadyāt pratyarthine prabhuḥ ||

kālaḥ arthasaṃbandhādeḥ | śaktiḥ kāryiṇām | kāryāṇāṃ sādhyabhūtārthānām | ślokasyārthas tu tenaiva prapañcitaḥ |

	sadyaḥ kṛte sadya eva māsātīte dinaṃ bhavet |

	ṣaḍābdike trirātraṃ syāt saptāhaṃ dvādaśābdike ||

	viṃśatyabde daśāhaṃ tu māsārthaṃ vā labheta sāḥ |

	māsaṃ triṃśatsamātīte tripakṣaṃ parato bhavet ||

śaktito vyavasthāṃ ca pradarśayati |

	kālaṃ saṃvatsarād arvāk svayam eva yathepsitam |

	saṃvatsaraṃ jaḍonmattamanaske vyādhipīḍite ||

	digantaraprapanne vā ajñātārthe ca vastuni | 

	mūlaṃ vā sākṣinō vātha paradeśe sthitā yadā ||

	tatra kālo bhavet puṃsām ā svadeśasamāgamāt ||

saṃvatsarād arvāg dinādinānāpakṣās tripakṣāntāḥ kāryāṇāṃ śaktyanusārataḥ sabhāpatinā vyavasthāpanīyāḥ | mūlaṃ vivādādhyāsitaṃ dhanam | tathā kāryāpekṣayā vyavasthāṃ spaṣṭayati |

	dinaṃ māsārdhamāsau vā ṛtuḥ saṃvatsaro 'pi vā |

	kriyāsthityanurūpas tu deyaḥ kālaḥ pareṇa tu ||

kriyāsthitiḥ kāryagurulāghavasthitiḥ | evaṃ vyavasthāpitānyatamakāle saṃprāpte pūrvapakṣākṣarārthasyānyūnānatiriktam uttaraṃ lekhyam ity āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	ekakāle samānīte pratyarthī sabhyasaṃnidhau |

	pūrvapakṣākṣarasamaṃ lekhayed uttaraṃ tataḥ ||

atra nṛpaṃ praty āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	yāvān yasmin samācāraḥ pāraṃparyakramāgataḥ |

	taṃ pratīkṣya yathānyāyam uttaraṃ dāpayen nṛpaḥ ||

uttaralakṣaṇaṃ tv āha prajāpatiḥ |

	pakṣasya vyāpakaṃ sāram asaṃdigham anākulam |

	avyākhyāgamyam ity etad uttaraṃ tadvido viduḥ ||

pakṣasya vyāpakaṃ kṛtsnapakṣācchādakam | sāraṃ prāgabhiyogottarakṣamam | asaṃdigdhaṃ khaṇḍaśleṣādirahitam | anākulam anvitārtham | avyākhyāgamyaṃ subodham | hārīto 'pi |

	pūrvapakṣārthasaṃbaddham anekārtham anākulam |

	analpam avyastapadaṃ vyāpakaṃ nātibhūri ca ||

	sārabhūtam asaṃdigdham apakṣaikāṃśasaṃbhavam |

	arthiśravanam agūḍhārthaṃ deyam uttaram īdṛśam ||

pūrvapakṣārthasaṃbaddham abhiyogānugatam | anekārthaṃ niṣkṛṣṭārthajātam | avyastapadaṃ niścitapratijñāpūrvakam | apakṣaikāṃśasaṃbhavam anavaśeṣitasvapakṣaikadeśam | arthiśravaṃ pūrvāvedakaśrutam | agūḍhārtham avakroktiprasiddhapadaikavedyam | evaṃlakṣaṇam uttaraṃ caturvidhaṃ jñeyam,

	caturvidhaḥ pūrvapakṣaḥ pratipakṣas tathaiva ca |

iti bṛhaspatismaraṇāt | kathaṃ punaḥ pratipakṣacāturvidhyam ity apekṣite nāradaḥ |

	mithyā saṃpratipattyā vā pratyavaskandanena vā |

	prāṅnyāyavidhisiddhyā vāpy uttaraṃ syāc caturvidham ||

itthaṃbhūtalakṣaṇā ceyaṃ tṛtīyā | tatra mithyāsaṃpratipattyor lakṣaṇam āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	abhiyukto 'bhiyogasya yadi kuryāt tu nihnavam |

	mithyā tat tu vijānīyād uttaraṃ vyavahārataḥ ||

	sādhyasya tathyavacanaṃ pratipattir udāhṛtā || iti |

pratyavaskandanasya ca lakṣaṇaṃ nāradenoktam |

	arthinā likhito yo 'rthaḥ pratyarthī yadi tat tathā |

	prapadya kāraṇaṃ brūyāt pratyavaskandanaṃ smṛtam || iti |

prāṅnyāyasya lakṣaṇam āha hārītaḥ |

	asminn arthe mamānena vādaḥ pūrvam abhūt tadā |

	jito 'yam iti ced brūyāt prāṅnyāyaṃ syāt tad uttaram || iti |

evam uktalakṣaṇāny uttarāṇi spaṣṭīkartuṃ prajāpatināpy uktāni |

	yāvad āveditaṃ kiṃcit matsaṃbandham ihārthinā |

	tāvat sarvam asadbhūtam iti mithyottaraṃ smṛtam ||

	asyaiva deyam evaitan nāsadbhāṣitam arthinā |

	iti saṃpratipattyākhyaṃ dvitīyam idam uttaram ||

	dattam evaṃ mamānena kiṃ tv asyāpi mayā punaḥ |

	pratidattam itīdṛk ca pratyavaskandanaṃ smṛtam ||

	asminn arthāntare pūrvam ārabdho 'smy aham arthinā |

	jitaś cāyaṃ mayā tatra prāṅnyāyavidhir ucyate ||

ayaṃ ca prāṅnyāyas triprakāra ity āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	vibhāvayāmi kulikaiḥ sākṣibhir likhitena vā |

	jitaś caiva mayāyaṃ prāk prāṅnyāyas triprakārakaḥ ||

kulikair iti prakṛtavyavahāradraṣṭṝṇām upalakṣaṇārtham | tathā mithyā caturvidhety āha sa eva |

	mithyaitan nābhijānāmi tadā tatra na saṃnidhiḥ |

	ajātaś cāsmi tatkāla iti mithyā caturvidhā || iti |

evaṃ saṃpratipatter āpa (?) gṛhītam, satyam, yathāyaṃ vakti tathaivety evamādayo bhedā yathāsaṃbhavam ūhanīyāḥ | pratyavaskandanasyāpi gṛhītaṃ pratidattam, pratigraheṇa vā labdham ityādayo bhedā draṣṭavyāḥ | atra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	pratharthividhir ākhyātaḥ saṅgatārthaprapādane |

	caturvidhasyāpy adhunā yan na grāhyaṃ tad ucyate ||

	prastutād anyamadhyasthaṃ nyūnādhikam asaṃgatam |

	avyāpy asāraṃ saṃdigdhaṃ pratipakṣaṃ na lekhayet ||

prastutād anyad arthilikhitābhiyogāparihārakam | madhyasthaṃ pratipakṣabhāvarahitam | asaṃgatam abhiyogānanugatam | kātyāyano 'pi |

	aprasiddhaṃ viruddhaṃ yad atyalpam atibhūri ca |

	saṃdigdhāsaṃbhavāvyaktam anyārthaṃ cātidoṣavat ||

	avyāpakaṃ vyastapadaṃ nigūḍhārthaṃ tathākulam |

	vyākhyāgamyam asāraṃ ca nottaraṃ śasyate budhaiḥ || iti |

atrādyān pañcottarābhāsān sa eva vyācaṣṭe |

	cihnākārasahasraṃ tu samayaṃ cāvijānatā |

	bhāṣāntareṇa vā proktam aprasiddhaṃ tad uttaram ||

lāñchanāvayavasaṃsthānasaṃkhyāsamayānabhijñoktam adeśabhāṣayoktaṃ cāprasiddham ity arthaḥ |

	pratidattaṃ mayā bālye pratidattaṃ mayā na hi |

	yad evam āha vijñeyaṃ viruddhaṃ tad ihottaram ||

pūrvāparaviruddhābhidhānaṃ viruddhottaram ity arthaḥ |

	jitaḥ purā mayāyaṃ ca tv arthe 'sminn iti bhāṣitum |

	purā mayāyam iti yat tadūnaṃ cottaraṃ smṛtam ||

asminn arthe purāyaṃ mayā jita iti vaktavye purā mayety etāvanmātram uttaram atyalpam ity arthaḥ |

	gṛhītam iti vācyaṃ tu kāryaṃ tena kṛtaṃ mayā |

	purā gṛhītaṃ yad dravyam iti yac catibhūri tat ||

gṛhītam ity etāvanmātreṇa satyottare vaktavye kāryaṃ tenetyādikam uttaram atibhūrīty arthaḥ |

	deyaṃ mayeti vaktavye mayādeyam itīdṛśam |

	saṃdigdham uttaraṃ jñeyaṃ vyavahāre budhais tathā ||

māyādeyam ity atra tv akārapraśleṣasaṃbhavād adeyam ity apy avagamāt saṃdigdham evaṃvidham ity arthaḥ | asaṃbhava samābhir deyaṃ dhanam asmatprapautraputreṇa dattam ity evaṃvidham uttaram | avyaktam etad uttaram iti sukhenābhidhātum aśakyam | etau cottarābhāsau spaṣṭāv iti na tena vyākhyātau | anyārthaṃ vyācaṣṭe |

	balābalena caitena sāhasaṃ sthāpitaṃ purā |

	anuktam etan manyante tad anyārtham itīritam ||

arthino yad asadvṛttakathana eva paryavasitaṃ mithoviruddhapadavac ca tad anyārtham ity arthaḥ | atidoṣavad atyuktyā doṣavat, śataṃ deyam ity ukte dviśataṃ dattam ityādi | avyāpakādicatuṣṭayaṃ tenaiva vyākhyātam |

	asmai dattaṃ mayā sārdhaṃ sahasram iti bhāṣite |

	pratidattaṃ tadardhaṃ yat tad ihāvyāpakaṃ smṛtam ||

	pūrvavādi kriyāṃ yāvat samyaṅ naiva niveśayet |

	mayā gṛhītaṃ pūrvaṃ no tad vyastapadam ucyate ||

pūrvapakṣaniscayād arvāk dīyamānaṃ mithyāvādyuttaraṃ vyastapadam ity arthaḥ |

	tat kiṃ tāmarasaṃ kaścid agṛhītaṃ pradāsyati |

	nigūḍharthaṃ tu tat jñeyam uttaraṃ vyavahārataḥ ||

agṛhītaṃ padmam ato na pradadāmīty udāhṛtottarābhāsasyārthaḥ | sārvabhaumaprayogāsiddhatāmarasādipadavad vakroktyādimac cottaraṃ nigūḍhārthaṃ vijñeyam iti slokārthaḥ |

	kiṃ tenaiva sadādeyaṃ mayādeyaṃ bhaved iti |

	etad ākulam ity uktam uttaraṃ tadvido viduḥ ||

ananvitānekapadārthavad ākulam ity arthaḥ | vyākhyāgamyaṃ svato duravabodham | asāraṃ tenoktam | 

	kākasya dantā no santi santītyādi yad uttaram |

	asāram iti tattvena samyaṅ nottaram iṣyate ||

kākadantasamudbhavottaravan niṣprayojanam asāram ity arthaḥ | tathaikasyāṃ bhāṣāyāṃ satyamithyādyanekottaram anuttaram ity āha sa eva |

	pakṣaikadeśe yat satyam ekadeśe ca kāraṇam |

	mithyā caivaikadeśe ca saṃkarāt tad anuttaram ||

nanu sāṃkarye 'pi tena tenottareṇa tasya tasyāṃśasya nirasanadvārottarasamudāyasya kṛtsnapakṣavyāpakatvasaṃbhavāt katham anuttaratā | satyam, ata evānuttaratvasamarthanārtham uktaṃ tenaiva |

	na caikasmin vivāde tu kriyā syād vādinor dvayoḥ |

	na cārthasiddhir ubhayoḥ na caikatra kriyādvayam || iti |

ayam arthaḥ: kriyā likhitādipramāṇam, tat pratyavaskandane prāṅnyāye ca pratyarthina eva bhavati, mithyottare tv arthina eva | satye tu na kasyāpīti vakṣyate | evaṃ ca yatra satyetareṣāṃ trayāṇāṃ saṃkaraḥ tatra pratyarthinaḥ pramāṇadvayam arthinaś caikaṃ pramāṇaṃ prāpnoti | yatra satyamithyetarayor dvayos tatra pratharthina eva pramāṇadvayam | yatra punar mithākaraṇayor mithyāprāṅnyāyayor vā tatrārthipratyarthinor ekam ekaṃ pramāṇam | na ca yathā prāptaṃ tathaivāstv iti vācyam, pramāṇaṃ hi sādhyasiddhyarthaṃ kriyate, ekasmin vyavahāre caikam eva sādhyam ekasyaiva vādinaḥ, tena tatra nobhayoḥ pramāṇam, ekasya vā pramāṇadvayaṃ bhavitum arhati, ubhayos sādhyābhāvāt | ekasya sādhyasya caikena pramāṇena siddhāv anyasya vaiyyarthyāt | satyasya tv itaraiḥ saṅkare yady api nāyaṃ doṣaḥ, tathāpy ekasmin vyavahāre pādacatuṣṭaye tadardhe ca samāptir viddhruddheti tatrāpy anuttaratvam eva | tasmād yuktam uktam "saṃkarāt tad anuttaram" iti | evaṃ ca sarvatra vyavahāre pakṣavyāpy ekam evottaraṃ grāhyam | yatra punaḥ sarvathā tathāvidham uttaraṃ na labhyate, kiṃ tu ekaikāṃśavyāpakam anekam uttaraṃ tatrāgatyottaravaśena nānāpratijñāḥ pakṣadoṣaparihārāya kṛtvā krameṇaikaikapratijñāyā ekaikam uttataṃ grāhyam | anyathā tatra nirṇayābhāva eva syāt | ata evoktam "saṅkarāt tad anuttaram" iti | uktavidhayā saṅkare nirākṛte syād evottaram ity abhiprāyaḥ | ata eva cāsminn eva viṣaye hārītenottaragrahaṇe paurvāparyaṃ praśnapūrvakam uktam |

	mithyottaraṃ kāraṇaṃ ca syātām ekatra ced ubhe |

	satyaṃ vāpi sahānyena tatra grāhyaṃ kim uttaram ||

pūrvam iti śeṣaḥ | pūrvaṃ yad grāhyaṃ tad āha |

	yat prabhūtārthaviṣayaṃ yatra vā syāt kriyāphalam |

	uttaraṃ tatra taj jñeyam asaṅkīrṇam ato 'nyathā ||

ayam arthaḥ | satyetarottarānekatve bahvarthaviṣayam agre grāhyam | saha satyenānekatve bahvartham api satyaṃ vihāyottarāntaram evādāv upādeyam, satye kriyāphalābhāvād iti | na caivaṃ kramavācipadādhyāhārāpatter yatrottarakāle pakṣavyāpakānekottaropanyāsaḥ, yathā: kenacin mānavena madīyā gaur naṣṭā dṛṣṭāsya sadmanīty abhiyukto vakti mithyaitad asmadbhavana eva sā saṃbhūtety evamādi | tadviṣayam evedaṃ vacanam iti vācyam | yata uktam "asaṅkīrṇam ato 'nyathā" iti, tasyāyam arthaḥ: asaṃkīrṇam uttaram evaṃkrame bhavati, ato 'nyathā yaugapadye saṃkīrṇam eva syād iti | pakṣavyāpakānekottare tu vikalpaviṣaye na jātucit saṃkarāvasaraḥ | tasmāt saṃkarottaraviṣayam evedaṃ vacanam | ata eva pakṣavyāpakānekottaraviṣaye vacanāntaram ārabdhaṃ tenaiva |

	mithyākaraṇayor vāpi grāhyaṃ kāraṇam uttaram || iti |

kāraṇottarasya ananyathāsiddhatvādinā mithyāto gurutaratvād ity abhiprāyaḥ | ato mithyākāraṇayor udāharaṇamātratvād uttarāntarasaṃnipāte 'pi gurutaraṃ grāhyam ity ūhyam | yatra punaḥ saṃkarottare tulyabalatayā na pūrvoktakramahetur asti tatrāpy aicchikakrameṇottaraṃ grāhyaṃ nirṇayasyāvaśyakatvāt | evaṃ nirūpitam uttaraṃ prativādinā svayam eva deyam | tathā ca hārītaḥ |

	tatrābhiyogānugatam uttaraṃ prativādinā |

	niṣkṛṣṭārthaṃ pradeyaṃ syāt doṣasaṃjñāvivarjitam ||

yadā punaḥ svayam eva na dadāti uttaram, pradānakālaś cātikrāntaḥ tadāpy āha sa eva |

	pūrvapakṣe yathārthaṃ tu na dadyād uttaraṃ yadā |

	pratyarthī dāpanīyaḥ syāt sāmādibhir upakramaiḥ ||

dāpanīyo nṛpeṇeti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	yathārtham uttaraṃ dadyād adadad dāpayen nṛpaḥ |

	sāmabhedādibhir mārgair yāvat so 'rthaḥ samuddhṛtaḥ ||

sāmādayo hārītena darśitāḥ |

	priyapūrvaṃ vacaḥ sāma bhedas tu bhayadarśanam |

	arthāpakarṣaṇaṃ dānaṃ daṇḍas tāḍanabandhanam ||

tathā vasiṣṭhenāpi |

	kauṭilyaṃ sāmabhedau ca daṇḍaś ceti catuṣṭayam |

	māyopekṣendrajālāni saptopāyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ || iti |

etair apy upāyair asādhyaṃ pratyāha sa eva |

	upāyaiś codyamānas tu na dadyād uttaraṃ tu yaḥ |

	atikrānte saptarātre jito 'sau dātum arhati || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyām uttarapādaḥ **

**atha vivādaviṣayāṇi kānicid vacanāni likhyante** 

tatra yājñavlkyaḥ |

	abhiyogam anistīrya nainaṃ pratyabhiyojayet || iti |

anistīrya aparihṛtyety arthaḥ | atrāpavādam āha sa eva |

	kuryāt pratyabhiyogaṃ tu kalahe sāhaseu ca || iti |

pratyaparādhasaṃbhava iti śeṣaḥ | kalahe pāruṣyadvaya ity arthaḥ | abhoyoktāraṃ ca pratyāha sa eva |

	abhiyuktau na cānyane noktaṃ viprakṛtiṃ nayet || iti |

anyenārthinābhiyuktaṃ tadabhiyogaparihārād arvāg anyo 'rthī nābhiyuñjīta | tathābhiyoktum uktaṃ tyaktvānyathā na vaktavyam ity arthaḥ | yaḥ punar anyathā vakti so 'nyathāvāditvena hīno bhavati | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	anyavādī kriyādveṣī nopasthātā niruttaraḥ |

	āhūtavipalāyī ca hīnaḥ pañcavidhaḥ smṛtaḥ || iti |

tatrānyavāditayā hīnas tena nirūpitaḥ |

	pūrvavādaṃ parityajya yo 'nyam ālambate punaḥ |

	vādasaṃkramaṇāt jñeyo hīnavādī sa vai naraḥ ||

pūrvavāda āvedanam | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	śrāvayitvā yathākāryaṃ tyajed anyad vaded asau |

	anyapakṣāśrayas tena kṛto vādi sa hīyate ||

tathā param abhiyujya nāham abhiyunajmi hatyevaṃ (?) viruddhaṃ yo vadet so 'py anyavāditayā hīna ity āha sa eva |

	na mayābhihitaṃ kāryam abhiyujya paraṃ vadet |

	vibruvaṃś ca bhaved evaṃ hīnaṃ tam api nirdiśet ||

tathā ca patralikhitaṃ pūrvapakṣam anyathā kurvann apy anyathāvāditayā hīna ity āha sa eva |

	lekhayitvā tu yo vākyaṃ hīnaṃ vāpy adhikaṃ punaḥ |

	vaded vādī sa hīyeta nābhiyogaṃ tu so 'rhati ||

lekhayitvā patra iti śeṣaḥ, bhūmyādāv āvāpoddhārasya (?) tenaivoktatvāt | abhiyogaḥ pūrvapakṣaḥ taṃ kartuṃ nārhatīty ārthaḥ | etac cānarhatvam uttare nivṛtte sati vadato draṣṭavyam | anivṛtte tūttare hīnataiva, nānarhatvam, ottaranivṛtteḥ (?) pūrvapakaśodhanasya mohādāv agatyābhyanujñānāt | tathā kriyādveṣitayānupasthāyitayā ca hīnas tenaiva nirūpitaḥ |

	sabhyāś ca sākṣiṇaś caiva kriyā jñeyā manīṣibhiḥ |

	tāṃ kriyāṃ dveṣṭi yo mohāt kriyādveṣī sa ucyate ||

	āhvānād anupasthānāt sadya eva prahīyate || iti |

āhvānānantaram anāgamane tadānīm eva hīno bhavatīty arthaḥ | tathā niruttaratayā hīnaṃ nirūpayitum āha sa eva |

	brūhīty ukto 'pi na brūyāt sadyo bandhanam arhati |

	dvitīye 'hani durbuddher vidyāt tasya parājayam ||

parājayo hīnatā | ata eva hārītaḥ |

	sāpadesaṃ haret kālam abruvaṃś cāpi saṃsadi |

	uktvā vaco vibruvaṃś ca hīyamānasya lakṣaṇam ||

sāpadeśaṃ savyājam | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	vyājenaiva tu yatrāsau dīrghakālam abhīpsati |

	sāpadeśaṃ tu taṃ vidyād vādahanikaraṃ smṛtam || iti |

āhūtavipalāyī tu abhiyogaparihārārtham āhvānaṃ buddhvā pracchannacārī | eteṣāṃ tūttarottarasya hīnatā gurvīti jñāpayituṃ hīnaḥ pañcavidha ity uktam, na punaḥ pañcavidha eva hīna ity avadhārayitum, vidhāntarato 'pi hīnānāṃ smaraṇāt | hīnatāyā gurutvajñāpanaṃ tūttarottarasya daṇḍabhūyastvajñāpanārtham | uktaṃ ca tathā kātyāyanena |

	anyavādī paṇān pañca kriyādveṣī paṇān dasa |

	nopasthātā daśa dvau ca ṣoḍaśaiva niruttaraḥ ||

	āhūtavipalāyī ca paṇān grāhyas tu viṃśatim ||

atra tṛtīyapañcamayoḥ daṇḍaprāptau viśeṣam āha sa eva |

	trir āhūtam anāyāntam āhūtavipalāyinam |

	pañcarātram atikrāntaṃ vinayet taṃ mahīpatiḥ ||

tathā prakarāntareṇāpi hīnas tena darśitaḥ |

	śrāvitavyavahārāṇām ekaṃ yatra prabhedayet |

	vādinaṃ lobhayec caiva hīnaṃ tam iti nirdiśet ||

bṛhaspatināpi |

	bhayaṃ karoti bhedaṃ vā bhīṣaṇaṃ vā nirodhanam |

	etāni vādino 'rthasya vyavahāre sa hīyate ||

arthavyavahāre bhayādīni samastāny asamastāni vā yena vādinā kṛtāni sa hīyata ity arthaḥ | bhīṣaṇaṃ mukhāntareṇa bhītyutpādanam | manunāpi |

	adeśyaṃ yaś ca disati nirdiśyāpahnute ca yaḥ |

	yaś cādharottarān arthān vihīnān nāvabudhyate ||

	apadiśyāpadeśaṃ ca punar yas tv apadhāvati |

	samyak prāṇihitaṃ cārthaṃ pṛṣṭaḥ san nābhinandati ||

	santi jñātāra ity uktvā diśety ukto diśen na yaḥ |

	dharmasthaḥ kāraṇair etair hīno 'sāv iti nirdiśet || iti |

ayam arthaḥ | adeśyaṃ nirṇayasamayāsaṃbhavinaṃ sākṣiṇaṃ yo nirdiśati, saṃbavinaṃ vā nirdiśya yo 'pahnute na mayā nitdiṣṭa iti, yaś cātmano vacanagatakramavirodhaṃ na jājāti, yaḥ punar apadeśaṃ mama pīḍā vartata ityādivyājam apadiśya apasarati, samyak praṇihitaṃ suṣṭhūktam (?) artham anūdyātra kiṃ bravīṣīti pṛṣṭo yo na kiṃcid uttaraṃ prastauti, yas ca sākṣiṇaḥ santīty uktvā kathaya tān ity ukto 'pi na kathayati asau hīna iti dharmādhikaraṇasthaḥ pūrvoktakāraṇair nirdised iti | eteṣv api hīneṣu doṣānurūpo daṇḍo grāhyaḥ | tathā ca hīnādhikāre kātyāyanaḥ |

	doṣānurūpaṃ saṃgrāhyaḥ punar vādo na vidyate || iti |

prakṛtārthasiddhyartham iti śeṣaḥ | ayaṃ ca pratiṣedho manyukṛtavivāda eva, yata āha nāradaḥ |

	sarveṣv arthavivādeṣu vākchale nāvasīdati |

	paśustrībhūmyṛṇādāne śāsyo 'py arthān na hīyate ||

paśvādisarvārthavivādeṣu vākchale pramādābhidhāne kṛte 'pi nāvasīdati nātyantaṃ hīyate, yatas tatra daṇḍyasyāpi na prakṛtārthahānir ity arthaḥ | atrāpavādam āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	ubhayor likhite vākye prārabdhe kāryaniścaye |

	anuktaṃ tatra yo brūyāt tasmād arthāt sa hīyate ||

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	saṃdigdhārthaṃ svatantro yaḥ sādhayed yaś ca niṣpatet |

	na cāhūto vadet kiṃcid dhīno daṇḍyaś ca sa smṛtaḥ ||

svatantraḥ parīkṣakanirapekṣaḥ | niṣpatet deyam adatvā niṣpatya tiṣṭhet, palāyeta vā | daṇḍagrahaṇenaiva hīnatvasiddheḥ punar hīnagrahaṇaṃ prakṛtād arthād dhīna iti jñāpanārtham | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	anivedya tu yo rājñe saṃdigdhe 'rthe pravartate |

	prasahya sa vineyaḥ syāt sa cāpy artho na siddhyati || iti |

bṛhaspatir api |

	āhūtaprapalāyī ca maunī sākṣiparājitaḥ |

	svavākyapratipannaś ca hīnavādī caturvidhaḥ ||

svavākyapratipannaḥ svavācaiva saṃpratipannaḥ | atrāpi caturvidhagrahaṇam eteṣām uttarottarasyāciraṃ prakṛtād arthād dhīnatvaṃ bhavatīti jñāpayituṃ na punaḥ prakṛtād arthād dhīnaś caturvidha eveti niyantum, vidhāntarasyāpy uktatvāt | tatra kadā kasya hīnatvam ity apekṣite āha sa eva |

	prapalāyī tripakṣeṇa maunakṛt saptabhir dinaiḥ |

	sākṣibhinnas tatkṣaṇena pratipannaś ca hīyate ||

tathā nirdiṣṭān sākṣipuruṣān avādayato 'py evaṃvidhahīnatvaṃ cireṇa bahavtīty āha sa eva |

	sākṣiṇas tu samuddiśya yas tu tān na vivādayet |

	triṃśadrātrāt tripakṣād vā tasya hāniḥ prajāyate ||

na vādayet kāmata iti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	sākṣiṇo yas tu nirdiśya kāmato na vivādayet |

	sa vādī hīyate tasmāt triṃśadrātrāt pareṇa tu || iti |

akāmataś cen na hīyate | ata eva bṛhaspatiḥ |

	ācārakaraṇe divye kṛtvopasthānaniścayam |

	nopasthito yadā kaścic chalaṃ tatra na kārayet  ||

	daivarājakṛto doṣas tasmin kāle yadā bhavet |

	avadhityāgamātreṇa na bhavet sa parājitaḥ || iti |

"chalaṃ tatra na kārayet" iti vadan anyatrārthahānipratipādakavacanacchalanirasanenāpi (?) vyavahāranayanaṃ kāryam iti jñāpayati | evaṃ cārthavivādeṣu yatra nārthahānivacanaṃ tatraiva hīnasya vado grāhyo nānyatrety avagantavyam | ata eva kātyānayanaḥ |

	palāyanānuttartvād anyapakṣāśrayeṇa ca |

	hīnasya gṛhyate vādo na svavākyajitasya tu || iti |

palāyanādāv avadhibhūtakālātikramaṇenāgamanādikartur arthahānyabhāvād vādo grāhya ity arthaḥ | tatra yadi hīnenetarasya parājayaḥ tadā viśeṣas tenaiva darśitaḥ |

	yo hīnavākyena jitas tasyoddhāraṃ vidur budhāḥ |

	svavākyahīno yas tu syāt tasyoddhāro na vidyate || iti |

yājñavalkyas tu duṣṭavādiparijñānārtham āha |

	deśād deśāntaraṃ yāti sṛkviṇī parileḍhi ca |

	lalāṭaṃ svidyate cāsya mukhaṃ vaivaṛṇyam eti ca ||

	pariśuṣyatskhaladvākyo viruddhaṃ bahu bhāṣate |

	vākcakṣuḥ pūjayati no tathoṣṭhau nirbhujaty api ||

	svabhāvād vikṛtiṃ gacchen manovākkāyakarmabhiḥ |

	abhiyoge 'tha sākṣye ca duṣṭaḥ sa parikīrtitaḥ || iti |

sṛkviṇī oṣṭhaprāntau | nirbhujati kuṭilīkaroti | svabhāvād vikṛtiṃ gacchet svābhāvikadharmād vaiparītyam evaṃ gacched ity arthaḥ | manur api |

	ākārair iṅgitair gatyā ceṣṭayā bhāṣitena ca |

	netravaktravikāraiś ca gṛhyate 'ntargataṃ manaḥ || iti |

duṣṭasyeti śeṣaḥ | evaṃ duṣṭāntaḥkaraṇatayā jñātasyāpi na daṇḍo na prakṛārthād dhānir vā | tayor munibhir anabhidhānāt | aduṣṭasyāpi kathaṃcid evaṃvidhacihnānvayasaṃbhavāt | duṣṭābhidhāyakavacanānāṃ ca tadrakṣaṇādāv avadhānavidhānārthatvenāvaiyarthyāt | ye punar ekāntaparājayabhayād arvāk pramāṇakaraṇāt  svato 'pi vādato nivartante te daṇḍyā ity āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	pūrvottare saṃniviṣṭe vicāre saṃpravartate |

	praśamaṃ ye mitho yānti dāpyās te dviguṇaṃ damam || iti |

mitho yānti nṛpaṃ vañcayitveti śeṣaḥ | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	āvedya pragṛhītārthāḥ praśamaṃ yānti ye mithaḥ |

	sarve dviguṇadaṇḍyāḥ syuḥ vipralambhān nṛpasya te || iti |

evaṃ cāvañcanayā praśāntānāṃ na daṇḍaḥ | ata eva bṛhaspatiḥ |

	pūrvottare 'bhilikhite prakrānte kāryanirṇaye |

	dvayoḥ saṃtaptayoḥ saṃdhiḥ syād ayaḥkhaṇḍayor iva ||

	sākṣisabhyavikalpas tu bhavet tatrobhayor api |

	ḍolāyamāne yau saṃdhiṃ prakuryātāṃ vicakṣaṇau ||

	pramāṇasamato yatra bhedaḥ śāstracaritrayoḥ |

	tatra rājājñayā saṃdhir ubhayor api śasyate || iti |

ekasya vādinaḥ ekāntaparājayād arvāk yau saṃdhiṃ prakuryātāṃ tau vicakṣaṇāv ity arthaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ vivādaviṣayāṇi**

**atha pratyākalitapādaḥ**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	ye tu tiṣṭhanti karaṇe teṣāṃ sabhyair vibhāvanā |

	kathayitvottaraṃ samyag dātavyaikasya vādinaḥ ||

teṣāṃ dharmādhikaraṇasthānāṃ madhye ekasyārthinaḥ pratyarthino vā vibhāvanā kriyā sabhair nirdhārayitavyety arthaḥ | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	śodhite likhite samyag iti nirdoṣa uttare |

	pratyarthino 'rthino vāpi kriyākaraṇam iṣyate ||

arthinaḥ pratyarthino vā yasya sādhyam asti asau tatsādhyasiddhaye saduttarānantaram eva pramāṇalekhanaṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	tato 'rthī lekhayet sadyaḥ pratijñātārthasādhanam || iti |

uttarasiddhisamantaram eva sādhyavān vādī pramāṇam udbhāvayed ity arthaḥ | kiṃ tatpramāṇam ity apekṣite sa evāha |

	pramāṇaṃ likhitaṃ bhuktiḥ sākṣiṇaś ceti kīrtitam |

	eṣām anyatamābhāve divyānyatamam ucyate || 

divyaṃ dhaṭādiḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	kriyā tu dvividhā proktā mānuṣī daivikī tathā |

	mānuṣī lekhyasākṣibhyāṃ dhaṭādir daivikī smṛtā ||

lekhyasākṣibhyāṃ bhuktyā ca proktā mānuṣīty arthaḥ | bhukter api manuṣyasaṃbandhitvāt | ata eva bṛhaspatiḥ |

	sākṣilekhyānumānaṃ ca mānuṣī trividhā smṛtā | iti |

anumānaṃ bhuktiḥ, svatvānurūpakatvāt | dhaṭādir api tenaiva darśitaḥ |

	dhaṭo 'gnir udakaṃ caiva viṣaṃ kośas ca pañcamam |

	ṣaṣṭaṃ ca taṇḍulāḥ proktaṃ saptamaṃ taptamāṣakam ||

	aṣṭamaṃ phālam ity uktaṃ navamaṃ dharmajaṃ bhavet |

	divyāny etāni sarvāṇi nirdiṣṭāni svayaṃbhuvā || iti |

anyāni tu dviyāni nāradena nirdiṣṭāni |

	satyaṃ vāhanaśastrāṇi gobījakanakāni ca |

	devatāpitṛpādāś ca dattāni sukṛtāni ca || iti |

caśabdo 'nyeṣām api putraśiraḥsparśanādīnāṃ saṃgrahaṇārthaḥ | ete ca dhaṭādayaḥ satyādayaś ca divi devaiḥ kṛtatvād divyadaivikasaṃjñādvayaśālinaḥ | tathā ca pitāmahaḥ |

	yasmād devaiḥ prayuktāni puṣarārthe manīṣibhiḥ |

	prarasparaviśuddhyarthaṃ tasmād divyāni nāmataḥ ||

atropakramasāmarthyād daivikāni nāmata iti labhyate, devaiḥ prayuktānīti nimittadarsanāt | upasaṃhārasāmarthyād divi saṃbhavanimittānīti gamyate, divyāni nāmata ity uktatvāt | tena śrutyarthābhām anena vacanena dhaṭādīnām ājigamanād ājyam itivad yaugikaṃ nāmadvayam uktam | śapathanāma nāradenaiva teṣām eva darśitam |

	saptarṣayas tathendrādyāḥ puṣkarārthe tapodhanāḥ |

	śepuḥ śapatham avyagrāḥ parasparaviśuddhaye || iti |

vyāso 'pi |

	arthānurupāḥ śapathāḥ smṛtāḥ satyadhaṛādayaḥ | iti |

yat tu bṛhaspatinoktam,

	dhaṭādyā dharmajāntā ca daivī navavidhā smṛtā |

iti, tatra svayaṃbhuveti śeṣo draṣṭavyaḥ | nāradasmṛtasatyādibhiḥ saha daivyā vastuto bahuvidhatvāt | yā punar nāradīye divyaśapathayoḥ bhedenoktiḥ,

	yadā sākṣī na vidyeta vivādaṃ vadatāṃ nṛṇām |

	tadā divyaiḥ parīkṣeta śapathair vā pṛthagvidhaiḥ ||

iti, sā guruṣu divyaśabdo laghuṣu śapathaśabdaḥ prāyika iti darśayitum, na punas tayor arthabhedakathanāya, loke tayoḥ paryāyaśabdatvāt | sākṣī na vidyate iti likhitāditrayābhāvopalakṣaṇarthaḥ | yājñavalkyenāśeṣamānuṣābhāve divyasmaraṇāt | ata eva,

	saṃbhave sākṣiṇāṃ prājño daivikīṃ varjayet kriyām |

	saṃbhave tu prayuñjāno daivikīṃ hīyate tataḥ || 

iti kātyāyanavacane 'pi sākṣigrahaṇaṃ mānuṣopalakṣaṇārtham iti mantavyam | tathā,

	divākṛte kāryavidhau grāmeṣu nagareṣu ca |

	saṃbhave sākṣiṇāṃ caiva daivī na bhavati kriyā ||

 iti nāradavacane 'pi divākṛtādisaṃkīrtanaṃ mānuṣapramāṇasaṃbhave divyaniṣedhārtham avagantavyam | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	yady ekadeśavyāptāpi kriyā vidyeta mānuṣī |

	sā grāhyā na tu pūrṇāpi daivikī vadatāṃ nṛṇām ||

viśiṣṭasādhye viśeṣyāṃśe mānuṣasaṃbhave viśiṣṭārthasādhakam api na divyaṃ grāhyam ity arthaḥ | viśeṣaṇāṃśasiddhis tu vibhāvitaikadeśanyāyād alpaśapathena vā kāryety abhiprāyaḥ | na ca vācyaṃ ekadeśa ity aviśeṣavacanād viśeṣaṇāṃśe viśeṣyāṃśe vā mānuṣasaṃbhave divyaṃ niṣidhyata iti | yata āha sa eva |

	sārabhūtaṃ padaṃ muktvā asārāṇi bahūny api |

	saṃsādhayet kriyā yā tu tu tāṃ jahyāt sāravarjitām || iti |

tathā vivādinoḥ kathaṃcid daivamānuṣayor anyatarat pramāṇam anyatareṇa vādinā kṛtaṃ nirṇāyakam ity aṅgīkāre 'pi mānuṣasaṃbhave tad eva nirṇāyakaṃ na daivikam ity āha sa eva |

	yady eko mānuṣīṃ brūyād anyo brūyāt tu daivikīm |

	mānuṣīṃ tatra gṛhṇīyān na tu daivīṃ riyāṃ nṛpaḥ || iti |

evaṃ ca sarvathā mānuṣāsaṃbhave divyam ity utsargaḥ | kvacid asyāpavādam āha sa eva |

	prakrānte sāhase vāde pāruṣye daṇḍavācike |

	balodbhaveṣu kāryeṣu sākṣiṇo divyam eva vā ||

ayaṃ ca vikalpo gūḍhasāhasiketaraviṣayaḥ | tatra mānuṣāsaṃbhavena vikalpāsaṃbhavāt | at evoktaṃ tenaiva |

	gūḍhasāhāsikānāṃ tu prāptaṃ divyaiḥ parīkṣaṇam |

	yukticihneṅgitākāravākcakṣuśceṣṭitair nṛṇām ||

gūḍhasāhāsikānāṃ musvaveṣṭanādivaśād (?) alakṣyamūrtīnām ity arthaḥ | yukticihnāder apy abhāve teṣāṃ divyam, na punaḥ sākṣyādyabhāvamātra iti darśayituṃ punar vacanārambhaḥ | tathottamasāhasikānāṃ prakaṭānām api divyenaiva parīkṣaṇam ity āha sa eva |

	uttameṣu ca sarveṣu sāhaseṣu vicārayet |

	sadbhāvaṃ divyadṛṣṭtena satsy sākṣiṣu vai bhṛguḥ ||

ṛṇavivādeṣu tu viśeṣam āha nāradaḥ |

	pramādād dhanino yatra na lekhyaṃ na ca sākṣiṇaḥ |

	arthaṃ cāpahṇute vādī tasyoktaḥ trividho vidhiḥ ||

vādī gṛhītadhanaḥ | vidhiḥ danasādhanopāyaḥ | so 'pi tenaiva darśitaḥ |

	codanā pratikālaṃ ca yuktiseśas tathaiva ca |

	tṛtīyaḥ śapathaḥ proktaḥ tai ṛṇaṃ sadhayet kramāt | \
pratikālaṃ codanā pratyarpaṇakālo yadā yadā prāptas tadā tadā madīyaṃ dīyatām iti triścatuḥpañcakṛtvo vā madhyasthajanasamakṣam anyenāpratihatā pratidānapreraṇā, sā prathama upāyaḥ | tadasaṃbhave yuktileśaḥ amuṣmin deśe amuṣmin kāle 'munārthasaṃbandhena iyatparimāṇam etatkarmārtham ṛṇaṃ gṛhītam tvayā ityādi dvitīyopāyaḥ | tasyāpy asaṃbhave tṛtīyopāyaḥ śapatha ityarthaḥ | ayaṃ cārthaḥ tenaiva darśitaḥ |

	abhīkṣṇaṃ codyamāno 'pi pratihanyān na tadvacaḥ |

	triścatuḥpañcakṛtvo vā parat(?) 'rthaṃ samācaret ||

	codanāpratidhāte tu yuktileśaiḥ samanvitāt |

	desakālarthasaṃbandhaparimāṇakriyādibhiḥ ||

	yuktiṣv apy asamarthāsu śapathair eva nirṇayet |

	arthakālabalāpakṣair agryambusukṛtādibhiḥ ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	ṛṇe lekhyaṃ sākṣiṇo vā yuktileśādayo 'pi vā |

	daivikī vā kriyā proktā prajānāṃ hitakāmyayā ||

tathā vivādamātraṃ pratyāha sa eva |

	pramāṇair hetunā vāpi divyenaiva tu niścayam |

	sarveṣv eva vivādeṣu sadā kuryān narādhipaḥ ||

	sarvābhāve tu yatnena nānyathaiva kadācana || iti

pramāṇasabdahetuśabdayor artham āha vyāsaḥ |

	likhitaṃ sākṣiṇo bhuktiḥ pramāṇaṃ trividhaṃ smṛtam |

	anumānaṃ vidur hetus tarkaś ceti manīṣiṇaḥ || iti |

evaṃ ca dṛṣṭapramāṇenāsiddhāv adṛṣṭaṃ pramāṇam āśrayaṇīyaṃ nānyatheti tātparyarthaḥ | kvacit dṛṣṭenāsiddhāv apy adṛṣṭaṃ nāśraṇīyam ity āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	prathame vā tṛtīye vā pramāṇaṃ daivamānuṣam |

	uttare syāc caturthe tu sasākṣijayapatrakam ||

prāṅnyāyottare sākṣijayapatryor anyatareṇāsādhayan vādī na prāg vijayīty abhiprāyaḥ | anenaivābhiprāyeṇa vyāso 'pi |

	prāṅnyāye jayapatreṇa prāḍvivākādibhis tathā |

	satyaṃ vādī samāpnoti yad yat tena niveditam ||

vādī pratyarthī, tasyaiva tatra sādhyavāditvāt | ata eva bṛhaspatiḥ |

	prāṅnyāye pratyavaskande pratyarthī sādhayet svayam |

	uttarārthaṃ pratijñārtham arthī mithyottare punaḥ ||

mithyottare 'bhyupagamābhāvena bhāṣārthasya sādhyatāhānāt pratijñātārtham arthyeva sādhayed ity arthaḥ | kāraṇottare tu bhāṣārthasyābhyupagamād eva sādhyatvāhānān na pratijñāvādinaḥ pratijñātārthasādhanam, kiṃ tūttarārthe arthinā yad anabhyupagataṃ kāraṇaṃ tad eva pratyarthinā pramāṇena sādhyam | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	prapadya kāraṇaṃ pūrvam anyad gurutaraṃ yadi |

	prativākyagataṃ brūyāt sādhyate yad dhi netarat ||

pūrvaṃ pratijñāvādinoktaṃ prapadya aṅgīkṛtya anyad gurutaram aṅgīkṛtapratijñātārthopamardanakṣamaṃ kāraṇaṃ pratyarpaṇādikaṃ prativākyagatam uttaravākyasthaṃ yadi pratyarthī brūyāt tadā tad eva kila tena sādhyate, arthinānaṅgīkṛtatvāt | netarat pratyarthināṅgīkṛtaṃ pratijñātārthajātam arthinā sādhyata ity arthaḥ | prapadyety upalakṣaṇārtham, tena prapratijñāvādinoktaṃ (?) mithyety uktvā kāraṇābhidhāne 'pi kāraṇam eva sādhyate,

	mithyākāraṇayor vāpi grāhyaṃ kāraṇam uttaram |

iti hārītasmaraṇāt | tathā satyottare na kasyāpi vādinaḥ kriyety āha sa eva |

	prāṅnyāyakāraṇoktau tu pratyarthī nirdiśet kriyām |

	mithyoktau pūrvavādi tu pratipattau na sā bhavet ||

bhāṣāyām uttare ca sādhyārthābhāvād ity abhiprāyaḥ | ataḥ saṃpratipattau dvipāttvavyavahāraḥ | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	mithyoktau sa catuṣpāt syāt pratyavaskandane tathā |

	prāṅnyāye ca sa vijñeyo dvipāt saṃpratipattiṣu ||

tena saṃpratipattau kriyānirdeśādyabhāvād uttarānta eva vyavahāraḥ samāpyate | evaṃ ca mithyākāraṇayor mānuṣī daivikī kriyā, prāṅnyāye tu mānuṣy eva satye na kācid ity anusaṃdheyam | mithyākāraṇayor api kvacin na daivikīty āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	vākpāruṣye mahīvāde niṣiddhā daivikī kriyā || iti |

tena tāṃ tatra na kalpayed ity abhiprāyaḥ | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	vākpāruṣye ca bhūmau ca divyaṃ na oarikalpayet |}| iti |

nanv anenaiva vākpāruṣye divyam uktam "prakrānte" ityadinā | satym uktaṃ tat tu mahāpāruṣyaviṣayam, idaṃ tv alpapāruṣyaviṣayam iti na kiṃcid viruddham | bhūmāv iti sthāvaropalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva pitāmaḥaḥ |

	sthāvareṣu vivādeṣu divyāni parivarjayet |

	sākṣibhir likhitenātha bhuktyā caitān prasādhayet ||

atra mānuṣāsaṃbhave hetunā nirṇayaḥ, tadasaṃbhave rājājñayeti mantavyam | tathā kvacid divyaniyamārtham āha sa eva |

	mahāśāpābhiśāpeṣu nikṣepaharaṇe tathā |

	divyaiḥ kāryaṃ parīkṣeta rājā satsv api sākṣiṣu ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	samatvaṃ sākṣiṇāṃ yatra divyais tatrāpi śodhayet |

	prāṇāntikavivāde vā vidyamāneṣu sākṣiṣu ||

	divyam ālambate vādī na pṛcchet tatra sākṣiṇam || iti |

bṛhaspatir api |

	likhite sākṣivāde ca saṃdeho jāyate yadā |

	anumāne ca saṃbhrānte tatra daivaṃ viśodhanam ||

anumānaṃ bhuktiḥ ulkāhastatvādiyuktiś ca | vyāso 'pi |

	mayaitan na kṛtaṃ lekhyaṃ kūṭam anyena karitam |

	adharīkṛtya tatpatram arthe divyena nirṇayaḥ ||

nirṇetavye 'rthe nirṇayaṃ divyena kuryād ity arthaḥ | kātyāyano 'pi |

	yatra syāt sopadhaṃ lekhyaṃ tad rājñaś śrāvitaṃ yadi |

	divyena śodhayet tatra rājā dharmāsanasthitaḥ ||

tathā kvacil lekhyasya kvacid bhukteḥ kvacit sākṣiṇaś ca sati saṃbhave niyamārtham āha sa eva |

	pūgaśreṇīgaṇādīnāṃ yā sthitiḥ parikīrtitā |

	tasyās tu sādhanaṃ lekhyaṃ na divyaṃ na ca sākṣiṇaḥ ||

	dvāramārgakriyābhogajalavāhādike tathā |

	bhuktir eva hi gurvī syāt na lekhyaṃ na ca sākṣiṇaḥ ||

	dattādatte 'tha bhṛtyānāṃ svāminā nirṇaye sati |

	vikrayādānasaṃbandhe krītvā dhanam ayacchati (?) ||

	dyūte samāhvaye caiva vivāde samupasthite |

	sākṣiṇaḥ sādhanaṃ proktaṃ na divyaṃ na ca lekyakam || iti |

evam uktvā pramāṇasya vyavasthā parīkṣakaiḥ paripālanīyety āha nāradaḥ |

	pramāṇāni pramāṇajñaiḥ paripālyāni yatnataḥ |

	sīdanti hi pramāṇāni paramāṇair avyavasthitaiḥ ||

avyavasthitaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ pramāṇakartāro yato vinaśyanti ataḥ kasyātra kiṃpramāṇaṃ lekhyam iti pratyākalanakuśalaiḥ pratyakalayitavyam ity arthaḥ | atra kaiścit paṇḍitaṃmanyaiḥ na sthāvareṣu likhitādikathanaṃ pramāṇaniyamāya, kiṃ tu prāyikatvapradarśanārtham, anyathā kathaṃcil lekhyādināśe nirṇayābhāvaḥ syād ity uktam, tad ayuktam, niyamārthatve 'pi yuktibhiḥ pārthivavacanād vā nirṇayasaṃbhavāt | ata eva pitāmaḥaḥ |

	lekhyaṃ yatra na vidyeta na bhuktir na ca sākṣiṇaḥ |

	na ca divyāvatāro 'sti pramāṇaṃ tatra pārthivaḥ ||

	niścetuṃ ye na śakyāḥ syur vādāḥ saṃdigdharūpiṇaḥ |

	teṣāṃ nṛpaḥ pramāṇaṃ syāt sa sarvasya prabhur yataḥ || iti |

ata eva dṛṣṛādṛṣṭapramāṇam uktvā uktaṃ vyāsena |

	eṣām abhāve rājājñā nirṇayaṃ tu vidur budhāḥ | iti |

pramāṇānāṃ svarūpato niṣadhavaśād vā asaṃbhave nirṇayo rājājñayā bhavatīty arthaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ pratyākalitapādaḥ **

**atha kriyāpādaḥ** 

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	śrutvā pūrvottaraṃ sabhyaiḥ nirdiṣṭā yasya bhāvanā |

	vibhāvayet pratijñātaṃ so 'khilaṃ likhitādinā ||

bhāvanā kriyā | nārado 'pi |

	pūrvavāde 'bhilikhite yathākṣaram aśeṣataḥ |

	arthī tṛtīyapāde tu kriyayā pratipādayet ||

pūrvavādo bhāṣā | abhilikhitaṃ pūrvapakṣābhibhāvakatayā likhitam uttaram iti yāvat | tṛtīyapādaḥ pratyākalitākhyaḥ | tasmin sati kriyā pramāṇam | evaṃ cāyam arthaḥ | tasmin sati kriyā pramāṇam | evaṃ cāyam arthaḥ: bhāṣottarapratyākalitākhyapādatraye sati kriyayā pratipādayet svakāryam arthī pramāṇena sādhayed iti | kāryakriyāśabdayor artham āha vyāsaḥ |

	kāryaṃ hi sādyam ity uktaṃ sādhanaṃ hi kriyocyate |

	dvibhedā sā punar jñeyā mānuṣī daivikī tathā ||

sādhanaṃ pramāṇam | bṛhaspatir api kriyābhedam āha |

	dviprakārā kriyā proktā mānuṣī daivikī tathā |

	ekeikānekadhā bhinnā munibhis tattvavedibhiḥ ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	pañcaprakāraṃ daivaṃ syān mānuṣaṃ trividhaṃ smṛtam || iti |

pañcaprakāram iti nāvadhāraṇārtham | taṇḍulataptamāṣādividhāntarasyāpi daivikasya smṛtyantare darśanāt | trividham iti niyamārtham eva, smṛtyuttarāvisaṃvādāt | ata evātra trividhaṃ smṛtam ity arthaḥ | yat punar nāradenoktam,

	likhitaṃ sākṣiṇaś cātra dvau vidhī parikīrtitau |

iti, na tat saṃkhyāniyamārtham | tathātve,

	likhitaṃ sākṣiṇo bhuktiḥ pramāṇaṃ trividhaṃ smṛtam |

iti svavacanena virodhāpattiḥ syād ato bhuktito bahuviṣayatvam itarayor iti vaktum "dvau vidhī parikīrtitau" ityuktam ity avagantavyam |tatra vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	laukikaṃ rājakīyaṃ ca lekhyaṃ vidyāt dvilakṣaṇam | iti |

laukikaṃ jānapadam | tathā ca saṃgrahakāraḥ |

	rājakīyaṃ jānapadaṃ dvividhaṃ likhitaṃ smṛtam | iti |

tatra rājakīyaṃ śāsanādibhedena caturvidhm ity āha vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	śāsanaṃ prathamaṃ jñeyaṃ jayapatraṃ tathāparam |

	ājñāprajñāpanāpatraṃ rājakīyaṃ caturvidham ||

tatra śāsanaṃ nirūpayitum āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	datvā bhūmiṃ nibandhaṃ vā kṛtvā lekhyaṃ tu kārayet |

	āgāmibhadranṛpatiparijñānāya pārthivaḥ ||

nibandhaḥ vāṇijyādikāribhiḥ prativarṣaṃ pratimāsaṃ vā kiṃcid dhanam asmai brāhmaṇāyāsyai devatāyai vā deyam ityādiprabhusamayasalbhyo 'rthaḥ | atra yady api dhanadātṛtvaṃ vāṇijyādikartuḥ, tathāpi nibandhakartur eva puṇyam, taduddeśenaivetarasya pravṛtteḥ | bhūmim iti prāmārāmādīnām upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva bṛhaspatiḥ |

	datvā bhūmyādikaṃ rājā tāmrapaṭṭe tathā paṭe |

	śāsanaṃ kārayed dharmyaṃ sthānavaṃśādisaṃyutam ||

kārayet saṃdhivigrahādyadhikāriṇeti śeṣaḥ | tasyaivātra lekhane kartṛtvaniyamāt | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

	rājñā tu svayam ādiṣṭaḥ saṃdhivigrahalekhakaḥ |

	tāmrapaṭṭe paṭe vāpi vilikhed rājaśāsanam ||

	kriyākārakasaṃbandhaṃ samāsārthakriyānvitam || iti |

kriyākārakayoḥ saṃbandho yasmin śāsane tat tathoktam | samāsārthakriyānvitaṃ saṃkṣiptārthopanyāsakriyayā samanvitam ity arthaḥ | tāmrapaṭṭādau lekhanīyam artham āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	abhilekhyātmano vaṃśyān ātmānaṃ ca mahīpatiḥ |

	pratigrahaparīmāṇadānacchedopavarṇanam || iti |

uddhṛtamahīmaṇḍalasya śrīpater varāhavapuṣaḥ varadānapratipādakam āśīrvādam ādāv ācāraprāptam abhilekhyānantaram ātmano vaṃśyān prapitāmahapitāmahapitrākhyān trīn uktakrameṇa śauryādiguṇavarṇanadvārātmānaṃ caturtham abhilekhya pratigrahaparimāṇādikaṃ lekhayed ity arthaḥ | pratigṛhyata iti pratigraho bhūmyādiḥ nibandhaś ca | tasya parimāṇam iyattā | dānacchedo dīyamānabhūmyāder maryādā | vyāso 'pi |

	samāmāstadardhāharnṛpanāmopalakṣitam |

	pratigrahītṛjātyādisagotrabrahmacārikam || iti |

saṃpradānasyāsādhāraṇatvāvabodhakaṃ jātikulaśākhādikam iti lekhanīyam ity uttarārdhasyārthaḥ | tathānyad api lekhanīyaṃ sa evāha |

	sthānaṃ vaṃśānupūrvyaṃ ca deśaṃ grāmam upāgatam |

	brāhmaṇasya tathā cānyān mānyān ashikṛtān likhet ||

	kuṭumbino 'tha kāryasthadūtavaidyamahattarān |

	mlecchacaṇḍālaparyantān sarvān saṃbodhaynn iti ||

	mātāpitror ātmanaś ca puṇyāyāmukasūnave |

	dattaṃ mayāmukāyātha dānaṃ sabrahmacāriṇe || iti |

bṛhaspatir api |

	anācchedyam anāhāryaṃ sarvabhāvyavivarjitam |

	candrārkasamakālīnaṃ putrapautrānvayānugam ||

	dātuḥ pālayituḥ svargaṃ hartur narakam eva ca |

	ṣaṣṭiḥ varṣasahasrāṇi dānacchedaphalaṃ likhet || iti |

āgāminṛpādibodhanārtham iti śeṣaḥ | ata eva vyāsaḥ |

	ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahasrāṇi dānacchedaphalaṃ tathā |

	āgāminṛpasāmantabodhanārthaṃ nṛpo likhet ||

tathā ślokāntaram api lekhanīyaṃ tenaiva paṭhitam |

	sāmānyo 'yaṃ dharmasetur nṛpāṇāṃ kāle kāle pālanīyo bhavadbhiḥ |

	sarvān etān bhāvinaḥ pārthivendrān bhūyo bhūyo yācate rāmabhadraḥ || iti |

tato rājā svayaṃ svahastaṃ likhet | tathā ca sa eva |

	samniveśaṃ pramāṇaṃ ca svahastaṃ ca likhet svayam | iti |

mataṃ me 'mukaputrasya amukasya mahīpater yad atropari likhitam iti svayam likhed ity arthaḥ | lekhakaś ca svanāma likhet tathā ca sa eva |

	saṃdhivigrahakārī ca bhaved yaś cāpi lekhakaḥ |

	svayaṃ rājñā samādiṣṭaḥ sa likhed rājaśāsanam ||

	svanāma tu likhet paścāt mudritaṃ rājamudrayā |

	grāmakṣetragṛhādīnām īdṛk syād rājaśāsanam || iti |

etac ca pratigrahītur arpaṇīyam, tasyopayogitvāt | ata eva viṣṇuḥ: "paṭe vā tāmrapṭṭe vā likhitaṃ samudrāṅkaṃ cāgāminṭpatiparijñānārthaṃ dadyāt" iti | saṃgrahakāro 'pi |

	rājasvahastacihnena rājādeśena saṃyutam |

	yuktaṃ rājābhidhānena mudritaṃ rājamudrayā ||

	svalipyanapaśabdoktisaṃpūrṇāvayavākṣaram |

	śāsanaṃ rājadattaṃ syāt saṃdhivigrahalekhakaiḥ || iti |

saṃdhivigrahalekhakaiḥ likhitam uktavidham anyasmai rājñā dattaṃ śāsanākhyaṃ syād ity arthaḥ | etac ca śāsanaṃ na dānasiddhyartham, tasya pratigraheṇaiva siddheḥ, kiṃ tu dattasya sthairyakaraṇārtham, sthiratve akṣayaphalaśruteḥ | tathā hi |

	ruṇaddhi rodasī cāsya yāvat kīrtis tarasvinī |

	tāvat kilāyamadhyās te sukṛtī vaibudhaṃ padam ||

anenaivābhiprāyeṇa yājñavalkyenāpy uktam |

	svahastakālasaṃpannaṃ śāsanaṃ kāreyet sthiram || iti |

kālasaṃpannaṃ vatsarādiviśeṣitadānādinopetam | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

	jñātaṃ mayeti likhitaṃ dātrādhyakṣākṣarair yutam |

	abdamāsatadardhāhorājamudrāṅkitaṃ tathā ||

	anena vidhinā lekhyaṃ rājaśāsanakṃ likhet || iti |

tathā ca sa eva jayapatraṃ nirūpayitum āha |

	vyavahārān svayaṃ dṛṣṭvā śrutvā vā prāḍvivākataḥ |

	jayapatraṃ tato dadyāt parijñānāya pārthivaḥ ||

kasmai dadyād ity apekṣite sa evāha |

	jaṅgamaṃ sthāvaraṃ yena pramāṇenātmasātkṛtam |

	bhāgābhiśāpasaṃdigdho yaḥ samyag vijayī bhavet ||

	tasmai rājñā pradātavyaṃ jayapatraṃ suniścitam ||

bṛhaspatir api |

	pūrvottarakriyāyuktaṃ nirṇayāntaṃ yadā nṛpaḥ |

	pradadyāj jayine lekhyaṃ jayapatraṃ tad ucyate ||

pūrvottarakriyāyuktam iti vṛttāntopalakṣaṇārtham | yata āha sa eva |

	yad vṛttaṃ vyavahāre tu pūrvapakṣottarādikam |

	kriyāvadhāraṇopetaṃ jayapatre 'khilaṃ likhet ||

vyāso 'pi |

	pūrvottarakriyāpādaṃ pramāṇaṃ tat parīkṣaṇam |

	nigadaṃ smṛtivākyaṃ ca yathāsabhyaṃ viniścitam ||

	etat sarvaṃ samāsena jayapatre vilekhayet || iti |

kriyāpādaṃ kriyābhimarśanapādaṃ pratyākalitapādam iti yāvat | nigadaṃ sākṣivacanam | yathāsabhyaṃ sabhyānatikrameṇa | samāsena saṃkṣepeṇa | kātyāyano 'pi |

	arthipratyarthivākyāni pratijñā sākṣivāk tathā |

	niryayaś ca yathā tasya yathā cāvadhṛtaṃ svayam ||

	etad yathākṣaraṃ lekhye yathāpūrvaṃ viśeśayet || iti |

yathāpūrvam ity etat tenaiva prapañcitam |

	abhiyoktrabhyuktānāṃ vacanaṃ prāṅ niveśayet |

	sabhyānāṃ prāḍvivākasya kulānāṃ vā tataḥ param ||

	niścayaṃ smṛtiśāstrasya mataṃ tatraiva lekhayet || iti |

mataṃ nṛpādīnām iti śeṣaḥ | matalekhanaṃ tu svahastena, parahastato matalekhanasya "yathā cāvadhṛtaṃ svayam" ity anenaiva pūrvam eva vihitatvāt | ata evoktaṃ tenaiva |

	siddhenārthena saṃyojyo vādī satkārapūrvakam |

	lekhyaṃ svahastasaṃyuktaṃ tasmai dadyāt tu pārthivaḥ ||

	sabhāsadaś ca ye tatra smṛtiśāstravidaḥ sthitāḥ |

	yathā lekhyavidhau tadvat svahastaṃ tatra dāpayet || iti |

rājā tān sabhyān jānapadalekhyavaj jayapatre svahastaṃ dāpayed ity arthaḥ | vṛddhavasiṣṭho 'pi |

	prāḍvivākādihastāṅkaṃ mudritaṃ rājamudrayā |

	siddhe 'rthe vādino dadyāj jayine jayapatrakam ||

evam uktaṃ jayapatraṃ paścātkārākhyam ity āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	anena vidhinā lekhyaṃ paścātkāraṃ vidur budhāḥ | iti |

ayaṃ ca paścātkāro nirṇayaviśeṣa eva na sarvatrety āha sa eva |

	nirastā tu kriyā yatra pramāṇenaiva vādinā |

	paścātkāro bhavet tatra na sarvāsu vidhīyate ||

kriyā sādhyam | prmāṇenaiveti vadaṃś catuṣpād vyavahāra eva paścātkāro na dvipād vyavahār iti kathayati | spaṣṭīkṛtaṃ caitat bṛhaspatinā |

	sādhayet sādhyam arthaṃ tu catuṣpādanvitaṃ jaye |

	rājamudrānvitaṃ caiva jayapatrakam iṣyate || iti |

dvipādvyavahāre tu bhāṣottarānvitaṃ jayapatram asty eva, paścātkārasyaiva tatrāsadanuvādakatvena pratiṣedhāt | anyad api jayapatraṃ tenaivoktam |

	anyavādyādihīnebhya itareṣāṃ pradīyate |

	vṛttānuvādasaṃsiddhaṃ tac ca syāj jayapatrakam ||

itareṣāṃ hīnavādinām ity arthaḥ | ājñāprajñāpanāpatre dve vasiṣṭhena darśite |

	sāmanteṣv atha bhṛtyeṣu rāṣṭrapālādikeṣu vā |

	kāryam ādiśyate yena tad ājñāpatram ucyate ||

	ṛtvikpurohitācāryamānyeṣv abhyarhiteṣu tu |

	kāryaṃ nivedyate yena patraṃ prajñāpanāya tat || iti |

bṛhaspatir anyad api rājakīyaṃ prasādalekhyākhyaṃ patram āha |

	deśādikaṃ yasya rājā likhitena prayacchati |

	sevāśauryādinā tuṣṭaḥ prasādalikhitaṃ hi tat || iti |

ato rājakīyaṃ pañcavidhaṃ caturvidham ity anāsthayoktam iti mantavyam | jānapadaṃ punar vyāsena nirūpitam |

	likhej jānapadaṃ lekhyaṃ prasiddhasthānalekhakaḥ |

	rājasaṃśakramayutaṃ varṣamāsārdhavāsaraiḥ ||

yutam ity anuṣajyate | vāsaraḥ dinam | anyad api lekhayitavyam ity āha sa eva |

	pitṛpūrvye nāmajātī dhanikarṇikayor likhet |

	dravyabhedapramāṇaṃ ca vṛddhiṃ cobhayasaṃmatām ||

ubhayasaṃmatiḥ dravyāder api viśeṣaṇam | ata eva yājñavalkyaḥ |

	yaḥ kaścid artho niṣṇātaḥ svarucyā tu parasparam |

	lekhyaṃ tu sākṣimat kāryaṃ tasmin dhanikapūrvakam ||

sākṣimat niṣṇātārthajñātṛbhūtamadhasthajananāmānvitam | tathā kāladhanikaṛṇikasākṣyādilekhanīyasya yāvatā viśeṣaṇena viśeṣaniṣṭhatvasiddhiḥ tāvadviśeṣaṇānvitaṃ kāryam ity āha sa eva |

	samāmāsatadardhānarnāmajātisvagotrakaiḥ |

	sabrahmacārikātmīyapitṛnāmādicihnitam ||

sabrahmacārikaṃ bahvṛcaḥ kaṭhaḥ ityādiśākhāprayuktaṃ guṇnāma, asmīyapitṛnāma, dhanikaṛṇikasākṣiṇāṃ pitṛnāma | ādiśabdena deśācārāvāptavārādi gṛhyate | ata eva vyāsaḥ |

	deśasthityā kriyādhānapratigrāhavicihnitam |

deśasthityā kriyā deśācārānusāreṇa karaṇam | ādhānam ādhiḥ | nārado 'pi |

	lekhyaṃtu sākṣimat kāryam aviluptakramākṣaram |

	deśācārasthitiyutaṃ samagraṃ sarvavastuṣu ||

vasiṣṭho 'pi |

	kālaṃ niveśya rājānaṃ sthānaṃ nivasitaṃ tathā |

	dāyakaṃ grāhakaṃ caiva pitṛnāmnā ca saṃ yutam ||

	jātiṃ svagotraṃ śākhāṃ ca dravyam ādhiṃ sasaṃkhyakam |

	vṛddhiṃ grāhakahastaṃ ca viditārthau ca sākṣiṇau || iti |

grāhakahastaniveśanaprakāram āha sa eva yājñavalkyaḥ |

	samāpte 'rthe ṛṇī nāma svahastena niveśayet |

	mataṃ me 'mukaputrasya yad atropari lekhitam ||

uparīti vadan pūrvalikhitākṣarasaṃsthānād adhastāt svahastākṣarasaṃsthānam iti darśayati | ṛṇīti sākṣiṇām api pradarśanārtham | tathā ca sa eva |

	sākṣiṇaṃ ca svahastena pitṛnāmakapūrvakam |

	atrāham amukaḥ sākṣī likheyur iti te samāḥ ||

yatra lekhye vilikhitāḥ sākṣiṇas te 'py amukaputro 'mukho 'trārthe sākṣīti pratyekaṃ likheyuḥ | te ca dvitvādisamasaṃkhyayā viśiṣṭā bhaveyuḥ | na tritvādiviṣamasaṃkhyayety arthaḥ | kenacid akārapraśleṣakalpanayā sākṣisaṃkhyāniyamo vaiparītyena varṇitaḥ | sa yasmin deśe tathaivācāraḥ tatraiv grāhyaḥ nānyatra svarasārthatvāt | sākṣiṇa iti bahuvacanaṃ gurutarakāryalekhyaviṣayam |

	uttamarṇādhamarṇau ca sākṣiṇau lekhakas tathā |

	samavāyena caikeṣāṃ lekhyaṃ kurvīta nānyathā ||

iti hārītena lekhyamātre sākṣiṇāv ity uktatvāt | evaṃ cānyakṛtalekhyasyottamarṇādhamarṇasākṣidvayalekhakarūpapañcapuruṣārūḍhatvāt pañcārūḍhaṃ patram iti loke vyavahāraḥ | sākṣisaṃkhyādhikatve tv ayaṃ vyavahāro gauṇa iti mantavyam | lekhyamātraṃ prakṛtya vyāsenāpy uktam |

	ṛṇihastaṃ nāmayutaṃ sākṣibhyāṃ pitṛpūrvakam | iti |

ato dviprabhṛtibhiḥ samair bhavitavyam iti niyamo deśācārāvirodhenānusaṃdheyaḥ | yadā tu lipyanabhijñaḥ sākṣī ṛṇī vā tadā nārada āha |

	alipijño ṛṇī yaḥ syāḷ lekhayet svamataṃ saḥ |

	sākṣī vā sākṣiṇānyena sarvasākṣisamīpataḥ ||

vijātīyalipijño 'pi svayam eva likhet lipijñatvāt,

	sarve jānapadān varṇān lekhye tu viniveśayet |

iti kātyāyanasmaraṇāc ca | sākṣisvahastalekhanānantaraṃ yājñavalkyaḥ |

	ubhayābhyarthite caitan mayā hy amukasūnunā |

	likhitaṃ hy amukeneti lekhako 'nte tato likhet ||

vyāso 'pi |

	mayobhayābhyarthitenāmukenānukasūnunā|

	svahastayuktaṃ svaṃ nāma lekhakas tv antato likhet ||

	evaṃ jānapade lekhye vyāsenābhihito vidhiḥ || iti |

ananto lekhyasyeti śeṣaḥ | evam uktalekhyam aṣṭavidham ity āha sa eva |

	cirakaṃ ca svahastaṃ ca tathopagatasaṃjñitam |

	ādhipatraṃ caturthaṃ ca pañcamaṃ krayapatrakam ||

	ṣaṣṭhaṃ tu sthitipatrākhyaṃ saptamaṃ saṃdhipatrakam |

	viśuddhipatrakaṃ caivam aṣṭadhā laukikaṃ smṛtam || iti |

nātra saṃkhyā vivakṣitā |vibhāgapatrāder api laukikatvāt | tatra cirakasya lakṣaṇam āha saṃgrahakāraḥ |

	cirakaṃ nāma likhitaṃ purāṇaiḥ pauralekhakaiḥ |

	arthipratyarthinirdiṣṭaiḥ yathāsaṃbhavasaṃstutaiḥ ||

	svakīyaiḥ pitṛnāmādyair arthipratyarthisākṣiṇām |

	pratināmabhir ākrāntam arthisākṣisvahastavat ||

	spaṣṭāvagamasaṃyuktaṃ yathāsmṛtyuktalakṣaṇam || iti |

saṃstutaiḥ praśastair ity arthaḥ | kātyāyanas tu svahastam āha |

	grāhakeṇa svahastena likhitaṃ sākṣivarjitam |

	svahastalekhyaṃ vijñeyaṃ pramāṇaṃ tat smṛtaṃ budhaiḥ ||

evam eva dāyakena likhitaṃ grāhakeṇābhyupagataṃ lekhyam upagatākhyaṃ vijñeyam | ādhipatram āha nāradaḥ |

	ādhiṃ kṛtvā tu yo dravyaṃ prayuṅkte svadhanaṃ dhanī |

	yat tatra kriyate lekhyam ādhipatraṃ tad ucyate ||

anvādhilekhye viśeṣam āha prajāpatiḥ |

	dhanī dhanena tenaiva paramādhiṃ nayed yadi |

	kṛtvā tad ādhilikhitaṃ pūrvaṃ cāsya samarpayet ||

krayapatraṃ pitāmanenoktam |

	krīte krayaprakāśārthaṃ kravye yat kriyate kvacit |

	vikretrānumataṃ kretrā jñeyaṃ tat krayapatrakam ||

sthitipatrādīni punaḥ kātyāyanenoktāni |

	cāturvidyapuraśreṇīgaṇapaurādikasthitiḥ |

	tadsiddhyarthaṃ tu yal lekhyaṃ tad bhavet sthitipatrakam ||

	abhiśāpe samuttīrṇe prāyaścitte kṛte janaiḥ |

	visuddhipatrakaṃ jñeyaṃ tebhyaḥ sākṣisamanvitam || iti |

bṛhaspatir api lekhyavibhāgam āha |

	bhāgadānakrayādhānasaṃviddāsaṛṇādibhiḥ |

	saptadhā laukikaṃ lekhyaṃ trividhaṃ rājaśāsanam ||

atrāpi na saṃkhyā vivakṣitā, adhikānām api lekhyānām etebhyo darśitatvāt | ata evātrādigrahaṇaṃ kṛtam, anyathā gaṇitair eva saptavidhatvasiddhe ādigrahaṇam apārthaṃ (?) syāt | tenaitat jñāyate lekhyasaṃkhyā nāvadhāraṇārtheti | ato vividhasaṃkhyāvad vacanānām avirodhaḥ | bhāgalekhyādikaṃ svayam eva vyācaṣṭte | 

	bhrātaraḥ saṃvibhaktā ye svarucyā tu parasparam |

	vibhāgapatraṃ kurvanti bhāgalekhyaṃ tad ucyate ||

	bhūmiṃ datvā tu yat patraṃ kuryāc candrārkakālikam |

	anācchedyam anāhāryaṃ danalekhyaṃ tu tad viduḥ ||

	gṛhakṣetrādikaṃ krītvā tulyamūlyākṣarānvitam |

	patraṃ kārayate yat tu krayalekhyaṃ tad ucyate ||

	jaṅgamaṃ sthāvaraṃ bandhaṃ datvā lekhyaṃ karoti yaḥ |

	gopyabhogyakriyāyuktam ādhilekhyaṃ tad ucyate ||

	grāmo deśaś ca yat kuryān mataṃ lekhyaṃ parasparam |

	rājāvirodhi dharmārthaṃ saṃvitpatraṃ vadanti tat ||

	vastrānnahīnaḥ kāntāre likhitaṃkurute tu yat |

	karmāṇi te kariṣyāmi dāsapatraṃ tad ucyate ||

	dhanaṃ vṛddhyā gṛhītvā tu svayaṃ kuryāc ca kārayet |

	uddhārapatraṃ tatproktaṃ ṛṇalekhyaṃ manīṣibhiḥ || iti |

anyad api laukikaṃ lekhyam āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	sīmāvivāde nirṇīte sīmāpatraṃ vidhīyate || iti 

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	datvarṇaṃ pāṭayet patraṃ śuddhau vānyat tu kārayet || iti |

lekhyaprayojanam āha marīciḥ |

	sthāvare vikrayādhāne vibhāge dāna eva ca |

	likhitenāpnuyāt siddhim avisaṃvādam eva ca ||

ādhānam ādhiḥ | ādyaś caśabdaḥ ṛṇādiniṣṇātārthasaṃgrahārthaḥ | avisaṃvādaḥ kālāntare 'pi niṣṇātārthasyānanyathābhāvaḥ | evaṃ ca sthāvarādāv apy avisaṃvādena siddhim ālocya rājavaṃśavarṣādilekhanīyānāṃ āvāpodvāpau kāryau, teṣāṃ dṛṣṭārthatvāt | ato na dānādilekhye dhanikaṛṇikādi lekhanīyam | nāpi ṛṇādilekhye pratigrahādikam | evam anyatrāpi lekhye lekhanīyam ūhanīyam, dṛṣṭaprayojanatvāl lekhyasyā | ata evākṛtaprayojanasya lekhyasya kāryākṣamatve nāśe vā lekhyāntaram utpādyam | ata evāha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	deśāntarasthe durlekhye naṣṭonmṛṣṭe hṛte tathā |

	bhinne dagdhe tathā chinne lekhyam anyatu tu kārayet ||

deśāntarasthe sarvathānetum aśakyasthānasthe | durlekhye durvabodhākṣare | bhinne dvidhā jāte | chinne śīrṇe | kātyāyano 'pi |

	malair yat bheditaṃ dagdhaṃ chidritaṃ vītam eva vā |

	tad anyat kārayel lekhyaṃ svedenollikhitaṃ tathā ||

vītaṃ vigatam | ullikhitam unmṛṣṭam | yat punar nāradenoktam,

	lekhye deśāntaranyaste śīrṇe durlikhite hṛte |

	satas tatkālakaraṇam asato dṛṣṭadarśanam ||

iti, tat tadaiva dhanadānodyataṛṇikaviṣayam | tatra lekhyāntarakaraṇe prayojanābhāvāt | kālakaraṇam, ānayanārthaṃ tasya patrasyānayanayogyakālakalpanam | dṛṣṭadarsanaṃ patralabhyapatrārthajñātṛjñāpanaṃ dhanapratipādane kāryam ity arthaḥ | etac ca patrapāṭanāsaṃbhave 'pi sākṣiṇāṃ sākṣitvnivṛttaye karyam | pratipādanaprakāśārthaṃ ca pratidattapatraṃ grāhyam | kālāntare tu dhane deye lekhyāntaraṃ kāryam eva | ata evoktaṃ tenāpi |

	chinnabhinnahṛtomṛṣṭadagdhadurlikhiteṣu ca |

	kartavyam anyal lekhyaṃ syād eṣa lekhyavidhiḥ smṛtaḥ || iti |

**iti smṛticandirkāyāṃ lekhyanirūpaṇam**

**atha lekhyaparīkṣā**

tatra kātyāyanaḥ |

	rājā kriyāṃ samāhūya yathānyāyaṃ vicārayet |

	lekhyācāreṇa likhitaṃ sākṣyācāreṇa sākṣiṇaḥ ||

suvyaktavarṇavākyādiko lekhyācāraḥ | so 'pi tenaiva darsitaḥ |

	varṇavākyakriyāyuktam asaṃdigdhaṃ sphuṭākṣaram |

	ahīnakramacihnaṃ ca lekhyaṃ tat siddhim āpnuyāt ||

kriyā sādhyam | cihnaṃ mudrā sā rājakīyalekhya eva | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	rājñā svahastasaṃyuktaṃ svamudrācihnitaṃ tathā |

	rājakīyaṃ smṛtaṃ lekhyaṃ sarveṣv artheṣu sākṣimat ||

tathā jānapadaṃ prakṛtyāha sa eva |

	lekhyaṃ tu dvividhaṃ proktaṃ svahastānyakṛtaṃ tathā |

	asākṣimat sākṣimac ca siddhir deśasthites tayoḥ ||

deśasthiteḥ deśācārānusāreṇa | tayoḥ siddhiḥ prāmāṇyam ity arthaḥ | svahastakṛte tu viśeṣam āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	vināpi sākṣibhir lekhyaṃ svahastalikhitaṃ tu yat |

	tat pramāṇaṃ smṛtaṃ sarvaṃ balopādhikṛtād ṛte ||

vināpīty apiśabdāt sasākṣikam api svahastalikhitam astīti gamyate | anyakṛtaṃ tu sākṣikam api svahastalikhitam astīti gamyate | anyakṛtaṃ tu sākṣimad eva pramāṇam | tathā ca pitāmahaḥ|

	vādibhyām abhyanujñātaṃ lekhakena sasākṣikam |

	likhitaṃ sarvakāryeṣu tat pramāṇaṃ smṛtaṃ budhaiḥ ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	deśācārayutaṃ varṣamāsapakṣādivṛddhimat |

	ṛṇisākṣilekhakānāṃ hastāṅkaṃ lekhyam ucyate ||

vṛddihgrahaṇam ādher upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva āha nāradaḥ |

	deśācāraviruddhaṃ yat vyaktādhividhilakṣaṇam |

	tat pramāṇaṃ smṛtaṃ lekhyam aviluptakramākṣaram ||

vyaktam ādhividher ādhikaraṇasya lakṣaṇaṃ yasmin lekhye tat tathoktam | yal lekhyam aviluptakramākṣarādilakṣaṇānvitaṃ tat pramāṇaṃ kālāntare 'pi vastutattvāvabodhakam ity arthaḥ | anevaṃvidham apramāṇam ity arthād eva siddham | tathāpi spaṣṭārtham āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	sthānabhraṣṭās tv apaṅktisthāḥ saṃdigdhā lakṣaṇacyutāḥ |

	yadā tu saṃsthitā varṇāḥ kūṭalekhyaṃ tadā bhavet ||

	deśācāraviruddhaṃ yat saṃdigdhaṃ kramavarjitam |

	kṛtaṃ ca svāminā yac ca sādhyahīnaṃ ca duṣyati || iti |

hārīto 'pi |

	yac ca kākapadākīrṇaṃ tal lekhyaṃ kūṭatām iyāt |

	bindumātravihīnaṃ yat saṃhitaṃ caritaṃ ca yat ||

bṛhaspatir api |

	yad ujjvalaṃ cirakṛtaṃ malinaṃ svalpakālikam |

	bhagnonmṛṣṭākṣarayutaṃ lekhyaṃ kūṭatvam āpnuyāt ||

	mumūrṣuśiśubhītārthastrīmattavyasanāturaiḥ |

	niśopadhibalātkārakṛtaṃ lekhyaṃ na sidhyati || iti |

nārado 'pi |

	mattābhiyuktastrībālabalātkārakṛtaṃ tu yat |

	tad apramāṇaṃ likhitaṃ bhayopādhikṛtaṃ tathā ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	mattenopādhibhītena tathonmattena pīḍitaiḥ |

	strībhir bālāsvatantraiś ca kṛtaṃ lekhyaṃ na sidhyati ||

mumūrṣvādikṛtam ayathārthaśaṅkayā na pramāṇatāṃ pratipadyata iti bārhaspatyādivacanānāṃ tātparyārthaḥ | evaṃ sākṣyādivaiguṇye 'pi na pramāṇam | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

	dūṣitaḥ karmaduṣṭo vā sākṣī yatra niveśitaḥ |

	kūṭalekhyaṃ tu tat prāhuḥ lekhako vāpi tadvidhaḥ ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	sākṣidoṣād bhaved duṣṭaṃ patraṃ vai lekhakasya vā |

	dhanikasyāpi vā doṣāt tathā dhāraṇakasya vā ||

atra ye gūḍhadoṣās te vivādina vaktavyāḥ | ye punaḥ prakaṭās te sabhyair ity āha sa eva |

	pramāṇasya hi ye doṣā vaktavyās te vivādinā |

	gūḍhās tu prakaṭāḥ sabhyaiḥ kāle śāstrapradarśanāt ||

pramāṇasya pramāṇatayā kīrtitasya | kāle pramāṇaparīkṣākāla ity arthaḥ | kālātikramaṇōktās tu doṣā na prāmāṇyaṃ vighnantīty āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	lekhyadoṣās tu ye kecit sākṣiṇāṃ caiva ye smṛtāḥ |

	vādakāle tu vaktavyāḥ paścād uktān na dūṣayet ||

paścād uktāt pramāṇaparīkṣāparyavasānāt paścān na dūṣayed ity arthaḥ | gūḍhadoṣodbhāvanaprakāram āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	sākṣilekhakakartāraḥ kūṭatāṃ yānti te tathā |

	tathā doṣāḥ prayoktavyā duṣṭair lekhyaṃ praduṣyati ||

atha vā, ārūḍhalekhakena na likhitam ārūḍhasākṣibhir vā na dṛṣṭaṃ duṣṭam ity udbhāvanīyam ity āha sa eva |

	na lekhakena likhitaṃ na dṛṣṭaṃ sākṣibhis tathā |

	evaṃ pratyarthinokte tu kūṭalekhyaṃ prakīrtitam ||

uktenārtheneti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	nātathyena pramāṇaṃ tu doṣeṇaiva tu dūṣayet |

	mithyābhiyoge daṇḍyaḥ syāt sādhyārthāc cāpi hīyate ||

evaṃ dūṣaṇavādyuditadoṣasaṃbhave tān doṣān itarasya sabhāpatiḥ nirūpayet | tathā ca sa eva |

	evaṃ duṣṭaṃ nṛpasthāne yasmin tad dhi vicāryate |

	vimṛśya brāhmaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ patradoṣān nirūpayet ||

tatra yadītareṇa te doṣā na parihṛtāḥ tadā duṣṭaṃ lekhyam, parihṛtāś ced aduṣṭam ity āha sa eva |

	yena te kūṭatāṃ yānti sākṣilekhakakārakāḥ |

	tena duṣṭaṃ bhavel lekhyaṃ śuddhaiḥ śuddhiṃ vinirdiśet ||

upagatākhyalekhyasya tv adhamarṇasaṃmatyā śuddhir no cen nety āha sa eva |

	dhanikena svahastena likhitaṃ sākṣivarjitam |

	bhavet kūṭaṃ na cet kartā kṛtaṃ hīti vibhāvayet ||

kartā dhaniko 'dhamarṇānumatyā kṛtam iti yad na vibhāvayet na sādhayet tadā na jānāmīty adhamarṇena lekhyaṃ kūṭaṃ bhaved ity arthaḥ | yadā punaḥ svahastanihnavena likhitaṃ dūṣayati tadā tadārūḍhasākṣyād ito duṣṭam aduṣṭaṃ veti niścetavyam | tathā ca sa eva |

	dattaṃ lekhye svahastaṃ tu ṛṇiko yadi nihnute |

	patrasthaiḥ sākṣibhir vācyo lekhakasya matena vā ||

akṛtatvena dūṣite 'py ayam eva niścaya ity āha sa eva |

	kṛtākṛtavivādeṣu sākṣibhiḥ patranirṇayaḥ || iti |

sākṣigrahaṇam upalakṣaṇam,

	dūṣite patrake vādī tadārūḍhāṃs tu nirdiśet |

iti tenaivoktatvāt | yat punar nāradenoktam,

	yasmiṃs tu saṃśayo lekhye bhūtābhūtakṛtaḥ kvacit |

	tat svahastakriyācihnayuktiprāptibhir uddharet ||

iti, yad api yājñavalkyena,

	saṃdigdhalekhyaśuddhiḥ syāt svahastalikhitādibhiḥ |

	yuktiprāptikriyācihnasaṃbandhāgamahetubhiḥ ||

iti, tad asakṣikasvahastakṛtalekhyaviṣayam | tatra sākṣyādispaṣṭanirnāyakābhāvāt | ata eva hārītaḥ |

	ṛṇisvahastasaṃdehe jīvato vā mṛtasya vā |

	tat svahastakṛtair anyaiḥ patrais tal lekhyanirṇayaḥ ||

svahastakṛtair iti pūrvoktakriyādyupalakṣaṇārtham | yatra punar asti sasākṣikasvahastakṛtalekhyādau sākṣyādi spaṣṭanirṇāyakaṃ na tatra lekhyāntarasādṛśyāt spaṣṭanirṇāyakena spaṣṭanirṇāyakena nirṇayaḥ | tad āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	pratyakṣam anumānena na kadācit prabādhyate |
