	tasmāl lekhyasya duṣṭasya vacobhiḥ sākṣiṇāṃ bhavet ||

	nirṇayaḥ svadhanārthaṃ hi patraṃ dūṣayati svayam || iti |

sākṣiṇāṃ vacobhir na punar adharṇavacanataḥ, tasyāśayadoṣasaṃbhavād ity arthaḥ | anenaivābhiprāyeṇa nāradenāpy uktam |

	likhitaṃ likhitenaiva sākṣimat sākṣibhir haret || iti |

avidyamānasākṣyādikaṃ likhitaṃ tatsajātīyalikhitādinā śodhayed ity arthaḥ | yat punas tenoktam,

	sākṣibhyo likhitaṃ jñeyaṃ likhitān na tu sākṣiṇaḥ |

iti, tal lekhyānārūḍhasākṣi**payam (?) | ataḥ sākṣyādimato lekhyā rūḍhasākṣyādibhir nirṇayaḥ | asākṣimataḥ svahastakṛtalekhyāntarasādṛśyādibhir ity anusaṃdheyam | kathaṃ tarhi mṛtasākṣyādimataḥ nirṇaya ity apekṣite kātyāyanaḥ |

	atha pañcatvam āpanno lekhakaḥ saha sākṣibhiḥ |

	tatsvahastādibhis teṣāṃ viśudhyet tu na saṃśayaḥ ||

teṣāṃ mṛtasākṣyādīnām | tat svahastādibhiḥ patrāntaraprasiddhahastagotravarṇasādṛśyaprabhṛtībhir ity arthaḥ | viṣṇur api |

	yatarṇī dhaniko vāpi sākṣiī vā lekhako 'pi vā |

	mriyate tatra tal lekhyaṃ tat svahastaiḥ prasādhayet || iti |

rājakīyaṃ pratyāha kātyāyanaḥ |

	paścātkāranibaddhaṃ yat tad yatnena vicārayet |

	yadi syād yuktiyuktaṃ tu pramāṇaṃ likhitaṃ tadā ||

	anyathā dūrataḥ kāryaṃ punar eva vinirṇayet |

	atathyaṃ tathyabhāvena sthāpitaṃ jñānavibhramāt ||

	nivartyaṃ tat pramāṇaṃ syāt yatnenāpi kṛtaṃ nṛpaiḥ || 

paścātkāranibaddhaṃ paścātkārākhyajapatraniveśitam ity arthaḥ | tathā,

	samudre tu yathā lekhye mṛtāḥ sarve 'pi tat sthitāḥ |

	likhitaṃ tat pramāṇaṃ tu mṛteṣv api hi teṣu vai ||

pramāṇaṃ mudrādibhir iti śeṣaḥ | ata eva śāsanaṃ mudrām udāhṛtyāha prajāpatiḥ |

	kāryo yatnena mahatā nirṇayo rājaśāsane |

	rājñā svahastatanmudrālekhakākṣaradarśanāt ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	mudrāśuddhaṃ kriyāśuddhaṃ bhuktiśuddhaṃ sacihnakam |

	rājñaḥ svahastasaṃśuddhaṃ śuddhim āyāti śāsanam ||

kriyāśuddham apaśabdānanvayādirahitam | jānapadalekhyam api kvacid bhuktyā śuddhim āyātīty āha sa eva |

	śaktasya saṃnidhāv artho yena lekhyena bhujyate |

	varṣāṇi viṃśatiṃ yāvat tat patraṃ doṣavarjitam ||

smṛtyantare 'py uktam |

	atha viṃśativarṣāṇi ādhir bhuktiḥ suniścitam |

	yena lekhyena tat siddhaṃ lekhyaṃ doṣavivarjitam ||

	sīmāvivāde nirṇīte sīmāpatraṃ vidhīyate |

	tasya doṣāḥ prayoktavyā yāvad varṣāṇi viṃśatim ||

	ādānasahitaṃ patram ṛṇalekhyaniveśitam |

	mṛtasāki pramāṇaṃ tu svalpabhoge 'pi tad viduḥ ||

ādhānam ādhiḥ | mṛtasākṣi pramītasākṣyādikam | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	mṛtāḥ syuḥ sākṣiṇo yatra dhanikarṇikalekhakāḥ |

	tad apy anarthaṃ likhitaṃ na ced ādhiḥ sthirāśrayaḥ ||

āśrayo bhuktiḥ | atha vā likhitabalāyātakiṃcidvṛddhyādidhanalabdhyādhamarṇasya purastāt tal lekhyakhyāpanena vā śuddhir ity āha sa eva |

	yadi labdhaṃ bhavet prajñaptir vā kṛtā bhavet |

	pramāṇam eva likhitaṃ mṛtā yady api sākṣiṇaḥ ||

prajñaptim eva prapañcayati |

	darśitaṃ pratikālaṃ yac chrāvitaṃ smāritaṃ tathā |

	lekhyaṃ sidhyati sarvatra mṛteṣv api hi sākṣiṣu ||

prajāpatir api kvacid bhuktyā śuddhim āha |

	hetvantarakṛte patre ārūḍho yatra nihnute |

	lekhyaṃ yasya bhaved dhaste tasya bhogaṃ vinirdiśet ||

nirṇāyakatveneti śeśaḥ | bhogagrahaṇam upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	lekhyaṃ yac cānyanāmāṅkaṃ hetvantarakṛtaṃ bhavet |

	vipratyaye parīkṣyaṃ tat saṃbandhāgamahetubhiḥ ||

hetvantarakṛtaṃ dāyāder vañcanārthaṃ kṛtam | vipratyayo vipratipattiḥ | saṃbandhaḥ prācīno dhanadānapratidānādilakṣaṇaḥ | āgamaḥ etāvato dhanasya saṃbhavo 'syāsti nety evamātmakaḥ | hetur anumānam | evaṃ dhanināmāṅkaṃ lekhyam api vañcanādihetukṛtam parīkṣyam | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	strībālārtān lipyavijñān vañcayanti svabāndhavāḥ |

	lekhyaṃ kṛtvā svanāmāṅkaṃ jñeyaṃ yuktyāgamais tu tat ||

	jñātvā kāryaṃ deśakālakuśalāḥ kūṭakārakāḥ |

	kurvanti sadṛśaṃ lekhyaṃ tad yatnena vicārayet ||

lipyavijño lipyanabhjñaḥ | kātyāyano 'pi |

	darṣaṇasthaṃ yathā bimbam asatsad iva dṛśyate |

	tathā lekhyasya bimbāni kurvanti kuśalā janāḥ ||

vyāso 'pi |

	lekhyam ālekhyavat kecit likhanti kuśalā narāḥ |

	tasmān na lekhyasāmarthāt siddhir aikāntikī matā ||

tena samyak parīkṣaṇiyam ity abhiprāyaḥ | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	puruṣāḥ santi te kobhāt kāryaṃ yaṃ brūyur anyathā |

	santi cānye durātmānaḥ kūṭasekhyakṛto janāḥ||

	parīkṣyam etad ubhayaṃ svayaṃ rājñā viśeṣataḥ |

	lekhyācāreṇa likhitaṃ sākṣyācāreṇa sākṣiṇaḥ || iti |

lekhyācāreṇa prāguditaśuddhihetujātenety arthaḥ | yat punas taddhetujātena na śuddhim āyāti lekhyaṃ tad apramāṇam eva, tena tat parityajya divyena nirṇayaṃ kuryāt,

	alekhyasākṣike daivīṃ vyavahāre vinirdiśet |

iti kātyāyanasmaraṇāt | tathā hārītenāpy anenaivābhiprāyeṇoktam |

	na mayaitat kṛtaṃ lekhyaṃ kūṭam anyena kāritam |

	adharīkṛtya tat patram arthe divyena nirṇayaḥ || iti |

yatra lekhye sarvathā kūṭaśaṅkānapagamaḥ tatra sādhyārthanirṇayo diveneti tātparyārthaḥ | udāharaṇatayoktasvahastalekhyasyānādaraṇīyatvāt | tena svahastagotracihnādisaṃbhave 'pi prativādino dṛḍhavipratipattyā kūṭaśaṅkānapagamo yatra bhavet tatrāpi divyena nirṇayaḥ | tathā ca prajāpatiḥ |

	yan nāmagotrais tattulyarūpaṃ lekhyaṃ kvacid bhavet |

	agṛhīte dhane tatra kāryo divyena nirṇayaḥ ||

tattulyarūpam avipratipannalekhyāntaratulyarūpam |m agṛhīte dhane prativadini dṛḍha ity arthaḥ | yat punar nāradenoktam,

	duṣṭe patre sphuṭaṃ doṣaṃ noktavān ṛṇiko yadi |

	tato viṃśativarṣāṇi krāntaṃ patraṃ sthiraṃ bhavet ||

iti, tasyāyam artha: dauṣṭyacirakālabhogābhyāṃ saṃdigdhaprāmāṇyakaṃ lekhyaṃ divyena sādhinārthaṃ sthiraṃ bhaved iti cirakālatvamātreṇa sthairyāsaṃbhavāt | yaḥ punaḥ lekhyadoṣān na pariharati tasya daṇḍam āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	kūṭoktau sākṣiṇāṃ vākyaṃ lekhakasya ca patrakam |

	nayecchuddhiṃ na yaḥ kūṭaṃ sa dāpyo daṇḍam uttamam ||

sākṣiṇāṃ vākyaṃ lekhakasya patraṃ ca prati kūṭoktāv uktavidhayā yo vādi kūṭaṃ śuddhiṃ na nayet, sa uttamasāhasakaṇḍya ity arthaḥ | sthāvarādau tu daṇḍāntaram āha sa eva |

	sthāvare vikrayādhāne lekhyaṃkūṭaṃ karoti yaḥ |

	sa samyag bhāvitaḥ kāryo jihvāpāṇyaṅghrivarjitaḥ ||

tenānyalekhyadhārakeṇaitallekhyāgamanakāraṇam udbhāvanīyam ity āha vyāsaḥ |

	yac cānyasya kṛtaṃ lekhyam anyahaste pradṛśyate |

	avaśyaṃ tena vaktavyaṃ patraṃ patrāgamaṃ tataḥ ||

tato lekhyasvāminaḥ sakāśād ity arthaḥ | tathā lekhyānāṃ mitho virodhe bādhyabādhakanirṇayārtham āha sa eva |

	svahastakāj jānapadaṃ tasmāt tu nṛpaśāsanam |

	pramāṇataram iṣṭaṃ hi vyavahārārtham āgatam ||

jānapadapadenātra gobalīvardanyāyāt svahastakṛtād anyad ucyate | nṛpaśabdenāpi lakṣaṇayā śāsanetarad rājakīyam, tenānyakṛtaṃ svahastakṛtād balavat, tasmād api rājakīyam, tato 'pi śāsanam ity arthaḥ | balavattvaṃ cottarottarasya kūṭatvāsaṃbhavatāratamyato 'vabodhyam | ata evopagatākhyalekhyād asākṣikaṃ svahastakṛtam, tasmāc ca sasākṣikaṃ svahastakṛtaṃ balavad ity avagantavyam | ata eva lekhyamātraṃ sākṣivacanato balavad ity āha saṃvartaḥ |

	lekhyasyopari yat sākṣyaṃ kūṭaṃ tad abhidhīyate |

	adharmasya hi tad dvāram ato rājā vivarjayet ||

lekhyaviruddhaṃ yat sākṣyaṃ tato durbalam ity arthaḥ | bṛhaspatir api |

	vācakair yatra sāmarthyam akṣarāṇāṃ vihanyate |

	kriyāṇāṃ sarvanāśaḥ syād anavasthā ca jāyate ||

kriyāṇāṃ lekhyakriyāṇām | kātyāyano 'pi |

	na divyaiḥ sākṣibhir vāpi hīyate likhitaṃ kvacit |

	lekhyadharmaḥ sadā śreṣṭho hy ato nānyena hīyate ||

lekhyena tu hīyat ity āha sa eva |

	tadyuktapratilekhyena tadviśiṣṭena vā sadā |

	lekhyakriyā nirasyeta nirasyānyena na kvacit ||

anyena sākṣyādinety arthaḥ | ata eva bṛhaspatiḥ |

	na jātu hīyate lekhyaṃ sākṣibhiḥ śapathena vā |

	adarśanāśrāvitābhyāṃ hāniṃ prāpnoty upekṣayā ||

bahukālavyāpinyeti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

	adṛṣṭāśrāvitaṃ lekhyaṃ pramītadhanikarṇikam |

	abaddhalagnakaṃ caiva bahukālaṃ na sidhyati || iti |

abaddhalagnakam ādhipratibhūrahitam | bahukālaṃ bahukālīnam, na sidhyati svata ity abhiprāyaḥ | kātyāyano 'pi |

	lekhyaṃ triṃśatsamātītam adṛṣṭāśrāvitaṃ ca yat |

	na tatsiddhim avāpnoti tiṣṭhatsv api hi sākṣiṣu ||

adarśane 'pi viśeṣam āha sa eva |

	prayukte śāntalābhe tu likhitaṃyo na darśayet |

	na yācate ca ṛṇikaṃ tatsaṃdigdhatvam āpnuyāt ||

ṛṇikam āsannam āḍhyaṃ ceti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	āḍhyasya nikaṭasthasya yac chaktena na yācitam |

	śuddhaṃ na śaṅkayā tatra lekhyaṃ durbalatām iyāt ||

evam aviśeṣeṇādarśanād ito lekhyahāniprāptāv apavādam āha sa eva |

	unmattajaḍabālānāṃ rājabhītapravāsinām |

	apragalbhabhayārtānāṃ na lekhyaṃ hānim āpnuyāt ||

saṃvartas tu lekhyābhāsā api bahukālīnā vicāraviṣayatāṃ bhajanta ity āha |

	balopādhikṛtaṃ caiva mattonmattakṛtaṃ tathā |

	ete cānye ca bahavaḥ cirasthā vādahetavaḥ ||

tenaivamādiṣūktaśuddhividhir anusaṃdheyo nirṇetṛbhir ity abhiprāyaḥ | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	dravyaṃ gṛhītvā yal lekhyaṃ parasmai saṃpradīyate |

	channam anyena cārūḍhaṃ saṃyataṃ cānyaveśmani ||

	datte vṛtte 'tha vā dravya kvacil likhitapūrvake |

	eṣa eva vidhir jñeyo lekhyaśuddhivinirṇaye || iti |

tatra nāradaḥ |

	śrutvottaraṃ kriyāpāde lekhyaṃ sādanam uddiśet |

	sāmantalakṣaṇopetā bhuktir vā cirakālikī ||

sādhanaśabdenātra gobalīvardanyāyāt sākṣiṇa ucyante, tenāyam arthaḥ: likhitaṃ sākṣiṇo vā gṛhakṣetrādivivādeṣu uddiśet bhuktir vā kīrtanīyeti | ata evānena sākṣiṣu viśeṣo varṇitaḥ |

	gṛhakṣetrādivādeṣa sāmantebhyo vinirṇayaḥ |

	nagaragrāmagaṇino ye ca vṛddhatamā narāḥ ||

	yad vadanti niyogasthās tad grāhyaṃ vyāvahārikam ||

etad uktaṃ bhavati: kṣetrādisthāvaravivāde mānuṣapramāṇānām anyatamaṃ pramāṇam uddiśet na nātu divyam iti | tatrāpi likhitabhuktī śreṣṭhe ity āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	likhitaṃ sākṣiṇo bhuktiḥ pramāṇatrayam iṣyate |

	pramāṇeṣu smṛtā bhukteḥ sallekhyasamatā nṛṇām ||

nṛṇāṃ pramāṇeṣv ity anvayaḥ | mānuṣapramāṇeṣv ity arthaḥ | sallekhyam anavadyalekhyam | kvacid bhukter eva śraiṣṭhyam itarābhyām āha sa eva |

	rathyānirgamanadvārajalavāhādisaṃśaye |

	bhuktir eva tu gurvī syāt pramāṇeṣv iti niścayaḥ ||

rathyādivyatiriktaviṣaye 'pi bhukyanugraham antareṇa netarayor gurutvam ity āha nāradaḥ |

	vidyamāne 'pi likhite jīvatsv api hi sākṣiṣu |

	viśeṣataḥ sthāvarāṇāṃ yan na bhuktaṃ tad asthiram ||

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	āgame 'pi balaṃ naiva bhuktiḥ stokāpi yatra no || iti |

āgame likhitasākṣiparijñeyakrayādāv (?) ity arthaḥ | anenāgamalekhyādet doṣaśaṅkāpanodakatayā stokabhuktir anugrāhakamātram eva na pramāṇam ity arthād uktam | uktaṃ ca kātyāyanena |

	śaktasya saṃnidhāv artho yasya lekhyena bhujyate |

	daśa varṣāṇy atikrāntaṃ tal lekhyaṃ doṣavarjitam ||

bṛhaspatināpi |

	yasyaikaśāsane grāmakṣetrārāmāś ca lekhitāḥ |

	ekadeśopabhoge 'pi sarve bhuktā bhavanti te || iti |

yat punar lekhyam anivāritapratikūladānasya svāminaḥ tad viphalam evety āha sa eva |

	paśyann anyasya dadataḥ kṣitiṃ yo na vicālayet |

	svāmī satāpi lekheyen na punas tām samāpnuyāt ||

satāpi samīcīnenāpīty arthaḥ | kṣitim iti deyadravyopalakṣaṇārtham | yad āha sa eva |

	rikthibhir vā parair dravyaṃ samakṣaṃ yasya dīyate |

	anyasya bhuñjataḥ paścāt na sa tal labdhum arhati ||

samakṣadānenāpratiṣidhyamānena svāmyanumatipūrvakatvasūcakena svāmino yadāgamalekhyaṃ tasya svatvasādhakatve pratihatir bhavatīty arthaḥ | anenārthalekhyena svārthasiddhim icchatā svāminā samakṣadānaṃ pratiṣeddhavyaṃ yatnata ity uktaṃ bhavati | evaṃ samakṣabhogāpratiṣedhe 'pi draṣṭavyam | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

	varṣāṇi viṃśatiṃ yasya bhuktā pṛthvīparair iha |

	sati rājñi samarthasya tasya seha na sidhyati ||

satāpi lekhyeneti śeṣaḥ | ata eva saṃvartaḥ |

	bhujyamāne gṛhakṣetre vidyamāne tu rājani |

	bhuktir yasya bhavet tasya na lekhyaṃ tatra kāraṇam ||

tasya bhoktur bhujyamānaṃ bhaved yatas tatropekṣasyāgamalekhyaṃ na kāraṇaṃ na sādhanam, bhogopekṣayā svatvāpattisūcikayā lekhyasādhakatvasya pratihatatvād ity arthaḥ | etac ca lekhyavaiyarthyakathanārtham uktaṃ na punar bhoktuḥ svāmitvapratipādanārthaṃ tasya bhogamātreṇa svāmitvāsiddheḥ | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	nopabhogabalaṃ kāryam āhartrā tatsutena vā |

	paśustrīpuruṣādīnām iti dharmo vyavasthitaḥ ||

ata eva vyāsena dhenudṛṣṭānto dattaḥ |

	ḍapekṣitā yathā dhenur vinā pālena nasyati |

	paśyato 'nyais tathā bhūmir bhuktā tena tu hīyate ||

yājñavalkyenāpi evam upekṣakasyāhānir evābhihitā, na punar bhoktuḥ svatvāpattiḥ |

	paśyato 'bruvato bhūmeḥ hānir viṃśativārṣikī |

	pareṇa bhujyamānāyā dhanasya daśavārṣikī || iti |

hāniś cātra likhitabalenātmīyatvaprasādhanamātrasyābhipretā, na punar bhūmyādau tatphale vā svatvasya, nopekṣāmātreṇa svatvam apaitīty uktatvāt | tenātra na dharmākhyanirṇayavaśād upekṣakasya hāniḥ, tadvaśenātmīyatvaprasādhanasaṃbhavāt, kiṃ tu dvitīyavyavahārākhyanirṇayād bhoktur anindyatvaṃ svāmino niruttaratvenāsvāmino jitatvāt | tad āha manuḥ |

	ajaḍaś ced apaugaṇḍo viṣaye cāsya bhujyate |

	bhagnaṃ tad vyavahāreṇa bhoktā tad dhanam arhati || iti |

vyavahāraśabdārtham āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	pramāṇaniścito yas tu vyavahāraḥ sa ucyate |

	vākchalānuttaratvena dvitīyaḥ parikīrtitaḥ || iti |

pramāṇaniścito mānuṣapramāṇaniścitaḥ | vākṣhalavyavahāreṇa niruttaratvena vā bhagnasyāpi vāstavo vyavahāro bhavaty eva | pramāṇarāhityena bhoktur jayasya śithilatvāt,

	chalaṃ nirasya bhūtena vyavahārān nayen nṛpaḥ |

iti yājñavalkyenāpy uktatvāt | evaṃ pratikūladānabhogayor apratiṣedhe sākṣiṇām api vaiyarthyaṃ daṇḍāpūpanyāyasiddhaṃ boddhavyam | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	upekṣāṃ kurvatas tasya tūṣṇīṃbhūtasya tiṣṭhataḥ |

	kāle 'tipanne pūrvokte vyavahāro na sidhyati ||

mānuṣapramāṇāt tasya svārtho na sidhyatīty arthaḥ | saṃgrahakāro 'pi |

	abhuktir āgamo modho bhujyamāne parair api | iti |

āgamaśabdenātra tatpramāṇabhūtalikhitasākṣiṇāv uktau ¦ ata eva prāyeṇa sākṣisādhyeṣv api hānim āha marīciḥ |

	dhenuvāhyālaṃkaraṇaṃ yācitaṃ prītikarmaṇā|

	catuḥpañcābdikaṃ deyam anyathā hānim āpnuyāt ||

atrāpavādam āha manuḥ |

	saṃprītyā bhujyamānāni na naśyanti kadācana |

	dhenur uṣṭro vahann aśvo yaś ca damyaḥ prayujyate ||

damyo vatsataraḥ | yācitake tv apavādam āha vyāsaḥ |

	yācñādharmeṇa (?) yad bhuktaṃ śrotiyai rājapūruṣaiḥ |

	suhṛdbhir bāndhavair vāpi na tad bhogena hīyate ||

"yat" alaṃkarādīty arthaḥ | ahānau kāraṇam apy āha sa eva |

	dharmokṣayaś śrotriye syāt bhayaṃ syād rājapūruṣe |

	snehaḥ suhṛdbāndhaveṣu bhuktam etair na hīyate ||

bhuktaṃ pañcavarṣād ūrdhvam apīti śeṣaḥ | anena sakāraṇopekṣāyāṃ na kadācid dhānir ity uktam | tena daśavārṣikaviṃśativārṣikahānyor api apavādaḥ sakāraṇopekṣāyām draṣṭavyaḥ | ata eva manuḥ |

	ādhiḥ sīmā bāladhanaṃ nikṣepopanidhiḥ striyaḥ |

	rājasvaṃ śrotriyadravyaṃ nopabhogena naśyati ||

sīmni tatratyacihnaiḥ susādhanatvam upekṣākāraṇam | strīṣv aprāgalbhyam | rājaśrotriyayor dṛṣṭādṛṣṭakaryavaiyagryam | aviśeṣṭeṣūpekṣārāraṇaṃ vyaktam | evaṃ saṃbandharūpopekṣākāranasaṃbhave 'py ahāniḥ | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

	sanābhibhir vāndhavair vā bhuktaṃ yat svajanais tathā |

	bhoge tatre na siddhiḥ syād bhogam anyatra kalpayet ||

tatra sanābyādibhoge saṃbandhitvenopekṣāsaṃbhavāt | bhūmyādihāner na siddhaḥ syād ity arthaḥ | pitāmaho 'pi |

	bhuktir balavatīṃ tatra bhoktā yatra paro bhavet |

	svagotre bhogināṃ bhuktir na śaktā śāśvatī nṛṇām ||

balavatī svapratikūlalekhyāder vaiyarthyakartī | svagotre svamātāpitṛbandhṣv ity arthaḥ | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	na bhogaṃ kalpayet strīṣu devarājadhaneṣu ca |

	bālaśrotriyavitte ca mātṛtaḥ pitṛtaḥ kramāt ||

devānām anirākartṛsvabhāvatvāt taddhanasyānyabhoge na hāniḥ | śrotriyagrahaṇam anyāsaktopalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	brahmacārī caret kaścit vrataṃ ṣaṭtriṃadābdikam |

	arthārthī vānyaviṣaye dīrghakālaṃ vasen naraḥ ||

	samāvṛtto vratī kuryāt svadhanānveṣaṇaṃ tataḥ |

	pañcāśadābdiko bhogas taddhanasyāpahārakaḥ ||

	prativedaṃ dvādaśābdaḥ kālo vidhārthināṃ smṛtaḥ |

	śilpavidyārthināṃ caiva grahaṇāntaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||

	suhṛdbhir bandhibhiś caiṣāṃ yat saṃbhuktam apaśyatām |

	nṛpāparādhināṃ caiva na tatkālena hīyate || iti |

etac cāpavādajātaṃ bhoktur āgamābhāve veditavyam | ata eva bṛhaspatiḥ |

	na strīṇām upabhogaḥ syād vinā lekhyaṃ kathaṃcana |

	rājaśrotriyavitte ca jaḍabāladhane na ca ||

strīṇāṃ dhana iti śeṣaḥ | vinā lekhyaṃ vināgamapramāṇaṃ | nārado 'pi |

	strīdhanaṃ narendrāṇāṃ na kathaṃcana jīryate |

	anāgamaṃ bhujyamānaṃ varṣāṇāṃ tu śatair api ||

narendrāṇāṃ ca dhanam ity arthaḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	pratyakṣaparibhogāc ca svāmino dviśatāḥ samāḥ |

	ādhyādīny api jīryante strīnarendradhanād ṛte ||

ādhyādīny apīti prauḍhivādaḥ, teṣām api bhogopekṣākāraṇasaṃbhavena strīdhananarendradhanatulyatvāt | anāgamam iti vadann āgamasaṃbhave jīryata eveti darśayati | darśitaṃ ca hārītena |

	bhaṭacāṭabalād bhuktaṃ hṛtaṃ guptam athāpi vā |

	snehapraṇayadattaṃ ca pradattaṃ bhāṭakena vā ||

	tathā vasanarakṣārthaṃ yācitaṃ praṇayena vā |

	evaṃ bahuvidhe bhoge āgamo nirṇayaḥ smṛtaḥ || iti |

vasanarakṣārthaṃ gṛharakṣaṇārtham | evaṃ copekṣākāraṇarahitā pratikūlā bhuktir āgamābhāve 'py uktakālā likhitasākṣiṇor vaiyarthyam āpādayatīty anusaṃdheyam | ato likhitasākṣiṇāv anukūlabhuktiyuktau pratikūlasamakṣadānādirahitau vṛhakṣetrādiviṣaye pramāṇatayā kīrtanīyau | bhuktiḥ punaḥ kīdṛgvidhā kīrtanīyety apakṣita uktam |

	sāmantalakṣaṇopetā bhuktir vā cirakālikī | iti |

sādhyabhūtakṣetrādeḥ samantato yat kṣetrādi tat svāminaḥ sāmantāḥ, tair vijñātā sāmantopetā | lakṣaṇopetā tu pitāmahena darśitā |

	sāgamā dīrghakālā ca vicchinnoparavojjhitā |

	pratyarthisaṃnidhānā ca bhuktiḥ pañcavidhā smṛtā ||

āgamā āgamamūlikā | tathā ca hārītaḥ |

	na mūlena vinā śākhā antarikṣe prarohati |

	āgamas tu bhaven mūlaṃ bhuktḥ śākhā prakīrtitā ||

kaḥ punar āgama ity apekṣite nāradaḥ |

	labdhaṃ dānakrayaprāptaṃ śauryaṃ vaivāhikaṃ tathā |

	bāndhavād aprajāj jātaṃ ṣaḍvidhas tu dhanāgamaḥ ||

labdhaṃ janmanā labdhaṃ paitṛkādi, atha vā darśanena labdhaṃ nidhyādi | bṛhaspatir api |

	vidyayā krayabandhena śauryāptaṃ bhāryayānvitam |

	sapiṇḍasyāprajasyāṃśaḥ sthāvaraṃ saptadhāpy ete ||

bandha ādhiḥ | so 'pi kvacit svatvanimittaṃ bhavatīti vakṣyāmaḥ | dīrghakālā triṃśadvarṣād analpikā | tathā ca sa eva |

	adhyāsanāt samārabhya bhuktir yasyāvighātinī |

	triṃśadvarṣā tv avicchinnā tasya tāṃ na vicālayet ||

adhyāsanaṃ parigrahaḥ | evaṃ ca dīrghakālā bhuktir āgamānugṛhītapramāṇam, adīrghakālā cet tad anugṛhītāgama ity anusaṃdheyam | ata eva pitāmaḥaḥ |

	nāgamena vinā bhuktiḥ nāgamo bhuktir bījataḥ |

	tayor anyonyasaṃbandhāt pramāṇatvaṃ vyavasthitam ||

pūrvoktavyavasthayeti śeṣaḥ | anenaivābhiprāyeṇa bṛhaspatir api |

	bhuktyā kevalayā naiva bhuktḥ siddhim avāpnuyāt |

	āgamenāpi śuddhena dvābhāṃ siddhyati nānyathā ||

kevalayā āgamarahatayety arthaḥ | evaṃ viśeṣaṇāntararahitayāpy asiddhiḥ | ata eva vyāsaḥ |

	sāgamo dīrghakālaś ca vicchedoparavojjhitaḥ (?) |

	pratyarthisaṃnidhānaś ca pañcāṅgo bhoga iṣyate ||

pañcāṅga iti vadan ekāṅgavaikalpe 'py aprāmāṇyam eva bhogasyeti darśayati | darśitaṃ ca nāradena |

	saṃbhogaṃ kevalaṃ yas tu kīrtayen nāgamaṃ kvacit |

	bhogacchalāpadeśena vijñeyaḥ sa tu taskaraḥ ||

tena sabhyasaṃnidhāv āgamādyaṅgam api kīrtanīyam ity abhiprāyaḥ | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	praṇaṣṭāgamalekhyena bhogārūḍhena vādinā |

	kālaḥ pramāṇaṃ dānaṃ ca kīrtanīyāni saṃsadi ||

dānagrahaṇam āgamopalakṣaṇārtham | caśabdaḥ sāntatyādiviseṣaṇasaṃgrahārthaḥ | evaṃ cāyarmaḥ (?) | bhogapramāṇavadinā bhogākhyaṃ pramāṇaṃ tadviśeṣaṇāni āgamadīrghakāladīni ca kīrtanīyāni, kīrtitāni ca tadvipratipattau sādhanīyāni, kīrtanamātre niścayābhāvāt | tatra dīrthakālādiviśiṣṭabhuktiniścayaḥ sākṣyadhīna ity āha saṃgrahakāraḥ |

	bhuktiprasādhane mukhyāḥ prathamaṃ tat kṛṣīvalāḥ |

	grāmaṇyaḥ kṣetrasāmantās tatsaṃdhāpayataḥ kramāt ||

tatsaṃdhapayataḥ dīrghakālādiviśeṣaṇaṃṇ bhuktiṃ codbhāvayata ity arthaḥ | āgamam udbhāvayatas tu likhitāditrayaṃ pramāṇam ity āha sa eva |

	likhitaṃ (?) sākṣiṇo bhuktiḥ kriyā kṣetragṛhādiṣu |

	āgamaḥ krayadānādau pratyākhyāte cirantane ||

utsannasattāpravāde krayādyāgame pratyākhyāte prativādinā nirākṛte sati kṣetrādiṣv āgamam udbhāvayato likhitasākṣibhuktayaḥ pramāṇam ity arthaḥ | nanu kathaṃ āgame bhuktiḥ pramāṇam, anāgamamūlāyā api bhukter parahārādau darśanāt | maivam, dīrghakālādiviśiṣṭāyā bhukter mūlāntarādarśane saty āgamamūlataivāvasīyate manvādismṛter iva vedamūlatā | nanu tathāpi smaraṇayogye kāle bhuktāv upakrāntāyāṃ yogyānupalabdhyā mūlabhūtāgamābhāvaniścayāt kathaṃ tatra bhuktibalenaivāgamasiddhiḥ | satyam, ata eva tasmin kāle upakrāntāyāṃ likhitasākṣibhyām evāgamo 'dhyavasīyate | smaraṇayogyakāle tu upakrāntāyāṃ svabalenāpīti yuktam āgame pramāṇatrayābhidhānam | etad eva kātyāyanenāpy uktam |

	smārte kāle kriyā bhūmeḥ sāgamā bhuktir iṣyate |

	asmārte 'nugamābhāvāt kramāt tripuruṣāgatā || iti |

anugamābhāvāt yogyānupalabdhyātmakabādhakābhāvād ity arthaḥ | etad uktaṃ bhavati | smaraṇayogyapañcādhikaśatavarṣaparyantātītakālamadhye prārabdhā bhuktiḥ svetarapramāṇāvagatāgamamūlaiva svatve pramānam iṣyate | svataḥ svamūlāvagate yogyānupalabdhyā vādhyamānatvāt | smaraṇāyogye punaḥ pañcādhikaśatavarṣaparyantātītakālāt prācīnakāle prārabdhā svadārḍhyāvagatāgamamūlikā vināpi mānāntarāvagatāgamamūlatāṃ svatve pramāṇam iti | kramāt tripuruṣāgatety asya tu vyākhyā saṃgrahakāreṇa kṛtā |

	svatantraiḥ pretapitṛkaiḥ bhuktā yā pūrvajais tribhiḥ |

	bhuktis tripuruṣā jñeyā yāvajjīvam anuṣṭhitā ||

iyaṃ ca prāyeṇāsmārtakālopakramabhukter udāharaṇārtham uditā, tena bhukter āgamapramāṇatve kramāt tripuruṣāgatatvam anupayogi, asmārtakālopakramatvam evopayujyate | ata eva bṛhaspatinā puruṣatrayātikramābhāve 'pi kālata eva bhuktes tripuruṣatvam uktam |

	pitā pitāmaho yasya jīvec ca prapitāmahaḥ |

	triṃśatsamā yā tu bhuktā bhūmir avyāhatā paraiḥ ||

	bhuktiḥ sā pauruṣī jñeyā dviguṇā ca dvipauruṣī |

	tripauruṣī ca triguṇā parataḥ syāc cirantanī ||

triṃśat samā pañcottareti seṣaḥ,

	varṣāṇi pañcatriṃśat tu pauruṣo bhoga ucyate |

iti smṛtyantara uktatvāt | evaṃ cāgamakartrāgamodbhāvanaṃ lekhyasākṣibhyām eva kāryam, bhogasyāsmārtakālīnopakramavato 'saṃbhavāt | ata eva bṛhaspatiḥ |

	yatrāhartābhiyuktaḥ syāl lekhyaṃ sākṣī tadā guruḥ |

	tadabhāve tu putrāṇāṃ bhuktir ekā garīyasī ||

tadabhāve āhartṛpuruṣābhāve | anenaivābhiprāyeṇa kātyāyano 'pi |

	āhartā bhuktiyukto 'pi lekhyadoṣān viśodhayet |

	tatsuto bhuktidoṣāṃs tu lekhyadoṣāṃs tu nāpnuyāt ||

sutagrahaṇaṃ pautrasyāpy upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva yājñavalkyaḥ |

	āgamas tu kṛto yena so 'bhiyuktas tam uddharet |

	na tatsutas tatsuto vā bhuktis tatra garīyasī ||

kṛtāgamenāgamoddharaṇaṃ lekhyasākṣibhyām eva kāryam | bhukteḥ smārtakālīnopakramatvenāgamodbhāvane 'pi kṣamatvāt | etat kṛtāgamasyāgamo bhogāt pṛthag eva sādhyaḥ | putrapautrayoś cācirantanabhoge tu bhogasādhananāntarīyakatayāpīty avagantavyam | tena cirantanopabhoge tatsādhanenaivālam ity āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	āhartā sādhayed bhuktim āgamaṃ cāpi saṃsadi |

	tatsuto bhuktim evaikāṃ (?) pautrādis tu na kiṃcana ||

tatputro bhuktim evaikāṃ cirantanīm ādyapuruṣeṇa bhoktum upakrāntakālād ārabhya vivādāt prācīnakālaparyantam uparavarāhityena pratipakṣatārhapuruṣasamakṣam anuvartamānaṃ sādhayed ity arthaḥ | putragrahaṇaṃ pautrasyāpi pradarśanārtham | pautrādir ity atadguṇo bahuvrīhiḥ | tena pautrasyāpi putravad eva draṣṭavyam | ata eva smṛtyantaram |

	āgamas tu kṛto yena sa daṇḍyas tam anuddharan |

	na tatsutas tatsuto vā bhogahānis tayor api |||

cirantanabhoge 'pīti śeṣaḥ | anena cirantanabhoge prapautrādīnām āgamānuddharaṇe 'pi na bhogyahānir ity arthād uktaṃ bhavati | uktaṃ ca viṣṇunā |

	tribhir eva tu yā bhuktā puruṣair bhūr yathāvidhi |

	lekhyābhāve 'pi tāṃ tatra caturthaḥ samavāpnuyāt ||

lekhyābhāve 'pi kriyādyāgamaprakāśakapramāṇābhāve 'pīty arthaḥ | ata eva bṛhaspatiḥ |

	rājāntarais tribhir bhuktaṃ pramāṇena vināpi yat |

	brahmadeyaṃ na hartavyaṃ tājñā tasya kadācana ||

pramāṇena āgamaprakāśakapramāṇenety arthaḥ | nārado 'pi |

	yad vināgamam atyantaṃ bhuktaṃ pūrvais tribhir bhavet |

	na tac chakyam apāhartuṃ kramāt tripuruṣāgatam ||

atyantaṃ vināgamaṃ bhuktyāpy upalabhyamānam āgamaṃ vinety arthaḥ | śaṅkho 'pi | "paitraṃ vināpy āgamena pūrvapūruṣābhyāṃ bhuktaṃ labheta" | pūrvavacanasamānartham etat | labheta caturthādir iti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	bhuktis traipuruṣī yatra caturthe saṃpravartitā |

	tadbhogaḥ sthiratāṃ yāti na pṛcched āgamaṃ kvacit ||

uktavidhabhoge tanmūlabhūtāgamaṃ prati kim api pramāṇaṃ kvacid api na pṛcched ity arthaḥ | sāntatyādivisiṣṭāṃ bhuktiṃ prati pramāṇaṃ pṛcched eva | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	āhartaivābhiyuktaḥ syād arthānām uddharet padam |

	bhuktir eva viśuddhā syāt prāptānāṃ pitṛtaḥ kramāt ||

padaṃ sthānam āgamam iti yāvat | viśuddhā sāntatyādimattayā pramāṇataḥ siddhā | prāptānāṃ caturthādīnām | bṛhaspatir api |

	avicchedena yad bhuktaṃ puruṣais tribhir eva tu |

	tatra naivāgamaḥ kāryo bhuktis tatra garīyasī ||

tatra caturthādiṣv āgamaniścayo nāvaśyaṃ kāryaḥ | yatas tatra bhuktiḥ pūrvapuruṣatrayāgatā sāntatyādiviśeṣaṇavattayā sādhitā garīyasī, vināpy āgamaniscayaṃ svatantraiva pramāṇam ity arthaḥ | tathā cāha sa eva |

	sthāvareṣu vivādeṣu bhuktis tripuruṣī ca yā |

	svatantraiva hi sā jñeyā pramāṇaṃ sādhyanirṇaye |

svatantrā svamūlabhūtāgamaniścayānapekṣety arthaḥ | kātyāyano 'pi |

	bhuktis tu dvividhā proktā sāgamānāgamā tathā |

	tripūruṣī yā svatantrānāgamālpā tu sāgamā ||

sāgamā niścitāgamety arthaḥ | nanu svatantrāpi niścitāgamaiva, svadārḍhyenaivāgamaniścayāt | maivam, cirantanyāḥ bhukteḥ asmārtakālīnabhogasya sāntatyādiviśeṣaṇavattayodbhāvanābhāvena kṛtsnāyā dārḍhyābhāvāt | na ca caturthādīnāṃ tadbhogasyāpy udbhāvanaṃ kāryam iti vācyam, "pautrādis tu kiṃcana" (BṛSm above) ity asmārthakālīnabhogasyodbhāvaniniṣedhāt,

	bhuktir eva viśuddhā syāt prāptānāṃ pitṛtaḥ kramāt |

iti smārtakālīnabhogasyaivodbhāvanavidhānāc ca | ataḥ svatantrā bhuktir aniścitāgamā | kathaṃ tarhi tasya svatve prāmāṇyam | ucyate: āgamaniścayābhāve 'pi evaṃ vidhāyāḥ prāmāṇyam iṣyate | sāgamapakṣasyātyantāsaṃbhāvitatvāt, bādhakasya cānāgamaniścayasyābhāvāt | tathā sāhasādau mithyāvāditvaniścayābhāvamātrāt sākṣiṇāṃ prāmāṇyam iṣṭam |

	sarvaḥ sākṣī saṃgrahaṇe cauryapāruṣyasāhase | iti |

tathehāpi sarvaṃ sustham | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	cirantanam avijñātaṃ bhogaṃ lobhān na cālayet | iti |

avijñātam anāgamatayety arthaḥ | etad uktaṃ bhavati: yathā chalānusāreṇa nirṇīto 'pi viṃśativārṣikabhogasya punar bhūtānusāreṇa cālanam iṣṭaṃ na tathā cirantanasyeti | hārīto 'pi |

	anyāyenāpi yad bhuktaṃ pitrā bhrātrātha vāpi ca |

	na tac chakyaṃ parāhartuṃ tṛtīyaṃ samupāgatam ||

tṛtīyam atikramya samupāgatam ity arthaḥ | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	anyāyenāpi yad bhuktaṃ pitrā pūrvatarais tribhiḥ |

	na tac chakyaṃ parāhartuṃ kramāt tripuruṣāgatam ||

pitrā saha pūrvatarais tribhir yad bhuktaṃ tad anyāyeneti vaktum aśaktam, kiṃ punar apahartum ity arthaḥ | yat punas tenoktam,

	āgamena viśuddhena bhogo yāti pramāṇatām |

	aviśuddhāgamo bhogaḥ prāmāṇyaṃ naiva gacchati || 

iti, tad atripuruṣāgatabhogaviṣayam, bhogamātraviṣayatve pūrvoktānekavacanavirodhāt,

	āgamo 'bhyadhiko bhogād vinā pūrvakramāgatāt |

iti yājñavalkyavacanavirodhāc ca | yat tu bṛhaspatinoktam,

	yasya tripuruṣā bhuktiḥ samyaglekhyasamanvitā |

	evaṃvidhā brahmadeyā hartuṃ tasya na śakyate ||

iti, tat smārtakālānatikrāntatripuruṣabhogaviṣayam | yat punar nāradenoktam,

	anāgamaṃ tu yo bhuṅkte bahūny abdaśatāny api |

	coradaṇḍena taṃ pāpaṃ daṇḍayet pṛthivīpatiḥ ||

iti, tad yena kenacit pramāṇena niścitānāgamabhogaviṣayam, anāgamam iti siddhavannirdeśāt (?) | niścitānāgamāś ca bhogās tenaiva darśitāḥ |

	anvāhitaṃ bhṛtanyastaṃ balāvaṣṭabdhayācite |

	apratyakṣaṃ ca yad bhuktaṃ ṣaḍ etāny āgamaṃ vinā ||

anvāhitam anyasmyau (?) dātum arpitam | yācitaṃ parakīyadravyam alaṅkārādyartham ānītam | balāvaṣṭabdhaṃ rājaprasādādibalena bhuktam | evaṃvidhasya cirantanasyāpi bhogasya na prāmāṇyam | tathā ca sa eva |

	grāmakṣetraṃ gṛhaṃ caiva bhuktaṃ yasya kramāgatam |

	rājaprasādād anyatra na tad bhuktaṃ paraṃ nayet ||

rājaprasādād anyāyabhūtād iti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca saṃvartaḥ |

	yā rājñā krodhalobhena chalanyāyena vā kṛtā |

	pradattānyasya (?) tuṣṭena na sā siddhim avāpnuyāt ||

yā khalv anyasya bhūḥ krodhādinā rājñā parabhogyatayā kṛtā, tuṣṭyā vānyasmai dattā, sā cirantanabhogenāpi na bhoktuḥ sidhyatīty arthaḥ | evaṃ śāsanavirodhena bhuktasyāpy asiddhir draṣṭavyā | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	yasya tripuruṣā bhuktiḥ pāramparyakramāgatā |

	na sā cālayituṃ śakyā pūrvakāc chāsanād ṛte ||

yat tu pitāmanenoktam,

	svahastakāj jānapadaṃ tasmāt tu nṛpaśāsanam |

	tatas traipuruṣo bhogaḥ pramāṇataram iṣyate || 

iti, tat pravādaparamparāyātaprasiddhāniścitāgamabhogaviṣayam, anyathā pūrvoktavacanavirodhāt | evaṃ pūrvapuruṣaprasādhitāgamāyā api bhukteḥ pramāṇataratvam avagantavyam | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	bhuktir balavatī śāstre hy avicchinnā cirantanī |

	vicchinnāpi hi sā jñeyā yātu pūrvaṃ prasādhitā ||

yā cirantanī pūrvapuruṣaprasādhitāgamā sā vicchinnāpi balavatī jñeyety arthaḥ | vyāso 'pi |

	āhartrā yābhiyuktena pramāṇena prasādhitā |

	bhūmiḥ sā tatsutāt prāptā na hartavyā kadācana ||

tatsutāt na hartavyety anvayaḥ | yadā tva abhiyuktenāhartrā na sādhitā tadā tatsutena cirantanabhogārūḍhenāpy āhartṛvad eva sādhyā | tathā ca brhaspatiḥ |

	uddharel lekhyam āhartā tatputro bhuktim eva tu |

	abhiyuktaḥ pramītaś cet tatputras tat samuddharet ||

pūrvābhiyogena bhukter adārḍhyāt taduddharaṇamātreṇātrāgamasiddhyabhāvad āgamam apy uddhared ity arthaḥ | lekhyagrahaṇaṃ sākṣiṇo 'pi pradarsanārtham | tasyāpy āhartṛkartṛkāgamoddharaṇe pramāṇatvāt | nārado 'pi |

	tathārūḍhavivādasya pretasya vyavahāriṇaḥ |

	putreṇa so 'rthaḥ saṃsādhyo na tadbhogān nivartate ||

yathāhartrā likhitasākṣibhyām evāgamaḥ saṃsādhyo bhavati tathety arthaḥ | putragrahaṇaṃ dhanagrāhiṇa upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva yājñavalkyaḥ |

	so 'bhiyuktaḥ paretaḥ syāt tasya rikthaṃ tam uddharet |

	na tatra kāraṇaṃ bhuktir āgamena vinākṛtā ||

tam āgamaṃ caturthādir apy avaśyaṃ samuddharet | yasmāt svatantrā bhukis tatrāpramāṇam, avigītatvābhāvād ity arthaḥ | evaṃ ca ya (?) yad uktaṃ nāradena,

	ādau tu kāraṇaṃ dānaṃ madhye bhuktis tu sāgamā |

	kāraṇaṃ bhuktir evaikaṃ saṃtatā yā cirantanī ||

iti, tad āhartṛnirṇītābhiyogābhāvaviṣayam iti mantavyam | akṣarārthas tu saṃgrahakāreṇa darśitaḥ |

	kṛtāgamasyoktakāle bhukte syāt prabhur āgamaḥ |

	tasyaivātmatṛtīyasya prabhur bhuktḥ sphuṭāgamā ||

	bhuktir yā sā caturthasya pramāṇaṃ saṃtatāgatā |

	parityaktāgamā bhuktiḥ kevalaiva prabhur matā || iti |

kṛtāgamasya āgamakartuḥ | uktakāle triṃśadvarṣātmaka ity arthaḥ | prabhuḥ pradhānam | sphuṭāgamā pramāṇaparicchinnāgamā, yā saṃtatāgatā bhuktiḥ cirantanī caturthādeḥ, pramāṇaṃ sā parityktāgamaniścayā | prabhuḥ svatvanirṇayakṣameti dvitīyaślokārthaḥ | yat punar vyāsenoktam,

	varṣāṇi viṃśatiṃ bhuktā svāmināvyahatā satī |

	bhuktḥ sā pauruṣī bhūmer dviguṇā tu dvipauruṣī ||

	traipauruṣī ca triguṇā na tato 'nveṣya āgamaḥ |

iti, tac caturthādibhukteṣv aṣṭyābdikyāḥ prārambhakālīnapuruṣāṇāṃ jīvatām abhāve cirantanakālīnabhogatulyatāpattau satyāṃ draṣṭavyam, anyathā

	smārte kāle kriyā bhūmeḥ sāgamā bhuktir iṣyate |

ityādivacanavirodhāpatteḥ | evaṃ ca pañcādhikaśatavarṣaparyantasya smārtakālatvābhidhānaṃ prāyikābhiprāyeṇeti mantavyam |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ bhuktinirūpaṇam**

**atha sākṣilakṣaṇāni** 

tatra manuḥ |

	yādṛśā dhanibhiḥ karyā vyavahāreṣu sākṣiṇaḥ |

	tādṛśāṃt saṃpravakṣyāmi yathā vācyam ṛtaṃ ca taiḥ ||

sākṣiṇāṃ lakṣaṇāni anuyojanavidhiṃ ca vakṣyāmīty arthaḥ | tatrādau lakṣaṇāni darśayati |

	gṛhiṇaḥ putriṇo maulāḥ kṣatraviṭchūdrayonayaḥ |

	arthajāḥ sākṣyam arhanti na ye kecid anāpadi ||

maulāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ | arthajñāḥ sādyam arthaṃ viditavantaḥ,

	samakṣadarśanāt sākṣyaṃ śravaṇāc caiva sidhyati |

iti tenaivoktatvāt | gṛhiṇa ityādiṣu pulliṅganirdeśo vivakṣitaḥ, upādeyagatatvāt | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	kulīnā ṛjavaḥ śuddhāḥ janmataḥ karmato 'rthataḥ |

	sākṣiṇaḥ sucayo 'nindyāḥ puruṣāḥ syuḥ suvṛddhayaḥ ||

evaṃvidhāḥ puruṣāḥ ṛṇādiṣu sākṣiṇaḥ syur ity arthaḥ | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

	dharmajñāḥ putriṇo maulāḥ kulīnāḥ satyavādinaḥ |

	śrautasmārtakriyāyuktā vigatadveṣamatsarāḥ ||

	śrotriyā naparādhīṇāḥ (?) sūrayaś cāpravāsinaḥ |

	yugānaḥ sākṣiṇaḥ kāryā ṛṇādiṣu vijānatā || iti |

śrotriyāḥ śrutipāṭhakāḥ | evam uktavidhā na jātu kūṭatāṃ pratipadyanta ity aha sa eva |

	jñātvā kāryaṃ desakālakusalāḥ kūṭakārakāḥ |

	kurvanti sadṛśaṃ lekhyaṃ naite syuḥ sākṣiṇo yathā ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	prakhyātakulaśīlāś ca lobhamohavivarjitāḥ |

	āptāḥ śuddhā viśiṣṭā ye teṣāṃ sākṣyam asaṃśayam ||

teṣām iti bahuvacanaṃ dvyekasaṃkhyāsākṣivākyam evaṃ na niścāyakam iti pratipādanārtham | ata eva manuḥ |

	tryavaraiḥ sākṣibhir bhāvyo nṛpabrāhmaṇasaṃnidhau | iti |

bhāvyaḥ sādhanīyaḥ trayaḥ avarā nikṛṣṭā yeṣāṃ te tryavarāḥ, tritvād ūnasaṃkhyā sākṣiṣv apraśatety arthaḥ | yat tūktaṃ bṛhaspatinā, 

	nava sapta pañca vā syuḥ catvāras traya eva vā |

	ubhau vā śrotriyau khyātau naikaṃ pṛcchet kadācana ||

iti, tatrobhāv iti likhitagūḍhasākṣiviṣayam | yato 'nantaram āha sa eva |

	likhitau dvau tathā gūḍhau tricatuḥpañca lekhitāḥ |

	yadṛcchāsmāritāḥ kulyās tathā cottarasākṣiṇaḥ || iti |

likhitādīnāṃ bheda upariṣṭād vakṣyate | yat punas tenoktam,

	dūtako ghaṭikāgrāhī kāryamadhyagatas tathā |

	eka eva pramāṇaṃ syān nṛpo 'dhyakṣas tathaiva ca ||

iti — ghaṭikāgrāhī ganakaḥ | adhyakṣaḥ prāḍvivākaḥ — yad api vyāsena,

	śubhakriyaś ca dharmajñaḥ sākṣī yatrānubhūtavān |

	pramāṇam eko 'pi bhavet sāhaseṣu viśeṣataḥ ||

iti, yad api kātyāyanena, 

	abhyantaras tu nikṣepe sākṣyam eko 'pi vācyate |

	arthinā prahitaḥ sākṣī bhavaty eko pi dūtakaḥ ||

	saṃstutaṃ yena saṃnyastaṃ tat tenaiva vibhāvayet |

	eka eva pramāṇaṃ sa vivāde tatra kīrtitaḥ ||

iti, tad etat sarvam ubhayānumatasākṣiviṣayam | bahutvavad ubhayasaṃmatatvasyāpy anāptatvaśaṅkāvyudāsakatvāt | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	atha vānumato yasya dvayor vivadamānayoḥ |

	sa sākṣy eko 'pi sākṣitve praṣṭavyaḥ syāt tu saṃsadi || iti |

evaṃ ca tryavarā iti saṃkhyāniyamo likhitagūḍhobhayānumatavyatiriktasākṣivixaya evety anusaṃdheyam | ubhayānumatasākṣiviṣaye likhitagūḍhasākṣiviṣaye ca nyūnasaṃkhyāpakṣasyāpi vihitatvāt | ata eva saṃgrahakāraḥ |

	kartavyāḥ sarvakāryeṣu tribhya ārabhya sākṣiṇaḥ |

	dvyekayoḥ pratiṣedhaḥ syād eko 'py ubhayasaṃmataḥ || iti |

sākṣiṇo likhitagūḍhavyatiriktāḥ | tribhya ārabhya kartavyā ity arthaḥ | sākṣiṇa ity anuvṛttau nāradaḥ |

	brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśaḥ śūdrā ye cāpy aninditāḥ |

	prativarṇaṃ bhaveyus te sarve sarveṣu vā punaḥ ||

sati saṃbhave vyavahartuḥ savarṇāḥ sākṣiṇaḥ ity arthaḥ | evaṃ varṇetarajātāv api vyavahartṛsajātīyā bhaveyuḥ,

	yathājāti yathāvarṇaṃ sarve sarveṣu vā smṛtāḥ |

iti yājñavalkyasmaraṇāt | jātigrahaṇaṃ śreṇyāder apy upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	śreṇiṣu śreṇipuruṣāḥ sveṣu vargeṣu vargiṇaḥ |

	bahirvāsiṣu bāhyāḥ syuḥ striyaḥ strīṣu ca sākṣiṇaḥ || iti |

atrāpavādam āha sa eva |

	śreṇyadiṣu tu vargeṣu kaścid ced dveṣyatām iyāt |

	tasya tebhyo na sākṣyaṃ syāt dveṣṭāraḥ sarva eva te ||

śreṇyādiṣu ye yasya dveṣaṃ kurvanti te tasya na sākṣiṇa ity arthaḥ | śreṇyādigrahaṇaṃ varṇādipradarśanārtham, dveṣagrahaṇaṃ cāyathārthakathanakāraṇavatām upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva manuḥ |

	āptāḥ sarveṣu varṇeṣu kāryāḥ kāryeṣu sākṣiṇaḥ |

	sarvadharmavido 'lubdhāḥ viparītāṃs tu varjayet ||

āptāḥ vipralambhakavyatirikāḥ | viparītān ayathārthavādakāraṇopetāny arjayed ity arthaḥ | tān evāha sa eva |

	nārthasaṃbandhino nāptā na sahāyā na vairiṇaḥ |

	na dṛṣṭadoṣāḥ kartavyā na vyādhyārtā na dūṣitāḥ ||

	na sākṣī nṛpatiḥ kāryo na kārukakuśīlavau |

	na śrotriyo na liṅgastho na saṅghebhyo vinirgataḥ ||

	nādhyadhīno na vaktavyo na dasyur na vikarmakṛt |

	na vṛddho na śuśur naiko nānyo na viakalendriyaḥ ||

	nārto na matto nonmatto na kṣuttṛṣṇopapīḍitaḥ |

	na śramārto na kāmārto na kruddho nāpi taskaraḥ || iti |

arthasaṃbandhinaḥ vipratipadyamānārthasya saṃbandhinaḥ | āptās tu kātyāyanena darśitāḥ |

	tadvṛttijīvino ye ca tatsevāhitakāriṇaḥ |

	tadbandhusuhṛdo bhṛtyā āptās te tu na sākṣiṇaḥ || iti |

sahāyāḥ pratibhūprabhṛtayaḥ | vairiṇaḥ vipratipannayor anyatarasya dṛṣṭadoṣāḥ kūṭasākṣitvenānyatra jñātāḥ | dūṣitāḥ sahāpātakādidoṣeṇa | nṛpatiḥ bahuvyāpāravyakulatvāt pratiṣidhyate | kārukaḥ śilpopajīvī hemakārādiḥ | kuśīlava raṅgāvatārī, tayor arthapravaṇatvāt pratiṣedhaḥ | śrōtriyo 'tra karmānuṣṭhānaniṣṭho vivakṣitaḥ, na punaḥ śrutipāṭhakaḥ, tasya sākṣitvenoktatvāt | liṅgastho brahmacārī yatiś ca | saṅghebhyo vinirgataḥ vānaprasthādiḥ | eteṣu śrotriyādiṣv ayathārthavādahetvabhāve 'pi vacanabalenaiva pratiṣedho 'dhyavaseyaḥ | ādhyadhīno mānasavyādhivihvalaḥ | vaktavyaḥ kuṣṭādīnā kutsitadehaḥ | dasyuḥ krūraceṣṭaḥ | vikarmakṛt śāstraviruddhakarmakṛt | vṛddhaḥ jarāvaśena skhalitabuddhiḥ | śiśuḥ apūrṇaṣoḍaśavarṣaḥ | eko vivadamānābhyām ananumataḥ | antyaḥ caṇḍālādiḥ | vikalendriyo badhirādiḥ | ārtādayo vyaktāḥ | teṣāṃ bhedaḥ pūrvam ukto 'trāpy anusaṃdheyaḥ | nārado 'pi varjanīyān āha |

	dāsanaikṛtikāśrāddhavṛddhastrībālacākrikāḥ |

	mattonmattapramattārtakitavagrāmayājakāḥ ||

	mahāpathikasāmudravaṇikpravrajitāturāḥ |

	yugmaikaśrotriyaācārahīnaklībakuśīlavāḥ ||

	nāstikavrātyadārāgnityāgino 'yājyayājakāḥ |

	ekasthālisahāyāricarajñātisanābhayaḥ ||

	prāgdṛṣṭadoṣaśailūṣaviṣajīvyāhituṇḍikāḥ |

	garadāgnidakīnāśaśūdrāpatyupapātakāḥ ||

	klāntasāhasikāśāntanirdhūtāntāvasāyinaḥ |

	bhinnavṛttāsamāvṛttajaḍatailikapauṣikāḥ ||

	bhūtāviṣṭanṛpadviṣṭavarṣanakṣatrasūcakāḥ |

	aghaśaṃsyātmavikretṛhīnāṅgabhagavṛttayaḥ ||

	kunakhī syāvadan śvitrī mitradhrukśaṭhaśauṇḍikāḥ |

	aindrajālikalubdhograśreṇīgaṇavirodhinaḥ ||

	vadhakṛccitrakṛnmūrkhaḥ patitaḥ kūṭakārakaḥ |

	kuhakaḥ pratyavasitaḥ taskaro rājapūruṣaḥ ||

	manuṣyaviṣamāṃsāsthimadhukṣīrāmbusarpiṣām |

	vikretā brāhmaṇas caiva dvijo vārdhuṣikas ca yaḥ ||

	cyutaḥ svadharmāt kulikaḥ sūcako hīnasevakaḥ |

	pitrā vivadamānaś ca bhedakṛc cety asākṣiṇaḥ || iti |

naikrtikaḥ pararandhrānveṣaṇaśīlaḥ | cākriko vaitālikaḥ | sāmudravaṇik vahitrayāyī (?) | yugmau dvitvaviśiṣṭau | ekasthālīty asya dvedhā vigrahaḥ, ekapākasadhanasthālī yasya puruṣasya, vipratipannayor anyatareṇa puruṣeṇa saha yasya vā ekaṃ bhojanashālam sa ekasthtālī ekapākaḥ sahabhojano veti yavat | ariṣu caratīty aricaraḥ śatrusaṃbandhīti yāvat | sanābhayas tu kātyāyanena darśitāḥ |

	mātṛṣvasṛsutāś caiva sodayīsutamātulāḥ |

	ete sanābhayas tūktāḥ sākṣyaṃ teṣu na yojayet || iti |

śailūṣo naṭaḥ | viṣajīvī viṣasya saṃgrahaṇarakṣaṇādivyāpāre niyuktaḥ | āhituṇḍikaḥ sarpagrāhī | garado viṣadaḥ | agnido gṛhadāhakaḥ | kīnāśaḥ kṛpaṇaḥ | klāntaḥ khinnaḥ | nirdhūto bahiṣkṛtaḥ | antāvasāyī pratilomajaḥ | bhinnavṛtto durācāraḥ | asamāvṛtto naiṣṭhikabrahmacārī | jaḍo mandabuddhiḥ | tailikaḥ tilaghātī, mahāyantrika iti yāvat | paupikaḥ apūpādivikrayī | varṣasūcako vṛṣṭisūcakaḥ, naimittika iti yāvat | nakṣatrasūcako jyautiṣavṛttiḥ | aghasaṃsī paradoṣaprakāśakaḥ | bhagavṛttiḥ svavṛttaye bhāryāveśyātvakārī | śauṇḍiko madyavikrayī | mūrkho devatāṃ gṛhītvā yācakaḥ | kuhako dāmbhikaḥ | pratyavasitaḥ pravrajyāto nivṛttaḥ | sūcakaḥ paradoxasūcanarthaṃ rājñā niyuktaḥ | bhedakṛt piśunaḥ | anye prasiddhāḥ | kātyāyano 'pi katipayān asākṣijanān āha |

	kulyāḥ saṃbandhinaś caiva vivāhyo bhaginīpatiḥ |

	pitā bandhuḥ pitṛvyaś ca śvasuro guravas tathā ||

	nagaragrāmadeśeṣu niyuktā ye padeṣu ca |

	vallabhāś ca na pṛccheyur bhaktās te rājapūruṣāḥ || iti |

ye kulyādayo rājapuruṣāntāḥ kīrtitāḥ te sākxyaṃ kartuṃ na pṛccheyuḥ na sākṣiṇaḥ syur ity arthaḥ |

	nanv ayam asākṣikathanaprapañco vyarthaḥ | lakṣaṇoktyaivārthād vilakṣaṇānām asākṣitvasiddheḥ, satyam evaṃ tathāpi yatra sarvadhā vihitasākṣiṇām alābhaḥ tatra manuṣyamātrasya sākṣitvam "na ye kecid anāpadi" iti manuvacanato 'rthāt prāptam, tatra keṣāṃcit pratiṣedhārtham "nārthasaṃbandhino nāptāḥ" ityādivacanaracanā kṛtety arthavān evāyaṃ prapañcaḥ | evaṃ ca lakṣaṇānvitasākxinām alābhe pratiṣedharāhityamātraśālināṃ sākṣitvaṃ vihitam ity anusaṃdheyam | ata eva teṣām api praśaṃsā vyāsena kṛtā |

	divyam oṣadhibhir mantraiḥ prāyeṇa vyabhicāryate |

	na khalv adoṣaduṣṭānāṃ vyabhicāro 'sti sākṣiṇām || iti |

yat punar manunoktam |

	anubhāvī tu yaḥ kāścit kuryāt sākṣyaṃ vivādinām |

	antarveśmany araṇye vā sarīrasyāpi vātyaye ||

	striyāpy asaṃbhave kāryaṃ bālena sthavireṇa vā |

	śiṣyeṇa bandhunā vāpi dāsena bhṛtakena vā || iti |

anubhāvī kāryābhijñaḥ | yad api nāradena,

	asakṣiṇo ye nirdiṣṭāḥ dāsanaikṛtikādayaḥ |

	kāryagauravam āsādya bhaveyus te 'pi sākṣiṇaḥ ||

iti — kāryagauravaṃ kāryasya praśastajñātuḥ rāhityam — tad etad sarvaṃ sāhasādysthirakarmaviṣayaṃ tatra praśastānāṃ durbalatvāt | ata eva saṃgrahakāraḥ |

	utkṛṣṭamadhyamābhāve niṣiddhā api sākṣiṇaḥ |

	sāhasādiṣu mantavyāḥ kālakāryānibandhanāḥ || iti |

atra viśeṣam āhośanā |

	dāso 'ndho badhiraḥ kuṣṭhī strībālasthavirādayaḥ |

	ete 'py anabhisaṃbandhāḥ sāhase sākṣiṇo matāḥ ||

anabhisaṃbandhāḥ mitrāribhāvarahitāḥ | sāhase sāhasādiṣv ity arthaḥ | abhisaṃbandhāś cet sāhasādiṣv api te varjanīyā eva | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	teṣām api na bālaḥ syān naiko na strī na kūṭakṛt |

	na bāndhavo na cārātir brūyus te sākṣyam anyathā ||

teṣāṃ dāsaneikṛtikādīnāṃ madhye 'pi vyaktānṛtahetuśālino bālādayo varjyā ity arthaḥ | vyaktānṛtahetavo 'pi teṣu tena darśitāḥ |

	bālo 'jñānād asatyāt strī pāpābhyāsāc ca kūṭakṛt |

	vibrūyād bāndhavaḥ snehād vairaniryātanād ariḥ ||

asatyāt asatyaśīlatvād ity arthaḥ | anenājñatvāsatyaśīlatvādyadharmaniṣṭhatvātyantotkaṭarāgadveṣaśālitvādīny eva vyakānṛtahetavo na punar bālatvād ayaḥ iti darsitam | evam ekasminn api naikatvaṃ vyaktānṛtahetuḥ api tu lubdhatvam ity āha manuḥ "eko lubhas tv asākṣī syat" iti | evaṃ cājñātvāsatyaśīlatvādidoṣāṇāṃ sadbhāve dāsādayo 'pi heyāḥ, tadabhāve tu bālādayo 'py upādeyāḥ iti sāhasādiviṣaye 'nusandheyam | yat punar manunoktam,

	sāhaseṣu tu sarveṣu steyasaṃgrahaṇeṣu ca |

	vāgdaṇḍayos ca pāruṣye na parīkṣete sākṣiṇaḥ || 

iti, yad api kātyāyanena,

	vyāghāteṣu nṛpājñāyāḥ saṃgrahe sāhaseṣu ca |

	steyapāruṣyayoś caiva na parīkṣeta sākṣiṇaḥ ||

iti, tad gṛhasthatvādiguṇagaṇaviṣayaparīkṣāyā niṣedhakaṃ na punar ajñatvādidoṣaviṣayaparīkṣāyā api, pūrvoktavacanavirodhāt | yat punaḥ kātyāyanenoktam,

	ṛṇādiṣu parīkṣeta sākṣiṇaḥ sthirakarmasu |

	sāhasātyayikaṃ caiva parīkṣā kutracit smṛtā ||

iti, yady atra sāhasādau parājaye vadhādigurutaradaṇḍaprāptisaṃbhāvanā, tatra parīkṣāvidhānārtham ṛṇādisāhacaryād ajñatvādidoṣaparīkṣāyāḥ sārvatrikatvena kutracid vidhānāsaṃbavāc ca | yat tu yājñavalkyenoktam,

	sarvaḥ sākṣī saṃgrahaṇe cauryapāruṣyasāhase |

iti, tad api guṇaparīkṣāmātranivṛttyartham ity avagantavyam |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ sākṣilakṣaṇāni **

**atha sākṣibhedāḥ** 

tatra kātyāyanaḥ |

	lekhyārūḍhaś cottaraś ca sākṣī mārgadvayānvitaḥ || iti |

prajāpatir āha |

	sākṣī dvibhedo vijñeyaḥ kṛta eko 'paro 'kṛtaḥ |

	lekhyārūḍhaḥ kṛto jñeya uttaro 'kṛta ucyate ||

lekhyārūḍho likhitādir ity ārthaḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	likhitaḥ smāritaś caiva yadṛcchābhijña eva ca |

	gūḍhaś cottarasākṣī ca sākṣī pañcavidhaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

tathā akṛtasākṣibhedo'pi tenaiva darśitaḥ |

	akṛtaḥ ṣaḍvidhaḥ sākṣī sūribhiḥ parikīrtitaḥ |

	grāmaś ca prāḍvivākas ca rājā ca vyavahāriṇām ||

	karyeṣv abhyantaro yaḥ syād arthinā prahitaś ca yaḥ |

	kulyāḥ kulavivādeṣu bhaveyus te 'pi sākxiṇaḥ || iti |

tatra tāvat kṛtānāṃ lakṣaṇam āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	jātināmādi likhitaṃ yena svaṃ pitryam eva ca |

	nivāsaś ca sa vijñeyaḥ sākṣī likhitasaṃjñikaḥ ||

	āhūya yaḥ kṛtaḥ sākṣī ṛṇanyāsakriyādike |

	smāryate ca muhur yaś ca smāritaḥ sa udāhṛtaḥ ||

	kriyamāṇe tu kartavye yaḥ kaścit svayam āgataḥ |

	atra sākṣī tvav asmākam ukto yādṛcchikas tu saḥ ||

	kuḍyavyavahito yas tu śrāvyate ṛṇibhāṣitam |

	viniṣkṛte tathābhūta (?) gūḍhasākṣī sa ucyate ||

	yatra sākṣī disaṃ gacchan mumūrṣur vā yathāśrutam |

	anyaṃ saṃśrāvayet taṃ tu vidyād uttarasākṣiṇam || iti |

likhite tu viśeṣam āha hārītaḥ |

	sudīrgheṇāpi kālena likhitaḥ siddhim āpnuyāt |

	ātmanaiva likhej jānann ajñas tv anyena lekhayet ||

yat punas tenaivoktam,

	āṣṭamād vatsarāt siddhiḥ smāritasyeha sākṣiṇaḥ |

	āpañcamāt tathā siddhir yadṛcchopagatasya ca ||

	ātṛtīyāt tathā varṣāt siddhir gūḍhasya sākṣiṇaḥ |

	ā vatsarāt tu siddhiṃ ca vadanty uttarasākṣiṇaḥ || 

iti, tat pūrvapakṣatvenābhihitam ity avagantavyam | yato 'nantaram āha sa eva |

	atha vā kālaniyamo na dṛṣṭaḥ sākṣiṇaṃ prati |

	smṛtyapekṣaṃ hi sākṣitvam āhuḥ śāstravido janāḥ ||

	yasya nopahatā buddhiḥ smṛtiḥ śrotuś ca sākṣiṇaḥ |

	sudīrgheṇāpi kālena sa sākṣī sākṣyam arhati || iti |

bṛhaspatināpy akṛtasākṣiṇo nirūpitāḥ |

	ghātitaṃ muṣitaṃ yatra sīmāyāś ca samantataḥ |

	akṛto 'pi bhavet sākṣī grāmas tatra na saṃśayaḥ ||

	nirṇīte vyavahāre tu punar nyāyo yadā bhavet |

	adhyakṣaḥ sabhyasahitaḥ sākṣī syāt tatra nānyathā ||

	arthipratyarthinor vākyaṃ yac chrutaṃ bhūbhṛtā svayam |

	sa eva tatra sākṣī syād visaṃvāde dvayor api ||

	ubhābhyāṃ yatra visvastaṃ kāryaṃ cāpi niveditam |

	gūḍhadhārī sa vijñeyaḥ kāryamadhyagatas tathā ||

	arthipratyarthivacanaṃ śṛṇuyāt preṣitas tu yaḥ |

	ubhayoḥ saṃmataḥ sādhur dūtakaḥ sa udāhṛtaḥ ||

	vibhāgādāv api ṛṇe jñātir yatropayujyate |

	dvayoḥ samāno dharmajñaḥ kulyaḥ sa parikīrtitaḥ || iti |

yat punas tenoktam,

	likhito lekhito gūḍhaḥ smāritaḥ kulyadūtakau |

	yādṛcchikaś cottaraś ca kāryamadhyagato 'paraḥ |

	nṛpo 'dhyakṣas tathā grāmaḥ sākṣī dvādasadhā smṛtaḥ || 

iti, tal likhitasyāvāntarabhedaṃ svanāmādilipikartṛtvakārayitṛtvarūpam āśrityoktam |

	ekādaśavidhaḥ sākṣī śāstre dṛṣṭo manīṣibhiḥ |

iti nāradenānādṛtyoktam ||

**iti smṛtiandrikāyāṃ sākṣibhedāḥ **

**athāsākṣibhedāḥ** 

tatra nāradaḥ |

	asākṣy api hi nirdiṣṭaḥ śāstre pañcavidho budhaiḥ |

	vacanād doṣato bhedāt svayam uktir mṛtāntaraḥ ||

asākṣitvahetūnāṃ pañcavidhatvāt tadvaśenāsākṣy (?) api pañcavidho budhair nirdiṣṭa ity arthaḥ | ata eva saṃgrahakāraḥ |

	dṛṣṭatvāt pratiṣiddhatvād akṛtatvad aniscayāt |

	ekāṅgavikalatvāc ca syād asādṣy api pañcadhā ||

	stenādiḥ śrotriyādiś ca svaṃbhūr bhinnagīr mithaḥ |

	mumūrṣuśrāvitād anyaḥ pañcamaḥ syāt mṛtāntaraḥ || iti |

duṣṭatvād asākṣī stenādiḥ pratiṣiddhatvāc chrotriyādiḥ | akṛtatvāt svayaṃbhūḥ, aniścayāt mathobhinnagīh (?), ekāṅgavikalatvāt mṛtāntara ity arthaḥ | nārado 'pi |

	stenāh sāhasikāś caḍṇāḥ (?) kitavā vadhakās tathā |

	asākṣiṇas te duṣṭatvāt teṣu satyaṃ na vidyate ||

	śrotriyās tāpasā vṛddhā ye ca pravrajitādayaḥ |

	asakṣiṇas te vacanān nātra hetur udāhṛtaḥ ||

	svayamuktir anirdiṣṭaḥ svayam evaitya yo vadet |

	sūcīty uktaḥ sa śāstreṣu na sa sākṣītvam arhati ||

	rājñā parigṛhīteṣu sākṣiṣv ekārthaniścaye |

	vacanaṃ yatra bhidyeta te syur bhedād asākṣiṇaḥ ||

	yo 'rthaḥ śrāvayitavyaḥ syāt tasminn asati cārthini |

	kva tad vadatu sākṣitvam ity asākṣī mṛtāntaraḥ || iti |

sūcī sūcakaḥ | yo 'rtha ity asyāyam arthaḥ: asminn arthe mayāsau sākṣī kṛta iti yo 'rtho 'rthinā svasyāsthiratvaṃ manvānena śravayitavyaḥ putrāder jñāpayitavyaḥ, tasminn arthe asatyajñāpite 'rthini cāsiti mṛte, tatsākṣitvam arthinā kṛtaṃ sākṣitvam arthiputrādiḥ (?) kva kasminn arthe kasya puruṣasya pramāṇoktikāle vadatv ity anavadhṛter asākṣī mṛtāntara iti | arthigrahaṇaṃ pratyarthino 'py upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva vyāsaḥ |

	arthī yatra na vidyeta tatra sākṣī mṛtāntaraḥ |

	pratyarthī vā mṛto yatra tatrāpy evaṃ prakalpayet ||

arthini prathyarthini vā mṛte tadīyaḥ sākṣī mumūrṣuśrāvitad anyo mṛtāntara ity arthaḥ,

	mṛtāntaro 'rthini prete mumūrṣuśrāvitād ṛte |

iti nāradasmaraṇāt | mumūrṣugrahaṇaṃ svasthasyāpy upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva smṛtyantaram |

	śrāvito 'nātureṇāpi yas tv artho dharmasaṃhitaḥ |

	mṛte 'pi tatra sākṣī syāt ṣaṭsu tv anvāhitādiṣu ||

evaṃ ca yad uktaṃ smṛtyartaraṃ (e?),

	nyāsānvāhitavirkrīte hṛte datte 'tha yācite |

	mumūrṣuśrāvitarṇe ca pṛcchet sākṣyaṃ mṛtāntaram

iti, tac chrāvitasya sākṣitvaṃ mṛte 'pi śrāvite 'rthini nāpaitīti jñāpanārtham, na punar mṛtāntarasyāpi kvacit sākṣitvavidhānartham ity avagantavyam, mṛtāntarasya sākṣitvāsaṃbhavāt | 

yathā śrāvitasya sākṣitvaṃ nāpagataṃ tathā sākṣidvaidhe 'py utkṛṣṭakoṭeḥ sākṣitvam akṣatam eva | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	dvaidhe bahūnāṃ vacanaṃ sameṣu guṇināṃ tathā |

	guṇidvaidhe tu vacanaṃ grāhyaṃ ye guṇavattarāḥ ||

saṃgrahakāras tv asyārtham āha |

	bahutvena guṇānāṃ vā tāratamyena niścayaḥ |

	sākṣivipratipattau syāt sarvasāmye pramāṇatā ||

aniścayād asākṣitvaṃ koṭyoḥ viśeṣāgrahaṇ evety arthaḥ | yat tu kātyāyaṇenoktam,

	sākṣiṇāṃ likhitānāṃ tu nirdiṣṭānāṃ ca vādinā |

	teṣām eko 'nyathāvādī bhedāt sarve na sākṣiṇaḥ || 

iti, tatra sarvaśabdenānyathāvādisahitānām eva bahūnām asākṣitvam uktaṃ na punaḥ kevalānām ity avagantavyam, anyathā "dvaidhe bahūnāṃ vacanam" ityādivacanavirodhāt | tathā svayamuktitvenāsākṣitvaṃ mā bhūd iti yena kenacit sākṣinirdeśo na kāryam ity āha sa eva |

	anyena hi kṛtaḥ sākṣī naivānyas taṃ vivādayet |

	tadabhāve niyukto vā bāndhavo vā vivādayet ||

arthī tadīyo vā sākṣiṇaṃ nirdiśen nānya ity arthaḥ | evaṃ cānyena nirdiṣṭo 'nirdiṣṭavad evāsākṣīty avagantavyam | atra prasaṅgād anyad api kiṃcid uktaṃ nāradena |

	dvayor vivadator arthe dvayoḥ satsu ca sākṣiṣu |

	pūrvapakṣo bhaved yasya bhaveyus tasya sākṣiṇaḥ ||

	ādharyaṃ pūrvapakṣasya yasminn arthavaśād bhavet |

	vivāde sākṣiṇas tatra praṣṭavyāḥ prativādinaḥ || iti |

atrodāharaṇam: yatraikaṃ kṣetraṃ pratigraheṇa prāpya bhuktvā tyaktvā deśāntaraṃ sakuṭumbo gataḥ, punar anyena labdhaṃ bhuktaṃ ca, so 'i deśavibhramādinā deśāntaraṃ sakuṭumbo gataḥ | punas tau dvāv api cirantanakālāpagame svavṛttilobhena svasthānam āgatya kṣetravivāde nirṇayārthaṃ dharmasthānaṃ yugapad āgatau, tataikaḥ pratijānīte: "jayaticandrākhyena rājñā svarājyakāle mahyaṃ dattam ity asmadīyam evaitat kṣetram" iti | itaro 'pi prajānīte: "haricandrākhyena rājñā jayaticandākhyasutena rājyārtham abhiṣiktena mahyaṃ dattam asmadīyam evaitat kṣetram" iti | atha vā itarasyaivaṃ pratijñā: "satyaṃ jayaticandreṇāsmai dattaṃ kiṃ tv etasya hastād dharicandreṇa tat kṣetraṃ krayeṇa gṛhītvā mahyaṃ dattam ity asmadīyam eva" iti | santi ca dvayor api vivādinoḥ sākṣiṇaḥ | tatredam uktam "dvayor vivadator arthe" iti | ayam arthaḥ: yasya vivadamānasya pūrvapakṣo bhavet pūrvakālikasya dānasya svatvahetutayopanyāsena pakṣo bhavet tasya sākṣiṇaḥ sabhyaiḥ praṣṭavyā bhaveyur netarasya sākṣiṇaḥ, teṣām uttarakāladanasākṣitvenāsākṣiprāyatvāt | yadā punar itarapratijñātārthavaśenaitasya hastāt krītvā mahyaṃ dattam ityadinā pūrvadānopanyāsapakṣasyādharyam akiṃcitkarataṃ bhavet tadā paścāt pratijānānasya sākṣiṇaḥ praṣṭavyāḥ | na pūrvaṃ pratijānānasya, siddhasādhyatvena vaiyarthyāt | kiṃ tv asākṣivad upakṣaṇīyās ta iti ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām asākṣibhedāḥ **

**atha sākṣyudbhāvanam**

tatra gautamaḥ: "vipratipattau sākṣinimittā satyavyavasthā" iti | tenottarānantaram arthinā sākṣiṇaḥ santi cen nirdeṣṭavyā ity abhiprāyaḥ | te ca nirdiṣṭāḥ sadoṣāś (?) ced dūṣayitavyāḥ | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	sakṣiṇo 'rthisamuddiṣṭān satsu doṣeṣu dūṣayet |

	aduṣṭān dūṣayan vādī tatsamaṃ daṇḍam arhati ||

tasamo duṣṭasākṣidaṇḍasamaḥ | yair dveṣyatvādihetubhir asākṣitvam uktaṃ te sākṣidoṣāḥ | te yady arthinirdiṣṭasakṣiṣu nigūḍhāḥ santi tadā pratyarthinā prakhyāpanīyā ity arthaḥ | yadi punaḥ prakaṭāḥ santi tadā sabhyair eva vaktavyāḥ | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	pramāṇasya hi ye doṣā vaktavyās te vivādinā |

	gūḍhās tu prakaṭāḥ sabhyaiḥ kāle śāstrapradarśanāt ||

	pramāṇasya hi ye doṣā vaktavyās te vivādinā |

	gūḍhās tu prakaṭāḥ sabhyaiḥ kāle śāstrapradarsanāt ||

pramāṇasya pramāṇatayā nirdiṣṭasya kāle nirṇayakāle ity arthaḥ | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	sākṣibhir gaditaiḥ sabhyaiḥ prakrānte nirṇaye tu yaḥ |

	punar vivādaṃ kurute tasya rājā vicārayet ||

gaditair arthinirdiṣṭaiḥ prakaṭadoṣarahitaiḥ sākṣibhir nirṇaye prakrānta ity arthaḥ | prakrāntagrahaṇaṃ nirṇayād ūrdhvaṃ dūṣaṇābhidhānakāla iti pratipādanārtham | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	lekhyadoṣās tu ye kecit sākṣiṇāṃ caiva ye smṛtāḥ |

	vādakāle tu vaktavyāḥ paścād uktān na dūṣayet ||

uktāt paścād dūṣayato daṇḍam āha sa eva |

	nātathyena pramāṇaṃ tu doṣeṇaiva tu dūṣayet |

	mithyābhiyoge daṇḍaḥ syāt sādhyārthāc cāpi hīyate ||

doṣeṇaiva tu dūṣayet na tu guṇābhāvena, tasya vacanaprāmāṇyavighātakāritvābhāvād ity abhiprāyaḥ | at evāpai guṇarahitasyāpi niṣiddhetarasya ṛṇādau sākṣitvam uktam | ato na guṇābhāvodbhāvanamātreṇa ṛṇādau nirdiṣṭasākṣiṇām asākṣitvasiddhiḥ, kiṃ tu dāsatvādiniṣiddhanimittodbhāvanenety avagantavyam | sāhasādau na tenāpi (?) kiṃ tv ajñatvāsatyaśīlatvādidoṣodbhāvanenaivety anusaṃdheyam | ata eva vyāsenāpi doṣodbhāvanenaivāsākṣitvam uktam |

	sākṣidoṣāḥ prayoktavyāḥ saṃsadi prativādinā |

	patre vilikhya tān sarvān vācyāḥ pratyuttaraṃ tu te ||

	pratipattau na sākṣitvam arhanti tu kadācana |

	ato 'nyathā bhāvanīyāḥ kriyayā prativādinā || iti |

pratipattir doṣāṅgīkāraḥ | kriyayā sākṣivyatiriktayeti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	anyais tu sākṣibhiḥ sādhye dūṣaṇe pūrvasākṣiṇām |

	anavasthā bhaved doṣas teṣām apy anyasaṃbhavāt ||

evaṃ prativādinā dūṣaṇapratipādanaṃ na prakaṭe dūṣaṇe kāryam, vaiyarthyāt | kiṃ tu sabhyair eva tathāvidhadūṣaṇaṃ grāhyam ity āha sa eva |

	sabhāsadāṃ prasiddhaṃ yal lokkasiddham athāpi vā |

	sākṣiṇāṃ dūṣaṇaṃ grāhyam asādhyaṃ doṣavarṇanāt ||

grāhyaṃ parīkṣakair iti śeṣaḥ | asādhyaṃ ca prativādinā tatra dūṣaṇam, prasiddhadoṣād varjanasiddher ity arthaḥ | yatra punar aprasiddhaṃ dūṣaṇaṃ kīrtitaṃ tatra tad asādhayato daṇḍam āha sa eva |

	asādhayan damaṃ dāpyaḥ pratyarthī sākṣiṇaḥ sphuṭam |

	bhavitāḥ sākṣiṇo varjyāḥ sākṣidharmanirākṛtāḥ ||

sphuṭaṃ yathā bhavati tathā sākṣidoṣam asādhayann ity arthaḥ | doṣatvena sādhitāḥ sākṣiṇo varjyāḥ, na tu daṇḍyā ity abhiprāyaḥ | varjiteṣu sākṣiṣu yady arthī pramāṇāntaraṃ prati nirākāṅkṣas tadāsau jito daṇḍya ity āha sa eva |

	jitasya vinayaṃ dāpyaḥ śāstradṛṣṭena karmaṇā |

	yadi vādī nirākāṅkṣaḥ sākṣisabhyeṣv avasthitaḥ ||

nirākāṅkṣaḥ pramāṇāntaraṃ pratīti śeṣaḥ | yadā tu sākāṅkṣaḥ tadā mānuṣābhāve divyenāpi jayāvadharaṇaṃ kāryam ity abhiprāyaḥ | yadā tu nirdoṣiṇaḥ sākṣiṇo bhaveyus tadā tair eva jayāvadhāraṇaṃ kāryam | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	sākṣiṇāṃ dūṣaṇe kāyaṃ pūrvaṃ sākṣiviśodhanam |

	śuddheṣu sākṣiṣu tataḥ paścāt kāryaṃ viśodhayet ||

tataḥ śuddhasākṣibhya ity arthaḥ | anena pūrvavyavahāramadhya eva pramāṇadoṣavivādanirṇayaḥ kāryaḥ | na punar vyavahārāntaranirṇayavat pūrvavyavahārasamāptyanantarakāla ity uktam | na ca vyavahāramadhye vyavahārāntaranirṇayasyānucitatvād ayuktam iti vācyam | pramāṇadoṣavivādanirṇayasya pūrvavyavahāraśeṣatvena tatraiva karyatvāt, pṛthakphalābhāvena vyavahārāntaratvābhāvāc ca | tathā ca sa eva |

	lekhyaṃ vā sākṣiṇo vāpi vivāde yasya dūṣitāḥ |

	tasya kāryaṃ na sidhyet tu yāvat tan na viśodhayet ||

vyāso 'pi |

	antaraprabhavo vādaḥ sarvasākṣisamudbhavaḥ |

	na yāti nirṇayaṃ yāvat tāvat pūrvaṃ vivarjayet ||

	pratyarthino 'rthino vāpi sākṣidūṣaṇasādhane |

	na tu sākṣyabhiyogaḥ syād vyavahārāntaraṃ tathā || iti |

ataḥ pramāṇadoṣavivādanirṇayaḥ pūrvavyavahāramadhya eva kartavya iti sthitam |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ sākṣyudbhāvanam**

**atha sākṣiparīkṣā**

tatra kātyāyanaḥ |

	rājā kriyāṃ samāhūya yathānyāyaṃ vicārayet |

	lekhyācāreṇa likhitaṃ sākṣyācareṇa sākṣiṇaḥ || iti |

sākṣyācāreṇa sākṣilakṣaṇajātenety arthaḥ | atra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	praṣṭavyāḥ sākṣiṇo ye tu varjyāś caiva narādhamāḥ |

	tān ahaṃ kathayiṣyāmi sāṃprathaṃ śāstracoditān ||

tatra tāvat praṣṭavyān āha |

	śrautasmārtakriyāyuktāḥ lobhadveṣavivarjitāḥ |

	kulīnāḥ sākṣiṇo 'nindyās tapodānadayānvitāḥ || iti |

tathā varjyān apy āha |

	mātuḥ pitā pitṛvyaś ca bhāryāyā bhrātṛmātulau |

	bhrātā sakhā ca jāmātā sarvavādeṣv asākṣiṇaḥ ||

	parastrīpānasaktāś ca kitavāḥ pūrvadūṣitāḥ |

	unmattārtāḥ sahasikā nāstikāś ca na sākṣiṇaḥ || iti |

etac ca sākṣyasākṣyabhidhānaṃ manunāradādibhir uktānāṃ sākṣiṇām asākṣiṇāṃ ca pardarsanārtham | ata eva śāstracoditān ity uktam | tathā svarādito 'pi sākṣiṇaḥ parīkṣyā ity āha sa eva |

	upasthitāḥ parīkṣyāḥ syuḥ svaravarṇeṅgitādibhiḥ || iti |

tatra ye nirvikārās te vastutaḥ sākṣiṇo bhavanti | ye punaḥ savikārās te kūṭasākṣiṇa ity avagantavyaḥ | ata eva manuḥ |

	bālavṛddhāturāṇāṃ tu sākṣyeṣu vadatāṃ mṛṣā |

	jānīyād asthirāṃ vācam utsiktamanasāṃ tathā ||

utsiktamanasām adhīrāṇām | viṣṇur api: "svabhāvād vikṛtau mukhavarṇavināśe cāsaṃbandhapralāpe kūṭasākṣiṇaṃ vidyāt" iti | nārado 'pi |

	yas tv ātmadoṣaduṣṭatvād asvastha iva lakṣyate |

	sthānāt sthānāntaraṃ gacched ekaikaṃ cānudhāvati ||

	kāsaty akasmāc ca bhṛśam abhīkṣṇaṃ niśvasaty api |

	vilikhaty avanīṃ padbhyāṃ bāhū vāsaś ca dhūnayet ||

	bhidyate mukhavarṇo 'sya lalāṭaṃ svidyate tathā |

	śoṣam āgacchataś cauṣṭhāv ūrdhvaṃ tiryak ca vīkṣate ||

	tvaramāṇa ivātyartham apṛṣṭo bahu bhāṣate |

	kūṭasākṣī sa vijñeyaḥ taṃ pāpaṃ vinayed bhṛsam || iti |

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	deśād deśāntaraṃ yāti sṛkvaṇī parileḍhi ca |

	lalāṭaṃ svidyate yasya mukhaṃ vaivarṇyam eti ca ||

	pariśuṣyatskhaladvākyo viruddhaṃ bahu bhāṣate |

	vākcakṣuḥ pūjayati no tathauṣṭhau nirbhujaty api ||

	svabhāvād vikṛtiṃ gacchet manovākkāyakarmabhiḥ |

	abhiyoge ca sākṣye ca duṣṭaḥ sa parikīrtitaḥ || iti |

evaṃ ca duṣṭacihnavihīnāḥ sākṣilakṣaṇalakṣitāś ca sākṣiṇo yady upasthitās tadā tair nirṇetavyam | atha viparītās tadā pramāṇāntareṇety anusaṃdheyam |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ sākṣiparīkṣā**

**atha sākṣyanuyojanavidhiḥ** 

tatra manuḥ |

	sabhāntaḥ sākṣiṇaḥ sarvān arthipratyarthisaṃnidhau |

	prāḍvivāko 'nuyuñjīta vidhinānena sāntvayan ||

anena vakṣyamāṇena vidhinā sarvān sākṣiṇo 'nuyuñjīta yathārthakathanonmukhān kurvītety arthaḥ | tam eva vidhiṃ darsayati |

	yad dvayor anayor vittha karye 'smin ceṣṭitaṃ mithaḥ |

	tad brūta sarvaṃ satyena yuṣmākaṃ hy atra sākṣitā ||

	samakṣadarśanāt sākṣyaṃ śravaṇāc caiva sidhyati |

	tatra satyaṃ bruvan sākṣī dharmārthābhyāṃ na hīyate ||

	satyaṃ sākṣye bruvan sākṣī lokān āpnoti puṣkalān |

	iha cānuttamām kīrtiṃ vāg eṣā brahmapūjitā ||

	brāhmaṇo vā manuṣyāṇām ādityas tejasām iva |

	śiro vā sarvagātrāṇāṃ dharmāṇāṃ satyam uttamam ||

	satyena pūjate sākṣī dharmaḥ satyena vardhate |

	tasmāt satyaṃ hi vaktavyaṃ sarvavarṇeṣu sākṣibhiḥ ||

	yasya vidvān hi vadataḥ kṣetrajño nātiśaṅkate |

	tasmān na devāḥ śreyāṃsaṃ loke 'smin puruṣaṃ viduḥ || iti |

brāhmaṇo vā brāhmaṇa ivety arthaḥ | evaṃ śiro vety atrāpi vāśabda upamānārtho 'vagantavyaḥ | yasya sākṣyaṃ vadataḥ sākṣiṇaḥ vidvān kṣetrajño natiśaṅkate, tasmāt śreyāṃsam asmin loke devā na vidur ity antyaślokasyārthaḥ | nārado 'pi |

	satyam eva paraṃ dānaṃ satyam eva paraṃ tapaḥ |

	satyam eva paro dharmo lokānām iti naḥ śrutiḥ ||

	satyaṃ devāḥ samāsena manuṣyās tv anṛtaṃ smṛtam |

	ihaiva tasya devatvaṃ yasya satye sthitā matiḥ ||

	nāsti satyāt paro dharmo nānṛtāt pātakaṃ param |

	sākṣidharme viśeṣeṇa satyam eva vaded ataḥ || iti |

vyāso 'pi |

	sākṣibhāve niyuktānāṃ devatā viyati sthitāḥ |

	pitaraś cāvalambante vitathākhyānaśaṅkayā ||

	satyavakyair vrajanty ūrdhvam adho yānty anyathākṛte |

	tasmāt satyaṃ pravaktavyaṃ bhavadbhiḥ sabhyasaṃnidhau || iti |

manur api |

	sākṣye 'nṛtaṃ vadan pāśair badhyate vāruṇair naraḥ |

	vivaśaḥ śatam ājātīs tasmāt sākṣī vaded ṛtam ||

	ātmaiva hy ātmanaḥ sākṣī gatir ātmā tathātmanaḥ |

	māvamaṃsthās tvam ātmānaṃ nṛṇāṃ sākṣiṇam uttamam ||

	manyante vai pāpakṛto na kascit pasyatīti naḥ |

	tāṃs tu devāḥ prapaśyanti yasyaivāntarapūruṣāḥ ||

	dyaur bhūmir āpo hṛdayaṃ candrārkāgniyamānilāḥ |

	rātriḥ saṃdhyā ca dharmaś ca vṛttajñāḥ sarvadehinām || iti |

śatam ājātīḥ satam yāvaj janmāni | nārado 'pi | 

	kuberādityavaruṇaśakravaivasvatādayaḥ |

	paśyanti lokapālāś ca nityaṃ divyena cakṣuṣā ||

tena vañcanāpi na sukarety abhiprāyaḥ | ucathyo 'pi | (?)

	yaḥ sākṣī kauṭasākṣyaṃ tu vivaded bhuvi nirbhayaḥ |

	ubhayoḥ sapta gotrāṇām ashastān nayati dhruvam ||

	saptajanmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ srīre yat tu tiṣṭhati |

	gṛhṇāti tasya sarvasvaṃ yas tu sākṣyaṃ mṛṣā vadet || iti |

bṛhaspatir api |

	kūṭasabhyaḥ kūṭasākṣī brahmahā ca samāḥ smṛtāḥ |

	bhrūṇahā vittahā caiṣāṃ nādhikaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ ||

manur api |

	sākṣī dṛṣṭaśrutād anyad vibruvann āryasaṃsadi |

	avaṅ narakam abhyeti pretya svargāc ca hīyate ||

vasiṣṭho 'pi |

	atha ced anṛtaṃ brūyāt sarvato 'medhyabhakṣaṇam |

	mṛto narakam āyāti tiryag gacchet tv anantaram ||

amedhyabhakṣaṇayutaṃ narakaṃ mṛto gacchatīty arthaḥ | kātyāyano 'pi |

	kālapāśāvṛtagrīvaṃ mudgarāhativihvalam (?) |

	kruddhaḥ kaṇḍakinīṃ bhūmiṃ taṃ nayed yamakiṅkaraḥ ||

	asipatravanāghātaśalalyāliṅganāturāḥ |

	pūyaśoṇitasaṃpūrṇāṃ nadīṃ pāsyanti dāruṇām || iti |

kālapāśāvṛtagrīvaṃ kṛṣṇāyasapāsabaddhagrīvam | nārado 'pi |

	nirayeṣu ca te śaśvaj jihvām utkṛtya dāruṇāḥ |

	asibhiḥ śātayiṣyanti balino yamakiṅkarāḥ ||

	śūle matyān ivākṣipya krośantam aparāyanam |

	avākśirasam utkṣipya kṣepsyanty agnau hradeṣu ca ||

	lohayantrādipīḍābhiḥ kṣutpipāsāsuvihvalaḥ (?) |

	prakṣipyate tathā ghore narake saṃpratāpane || iti |

uśanāpi |

	lohagṛdhramukhotkhātalocanādrīkṛtānanāḥ |

	patiṣyanty andhatāmisre narake pāpamohitāḥ||

pitāmaho 'pi |

	gṛhāntataptasaṃdaṃśajihvātroṭanamūrchitam |

	kiṅkarāḥ pātayiṣyanti mahārauravaraurave ||

vyāso 'pi |

	badhyante vāruṇaiḥ pāśaiḥ sākṣiṇo 'nṛtavādinaḥ |

	ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahasrāṇi tiṣṭhanti narake dhruvam ||

	teṣāṃ varvaśate pūrṇe pāśa ekaḥ pramucyate |

	kāle 'tīte muktapāśaḥ tiryagyoniṣu jāyate || iti |

nārado 'pi |

	api cen narake kalpaṃ vaseyuḥ kūṭasākṣiṇaḥ |

	paravittaharā ye ca rājānaś cāpy adhārmikāḥ ||

	anubhūya ca duḥkhārtāḥ ciraṃ narakavedanām |

	ihāyāsyantyabhavyāsu gṛdhrakākādiyoniṣu || iti |

vasiṣṭho 'pi |

	sūkaro daśavarṣāṇi śatavarṣāṇi gardabhaḥ |

	śvā vai dvādaśavarṣāṇi bhāso varṣāṇi viṃśatiḥ ||

	krimikīṭapataṅgeṣu catvāriṃsat tathaiva ca |

	mṛgastu daśavarṣāṇi jāyate mānavaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

	mānuṣyaṃ tu yad āpnoti mūko 'ndhaś ca bhavet tu saḥ |

	dāridryaṃ tu bhavet tasya punar janmani janmani || iti |

vyāso 'pi |

	mānavo jāyate paścāt saṃparityaktabāndhavaḥ |

	paṅgvandhabadhiro mūkaḥ kuṣṭhī nagnaḥ pipāsitaḥ ||

	bubhukṣitaḥ śatrugṛhe bhikṣate bhāryayā saha |

	jñātvā tv anṛtato doṣān jñātvā satye ca sadguṇān ||

	śreyaskaram (?) ihāmutra satyaṃ sākṣye vaded ataḥ | iti |

evaṃ saṃbodhanam etair eva vacanaiḥ kāryam, na puruṣāntararacitaiḥ | yata āha nāradaḥ |

	paurāṇair dharmavacanaiḥ satyamāhātmyakīrtanaiḥ |

	anṛtasyāpavādaiś ca bhṛśam uttrāsayed api || iti |

ārṣaiḥ sastutikasatyavādavidhivacanaiḥ sākṣiṇāṃ protsāhanam, anṛtapratiṣedhavacanaiḥ duritāpūrvaphalasahitair atyarthaṃ bhīṣaṇam api kuryād ity arthaḥ |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ sākṣyanuyojanavidhiḥ **

**atha sākṣyapraśnavidhiḥ**

tatra manuḥ |

	devabrāhmaṇasāṃnidhye sākṣyaṃ pṛcched ṛtaṃ dvijān |

	udaṅmukhān prāṅmukhān vā pūrvāhṇe vai śuciḥ śucīn ||

dvijān iti sākṣipuruṣopalakṣaṇārtham, upāttaviśeṣaṇatvāt | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	āhūya sākṣiṇaḥ pṛcchen niyamya śapathair bhṛśam |

	samastān viditācārān vijñātārthān pṛthak pṛthak ||

bhayāvahaiḥ śapathaiḥ satyaniṣṭhān kṛtvā pratyekaṃ pṛcched ity arthaḥ | te ca śapathās tena darśitāḥ |

	satyena śāpayed vipraṃ kṣatriyaṃ vāhanāyudhaiḥ |

	gobījakāñcanair vaisyaṃ śūdraṃ sarvais tu pātakaiḥ ||

satyādīṣṭavighātopadarśanena viprādīn, vakṣyamāṇāniṣṭāpattidarśanena śūdraṃ śāpayed ity arthaḥ | praśne tu viśeṣo manunā darśitaḥ |

	brūhīti brāhmaṇaṃ pṛcchet satyaṃ brūhīti pārthivam || iti |

evaṃ cānyathā bruvataḥ satyaṃ te naśyati, ato 'vadhārya brūhīti brāhmaṇe | kṣatriye tu anyathāvadatas tava vāhanāyudhāni viphalāni bhaviṣyanti, ato 'vadhārya satyaṃ brūhīti praśno 'vagantavyaḥ | vaiśye tu praśne viśeṣāsmṛteḥ gobījakāñcanair viyogaḥ syāt yady anyathā bhrūyā ity evaṃ śapathena niyamya yathākāmaṃ pṛcchet | śūdre tu praśnavākyaprakāro manunā prapañcitaḥ |

	brahmaghno ye smṛtā lokāḥ ye ca strībālaghātinaḥ |

	mitradruhaḥ kṛtaghansya te te syur vadato mṛṣā ||

	janmaprabhṛti yat kiṃcit puṇyaṃ bhadra tvayā kṛtam |

	tat te sarvaṃ śuno gacched yati brūyās tvam anyathā ||

	eko 'ham asmīty ātmānaṃ yas tvaṃ kalyāṇa manyase |

	nityaṃ sthitas te hṛdy eṣa puṇyapapekṣitā muniḥ ||

	yamo vaivasvato devo yas tavaiṣa hṛdi sthitaḥ |

	tena ced avivādas te mā gaṅgāṃ mā gukūn gamaḥ  ||

	nago muṇḍaḥ kapālena bhikṣārthī kṣutpipāsitaḥ |

	andhaḥ śatrugṛhaṃ gacchet yaḥ sākṣyam anṛtaṃ vadet ||

	avākchirās tamasy andhe kilbiṣī narakaṃ vrajet |

	yat praśnaṃ vitathaṃ brūyāt pṛṣṭaḥ san dharmaniścaye ||

	andho matsyān ivāśnāti sa naraḥ kaṇṭakaiḥ saha |

	yo bhāṣate 'rthavaikalyam apratyakṣaṃ sabhāṃ gataḥ ||

	yāvato bāndhavān yasmin hanti sākṣye 'nṛtaṃ vadan |

	tāvataḥ saṃkhyayā tasmin śṛṇu saumyānupūrvaśaḥ ||

	pañca paśvanṛte hanti daś hanti gavānṛte |

	śatam aśvānṛte hanti sahasraṃ puruṣānṛte ||

	hanti jātān anjātāṃś ca hiraṇyārthe 'nṛtaṃ vadan |

	sarvaṃ bhūmyanṛte hanti mā sma bhūmyanṛtaṃ vadīḥ ||

	apsu bhūmivad ity āhuḥ strīṇāṃ bhoge ca maithune |

	abjeṣu caiva ratneṣu sarveṣv aśmamayeṣu ca ||

	etān doṣān avekṣya tvaṃ sarvān anṛtabhāṣaṇe |

	yathāśrutaṃ yathādṛṣṭaṃ sarvam evāñjasā vada || iti |

kuruḥ kurukṣetram | añjasā śuddhena hṛdayena | atra kecit: "nagno muṇḍaḥ" ityādiślokatrayam apakṛṣyānuyojanavidhau niveśanīyam, anyathānanvayaḥ syād iti manyante | tadā "mā kurūn gamaḥ" ityabhidhanānantaraṃ "yāvato bāndhavān" ityādyabhidhātavyam ity agantavyam | ayaṃ ca śūdrapraśnavidhir anāpadi hīnavṛttyupajīvināṃ dvijānām api bhavati, teṣām alpaśapathena niyantum aśkyatvāt | ata eva manuḥ |

	gorakṣakān vāṇijakān tathā kārukuśīlavān |

	preṣyān vārduṣikāṃś caiva viprāñ chūdravad ācaret ||

	ye vyapetāḥ svakarmabhyaḥ parapiṇḍopajīvinaḥ |

	dvijatvam abhikāṃkṣanti tāṃś ca śūdravad ācaret ||

dvijatvam abhikāṃkṣantīti (?) vadann advijātīnām ambaṣṭādīnāṃ śūdravad eva praśnavidhiṃ darśayati |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ sākṣyapraśnavidhiḥ**

**atha sākṣyavādavidhiḥ**

tatra kātyāyanaḥ:

	sabhāntasthais tu vaktavyaṃ sākxyaṃ nānyatra sākṣibhiḥ |

	sarvasākṣyeṣv ayaṃ dharmo hy anyatra sthāvareṣu tu ||

anyatra sthāvasyoparīty arthaḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	arthasyopari vaktavyaṃ tayor api vinā kvacit |

	catuṣpadeṣv ayaṃ dharmo dvipadasthāvareṣu ca ||

tayoḥ pūrvoktasthānayoḥ | te sthāne vināpi kvacid vadharūpavivāde sākṣyaṃ vaktavyam ity arthaḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	vadhe vet prāṇināṃ sākṣyaṃ vādayec chivasaṃnidhau |

	tadabhāve tu cihnasya tāny athaiva pravādayet ||

cihnasya sṛṅgādeḥ | sakṣyavādaprakāram āha vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	prāṅmukho 'svasthitaḥ sākṣī śapathaiḥ śāpatiaḥ svakaiḥ |

	hiraṇyaṃ gośakṛd darbhān tān saṃspṛśya vaded ṛtam ||

bṛhaspatir api |

	vihāyopanduṣṇīṣaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ pāṇim uddharet |

	hiraṇyagośakṛddarbhān samādāya ṛtaṃ vadet ||

dakṣiṇaṃ pāṇim uddharet prāvṛtaṃ vastraṃ yajñopavītavat kuryād ity arthaḥ | ṛtaṃ vaded ity asya kvacd viṣaye 'pavādam āha manuḥ |

	śūdraviṭkṣatraviprāṇāṃ yathokte tu bhaved vadhaḥ |

	tatra vaktavyam anṛtaṃ tad dhi satyād viśiṣyate ||

bṛhaspatir api |

	sakṛt pramādāparādhivipraṃ vyāpadi pīḍitam |

	bhaṭādibhir vidhyamānaṃ rakṣed uktvānṛtāny api ||

apiśabdād atrāpy anṛtoktyā kiṃcid pāpaṃ bhavatīti gamyate | ata eva prāyaścittam āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	varṇināṃ hi vadho yatra tatra sākṣyam anṛtaṃ vadet |

	tatpāvanāya nirvāpyaḥ caruḥ sārasvato dvijaiḥ ||

manur api |

	vāgdevatyais tu carubhir yajeraṃs te sarasvatīm |

	anṛtasyainasas tatra kurvāṇāḥ niṣkṛtiṃ parām ||

	kūśmāṇḍair vātha juhuyāt ghṛtam agnau yathavidhi |

	udityṛcā vā vāruṇyā tṛcenābdevatena vā || iti |

viṣṇur api: "tatpāvanāya kūśmāṇḍībhir dvijo 'gnau juhuyāt | śūdraś caikāhikaṃ godaśakasya grāsaṃ dadyāt" iti | yat tv gautamenoktam, "nānṛtavacane doṣo jīvanaṃ cet tadadhīnam" iti, yad api vyāsena:

	na narmayuktaṃ vacanaṃ hinasti na strīṣu nityaṃ na vivāhakāle |

	prāṇātyaye sarvadhanāpahāre pañcānṛtāny āhur apātakāni ||

iti, tayor ayam arthaḥ: "sākṣidharme viśeṣeṇa" ityādibhir vacanair yad adhikapātakam uktam, tad atra nāstīti | anyatra asty eva | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "nāsamavetāḥ pṛṣṭāḥ prabrūyur avacane na doṣiṇaḥ syuḥ" iti | caśabdād anṛtavacane cety avagamya ity uktaṃ vyākhyātṛbhiḥ | asamavetapratiṣedhaḥ samavetānāṃ sākṣibhāva eva na sarvatra | ata āha vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	samavetais tu yad dṛṣṭaṃ vaktavyaṃ tu tathaiva tat |

	vibhinnenaiva yat kāryaṃ vaktavyaṃ tat pṛthak pṛthak ||

	bhinnakāle tu yat kāryaṃ jñātaṃ vā yatra sākṣibhiḥ |

	ekaikaṃ vādayet tatra vidhir eṣa prakīrtitaḥ || iti

atha sākṣivacoviṣayāṇi kānicit vacanāni likhyante | tatra kātyāyanaḥ |

	svabhāvoktaṃ vacas teṣāṃ grāhyaṃyad doṣavarjitam |

	ukte tu sākṣiṇo rājñā na praṣṭavyāḥ punaḥ punaḥ ||

	svabhāvenaiva yad brūyuḥ yad grāhyaṃ vyāvahārikam |

	ato yad anyad vibrūyur dharmārthaṃ yad apārthakam ||

nārado 'py apārtham āha |

	nirdiṣṭeṣv arthajāteṣu sākṣī cet sākṣya āgate |

	na brūyād akṣarasamaṃ na tan nigaditaṃ bhavet ||

sākṣya āgate sakṣyavādāvasare akṣarasamam akṣarānurūpaṃ pṛṣṭārtham iti yāvat | anenāpṛṣṭārthasamarpakam apārtham ity uktam | evaṃ pṛṣṭārthanyūnādhikārthaṃ ca vyartham, tathā ca sa eva |

	ūnam abhyadhikaṃ vārthaṃ (?) vibrūyur yatra sākṣiṇaḥ |

	tad apy anuktaṃ vijñeyam eṣa sākṣividhiḥ smṛtaḥ ||

yatra ṛṇādisthiraprāyavivādeṣv ity arthaḥ | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	ṛṇādiṣu vivādeṣu sthiraprāyeṣu niścitam |

	ūne vāpy adhike vārthe prokte sādhyaṃ na sidhyati ||

yāvat pratijñātārthasādhanārtham uddiṣṭaṃ sākṣivākyam ūnādhikaṃ cet saṃdehāpādakam eva , na punaḥ pratijñātārthaikadeśasādhanārtham uddiṣṭaṃ sākṣivākyam api tato nyūnādhikaṃ cet evam evāpramāṇam ity etasmād eva vacanād avagantavyam, sādhyaṃ na sidhyatīti sāmānyenābhidhānāt | asthirakarmasu punaḥ sidhyaty eva sādhyam ity āha sa eva |

	sādhyārthāṃśe 'pi gadite sākṣibhiḥ sakalaṃ bhavet |

	strīsaṃgrahe sāhase caurya yat sādhyaṃ parikalpitam ||

yat punaḥ tenoktam,

	ūnadhikaṃ tu yatra syāt tat sākṣyaṃ tatra varjayet |

	sākṣī tatra na daṇḍyaḥ syād abruvan daṇḍam arhati ||

tat sthirakarmaviṣayam | evaṃ nirdiṣṭārthaikadesavisaṃvāde 'pi viphalaṃ sākṣivacanam ity āha sa eva |

	deśaṃ kālaṃ dhanaṃ saṃkhyāṃ rūpaṃ jātyākṛtī vayaḥ |

	visaṃvaded yatra sākṣye tad anuktaṃ vidur budhāḥ ||

nārado 'pi |

	deśakālavayodravyapramāṇākṛtijātiṣu |

	yatra vipratipattiḥ syāt sākṣyaṃ tad api viplutam ||

evaṃ ca, ṛṇādau sthirakarmaṇi anyūnātiriktaṃ pṛṣṭārthasamarpakaṃ sākṣivacanaṃ pramāṇaṃ nānyad ity anusaṃdheyam | ata eva vyāsaḥ |

	kālākṛtivayodravyadesajātipramāṇataḥ |

	anyūnaṃ cen nigaditaṃ siddhaṃ sādhyam vinirdiśet ||

bṛhaspatir api |

	yatrāśeṣaḥ pratijñārthaḥ sākṣibhiḥ prativarṇitaḥ |

	sa jayī syād anyathā tu sadhyārthaṃ na samāpnuyāt ||

prativarṇitaḥ satyatveneti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	yasyocuḥ sākṣiṇaḥ satyāṃ pratijñāṃ sa jayī bhavet |

	anyathā vādino yasya dhruvas tasya parājayaḥ ||

sākṣiṇaḥ sarve yasya vādinaḥ prativādino vā pratijñāṃ sādhyoktiṃ satyāṃ ūcur ity arthaḥ | yasya punaḥ pratijñāṃ kecit sākṣiṇaḥ satyām ūcuḥ, kecit tv anyathā tatrāha manuḥ |

	bahutvaṃ parigṛhṇīyāt sākṣidvaidhe narādhipaḥ |

	sameṣu ca guṇōtkṛṣṭān guṇidvaidhe dvijottamān ||

nārado 'pi |

	sākṣivipratipattau tu pramāṇaṃ bahavo matāḥ |

	tatsāmye śucayo grāhyāḥ tatsāmye smṛtimattarāḥ ||

	smṛtimatsākṣisāmyaṃ tu vivāde yatra dṛśyate |

	sūkṣmatvāt sākṣidharmasya sākṣyaṃ vyāvartayet tataḥ || iti |

śucigrahaṇaṃ gṛhasthatvādiguṇavatām upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva yājñavalkyaḥ |

	dvaidhe bahūnāṃ vacanaṃ sameṣu guṇināṃ tathā |

	guṇidvaidhe tu vacanaṃ grāhyaṃ ye guṇavattarāḥ ||

atra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	likhite sākṣivāde ca saṃdeho jāyate yadā |

	anumāne ca saṃbhrānte tatra daivaṃ viśodhanam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ sākṣiviṣayāṇi **

**athānyāny api sākṣiviṣayāṇī kānicid vacanāni likhyante**

tatra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	na dadāti hi yat sākṣyaṃ jānann api narādhamaḥ |

	sa kūṭasākṣiṇāṃ pāpais tulyo daṇḍena caiva hi ||

yo vipratipannam arthaṃ paramārthato jānann api daurātmyāt sākṣyaṃ nāṅgīkaroti asau kūṭasākṣivat pāpī daṇḍyaś cety arthaḥ | nārado 'pi |

	śrāvayitvā tato 'nyebhyaḥ sākṣitvaṃ yo vinihnute |

	sa vineyo bhṛśataraṃ kūṭasākṣyadhiko hi saḥ ||

yadā pūrvam ahaṃ sākṣīti srāvitaḥ sākṣiṇām āgamanakāle ahaṃ na sākṣīty apalapati asāv atyarthaṃ daṇḍya ity arthaḥ | bṛhaspatir api |

	ahūto yas tu nāgacchet sākṣī rogavivarjitaḥ |

	ṛṇaṃ damaṃ ca dāpyaḥ syāt tripakṣāt paratas tu saḥ ||

vasiṣṭho 'pi |

	yaḥ sākṣī naiva nirdiṣṭo nāhūto naiva coditaḥ |

	brūyān mithyeti tathyaṃ vā daṇḍyaḥ so 'pi narādhamaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ |

	apṛṣṭaḥ sarvavacane pṛṣṭasyākathane tathā | 

	sākṣiṇaḥ saṃniroddhavyāḥ garhyā daṇḍyāś ca dharmataḥ ||

	vākpāruṣye chale vāde dāpyāḥ syus triśataṃ damam |

	ṛṇādivādeṣu dhanaṃ te syur dāpyā ṛṇaṃ tathā || iti |

dhanaṃ daṇḍadhanam | ta ity saranāmnā praśnasyottaram akathayanta eva pratyavamṛśyante, teṣām atyarthaṃ prakṛtatvāt | ata evāha sa eva |

	sākṣī sākṣyaṃ na ced brūyāt samadaṇḍaṃ vahed ṛṇam |

	ato 'nyeṣu vivādeṣu triśataṃ daṇḍam arhati ||

anyeṣu ṛṇādito 'nyeṣv ity arthaḥ (?) | tathā ca manuḥ |

	tripakṣād abruvan sākṣyam ṛṇādiṣu naro 'gadaḥ |

	tad ṛṇaṃ prāpnuyāt sarvaṃ dasabandhaṃ ca sarvataḥ ||

agadaḥ svasthaḥ, tad ṛṇaṃ sākṣirūpapramāṇasādhyaṃ dhanam, sarvaṃ savṛddhikaṃ prāpnuyāt dāpya ity arthaḥ | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	abruvan hi naraḥ sākṣyam ṛṇaṃ sadaśabandhakam |

	rājñā sarvaṃ pradāpyaḥ syāc chaṭcatvāriṃśattame 'hani || (??)

daśabandhaśabdhena daśamoṃśa ucyate | sa ca daṇḍatvād rājñā grāhyam ity uktaṃ vyākhyātṛbhiḥ | atrādhamarṇena na kiṃcid dātavyam, tad deyam eva abruvan sākṣī dāpya iti pūrvavacanasya tātparyārthatvāt | na cābruvatā sākṣiṇā svena dattam adharmaṇato grāhyam, svāparādhena dattatvāt | ṣaṭcatvāriṃśattame 'hanīti grahaṇāt tato vārbruvan (?) na dāpya iti gamyate | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	samyakkriyāparijñāne deyaḥ kālas tu sākṣiṇam |

	saṃdigdhaṃ yatra sākṣyaṃ tu sadyaḥ spaṣṭaṃ vivādayet ||

evaṃ ca yad uktaṃ tena,

	na kālaharaṇaṃ kāryaṃ rājñā sākṣiprabhāṣaṇe |

	mahān doṣo bhavet kālād dharmavyāvṛttilakṣaṇaḥ || 

iti, tat spaṣṭasākṣiviṣayam ity avagantavyam, saṃdigdhasākṣye kāladānavidhānāt | yaḥ punaḥ sākṣī praśnavākyaṃ śrāvitaḥ san vādakāle rāgadveṣāndho nāham atra sākṣī bhavamīti svasākṣitvam apalapati tasya daṇḍam āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	yaḥ sākṣyām śrāvito 'nyebhyo nihnute tat tamovṛtaḥ |

	sa dāpyo 'ṣṭaguṇaṃ daṇḍaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ tu vivāsayet ||

vivādād ity anuṣajyate | tena vivādaparājayo daṇḍaḥ, tam aṣṭaguṇaṃ dāpya ity artho 'vagantavyaḥ | vivāsayed ity asya nagnīkaraṇaṃ gṛhabhaṅgaḥ, svarāṣṭrabahiṣkāro vārthaḥ | atra tu daṇḍāvivṛddhisāhacaryāt svarāṣṭrabahiṣkārarūpo 'rthaḥ pratyetavyaḥ | kātyāyanasmṛtyā sākṣyaṃ punar anyathā punar anyathā bruvāṇā api sākṣiṇo daṇḍyā ity āha |

	uktvānyathā bruvāṇāś ca daṇḍyāḥ syur vākchalānvitāḥ | iti |

gautamas tu prathamata eva "anyathā bruvāṇo garhyo daṇḍyś ca" ity āha | "mithyāvacane dāpyo daṇḍyas ca sākṣye" iti | yājñavalkyas tv evaṃvidhasākṣiṇo daṇḍe viśeṣam āha |

	pṛthak pṛthag daṇḍanīyāḥ kūṭakṛt sākṣiṇas tathā |

	vivādād dviguṇaṃ daṇḍaṃ vivāsyo brāhmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

kṛṭaṃ sākṣyaṃ kurvann iti kūṭakṛtaḥ mithyāvādina iti yāvat | te rājñā pṛthak pṛthag daṇḍanīyāḥ | vivādaparājayanibandhanadamāt dviguṇaṃ damam ity arthaḥ | vivāsyo brāhmaṇa ity aviśeṣeṇokte 'pi yatra kṣatriyādīnām alpadhanena dviguṇo damaḥ sampadyate, tatra brāhmaṇasya nagnīkaraṇarūpavivasanaṃ daṇḍaḥ | yatra tu bahudhanena kṣatriyādīnām, tatra svarāṣṭrabahiṣkārarūpavivāsanaṃ brāhmaṇasyeti mantavyam, daṇḍatāratamyasya doṣatāratamyānuvidhāyitvāt | ata eva manunānṛtabījanibandhanadoṣatāratamyānusāreṇa daṇḍavaicitryam uktam |

	lobhān mohād bhayān maitrāt kāmāt krodhāt tathaiva ca |

	ajñānād bālabhāvāc ca sākṣyaṃ vitatham ucyate ||

	teṣām anyatame sthāne yaḥ sākṣyam anṛtaṃ vadet |

	tasya daṇḍaviśeṣāṃs tu pravakṣyāmy anupūrvaśaḥ ||

	lobhāt sahasraṃ daṇḍyas tu mohāt pūrvaṃ tu sāhasam |

	bhayād vai madhyamo daṇḍo maitrāt pūrvaṃ caturguṇam ||

	kāmād daśaguṇaṃ pūrvaṃ krodhāt tu triguṇaṃ param |

	ajñānāt dve śate pūrṇe bāliśyāc chatam eva tu ||

	etān āhuḥ kauṭasākṣye proktān daṇḍān manīṣiṇaḥ || iti \

lobho 'rthapartavam | mohaḥ samyakpra**rthānavadhāraṇam | bhayam aniṣṭaprāptiśaṅkā | maitrī snehātisayaḥ | kāmo rativiṣayābhilāṣaḥ | krodho 'marṣaḥ | ajñānaṃ samakṣadarśanaśravaṇasamaya evānyathājñānam | bāliśyam aprāptabuddhisthairyam | atra lobhabhayamaitranimittānṛte tulyadoṣe vacobhaṅgyottamasāhasa uktaḥ | kāmato 'nṛte tu tato doṣabāhulyāt sārdhottamasāhasadvayam uktam | krodhanimitte punas tato 'pi doṣabāhulyād uttamasāhasatrikam uttamam | mohe tv alpadoṣatvāt prathamasāhasa uktaḥ | ajñāne tu tato 'lpadoṣatvāt kārṣāpaṇaśatadvitayam uktam | bāliśye punas tato 'py alpadoṣatvāt tadartham evoktam iti mantavyam | idaṃ ca daṇḍavaicitryaṃ brāhmaṇasyāpi kūṭasākṣiṇo jñeyam "etān āhuḥ kauṭasākṣye" (MDh 8.122) ity aviśeṣasmṛteḥ | 

	kauṭasākṣyaṃ tu kurvāṇāṃs trīn varṇān dhārmiko nṛpaḥ |

	pravāsayed daṇḍayitvā brāhmaṇaṃ tu vivāsayet || iti |

kauṭasākṣyāvṛttiviṣaye brāhmaṇasya viśeṣasmaraṇāc ca | kaḥ punar atra viśeṣaḥ | na tāvad daṇḍayitvā pravāsanaṃ kṣatriyādeḥ | brāhmaṇasya tu pravāsanamātram iti viseṣo yuktaḥ, sakṛt kṛte 'pi kauṭasākṣye brāhmaṇasya yājñavalkyena pravāsanavidhānāt abhyāse 'dhikadaṇḍānuktiprasakteḥ | ato yat kaiścid uktaṃ tusabdo brāhmaṇe dhanadaṇḍanivṛttyartha iti, tad apāstam | kathaṃ tarhi brāhmaṇe daṇḍaviśeṣa uktaḥ (?) | ucyate | pravāsaśabdenātra dantachandcchedanaṃ (?) jihvācchedo māraṇaṃ cocyate | vivāsaśabdena tu nagnīkaraṇādikam | tena daṇḍayitvety asyānuṣaṅge 'pi viśeṣoktir yuktā | pravāsanavivāsanāvāntarabhedād dantacchadaddhedādayo nagnīkaraṇādayaś ca kauṭasākṣyaviṣayānusāreṇābhyāsasaṃkhyāvivṛddhyanusāreṇa canusaṃdhātavyāḥ | anavadhāritahetuke kauṭasākṣye sakṛt kṛte "pṛthak pṛthak" ityadivacanokto yājñavalkīyo daṇḍaḥ, anyatra mānava iti cānusaṃdheyam | yat punar viṣṇunoktam "kūṭasākṣiṇāṃ sarvasvāpahāraḥ kāryaḥ" iti, tad bhūmyanṛtaviṣayam iti kaiścid uktam, śūdrādyasharmajātiviṣayaṃ vā draṣṭavyam | kūṛasākṣigrahaṇaṃ tannirdesakasyāpi pradarśanārtham | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	yena kāryasya lobhena nirdiṣṭāḥ kūṭasākṣiṇaḥ |

	gṛhītvā tasya sarvasvaṃ kuryān nirviṣayaṃ tataḥ ||

nirviṣayaṃ svadeśān nirvāsanam | yena punaḥ nirdiṣṭasākṣiṇāṃ kūṭatvāyodyamaḥ kṛtaḥ sa hīno bhavatīty āha nāradaḥ |

	na pareṇa samuddiṣṭam upeyāt sākṣiṇaṃ rahaḥ |

	bhedayeta na cānyena hīyetaivaṃ samācaran ||

tena tathā carantaṃ hīnadaṇḍena daṇḍayed ity abhiprāyaḥ | evaṃ kūṭasākṣiṇaṃ tan nirdeśakaṃ daṇḍayitvā ca kūṭasākṣivacanān nirṇītaṃ kāryaṃ nivartanīyam | tathā ca manuḥ |

	yasmin yasmin vivāde tu kauṭasākṣyaṃ kṛtaṃ bhavet |

	tat tat kāryaṃ nivarteta kṛtaṃ cāpy akṛtaṃ bhavet ||

kasmin punaḥ kārye kauṭasākṣyaṃ bhavatīty apekṣite yājñavalkyaḥ |

	ukte 'pi sākṣibhiḥ sākṣye yady anye guṇavattarāḥ |

	dviguṇā vānyathā brūyuḥ kūṭāḥ syuḥ pūrvasākṣiṇaḥ ||

asyārthaḥ: yatrārthinā saṃnihitā asaṃnihitāś ca bahavaḥ sākṣiṇo nirdiṣṭāḥ, tatrāsaṃnihitānayane kleśam ālocya yadā saṃnihitair evālam ity aṅgīkṛtya tadvacanān nirṇītam arthinaḥ parājaya iti taṃ ca parājayaṃ kauṭasākṣyanibandhanam iti manyamāno 'rthī punaḥ pūrvam uddiṣṭān asaṃnihitān saṃnihitebhyo guṇavattarān dviguṇān vānīya vijayī bhavati, tadā pūrvasaṃnihitāḥ sākṣiṇaḥ kūṭāḥ syur iti | kātyāyano 'pi |

	yatra vai bhāvitaṃ kāryaṃ sākṣibhir vādinā bhavet |

	prativādī yadā tatra bhāvayet kāryam anyathā ||

	bahubhiś ca kulīnair vā pūrvāḥ syuḥ kūṭasākṣiṇaḥ | iti |

asyārthaḥ: arthinā nirdiṣṭeṣu sākṣiṣv arthipakṣānukūlam abhihitavatsu yadā pratyarthī saṃkhyayā guṇair vādhikān sākṣiṇaḥ pūrvoktaviparītaṃ vādayati, tadārthisākṣiṇaḥ kūṭāḥ syur iti | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca ekasmin vyavahāre katham arthipratyarthinoḥ sākṣisaṃbhavaḥ, 

	na caikasmin vivāde tu kriyā syād vādinor dvayoḥ | (KSm 190)

iti pratiṣiddhatvāt | ata eva "yatra vai bhāvitam" ityādivacanasya punar bādhaviṣayatvam āśrīyate | tena na kaścid virodhaḥ | ekasya sākṣitvaviṣaye tu manur āha |

	yasya dṛśyeta saptāhād uktavākyasya sākṣiṇaḥ |

	rogo 'gnir jñātimaraṇam ṛṇaṃ dāpyo damaṃ ca saḥ ||

saptāhāvadhikaṃ daivikavyasanodbhāvenaikasya sākṣiṇaḥ parīkṣaṇaṃ kartavyam ity arthaḥ | etac ca parīkṣaṇaṃ dūtakādeḥ sākṣiṇaḥ kāryam, na punar guṇānvitasya nṛpādhyakṣyor vā, tatraikaikasyāpy anṛtasaṃbhāvanāsaṃbhavāt | ata eva vyāsaḥ |

	maṇimantrauṣadhibalāt pradattaṃ cāvidhānataḥ |

	visaṃvaded divyam api na tu sākṣī guṇānvitaḥ ||

ata eva bṛhaspatinā dūtakādeḥ nṛpādhyakṣayoḥ vyavadhānaṃ kṛtam |

	sūtako ghaṭikāgrāhī kāryamadhyagatas tathā |

	eka eva pramāṇaṃ syān nṛpo 'dhyakṣas tathaiva ca || iti |

ghaṭikāgrāhī gaṇakaḥ | itarau kātyāyanena darsitau |

	abhyantaras tu nikṣepe sākṣyam eko 'pi vācyate |

	arthinā prahitaḥ sākṣī bhavaty eko 'pi dūtakaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ sākṣiviṣayāṇi **

**sākṣiprakaraṇaṃ samāptam**

**athāsākṣipratyayāḥ** 

tatra nāradaḥ |

	asākṣipratyayās tv anye ṣaḍvivādāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |

	lakṣaṇāny eva sākṣitvam eṣām āhur manīṣiṇaḥ ||

agnidatvādivivādeṣūlkāhastatvādicihnāny eva sākṣikaryaṃkurvantīty arthaḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	ulkāhasto 'gnido jñeyaḥ sastrapāṇis ca ghātukaḥ |

	keśākeśī gṛhītaś ca yugapatparadārikaḥ ||

	kuddālapāṇir vijñeyaḥ setubhettā samīpagaḥ |

	tathā kuṭhārapāṇis tu vanacchettā prakīrtitaḥ ||

	pratyagracihnair vijñeyo daṇḍapāruṣyakṛn naraḥ |

	asākṣipratyayā hy ete pāruṣye tu parīkṣaṇam || iti |

pratyagracihnaiḥ nūtanakṣatādibhiḥ | asākṣiprayayāḥ vināpi sākṣibhiś cihnair eva vigatasaṃśayāḥ, pāruṣye tu parīkṣaṇaṃ daṇḍapāruṣye kṛtrimacihnavivekāya parīkṣaṇaṃ kartavyam ity arthaḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	kaś cit kṛtvātmanaś cihnaṃ dveṣāt param upadravet |

	yuktihetvarthasaṃbandhais tatra yuktaṃ parīkṣaṇam ||

tatra pāruṣya ity arthaḥ | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanv</span> idam anarthakaṃ vacaḥ,

	talavad dṛśyate vyoma khadyto havyavāḍ iva |

	na talaṃ vidyate vyomni na khadyoto hutāśanaḥ ||

	tasmāt pratyakṣadṛṣṭe 'pi yuktam arthaṇ parīkṣitum |
