	parīkṣya jñāpayann arthān adharmāt parihīyate ||

iti, ulkāhastādau sarvatra parīkṣaṇasya tenaiva vihitatvāt |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | tatraivopāyavidhānārthaṃ parīkṣaṇam anūdyata ity adoṣaḥ | evaṃ cauryavivādo 'pi kācid asākṣipratyayo 'vagantavyaḥ | tathā va śaṅkhalikhitau: "keśākeśī saṅgrahaṇāt pāradārikaḥ ulkāhasto 'gnidaḥ śastrapāṇir ghatukaḥ loptrahastaś coraḥ" iti | loptram apahṛtaikadeśādiliṅgam, atrāpi parīkṣaṇaṃ kāryam | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	yāty acoro 'pi coratvaṃ coraś cāyāty acoratām |

	acoraś coratāṃ prāpto māṇḍavyo vyavahārataḥ || iti |

ataḥ parīkṣaṇam āvaśyakam ity abhiprāyaḥ | ata eva bṛhaspatiḥ |

	likhite sākṣivāde ca saṃdeho yatra jāyate |

	anumāne ca saṃbhrānte tatra daivaṃ viśodhanam ||

anumānam ulkhāhastatvādiyuktiḥ |

	anumānaṃ vidur hetus tarkaś ceti manīṣiṇaḥ |

iti vyāsasmaraṇāt ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām sākṣipratyayāḥ **

**atha divyanirūpaṇam**

tatra pitāmahaḥ |

	yasmin yasmin vivāde tu sākṣiṇāṃ nāsti saṃbhavaḥ |

	sāhaseṣu viśeṣeṇa tatra divyāni dāpayet ||

sākṣigrahaṇaṃ mānuṣapramāṇopalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva yājñavalkyaḥ |

	pramāṇaṃ likhitaṃ bhuktḥ sākṣiṇaś ceti kīrtitam |

	teṣām anyatamābhāve divyānyatamam ucyate ||

eṣām anyatamābhāva iti yuktyabhāvasyāpy upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	yuktiṣv asamarthāsu śapathair eva nirṇayet |

	arthakālabalāpekṣam agnyambusukṛtādibhiḥ ||

arthāpekṣaṃ siṣādhayipitārthālpatvamahattvarūpam ity arthaḥ | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

	arthānurūpāḥ śapathāḥ smṛtāḥ satyadhaṭādayaḥ || iti |

tatrārthālpatvānurūpāḥ satyādaya ity āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	satyaṃ vāhaśastrāṇi gobījakanakāni ca |

	devabrāhmaṇapādāś ca putradāraśirāṃsi ca ||

	ete tu śapathāḥ proktāḥ svalpe 'rthe sukarāḥ sadā || iti |

svalpe 'rthe iti svalpapīḍāyā ap siṣādhayiṣitāyāḥ pradarśaṇārtham | ata eva sāmānyenoktaṃ nāradena |

	satyaṃ vāhanaśastrāṇi gobījakanakāni ca |

	devatāpitṛpādāś ca dattāni sukṛtāni ca |

	ity ete śapathāḥ proktāḥ manunā svalpakāraṇe || iti |

svalpakāraṇe svalpāparādha ity arthaḥ | sukṛtāni ceti caśabdenānye 'pi lokaprasiddhāḥ śapathāḥ saṃgṛhyante | ata eva śaṅkhalikhitau "iṣṭāpūrtapradānam anyāṃś ca śapathān kārayet" iti | yat punar nāradenoktam,

	kāraṇe mahati proktaṃ divyaṃ vādārthināṃ nṛṇām |

iti, yad api pitāmahena,

	mahāparādhe divyāni dāpayet pṛthivīpatiḥ |

iti, tat tulādidivyaviṣayam | yad āha yājñavalkyaḥ,

	tulāgnyāpo viṣaṃ kośo divyānīha viśuddhaye |

	mahābhiyogeṣv etāni śīrṣakasthe 'bhiyoktari || iti |

agniśabdena taptāyaḥpiṇḍas taptamāṣas taptaphālaṃ ca nirdisyate sāmānyenābhidhānāt | tena taptamāṣaphāle apy asmād eva vacanāt mahābhiyoge śīrṣakasthe cābhiyoktari vihite iti boddhavyam | śīrṣakaṃ vivādaparājayanibandhano daṇḍaḥ, vyavahāraśirasthānīyatvāt, tatra tiṣṭhatīti śīrṣakasthaḥ | etad uktaṃ bhavati "na mahābhiyogamātre tulādīni bhavanti, kiṃ tu yatraitasya jaye 'ham itthaṃ daṇḍya iti śarīradaṇḍam arthadaṇḍaṃ vā mithyābhiyogino vihitam abhiyoktā svakṛtābhiyogadārḍhyakhyāpanāyāṅgīkurute tatraiva, iti | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	śirovartī yadā na syāt tadā divyaṃ na dīyate | iti |

śirovartī yadā na syād abhiyoktety śeṣaḥ | tathā ca pitāmahaḥ |

	abhiyoktā śirasthāne divyeṣu parikalpyate |

	abhiyuktāya datavyaṃ divyaṃ srutinidarśanāt ||

divyaṃ dhaṭādipañcakeṣv anyatamam, "etāni" iti yājñavalkyena viśeṣitatvāt | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	yathāvidhānena sadā pañca divyāni dharmataḥ |

	dadad rājābhiyuktānāṃ pretya ceha ca nandati ||

anena abhiyoktṝṇām etāni divyāni bhavantīty arthād uktam | uktaṃ ca kātyāyanena |

	na kāścid abhiyoktāraṃ divyeṣu viniyojayet |

	abhiyuktāya dātavyaṃ divyaṃ divyaviśāradaiḥ ||

kaścit sabhāpatyādiḥ | divyaviśāradāḥ prāḍvivākādayaḥ | anenārthipratyarthinor anyatarecchayā divyāṅgīkāre nāyaṃ niyama ity arthād uktam | uktaṃ ca yājñavalkyena |

	rucyā vānyataraḥ kuryād itaro varatec chiraḥ | iti |

nāradenāpy uktam |

	abhiyoktā śirasthāne sarvatraiva prakalpitaḥ |

	icchayā tv itaraḥ kuryād itaro vartayec chiraḥ ||

sarvatra śirovati divyapañcaka ity arthaḥ | abhiyuktasya śirovartanam anapalāpadārḍhyakhyāpanārtham | ata eva etasya jaye 'ham itthaṃ daṇḍya ity apalāpino vihitadaṇḍāṅgīkaraḥ | tathā kvacid viṣaye na ko 'pi śiro vartayed ity āha sa eva |

	śiro'vasthāyini nare abhiyoktary upasthite |

	divyapradānam ucitam anyatra nṛpaśāsanāt ||

nṛpaśāsanāt nṛpājñayā tv aśirāṃsy api dhaṭādīni bhavanti | tathā ca sa eva |

	aśirāṃsi ca divyāni rājā bhṛtyeṣu dāpayet | iti |

yājñavalkyas tv aparādhaviśeṣe śiro'vasthānaniyamasyāpy apavādam āha |

	vināpi śīrṣakāt kuryāt nṛpadrohe 'tha pātake |

śīrṣakāt śīrṣakavartanād ity arthaḥ | tathā viṣṇuḥ: "rājadrohasāhaseṣu vinā śīrṣakavartanāt" iti | tulādīni niyojyānīti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	pārthivaiḥ śaṅkitānāṃ tu tulādīni niyojayet |

	ātmaśuddhvidhāne ca na śiras tatra kalpayet ||

	lokāpavādaduṣṭānāṃ śaṅkitānāṃ ca sasyubhiḥ |

	tulādīni niyojyāni na śiras tatra vai bhṛguḥ || iti |

dasyubhiḥ saha vāsena śaṅkitānām ity arthaḥ | yat punas tenoktam,

	na śaṅkāsu śiraḥ kośe kalpayet tu kadācana |

iti, tac chaṅkābhiyoge kośasya ṛṇādāv apy aśiras tv aniyamārtham, kadācanety abhidhānāt | śaṅkābhiyoge ca kośo vyāsenābhihitaḥ |

	dhaṭo 'gnir viṣatoyaṃ ca pramāṇaṃ tu caturvidham |

	daivikasya prabhedo 'yaṃ kośaḥ śaṅkāsu pañcamaḥ ||

śaṅkāsv iti viśvāsādīnāṃ pradarśanārtham | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	śaṅkāviśvāsasaṃdhāne vibhāge rikthināṃ sadā |

	kriyāsamūhakartṛtve kośam eva pradāpayet ||

pitāmaho 'pi |

	visrambhe sarvaśaṅkāsu saṃdhikārye tathaiva ca |

	eṣu kośaḥ pradātavyo nityaṃ cittaviśuddhaye ||

kośaḥ śirorahita iti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	śiraḥsthāyivihīnāni divyāni parivarjayet |

	dhaṭādīni viṣāntāni kośa eko 'śirāḥ smṛtaḥ ||

śaṅkābhiyogādiviṣaya iti śeṣaḥ | mahātattvābhiyoge kośo 'pi śiraḥsthāyivihīno varjya eva | "śīrṣakasthe 'bhiyoktari" iti pañcadivyaśeṣatayā yājñavalkyenoktatvāt | mahātattvādiyogeṣv api rājaprāḍvivāketarasabhāyāṃ tu na dhaṭādidivyapañcake śiraḥkalpanam asti | 

	vāgdaṇḍo dhigdamaś caiva viprāyattāv ubhau smṛtau |

	arthadaṇḍavadhāv uktau rājāyattāv ubhāv api || iti |

rājaprāḍvivākasabhāyām eva daṇḍasy vyavahāraśiraḥsthānīyasyokteḥ | tataś ca,

	śiraḥsthāyivihīnāni divyāni parivarjayet |

ityādivacanaṃ rājaprāḍvivākasabhāviṣayam eveti mantavyam | evaṃ ca yat pitāmahena "mithyākriyā pūrvavāde" ity asyānyathākaranārtham uktam,

	abhiyuktāya dātavyaṃ divyaṃ śrutinidarśanāt |

iti, tad api rājaprāḍvivākasabhāviṣayam evety avagantavyam, na tadvyatiriktasabhāyām | ata eva "mithyākriyā pūrvavāde" iti vacanoktārthānatikrameṇa sabhair divyābhidhānaṃ kriyamāṇaṃ yuktam iti likhitādivad eva bhavatīti mantavyam | na ca,

	taṇḍulāś caiva kośaś ca śaṅkāsv etau niyojayet |

iti pitāmahavacane taṇḍulasāhacaryāc chaṅkāsv eva kośa iti śaṅkā kāryāḥ | "śīrṣakasthe" ityādipūrvoktayājñavalkyavacanavirodhāpatteḥ | taṇḍulasāhacaryaṃ tv alpābhiyoge 'pi kośo bhavatīti jñāpanārtham | ata eva nāradaḥ "kośam alpe pi dāpayet" iti | evaṃ ca "mahābhiyogeṣv etāni" iti yājñavalkyenokto niyamas tulādiviṣāntaviṣaya evety anusaṃdheyam | kośasyāpi niyame pūrvoktanāradavacanavirodhaḥ syāt | ata eva saṃgrahakāraḥ |

	dhaṭādīni viṣāntāni guruṣv artheṣu dāpayet | iti |

yat punas tenoktam,

	kośādīni punas trīṇi laghvartheṣu yathākramam |

iti, tadapahāra eva laghvarthaniyamakathanārtham, na punar apahnave 'pi (?), kośataṇḍulataptamāṣāṇāṃ gurvarthāpahnave vihitatvena laghvartheṣv eveti niyamāsaṃbhavāt | laghvartheṣv api śaṅkāsv eva taṇḍulāḥ 

	taṇḍulāś caiva kośaś ca śaṅkāsv etau niyojayet |

iti pitāmahasmaraṇāt | taptamāṣo 'pi laghvartheṣu śaṅkāyām eva,

	alpacauryādiśaṅkāyāṃ taptamāṣakam ādiśet |

iti tenaiva smṛtatvāt | phālam api kvacil laghvarthe pradātavyam | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	gocarasya pradātavyaṃ sabhyaiḥ phālaṃ prayatnataḥ | iti |

evaṃ ca,

	mahābhiyogeṣv etāni śīrṣakasthe 'bhiyoktari |

iti niyamo 'gnāv ucyamāno 'yaḥpiṇḍāgniviṣayo na taptamāṣaphālāgniviṣaya ity avagantavyam | ata evāgnidivyānāṃ pṛthaṅnirdeśo bṛhaspatinā kṛtaḥ |

	dhaṭo 'gnir udakaṃ caiva viṣaṃ kośaś ca pañcamam |

	ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca taṇḍulāḥ proktaṃ saptamaṃ taptamāṣakam ||

	aṣṭamaṃ phālam ity uktaṃ navamaṃ dharmajaṃ bhavet |

	divyāny etāni sarvāṇi nirdiṣṭāni svayaṃbhuvā || iti |

dharmajaṃ tu mahābhiyogabahiṣkṛtatvāl laghvartheṣv eva niyatam iti mantavyam | yat tu pitāmahenoktam,

	hantṝṇāṃ yācamānānāṃ prāyaścittārthināṃ nṛṇām |

	saṃdigdhe 'rthe 'bhiśastānāṃ dharmādharmaparīkṣaṇam ||

tasyāyam arthaḥ | hiṃsādhanapātakādyabhiyogeṣv alpeṣv abhiśastānāṃ dharmajaṃ divyam iti ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ divyanirūpaṇam**

**athābhiyogālpatvamahattvajñānopayogīni kānicid vacanāni likhyante** 

tatra manuḥ |

	lokasaṃvyavahārārthaṃ yāḥ saṃjñāḥ prathitā bhuvi |

	tāmrarūpyasuvarṇānāṃ tāḥ pravakṣyāmy aśeṣataḥ ||

daṇḍadivyaśāstrārthavyāmohāpanupattaye (?) tāmrādīnāṃ parimāṇanibandhanāḥ saṃjñāḥ pradarśyanta ity arthaḥ | pratijñātārthaṃ darśayati |

	jālāntaragate bhānau yat sūkṣmaṃ dṛśyate rajaḥ |

	prathamaṃ tat pramāṇānāṃ trasareṇuṃ pracakṣate ||

	trasareṇavo 'ṣṭau vijñeyā likṣaikā parimāṇataḥ |

	tā rājasarṣapas tisras te trayo gaurasarṣapaḥ ||

	sarṣapāḥ ṣaḍyavo madhas triyavaṃ tv ekakṛṣṇalam |

	pañcakṛṣṇalako māṣaḥ te suvarṇas tu ṣoḍaśa ||

	palaṃ suvarṇāś catvāraḥ palāni dharaṇaṃ daśa |

	dve kṛṣṇale samadhṛte vijñeyo rūpyamāṣakaḥ ||

	te ṣōḍaśa syād dharaṇaṃ purāṇaṃ caiva rājatam |

	kārṣāpaṇas tu vijñeyas tāmrikaḥ kārṣikaḥ paṇaḥ ||

	dharaṇāni daśa jñeyaḥ śatamānas tu rājatam |

	catuḥsuvarṇako niṣko vijñeyas tu pramāṇataḥ || iti |

eteṣāṃ ślokānāṃ tātparyārthaḥ prātilomyenocyate | niṣkaśatamānaśabdāv ekapale rūpyadravye vartete | ata eva rūpyasaṃjñādhikāre,

	śatamānaṃ tu daśabhiḥ dharaṇaiḥ palam eva tu |

	niṣkaḥ suvarāś catvāraḥ,

iti yājñavalkyenoktam | paṇakārṣāpaṇasabdau palacaturthāṃśakarṣasya tāmradravyasya nāmadheyam | purāṇadharaṇaśabdau paladaśamāṃśasya rūpyadravyasya nāmanī | karṣacatvāriṃśattamāṃśasya rūpyadravyasya māpasaṃjñā | daśapalasya dharaṇasaṃjñā | sā ca rajatetaradravyaviṣaye veditavyā | rājatadharaṇasyālpaparimāṇatvāt palasaṃjñā sarvadravyaviṣaye 'vagantavyā, viśeṣāsmṛteḥ | suvarṇaśabdas tu kāñvanakarṣavacanaḥ "suvarṇavistau hemnokṣe" ity amarasaṃhena viśeṣitatvāt | akṣekarṣa ity arthaḥ "te ṣoḍaśākṣaḥ karṣo 'strī" iti tenaivoktatvāt |karṣaṣoḍaśabhāgasya māṣasaṃjñā | sā ca rūpyadravyād anyatra vijñeyā, rūpyamāṣakasya karṣacatvāriṃśattamāṃśatvāt | kṛṣṇalaśabdas tu kārṣāśītibhāgavācī, māṣapañcamāṃśatvāt | evaṃ sarṣapalikṣātrasareṇupadārtheṣv api dravyeyattā svayam ūhanīyā | "yavo madhyaḥ" ity atra madhyasabdaḥ ślokapūraṇārtha ity uktaṃ tadbhāṣye | trasareṇau padmarajaḥsaṃjñāpi purāṇe darśitā |

	aṣṭānāṃ paramāṇūnāṃ samavāyo yadā bhavet |

	trasareṇuḥ samākhyātas tat padmaraja ucyate || iti |

māṣaśabdaḥ kārṣāpaṇasya viṃśatitame bhāge vartata ity āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	māṣo viṃśatibhāgas tu jñeyaḥ kārṣāpaṇasya tu |

	kākaṇī tu caturbhāgā māṣakasya paṇasya ca ||

	pañcanadyāḥ pradeśe tu saṃjñeyaṃ vyāvahārikī || iti |

suvarṇaśabdo dvādasapalavācīty āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	tāmrakarṣakṛtā mudrā vijñeyaḥ kāṣikaḥ paṇaḥ |

	sa eva cāṇḍikā proktā tāś catasras tu dhānakā ||

	tā dvādaśa suvarṇās tu dīnārākhyaḥ sa eva tu || iti |

kātyāyano 'pi |

	kārṣāpaṇo 'ṇḍikā jñeyā tāś catasras tu dhānakaḥ |

	te dvādaśa suvarṇās tu dīnāraś citrakaḥ smṛtaḥ || iti |

pale tu vikalpo yājñavalkyena darśitaḥ |

	palaṃ suvarṇāś catvāraḥ pañca vāpi prakīrtitam | iti |

rājato 'pi kārṣāpaṇo 'stīty āha nāradaḥ |

	kārṣāpaṇo dakṣiṇasyāṃ diśi raupyaḥ pravartate | iti |

vyāsas tu sauvarṇaniṣkasya pramāṇam āha |

	palāny aṣṭau suvarṇasya suvarṇāś ca caturdaśa |

	etan niṣkapramāṇaṃ tu vyāsena parikīrtitam || iti |

atra manūktapramāṇāntaramāxādiḥ divyadaṇḍaviṣaye deśavyavahāravirodhe 'pi grāhya eva | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	saṃkhyā raśmirajomūlā manunā samudāhṛtā |

	kārṣāpaṇānto sā divye niyojyā vinaye tathā || iti |

kārṣāpaṇāntagrahaṇaṃ niṣkapramāṇe tu nāyaṃ niyama iti pratipādanārtham | tena niṣkāntareṇa divyaṃ kiṃcid uttaratrocyamānam aviruddham |

**iti smṛticandrikāyām abhiyogālapatvamattvajñānopayogīni **

**atha dhanaparimāṇato divyavyavasthā**

tatra kātyāyanaḥ |

	dattasyāpahnavo yatra pramāṇaṃ tatra kalpayet | iti |

apahnavo 'palāpaḥ | kathaṃ kalpayed ity apekṣite sa evāha |

	sarvaṃ dravyaprāmāṇaṃ (?) tu jñātvā hema prakalpayet |

	hemapramāṇayuktaṃ tu tadā divyaṃ niyojayet ||

	jñātvā saṃkhyāṃ suvarṇasya satanāśe viṣaṃ smṛtam |

	aśītes tu vināśe vai dadyāc caiva hutāśanam ||

	ṣaṣṭyā nāśe jalaṃ deyaṃ catvāriṃśati vai dhaṭam |

	viṃśaddasavināśe tu koṣapānaṃ vidhīyate ||

	pañcādhikasya vai nāśe tadarhārdhasya taṇḍulāḥ |

	tadarthārdhavināśe tu spṛśet putrādimastakam ||

	tadardhārthavināśe tu laukikyaś ca kriyāḥ smṛtāḥ || iti |

sarvatra vināśaśabdasyāpahnavārthatā pratyetavyā, "dattasyāpanavo yatra" ity upakrāntatvāt | viṃśaddaśavināśe triṃśadvināśe viṃśadnāśe vety arthaḥ | pañcabhyo 'dhikaḥ pañcādhikaḥ ṣaṭprabhṛtir (?) iti yāvat | tadardhārdhasya sārdhasuvarṇaprasṛter vināśe taṇḍulāḥ | tadardhārdhavināśe tv aṣṭāṃśonasuvarṇārdhaprasṛter vināśe taṇḍulāḥ | tadardhārdhavināśe tv aṣṭāṃśonasuvarṇārdhaprasṛter vināśe putradāraśiraḥsparśanam | tadardhārdhavināśe tu sārdhasaptakṛṣṇalaprasṛter vināśe tu dravyāṣṭaguṇavacanādayo laukikāḥ śapathāḥ | caśabdaḥ smārthaśabdānāṃ saṃgrahārthaḥ | ata eva viṣṇuḥ: "sarveṣv evārthajāteṣu mūlyaṃ kanakaṃ kalpayet tatra kṛṣṇalone śūdraṃ dūrvākaraṃ śāpayet, dvikṛṣṇalone tilakaram, trikṛṣṇalone rajatakaram, catuḥkṛṣṇalone suvarṇakaram, pañcakṛṣṇalone sīroddhṛtamahīkaram, dviguṇe 'rthe yathābhihitā samayakriyā vaiśyasya, triguṇe 'rthe rājanyasya, caturguṇe 'rthe brāhmaṇasya" iti |sīroddhṛtamahīkaraṃ lāṅgaloddhṛtahastam ity arthaḥ | ūnagrahaṇam adhike śāpavinivṛttyartham | śāpe tu viśeṣam āha manuḥ |

	satyena śāpayed vipraṃ kṣatriyaṃ vāhanāyudhaiḥ |

	gobījakāñcanair vaiśyaṃ śūdraṃ sarvais tu pātakaiḥ ||

asyārthaḥ: yady aham arthāpahnavī syāṃ tadā satyābhidhānadharmo mama niṣphalaḥ syād iti śapathakāriṇaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ vācayet | evaṃ kṣatriyādīn, satyābhidhānadharmo mama niṣphalaḥ syād ity asya sthāne vā hanāyudhāni mama niṣphalāni syur iti kṣatriye | gobījakāñcanāni niṣphalāni syur iti vaiśye | sarvāṇi pātakāni mama syur iti śūdre viśeṣa iti | pādasparśādīnāṃ viṣayaḥ smṛtyantare darśitaḥ |

	niṣke tu satyavacanaṃ dviniṣke pādalambhanam |

	ūnatrike tu puṣpaṃ syāt kośapānam ataḥ param ||

niṣkaśabdenātra kāñcanakarṣacaturthāṃśo mudrāmudritaḥ pratipādyate | tatrāpi kvacid deśe niṣkasya vyavahārāt | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> manūkto māṣādiḥ divyādiviṣaye grahītavya iti niyamān na vyāvahārikaniṣkapratipādanaṃ yuktam |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>, niṣke manūktagrahaṇaniyamo nāstīty uktatvāt | kiṃ ca tatra manūktaniṣkasya rājatapalātmakasya mūlyaṃ kāñcanakārṣārdhād adhikaṃ bhavati | tatra satyavacanavidhau (?) "caturguṇe 'rthe brāhmaṇasya" iti viṣṇuvacanavirodhaḥ syāt | caturguṇasya hi kṛṣṇalapañcakasya karṣacaturthāṃśatvāt | tasmād vyāvahārikaniṣkāśrayeṇa satyavacanādivyavasthoketi mantavyam | pāriśeṣyād iṣṭāpūrtādisukṛtadānam, jātiśapathaviṣayād adhike dharmajadivyaviṣayād ūne dhane 'vagantavyam | dharmajasya tu viṣayam āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	śate hṛte 'pahṇute ca dātavyaṃ dharmaśodhanam | iti |

kārṣāpaṇaśataprabhṛti nikṛṣṭasya, dviśataprabhṛti madhyamasya, catuḥśataprabhṛty uttamasya, dharmajaṃ divyaṃ bhavatīty arthaḥ |

	eṣā saṃkhyā nikṛṣṭānāṃ madhyānāṃ dviguṇā smṛtā |

	caturguṇottamānāṃ tu

iti tenaivābhidhānāt | kārṣāpaṇamūlyaṃ vyāvahārikaniṣkasyāśītitamo bhāgo bhavati | kṛṣṇalaṃ tu vyāvahārikaniṣkasya viṃśatitamo bhāgaḥ | suvarṇaḥ punar vyāvahārikaniṣkacatuṣkaṃ bhavati | evaṃ ca sarvadivyānāṃ vyāvahārikaniṣkato vyavasthaivaṃ veditavyā | catuḥśataniṣkaprabhṛti viṣam, viṃśatyuttaratriśataniṣkaprabhrty agniḥ, catvāriṃśaduttaradiviśataniṣkaprabhṛti jalam, ṣaṣṭyuttaraśataniṣkaprabhṛti dhaṭaḥ | viṃśatyuttaraśataniṣkaprabhṛti vā catvāriṃśanniṣkaprabhṛti vā caturviṃśatiniṣkaprabhṛti vā bhavati | ṣaṇṇiṣkaprabhṛti taṇḍulāḥ | pañcaniṣkaprabhṛty uttamasya dharmajaṃ divyam, triniṣkaprabhṛti taṇḍulāḥ | pañcaniṣkaprabhṛty uttamasya dharmajaṃ divyam, triniṣkaprabhṛty alpābhiyogavihitaḥ kośaḥ, kiṃcid ūnatriniṣkaprabhṛti puṣpam, sārdhadviniṣkaprabhṛti dharmajaṃ divyam, madhyamasya dviniṣkaprabhṛti devatāpratimāyāḥ pitur brāhmaṇasy pādasparśanam | sārdhaniṣkaprabhṛti putradāraśiraḥsparśanam | pādādhikaniṣkaprabhṛti nikṛṣṭasya madhyamaṃ divyam, niṣkaprabhṛtīṣṭāpūrtādisukṛtadānam, niṣkadasamāṃśacatuṣṭayaprabhṛti laukikāḥ śapathaḥ niṣkaviṃśatitamāṃśaprabhṛti jātiśapathāḥ | teṣu dūrvākaratvādidharmāḥ yathāviṣṇuvacanaṃ boddhavyāḥ | saiṣā vyavasthā dharmajetareṣāṃ dhaṭādīnāṃ na dhanāpahāraviṣaye kalpanīyā | prakārāntareṇa dhanāpahāraviṣaye teṣāṃ yato vyavasthām āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	viṣaṃ sahasre 'pahṛte pādone ca hutāśanaḥ |

	tribhāgone ca salilam ardhe deyo dhaṭaḥ sadā ||

	catuḥśatābhiyoge tu dātavyas taptamāṣakaḥ |

	triśate (?) taṇḍulā deyāḥ kośaś caiva tadardhake ||

	śate hṛte 'pahnute ca dātavyaṃ dharmaśodhanam |

	gocarasya pradātavyaṃ sabhyaiḥ phālaṃ prayatnataḥ ||

	eṣā saṃkhyā nikṛṣṭānāṃ madhyānāṃ dviguṇā smṛtā |

	caturguṇottamānāṃ tu kalpanīyā parīkṣakaiḥ || iti |

atra mahābhiyoge niyatadhaṭasya pañcaśatādikārṣāpaṇāpahāre 'bhidhānāt tadādikārṣāpaṇasaṃbandhyabhiyogo mahābhiyogas tadādikonyūnakārṣāpaṇasaṃbandhī tv alpābhiyoga ity avagantavyam | ata eva saṃgrahakāraḥ |

	ṛṇaṃ vā yadi vā daṇḍaḥ prāyaścittam athāpi vā |

	yatra pañcaśatādiḥ syāt tat kāryaṃ guru kīrtyate ||

	yatrārabhya daśabhyas ev etāny ā saikacatuḥśatāt |

	kāryaṃ tal laghu nirdiṣṭaṃ smṛtitantraviśāradaiḥ || iti |

ā saikacuatḥśatād ā pañcaśatād ity arthaḥ | ṛṇam iti vivādāspadaṃ dhanam anāsthayoktam | adhanābhiyogamahattvālpatve tatra vihitadaṇḍadhanaprāyaścittapratyān(?)mānadhanayor anyatarasaṃkhyayā pratyetavye iti tātparyārthaḥ | yat tu yājñavalkyenoktam,

	nāsahasrād dharet phālaṃ na viṣaṃ na tulāṃ tathā |

iti, tac caritrādito madhyamapuruṣā ye bhavanti teṣāṃ pratiṣedhārtham | adhamānāṃ sahasrād arvāg apahāre 'pahnave vā mahābhiyogābhāvāt | evaṃ cottamānāṃ dvisahasrād arvāg alpābhiyogatvād dhaṭādipratiṣedho 'vagantavyaḥ | yat punaḥ pitāmahenoktam,

	sahasre tu dhaṭaṃ dadyāt sahasrārdhe tathāyasam |

	ardhasyārdhe tu salilaṃ tasyārdhe tu viṣaṃ smṛtam ||

iti, tat prāgdṭṣṭadoṣapuruṣaviṣayam | yad āha viṣṇuḥ: "prāgdṛṣṭadoṣaṃ svalpe 'py arthe divyānām anyatamam eva kārayet" iti | evaṃ cottamasyāpi prāgdṛṣṭadoṣasya sahasre taturguṇāt svalpe 'rthe dhaṭo bhavatīti pitāmahavacanasya tātparyārthaḥ pratyetavyaḥ | evaṃ nṛpadroheṣu mahāpātakābhiyoge ca svalpe 'py arthe divyāni bhavantīty āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	nṛpārtheṣv abhiśāpe ca vahehuḥ śucayaḥ sadā | iti |

viṣṇur api: "atha samayakriyā rājadrohe sāhaseṣu yathākāmam" iti | samayakriyā dhaṛādidivyakaraṇam | tathā ca gobalīvardanyāyena dhaṭādikam evātrāha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	ete tu śapathāḥ proktāḥ svalpe 'rthe sukarāḥ sadā |

	sāhaseṣv abhiśāpeṣu divyāny āhur viśodhanam || iti |

evaṃ ca sāhasādau satyādayaḥ śapathāḥ kadācid api na bhavantīti mantavyam | apahāre 'pi vyāvahārikaniṣkasaṃkhyayā vyavasthā vyākhyāsyate:

	uttamasya puruṣasya pañcāśanniṣkaprabhṛti viṣam, niṣṅārdhādhikasaptatriṃśanniṣkaprabhṛty agniḥ, yavonasaptakṛṣṇalādhikatrayastriṃśanniṣkaprabhṛtu jalam, pañcaviṃśanniṣkaprabhṛti dhaṭaḥ, viṃśatiniṣkaprabhṛtitaptamāṣaḥ, pañcadaśaniṣkaprabhṛti taṇḍulāḥ, niṣkārdhādhikasaptaniṣkaprabhṛti kośaḥ, pañcaniṣkaprabhṛti dharmajaṃ divyam, govyakticatuṣṭayamprabhṛti pālam |

	madhyamasya tu puruṣasya pañcaviṃśatiniṣkaprabhṛti viṣam, sapādaniṣkonaviṃśatiniṣkaprabhṛty agniḥ, yavasahitatrayodaśakṛṣṇalādhikaṣoḍaśaniṣkaprabhṛti jalam, niṣkārdhādikadvādaśaniṣkaprabhṛti dhaṭaḥ, daśaniṣkaprabhṛti taptamāṣaḥ, niṣkārdhādhikasaptaniṣkaprabhṛti taṇḍulāh, niṣkapādonacaturniṣkaprabhṛti kośaḥ, sardhadviniṣkaprabhṛti dharmajaṃ divyam, govyaktidvayaprabhṛti phālam |

	nikṛṣṭasya tu puruṣasya sārdhadvādaśaniṣkaprabhṛti viṣam, sārdhasaptakṛṣṇalādhikanavatiniṣkaprabhṛty agniḥ, yavonasaptakṛṣṇalādhikāṣṭaniṣkaprabhṛti jalam, sapādaṣaṇṇiṣkaprabhṛti dhaṭaḥ, pañcaniṣkaprabhṛti taptamāṣaḥ, pādonacaturniṣkaprabhṛti taṇḍulāḥ, pādārdhonadviniṣkaprabhṛti kośaḥ, sapādaniṣkaprabhṛti dharmajaṃ divyam, ekagovyaktiprabhṛti phālam |

	prāgdṛṣṭadoṣāṇām uktāvadhibhyo 'lpadhane 'pi tat tad divyaṃ deyam | nṛpadrohābhiśāpasāhaseṣu ca tathaiva deyam | satyādipuṣpādiśapathānāṃ tu vyavasthāviśeṣasya atrādarśanād apahnava (?) iva vyavasthāstheyā, viṣṇuvacane smṛtyantaravacane cāpahnava iti viśeṣasmaraṇāc ceti ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ dhanaparimāṇato divyavyavasthā**

**atha vivādijātyādito vyavasthā**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	ṛṇādikeṣu kāryeṣu visaṃvāde parasparam |

	dravyasaṃkhyānvitā deyā puruṣāpekṣayā tathā ||

puruṣāpekṣayā vivādinor jātyādyapekṣayety arthaḥ | tatra jātyapekṣayā vyavasthām aha nāradaḥ |

	brāhmaṇasya dhaṭo deyaḥ kṣatriyasya hutāśanaḥ |

	vaiśyasya salilaṃ deyaṃ śūdrasya viṣam eva tu |

	sādhāraṇaḥ samastānāṃ kośaḥ prokto manīṣibhiḥ || iti |

anityā ceyaṃ vyavasthā | yad āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	sarveṣu sarvadivyaṃ vā viṣavarjaṃ dvijottame || iti |

liṅgasāmarthyābhāvavayobhyo 'pi vyavasthām āha nāradaḥ |

	klībāturān satyahīnān paritaś cārditān narān |

	bālavṛddhastryandhkāṃś ca parīkṣeta dhaṭe sadā ||

nityā tv iyaṃ vyavasthā, sadety abhidhānāt | dhaṛagrahaṇam agnyambyviṣāṇāṃ parisaṅkhyānārtham, na punaḥ kośāder api | yad āha sa eva |

	strīṇāṃ tu na viṣaṃ proktaṃ na cāpi salilaṃ smṛtam |

	dhaṭakośādibhis tāsām antas tattvaṃ vicārayet || iti |

dhaṭakośādibhir iti vadann agner api pratiṣedhaṃ darsayati | darśitaṃ ca sākṣād api tena |

	na majjanīyaṃ strībālaṃ dharmaśāstravicakṣaṇaiḥ |

	rogiṇo ye ca vṛddhāḥ syuḥ pumāṃso ye ca durbalāḥ ||

	sāhase 'py āgatān etān naiva toye nimajjayet |

	na cāpi hārayed agniṃ na viṣeṇa viśodhayet || iti |

yat punaḥ pitāmanenoktam,

	savratānāṃ kṛśāṅgānāṃ bālavṛddhatapasvinām |

	strīṇāṃ tu na bhaved divyaṃ yadi dharmas tv avekṣyate || 

iti, tad agnyambuviṣayam, dhaṭakośādīnām api pratiṣedhe pūrvoktavacanavirodhāt | evaṃ ca klībādīnām agnyambuviṣavarjyāni dvyāni bhavantīty anusaṃdheyam | tathā lohakārādīnām api na sarvāṇi divyāni bhavantīty āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	na lohaśilpinām agniṃ salilaṃ nāmbusevinām |

	mantrayogavidāṃ caiva viṣaṃ dadyāc ca na kvacit ||

	taṇḍulair na niyuñjīta prāṇinaṃ mikharogiṇam || iti |

pitāmaho 'pi |

	kuṣṭhināṃ varjayed agniṃ salilaṃ śvāsakāsinām |

	pittaśleṣmavatāṃ nityaṃ viṣaṃ tu parivarjayet ||

	madyapastrīvyasanināṃ kitavānāṃ tathaiva ca |

	kośaḥ prājñair na dātavyo ye ca nāstikavṛttayaḥ || iti |

nārado 'pi |

	mahāparādhe nirdharme kṛtaghne klībakutsite |

	nāstike dṛṣṭadoṣe ca kośadānaṃ vivarjayet ||

mahāparādhe pūrvasiddhamāhāparādhaśālinīty arthaḥ | evaṃ ca klībasya agnyādivat kośo 'pi varjya ity anusaṃdheyam | yat punaḥ katyāyanenoktam,

	mātāpitṛdvijagurubālastrīrājaghātinām |

	mahāpātakayuktānāṃ nāstikānāṃ viśeṣataḥ ||

	liṅgināṃ praśaṭhānāṃ tu mantrayogakriyāvidām |

	varṇasaṃkarajātānāṃ pāpābhyāsapravartinām ||

	eteṣv evābhiyogeṣu nindyeṣv eva ca yatnataḥ |

	divyaṃ prakalpayen naiva rājā dharmaparāyaṇaḥ || 

iti, tat teṣāṃ sākṣād divyakartṛtvaniṣedhārtham, na punar divyena parīkṣāyāḥ | yato 'nantaram evoktam tenaiva |

	etair eva niyuktānām sādhūnāṃ divyam arhati |

	necchanti sādhavo yatra tatra śodhyaḥ svakair naraiḥ || iti |

divyam arhati rājā kalpayitum iti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	eṣu vādeṣu divyāni pratiṣiddhāni yatnataḥ |

	kārayet svajanais tāni nābhiśaptaṃ tyajen manuḥ ||

tyajet uktaprakāreṇa viśodhayed iti śeṣaḥ | yat punas tenoktam,

	aspṛśyadhanadāsānāṃ mlecchānāṃ pāpakāriṇām |

	prātilomyaprasūtānāṃ niścayo na tu rājani ||

	tat prasiddhāni divyāni saṃśaye teṣu nirdiśet ||

iti, tat tair niyuktasvajanālābhaviṣayam ity avagantavyam |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ vivādijātyādito divyavyavasthā**

**athartuto dviyavyavasthā**

tatra pitāmahaḥ |

	dhaṭaḥ sarvartukaḥ prokto vāte vāti vivarjayet |

	agniḥ śiśirahemantavarṣāsu parikīrtitaḥ ||

	śaradgrīṣme tu salilaṃ hemante śiśire viṣam || iti |

dhaṭagrahaṇaṃ kośasyāpi pradarśanārtham | kośas tu sarvadā deyaḥ "tulā syāt sārvakālikaḥ" iti nāradasmaraṇāt | kośagrahaṇaṃ taṇḍulaprabhṛtīnāṃ pradarśanārtham ity uktaṃ tad vyākhyātṛbhiḥ | tenāgnyambuviṣāṇām evartuto vyavasthā | ata eva teṣām eva ṛtvantarapratiṣedhas tena darśitaḥ |

	na śīte toyasiddhiḥ syāt noṣṇakāle 'gniśodhanam |

	na prāvṛṣi viṣaṃ dadyāt pravāte tu tulāṃ nṛpaḥ || iti |

pravāte vātātiśaya ity arthaḥ | viṣṇur api: "na kuṣṭhyasamarthalohakārāṇām agnir deyaḥ, śaradgrīṣmayoś ca na kuṣṭhipaittikabrāhmaṇānāṃ viṣaṃ deyam, prāvṛṣi ca na śleṣmavyādhyarditānāṃ bhīrūṇāṃ śvāsakāsinām ambujīvināṃ codakam, hemantaśiśirayoś ca na nāstikebhyaḥ kośo deyaḥ vyādhimaraṇopaspṛṣṭe ca" iti | hemantagrahaṇaṃ puṣyamāsasya pratiṣedhārtham, na punar mārgaśīrṣasyāpi, tasya śītātiśayābhāvenodakadivyavirodhitvābhāvāt | atra pitāmahaḥ |

	caitro mārgaśirāś caiva vaiśākhaś ca tathaiva ca |

	ete sādhāraṇā māsā divyānām avirodhinaḥ || iti |

ata ete māsāḥ sarvadivyakālā bhavantīty arthaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ ṛtuto divyavyavasthā**

**atha divyadeśāḥ**

atra pitāmahaḥ |

	prāṅmukho niścalaḥ kāryaḥ śucau deśe dhaṭaḥ sadā |

	indrasthāne sabhāyāṃ vā rājadvāre catuṣpathe ||

indrasthānaṃ prakhyātadevatāyatanam, "sabhā rājakuladvāradevāyatanacatvare" it nāradasmaraṇāt | atra vyavasthām āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	indrasthāne 'bhiśastānāṃ mahāpātakināṃ nṛṇām |

	nṛpadrohapravṛttānāṃ rājadvāre prayojayet ||

	prātilomyaprasūtānāṃ divyaṃ deyaṃ catuṣpathe |

	ato 'nyeṣu tu kāryeṣu sabhāmadhye vidur budhāḥ || iti |

divyam iti sāmānyenābhidhānāt dhaṭasyaiveyaṃ deśavyavasthā, kiṃ tva anuktadeśaveśeṣāṇām anyeṣām apīty avagantavyam | vihitadeśādyanādare divyaprāmāṇyahānir bhavatīty āha sa eva |

	adeśakāladattāni bahirvāsakṛtāni ca |

	vyabhicāraṃ sadārtheṣu kurvantīha na saṃśayaḥ ||

vāsaḥ nivāsaḥ janasthānam, tasmād bahiḥ nirjanapradeśa iti yāvat | anena janasamakṣaṃ eva divyāni deyānīty arthād uktam | uktaṃ ca pitāmahena |

	pratyakṣaṃ dāpayed divyaṃ rājā vādhikṛto 'pi vā |

	brāhmaṇānāṃ śrutavatāṃ prakṛtīnāṃ tathaiva ca ||

adhikṛtaḥ prāḍvivākaḥ |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ divyadeśāḥ**

**atha dhaṭanirmāṇavidhiḥ** 

tatra nāradaḥ |

	khādiraṃ kārayet tatra nirvraṇaṃ śuklavarjitam |

	śiṃśupāṃ tadalābhe tu sālaṃ vā koṭarair vinā ||

	añjanas tindukīsāraṃ nimiśo raktacandanam |

	evaṃvidhāni kāṣṭhāni dhaṛārthaṃ parikalpayet || iti |

evaṃvidhānīti vadan pūrvoktānām alābhe yajñiyaṃ vṛkṣāntaram api bhavatīti darśayati | darśitaṃ ca pitāmahena |

	chitvā tu yajñiyaṃ vṛkṣaṃ vidhivan mantrapūrvakam |

	praṇamya lokapālebhyas tulā kāryā manīṣibhiḥ ||

	mantras somyo vānaspatyacchedane japya eva tu || iti |

saumyavānaspatyayor vikalpaḥ tulyakāryatvād iti kaiścid uktam | tulāgrahaṇaṃ tatparikarasyāpi pradarśanārtham, tena pādastambhādyartham api vṛkṣacchedanaṃ kāryam | ata eva saparikarāyās tulāyāḥ pramāṇam uktaṃ tenaiva |

	caturhastā tulā kāryā pādau kāryau tathāvidhau |

	antaraṃ tulayor hastau bhaved adhyartha eva vā ||

pādau tulādhārakāṣṭhādhārārthau stambhau, tathāvidhau caturhastapramāṇāv ity arthaḥ | etac ca pādayoḥ pramāṇaṃ nikhananīyahastadvayād uparitanabhāgasya veditavyam | ato nikhananīyabhāgena saha ṣaḍḍhastau bhavataḥ | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

	hastadvayaṃ nikheyaṃ tu proktaṃ muṇḍakayor dvayoḥ |

	ṣaḍḍhastaṃ tu tayoḥ proktaṃ pramāṇaṃ parimāṇataḥ ||

akṣasya tu pramāṇaṃ pādayor antarālābhidhānenaivārthasiddham iti na pṛthag uktam | tena pādastambhamastakadeśāt bahir aniḥsṛto yathā bhavati tathā hastadvayāt sārdhahastād vābhyadhiko 'kṣaḥ kārya ity avagantavyam | hastaḥ punaś caturviṃśatyaṅgula iti smṛtyantare darśitaḥ |

	tiryagyavodarāṇy aṣṭāv ūrdhvā vā vrīhayas trayaḥ |

	pramāṇam aṅgulasyoktaṃ vitastir dvādaśāṅgulā ||

	hasto vitastidvitayam | iti |

yāvati tu sthaulye kṛte dārḍhyaṃ bhavati tāvat sthaulyaṃ tulādīnāṃ kāryam, viśeṣāsmṛteḥ(?) | ācārād vā viśeṣaḥ sthaulye veditavyaḥ | tulāyāṃ tv apare viśeṣāḥ pitāmahena darśitāḥ |

	caturaśrā tulā kāryā dṛḍhā ṛjvī tathaiva ca |

	kaṭakāni ca deyāni triṣu sthāneṣ yatnataḥ ||

kaṭakāni lohavalayāni | triṣu sthāneṣu upāntayor madhye ca | kaṭakānīty ayomayānām anyeṣām apy upalakṣaṇārtham, tenopāntayor āyasakīlakau śikyapāśadhāraṇārthāvipuvad (?) vakrāgrau karkaṭakaśṛṅgasaṃnibhau deyau | madhye tv āyasapāśo 'kṣakāṣṭhe tulāyojanārtho deyaḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	caturaśrā sthitisthānair dhaṭakarkaṭakādibhiḥ | iti |

dhaṭaśabdenātra tulāmadhyasaṃbandhī pāśo lakṣyate | karkaṭakaśabdenātra upāntyakīlakau sādṛśyād ucyete | tenāyam arthaḥ: ayomayaiḥ pāśaprabhṛtibhiḥ sthitihetubhis tulāyāṃ bhavitavyam iti | ādiśabdenākṣamadhye 'py ekena karkaṭakena bhavitavyam iti darśayati | tathā stambhādisthāpanaprakāro 'pi tena darśitaḥ |

	dakṣiṇottarasaṃsthānāv ubhāv ekāgra (katra) saṃyatau |

	antau kṛtvā same deśe tayoḥ saṃsthāpayet tulām ||

asyārthaḥ: samāyāṃ bhūmau dakṣiṇottarabhāvena sthitayoḥ pādastambhayor ubhāv antau ekatra akṣakāṣṭhe saṃghāṭitau kṛtvā tayoḥ ghaṭakākṣakāṣṭhamadhye tulāṃ sthapayed iti | sthāpanaṃ ca tatra kathaṃ kāryam ity apekṣite sa evāha |

	āyasena tu pāśena madhye saṃgṛhya dharmavit |

	yojayet tu susaṃyuktāṃ tulāṃ prāgaparāyatām (?) ||

prāgaparāyatāṃ pūrvapaścimadīrghām ity arthaḥ | prāgagratā ca kāryety āha pitāmaḥaḥ |

	prāṅmukho niścalaḥ kāryaḥ śucau deśe dhaṭaḥ sadā | iti |

niścalatvasidhyartham āha nāradaḥ |

	hastadvayaṃ nikheyaṃ tu pādayor ubhayos tathā | iti |

tatheti vadan anyad api kiṃcid dhaṭāṅgabhūtaṃ toraṇādikaṃ kāryam iti darśayati | darśitaṃ ca pitāmahena |

	toraṇe tu tathā kārye pārśvayor ubhayor api |

	dhaṭād uccarate syātāṃ nityaṃ daśabhir aṅgulaiḥ ||

	avalambau ca kartavyau toraṇābhyām adhomukhau |

	mṛnmayau sūtrasaṃbaddhau dhaṭamastakacumbakau ||

	dhaṭaṃ tu kāreyan nityaṃ patākādhvajaśobhitam |

	viślām ucchritāṃ śubhrāṃ dhaṭaśālāṃ tu kārayet ||

	yatrastho nopahanyeta bahiś caṇḍālavāyasaiḥ |

	tatraiva lokapālādīn sarvadikṣū niveśayet ||

	trisaṃdhyaṃ pūjayec cainān gandhamālyānulepanaiḥ |

	kavāṭabījasaṃyuktāṃ paricārakarakṣitām ||

	mṛtpānīyāgnisaṃyuktām aśūnyāṃ kārayen nṛpaḥ || iti |

atra śālāracanādikaṃ dhaṭadhāraṇaprayuktam eva notpattiprayuktam iti, dhāraṇānicchāyām ananuṣṭheyam eveti kaiś cid uktam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ dhaṭanirmāṇavidhiḥ **

**atha sarvadivyasādhāraṇavidhiḥ**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	snehāt krodhāl lobhato vā bhedam āyānti sākṣiṇaḥ |

	vidhidattasya divyasya na bhedo jāyate kvacit ||

ato divyaṃ vidhivad deyam ity abhiprāyaḥ | vidhiś ca pitāmahena darśitaḥ |

	divyeṣu sarvakāryāṇi prāḍvivākaḥ samācaret |

	adhvareṣu yathādhvaryuḥ sopavāso nṛpājñayā ||

sarvakāryāṇi sādhāraṇāny asādhāraṇāni cety arthaḥ | tatra sādhāraṇāni tenaiva darśitāni |

	tata āvāhayed devān vidhinānena dharmavit | iti |

anena vakṣyamāṇenety arthaḥ | tam eva vidhiṃ darśayati |

	prāṅmukhaḥ prāñjalir bhūtvā prāḍvivākas tato vadet |

	ehy ehi bhavan dharma asmin divye samāviśa |

	sahito lokapālaiś ca vasvāityamarudgaṇaiḥ || iti |

tataḥ divyopakalpanānantaram ity arthaḥ, asmin divya iti mantraliṅgāt,

	āvāhya tu dhaṭe dharmaṃ paścād aṅgāni vinyaset |

iti tenaivābhidhānāc ca | dhaṭagrahaṇam upakalpitadivyopalakṣaṇārtham, sarvadivyeṣudharmāvānasyāṅgavinyāsasya ca vakṣyamāṇatvāt | aṅgāni vinyased ity asyārthaḥ tenaiva darśitaḥ |

	indraṃ pūrve tu saṃsthāpya preteśaṃ dakṣiṇe tathā |

	varuṇaṃ paścime bhāge kuberaṃ cottare tathā ||

	agnyādilokapālāṃś ca koṇabhāgeṣu vinyaset |

	indraḥ pīto yamaḥ śyāmo varuṇaḥ sphaṭikaprabhaḥ ||

	kuberas tu suvarṇābhaḥ hy agniś cāpi suvarṇabhaḥ |

	tathaiva niṛtiḥ śyāmo vāyur dhūmraḥ praśasyate ||

	īśānas tu bhaved rakta evaṃ dhyāyet kramādimān |

	indrasya dakṣiṇe pārśve vasūn āvāhayed budhaḥ ||

	dharo dhruvas tathā soma āpaś caivānilo 'nalaḥ |

	pratyūpaś ca prabhāsaś ca vasavo 'ṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ ||

	deveśeśānayor madhya ādityānāṃ tathāyanam |

	dhātāryamā ca mitraś ca varuṇo 'ṃśur bhagas tathā ||

	indro vivasvān pūṣā ca parjanyo daśamaḥ smṛtaḥ |

	tatas tvaṣṭā tato viṣṇur ajaghanyo jaghanyajaḥ ||

	ity ete dvādaśādityā nāmabhiḥ parikīrtitāḥ |

	agneḥ paścimabhāge tu rudrāṇām ayanaṃ viduḥ ||

	vīrabhadraś ca śambhuś ca giriśaś ca mahāyaśāḥ |

	ajaikapādahirbudhnyaḥ pinākī cāparājitaḥ ||

	bhuvanādhīśvaraś caiva kapālī ca viśāṃpatiḥ|

	sthāṇur bhagaś ca bhagavān rudrāś tv ekādaśa smṛtāḥ ||

	preteśarakṣomadhye ca mātṛsthānaṃ prakalpayet |

	brāhmī māheśvarī caiva kaumārī vaiṣṇavī tathā ||

	vārāhī caiva māhendrī cāmuṇḍā gaṇasaṃyutā |

	nirṛter uttare bhāge gaṇeśāyatanaṃ viduḥ ||

	varuṇasyottare bhāge marutāṃ sthānam ucyate |

	gaganasparśano vāyur anilo mārutas tathā ||

	prāṇaḥ prāṇeśajīvau ca maruto 'ṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ |

	dhaṭasyottarabhāge tu durgām āvāhayed budhaḥ || iti |

atrāpi pūrvavad dhaṭagrahaṇam upakalpitadivyopalakṣaṇārtham | evaṃ yathāsthānam āvāhitānāṃ devānāṃ pūjanaṃ kuryāt | tathā ca sa eva |

	etāsāṃ devatānāṃ tu svanāmnā pūjanaṃ viduḥ | iti |

tatra ca kramam āha sa eva |

	bhūṣāvasānaṃ dharmāya datvā cārghyādikaṃ kramāt |

	ardhyādi paścād aṅgānāṃ (?) bhūṣāntam upakalpayet ||

aṅgīnām indrādidurgāntānām ity arthaḥ | teṣām ardhyādyupakalpanaṃ padārthānusamayena kāryam, na kāṇḍānasamayena, tathātve prayogavacanāvagatasahatvabādhāpatteḥ | durgāyau bhūṣaṇaṃ datvā dharmasyendrādidurgāntānāṃ ca gandhādiparicaryāṃ pūrvavat kuryāt | tathā ca sa eva |

	gandhādikāṃ nivedyāntāṃ paricaryāṃ kalpayet | iti |

tataś catasṛṣu dikṣu caturbhir homaḥ kartavyaḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	caturdikṣu tathā homaḥ kartavyo vedapāragaiḥ |

	ājyena haviṣā caiva samidbhir homasādhanaiḥ ||

	sāvitryā praṇavenātha svāhāntenaiva homayet || iti |

laukikam agniṃ caturdiṣu pratiṣṭhāpyaikaikasyāṃ diśy ekaikaḥ ṛtvik samidājyacarūn pratyekam aṣṭottaraśataṃ tatsavitur iti mantreṇobhayataḥ praṇavena svāhākārāntena juhuyād ity arthaḥ | yady apy atra saṃkhyā noktā, tathāpi,

	anuktasaṃkhyā yatra syāc chatam aṣṭottaraṃsmṛtam|

iti smṛtyantarāt siddhety avadheyam | etat sarvaṃ pūrvāhṇe kartavyaṃ tasya pradhānakālatvāt | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	ahorātroṣite snāte ārdravāsasi mānave |

	pūrvāhṇe sarvadivyānāṃ pradānam anukīrtitam ||

yat tu yājñavalkyenoktam,

	sacelasnātam āhūya sūryodaya upoṣitam |

	kārayet sarvadivyāni nṛpabrāhmaṇasaṃnidhau ||

iti, tatra sūryodayapadena pūrvāhṇa eva vacobhaṅgyā vihita ity avagantavyam | pūrvāhṇaś cādityavārānvita eva grāhyaḥ śiṣṭācārabalāt | homād anantaraṃ pitāmahaḥ |

	yaṃ cārtham abhiyuktaḥ syāl likhitvā taṃ tu patrake |

	mantreṇānena sahitaṃ tat kāryaṃ tu śirogatam ||

anena vakṣyamāṇenety arthaḥ | tam eva mantraṃ darsayati |

	ādityacandrāv anilo 'nalaś ca dyaur bhūmir āpo hṛdayaṃ yamaś ca |

	ahaś ca rātriś ca ubhe ca saṃdhye dharmaś ca jānāti narasya vṛttam || iti |

ayaṃ ca vidhiḥ sarvadivyasādhāraṇa ity āha sa eva |

	imaṃ mantravidhiṃ kṛtsnaṃ sarvadivyeṣu yojayet |

	imaṃ mantravidhiṃ kṛtsnaṃ sarvadivyeṣu yojayet |

	āvāhanaṃ ca devānāṃ tathaiva parikīrtitam ||

dharmāvāhanādi śodhyaśirasi patrāropaṇāntaṃ sarvadivyeṣu kartavyam ity arthaḥ | tathā sarvadivyeṣu prayogāvasāne ṛtvigādibhyo dakṣiṇāṃ tuṣṭikarīṃ dadyāt | tathā ca sa eva |

	ṛtvikpurohitācāryān dakṣiṇābhiś ca toṣayet || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ sarvadivyasādhāraṇavidhiḥ **

**atha dhaṭāropaṇavidhiḥ**

tatra nāradaḥ |

	śikyadvayaṃ samāsajya dhaṭakarkaṭayor dṛḍham |

	ekatra śikye puruṣam anyatra tulayec chilām ||

vidhivan nirmitadhaṭakarkaṭakadvaye śikyadvayapāśau samāsajyety arthaḥ | śilāgrahaṇaṃ mṛdāder upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva pitāmahaḥ |

	śikyadvayaṃ samāsajya pārśvayor ubhayor api |

	prāgagrān kalpayed darbhān śikyayor ubhyor api ||

	paścime tolayet kartṝn anyasmin mṛttikāṃ śubhām |

	iṣṭakābhasmapāṣāṇakapālāsthivivarjitām || iti |

iṣṭakāpāṣāṇayor mṛdā saha samuccayo nivāryate na tu vikalpaḥ, tayor api vihitatvāt | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	piṭakaṃ pūrayet tasminn iṣṭakāgrāvapāṃsubhiḥ | iti |

iṣṭakābhiḥ grāvabhiḥ pāṃsubhir vety arthaḥ | māṣair vā piṭakaṃ pūrayet, "māṣarāśim athāpi vā" iti smṛtyantaravacanāt | evaṃ ca śilāmṛttikeṣṭakāgrāvapāṃsumāṣāṇāṃ pratimānatve vikalpo veditavyaḥ | ata eva nāradenoktam |

	mṛtpiṇḍam abhiśastaṃ ca tulāyāṃ dhārayet samam |

	dhārayed uttare pārśve puruṣaṃ dakṣiṇe śilām || iti |

uttare pārśva ity etad dakṣiṇodagāyatatvena nirmitatulāviṣayam | yady api tathā nirmāṇaṃ pūrvam anupadiṣṭam, tathāpy asmād eva vacanāt pūrvāparasaṃsthānau pādastanbhau kṛtvodagagrā tulā kadācit kāryety arthāt siddham iti na kaścid virodhaḥ | tulāṃ dhārayed vaṇigādīnām anyatama iti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca viṣṇuḥ: "tāṃ ca vaṇiksuvarṇakārakāṃsyakārāṇām anyatamo bibhṛyāt" iti | tāṃ tulām ity arthaḥ | anyatamena dhṛtāyāḥ samatānirīkṣaṇārthaṃ rājñā te sarve niyoktavyāḥ | tathā ca pitāmahaḥ |

	parīkṣakā niyoktavyāḥ tulāmānaviśāradāḥ |

	vaṇijo hemakārāś ca kāṃsyakārās tathaiva ca ||

niyuktāś ca samatām nirīkṣeran | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	suvarṇakārā vaṇijaḥ kusalāḥ kāṃsyakarakāḥ |

	tāṃ tulām anvavekṣeran tulādhāraṇakovidāḥ ||

nrīkṣakān pratyāha pitāmahaḥ |

	kāryaḥ parīkṣakair nityam avalambasamo dhaṭaḥ |

	udakaṃ ca pradātavyaṃ dhaṭasyopari paṇḍitaiḥ ||

	yasmin na plavate toyaṃ sa vijñeyaḥ samo dhaṭaḥ || iti |

toraṇayor lambamānau mṛṇmayāv avalambau tayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ kaṭakadvayoparibhāgena samo yasya so 'valambasamo dhaṭaḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	prathamārohaṇe grāhyaṃ pramāṇaṃ nipuṇaiḥ saha |

	tulāśirobhyāṃ tulyaṃ tu toraṇanyastalakṣaṇam ||

samatāvadhāraṇāntaraṃ viṣṇuḥ: "pratimānapuruṣau samadhṛtau sucihnitau kṛtvā puruṣam avatārayet" iti | sucihnitau samatādaśāyāṃ yeṣv avayaveṣu śkyarajjavaḥ saṃyuktās tatra tatra pāṇḍurekhāṅkitāv ity arthaḥ | avatāraṇānantaraṃ pitāmahaḥ |

	tolayitvā naraṃ pūrvaṃ paścāt tam avatārya tu |

	dhaṭaṃ tu kārayen nityaṃ patākādhvajaśobhitam || iti |

evam upakalpanānantaraṃ dharmāvāhanādi śodhyaśirasi patrāropaṇāntaṃ sarvadivyasādhāraṇavidhiṃ kuryāt | tathā ca sa eva |

	imaṃ mantravidhiṃ kṛtsnaṃ sarvadivyeṣu yojayet |

	āvāhanaṃ ca devānāṃ tathaiva parikalpayet || iti |

tatra dharmārādhanasādhaneṣu viśeṣam āha nāradaḥ |

	raktair gandhaiś ca mālyaiś ca dadhyapūpākṣatādibhiḥ |

	arcayet tu dhaṭaṃ pūrvaṃ tataḥ śiṣṭāṃs tu pūjayet || iti |

dhaṭaṃ dhaṭādhiṣṭhitaṃ dharmam, śiṣṭān indrādīn | śodhyaśirasi patrāropaṇanantaraṃ pitāmahaḥ |

	dhaṭam āmantrayec caivaṃ vidhinānena śāstravit |

	tvaṃ dhaṭa brahmaṇā sṛṣṭaḥ parīkṣārthaṃ durātmanām ||

	dhakārād dharmamūrtis tvaṃ ṭakārāt kuṭilaṃ naram |

	dhṛto bhāvayase yasmād dhatas tenābhidhīyase || iti |

śāstravit prāḍvivākaḥ,

	divyeṣu sarvakāryāṇi prāḍvivākaḥ samācaret |

iti tenaivoktatvāt | tataḥ śodhyo 'pi taṃ dhaṭam āmantrayet | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	tulādhāraṇavidvadbhir abhiyuktas tulāśritaḥ |

	pratimānasamībhūto rekhāṃ kṛtvāvatāritaḥ ||

	tvaṃ tule satyadhāmāsi purā devair vinirmitā |

	tat satyaṃ vada kalyāṇi saṃśayān māṃ vimocaya ||

	yady asmi pāpakṛn mātaḥ tato māṃ tvam adho naya |

	śuddhaś ced gamayordhvaṃ māṃ tulām ity abhimantrayet || iti |

tvaṃ tule ityādinā ūrdhvaṃ mām ity antena mantreṇa punar āropaṇāt prāk tulām abhimantrayet śodhya ity arthaḥ | tatas taṃ prāḍvivākaḥ punar āropayet | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	samayaiḥ parigṛhyātha punar āropayen naram |

	nivāte vṛṣṭirahite śirasyāropya patrakam ||

samayaiḥ parigṛhya tulādhārakaṃ śapathair niyamyety arthaḥ | śapathāś ca tenaiva darśitāḥ |

	brahmaghno ye smṛtā lokā ye lokāḥ kūṭasākṣiṇaḥ |

	tulādhārasya ye lokās tulāṃ dhārayato mṛṣā || iti |

punarāropaṇānantaraṃ nāradaḥ |

	tasminn eva kṛte lakṣye lakṣyaṃ kṛtvā dvijottamaḥ |

	dharmaparyāyaśabdena dhaṭa ity abhidhīyase ||

	tvaṃ vetsi sarvabhūtānāṃ pāpāni sukṛtāni ca |

	tvam eva deva jānīṣe na vidur yāni mānavāḥ||

	vyavahārābhiśasto 'yaṃ mānavas tolyate tvayā |

	tad enaṃ saṃśayārūḍhaṃ dharmatas trātum arhasi ||

	devāsuramanuṣyāṇāṃ satye tvam atiricyase |

	satyasaṃdho 'si bhagavañ chubhāśubhavibhāvanaiḥ ||

	ādityacandrāv anilo 'nalaś ca dyaur bhūmir āpo hṛdayaṃ yamaś ca |

	ahaś ca rātriś ca ubhe ca saṃdhye dharmaś ca jānāti narasya vṛttam || iti |

śodhyaṃ śikye yathāsaṃniveśaṃ nidhāya dharmetyādi vṛttam ityantaṃ prāḍvivāko vadec ity arthaḥ | mantroccāraṇānantaraṃ pitāmahaḥ |

	jyotirvit brāhmaṇaśreṣṭhaḥ kuryāt kālaparīkṣaṇam |

	vināḍyaḥ pañca vijñeyāḥ parīkṣyāḥ kālakovidaiḥ ||

	sākṣiṇo brāhmaṇaśreṣṭāḥ yathādṛṣṭārthavādinaḥ |

	jñāninaḥ śucayo 'lubdhāḥ niyoktavyāḥ nṛpeṇa tu ||

	teṣāṃ vacanato gamyaḥ śuddhyaśuddhivinirṇayaḥ || iti |

triśatagurvakṣaroccāraṇakālaḥ pañcavināḍyātmako bhavati | tathā ca smṛtyantaram |

	daśagurvakṣaraḥ prāṇaḥ ṣaṭprāṇaḥ syād vināḍikā | iti |

evaṃ ca jyotirvid brāhmaṇo gurvakṣaroccāraṇena pañcavināḍyātmakakālamānaṃ kuryāt | śodhyas tāvatkālaṃ tulām āruhyāsīta | tasmin kāle jayaparājayalakṣaṇaiḥ śuddhyaśuddhivinirṇayaṃ niyuktāḥ sākṣiṇaḥ kuryur iti pūrvoktavacanānām arthaḥ pratyetavyaḥ | kāni punar jayaparājayalakṣaṇānīty apekṣite nāradaḥ |

	tulito yadi vardheta viśuddhaḥ syān na saṃśayaḥ |

	samo vā hīyamāno vā na viśuddho bhaven naraḥ ||

yat punaḥ pitāmahenoktam,

	hīyamāno na śuddhaḥ syād ekeṣāṃ tu samo 'śuciḥ |

	alpapāpaḥ samo jñeyo bahupāpas tu hīyate || iti |

tatraikeṣām iti pūjanārtham, na tu svamate samasthaśuddhitvadyotanārtham | alpapāpino 'py aśucitvāt | tena hīyamānasamayoḥ parājaye na kaścid viśeṣaḥ | daṇḍe prāyaścitte ca paraṃ viśeṣaḥ, daṇḍaprāyaścittayor doṣānusāritvāt | yat tūktaṃ bṛhaspatinā,

	dhaṭe 'bhiyuktas tulito hīnaś ced dhānim āpnuyāt |

	tatsamas tu punas tolyo vardhito vijayī bhavet || 

iti, tasyāyam arthaḥ: samasyāścutvaniścayo na prathamatolanaparyāye kāryaḥ, kiṃ tu punas tolyamānasya tu yadi samastaiva bhavati tadānīm aśuddhir avadhāraṇīyeti | evaṃ śikyacchedādāv api punas tolyamānasya śuddhir aśuddhir vāvadhāraṇīyā | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	śikyacchede tulābhaṅge tathāpi tu guṇasya vā |

	śuddhes tu saṃśaye caiva parīkṣeta punar naram ||

śuddhes tu saṃśayo nāradena prapañcitaḥ |

	tulāśirobhyām udbhrāntaṃ vicalaṃ nyastalakṣaṇam |

	yadā vāyuprapanno 'sau gacchaty ūrdhvam adho 'pi vā ||

	nirmuktaḥ sahasā vāpi tadā naikataraṃ vrajet || iti |

ayam arthaḥ: yadā tulāntau tiryak pracalitau, yadā ca samatājñānārthaṃ nyastam udakādi calitam, yadā ca vāyunāpreritā tulā ūrdhvam adhaś ca kampate, yadā ca tulā dhārakeṇa hastāt pramucyate tadā jayaṃ parājayaṃ vā na niścinuyād iti | yat punas tenoktam,

	kakṣyacchede tulābhaṅge dhaṭakarkaṭayos tathā |

	rajjucchede 'kṣabhaṅge ca mūrchitaḥ śuddhim āpnuyāt ||

iti, tad aparidṛśyamānakāraṇakaśikyacchedādiviṣayam, daivikasyaiva śikyacchedādeḥ śuddhikāṇatvāt (?) | tatra pitāmahaḥ |

	śaṃsanti sākṣiṇaḥ sarve śuddhyaśuddhī nṛpe tathā |

	sadbhiḥ parivṛto rājā śuddham āhūya pūjayet ||

	ṛtvikpurohitācāryān dakṣiṇābhiś ca toṣayet |

	evaṃ kārayitā rājā bhuktvā bhogān manoramān ||

	mahatīṃ kīrtim āpnoti brahmabhūyāya kalpate | iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ dhaṭāropaṇavidhiḥ**

**athāgnividhiḥ**

tatra pitāmahaḥ |

	agner vidhiṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāvac chāstracoditam |

	kārayen maṇḍalāny aṣṭau purastān navamaṃ tathā ||

prakhyātadevatāyatanādivihitadeśe bhūśuddhim uddhananāvokṣaṇābhyāṃ kṛtvā tatra nava maṇḍalāni prāgapavargāṇi prāḍvivākaḥ sopavāso nṛpājñayā pravṛttaḥ kuryād ity arthaḥ | tāni ca gomayena kāryāṇi,

	gomayena kṛtāni syur adbhiḥ paryukṣitāni ca |

iti tenaiva smṛtatvāt | teṣām antarālaparimāṇe ubhe api yājñavalkyena darśite |

	ṣoḍaśāṅgulakaṃ jñeyaṃ maṇḍalaṃ tāvad antaram | iti |

maṇḍalāni teṣām antarālāni ca pratyekaṃ ṣaḍaśāṅgulaparimāṇāni kāryāṇīty arthaḥ | maṇḍaladevatās tu pitāmahena darśitāḥ |

	āgneyaṃ maṇḍalaṃ tv ādyaṃ dvitīyaṃ vāruṇaṃ smṛtam |

	tṛtīyaṃ vasudevatyaṃ caturthaṃ yamadevatam ||

	pañcamaṃ tv indradevatyaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ kauberam ucyate |

	saptamaṃ somadevatyaṃ sāvitraṃ tv aṣṭamaṃ tathā ||

	navamaṃ sarvadevatyam iti divyavido (?) viduḥ | iti |

agnir atra pūjyata ity āgneyam, haviṣṭvena (?) sūktatvena vā vā maṇḍalasyāgreyatvāsaṃbhavāt | evaṃ vāruṇatvādikam api maṇḍalasya pūjādhikaraṇatayā draṣṭavyam | tena "praitu hotuś camasaḥ" ityādipraiṣamantrasthayā hotuś camasa ityādisamākhyayā hotrādīnāṃ tatra camasabhakṣaprāptivad āgneyādisamākhyayaivāgnyādīnāṃ tatra tatra maṇḍale pūjanaṃ kāryam ity asmād eva vacanāt prasiddham | ato maṇḍalānāṃ prokṣaṇānantaraṃ maṇḍalādhidevatāpūjanaṃ kuryāt | tataḥ pratimaṇḍalaṃ prāgagrān kuśān kṣipet,

	maṇḍale maṇḍale deyāḥ kuśāḥ śāstrapracoditāḥ |

iti tenaiva smṛtatvāt | tataḥ prathamamaṇdalād dakṣiṇato 'natidūre laukikāgniṃ pratiṣṭhāpya śāntihomaṃ kuryāt,

	śāntyarthaṃ juhuyād agnau ghṛtam aṣṭottaraṃ śatam |

iti smaraṇāt | homaś ca "agnaye pāvakāya svāhā" ity anena mantreṇa kārya ity uktaṃ vyākhyātṛbhiḥ | tatas tasmin agnau lohapiṇḍaṃ tāpayet | tathā ca pitāmahaḥ |

	aśrihīnaṃ samaṃ kṛtvā aṣṭāṅgulam ayomayam |

	piṇḍaṃ tu tāpayed agnau pañcāśatpalakṃ samam ||

samam animnonnatam | punaḥ samagrahaṇaṃ samantāt tāpayed iti vidhānārtham | ṣoḍaśapalakaṃ vā piṇḍaṃ tapayet | "atha saptāśvatthaparṇāntaritaṃ ṣoḍaśapalam agnivarṇaṃ lohapiṇḍam añjalinādāya saptamaryādāṃ gacchet" iti śaṅkhalikhitasmaraṇāt | tāpanaṃ tu lohakāreṇa kāryam ity āha nāradaḥ |

	jātyaiva lohakāro yaḥ kuśalaś cāgnikarmaṇi |

	dṛṣṭaprayogaś cānyatra tenāyo 'gnau tu tāpayet ||

dṛṣṭaprayogaś cānyatrety anena yathā loke lohaśuddhyarthaṃ sutaptaṃ loham udake nikṣipya punaḥ saṃtāpyodake nikṣipya punaḥ saṃtāpanaṃ lohekāryasiddhyarthaṃ (?) kriyate tathātrāpi kartavyam iti darśitam | tatra tṛtīyatāpe vartamāne dharmāvāhanādi śodhyaśirasi patrāropaṇāntaṃ sarvadivyasādhāraṇavidhiṃ kuryāt | tathā ca pitāmahaḥ |

	imaṃ mantravidhiṃ kṛtsnaṃ sarvadivyeṣu yojayet |

	āvāhanaṃ ca devānāṃ tathaiva parikalpayet || iti |

tatra dharmārādhanasādhaneṣu viśeṣam āha sa eva |

	tatra pūjāṃ hutāśasya kārayen manujādhipaḥ |

	raktacandanadhūpābhyāṃ raktapuṣpais tathaiva ca || iti |

hutāśasya lohapiṇḍāgnāv āvāhitasya dharmasyeti yāvat | raktacandanaṃ ca dhūpaś ca raktacandanadhūpau, tābhyām | indrādyārādhanasādhaneṣu nāyaṃ niyamaḥ, hutāśasyeti viśeṣitatvāt | śirasyāropite pratijñāpatre saty anantaraṃ śodhyasya kartavyam āha hārītaḥ |

	prāṅmukhas tu tatas tiṣṭhet prasāritakarāṅguliḥ |

	ārdravāsāḥ śuciś caiva śirasy āropya patrakam ||

sthitiś cādhyamaṇḍale kartavyā,

	paścime maṇḍale tiṣṭhet prāṅmukhaḥ prāñjaliḥ śuciḥ |

iti pitāmahasmaraṇāt | śodhyasya prāḍvivākasya ca kartavyam āha viṣṇuḥ |

	karu vimṛditavrīhī tasyādāv eva lakṣayet | iti |

vimṛditā vrīhayo yābhyāṃ tau vimṛditavrhī | anena karābhyāṃ vrīhimardanaṃ kṛtvā śodhyaḥ prasāritakarāṅguliḥ syād ity arthād uktam | lakṣayed ity asyārtho nāradena prapañcitaḥ |

	lakṣayet tasya cihnāni hastayor ubhayor api |

	prākṛtāni ca gūḍhāni savraṇāny avraṇāni ca ||

agnidhāraṇāt prāktanāny etānīti jñāpanarthaṃ tasya śodhyasya karadvayasthitavraṇādisthāneṣu alaktakādirasena haṃsapadāni kuryād ity arthaḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	hastakṣateṣu sarveṣu kuryād dhaṃsapadāni tu | iti |

tataḥ kartavyam āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	karau vimṛditavrīhī lakṣayitvā tato nyaset |

	saptāśvatthasya parṇāni tāvat sūtreṇa veṣṭayet ||

viṣṇur api: "tataḥ prāṅmukhasya prasāritabhujadvayasya saptāśvatthasya patrāṇi karayor dadyāt, tāni ca karadvayasahitāni sūtreṇa veṣṭayet" iti | ubhayatrāpi tataḥ śabdenedaṃ jñāyate: hastāṅkanapatranyasanayor madhye yat smṛtyantaroktaṃ homādi tad asmin mate na kartavyam iti | evaṃ ca yad uktaṃ nāradena:

	kṛtvaivam abhiśastasya prathamaṃ hastalakṣaṇam |

	śāntyarthaṃ juhuyān mantrair ghṛtenāgnau yathāvidhi ||

	tarpiteṣv atha deveṣu lokapāleṣu caiva hi |

	ādityābhimukho bhūtvā imaṃ mantram udīrayet ||

	tvam agne sarvabhūtānām antaś carasi sākṣivat |

	havyaṃ vahasi devānāṃ hutaḥ śāntiṃ prayacchasi ||

	pracchannāni manuṣyāṇāṃ pāpāni sukṛtāni ca |

	tvam eva deva jānīṣe na vidur yāni mānavāḥ ||

	vyavahārābhiśasto 'haṃ vahne tiṣṭhāmi saṃśaye |

	tasmān māṃ saṃśayārūḍhaṃ dharmatas trātum arhasi ||

	evam uktavatas tasya prāṅmukhasya tu dhīmataḥ |

	patrair añjalim āpūrya āśvatthaiḥ saptabhiḥ smaiḥ || iti |

maitraiḥ "ākṛṣṇena" ityādibhiḥ navabhiḥ grahaprakāśakaiḥ | deveṣu vasvādityarudreṣu lokapāleṣu ca tattannāmnā hutaghṛtādyāhutibhis tarpiteṣu satsv ity arthaḥ | tad etat sarvaṃ vaikalpikam iti mantavyam | yat tu patraviśeṣaṇam uktaṃ samair iti tan nityam, tena pakṣadvaye 'pi samaparimāṇaiḥ patrair bhavitavyam | tathā veṣṭanasūtreṣv api viśeṣas tena darśitaḥ |

	veṣṭayīta sitair hastau saptabhiḥ sūtratantubhiḥ | iti |

sitaiḥ śvetair ity arthaḥ | yat tu smṛtyantaram,

	ayas taptaṃ tu pāṇibhyām arkapatrais tu saptabhiḥ |

	antarhitaṃ haran śuddhas tv adagdhaḥ saptame pade ||

iti, tad aśvatthapatrālābhaviṣayam | yad āha pitāmahaḥ |

	pippalāj jāyate vahniḥ pippalo vṛkṣarāṭ smṛtaḥ |

	atas tasya tu patrāṇi hastayor nikṣiped budhaḥ || iti |

yasmāt praśasto 'śvatthaḥ tasmāt patrāṇy eva sati saṃbhave grāhyāṇīty arthaḥ | śamīpatrādīni punaḥ pūrvoktapatraiḥsaha samuccīyante | tathā ca smṛtyantaram |

	sapta pippalapatrāṇi samīpatrāṇy athāpi vā |

	dūrvāyāḥ sapta patrāṇi dadyāt tāṃś cākṣatān nyaset ||

tathā kusumāni ca nyaset,

	sapta pippalapatrāṇi akṣatān sumanodadhi (?) |

iti pitāmahasmaraṇāt | sumanasaḥ kusumāni | tatas taptalohapiṇḍe prāḍvivākaḥ "tvam agne devāḥ" ityadinā "mahānala" ityantena mantreṇa lohapiṇḍastham agnim abhimantrayet | tathā ca pitāmahaḥ |

	tāpite tu tataḥ paścād agnim āvāhayec chuciḥ |

	āvāhanaṃ tu devānāṃ kṛtvā pūrvavidhānavit ||

	tvam agne devāś catvāras tvaṃ ca yajñeṣu hūyase |

	tvaṃ mukhaṃ sarvadevānāṃ tvaṃ mukhaṃ brahmavādinām ||

	jaṭharastho hi bhūtānāṃ tato vetsi śubhāśubham |

	pāpaṃ punāsi vai yasmāt tasmāt pāvaka ucyase ||

	pāpeṣu darśayātmānam arciṣmān bhava pāvaka |

	atha vā śuddhabhāveṣu śīto bhava mahānala || iti |

devānāṃ dharmādīnām āvāhanagrahaṇam āvāhanādeḥ śodhyakarasaṃskārakusumanidhānāntasya karmaṇa upalakṣaṇārtham | viṣṇus tu lohapiṇḍasthāgnyabhimantraṇe mantrāntaram āha |

	tvam agne sarvabhūtānām antas carasi sākṣivat |

	tvam evāgne vijānīṣe na vidur yāni mānuṣāḥ ||

	vyavahārābhiśasto 'yaṃ mānuṣaḥ suddhim icchati |

	tad enaṃ saṃśayād asmād dharmatas trātum arhasi ||

samuccayenāsya mantrasya abhimantraṇasādhanatvaṃ na punar vikalpena, prārthanīyārthasya śodhyavyaktiviśeṣaniṣṭhatayā prakāśakatvena bhinnakāryatvāt | yat tu,

	tṛtīyatāpe saṃtaptaṃ brūyāt sabhyapuraskṛtam |

	śṛṇv imaṃ mānavaṃ dharmaṃ lokapālair adhiṣṭhitam ||

	tvam agne sarvadevānāṃ pavitraṃ paramaṃ mukham |

	tvam eva sarvabhūtānāṃ hṛdistho vetsi ceṣṭitam ||

	satyānṛte ca jihvā vā tvattaḥ samupalabhyate |

	devādibhir idaṃ proktaṃ nānyathā kartum arhasi ||

	anenāsāv idaṃ prokto mithyāvādam asau vadet |

	sarvathā ca yathā mithyā tathāgniṃ dhārayāmy aham ||

	sa eṣa tvāṃ dhārayati satyenānena mānavaḥ |

	satyavākyasya cāsya tvaṃ śīto bhava hutāśana ||

	mṛṣāvākyasya pāpasya daha hastau ca pāpinaḥ ||

iti, yat tu nāradoktam agnyabhimantraṇam, tat viṣṇupitāmahoktenāgnyabhimantraṇena vikalpyate, ekārthatvāt | yadā nāradoktāgnyabhimantraṇaṃ kriyate tadābhimantraṇānantraṃ kartavyam āha sa eva |

	amum arthaṃ ca patrastham abhiyuktaṃ yathārthataḥ |

	saṃśrāvya mūrdhni tasyaiva nyasya deyo yathākriyam ||

pūrvoktābhimantraṇamantrārthaṃ śirasi nihitapatrasthamantrārthaṃ ca saṃśrāvya tat patraṃ yathāsthānaṃ nidhāya lohapiṇḍo deya ity arthaḥ | yadā tu viṣṇupitāmahoktāgnyabhimantraṇaṃ kriyate tadā tasmin kṛte kartavyam āha pitāmahaḥ |

	tatas taṃ samupādāya rājā dharmaparāyaṇaḥ |

	saṃdaṃśena niyukto vā hastayos tasya nikṣipet ||

saṃdaṃśena taṃ lohapiṇḍaṃ samupādāyety anvayaḥ | niyuktaḥ prāḍvivākaḥ | nikṣepaṇāt prāk śodhyasya pakṣadvaye 'pi kartavyam āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	tvam agne sarvabhūtānām antaś carasi pāvaka |

	sākṣivat puṇyapāpebhyo brūhi satyaṃ kave mama ||

	tasyety uktavato lohaṃ pañcāśatpalikaṃ samam |

	agnivarṇaṃ nyaset piṇḍaṃ hastayor ubhayor api ||

ityuktavataḥ pūrvoktāgnyabhimantraṇaṃ kṛtavatas tasya śodhyasyety arthaḥ | nyaste lohapiṇḍe śodhyasya kartavyam āha sa eva |

	sa tam ādāya saptaiva maṇḍalāni śanair vrajet | iti |

asyārtho viṣṇunā vivṛtaḥ: "tam ādāya nātidrutaṃ na ca vilambitaṃ maṇḍaleṣu padanyāsaṃ kurvan vrajet" iti | maṇḍaleṣu dvitīyādiṣv aṣṭamānteṣv ity arthaḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	hastābhyāṃ taṃ samādāya prāḍvivākasamīritaḥ |

	sthitvaikasmiṃs tato 'nyāni vrajet sapta tv ajihmagaḥ ||

	asaṃbhrāntaḥ śanair gacched akruddhaḥ so 'nalaṃ prati |

	na pātayet tām aprāpya yā bhūmiḥ parikalpitā ||

	na maṇḍalam atikrāmen na cārvāk sthāpayet padam |

	maṇḍalaṃ cāṣṭamaṃ gatvā tato 'gniṃ visṛjen naraḥ || iti |

ekasmin ādye maṇḍala ity arthaḥ | tato 'nyāni dvitīyādīni | agnivisarjanaṃ ca navame maṇḍale kartavyam,

	aṣṭamaṃ maṇḍalaṃ gatvā navame nikṣiped budhaḥ |

iti pitāmahasmaraṇāt | nikṣepānantaraṃ parīkṣakasya kartavyam āha naradaḥ |

	tasyaiva muktapiṇdasya kuryāt karanirīkṣaṇam | iti |

śuddhyaśuddhiparijñānārtham iti seṣaḥ | tatrāśuddhipratyāyakāni lakṣaṇāny āha sa eva |

	pūrvadṛṣṭeṣu cihnaṣu tato 'nyatrāpi lakṣayet |

	maṇḍalaṃ raktasaṅkāśaṃ yatrānyac cāgnisaṃbhavam ||

	so 'viśuddhas tu vijñeyo 'satyadharmavyavasthitaḥ || iti |

yasya karataladvayamadhye yatrakutracid āhāritaṃ sphoṭakādyupalabhyate tam aśuddhaṃ vijānīyād ity arthaḥ | yasya punar nopalabhyate sa śuddho vijñeyaḥ | tathā ca viṣṇuḥ |

	yo hastayoḥ kvaciddagdhas tam aśuddhaṃ vinirdiset |

	na dagdhaḥ sarvathā yas tu sa viśuddho bhaven naraḥ ||

yadā tu dagdhādagdhasaṃdehaḥ tadāha nāradaḥ |

	jñānena na vibhāgaś ced dagdhāv iti karau tadā |

	vrīhīn atiprayatnena saptavārāṃs tu dāpayet ||

	mardito yadi no dagdhaḥ sabhyais tv evaṃ viniścitam |

	mocyaḥ śuddhas tu satkṛtya dagdho daṇḍyo yathākramam || iti |

pitāmaho 'pi |

	hṛte ca mardayet paścād vrīhīn vā yadi vā yavān |

	nirvikāre dinasyānte śuddhaṃ tam iti nirdiśet || iti |

nirvikāre karadvaye sthite śuddham iti taṃ nirdiśed ity arthaḥ | kecit "nirvikārau yadā hastau" iti paṭhanti | tanmate haraṇāntaram eva mardanena śuddhir avadhāraṇīyā | nanu "dinasyānte śuddhaṃ tam iti nirdiśet" iti pāṭhe,

	muktvāgniṃ mṛditavrīhir adagdhaḥ śuddhim āpnuyāt |

iti yājñavalkyavacanavirodhaḥ syāt | maivaṃ vocaḥ, "prahṛtya paridhīn juhoti" itivad ānantaryābhāve 'pi ktvānirdeśopapatteḥ | yat punas tenoktam,

	antarā patite piṇḍe saṃdehe vā punar haret |

iti, tat vrīhimardane kṛte 'pi yatra saṃdeho nāpaiti tadviṣayam, kiṃ satyānṛtavaśād adāhadāhau uta dṛṣṭavyavadhānādikāraṇavaśād iti yatra saṃdehas tadviṣayaṃ ca | "antarā patite piṇḍe" ity atra dagdhaś ca nopalabhyate iti śeṣo 'vagantavyaḥ | dagdhasyopalambhe tv aśuddhiniścayena punarharaṇānavakāśāt | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	yas tv antarā pātayati dagdaś ca na vibhāvyate |

	punas taṃ hārayed agniṃ sthitir eṣā dṛḍhīkṛtā ||

dagdhaś ca na vibhāvyate karataladvayābhyantare iti śeṣaḥ | anyatra dagdhavibhāvane 'pi punar hārayed eva | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	praskhalaty abhiyuktaś cet sthānād anyatra dahyate |

	adagdhaṃ taṃ vidur devās tasya bhūyo 'pi dāpayet ||

bhūyo 'pi punar apīty arthaḥ | atra nāradaḥ |

	anena vidhinā kāryo hutāśasamayaḥ sadā |

	ṛte grīṣmād asāv uktaḥ kāle 'nyasmiṃs tu śītale || iti |

**iti smṛticandikāyām agnividhiḥ **

**atha jalaviṣayor utsannānuṣṭhānatvāt tadvidhim anākhyāya kośavidhir ucyate** 

tatra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	devān ugrān samabhyarcya tatsnānodakam āharet | iti |

ugrā devā rudradurgādityādayaḥ | teṣām anyatamaṃ devaṃ prāḍvivākaḥ kṛtopavāso gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ saṃpūjya snāpayitvā tatsnānodakaṃ divyadeśaṃ nayed ity arthaḥ | naraṃ tatra nidhāya dharmāvāhanādi śodhyaśirasi patrāropaṇāntaṃ sarvadivyasādhāraṇavidhiṃ vidhāya śodhyaṃ ca prāṅmukhaṃ kṛtvā pūrvanihitodakāt prasṛtitrayaṃ pāyayet | prasṛtitrayamaṇḍalaṃ ca tasminn eva kāle gomayena kāryam iti vyākhyatṛbhir uktam | ādityābhimukhaṃ kṛtvā saṃśrāvya pāyayet | tathā ca yājñavlkyaḥ |

	saṃśrāvya pāyayet paścāj jalāt tu prasṛtitrayam | iti |

kiṃ saṃśrāvyety apekṣite nāradaḥ |

	enaś ca śrāvayitvā tu pāyayet prasṛtitrayam | iti |

enaḥ pāpaṃ tac ca tatphalābhidhānamukhena tenaiva darśitam |

	svecchayā yaḥ pibet kośaṃ kascic ched dūṣito naraḥ |

	visaṃvaden naro lobhāc chalī bhavati durmatiḥ ||

	ātmanaḥ kāmakāreṇa kośaṃ pītvā visaṃvadet |

	daridro vyādhito mūrkhaḥ saptajanmani jāyate ||

	balāt kośaṃ hi yo datvā hitam icchen na cātmanaḥ |

	sa vināśī bhavet tasya tac ca kāryaṃ na sidhyati || iti |

atrāntyaślokam abhiyoktā śrāvayitavyaḥ sāmarthyāt | śodhyas tu śrāvitaṃ śrutvedaṃ matyā na kṛtam iti vadan pibet | tathā ca viṣṇuḥ: "ugrān devān abhyarcya tatsnānodakāt prasṛtitrayaṃ pibed idaṃ matyā na kṛtam iti vyāharan devatābhimukhaḥ" iti | evaṃ yasya kasyacid ugradevasya snānodakam āhṛtya kośānuṣṭhāne prāpte niyamārtham āha pitāmahaḥ |

	bhakto yo yasya devasya pāyayet tasya tajjalam |

	samabhāve tu devānām ādityasya tu pāyayet ||

	durgāyāḥ pāyayec corān ye ca śastropajīvinaḥ |

	bhāskarasya tu yat toyaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ tan na pāyayet || iti |

tathā snāpanīyapradesaniyamam āha sa eva |

	durgāyāḥ snāpayec chūlam ādityasya tu maṇḍalam |

	anyeṣām api devānāṃ snāpayed āyudhāni tu || iti |

prasṛtitrayapānād anantaraṃ kātyāyanaḥ |

	atha daivavisaṃvādaḥ trisaptāhāt tu dāpayet |

	abhiyuktaṃ prasannena tam arthaṃ daṇḍam eva ca ||

daivavisaṃvādo daivikavyādhīnām āvirbhāvaḥ | daivikāś ca vyādhayas tenaiva darśitāḥ |

	kṣayātisāravisphoṭās tālvasthiparipīḍanam |

	netraruggalarogaś ca tathonmādaḥ prajāpate ||

	śiroruk bhujabhaṅgaś ca daivikā vyādhayo nṛṇām || iti |

anyāny api parājayanimittāni viṣṇunā darsitāni |

	yasya pasyed dvisaptāhāt trisaptāhād athāpi vā |

	rogo 'gner jñātimaraṇaṃ rājadaṇḍam athāpi vā ||

	tam aśuddhaṃ vijānīyāt tathā suddhaṃ viparyaye || iti |

nāradenārthabhraṃśādayo 'pi parājaye uktāḥ |

	saptāhābhyantare yasya dvisaptāhena vā punaḥ |

	rogo 'gnir jjātimaraṇam arthabhraṃśo dhanakṣayaḥ ||

	pratyātmikaṃ bhaved yasya vidyāt tasya parājayam || iti |

pratyātmikaṃ na samudāyaprayuktam | artho 'tra putrādir abhipretaḥ, anyathā dhanaśabdavaiyarthyāt | ata eva bṛhaspatiḥ |

	saptāhād vā dvisaptāhād yasyārtir na prajāyate |

	putradāradhanānāṃ ca sa śuddhaḥ syān na saṃśayaḥ ||

pitāmahenāvadhyantaram apy uktam |

	trirātrāt saptarātrād vā dvisaptāhād athāpi vā |

	vaikṛtaṃ yasya dṛśyeta pākakṛt sa tu mānavaḥ ||

yasya śodhyasyety arthaḥ | na kevalaṃ śodhyasya vikṛtatvāpattau pāpakṛttvam, api tu svakīyajanasya vikṛtatvāpatāv apīty āha sa eva |

	tasyaikasya na sarvasya janasya yadi tad bhavet |

	rogo 'gnir jñātimaraṇaṃ saiva tasya vibhāvanā ||

tad rogādivaikṛtaṃ kṛtakośapānasyaikasya yadi bhavet tad eva pāpakṛttvam iti na, kiṃ tu tadīyajanasya sarvasya madhye yadā yasya kasyacid bhavet tadāpīty arthaḥ | manunāpy avadhyantaram uktam |

	na cārtim ṛcchati kṣipraṃ sa jñeyaḥ śapathaiḥ śuciḥ || iti |

ārtiḥ pūrvokto rogādiḥ | kṣipraṃ śīghram, ekarātrād arvāg iti yāvat | ayaṃ cāvadhiḥ svalpakāryanirṇāyakasatyādisapathaviṣayaḥ svalpakālīnāyāḥ śuddhibhāvanāyās tatraivocitatvāt, satyādiśapathān prastutyābhihitatvāc ca | trirātrādyavadhayas tu kośaviṣayāḥ, kośam adhikṛtyābhidhānāt | tatrāpi trirātrāvadhis taṇḍulaviṣayadravyād arcācīnadravyaviṣayaḥ | dvisaptāhāvadhis tu mahābhiyogaviṣayaḥ | trisaptāhāvadhis tu,

	viṃśaddasavināśe tu dośapānaṃ vidhīyate |

iti pratipāditakośaviṣaya ity avagantavyam aucityāt | sarvatrāvadhau ūrdhvam avadher vaikṛtadarśane 'pi na pāpakṛc chodhyaḥ, avadhisāmarthyāt | ūrdhvakālīnasya rogāder nimittānantarakāritvāt | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	ūrdhvaṃ yasya dvispatāhād vaikṛtaṃ sumahad bhavet |

	nābhiyojyāḥ sa viduṣā kṛtakālavyatikramāt ||

dvisaptāhād iti pūrvoktāvadhīnām upalakṣaṇārtham, "kṛtakālavyatikramāt" iti hetor avadhyantare 'pi samānatvāt ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ kośavidhiḥ **

**atha taṇḍulavidhiḥ**

tatra pitāmahaḥ |

	taṇḍulānāṃ pravakṣyāmi vidhiṃ lakṣaṇacoditam |

	caurye tu taṇḍulā deyā nānyasminn iti niścayaḥ ||

anyasmin strīsaṃgrahaṇādyadhanavivāde (?) ity arthaḥ | dhanavivāde tu cauryād anyatrāpi taṇḍulā deyāḥ "tadarthārdhasya taṇḍulāḥ" iti kātyāyanenoktatvāt | na ca tadvacanaṃ cauryaviṣayam evāstv iti vācyam "dattasyāpahnavo yatra" ity upakramavirodhāpatteḥ | ataś cauryagrahaṇam arthavivādapradarsanārtham iti mantavyam | atra prayogo dvyahakālaḥ | tatra pūrvedyur yat kartavyaṃ tad āha sa eva |

	taṇḍulān kṣālayec chuklān śālīyān yasya kasyacit |

	mṛnmaye bhājane kṛtvā ādityasyāgrataḥ suciḥ ||

	snānodakena saṃmiśrān rātrau tatraiva vāsayet |

	āvāhanādi pūrvaṃ tu kṛtvā rātrau vidhānataḥ || iti |

śucir bhūtvā prāḍvivāko rātrāv ādityasya purato 'natidūre taṇḍulān upakalpya, dharmāvāhanādi hemāntaṃ sarvadivyasādhāraṇavidhiṃ vidhāyādityasnānodakena yathāsthitāṃs taṇḍulān āplutya, prabhātaparyantaṃ tathaiva sthāpayed ity arthaḥ | prabhāte ca yat kartavyaṃ tad api tena darśitam |

	prabhāte kāryiṇe deyās triḥ kṛtvā prāṅmukhāya tu | iti |

rātrāv adhivāsitās taṇḍulāḥ śodhyāya bhakṣaṇārthaṃ trivāraṃ deyā ity arthaḥ | śodhyasya ca yad anuṣṭheyaṃ tad apy anuvādavyājena sa eva darśayati |

	prāmukhopoṣitaṃ snātaṃ siroropitapatrakam |

	taṇḍulān bhakxayitvā tu patre niṣṭhīvayet tridhā || iti |

prāṅmukhatvādi niṣṭhīvanāntaṃ prāḍvivākena kārayitavyam | śodhyena ca kartavyam ity arthaḥ | patre ca viśeṣas tenaiva darsitaḥ |

	bhūrjasyaiva tu nānyasya abhāve pippalasya tu | iti |

etac ca prabhātakṛtyaṃ bhakṣaṇādi sūryagrahe kartavyam ity āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	sopavāsaḥ sūryagrahe taṇḍulān bhakṣayec chuciḥ | iti |

tathā śuddhyaśuddhinimittāni ca tena darśitāni |

	śuddhiḥ syāc chuklaniṣṭhīve raktamiśre ca doṣabhāk | iti |

na kevalaṃ raktamiśre doṣabhāk api tu nimittāntare 'pīti caśabdārthaḥ | ata eva pitāmahaḥ |

	śoṇitaṃ dṛśyate yasya hanus tālu ca śīryati |

	gātraṃ ca kampate yasya tam aśuddhaṃ vinirdiśet ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ taṇḍulavidhiḥ **

**ata taptamāṣavidhiḥ**

tatra pitāmahaḥ |

	taptamāṣasya vakṣyāmi vidhim uddharaṇe śubham |

	kārayed āyasaṃ pātraṃ tāmraṃ vā ṣoḍaśāṅgulam ||

	caturaṅgulakhātaṃ tu mṛnmayaṃ vātha maṇḍalam || iti |

maṇḍalaṃ parimaṇḍalaṃ vartulam iti yāvat | evaṃvidhaṃ pātraṃ ghṛtatailābhyāṃ gavyaghṛtenaiva vā pūrayitvā laukikam agniṃ divyadeśe pratiṣṭhāpya tatra tāpayet | tathā ca sa eva |

	pūrayet ghṛtatailābhyāṃ viṃśatyā vai palais tu tat |

	gavyaṃ ghṛtam upādāya tad agnau tāpayec chuciḥ ||

kecid atra vāśabdādyaśrapaṇāt (?) ghṛtatailagavyaghṛtānāṃ samuccayam icchanti, tad asat | vrīhiyavayor iva nirapekṣaśrutibalenaiva vikalpāvagateḥ | ato viṃśatipalaṃ ghṛtatailaṃ gavyaṃ vā ghṛtaṃ pātre nikṣipya tāpayet | pakṣadvaye 'pi tāpe vartamāne dharmāvāhanādi śodhyaśirasi patrāropaṇāntaṃ sarvadivyasādhāraṇavidhiṃ vidadhyāt | tataḥparaṃ pakṣadvaye prakārabhedaḥ, tatra tāvat ghṛtatailatāpanapakṣe bhedam āha sa eva |

	suvarṇamāṣake tasmin sutapte nikṣipet tataḥ |

	aṅguṣṭhāṅgulayogena taptamāṣakam uddharet ||

	karāgraṃ yo na dhunuyāt visphoṭo vā na jāyate |

	śuddho bhāvati dharmeṇa nirvikārakarāṅguligh || iti |

māṣakaṃ karṣaṣoḍaśāṃśapramāṇam | suvarṇagrahaṇam atra dvikṛṣṇalapramāṇarājatamāpanivṛttyartham (?), tasyālpatvena durgrahatvāt | tataś ca haimaṃ tāmraṃ vā māṣakaṃ nikṣiped ity arthaḥ | tasmin ghṛtataile aṅguṣṭhāṅguliyogena tarjanyaṅguṣṭhamadhyamānāṃ samūhenety arthaḥ | gavyaghṛtatāpanapakṣe 'pi kṛte sarvadivyasādhāraṇavidhau viśeṣam āha sa eva |

	sauvarṇīṃ rājatīṃ tāmrīm āyasīṃ vā suśodhitām |

	salilena sakṛddhautāṃ prakṣipet tatra mudrikām ||

	bhramadvīcītaraṅgāḍhye anakhasparśagocare |

	parīkṣetārdraparṇena carukāraṃ saghoṣakam ||

	tataś cānena mantreṇa sakṛt tad abhimantrayet |

	paraṃ pavitram amṛtaṃ ghṛtaṃ tvaṃ yajñakarmasu ||

	daha pāvaka pāpaṃ tvaṃ himaśītaṃ śucau bhava |

	upoṣitaṃ tataḥ snātam ārdravāsasamāgatam ||

	grāhayen mudrikāṃ tām tu ghṛtamadhyagatāṃ tathā |

	pradeśinīṃ ca tasyātha parikṣeran parikṣakāḥ ||

	yasya visphoṭakā na syuḥ śuddho 'sāv anyathāśuciḥ || iti |

atra pradeśinyaiva mudrikoddhāraṇam, tasyāḥ parīkṣāvidhānāt ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ taptamāṣavidhiḥ **

**atha phālavidhiḥ**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	āyasaṃ dvādaśapalaṃ ghaṭitaṃ phālam ucyate |

	aṣṭāṅgulaṃ bhaved dīrghaṃ caturaṅgulavistaram ||

evaṃvidhaṃ divyadeśapratiṣṭhāpitāgau nikṣipya dharmāvāhanādau śodhyaśirasi patrāropaṇānte sarvadivyasādhāraṇavidhāv anuṭṣṭhite sutaptaṃ kuryāt | sutapte kṛte kartavyam āha sa eva |

	agnivarṇaṃ tu tac coro jihvayā lehayet sakṛt |

	na dagdhaś cec chucim iyād anyathā tu sa hīyate ||

coragrahaṇaṃ śodhyopalakṣaṇārtham ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ phālavidhiḥ**

**atha dharmajavidhiḥ**

tatra pitāmahaḥ |

	adhunā saṃpravakṣyāmi dharmādharmaparīkṣaṇam |

	rājataṃ kārayed dharmam adharmaṃ sīsakāyasam ||

	likhet bhūrje paṭe vāpi dharmādharmau sitāsitau |

	abhyukṣya pañcagavyena gandhamālyaiḥ samarcayet ||

	sitapuṣpas tu dharmaḥ syād adharmo 'sitapuṣpadhṛk |

	evaṃ vidhāyopalipya piṇḍayos tu nidhāpayet ||

	gomayena mṛdā vāpi piṇḍau kāryau samantataḥ |

	mṛdbhāṇḍake 'nupahate sthāpyau cānupalakṣitau ||

	upalipte śucau deśe devabrāhmaṇasaṃnidhau |

	āvāhayet tato devān lokapālāṃś ca pūrvavat ||

	dharmāvāhanapūrvaṃ tu pratijñāpatrakaṃ likhet |

	yadi pāpavimukto 'haṃ dharmas tv āyātu me kare ||

	abhiyuktas tataś caikaṃ pragṛhṇītāvilambitaḥ |

	dharme gṛhīte śuddhaḥ syād adharme tu sa hīyate ||

	evaṃ samāsataḥ proktaṃ dharmādharmaparīkṣaṇam || iti |

sīsakāyasaṃ sīsakamiśrāyasanirmitam | āyasanirmitaṃ veti varṇayanti | piṇḍayos tau nidhapayet piṇḍayor abhyantare tau sthāpayed ity arthaḥ | piṇḍau samaparīmāṇau kartavyau,

	samau kṛtvā nave kumbhe sthāpyau cānupalakṣitau |

ity bṛhaspatismaraṇāt |

	yadi pāpavimukto 'haṃ dharmas tv āyātu me kare |

iti mantraṃ śodhyo brūyāt, aham iti mantraliṅgāt | anyat sarvaṃ vyaktārtham ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ dharmajavidhiḥ**

**samāptaṃ ca divyaprakaraṇam**

**kriyāpādaś ca samāptaḥ**

**atha nirṇayādikṛtyam**

tatra saṃgrahakāraḥ |

	uktaprakārarūpeṇa svamatasthāpitā kriyā |

	rājñā parīkṣya sabhyais ca sthāpyau jayaparājayau ||

	yo yathoktānyatamayā kriyayārthaṃ prasādhayet |

	bhāṣākṣarasamaṃ sādhyaṃ sa jayī parikīrtitaḥ ||

	asādhayan sādhayitvā viparītārtham ātmanaḥ |

	dṛṣṭakāraṇadoṣo yaḥ punaḥ sa tu parājayī || iti |

atra vyāsaḥ |

	jitaṃ tu daṇḍayed rājā jetuḥ pūjāṃ pravartayet |

	ajitā api daṇḍyāḥ syuḥ vedaśāstravirodhinaḥ ||

pūjā ca gandhamālyavastrādinā karyā,

	jetuḥ pravartate pūjā gandhamālyāmbarādinā |

iti tenaiva smṛtatvāt | pūjāpravartanānantaraṃ kātyāyanaḥ |

	siddenārthena saṃyojyo vādī satkārapūrvakam |

	lekhyaṃ svahastasaṃyuktaṃ tasmai dadyāt tu pārthivaḥ ||

nārado 'pi |

	madhye yat sthāpitaṃ dravyaṃ calaṃ vā yadi vā sthiram |

	paścāt tat sodayaṃ dāpyaṃ jayine patrasaṃyutam ||

patraṃ jayapatram | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	pūrvottarakriyāyuktaṃ nirṇayāntaṃ yadā nṛpaḥ |

	pradadyāj jayine lekhyaṃ jayapatraṃ tad ucyate ||

jayapatre ca yad vaktavyaṃ tad akhilaṃ lekhyavidhāv uktam, tad atrānusaṃdheyam | "siddhenārthena saṃyojyaḥ" ity asya kvacid viṣaye viśeṣam āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	nihnute likhitaṃ naikam ekadeśavibhāvitaḥ |

	dāpyaḥ sarvaṃ nṛpeṇārthaṃ na grāhyas tv aniveditaḥ ||

asyārthaḥ: niṣkavastrābharaṇādyanekaṃ pratijñākāle likhitaṃ yadā prativādī nihnute mithyaitd ity uktavān | ekadeśavibhāvitaḥ vādinā caikadeśapramāṇata eva satyaṃ mayety aṅgīkaritaḥ sa sarvam eva pratijñātam artham arthine nṛpeṇa dāpyaḥ | naivaṃ pratijñāyāṃ likhitaḥ | paścād vādinocyamāno 'rthaḥ nṛpeṇa na dāpyatayā grahītavya iti | etad uktaṃ bhavati |

	chalaṃ nirasya bhūtena vyavahārān nayen nṛpaḥ |

ity uktam evaṃvidhaviṣaye nṛpeṇa nādartavyam, duṣṭāśayatvasyātra siddhatvād iti | na ca vācyaṃ chalānusāritvāt sarvadāpanam api nṛpeṇa nādaraṇīyam iti | tad āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	sarvāpalāpaṃ yaḥ krtvā mitho 'lpam api saṃvadet |

	sarvam eva tu dāpyaḥ syād abhiyukto bṛhaspatiḥ ||

ādarārthaṃ bṛhaspatigrahaṇam | nārado 'pi sarvadāpanam ādartavyam iti darśayitum abhiyuktadeyatvam āha |

	anekārthābhiyuktena sarvārthavyapalāpinā |

	vibhāvitaikadeśena deyaṃ yad abhiyujyate ||

nanu prācīnavacanānāṃ prāguktārthābhidhāne darmanirṇayārthatā na syāt chalānusāreṇa teṣāṃ vyavahāranirṇayābhidhāyakatvāt | satyam | tathāpi na doṣaḥ, prāguktaviṣaye vyavahāranirṇayasya sarmanirṇayabādhakatvāt | ata eva bṛhaspatiḥ |

	kevalaṃ śāstram āśritya kriyate yatra nirṇayaḥ |

	vyavahāraḥ sa vijñeyo dharmas tenāpi hīyate || iti |

yatra prāguktaviṣyādāv ity arthaḥ | yat tu kātyāyanenoktam,

	anekārthābhiyoge 'pi yāvat saṃsādhayed dhanī |

	sākṣibhis tāvad evāsau labhate sādhitaṃ dhanam || 

iti, tad yatra duṣṭāśayatvasyātyantadārḍhyābhāvas tadviṣayam | prācīnavacaneṣv ivātra prativādinaḥ sarvāpalāpalakṣaṇadauṣṭyakathanāṃśābhāvāt | kecid asya vacanasya putrādideyapitrādiṛṇaviṣayatvaṃ vadanti "tatraiva nābhijānāmi" ity uttaratrayasaṃbhavād iti vadantaḥ | tan na samīcīnam, svakṛtaṛṇavivāde 'pi vismaraṇādinottaratrayasya saṃbhavāt | putrādeḥ pitrādikṛtaṛṇavivāde mithyaitad ity uttaram uktavato nihnavavāditve 'pi sādhitamātradānaprasaṅgāc ca | atha putrāder mithyaitad ity uttaraṃ na saṃbhavatīty ucyate | maivaṃ vocaḥ, ṛṇagrahaṇakāle prabuddhasya aprabuddhasyāpi mātrādivacanatas tatsaṃbhavāt | atha nābhijānāmīty uttaram uktavati putrādau sādhitamātralābhavacanam ity ucyate, tarhi nābhijānāmītyādyuttaratrayaviṣayakatvaṃ tasya parikalpyatām, kiṃ putrādiviṣayatvena | atha,

	putrapautrai ṛṇaṃ deyaṃ nihnave sākṣibhāvitam |

iti smaraṇāt, putrādiviṣayatvam ity ucyate, tarhi mithyaitad ityuktaputrādiviṣayatvaṃ na punaḥ nābhijānāmīty uktavatputrādiviṣayatvam, "nihnave sākṣibhāvitam" iti smaraṇāt |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye</span> tv anyathā vyavasthāpayanti sarvārthadāpanavacanaṃ pratijñātārthānāṃ madhe yady ekam apy artham arthī sādayati, tadā sarvān etān arthān ahaṃ dadāmīty evaṃ sāvaṣṭambhoktiyuktanihnavaviṣayam | tadrahitaviṣayaṃ tu sādhitamātralābhāvacanam iti | etad apy ayuktam, "nihnute likhitaṃ naikam" ity api śeṣeṇābhidhānāt | na ca chalodāharanaparatvād asya vakyasya tatsiddhaye sāvaṣṭambhanihnavaviṣayatvam āsthīyata iti yuktam, sarvāpalāpacchalam ādāya vyavahārasamāptyabhidhānāt | tāvataiva vākyasya chalodāharaṇaparatvasiddheḥ | bhāṣābalenaivoktaviṣaye sarvadāpanāt anuvādakaṃ ca "nihnute" ityādivacanam, tatsamānarthaṃ vacanadvayam api syāt | na ca,

	anekārthābhiyoge 'pi yāvat saṃsādhayed dhanī |

ityādikātyāyanavacanaparihārāyaivam āśrīyata iti yuktam | tadvirodhasya ṛjumārgena parihṛtatvād ity alam ativistarakāriṇā matāntaropanyāsanirāsena |

	dāpanaprakāras tu kātyāyanena darsitaḥ |

	rājā tu svāmine vipraṃ sāntvenaiva pradāpayet |

	deśācāreṇa cānyāṃs tu duṣṭān saṃpīḍya dāpayet ||

	rikthinaṃ suhṛdaṃ vāpi chalenaiva pradāpayet || iti |

na kevalaṃ rājā svāmine pradāpayet, svayam api daṇḍaṃ gṛhṇīyād ity āha nāradaḥ |

	ṛṇikaḥ sadhano yas tu daurātmyān na prayacchati |

	rājñā dāpayitavyaḥ syād gṛhītvāṃśaṃ tu viṃśakam ||

dāpyārthasya yāvān viṃśatitamo bhāgaḥ tāvantam artham adhamarṇikāt gṛhṇīyād ity arthaḥ | etad api pratipannaṛṇikaviṣayam | vipratipannaṛṇitve tv āha viṣṇuḥ: "uttamarṇaś ced rājānam iyāt tadvibhāvito 'dharmarṇo rājñe dhanadaśabhāgasamaṃ daṇḍaṃ dadyāt | prāptārthaś cottamarṇo viṃśatitamam aṃśam" iti | prāptārthena dānabhṛtitvena, na daṇḍatvena niraparādhitvāt | yadā tv adhamarṇo rājānam iyāt tadā (?) manur āha |

	yaḥ sādhayantaṃ chandena vedayed dhanikaṃ nṛpe |

	sa rājñarṇacaturbhāgaṃ dāpyas tasya ca taddhanam ||

yo rājñaḥ priyo 'dhamarṇas tadājñayā pratibandhanaṃ kariṣyāmīti buddhyā dhanikaṃ chandena svecchayā svecchayā sādhayantaṃ prayuktadhanayācane 'pravṛttaṃ nṛpe vedayet māṃ pīḍayiṣyatīty āvedayet, asau ṛṇaṃ taccaturbhāgasamaṃ ca daṇḍaṃ rājñā dāpya ity arthaḥ | yat punas tenoktam,

	yo yāvan nihnavītārthaṃ mithyā yāvati vārayet |

	tau nṛpeṇa hy adharmajñau dāpyau taddviguṇaṃ damam || MDh 8.59

iti tadudvṛttādhamarṇottamarṇaviṣaya, "adharmajñagrahaṇāt" ity uktaṃ tadbhāṣye (Medhātithi on MDh 8.60) | yat tu yājñavalkyenoktam,

	nihnave bhāvito dadyad dhanaṃ rājje ca tatsamam |

iti, tad udvṛttādharmaṇasyoktadaṇḍaparyāptadhanāsaṃbhaviṣaye veditavyam, anyathā pūrvoktaviṣṇumanuvacanavirodhasya durvāratvāt | mithyābhiyoginas tu aparyāptadhanasyāpi na tatsamadaṇdaḥ | yad āha sa eva,

	mithyābhiyogī dviguṇam abhiyogād dhanaṃ vahet | iti |

abhiyogāt abhiyuktadhanāt dviguṇaṃ dhanaṃ vahet rājñe dadyad ity arthaḥ | tāvad dhanābhāve tu "ānṛṇyaṃ karmaṇā gacchet" ityādyanukalp 'vagantavyaḥ | yat tu nāradenoktam,

	na ca mithyābhiyuñjīta doṣo mithyābhiyoginaḥ |

	yas tatra vinayaḥ proktaḥ so 'bhiyoktāram āvrajet ||

iti, tatpratipadoktadaṇḍābhāvaviṣayaṃ sāmānyaśāstratvāt | tena nihnave asadvṛttasya yo daṇḍo 'bhihito viṣṇunā sa eva sadvṛttasya mithyābhiyogino bhavatīty avagantavyam | tathā,

	nihnave tu yadā vādī svayaṃ tat pratipadyate |

	jñeyā sā pratipattis tu tasyārdho vinayaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

iti vyāsena yo daṇḍo 'bhihitaḥ sa eva mithyābhiyoge 'pi svayaṃ tatpratipadyamānasya bhavatīti cāvagantavyam | yat punar manunoktam,

	arthe 'pavyayamānaṃ tu kāraṇena vibhāvitam |

	dāpayed dhanikasyārthaṃ daṇḍalesaṃ ca śaktitaḥ || (MDh 8.51)

iti, taddaśamāṃśadaṇḍadanāsamarthasadvṛttādhamarṇaviṣayam ity uktaṃ tadbhāṣye (Medh on MDh 8.52) | kāraṇeneti vadan dvipādavyavahāre tv arthadāpanam eva, na daṇḍadāpanam, tatra nihnavamithyābhiyogayor abhāvād iti darsayati | evam eva catuṣpāde 'pi vyavahāre śaṅkābhiyogājñānottarādinā mithyābhiyoganihnavābhave daṇḍābhāvo 'dhyavaseyaḥ | yat tu smṛtyantaram,

	ādye tu daṇḍapādaḥ syāt dvitīye 'rdhaṃ tṛtīyake |

	pādanyūnaṃ caturthe ca pāde saṃpūrṇadaṇḍabhāk ||

iti, tad vigītatvād apramāṇam iti prapañcitaṃ visvarūpacāryeṇa | ato nihnavamithyābhiyoganimitto daṇḍaś catuṣpady eva vyavahāre nimittasadbhāvaviṣaye grahītavyaḥ | tatra ṛṇādānaviṣayavyavahāre daṇḍaviśeṣo darśitaḥ | nikṣepādiviṣayavyavahāre tu daṇḍaviseṣas tatra tatra pade vakṣyate | yat punaḥ kātyāyanenoktam,

	śatārdhaṃ dapayec chuddham aśuddho daṇḍabhāg bhavet |

iti, tad divyāviśeṣāvadhṛtaśuddhapuruṣaviṣayam | yato 'nantaram āha sa eva |

	viṣe toye hutāśe ca tulākośe ca taṇḍule |

	taptamāṣakadivye ca kramād daṇḍaṃ prakalpayet ||

	sahasraṃ ṣaṭsataṃ caiva tathā pañcaśatāni tu |

	catustridvyekam evaṃ ca hīnaṃ hīneṣu kalpayet || iti |

ayaṃ ca divyanibandhano daṇḍo nihnavamithyābhiyogayor anyataranibandhena daṇḍena samuccīyate, nimittasmuccayāt | paṇas tu śāstroktadaṇḍena samuccīyate ity āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	sapaṇas cet vivadaḥ syāt tatra hīnaṃ tu dāpayet |

	daṇḍaṃ ca svapaṇaṃ caiva dhanine dhanam eva ca ||

nārado 'pi |

	vivāde sottarapaṇe dvayor yas tatra hīyate |

	sa paṇaṃ svakṛtaṃ dāpyo vinayaṃ ca parājaye || iti |

atra kātyāyanaḥ |

	evaṃ dharmāsanasthena samenaiva vivadinā |

	kāryāṇāṃ nirṇayo dṛśyo brāhmaṇaiḥ saha nānyathā ||

bṛhaspatir api |

	rājñā yatnena kartavyaṃ saṃdigdhārthavicāraṇam |

	trayas tatropacīyante hānir ekasya jāyate ||

	jetāpnoti dhanaṃ pūjāṃ jito vinayanigraham |

	jayaṃ dānaṃ damaṃ rājā sabhyāḥ puṇyam avāpnuyuḥ || iti |

nārado 'pi |

	evaṃ paśyan sadā rājā vyavahārān samāhitaḥ |

	vitatyeha yaśo dīptaṃ śakrasyaiti salokatām ||

bṛhaspatir api |

	evaṃ śāstroditaṃ rājā kurvan nirṇayapālanam |

	vitatyeha yaśo loke mahendrasacivo bhavet ||

	sākṣilekhyānumānena prakurvan kāryanirṇayam |

	vitatyeha yaśo rājā bradhnasyāpnoti viṣṭapam || iti |

manur api |

	kāmakrodhau tu saṃyamya yo 'rthaṃ dharmeṇa paśyati |

	prajās tam anuvartante samudram iva sindhavaḥ ||

	yas tv adharmeṇa kāryāṇi mohāt kuryān narādhipaḥ |

	acirāt taṃ durātmānaṃ vaśe kurvanti śatravaḥ || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyām nirṇayādikṛtyam **

**athānyāny api daṇḍaviṣayāṇi kānicid vacanāni likhyante**

tatra nāradaḥ |

	śārīraś cārthadaṇḍaś ca daṇḍas tu dvividhaḥ smrtaḥ |

	śārīras tāḍanādis tu maraṇāntaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||

	kākaṇyādis tv arthadaṇḍaḥ sarvasvāntas tathaiva ca || iti |

atra śārīro daṇḍabhedaḥ parigaṇayituṃ śakyo nārthadaṇḍabhed ity āha sa eva |

	śārīro daśadhā prokto hy arthadaṇḍas tv anekadhā | iti |

daśadheti na saṃkhyāniyamārtham, atho bahuvidhasya śāriradaṇḍasya vakṣyamāṇatvāt | tathā hi manunā tāvan navavidhaḥ śārīro daṇḍa iti darśitaḥ |

	daś sthānāni daṇḍasya manuḥ svāyaṃbhuvo 'bravīt |

	upastha udaraṃ jihvā hastau pādau ca pañcamam ||

	cakṣur nāsā ca karṇau ca dhanaṃ dehas tathaiva ca || iti |

upasthaḥ strīpuṃsayor liṅgam | tannigraho 'gamyāgamane | caurye tv āhāranivṛttyādinājaṭharasya nigrahaḥ | vākpāruṣye jihvāyāḥ | daṇḍapāruṣye hastayoḥ | pādaprahārādau pādayoḥ | gopyanirīkṣaṇādau cakṣuṣaḥ | parastrīstanānulepanagandhagrahaṇādau nasikāyāḥ | rājamantraśravaṇādau karṇayoḥ | utkocapradānādau vyayapratibandhādinā dhanasya | mahāpātakādau dehasya | ayaṃ copasthādīnām nigraho yatrāgamyāgamanacauryadau kṣatraviṭśudrāṇāṃ daṇḍaviśeṣo nāmnātas tatra kāryaḥ,

	triṣu varṇeṣu tāni syur akṣato brāhmaṇo vrajet | (MDh 8.124)

iti kṣatriyādiṣu sāmānyenābhidhānāt | akṣato brāhmaṇaḥ pūrvoktadaṇḍasthāneṣv adaṇḍito brāhmaṇa ity arthaḥ | vrajed it vadan yo nirvāsito deśāntaraṃ gacchati tasyaivoktadaśasthāneṣv adaṇḍo na punar brāhmaṇamātrasyeti darsayati | ata eva nirvāsanavidhiśeṣatayāpi tenoktam |

	na jātu brāhmaṇaṃ hanyāt sarvapāpeṣv avasthitam |

	rāṣṭrād enaṃ bahiṣkuryāt samagradham akṣatam || (MDh 8.380)

yasya tu na bahiṣkāraḥ tasya kṣatriyādivad eva daṇḍaḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	caturṇām api varṇānāṃ prāyaścittam akurvatām |

	śārīraṃ dhanasaṃyuktaṃ daṇḍaṃ dharmyaṃ prakalpayet ||

yat tu gautamenoktam: "na śārīro brāhmaṇadaṇḍaḥ" iti, tad vadharūpasyāṅgabhaṅgātmakasya niṣedhārtham, na punar aṅganigrahātmakasyāpi | tathātve pūrvoktavacanavirodhāt | ata eva bṛhaspatinā viśeṣitaḥ |

	mahāpātakayukto 'pi na vipro vadham arhati || iti |

hārītenāpi |

	na tv aṅgabhedaṃ viprasya pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ | iti |

evaṃ cāṅganigrahātmaka eva śārīro daṇḍo viprasya na tu vadhādyātmaka ity anusaṃdheyam | ata evāpastambaḥ: "cakṣurnirodhas tv eteṣu brāhmaṇasya" iti | nirodhaś cakṣuṣo bandhanādinā kāryo na tv āśrayoddharaṇena, aṅgabhaṅgasya niṣiddhatvāt | yat tu śaṅkenoktam: "trayāṇām api varṇānāṃ dhanāpahāravadhabandhakriyā | vivāsanāṅkakaraṇaṃ brāhmaṇasya" iti, tad daridrabrāhmaṇaviṣayam | tathā ca brāhmaṇaṃ prakṛtya gautamaḥ: "karmaviyogavikhyāpanavivāsanāṅkakaraṇāny avṛttau" iti | avṛttau nirdhana ity arthaḥ | etad uttamasāhasaviṣayam | ṛṇāpalāpādiviṣaye tu manur āha |

	kṣatravṭśūdrayonis tu daṇḍaṃ dātum aśknuvan |

	ānṛṇyaṃ karmaṇā gacched vipro gacchec chanaiḥ śanaiḥ ||

karmakaraṇāsāmarthye tu kātyāyana āha |

	dhanadānāsahaṃ budhvā svādhīnaṃ karma kārayet |

	aśaktau bandhanāgāraṃ praveśyo brāhmaṇād ṛte ||

manur api |

	strībālonmattavṛddhānāṃ daridrānātharogiṇām |

	śaphāvidalarajjvādyair vidadhyān nṛpatir damam ||

evaṃ ca bandhanāṅkakaraṇakarmakaraṇabandhanāgarapraveśanatāḍanarūpāḥ śārīradaṇḍabhedāḥ pañca vijñeyāḥ | ataḥ "śarīro daśadhā" ity upalakṣaṇārtham uktam, nāvadhāraṇārtham iti mantavyam | "daṇḍas tu dvividhaḥ smṛtaḥ" ity etad apy upalakṣaṇārtham eva, vidhāntarasyāpi smṛtatvāt | tathā hi |

	śiraso daṇḍanaṃ muṇḍas tasya nirvāsanaṃ purāt |

	lalāṭe cābhiśastāṅkaḥ prayāṇaṃ gardabhena ca ||

tasya brāhmaṇasyety arthaḥ | brāhmaṇasya prakṛtatvāt | atha vadhasthāne muṇḍanaṃ daṇḍa ity āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	brāhmaṇasya vadho mauṇḍyaṃ purān nirvāsanaṃ tathā |

	lalāṭe cābhiśastāṅkaḥ prayāṇaṃ gardabhena ca |

evaṃ ca kṣatriyādau vadha eva na muṇḍanam | tatra pratinidhitvenāsmṛtatvāt | ata eva manuḥ |

	mauṇḍyaṃ prāṇāntiko daṇḍo brāhmaṇasya vidhīyate |

	itareṣāṃ tu varṇānāṃ daṇḍaḥ prāṇāntiko bhavet ||

uttamasāhasa iti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	vadhaḥ sarvasvaharaṇaṃ purān nirvāsanāṅkane |

	tadaṅgaccheda ity ukto daṇḍa uttamasāhase ||

	aviśeṣeṇa sarveṣām eṣa daṇḍavidhiḥ smṛtaḥ |

	vadhād ṛte brāhmaṇasya na vadhaṃ brāhmaṇo 'rhati || iti |

vadhād ṛta ity aṅgacchedasyāpy upalakṣaṇārtham,

	na tv aṅgabhedaṃ viprasya pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ |

	tapasā cejyayā caiva brāhmaṇaḥ pūjyate sadā ||

iti hārītasmaraṇāt | manus tu vadhadaṇḍaparityāge hetum āha |

	na brāhmaṇavadhāt pāpāt nādharmo vidyate kvacit |

	tasmāt tasya vadhaṃ rājā manasāpi na cintayet ||

ato mahāpātakayukto 'pi vipro na vadhya ity āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	mahāpātakayukto 'pi na vipro vadham arhati | iti |

kiṃ tarhy arhatīty apekṣite 'nantaram uktaṃ tenaiva |

	nirvāsanāṅkane mauṇḍyaṃ tasya kuryān narādhipaḥ | iti |

nirvāsanam atra deśato na punaḥ purāt | tad āha baudhāyanaḥ: "taptenāyasena lalāṭe 'ṅkiyitvā viṣayān nirvāsanam" iti | kuryād iti śeṣaḥ | aṅkane tu viśeṣo nāradena darśitaḥ |

	gurutalpe bhagaḥ kāryaḥ surāpāne surādhvajaḥ |

	steye tu śvapadaṃ kāryaṃ brahmahaṇy aśirā pumān |

aṅkanaṃ tv idaṃ na kṣatriyādiṣu kartavyam | yad āha uśanā |

	brāhmaṇasyāparādheṣu caturṣv aṅko vidhīyate |

	gurutalpe surāpāne steye brāhmaṇahiṃsane ||

	itareṣāṃ tu varṇānām aṅkanaṃ natra karayet || iti |

kas tarhi daṇdas tatrety apakṣite bṛhaspatiḥ |

	mahāparādhayuktāṃś ca vadhadaṇḍena śāsayet | iti |

yadā tu vadhadaṇḍena mahāparādhino nigrahītuṃ na śakyās tadā manur āha |

	vadhenāpi yadā tv etān nigrahītuṃ na śaknuyāt |

	tadaiṣu sarvam apy etat prayuñjīta catuṣṭayam || 

kiṃ taccatuṣṭayam ity apekṣite yājñavalkyaḥ |

	vāgdaṇḍas tv atha dhigdaṇḍo dhanadaṇḍo vadhas tathā |

	yojyāḥ samastā vyastā vāpy aparādhavaśād ime ||

vāgdaṇḍaḥ paruṣaśāpavacanātmakaḥ | dhigdaṇḍo dhig iti kutsanam | samastānāṃ yojane kramam āha manuḥ |

	vāgdaṇḍaṃ prathamaṃ kuryād dhigdaṇḍaṃ tadanantaram |

	tṛtīyaṃ dhanadaṇḍaṃ tu vadhadaṇḍam ataḥ param ||

vyastānāṃ tu yojane vyavasthām āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	khalvāparādhe vāgdaṇḍo dhigdaṇḍaḥ pūrvasāhase |

	madhyame tv arthadaṇḍas tu rājadroheṣu bandhanam ||

	nirvāsanaṃ vadho vāpi kāryam ātmahitaiṣiṇā |

	vyastāḥ samastā ekasya mahāpātakakāriṇaḥ || iti |

tathā puruṣāpekṣayāpi vyavasthā tenaiva darsitā |

	mitrādiṣu prayuñjīta vāgdaṇḍaṃ dhik tapasvinām |
