	vivādino narāṃś cānyān doṣiṇo 'rthen daṇḍayet ||

ādigrahaṇena mānyā janā gṛhyante,

	gurūn purohitān pūjyān vāgdaṇḍenaiva daṇḍayet |

	vivādino narāṃś cānyān dhigdhanābhyāṃ ca daṇḍayet ||

iti tenaivoktatvāt | yat tu śaṅkhenoktam: "adaṇḍyau mātāpitarau snātakapurohitau parivrājakavānaprasthau janmakarmaśrutiśīlaśaucācāravantaś ca" iti | yad api kātyāyanena,

	ācāryasya pitur mātur bāndhavānāṃ tathaiva ca |

	eteṣām aparādheṣu daṇḍo naiva vidhīyate ||

iti, tac chārīrārthadaṇdayor niṣedhārtham, na punar daṇḍamātrasya | yad āha manuḥ:

	pitācāryaḥ suhṛn mātā bhāryā putraḥ purohitaḥ |

	nādaṇḍyo nāma rājño 'sti dharmād vicalitaḥ svakāt ||

bṛhaspatir api:

	ṛtvikpurohitāmātyāḥ putrāḥ saṃbandhibāndhavāḥ |

	dharmād vicalitā daṇḍyā nirvāsyā rājahiṃsakāḥ ||

yat tu gautamenoktam: "ṣaḍbhiḥ parihāryo rājñāvadhyaś cābandhyaś cādaṇḍyaś cābahiṣkāryaś cāparivādyas cāparihāryaś ca" iti, tad etat: "sa eṣa bahuśruto bhavati | lokavedavedāṅgavit | vākovākyetihāsapurāṇakuśalaḥ | tadapekṣaḥ tadvṛttiḥ | catvāriṃśatā saṃskāraiḥ saṃskṛtaḥ | triṣu karmasv abhirataḥ | ṣaṭsu vā | sāmayacārikeṣv abhivinītaḥ" iti pratipāditabahuśrutaviṣayam | ato na prācīnavacanavirodhaḥ | kātyāyano 'py adaṇḍyam āha |

	prāṇātyaye tu yatra syād akāryakaraṇaṃ kṛtam |

	daṇḍas tatra tu naiva syād eṣa dharmyo bhṛgusmṛtaḥ ||

nāradas tu vihitadaṇḍārdhen daṇḍam āha |

	ayuktaṃ sāhasam kṛtvā pratyāpattiṃ vrajet tu yaḥ |

	bhrūyat svayaṃ vā sadasi tasya cārdho damaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

vyāso 'pi |

	vyādhinā pīḍito yas tu yaḥ kaścid api tāmyati |

	naitan mayā punaḥ kāryaṃ brūyāt tasyārdhako damaḥ ||

atra pakṣāntaram āha gautamaḥ: "anujñānaṃ vā vedavit samayavacanāt" iti | anujñānam adaṇḍayitvotsarjanam | tathā vihitadaṇḍād abhyadhikam ūnaṃ vā doṣiṇaḥ pīḍājananasamarthaṃ daṇḍaṃ vidadhyād ity āha sa eva: "daṇḍo damanād ity āhus tenādāntān damayet" iti | yāvati pīḍāviśeṣe damanakāryopaśamas tāvat pīḍākaraṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	anubandhaṃ parijñāya deśakālau ca tattvataḥ |

	sārāparādhāv ālocya daṇḍaṃ daṇḍyeṣu pātayet ||

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	jñātvāparādhaṃ deśaṃ ca kālaṃ balam athāpi vā |

	vayaḥ karma ca vittaṃ ca daṇḍaṃ daṇḍyeṣu pātayet ||

tatrodāharaṇam āha manuḥ |

	kārṣāpaṇaṃ bhaved daṇḍyo yaś cānyaḥ prākṛto janaḥ |

	tatra rājño bhaved daṇḍaḥ sahasram iti dhāraṇā ||

prākṛto daridraḥ | rājā aiśvaryeṇādhiṣṭhitaḥ | kātyāyano 'pi |

	yena doṣeṇa śūdrasya daṇḍo bhavati dharmataḥ |

	tena cet kṣatraviprāṇāṃ dviguṇo dviguṇo bhavet ||

	pravrajyāvasitaṃ śūdraṃ japahomaparāyaṇam |

	vadhena śāsayet pāpaṃ daṇḍyo vā dviguṇaṃ damam ||

bṛhaspatir api |

	vadhārhaḥ suvarṇaśataṃ damaṃ dāpyas tu pūruṣaḥ |

	aṅgacchedārhakas tv ardhaṃ saṃdaṃśārhas tadardhakam ||

	tāḍanaṃ bandhanaṃ caiva tathaiva ca viḍambanam |

	eṣa daṇḍo hi dāsasya nārthadaṇḍo bṛhaspatiḥ ||

nārado 'pi |

	kākaṇyādis tu yo daṇḍaḥ sa tu māṣaparaḥ smṛtaḥ |

	māṣāvarārdho yaḥ proktaḥ kārṣāpaṇaparas tu saḥ ||

	kārṣāpaṇāvarārdhas tu catuṣkārṣāpaṇottaraḥ |

	dvyavaro 'ṣṭaparaś cānyas tryavaro dvādaśāntataḥ ||

	kārṣāpaṇās tu ye proktāḥ sarve te syuś caturguṇāḥ || iti |

kākaṇyādiśabdarthā divyaprakaraṇe darśitāḥ | atra kātyāyanaḥ |

	kalpito yasya yo daṇḍas tv aparādhasya yatnataḥ |

	paṇānāṃ grahaṇaṃ tu syāt tanmūlyaṃ vātha rājani ||

	māṣapādo dvipādo vā daṇḍo yatra pravartinaḥ |

	anirdiṣṭaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ māṣakaṃ tu prakalpayet ||

	yatrokto māṣakair daṇḍo rājataṃ tatra nirdiset |

	kṛṣṇalaiś coktam eva syād uktadaṇḍaviniścayaḥ || iti |

paṇānāṃ kārṣāpaṇānām ity arthaḥ | teṣāṃ saṃkhyābhedanindhanāḥ (?) paribhāṣikyaḥ saṃjñā manunā darśitāḥ |

	paṇānāṃ dve śate sārdhe prathamaḥ sāhasaḥ smṛtaḥ |

	madhyamaḥ pañca vijñeyaḥ sahasraṃ caiva cottamaḥ ||

iyaṃ paribhāṣā prathamāparādhaviṣaye 'nuvartavyāḥ | punaḥpunar aparādhaviṣaye tv āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	sāśītipaṇasahasro daṇḍa uttamasāhasaḥ |

	tadardhaṃ madhyamaḥ proktas tadardham adhamaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

ato yatra yatrottamasāhasādiśabdair daṇḍo nigadyate tatra tatra etat saṃkhyākāḥ kārṣāpaṇās tanmūlyaniṣkādayo vā grahītavyāḥ | evam uktaprakāro daṇḍaḥ sarvalokānandahetur ity āha sa eva |

	yathāśāstraṃ prayuktaḥ san sadevāsuramānavam |

	jagad ānandayet sarvam anyathā tat prakopayet ||

tathocchāstradaṇḍanasya nindāṃ viparītasya praśaṃsām cāha sa eva |

	adharmadaṇḍanaṃ svargakīrtilokavināśanam |

	samyak tu daṇḍanaṃ rājñaḥ svargakīrtijayāvaham ||

daṇḍyās tu tena daṇḍena kṣīṇapāpā bhavantīty āha nāradaḥ |

	rājabhir dhṛtadaṇḍās tu kṛtvā pāpāni mānavāḥ |

	nirmalāḥ svargam āyānti santaḥ sukṛtino yathā ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	śuddhis tu śāstratattvajñaiś cikitsā samudāhṛtā |

	prāyaścittaṃ ca daṇḍaṃ ca tābhyāṃ sā dvividhā smṛtā ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ daṇḍaviṣayāṇi **

**atha punarnyāyaḥ**

tatra nāradaḥ |

	strīṣu rātrau bahir grāmād antarveśmanyarātiṣu (?) |

	vyavahāraḥ kṛto 'py eṣaḥ punaḥ kartavyatām iyāt ||

strībhiḥ śatrubhir vā rahasi vā nirṇīto vyavahāro 'jñānapakṣapātayoḥ saṃbhavāt punarvicāraṇīya ity arthaḥ | evaṃ balātkāreṇa rāgadveṣādyupādhinā vā nirṇītaṃ nivartya vyavahārāntaraṃ pravartanīyam | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	balopādhivinirvṛttān vyavahārān nivartayet | iti |

tataḥ paścād vyavahārāntaraṃ pravartayed ity abhiprāyaḥ | tathā vyavahartṛvaiguṇye 'py evaṃ kāryam ity āha sa eva |

	mattonmattārtavyasanibālabhītādiyojitaḥ |

	asaṃdigdhakṛtaś caiva vyavahāro na sidhyati ||

ādiśabdena vṛddhayojitādayo vyavaharā gṛhyante | ata eva manuḥ |

	mattonmattārtādyadhīnaiḥ bālena sthavireṇa vā |

	asaṃbandhakṛtaś caiva vyavahāro na sidhyati ||

asaṃbandhaḥ arthipratyarthisaṃbandharahitaḥ | nārado 'pi |

	purarāṣṭraviruddhas ca yas ca rājñā vivarjitaḥ |

	anādeyo bhaved vādaḥ dharmavibhir udāhṛtaḥ ||

hārīto 'pi |

	rājñā vivarjito yas tu svayaṃ pauravirodhakṛt |

	rāṣṭrasya vā samas tasya prakṛtīnāṃ tathaiva ca ||

	anye vā ye pure grāme mahājanavirodhakāḥ |

	anādeyās tu te sarve vyavahārāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||

evaṃ caivaṃvidhavyavahāraṃ tīritam apy anuśiṣṭam api nivṛtya vyavahārāntaraṃ kartavyam iti tātparyārtho 'nusaṃdheyaḥ (?) | tīritānuśiṣṭayor bhedam āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	asat sad iti yaḥ prakṣaḥ sabhyair evāvadhāryate |

	tīritaḥ so 'nuśiṣṭas tu sākṣivākyāt prakīrtitaḥ ||

sākṣivākyād avadhārito 'nuśiṣṭa ity arthaḥ | yat punar manunoktam,

	tīritaṃ cānuśiṣṭaṃ ca yatra kvacana yad bhavet |

	kṛtaṃ tad dharmayor vidyāt na tad bhūyo nivartayet ||

iti, tat strīkṛtatvādinivṛttihetvabhāvaviṣaya (?) evotsargamātram iti mantavyam | ata eva tasyāpavādam āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	kulādibhir niścite 'pi na saṃtoṣaṃ gatas tu yaḥ |

	vicārya tat kṛtaṃ rājā kukṛtaṃ punar uddharet ||

vihitanirṇetṛnirṇīte 'pi vyavahārasamāptir anyāyeneti yadi vivādī manyate tadāpi punarnyāyaḥ kārya ity arthaḥ | kukṛtatve siddhe prāṅnyāyadraṣṭṝṇāṃ daṇḍam āha nāradaḥ |

	durdṛṣṭe vyavahāre tu sabhyās te daṇḍam āpnuyuḥ |

	na hi jātu vinā daṇḍāt kaścin mārge 'vatiṣṭhate ||

ayaṃ ca sabhyānām eva daṇḍaḥ jetuḥ durdarśanāprayojakatve veditavyaḥ | prayojakatve tatrāsyāpi daṇḍaḥ, tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	niścitya bahubhiḥ sārdhaṃ brāhmaṇaiḥ śāstrapāragaiḥ |

	daṇḍayej jayinā sākaṃ (?) pūrvaṃ sabhyāṃs tu doṣiṇaḥ ||

jayinā sākaṃ daṇḍanam api sabhyadaṇḍaprakaraṇoktavidhinaivety āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	durdṛṣṭāṃs tu punar dṛṣṭvā vyavahārān nṛpeṇa tu |

	sabhyāḥ sajayino daṇḍyā vivādād dviguṇaṃ damam ||

durdṛṣṭān sajayisabhyadoṣeṇety arthaḥ | yadā tu sākṣidoṣeṇa vyavahārasya duṣṭatā, tadā sākṣidaṇḍaprakaraṇoktavidhinā sākṣiṇa eva daṇḍyā na jayī nāpi sabhyāḥ | yadā punaḥ sajayisākṣidoṣeṇa, tadā ta eva daṇḍyāḥ, na sabhyā ity abhiprāyaḥ | evam asaṃtoṣamātreṇa punarnyāyaḥ prakṛtasya nirṇayasya nyāyābhāsatve sati vidhātavyaḥ | samyaṅnyāyatve nārada āha |

	tīritaṃ cānuśiṣṭaṃ ca yo manyeta vidharmataḥ |

	dviguṇaṃ daṇḍam āsthāya tat kāryaṃ punar uddharet ||

vidharmataḥ dharmaśāstravirodhato jātam iti yo vivādī samyaṅnirṇītam apy auddhatyāt manyata ity arthaḥ | atra vyavahārasamāpter anyathātvāsaṃbhavāt punarnyāyānantaram api prāṅnyāyaparājita evāṅgīkṛtadaṇḍena daṇḍya ity āha yājñavlkyaḥ |

	yo manyetājito 'smīti nyāyenāpi parājitaḥ |

	tam āyāntaṃ punar jitvā dāpayet dviguṇaṃ damam ||

evaṃ sadaṇḍaḥ punarnyāyaḥ sanṛpottarasabhāyām eva, nṛpasyaiva daṇḍane 'dhikārāt | nṛparahitāyāṃ tūttarasabhāyāṃ daṇḍavirahitaḥ punarnyāyaḥ kāryaḥ daṇḍāṃśasya nṛpaikakāryatvāt | uttarasabhayā ca (?) pūrvasabhāto jyāyasyā bhavitavyam, anyathā saṃdehānivṛttaiḥ | sbhyānāṃ ca jyāyastvatāratamyaṃ nirṇetṛnirṇayaprakaraṇe darśitam | nṛpasabhādṛṣṭasya kudṛṣṭatvaśṅkāyāṃ tu prakṛṣṭanṛpāntarasabhāyāṃ punarnyāyaḥ, tathā ca smṛtyantaram |

	nyāyāpetaṃ yad anyena rājñājñānakṛtaṃ bhavet |

	tad apy anyāyavihitaṃ punarnyāye niveśayet ||

yat punaḥ pitāmahenoktam,

	grāme dṛṣṭaḥ puraṃ yāyāt pure dṛṣṭas tu rājani |

	rājñā dṛṣṭaḥ kudṛṣṭo vā nāsti tasya punar nayaḥ ||

iti, tat pūrvasabhātaḥ prakṛṣṭasabhāntarālābhaviṣayam | svavākyajitasya tu prakṛṣṭasabhāntarasadbhāve 'pi na punarnyāya ity āha nāradaḥ |

	sākṣisabhyāvasannānāṃ dūṣaṇe darśanaṃ punaḥ |

	svavācaiva jitānāṃ tu noktaḥ paunarbhavo vidhiḥ ||

sākṣivākyāt sabhyair eva kṛtād vā nirṇayāt parājitānāṃ vyavahārasya punardarśanaṃ pūrvadarśanasya dūṣaṇe satīty arthaḥ | sabhyagrahaṇam amātyāder upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva manuḥ |

	amātyaḥ prāḍvivāko vā yaḥ kuryāt kāryam anyathā |

	tat svayaṃ nṛpatiḥ kuryāt taṃ sahasraṃ ca daṇḍayet || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ punarnyāyaḥ **

**atha kṛtanivartanam**

tatra manuḥ |

	yogādhamanavikrītaṃ yogadānapratigraham |

	yatra vāpy upadhiṃ paśyet tat sarvaṃ vinivartayet ||

yogaḥ parakīyadhansyātmīyatvāpādakahetvabhāve 'pi yācitakādinā hastagatatvādisaṃbandhaḥ | adhamanaṃ bandhakaraṇam, yogenādhamanam | evaṃ yogavikrītādāv api vigrahaḥ | yamo 'pi |

	balād dattaṃ balād bhuktaṃ bhalād yac cāpi lekhitam |

	sarvān balakṛtān arthān nivartyān āha vai manuḥ ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	unmattenaiva mattena tathā bhāvāntareṇa vā |

	yad dattaṃ yat kṛtaṃ vātha pramāṇaṃ naiva tad bhavet ||

nārado 'pi |

	yad bālaḥ kurute kāryam asvatantras tathaiva ca |

	akṛtaṃ tad iti prāhuḥ śāstre śāstravido janāḥ ||

bālāsvatantrāv api tena nirūpitau |

	garbhashaiḥ sadṛśo jñeya āṣṭamād vatsarāc chiśuḥ |

	bāla āṣoṣaśād varṣāt paugaṇḍas cāpi śabdyate ||

	parato vyavahārajñaḥ svatatraḥ pitaraṃ vinā || iti |

anena pitṛmān asvatantra ity arthād uktam | uktaṃ ca śaṅkhalikhitābhyām: " asvatantrāḥ pitṛmantaḥ" iti | pitṛgrahaṇaṃ matur api pradarśanārtham | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	jīvator na svatantraḥ syāj jarayāpi samanvitaḥ | iti |

jīvator mātāpitor iti śeṣaḥ,

	tayor api pitā śreyān bījaprādhānyadarśanāt |

	abhāve bījino mātā tadabhāve tu pūvajaḥ || 

iti tenaivānantaram uktatvāt | anena jyeṣṭhavān apy asvatantra ity uktam | na kevalaṃ pitṛmātṛjyeṣṭhavān evāsvatantra ity āha sa eva |

	asvatantrāḥ striyaḥ putrā dāsā ye ca parigrahāḥ || iti |

parigrahā upajīvinaḥ | kāryaviśeṣeṣu strīṇām asvātantryam ity āha hārītaḥ |

	dānārthe vā dhanārthe vā dharmārthe vā viseṣataḥ |

	ādāne vā visarge vā na strī svātantryam arhati ||

anyān apy asvatantrān āha nāradaḥ |

	asvatantrāḥ prajāḥ sarvāḥ svatantraḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ |

	asvatantraḥ smṛtaḥ śiṣyaḥ ācārye tu svatantratā ||

atra svatantranirūpaṇaṃ cāsvatantrakṛtaṃ kāryaṃ tenaiva nivartanīyam iti darśayitum | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	asvatantrakṛtaṃ kāryaṃ tasya svāmī nivartayet |

	na bhartrā vivadetānyo bhītonmattakṛtād ṛte ||

bhītōnmattādikṛtanivartane rājña evādhikārāt bhītonmattādisvāminā kṛtanivartakena mahān yasya vivādo nātyantānucita ity abhiprāyaḥ | asvatantrakṛtanivartanasya kvacid apavādam āha nāradaḥ |

	etāny eva pramāṇāni bhartā yady anumanyate |

	putraḥ patyur abhāve vā jāyā vā patiputrayoḥ ||

	tathā dāsakṛtaṃ kāryam akṛtaṃ paricakṣate |

	anyatra svāmisaṃdeśān na dāsaḥ prabhur ātmanaḥ ||

	putreṇa ca kṛtaṃ kāryaṃ yat syād acchandataḥ pituḥ |

	tad apy akṛtam evāhuḥ dāsaḥ putraś ca tau samau || iti |

asvatantrakṛtanivartanaṃ svatantānumatyabhāvaviṣaye kāryam ity arthaḥ | kātyāyano 'pi |

	na kṣetragṛhadāsānāṃ dānādhamanavikrayāḥ |

	asvatantrakṛtāḥ siddhiṃ prāpnuyur nānuvarṇitāḥ ||

anuvarṇitās tu siddhiṃ prāpnuvantīty āha sa eva |

	pramāṇaṃ sarva evaite paṇyānāṃ krayavikarye |

	yadi saṃvyavahāraṃ te kurvanto 'py anumoditāḥ ||

evaṃ kṣetrādīnāṃ krayādikaraṇe svatantreṇa niyuktāḥ bhrātrādayo 'svatantrāḥ pramāṇaṃ syur ity āha sa eva |

	kṣetrādīnāṃ tathaiva syuḥ bhrātā bhrātṛsutaḥ sutaḥ |

	nisṛṣṭāḥ kṛtyakaraṇe guruṇā yadi gacchatā ||

nisṛṣṭāḥ niyuktā ity arthaḥ | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	yaḥ svāminā niyuktas tu dhanāyavyayapālane |

	kusīdakṛṣivāṇijye nisṛṣṭārthas tu sa smṛtaḥ ||

	pramāṇaṃ tatkṛtaṃ sarvaṃ lābhālābhavyayodayam |

	svadeśe vā videśe vā svāmī taṃ na visaṃvadet || iti |

kātyāyano 'pi nisṛṣṭārthakṛtaṃ kāryaṃ na svāmī parivartayitum arhatīty āha |

	nisṛṣṭārthas tu yo yasmin tasminn arthe prabhus tu saḥ |

	tad bhartā tatkṛtaṃ kāryaṃ nānyathā kartum arhati ||

evam anumatiniyuktyor abhāve 'pi kuṭumbabharaṇārtham asvatantakṛtaṃ svatantro nānyathākartum arhatīty āha manuḥ |

	kuṭumbārthe tv adhīno 'pi vyavahāraṃ samācaret |

	svadese vā videśe vā tannyāyān na vicālayet ||

evam āpatpratīkārārthe 'pi draṣṭavyam | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	strīkṛtāny apramāṇāni kāryāṇy āhur anāpadi |

strīgrahaṇam asvatantropalakṣaṇārtham | evaṃ cāpadyasvatantrakṛtāny api pramāṇānīty ārthiko 'rthaḥ pratyetavyaḥ | atrāpavādapradarśanārtham āha sa eva |

	viśeṣato gṛhakṣetradānādhamanavikrayāḥ | iti |

gṛhakṣetrayor dānādhamanavikrayās tv āpady apy asvatantrakṛtā na sidhyantīty arthaḥ | evaṃ tadbhāṣye vyākhyātam | tathā svatantreṇāpy asvatantrakalpena krtaṃ kāryaṃ na sidhyatīty āha nāradaḥ |

	svatantro 'pi hi yat kāryam kuryad aprakrtiṃ gataḥ |

	tad apy akrtam evāhur svatantratvahetutaḥ ||

svatantrāś ca tenaiva nirūitāḥ |

	trayaḥ svatantrā loke 'smin rājācāryas tathaiva ca |

	pratiprati ca sarveṣāṃ varṇānāṃ svagṛhe gṛhī ||

	svātantryaṃ tu smṛtaṃ jyeṣṭhe jyaiṣṭhyaṃ guṇavayaḥkṛtam || iti |

gṛhīti vadan gṛhiṇyāḥ svatantratā nāstīti darśayati | tena yady api mātṛmato 'svatantratoktā, tathāpi mātuḥ svatantratāvagantavyā | ata evābhartṛkayā kṛtasya kāryasya putrādyanumatyaiva siddhir uktā | "prakṛtiṃ gataḥ" ity asyāpy arthas tenaiva darśitaḥ |

	kāmakrodhābhibhūtārtā bhayavyasanapīḍitāḥ |

	rāgadveṣaparītāś ca jñeyās tv aprakṛtiṃ gatāḥ ||

evaṃ ca svatantraprakṛtisthakṛtaṃ kāryaṃ sidhyati, na tv aprakṛtisthasvatantrakrtam ity āha sa eva |

	kule jyeṣṭhas tathā śreṣṭhaḥ prakṛtisthaś ca yo bhavet |

	tat kṛtaṃ syāt kṛtaṃ kāryaṃ nāsvatantrakṛtaṃ kvacit ||

svatantraprakṛtisthakṛtam api putravikrayādi kāryaṃna sidhyati, tatra tasyāsvatantratvād ity āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	sutasya sutadārāṇāṃ vaśitvaṃ tv anuśāsane |

	vikraye caiva dāne ca vaśitvaṃ na sute pituḥ ||

ataḥ sutavikrayādi kāryaṃ svatantraprakṛtisthakṛtam api nivartanīyam ity abhiprāyaḥ | ekaputraviṣayam etad iti dattāpradānikākhyapade vakṣyāmaḥ | evam anekavārakṛtaikartṛkaikakarmakavikrayādāv (?) api punar vikrayādir vaśitvābhāvān na sidhyatīty āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	sarveṣv arthavivādeṣu balavaty uttarā kriyā |

	ādau pratigrahe krīte pūrvā tu balavattarā || iti |

tenottarādikriyā nivartanīyety abhiprāyaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ kṛtanivartanam**

**atha bālādidhanaviṣayāṇi kānicid vacanāni likhyante**

tatra manuḥ |

	bāladāyadakaṃ rikthaṃ tāvad rājānupālayet |

	yāvat syāt sa samāvṛtto yāvad vātītaśaiśavaḥ ||

bāladāyādakaṃ bālasvāmikaṃ rikthaṃ dravyam | avidyamānāptapuruṣaviṣayam etat | bālagrahaṇaṃ svadhanarakṣaṇāsamarthopalakṣaṇārtham iti spaṣṭayitum āha sa eva |

	vaśāputrāsu caivaṃ syād rakṣaṇaṃ niṣkulāsu ca |

	pativratāsu ca strīṣu vidhavāsv āturāsu ca ||

vaśā vandhyā | aputrā avidyamānaputrā | niṣkulā svapakṣahīnā | vaśāprabhṛtīnāṃ dhanaṃ ye 'paharanti teṣāṃ daṇḍam āha sa eva |

	jīvantīnāṃ tu tāsāṃ ye tad dhareyuḥ svabāndhavāḥ |

	tāñ chiṣyāc coradaṇḍena dhārmikaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ ||

rakṣaṇasamarthasyāpi dhanaṃ tatsthānāparijñānādinā svāmy anupāttam anyena tūpādāya rājñe vijñāpitaṃ janasamūheṣu vikhyāpya rājñā rakṣyam ity āha gautamaḥ: "praṇaṣṭam asvāmikam adhigamya rājñe prabrūyuḥ | vikhyāpya saṃvatsaraṃ rājñā rakṣyam" iti | yat tūktaṃ manunā,

	praṇaṣṭasvāmikaṃ rikthaṃ rājā tryabdaṃ nidhāpayet |

iti, tad atyantadūradeśe svāmisthitisaṃbhāvanāviṣayam | nidhāpanaṃ ca svadhanāmiśrabhāvena rājñā kāryam, tathā ca sa eva |

	praṇaṣṭādhigataṃ dravyaṃ tiṣṭhed yuktair adhiṣṭhitam |

	ye tatra coro gṛhṇīyuḥ tān rājebhena ghātayet ||

svāminaṃ prati praṇaṣṭam anyena ca labdhaṃ praṇaṣṭādhigatam | ibhena hastinā | praṇaṣṭādhigatasya dravyasya pratyarpaṇam āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	praṇaṣṭādhigataṃ deyaṃ nṛpeṇa dhanine dhanam | iti 

dhanī ca tad dhanaṃ svāmitvam udbhāvya gṛhṇīyāt | tathā ca manuḥ |

	mamedam iti yo brūyāt so 'nuyojyo yathāvidhi |

	saṃvādya rūpasaṃkhyādīn svāmī tad dravyam arhati ||

yo memedam iti brūyāt sa tasya svāmitvajñānāya rājapuruṣaiḥ kasmin deśe kasmin kāle kīdṛgvarṇaṃ kīdṛśasaṃsthanaṃ kiṃsaṃkhyākaṃ kiṃparimāṇakaṃ praṇaṣṭam iti pṛṣṭo yādṛśaṃ praṇaṣṭasya saṃsthānādikaṃ tādṛśam eva vadan tad dravyaṃ grahītum arhatīty arthaḥ | pratyuta paradravyāpahāre pravṛttatvā daṇḍam arhatīty āha sa eva |

	avedayāno naṣṭasya deśaṃ kālaṃ ca tattvataḥ |

	varṇaṃ rūpaṃ pramāṇaṃ ca tatsamaṃ daṇḍam arhati ||

tattvataḥ avedayāno visaṃvādaṃ kurvāṇaḥ tatsamaṃ praṇaṣṭādhigatasamam | praṇaṣṭādhigataṃ saṃvatsarād arvāg eva grahītum arhatīty āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	śaulkikaiḥ sthānapālair vā naṣṭāpahṛtam āhṛtam |

	arvāk saṃvatsarāt svāmī hareta parato nṛpaḥ ||

atyantadūradeśasthasvāmiviṣaye tu manur āha |

	arvāk tryabdād dharet svāmī parato nṛpatir haret | iti |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> nṛpatir hared ity etat paradravyāpahārapratiṣedhaśāstraviruddham |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span>, ata evāsya pṛthaṅnihitasthānāt nṛpatiḥ svadhanasthānam āhared ity artho 'vagantavyaḥ | evaṃ cāvadhim atikramyāgatāyāpi svāmine rūpasaṃkhyādibhir bhāvitaṃ praṇaṣṭādhigataṃ deyam eva | kiṃ tu tataḥ kiṃcid dravyam avadhyatikramāparādhāt nṛpo gṛhṇīyāt | tathā ca sa eva |

	ādadītātha ṣaḍbhāgaṃ praṇaṣṭādhigatāt nṛpaḥ |

	daśamaṃ dvādaśaṃ vāpi satāṃ dharmam anusmaran ||

athety atikrāntāvadheḥ svāminaḥ samāgamanānantaryam ucyate | samāgamasyātyantavilambe ṣaṣṭho bhāgaḥ | ativilambe tu daśamo bhāgaḥ vilambābhāve tu dvādaśo bhāga iti vyavasthā mantavyā | yat tu gautamenoktam: "ūrdhvam adhigantuś caturthaḥ rājñaḥ śeṣaḥ" iti, tad atikrāntāvadhikasya svāmino nāśaniscayaviṣaye draṣṭavyam | svāmini dhriyamāṇe tv adhigantuḥ nṛpabhāgacaturhāṃśo bhavatīty asmād eva vacanāt gamyate | yat tu yājñavalkyenoktam |

	paṇān ekaśaphe dadyāt caturaḥ pañca mānuṣe |

	mahiṣe 'ṣṭa gavāṃ dvau dvau pādaṃ pādam ajāvike || iti |

tad ekaśaphādau viśeṣaśāstraṃ manūktaṣaḍbhāgādyādānavidher bādhakam iti kaiścid vyākhyātṛbhir uktam | anyais tv ekaśaphādāv adhigantre deyaṃ nirūpayituṃ tad ity uktam | praṇaṣṭādhigatanidhiharaṇam adhikṛtya viśeṣam āha manuḥ |

	mamāyam iti yo brūyān nidhiṃ satyena mānavaḥ |

	tasyādadīta ṣaḍbhāgaṃ rājā dvādaśam eva cā ||

	anṛtaṃ tu vadan daṇḍyaḥ sa vittasyāṃśam aṣṭamam || iti |

mamāyam, yato mayā matpuruṣair vā nihita iti satyena rūpasaṅkhyāsaṃvādādipramāṇena jñāpayed ity arthaḥ | svāmino nirguṇatve ṣaḍbhāgam ādadīta | saguṇatve tu dvādaśabhāgam iti vyavasthātra mantavyā | tathā nidhisvāmino vidvadbrāhmaṇatve tu tena rājñe na kiṃcid api dātavyam ity āha sa eva |

	vidvāṃs tu brāhmaṇo dṛṣṭvā pūrvopanihitaṃ nidhim |

	aśeṣato 'py ādadīta sarvasyādhipatir hi saḥ ||

pūrvopanihitaṃ svapitrādibhir upanihitam | vidvadgrahaṇaṃ ṣaṭkarmino 'py upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva vasiṣṭhaḥ: "brāhmaṇaś ced adhigacchet ṣaṭkarmasu vartamānaḥ sarvaṃ haret" iti | ṣaṭkarmasu yajanādiṣv ity arthaḥ | yat punar manunoktam,

	nidhīnāṃ hi purāṇānāṃ dhātūnām eva ca kṣitau |

	ardhabhāg rakṣaṇād rājā bhūmer adhipatir hi saḥ ||

iti, tad uktalakṣaṇabrāhmaṇādhigatāsmaryamāṇasvāmikanidhiviṣayam, purāṇānām ity abhidhānāt | yat tu vasiṣṭhenoktam: "aprajñāyamānaṃ vittaṃ yo 'dhigacched rājā tad dhared adhigantre ṣaṣṭham aṃśaṃ pradāya" iti, tad uktalakṣaṇarahitādhigantṛviṣayam | ata eva yājñavalkyaḥ | 

	itareṇa nidhau labdhe rājā ṣaṣṭhāṃśam āpnuyāt |

	aniveditavijñāto dāpyas tad daṇḍam eva ca ||

vidyāṣaṭkarmasaṃpannabrāhmaṇād itarasmai nidhyadhigantre dātuṃ rājā ṣaṣṭhāṃśam adhigatanidhisakāśād āhared iti pūrvārdhasyārthaḥ | adhigatanidhivañcakāt taṃ nidhiṃ sarvaṃ śaktyapekṣayā daṇḍaṃ ca rājā gṛhṇīyād ity uttarādhasyārthaḥ | rājña evādhigantṛtve manur āha |

	yatra paśyen nidhiṃ rājā purāṇaṃ nihitaṃ kṣitau |

	tasmād dvijebhyo dattvārdhaṃ śeṣaṃ kośe niveśayet ||

svakīyanidher adhigame tu sarvaṃ kośe niveśayet, "nidhyadhigamo rājadhanam" iti gautamasmaraṇāt | corahṛtaṃ dhanaṃ prati tenoktam: "corahṛtam apajitya yathāsthānaṃ gamayet, kośād vā dadyāt" iti | prathamapakṣakaraṇāsamarthaviṣaye dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ | yathāha vyāsaḥ |

	pratyāhartum aśaktas tu dhanaṃ corair hṛtaṃ yadi |

	svakośāt tad dhi deyaṃ syād aśaktena mahīkṣitā || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ bālādidhanaviṣayāṇi**

**iti sakalavidyāviśārada - śrīkeśavādityabaṭṭopadhyāyasūnu - **

**yājñika - devaṇabhaṭṭopādhyāya -somayajivicaritāyāṃ**

**smṛticandrikāyāṃ vyavahārakāṇḍe **

**prathamaḥ paricchedaḥ**



**dvitīyaparicchedaḥ**

	bṛhaspatimukhānekamunivāgvāgurāntaram |

	praviṣṭo devaṇācāryaḥ kurute padasaṃgraham ||

**tatra dhanaprayogavidhiḥ**

sarvavyavahārapadasādhāraṇo vidhikalāpaḥ prāk pratipāditaḥ | saṃpati pratipadam asādhāraṇo vidhikalāpaḥ pripādyate | padānāṃ cāṣṭādaśānāṃ svarūpam avāntarabhedajātaṃ ca dvitīye prakaraṇe darśitam | iha padoddeśakramenādāv ṛṇādānākhyapadasya vidhir ucyate | tatrāpy ādau dhanadānadharmā ucyante | tatra dhaninaṃ praty āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	paripūrṇaṃ gṛhītvādhiṃ bandhaṃ vā sādhulagnakam |

	lekhyārūḍhaṃ sākṣimad vā ṛṇaṃ dadyād dhanī sadā ||

paripūrṇaṃ savṛddhikamūladravyaparyāptam ity arthaḥ | kaḥ punar ādhiḥ katividhaś cety apekṣite sa eva |

	ādhir bandhaḥ samākhyātaḥ sa ca proktaś caturvidhaḥ |

	jaṅgamaḥ sthāvaraś caiva gopyo bhogyas tathaiva ca ||

	yādṛcchikaḥ sāvadhiś ca lekhyārūḍho 'tha sākṣimān || iti |

yady apy atrādhir aṣṭavidho darśitaḥ, tathāpi gopyabhogyayādṛcchikasāvadhirupabhedānām atrānekaviśeṣavidhyupayogārthatātparyātiśayena kathaṃ nānyeṣām iti vaktuṃ proktaś caturvidha ity uktam | yāvad ṛṇaṃ tava na dadāmi tāvad ayam ādhir ity evaṃ kālaviśeṣāvadhiśūnyatayā kṛto yādṛcchikaḥ | dīpotsavakāle ṛṇaṃ datvā ayam ādhir mayā mokṣyate no cet tavaiva bhavatīty evaṃkṛtaḥ sāvadhiḥ | yady evam ādhir eva bandha itīhocyate kathaṃ tarhi pūrvasmin vacane "bandhaṃ vā" iti bedhenoktam, ucyate: tatra bandhapadasya yo vivakṣitārthaḥ sa hi nāradena darśitaḥ |

	nikṣepo mitrahastastho bandho viśvāsakaḥ smṛtaḥ || iti |

uttamarṇādhamarṇayor yaḥ sakhā tasya pārśve nikṣiptam evādhamarṇadhanam uttamarṇaviśvāsārtham adharmarṇenopadiṣṭaṃ bandha iti gīyata ity arthaḥ | lagnakaḥ pratibhūḥ | sa ca svāmyādivyatirikto grāhyaḥ, svāmyādau dhanasiddher duṣkaratvāt | ata eva tanniṣedhaḥ kātyāyanena darśitaḥ |

	na svāmī na ca vai śatruḥ svāminādhikṛtas tathā |

	niruddho daṇḍitaś caiva saṃdighaś caiva na kvacit ||

	naiva rikthī na mitraṃ na ca caivātyantavāsinaḥ |

	rājakāryaniyuktaś ca ye ca pravrajitā narāḥ ||

	nāśakto dhanine dātuṃ daṇḍaṃ rājñe ca tatsamam |

	nāvijñāto grahītavyaḥ pratibhūtvakriyāṃ prati || iti |

saṃdigdho 'bhiśastaḥ | atyantavāsino naiṣṭhikabrahmacāriṇaḥ | tatsamaṃ vivādāspadībhūtadravyasamam | naiva rikthīty avibhaktaviṣayam | yad āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	bhrātṝṇām atha dampatyoḥ pituḥ putrasya caiva hi |

	prātibhāvyam ṛṇaṃ sākṣyam avibhakte na tu smṛtam || iti |

nārado 'pi |

	sākṣitvaṃ prātibhāvyaṃ ca dānaṃ grahaṇam eva ca |

	vibhaktā bhrātaraḥ kuryuḥ nāvibhaktāḥ parasparam ||

"lekhyārūḍhaṃ sākṣimat" iti cādyaślokagatam ṛṇasya viseṣaṇaṃ mantavyam | tatra yena prakāreṇa ṛṇasya lekhyārūḍhatā kartavyā diṅmātreṇa tam eva prakāram āha saṅgrahakāraḥ |

	cirakaṃ nāma likhitaṃ purāṇaiḥ pauralekhakaiḥ |

	arthipratyarthinirdiṣṭaiḥ yathāsaṃbhavasaṃstutaiḥ ||

	svakīyaiḥ pitṛnāmādyair arthipratyarthisākṣiṇām |

	pratināmabhir ākrāntam arthisākṣisvahastavat ||

	spaṣṭāvagamasaṃyuktaṃ yathāsmṛtyuktalakṣaṇam || iti |

saṃstutaiḥ praśastaiḥ | pratiśabdo 'trākrāntapadena saṃbadhyate | vistaras tv asya lekhyaprakaraṇe jānapadākhyalekhyābhidhāne draṣṭavyaḥ | sākṣimattāprakārasya diṅmātraṃ tu vyāsenoktam |

	dharmajñāḥ putriṇo maulāḥ kulīnāḥ satyavādinaḥ |

	śrautasmārtakriyāyuktā vigatadveṣamatsarāḥ |

	yuvānaḥ sākṣiṇaḥ kāryā ṛṇādiṣu vijānatā || iti |

vistaras tv asyāpi sākṣiprakaraṇādau draṣṭavyaḥ | evam uktavidhinā sadā dhanī ṛṇaṃ dadyāt | vṛddhyarthaṃ dhanaprayogaṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | vṛddhiparimāṇabhedās tūttaratra vṛddhiprakaraṇe vakṣyante,

	dadyur vā svakṛtāṃ vṛddhiṃ sarve sarvāsu jātiṣu |

ityādivacanaiḥ | te cātrānusaṃdheyāḥ | evam anekaniyamānubandhaṃ dhanaprayogaṃ kurvato dṛṣṭam eva phalam, dṛṣṭārthamātrārthatvād āsāṃ smṛtīnām | ata eva vyatirekamukhena dṛṣṭārtham evāha hārītaḥ |

	ādhiḥ vinā lagnakaṃ vā prayuktaṃ bandhakād vinā |

	sākṣilekhyavihīnaṃ tu visaṃvāde na sidhyati ||

nārado 'pi |

	visrambhahetū dvāv atra pratibhūr ādhir eva ca |

	likhitaṃ sākṣiṇas ca dve pramāṇe vyaktikārake ||

visrambho viśvāsaḥ | vyaktir abhivyaktiḥ | evaṃ cābandhakādiprayogo 'pi labhyet | tathā prayoge 'pi prayuktasya dhanasya kathaṃcit siddhisaṃbhavāt | ata evābandhakaprayoge 'pi vṛddhiniyamo vakṣyate,

	saṃbandhe bhāga āśītaḥ ṣāṣṭo bhāgaḥ salagnake |

	nirādhāne dvikasataṃ māsalābhā udāhṛtāḥ ||

ityādinā | asvatantreṣu prayoganiṣedham āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	na strībhyo dāsabālebhyaḥ prayacchet kvacid uddhṛtam |

	dātā na labhate tat tu tebhyo dadyāt tu yad vasu ||

stryādīnām asvatantratvād ity abhiprāyaḥ | uddhṛtaṃ prayogāya gṛhītam |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ dhanaprayogavidhiḥ**

**nirdoṣadhanikasyādhiviṣayāṇi**

 

atha ādhiviṣayāṇi kānicidvacanāni likhyante | tatra hārītaḥ |

	bandhaṃ yathā sthāpitaṃ syāt tathaiva pratipālayet | iti |

adhigrahaṇād (?) ūrdhvam ādher nāśahrāsavikārāsāratvavyaktyantaratvādayo yathā na bhavanti tathā dhanī pratyarpaṇaparyantaṃ prayatena (?) pālayed ity arthaḥ | evaṃ pālyamāne 'py ādhau daivādivaśān nāśādir yadi bhavet tadā na kaścid doṣo dhanina ity āha sa eva |

	daivarājopaghāte tu na doṣo dhaninaḥ kvacit | iti |

agnideśopaplavādir daivopaghātaḥ | anaparādhe 'py ucchṛṅkhalatvena rājñā kṛtaḥ paropaghāto rājopaghātaḥ | atra kātyāyanaḥ |

	ādhīkṛtaṃ tu yat kiṃcid vinaṣṭaṃ daivarājataḥ |

	tatrarṇaṃ sodayaṃ dāpyo dhaninām adhamarṇakaḥ ||

pakṣāntaram apy āha vyāsaḥ |

	daivarājopaghāte tu na doṣo dhaninaḥ kvacit |

	ṛṇaṃ dāpyas tu tannāśe bandhaṃ vānyam ṛṇī tadā ||

evam ādher asāratve 'py anusaṃdheyam | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	rakṣyamāṇō 'pi yatrādhiḥ kāleneyād asāratām |

	ādhir anyo 'tha vā kāryo deyaṃ vā dhanine dhanam ||

asāratā savṛddhikamūladravyāparyāptatā (?) | kecid ekasaṃvatsarabhavavṛddhisahitamūladravyāparyāptatām asāratām āhuḥ, tac cintyam, evaṃvidhaviśeṣāśrayaṇe kiṃ kāraṇam iti codyasaṃbhavāt | anyaḥ pūrvasthito vā ādhiḥ paryāptaḥ kāryaḥ | anyagrahaṇasya paryāptatvena bhāvyam ity etāvanmātraparatvāt | yato 'sāratve 'pi paryāptaye kiṃcid deyaṃ kvacid ity āha hārītaḥ |

	ādheḥ samadhikaṃ dravyaṃ gṛhītaṃ grāhakeṇa tu |

	adhikaṃ tava dāsyāmi tad dadyād dhanikasya saḥ ||

grāhakeṇa ṛṇikena | adhikaṃ pūrakam | yady api daivādinimittakādhyapacāre pakṣadvayam uktam, tathāpi dhanikadoṣarāhitye sphuṭe sati corasvajanādinimittakādhyapacāre 'pi etat pakṣadvayaṃ veditavyam | daivādigrahaṇasya dhanikadoṣavihīnanimittaparatvena kṛtatvāt | ata eva,

	daivarājopaghāte tu na doṣo dhaninaḥ kvacit |

iti vyāsahārītābhyām uktam | ata eva cādhyantaradānapakṣaṃ dhanikadoṣavihīnatvenaivāha kātyāyanaḥ |

	na ced dhanikadoṣeṇa nipated vikriyeta vā |

	ādhim anyaṃ sa dāpyaḥ syād ṛṇān mucyeta narṇikaḥ || iti |

dhanikadoṣād anyata ādhyapacāre ṛṇika ṛṇān na mucyate | tenānyam ādhiṃ sa ṛṇiko dhanine rājñā dāpya ity arthaḥ | yat tu smṛtyantaram,

	srotasāpahṛte kṣetre rājñā caivāpahārite |

	ādhir anyo 'dhikartavyo deyaṃ vā dhanine dhanam || 

iti, tad api dhanikasyādoṣe pakṣadvayavidhiparam, anyathā agnyādyapahṛte pakṣadvayam anenānuktaṃ syāt |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ nirdoṣadhanikasyādhiviṣayāṇi**

**atha sadoṣadhanikasyādhiviṣayāṇi**

atra hārītaḥ |

	bandhaṃ yathā sthāpitaṃ syāt tathaiva pratipālayet |

	anyathā naśyate lābho mūlaṃ vā tadvyatikramāt ||

yathā yena prakāreṇa gopyatvena bhogyatvena vāsthāpitam adhamarṇenādhīkṛtaṃ tathaiva gopyam ādhiṃ gopyatvenaiva bhogyaṃ bhogyatvenaiva dhanī pālayet | anyathā gopyaṃ bhogyatvena bhogyaṃ vā gopyatvena pālitaṃ cet samayātikramāl lābho naśyate, mūlaṃ vā dravyaṃ naśyata ity arthaḥ | yājñavalkyo 'pi lābhanāśam āha: "gopyādhibhoge no vṛddhiḥ" iti | bhoge balād iti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	no bhoktavyo balād ādhir bhuñjāno vṛddhim utsṛjet | 

iti bhogapratiṣedhaṃ kurvantam ādhātāram ākramya gopyādhiṃ bhuñjānasya atyantāparādhitvāt alpabhoga eva sarvavṛddhināśaḥ syād iti arthaḥ | sarvamūlanāśas tu nāsmin viṣaye vikalpyate | atyantādhikahānitvāt | tena mūlaṃ veti hārītavacanaṃ sarvamūlanāśarūpapakṣāntarābhidhāyakaṃ balātkārakṛtamahābhogaviṣayam iti mantavyam | yas tv ādhātāraṃ vañcayitvā gopyādhiṃ bhuṅkte tasya bhogānusāreṇa lābhadravya eva bhāgaśo nāśa ity āha manuḥ |

	yaḥ svāminānanujñātam ādhiṃ bhuṅkte vicakṣaṇaḥ |

	tenārthdvṛddhir moktavyā tasya bhogasya niṣkṛtiḥ ||

ardhagrahaṇam ananujñātabhogānusāreṇa kalpitaniṣkṛtikṣamaparimāṇopalakṣaṇārtham | anyathā mahābhogasyārdhavṛddhivisarjanena niṣkṛtyasaṃbhavāt tasya bhogasya niṣkṛtir iti vākyaśeṣavirodhaḥ syāt | atha virodhaparihārārtham alpabhogaviṣayam evaitad vacanam ity ucyate ta(syā)dānanujñātamahābhogaviṣaye (?) lābhahānir anenānuktā syāt | na cānenānuktatve 'pi "gopyādhibhoge no vṛddhiḥ" iti yājñavalkyavacanena tatra lābhahānir ucyate ity vācyam, balakṛtālpabhogaviṣayatvāt tasya | tasmād arthagrahaṇasyopalakṣaṇatvam eveti yuktam | bhogyādhau tu gopyatvena pālite lābhasyaiva nāśaḥ | samayātikramamātreṇa mūlanāśapakṣānavatārāt | na ca bhogyādhau vṛddhyabhāvāl lābhanāśapakṣasyāpy anavatāra iti vācyam, bhogasyāpi lobhatvāt | na ca tatrābhoge vṛddhilābho bhaviṣyatīti vācyam | yat āha manuḥ |

	na tv evādhau sopakāre kausīdīṃ vṛddhim āpnuyāt | iti |

sopakāre ādhau bhogyādhāv ity arthaḥ (?) | etad uktaṃ bhavati: ādhibhogamātrārthaṃ prayuktadhanasyātmāparādhād ito bhogālābhe lābhahānir eva, na punar aṅgīkṛtavṛddhisiddhir iti | ādhātrādyaparādhād abhoge (?) tu bhuñjānād adhamarṇād vā bhogalābha eva grāhyo dhaninā na tu vṛddhir iti mantavyam | yady evaṃ bhogyādhau na kadcid api vṛddhiḥ, kathaṃ tarhi yājñavalkyena,

	gopyādhibhoge no vṛddhiḥ sopakāre 'tha hāpite |

iti bhogyādhāv apy upekṣayā kāryākṣamatve dhanikena kṛte vṛddhipratiṣedhaḥ kṛtaḥ, prāptyabhāvāt pratiṣedhānupapatteḥ | ucyate: yatrādhātā ādher upabhogaṃ vṛddhidānam apy āpady abhyupagacchati, tatra prāptā vṛddhiḥ "sopakāre 'tha hāpite" ity anena pratiṣidhyate | na ca vṛddhibhogayoḥ samuccayenābhyupagatir eva nāsti, "na tv evādhau" iti manuvacananivāritatvād iti vācyam | manuvacanasya bhogyādhau kadācid abhoge 'stu vṛddhir iti śaṅkāvyudāsārthatvāt | tasmād anyathā pālite sarvatrādhau lābhanāśo na gopyamātra iti siddham | etena gopye lābhasya hāniḥ, bhogye tu lābhāvāvān mūlahānir iti śambhūktaṃ nirastam | kātyāyano 'py anyathāpālane kvacid amūladhananāśena saha lābhanāśasya vikalpam āha |

	akāmam ananujñātam ādhiṃ yaḥ karma kārayet |

	bhoktā karmaphalaṃ dāpyo vṛddhiṃ vā labhate na saḥ ||

karmaphalaṃ dāsyādyādhau vetanam, śakaṭādyādhau bhāṭakādikam, na tu dāsyādikṛtāvaghātādikarmaṇah phalaṃ taṇḍuladikam, aparādhānanurūpatvāt | atrāpi karmānusāreṇeti draṣṭavyam | dāpyo bandhasvāmine rājñeti śeṣaḥ | akāmam iti dāsyādibuddhimadādhiviṣayam, anyatrāsaṃbhavāt | tathā karma kurvāṇe 'y aśvādyādhāv atikramakaraṇe daṇḍo na mūladhanahānir bhavatīty āha sa eva |

	yas tv ādhiṃ karma kurvāṇaṃ vācā daṇdena karmabhiḥ |

	pīḍayed bhartsayec caiva prāpnuyāt pūrvasāhasam ||

akurvati pīḍanabhartsanakāriṇo 'pi na daṇḍaḥ, kurvāṇam ity abhidhānāt | kvacid daṇḍādhyapagamābhyāṃ hānir ity āha sa eva |

	balād akāmaṃ yatrādhim anisṛṣṭaṃ praveśayet |

	prāpnuyāt sāhasaṃ pūrvam ādhātā cādhim āpnuyāt ||

anisṛṣṭam anāhitam, bhogyādhau balād alpasyāpy anāhitasya bhoge bhoktur daṇḍaḥ sarvamūlanāśaś ca syād iti tātparyārthaḥ | vañcanayā tu bhoge kṛte bhogānusāreṇa mūlanāśaḥ, anyathā balād grahaṇānarthakyāpatteḥ | yas tv ādhau hrāsādikaṃ karoti taṃ pratyāha yājñavalkyaḥ: "naṣṭo deyaḥ" iti | dhaninaḥ pramādān naṣṭo vikrtiṃ gato bandhaḥ pūrvavat kṛtvādhamarṇāyottamarṇena deya ity arthaḥ | adhamarṇāc ca salābham ṛṇam uttamarṇo gṛhṇīyāt | avikṛtasyaivādher arpitatvāt | atha vikṛtam evādhim arpayati tadā ṛṇam eva labhate lābhahāneḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	upacāras tathaivāsya lābhahāniviparyaye |

	pramādād dhaninas tadvad ādhau vikṛtim āgate || iti |

atra pūrvārtham"bandhaṃ yathā sthāpitam" ityādihārītavacanasamānārtham | uttarārdhasya tv ayam arthaḥ | yadvad viparyaye lābhāhāniḥ tadvad vikṛtim āgate yadi vikṛtam evārpayed iti | ayaṃ ca pakṣo vikṛtasyādheḥ pūrvavatkaraṇaparyāptalābhasadbhave, anyathā prācīna eva pakṣaḥ | pramādād iti dhanikadoṣopalakṣaṇārtham | tena bhogavyatiriktadoṣād vikṛtim āgate 'py ādhau pūrvavat kṛtvārpaṇaṃ lābhahānir vā | bhogād vikṛtim āgate tu gopyādhau dvayam apīty anusaṃdheyam | vikṛtim āgata ity anenaiva hrāsavyaktyanyatvāsāratvādy api saṃgṛhītam ādher ayathāsvarūpatvataulyāt | tena tarāpy eṣa eva vidhir jñeyaḥ | bhogād asāratve tu mūladravyam eva hīyata ity āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	bhukte tv asāratāṃ prāpte mūlahāniḥ prajāyate | iti |

asāratvānusāreṇety abhiprāyaḥ | yadā tu dhanikadoṣād ādhiḥ vidhvastas tadā mūlyadvāreṇādhiṃ datvā dhanī salābham ṛṇaṃ gṛhṇīyāt | tad āha vyāsaḥ |

	grahītṛdoṣān naṣṭaś ced bandho hemādiko bhavet |

	ṛṇaṃ salābhaṃ saṃśodhya tanmūlyaṃ dāpayed dhanī ||

ādhito 'py adhikabhūtasalābharṇaviṣayam etat | ṛṇaparyāptādhināśe tv āha nāradaḥ: "vinaṣṭe mūlanāśaḥ syāt" iti | salābharṇaparyāptādhināśe tu salābarṇanāśaḥ syād ity etad apy āha hārītaḥ |

	tatsamo dviguṇo vādhir dhanikasya samarpitaḥ |

	ādhau naṣṭe dhanaṃ naṣṭaṃ dhanikasyādhir eva ca ||

dhanaṃ samaṃ dviguṇaṃ vā | dhanikasyādhināśo 'trādhyantarālābhāt | etad uktaṃ bhavati | dhvastādhidhanasamānadhananāśaḥ dhanikasya syād iti | salābharṇāt bahumūlyādhināśe tu salābharṇādurvaritādhimūlyam (?) ādhidātre deyam ity āha bṛhaspatiḥ | 

	bahumūlyo yatra naṣṭaḥ ṛṇikaṃ tatra toṣayet | iti |

na ca toṣayed iti vacanād yāvatā dhanena tuṣyati tāvad dhanaṃ deyam iti śaṅkanīyam | yata āha manuḥ |

	mūlyena toṣayed enam ādhisteno 'nyathā bhavet | iti |

salābharṇāpagatāvaśiṣṭādhyaṃśasya mūlyenety arthaḥ | yadi dhanī mūlyena ṛṇikaṃ na toṣayati tadā tv ādhipratyarpaṇapratibhūr mūlyena ṛṇikaṃ toṣayet | tathā ca hārītaḥ |

	khādako vittahīnaś cel lagnako vittavān yadi |

	mūlyaṃ tasya bhaved deyaṃ na vṛddhiṃ dātum arhati ||

ādhīkṛtasya dhanasya prītidattadhanasyeva kāritavṛddhyasaṃbhavād ity abhiprāyaḥ | khādakho bandhakhādakaḥ | ādhināśaka iti yāvat | lagnakaḥ pratibhūḥ | mūlyaṃ khāditādher mūlyam | yady atra ṛṇiko balād vṛddhiṃ gṛhṇāti tadā gṛhītavṛddhyā sahāparādhānurūpadaṇḍabhāg ity āha sa eva |

	dviguṇaṃ triguṇaṃ vāpi yaḥ sādhayati lagnakam |

	rājagāmi tu tad dravyaṃ sādhako daṇḍam arhati ||

lagnakagrahaṇaṃ dhanikasyāpy upalakṣaṇārtham | avidhyamānavṛddhisādhananyāyasya dhanike 'pi tulyatvāt | evaṃ dhanio 'py anyāyakṛd daṇḍabhāk | tathā ca katyāyanaḥ |

	ādhiṃ duṣṭena lekhyena buṅkte yam ṛṇikād dhanī |

	nṛpo damaṃ dāpayitvā ādhilekhyaṃ vināśayet ||

ṛṇikadravyabhoganiṣkṛtyarthaṃ vṛddhihānir atrāpy unneyā ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ sadosadhanikādhiviṣayāṇi **

**athādheḥ svatvadhvaṃsādiviṣayāṇi**

tatra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	ādhiḥ praṇaśyed dviguṇe dhane yadi na mokṣyate | iti |

prayuktārthe dviguṇībhūte yadi gopyādhir na mokṣyate tadāsau praṇaśyati, adharmarṇasya svaṃ na bhaved ity arthaḥ | kṛtakālas tv ādhir gopyo bhogyo vā saṃpratipanne kāle yadi na mokṣyate tadā tasyāpi pūrvavan nāśam āha sa eva: "kāle kālakṛto naśyet" iti | yady aham idam iyatā kālena ṛṇaṃ na dadāmi tadādhir evānṛṇāya tava bhaviṣyatītry evam abhihitaḥ kālakṛtaḥ | atra dhaninaḥ svatvāpattim āha vyāsaḥ |

	hiraṇye dviguṇībhūte pūrṇe kāle kṛtāvadhau |

	bandhakasya dhanī svāmī dvisaptāhaṃ pratīkṣya tu ||

anenārvāk caturdasadinād ādhināśo 'pi nety arthād uktam | uktaṃ ca sākṣād evānantaram |

	ato 'ntarā dhanaṃ datvā ṛṇī bandhakam āpnuyāt | iti |

ato 'ntarā caturdasadinād argāv ity ārthaḥ | nanūrdhvam api caturdaśadinād dhanaṃ datvā bandhakam ṛṇī kim iti nāpnoti, svatvadhvaṃsakābhāvāt | dhanadvaiguṇyam avadhibhūtakālātikramaṇaṃ ca taddhvaṃsakam iti cet, na, dānavikrayāder eva taddhvaṃsakatvāt | ādiśabdaparigṛhītavarfgāntargataṃ dvaiguṇyādikam apīti cet, na, svatvadhvaṃsakatayā lokaprasiddhānām evādiśabdena parigrahāt | dvaiguṇyādikam api tatheti cet, na — na hi loke dvaiguṇyādes tathā prasiddhir asti | ucyate — satyaṃ dvaiguṇāder nasty eva tathā prasiddhiḥ, dravyavinimayasya tu tathā prasiddhir asty eva tilavikrayapratiṣedhād vikrayākaraṇe 'pi vinimayena tilānāṃ svatvanivṛttidarśanāt | tataś cātrāpi kṛtakālādhau ṛṇagrahaṇakāla eva yady aham iyatā kālena na dadāmi tadādhir evānṛṇyāya tava bhaviṣyatīti dhanikarṇikayor dhanavinimayasaṃpratipatter jñātatvād avadhibhūtakāle svatvadhvaṃso yukta eva | etad eva nāśanimittaṃ yājñavalkyena "kālakṛtaḥ" ity anenoktam | dvaiguṇye tu yad api ṛṇagrahaṇakāle yady ahaṃ dvaiguṇye 'py ādhiṃ na mokṣayāmi tadādhir evānṛṇyāya tava bhaviṣyatīti dhanikarṇikayor dhanavidhimayasaṃpratipattiniyamābhāvaḥ | tathāpi yatraiveyaṃ saṃpratipattiḥ kṛtā tatraiva dvaiguṇye svatvadhvaṃsaḥ, hetusadbhāvāt, tadviṣayaṃ ca "ādhiḥ praṇaśyet" iti vacanam ity anavadyam | evaṃ krayapratigrahādyabhāve 'pi vinimayenaivādhau dhanikasya svatvāpattiḥ vrīhyādāv iva tilaviniyamakartur iti yuktam uktam "bandhakasya dhanī svāmī" iti | dvisaptadinapratīkṣaṇaṃ tu vinimayadārḍhyajñānārtham uktam | dravyavikrayāder iva dṛḍhavinimayasaiva svatvadhvaṃsādinimittatvāt | evaṃ ca "ato 'ntarā dhanaṃ datvā" ity api vacanaṃ yuktam eva | yat tu bṛhaspatinoktam,

	pūrṇāvadhau śāntalābhe bandhe svāmī dhanī bhavet |

	anirgate daśāhe tu ṛṇī mokṣitum arhati ||

iti, tad vṛddhyarthaprayuktavastrādiviṣayam, "brāhmaṇebhyo dadhi dīyatām" ityādivat sāmānyaviśeṣanyāyāt | lābhaśāntir api vastrādau traiguṇyādividhāyakavacanānusāreṇavagantavyā | evaṃ ca caturdaśadinād ūrdhvam ādhau svatvāpatteḥ yatheṣṭaviniyogo hiraṇyaprayoktur aviruddhaḥ | vastrādiprayoktus tu dasadinād ūrdhvam eveti mantavyam | yat punas tenoktam,

	gopyādhiḥ dviguṇād ūrdhvaṃ kṛtakālo yathāvidhi |

	āvedayitvarṇikule bhoktavyaḥ samanantaram ||

iti, tat svatvāpatter arvāg ādher abhogamātravidhiparam, na punar yatheṣṭaviniyogo na kadācit tv ādher astīty evaṃparam, samanantaram ity abhidhānāt | tasmān na bārhaspatyavacanayoḥ parasparavirodhaḥ | nāpi vyāsabṛhaspativacanayoḥ | yat punar manunoktam,

	na cādheḥ kālasaṃrodhān nisargo 'sti na vikrayaḥ |

iti, tasyāyam arthaḥ: kālasaṃrodhaḥ cirakālāvasthānād dviguṇībhūte 'py amokṣaṇam iti yāvat | tasmāt kālasaṃrodhāt kevalād ṛṇagrahaṇakāle vinimayasaṃpratipattirahitād ādher na nisargo 'sti nānyatrādhīkaraṇaṃ dānaṃ vāsti, vikrayaś ca nāsti, kiṃ tu śāntalābhas tiṣṭhaty eva tāvad yāvad ādhātrā na vimokṣyata iti | yadā tu śāntalābhe dhane bandhakasya tathaivāvasthitasya mocanāt prāk ṛṇikasya maraṇādir bhavet tatra kiṃ kāryam ity apekṣite āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	hiraṇye dviguṇībhūte mṛte naṣṭe 'dhamarṇike |

	dravyaṃ tadīyaṃ saṃgṛhya vikrīṇīta (?) samākṣikam ||

	rakṣed vā kṛtamūlyaṃ tu daśāhaṃ janasaṃsadi |

	ṛṇānurūpaṃ parato gṛhṇītānyat tu varjayet || iti |

hiraṇye dviguṇībhūte paścād ādhimokṣaṇād arvāg it śeṣaḥ | naṣṭe kutra gata iti cirakālam avijñāte | adharmarṇagrahaṇam ṛṇadādādhikāriṇaḥ putrāder upalakṣaṇārtham | dravyam ādhīkṛtadravyam | ṛṇānurūpaṃ dviguṇadravyaparyāptam | anyat tu varjayed iti vadan hiraṇye dviguṇībhūte 'pi dhane dhanikasyādāv asvāmitvaṃ darśayati | tataś ca vinimayahīnādhiviṣayam anuvacanavad etad api vacanaṃ mantavyam | "hiraṇye dviguṇībhūte" ity udāharaṇatayoktam, tataś ca vastrādau śāntalābhe 'pi vacanam etad ūhyam | ata eva sāmānyenoktam kātyāyanena |

	ādhātā yatra na syāt tu dhanī bandhaṃ nivedayet |

	rājñe tataḥ savikhyāto vikreya iti dhāraṇā ||

	savṛddhikaṃ gṛhītvā tu śeṣaṃ rājany athārpayet || iti |

ādhātṛgrahaṇamātrāpi pūrvavad upalakṣaṇārtham | rājany arpayed iti jñātyādipratyāsannābhāvaviṣayam, tatsadbhāve tatraivārpaṇasya nyāyyatvāt | yatra śeṣārpaṇaṃ kriyate tenaiva yadi savṛddhikaṃ dhanaṃ datvā bandho gṛhyate tadā na vikrayaḥ prayojanasya viddhatvāt | ata eva tiṣṭhed veti pratīkṣaṇapakṣo 'py uktaḥ | anyatra tv ādhīkaraṇam apy asmin viṣaye na viruddham, daṇḍpūpanyāyāt | kiṃ tu mūlamātram evānyatrādhīkṛtyādeyaṃ na tu savṛddhikam | yad āha prajāpatiḥ,

	dhnī dhanena tenaiva param ādhiṃ nayed yadi |

	kṛtvā tad ādhilikhitaṃ pūrvaṃ cāsya samarpayet || 

iti, yad bandhasvāmini dhanaṃ prayuktaṃ tattulyenaiv dhanena paraṃ dhanikāntaram ādhiṃ nayet, na tv adhikenety arthaḥ | ayaṃ cānvādhau niyamastampratipattyā (?) dvaiguṇyādarvādaganvādhau (?) draṣṭavyaḥ | evam ukto jñātyādāv arpaṇānto vidhiḥ bahumūlyādhiviṣaya eva, śeṣārpaṇādes tatraiva saṃbhavāt | samamūlye 'py evaṃ vikrīya gṛhītvā ṛṇaśeṣam ṛṇādānādhikāriṇi kathaṃcid ātte (?) gṛhṇīyād ityādyuktavacanata evohyam | yadā tv ādhātā svalpamūlyadhanaṃ sukṛtaṃ vādhāya ṛṇaṃ gṛhītvā dvaiguṇye jāte 'pi śāntalābhaṃ dhanaṃ na vardhate, na cādher ādhānāntaraṃ vikrayaṇaṃ vā dhaninā kartuṃ mayy avasthite śakyam iti buddhyā ṛṇadāne vilambam evālambate tadāsau rājñā dāpya ity āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	caritrabandhakakṛtaṃ savṛddhyā dāpayed dhanam | iti |

dvyarthīṃ cāyaṃ granthaḥ | ekas tāvad arthaḥ | svacchāśayādhamarṇāṅgulīyakādyalpamūlyaṃ (?) bandhakam abhūt tac caritrabandhakam, tena kṛtam upāttam ṛṇam adadatam adhamarṇam uttatamārṇāya savṛddhikaṃ savṛddhikaṃ rājā dvaiguṇyād ūrdhvaṃ dāpayed iti | anyas tu: caritraṃ iṣṭāpūrtādiko dharmaḥ, sa eva bandhakam ādhiḥ tena kṛtam ityādi samānam | evaṃvidhe tv ādhau dhanam aprayacchato 'dhamarṇasya nāsty ānṛṇyam ity abhiprāyaḥ | akṛtakālaphalabhogyādhāv apy ānṛṇyam adharmarṇasya dhanadānata eva nānyataḥ, phalabhogād avṛddhikatve 'pi mūlānapāyāt | na cādhinauva tad apāya iti vācyam, yad āha sa eva: "phalabhogyo na naśyati" iti | mūladhāpradāne tavaivādhir bhaviṣyatīti vinimayasaṃpratipatter dhanagrahaṇānantarakṣaṇa eva mūladhanāpradānād ādhināśāpattyāsaṃbhavanirastatvād anyasya nāśakasyāvidhyamānatvād ity abhiprāyaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām ādheḥ svatvadhvaṃsādiviṣayāṇi **

**athādhisiddhiviṣayāṇi**

tatra nāradaḥ |

	ādhis tu dvividhaḥ proktaḥ jaṅgamaḥ sthāvaras tathā |

	siddhir asyobhayasyāpi bhogo yady asti nānyathā ||

siddhiḥ ādhitvasiddhiḥ | anyathā vinā bhogam adhamarṇoddiṣṭasyottamarṇasvīkāramāreṇeti yāvat | gopyādhau nirbhoge bhogasthānīyabhāṇḍāgārāntarnidhānādivyāpārād ādhitvasiddhir (?) adhyavaseyā | evam asmākam etadīyaṃ gṛhādyādhir iti ṛṇikasaṃnidhau madhyasthajaneṣv āvedanaṃ dūrasthatvādinā bhogādyabhāve tv ādhisādhakam ity avagantavyam | ata eva vyatirekamukhena pūrvokteṣu sādhakatvam āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	na bhuṅkte yaḥ svam ādhānaṃ nādadyān na nivedayet |

	pramītasākṣī ṛṇikaḥ tasya lekhyam apārthakam || \
svam ādhānam | lekhyam ādhilekhyam | siddheḥ saṃdigdhalekhyaśuddhir api prayojanam ity arthād uktam | evam evādhīyamānavyaktiviśeṣollekhanena lekhanam apy ādhisādhakam | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	marādācihnitaṃ kṣetraṃ grāmaṃ vāpi yadā bhavet |

	grāmādayaś ca likhyante tadā siddhim avāpnuyāt ||

grāmādayaś ca kṣetrādhyādher vyāvartakatveneti seṣaḥ | ādhiśabdena deśādayo gṛhyante ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām ādhisiddhiviṣayāṇi**

**athādhyādivivādāpanodaviṣayāṇi**

tatra viṣṇuḥ |

	dvayor nikṣipta ādhau tu vivadetāṃ yadā narau |

	yasya bhuktir jayas tasya balātkāraṃ vinā kṛtā ||

tasyaiva bhogād ādhisiddher jātatvād ity abhiprāyaḥ | dvayor api bhuktiyuktatve tv āha bṛhasptatiḥ |

	kṣetram ekaṃ dvayor bandhe dattaṃ yat samakālikam |

	yena bhuktaṃ bhavet pūrvaṃ tasya tatsiddhim āpnuyāt ||

dattam adharmarṇenoddiṣṭam ity arthaḥ | kṣetragrahaṇaṃ bhogyādher upalakṣaṇārtham | ata evāviseṣeṇāha vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	tulyakāle 'bhisṛṣṭānāṃ lekhyānām ādhikarmaṇi |

	yena bhuktaṃ bhavet pūrvaṃ tasyādhir balavattaraḥ ||

tulyakālotpannānāṃ lekhyānāṃ sadbhāvasāmye 'pi bhogyādhsiddhau bhogasya pradhānakāraṇatvāt tatprāthamyanibandhanā balavattā yuktety arthaḥ | bhogaviśeṣe 'py āha sa eva |

	yady ekadivase tau tu bhoktukāmāv upāgatau |

	vibhajyādiḥ samaṃ tena bhoktavya iti niścayaḥ ||

tena tābhyām ity arthaḥ | gopyādhāv api tadupādānādikartur jayaḥ, tasyaivādhisiddher jātatvāt | dvayos tatsiddisāmye 'py āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	ādhim ekaṃ dvayor yas tu kuryāt kā pratipad bhavet |

	tayoḥ pūrvakṛtaṃ grāhyaṃ tatkartā coradaṇḍabhāk ||

ṛṇagrahaṇopakramatvād ādhikriyā pratipad ity ucyate | pūrvakṛtaṃ pūrvam upādānādinā siddham | ādhiviśeṣe daṇḍaviśeṣam āha viṣṇuḥ: "gocarmamātrādhikāṃ bhuvam anyasyādhīkṛtāṃ tasmād anirmocyānyasya yaḥ prayacchet sa vidhayḥ ūnā cet tu ṣoḍaśasuvarṇaṃ daṇḍyaḥ" iti | upādānādau yaugapadye 'py āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	tulyakālopasthitayor dvayor api samaṃ bhavet || iti |

upasthitayor upādānādikaṃ kartum iti śeṣaḥ | sākṣilekhyamātrasiddhānām ādhyādīnāṃ madhye lekhyasiddhaṃ virodhe grāhyam ity āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	ādhānaṃ vikrayo dānaṃ lekhyasākṣikṛtaṃ yadā |

	ekakriyāviruddhaṃ tu lekhyaṃ tatrāpahārakam ||

lekhyaṃ lekhyakṛtaṃ lekhyasiddam iti yāvat | apahārakaṃ balavat | lekhyasiddhatvāviseṣe 'pi balābalam āha sa eva |

	anirdiṣṭaṃ ca nirdiṣṭam ekatra ca vilekhitam |

	viśeṣalikhitaṃ jyāya iti kātyāyano 'bravīt ||

ekatrādhīkaraṇādau viśeṣalikhitaṃ nirdiṣṭalikhitaṃ tat anirdiṣṭalikhitājjyāya ity arthaḥ | lekhye nirviśitaṃ vilekhitam | anirdiṣṭanirdiṣṭapadayor arthaṃ svayam eva vyācaṣṭe |

	yo vidyamānaṃ pradhanam snādiṣṭasvarūpakam |

	ākāśabhūtam ādadhyād ādiṣṭaṃ naiva tad bhavet ||

	yad yat tadāsya vidyeta tad ādiṣṭaṃ vinirdiśet || iti |

praśabdaḥ pādapūraṇārthaḥ | anādiṣṭasvarūpakam anirūpitasvarūpakam | ākāśabhūtam avidyamānaprāyam | ādiṣṭaṃ naiva tad bhavet nirdiṣṭaṃ nai tad bhavet, anirdiṣṭaṃ bhaved iti yavat | ādiṣṭaṃ nirdiṣṭam | evaṃ cāyam arthaḥ: ādhātur ādhīkaraṇakāle yad yad dhanaṃ vidyeta nirūpitasvarūpaṃ ca tat tad dhanam ādhitvenādiṣṭaṃ san nirdiṣṭam ity ucyate | tad viparītaṃ tu dhanam ādhitvena kalpyamānam anirdiṣṭam ity ucyata iti | ādhīkaraṇakāle vidyamānatvasāmye 'py āha sa eva |

	yas tu sarvasvam ādiśya prāk paścān nāmacihnitam |

	ādadhyāt tat kathaṃ tu syāc cihnitaṃ balavattaram ||

asyārthaḥ: yaḥ pūrvam aviśeṣeṇa sarvasam ādhitvenoddiśya kasyacid dhastād ṛṇaṃ gṛhītvā kālāntare punar dhanikasaṃpratipattyā kṣetrādikaṃ kiṃcid eva ghaṭṭādicihnitaṃ pūrvagṛhītaṛṇārtham eva dadyat, tatra cihnitaṃ balavattaram | pūrvādher ādhikriyāntarādidriyāpratibandhakadhanikenaiva tyaktatvād iti | cihnitam iti virodhyantarakriyopalakṣaṇārtham | tena yadā prathamam ādhim ādāya dhanī dhanaṃ datvā pascād avañcakatvaṃ vijñāya ādhim antareṇaivāta ūrdhvam ṛṇam āstāṃ tvyīti prakarāntareṇa punaḥ kriyāṃ karoti, tadā nirādhikriyaiva balavatīty avagantavyam | ata eva yājñavalkyaḥ |

	sarveṣv arthavivādeṣu balavaty uttarā kriyā | iti |

tena pūrvasyāḥ kriyāyā bādhikā (?) bhavatīty abhiprāyaḥ | udāharaṇāntaraṃ tu: aśītibhāgavṛddhike dhane punas tadardhavṛddhike sauhārdādivaśāt kṛte saty aśītibhāgavṛddhikriyāyāḥtadardhabhāgavṛddhikriyayā bādhanam | cihnitādikaṃ ca pūrvoktam atraivodāharaṇam ity anusaṃdheyam | kvacid apavādam uttarakriyābalavattvasyāha sa eva |

	ādhau pratigrahe krīte pūrvā tu balavattarā | iti |

svāmitvapratibandhāpagamābhyāṃ prāg eva pūrvasyāḥ kriyāyāḥ kṛtatvād ity abhiprāyaḥ | anenaivābhiprāyeṇa vasiṣṭho 'pi |

	yaṃ pūrvataram ādhāya vikrīṇāti tu tam punaḥ |

	kim etayor balīyaḥ syāt prāktanaṃ balavattaram ||

yady apy ādhīkaraṇena na svāmibhāvo nivartate, tathāpi pratibadhyate | tataś ca pratibandhasvāmibhāvena kṛto vikrayaḥ pareṇa kṛta ivāsiddhatvād durbalo bādhya evety anavadyam | ādhyādīnāṃ yaugapadye 'py āha sa eva |

	kṛtaṃ yatraikadivase dānādhamanavikrayam |

	trayāṇām iti saṃdehe kathaṃ tatra vicintayet ||

	trayo 'pi tad dhanaṃ dharmyaṃ vibhajeyur yathāṃśataḥ |

	ubhau kriyānusāreṇa tribhāgena pratigrahī || iti |

yatra trayāṇāṃ dānādikaṃ kṛtaṃ tatra katham iti saṃdehe nirṇayāya vicintayed ity arthaḥ | ubhau dhanikakretārau | kriyānusāreṇa dattadhanānusāreṇa | dhane kriyetiśabdaḥ karaṇavyutpattyā vartitum utsahate | bṛhaspatir api |

	kṛtaṃ ced ekadivase vikrayādhipratigraham |

	trayāṇām api saṃdigdhe kathaṃ tatra vicāraṇā ||

	trīṇy evātra pramāṇāni vibhajeyur yathāṃśataḥ |

	ubhau cārthānusāreṇa tribhāgena pratigrahī || iti |

arthānusāreṇa bhāgadvayaṃ gṛhṇīyātām iti seṣaḥ | evaṃ pūrvavacane 'pi kriyānusāreṇety atra viśeṣo draṣṭavyaḥ | tribhāgena pratigrahī saṃbadhyata iti śeṣaḥ | pratigraha iti tu pāṭhe pūrvavacanavan niṣpadyata iti viśeṣo grāhyaḥ |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ vivādāpanodaviṣayāṇi **

**athādhimocanaviṣayāṇi**

tatra vyāsaḥ |

	gopyādhiṃ dviguṇād ūrdhvaṃ mocayed adhamarṇakaḥ || iti |

dviguṇād ūrdhvaṃ prayuktadhane śāntalābhe satīty arthaḥ | mocayet savṛddhikamūladāneneti śeṣaḥ | etac ca dvaiguṇyādinibandhanādhināśābhāvaviṣaye veditavyam | tannibandhanādhināśaviṣaye tu tannāśāt prāg eva mocayet | tathā coktaṃ tenaiva |

	dhanam atra savṛddhikamūlaṃ vivakṣitam | ato 'ntarā ṛṇikapratīkṣaṇāyoktakālamadhyakāla ity arthaḥ | ṛṇikapratīkṣaṇakalaś ca lābhaśāntim ārabhya dvisaptadinam | lābhaśāntitaḥ pūrvakālamadhye 'pi savṛddhike dhane datte bandhāvāptir daṇḍāpūpanyāyād anenaiva vacanenokteti mantavyam | phalabhogyādhiṃ tu mūlamātraṃ datvā phalakālānte vartamānam āpnuyād ṛṇīty āha sa eva |

	phalabhogyaṃ pūrvakālaṃ datvā dravyaṃ tu sāmakam | iti |

"ṛṇī bandhakam āpnuyāt" iti pūrvārdhe paṭhitam ihānuṣajyate | samam eva sāmakam, mūlamātram iti yāvat | phalabhogyagrahaṇāt svarūpeṇa bhogyavastrādyādhau na kālavyavasthā | tatra dhaninaṃ pray āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	dhanaṃ mūlīkṛtaṃ datvā yadādhiṃ prārthayed ṛṇī |

	tadaiva tasya moktavyo hy anyathā doṣabhāg dhanī ||

bhogyādhāv evam eva | gopyādhau tu mūlīkṛtaṃ savṛddhikaṃ datvā yadā prārthayate tadaiva moktavyam | mūlīkṛtagrahaṇasyādhamarṇadeyadhanaparatvāt | doṣaḥ steyadoṣaḥ | ata eva yājñavalkyaḥ |

	upasthitasya moktavya ādhiḥ steno 'nyathā bhavet | iti |

upasthitasya dhanadānapūrvakam ādhimokṣāyopasthitasya | stenaḥ stenavad daṇḍya ity arthaḥ | upasthitasya deśataḥ kālato vā dhanikavyavadhāne sati dhanikakuṭumbenādhir moktavyaḥ | etad apy arthād āha sa eva |

	prayojake sati dhanaṃ kule nyasyādhim āpnuyāt | iti |

prayojako dhanaprayoktā | āpnuyāt tadānīm evati śeṣaḥ | atha vā, adhamarṇaḥ prayoktṛkule nyastadhano 'pi prayoktur āgamanād ūrdhvam evādhiṃ tanmūlyadhanaṃ vā ṛṇāpākaraṇakāle parikalpitam avṛddhikam āpnuyāt | etad apy āha vacobaṅgyā sa eva |

	tatkākakṛtamūlyo vā tatra tiṣṭhed avṛddhikaḥ | iti |

tiṣṭhed ādhir iti śeṣaḥ | tatra prayoktṛkula ity arthaḥ | saty api dhanaprayojake dhane śāntalābhe 'pi kvacid viṣaye cireṇaivādhim ṛṇī samāpnuyād ity āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	kṣetrādikaṃ yadā bhuktam utpannam adhikaṃ tataḥ |

	mūlodayaṃ praviṣṭaṃ cet tadādhiṃ prāpnuyād ṛṇī ||

ādhīkṛtaṃ kṣetrādikaṃ dhanikena lābhaśānteḥ paścād eva yadā bhuktaṃ tato bhujyamānād yadi dhanam utpannam adhikaṃ kṣetrārthavyayād abhyadhikaṃ mūlodayatulyaṃ yadā yasmin kāle dhanini praviṣṭaṃ tadā tasmin kāla evādhim ṛṇī labhata ity arthaḥ | evam ādhilābhaḥ kasmin viṣaye bahavtīty apekṣite sa evāha |

	pāribhāṣya yadā kṣetraṃ pradadyād dhanike ṛṇī |

	tvayaitac chāntalābhe 'rthe bhoktavyam iti niścitam ||

	praviṣṭe sodaye dravye pradātavyaṃ tvayā mama || iti |

tvayaitad ityādi (?) paribhāṣya yadā ṛṇagrahaṇakāle kṣetrādyādhiṃ pradadyāt, tadā prāguktavidhayādhilābha ity arthaḥ | evam evādher lābho 'nayaiva paribhāṣayā lābhaśānteḥ paścād ādhau datte bhavatīty āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	yadā tu dviguṇībhūtam ṛṇam ādhau tadā khalu |

	mocya ādhis tadutappne praviṣṭe dviguṇe dhane ||

ādhau tadā datta iti śeṣaḥ | ata eva viṣṇuḥ: "gṛhītadhanapraveśārtham eva yat sthāvaraṃ dattaṃ tad gṛhītadhapraveśe dadyāt" | evaṃbhūtaparibhāṣayā cābhihitaṃ kṣayādhim ācakṣate laukikāḥ | evaṃbhūtaparibhāṣākaraṇe tu sodayād atyantābhyadhike 'pi praviṣṭe sāmakadānaṃ vinā na kadācid ādhilādha (bha?) ity anusaṃdheyam | tathānyatrāpi kvacid viṣaye sāmakadānaṃ vinā nādhilābha ity āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	yatrāhitaṃ gṛhakṣetraṃ bhogena prakarṣānvitam |

	tatrarṇī nāpnuyād bandhaṃ dhanī caiva ṛṇaṃ tathā ||

	pūrṇe prakarṣe tatsvāmyaṃ tūbhayoḥ parikīrtitam |

	apūrṇe 'pi prakuryātāṃ parasparamatena tau || iti |

viṣayajñānaṃ vinā nāsyārtho jñātuṃ śakya iti viṣayas tāvad abhidhīyate — śāntalābhe dhane jāte vṛddhimātrāvāptyartham ayam ādhir bhoktavya iti paribhāṣāṃ kṛtvādhir dattaḥ, ṛṇagrahaṇakāle lābhaśāntikāle vāsvāc cādher etāvati kāla utpannaṃ vṛddher aparyāptam api samagravṛddhyartham evāstv iti paribhāṣākaraṇakāle 'nuktaṃ ca | atha vā tatrāsmāc cādher ityādy astv ity antam uktam eveti dvidhā viṣayaḥ | artho 'py abhidhīyate — ādhyutpanno 'rthaḥ utpattyarthavyayād avaśiṣṭaḥ prakarṣapadenātroktaḥ, tasmain samagravṛddhyaparyāpte dhanini praviṣṭe ṛṇī mūlamātraṃ datvā bandhaṃ paribhāṣitakālātyaye 'pi nāpnuyāt | dhanī ca ṛṇamūlamātraṃ tadā nāpnuyāt na gṛhṇīyāt, kiṃ tu pūrṇe prakarṣe samagravṛddhiparyāpte dhanino mūlamātre ṛṇino bandha ity evam ubhayos tatsvāmyaṃ parikīrtitam | tasmāt tasminn eva kāle sāmakaṃ datvādhiṃ mocayed iti śeṣaḥ | yadāpy apūrṇaḥ samagravṛddher aparyāptaḥ prakarṣaḥ tadāpi svāmyaṃ prakuryātāṃ parasparamatena vṛddher aparyāptam api samagravṛddhyartham evāstv iti paribhāṣākaraṇakāle kṛtena tau dhanikarṇikāv iti | svāmyakaraṇasya ca phalaṃ paribhāṣitakālātyaye samagravṛddhiparyāptaprakarṣapraveṣābhāve 'pi sāmakam eva datvā ṛṇikena bandhamocanam | parasparamateneti vadan tadabhāve dhaninaḥ svāmyaṃ vṛddhiśeṣe 'pīti darśayati | tathā paribhāṣitakālaikadeśa eva samagravṛddhiparyāptaprakarṣapraveśe 'py āha sa eva |

	yadi prakarṣitaṃ tat syātadā (?) na dhanabhāg dhanī |

	ṛṇī na labhate bandhaṃ parasparamataṃ vinā || iti |

dvayor api vacanayoḥ paribhāṣitakālātyaya iti śeṣo draṣṭavyaḥ | evaṃ cāyam arthaḥ — tad bandhakaṃ yadi prakarṣitaṃ samagravṛddhiparyāptaprakarṣānvitaṃ paribhāṣitakālaikdeśe syāt tadā na paribhāṣitakālātyaye sati dhanī dhanabhāk, ṛṇī ca tasmin sati na labhate bandham, kiṃ tu samagravṛddhiparyāptaparkarṣāntaram eva dhanī mūladhanabhāk ṛṇī ca mūlamatraṃ datvā bandhaṃ labhata iti | parasparamataṃ vineti vadan idaṃ darśayati: paribhāṣitakālaikadeśe samagravṛddhiparyāptaprakarṣapraveśo 'stu vā mā vā, sarvathā yāvat paribhāṣitakālaṃ vṛddhyartham ādhibhogaḥ kriyatām iti ṛṇikenokte yatra dhanikena om ity uktaṃ tatra vṛddher abhyadhikaprakarṣapraveśe 'pi paribhāṣitakālātyaya eva sāmakaṃ datvā bandhakam ṛṇī labhate, na punaḥ paribhāṣitakālamadhya iti | anenaiva vyākhyānena,

	yāvat prakarṣitaṃ tat syāt tāvan na dhanabhāg dhanī |

	ṛṇī na labhate bandhaṃ parasparamataṃ vinā ||

iti vyāsavacanam api vyākhyātam |

**iti smṛticandrikāyām ādhiprakaraṇam**

**atha pratibhūbhedāḥ**

atha pratibhūviṣayāṇi kānicid vacanāni likhyante | tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	darśane pratyaye dāne ṛṇidravyārpaṇe tathā |

	catuṣprakāraḥ pratibhūḥ śāstre dṛṣṭo manīṣibhiḥ ||

pratyayo viśvāsaḥ | dānam ṛṇāpākaraṇārtham arthārpaṇam | ṛṇidravyārpaṇam ṛṇino yad dravyaṃ gṛhopakaraṇādi tadarpaṇam | catuṣprakārapratibhuvām aṅgīkāraprakāro 'pi tenaiva darśitaḥ |

	āhaiko darśayiṣyāmi dādhur eṣo 'paro 'bravīt |

	dātāham etad draviṇam arpayāmīti cāparaḥ ||

eko darśanapratibhūr aham enaṃ palāyanapravṛttaṃ darśayiṣyāmīti prātibhāvyaṃ bhajann āha | aparaḥ pratyayapratibhūḥ eṣa sādhur vañcakaḥ matpratyayenāsya dhanaṃ dehīti brūte | dānapratibhūḥ yadā yadā yan na dadāti draviṇaṃ gṛhītaṃ savṛddhikaṃ tadā tasya draviṇasya aham eva dāteti vadati | aparaḥ ṛṇidravyārpaṇapratibhūr yadāyaṃ gṛhītaṃ dhanaṃ na dadāti tadāham etadīyaṃ dhanam arpayāmīti bravītīti vākyacatuṣṭayasyārthaḥ | hārīto 'pi |

	abhaye pratyaye dāne upasthāne 'rthadarśane |

	pañcasv eṣu prakāreṣu grāhyo hi pratibhūr budhaiḥ ||

abhayam upadravākaraṇam | upasthānam atra bandhadravyārpaṇam abhimataṃ na darsanam, tasya svapadenaivopattatvāt | pañcasv ity asyāghaṭanāc ca | vyāso 'pi |

	lekhye 'kṛte ca dviye vā dānapratyayadarśane |

	gṛhītabandhopasthāne ṛṇidravyārpaṇe tathā ||

pratibhuvo grāhyā iti śeṣaḥ | lekhye 'kṛte lekyādarśane, divye vākṛta ity anuṣaṅgaḥ | etad uktaṃ bhavati: vivādanirṇayāya dṛṣṭam adṛṣṭaṃ vā pramāṇaṃ yatra kālavyavadhānena bhaviṣyati tatrāpi pramāṇāya pratibhūr grāhya iti | dānapratyayadarśanāni prāg eva vyākhyātāni | gṛhītabandhopasthānaṃ yācakatvena kretur darśanādyarthaṃ vā uttamarṇānujñayādharmarṇagṛhītasya bandhasya punar arpaṇam | kātyāyano 'pi |

	dānopasthānavādeṣu viśvāsasapathāya ca |

	lagnakaṃ kārayed evaṃ yathāyogaṃ viparyaye ||

upasthānaṃ darsanam | vādo vivādaḥ | tatra prativādyānayanānantaraṃ sabhyair lagnakagrahaṇaṃ sādhitadhanādiprāptyarthaṃ kāryam | dāsādau coratvādiśaṅkāyāṃ viśvāsāya pratibhūḥ kāryaḥ | śapathāya lagnakagrahaṇaṃ śapathavilambe kāryam | evam anyatrāpi viparyaye kāryasya nyāyaviṣaye yathāsaṃbhavaṃ lagnakaṃ kārayed ity anvayaḥ | tataś ca pūrvādhvikrayadāneṣy dhūrtadayādasaṃbhavanāyāṃ satyāṃ gopyādhāv ādhipālākhyaḥ pratibhūr bhogyādhau bhuñjāpakākhyo bahumūlyādāv api pratyarpakākhyaś cānenaiva saṃgṛhīta ity avagantavyam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām prabhūbhedāḥ **

**atha pratibhuvām asādhāraṇā vidhayaḥ**

atha kātyāyanaḥ |

	darśanapratibhūr yas taṃ deśe kāle ca darśayet | iti |

yo yasya darśanapratibhūr abhūt sa yatra deśe kāle ca dhanikasya taddarśanāpekṣā tatra taṃ darśayed ity arthaḥ | darśitaś cet prātibhāvyād asau mocya ity āha sa eva |

	yady asau darsayet tatra moktavyaḥ pratibhūr bhavet | iti |

yas tu tatra na darśayati taṃ praty āha manuḥ |

	yo yasya pratibhūs tiṣṭhed darsanāyeha mānavaḥ |

	adarśayan sa taṃ tasya prayacchet svadhanād ṛṇam ||

ṛṇam atra savṛddhikaṃ vivakṣitam, pratibhūputradeyarṇe 'pi savṛddhikatvasmaraṇāt | yadā tu darśanīyaḥ kutra gata ity ajñātaḥ tadā tv āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	naṣṭasyānveṣaṇe kālaṃ dadyāt pratibhuve dhanī |

	deśānrūpataḥ pakṣaṃ masaṃ sārdham athāpi vā ||

sārdhamāsād adhikaṃ na dadyāt, niyamārthatvād vacanasya | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	naṣṭasyānveṣaṇārthaṃ tu deyaṃ pakṣatrayaṃ param |

	yady asau darsayet tatra moktavyaḥ pratibhūr bhavet ||

	kāle pratīte pratibhūr yadi taṃ naiva darśayet |

	sa tam arthaṃ pradāpyaḥ syāt prete caivaṃvidhaḥ smṛtaḥ || iti |

paraṃ paramāvadhirūpam | pratīte pratipanne 'nveṣaṇārthaṃ kalpita iti yāvat | tam arthaṃ darśanīyād yal labhyam | evaṃvidhiḥ sa tam arthaṃ pradāpyaḥ syād iti vidhiḥ | yadi pratibhuvā darśanīyo daivakṛte rājakṛte vā nimitte asati na darśitaḥ tadaiva prāgukto vidhir ity āha sa eva |

	darśane pratibhūr yas tu deśe kāle na darśayet |

	nibandham āvahet tatra daivarājakṛtād ṛte ||

nibandhaṃ deyadravyam | āvahet dhanine prāpayet | daivakṛtaṃ dīrgharogajñātimaraṇādi, rākakṛtam āsedhanabandhanādi | anyeṣāṃ tu keṣāṃcit pratibhuvāṃ vidhim āha nāradaḥ |

	ṛṇiṣv apratikurvatsu pratyaye cātha hāpite |

	pratibhūs tad ṛṇaṃ dadyād anupasthāpayaṃs tathā ||

ṛṇiṣv apratikurvatsv iti dānapratibhūviṣayam | pratyaye cātha hāpite iti pratyayapratibhūviṣayam | anupasthāpayann iti kathaṃcid adhamarṇagṛhītabandhopasthānapratibhūviṣayam | apratikurvatsu śāṭhyena nirdhanatvādinā vā ṛṇam adadatsu | pratyaye hāpite viśvāse vyabhicarite | anupasthāpayan uttamarṇapārśvasthm ādhiṃ kathaṃcid adhamarṇagataṃ punar uttamarṇasamīpastham akurvan | pitāmaho 'pi |

	ādhipālakṛtas tv ādhiḥ mitakālopalakṣitaḥ |

	na cet sa dhanine dattaḥ tasyādhes taiḥ samarpaṇam ||

acireṇa ṛṇī svāparādhādinānyākrāntaṃ yadi nādhim arpayati tadāsmābhir ādhiḥ samarpyata iti vadadbhir yaiḥ pratibhūbhir ya ādhir arpaṇīyatayāṅgīkṛtaḥ, tasya ṛṇikenāsamarpitasya taiḥ samarpaṇaṃ kāryam ity arthaḥ | tair iti bahuvacanam ekatvādisaṃkhyopalakṣaṇārtham, ata eva hārītaḥ |

	viśvāsārthaṃ kṛtas tv ādhir na prāpto dhaninā yadā |

	prāpaṇīyas tadā tena deyaṃ vā dhanine dhanam ||

tena ādhipālenety arthaḥ |yadā prāpayitum aśakyaṃ tadaiva dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ | bahumūlyādhāv adhamarṇāyādhipratyarpaṇapratibhūr yaḥ tam api praty āha sa eva |

	khādako vittahīnaś cel lagnako vittavān yadi |

	mūlyaṃ tasya bhaved deyaṃ na vṛddhiṃ dātum arhati ||

khādako bandhabhakṣakaḥ bahumūlyādhināśako dhanika iti yāvat | mūlyaṃ bahumūlyasyādher mūlyam | sākṣāt pratibhūr apy atra vṛddhiṃ dātuṃ nārhati | khādakenāpy atra "mūlyena toṣayed enam" it vacanān mūlyamātram eva deyam | evam avaśiṣṭapratibhuvām api smṛtyantareṣu deyadravyavidhayo draṣṭavyāḥ | pratyaye lekhye divyadarśane cākṛte sati "ṛṇaṃ dāpyāḥ pratibhuvaḥ" ityādidāpanavidhāyakasmṛtyantarād vā unneyāḥ, tulyanyāyād vā kalapanīyāḥ | tathā hi, ṛṇidravyārpaṇapratibhūr apratikurvati ṛṇike ṛṇadravyam (?) arpayet | abhayapratibhūr bhayopasthitau tatpratīkāram ācaret | pramāṇapratibhūḥ pramāṇākaraṇe vivādāspadaṃ dhanaṃ dadyāt | vivādapratibhūr apratikurvati vādini sādhitadhanaṃ daṇḍadhanaṃ ca dadyāt | dāsādyapahṛtaṃ punar alabdhaṃ cet viśvāsapratibhūr mūlyadvāreṇa dadyād ityādyās tatra tatra kalpanīyāḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ pratibhuvām asādhāraṇavidhiḥ**

**atha pratibhūputrādīnāṃ vidhayaḥ**

tatra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	darśanapratibhūr yatra mṛtaḥ prātyayiko 'pi vā |

	na tatputrā ṛṇaṃ dadyur dadyur dānāya yaḥ sthitaḥ ||

prātyayikaḥ pratyayapratibhūḥ, tasmin mṛte darśanapratibhuvi ca tayoḥ putrāḥ prātibhāvyāyātaṃ paitṛkam ṛṇaṃ na dadyuḥ | dānapratibhuvi tu mṛte tasya putrāḥ pūrvoktam ṛṇaṃ dadyur ity arthaḥ | yadā tu ṛṇaṃ jīvanaśālinaḥ pūrvoktāḥ pratibhuvo na dadyuḥ, mṛtasya dānapratibhuvaḥ putrāś ca tadā te dāpanīyā iti rājño vidhim āha sa eva |

	ādau tu vitathe dāpyāv itarasya sutā api |

apiśabdād dānapratibhūr api jīvanadaśāyāṃ visaṃvāde dāpya iti darśayati | darśitaṃ ca sākṣād eva bṛhaspatinā |

	ādyau tu vitathe dāpyau tatkālāveditaṃ dhanam |

	uttarau tu visaṃvāde tau vinā tatsutau tathā ||

ādyau darśanapratyayapratibhuvau | vitathe aham enaṃ darśayiṣyāmi sādhur eṣa ity evaṃvidhayoḥ pratibhūvākayayor mithyātve | uttarau dānarṇidravyārpaṇapratibhuvau | visaṃvāde śāṭhyādinā dhane vā jāta ity arthaḥ | etad uktaṃ bhavati: ṛṇaṃ vānyad vā dhanādikam ahaṃ tava dāsyāmīty evaṃ pratibhuvā yatrāṅgīkṛtaṃ tatra pratibhūr dāpyaḥ, tasyābhāve tatputro vā dāpyaḥ | anyatra tu pratibhūr eveti | evaṃ ca pramāṇapratibhuvāṃ tv evam anaṅgīkārāt pramāṇapratibhuva eva dāpyāḥ, na putrāḥ | vivādapratibhuvā tu sādhitadhanaṃ daṇḍadhanaṃ ca dāsyāmīty aṅgīkṛtatvād dānapratibhūvat sati saṃbhave sa eva dāpyo 'nyathā tu tatputra ity avagantavyam | ata eva vyāsaḥ |

	vipratyaye lekhyadivyadarsane cākṛte sati |

	ṛṇaṃ dāpyāḥ pratibhuvaḥ putraṃ teṣāṃ na dāpayet ||

	dānavādapratibhuvau dāpyau tatputrakau tadā || iti |

vipratyaye vitathe pratyaye pratyayapratibhūr dāpya ity arthaḥ | evam anyeṣām abhayagṛhītabandhopasthāpanādipratibhuvām aṅgīkārānaṅgīkaraprakāram ālocya pratyayapratibhūvad dānapratibhūvad vā dāpanavidhaya ūhyāḥ | yat punar manunā "prātibhāvyaṃ vṛthādānam" ityādy abhidhāya "na putro dātum arhati" ity uktam, tat darśanapratibhūviṣayaṃ yato 'nantaram āha sa eva |

	darśanaprātibhāvye tu vidhiḥ syāt pūrvacoditaḥ | iti |

pūrvaśloke coditaḥ "prātibhāvyaṃ na putro dātum arhati" iti darsanaprātibhāvyaviṣaye jñeya ity arthaḥ | tatra viṣaye kvacit tasyāpavādam āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	gṛhītvā bandhakaṃ yas tu darśanapratibhūḥ sthitaḥ |

	vibhāvya vādinā tatra dāpyaḥ syāt tatsutopṛyaṇam (?) ||

svavisrambhārtham adhamarṇād arthaṃ gṛhītvā yo darsanapratibhūtvam āpadya sthitaḥ saṃsthito mṛta iti yāvat | tasya suto vādinā dhaninā ṛṇikārthadhāraṇanibandhanaṃ prātibhāvyam iti  vibhāvya yācyamānaḥ prātibhāvyāgatam ṛṇaṃ dāpya ity arthaḥ | yady api tatsutagrahaṇād darsanapratibhūsutaviṣayo 'yam apavādaḥ, na pramāṇapratibhūsutaviṣaya iti pratibhāti, tathāpi pratibhūsutadāpane pramītasya pitur adhamarṇād arthagrahaṇapūrvakaṃ prātibhāvyam atra vivakṣitaṃ nimittam, na tu darsanapratibhūsutatvam apīty asmād eva vacanād apavādo 'nyatrāpi vivakṣitanittamasadbhāve smṛta eveti mantavyam | vivakṣitanimittadyotanārtham eva ca manunā praśnottaratvenāpavādo darśitaḥ |

	adātari punar dātā vijñātaprakṛtāv ṛṇam |

	paścāt pratibhuvi prete parīpset kena hetunā ||

	nirādiṣṭadhanaś cet tu pratibhūḥ syād alaṃdhanaḥ |

	svadhanād eva tad dadyān nirādiṣṭa iti sthitiḥ || iti |

atra padārthāḥ prathamam ucyante: adātari darśayitari, dātā dhanaprayoktā vijñātaprakṛtau prāyeṇāyaṃ kiṃcid gṛhītvā kasyacit pratibhūr bhavatīti vijñātasvabhāve ṛṇaṃ prātibhāvyāgatam ṛṇaṃ parīpsel labdhum icchet | vākyārthas tu: adātari vijñātaprakṛtau pratibhuvi prete paścāt tatputrād ṛṇaṃ dātā "na ta (?) tatputrā ṛṇaṃ dadyuḥ" iti śāstrāviruddhena kena hetunā parīpsed iti | uttaraślokavyākhyāpy evaṃ kriyate: nirādiṣṭaṃ samarpitaṃ bandhatvena dhanaṃ yasyāsau nirādiṣṭadhanaḥ | alaṃ paryāptaṃ bandhatvenopāttaṃ dhanaṃ yasyāsāv alaṃdhanaḥ | nirādiṣṭaśabdena samastena nirādiṣṭadhanasya darśanapratibhuvaḥ putro lakṣyate | sthitiḥ śāstramaryādā | vākyārthas tu: nirādiṣṭadhano 'laṃdhano darśanapratibhūr mṛtaś cet syān nirādiṣṭaḥ svadhanād eva tad ṛṇaṃ dadyād iti sthitir iti | anena nirādiṣṭadhanatvenaiva hetunā parīpsed ity uttaram arthād uktam | asyaiva vacanasyādhyāhāralakṣaṇāśrayaṇaṃ vihārārthāntaram ucyate: nirādiṣṭadhanaḥ pratibhūr alaṃdhanaś cet syāt sa eva nirādiṣṭaḥ svadhanād eva dadyād iti | anirādiṣṭadhanavad adhamarṇaṃ darśayan na mucyate nirādiṣṭadhanaḥ, kiṃ tu dānapratibhūvad dadyād iti tātparyārthaḥ | etac cārthāntaraṃ devasvāminoktam | pratibhūsutadevaviṣaye tu viśeṣaṃ āha vyāsaḥ |

	ṛṇaṃ paitāmahaṃ pautraḥ prātibhāvāgataṃ sutaḥ |

	samaṃ dadyāt tatsutau tu na dāpyāv iti niscayaḥ ||

sutaḥ pratibhūsutaḥ | samaṃ mūlamātram | tatsutau pautrapratibhūsutayoḥ sutau | yat tu manunoktam,

	dānapratibhuvi prete dāyādān api dāpayet |

iti, tatra dāyādaśabdaḥ suteṣv eva vyavatiṣṭhate, anyathā sapiṇḍamātrābhidhāne "tatsutau tu na dāpyav iti niścayaḥ" it pūrvoktavacanavirodhāpatteḥ,

	prātibhāvyāgataṃ pautrair dātavyaṃ na kvacid bhavet |

iti bṛhaspativacanavirodhāpatteś ca | anekapratibhūdeyaviṣaye tu viśeṣam āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	bahavaḥ syur yadi svāṃśaiḥ dadyuḥ pratibhuvo dhanam |

	ekacchāyāśriteṣv eṣu dhanikasya yathāruci ||

ekasyādhamarṇasya chāyāṃ sakaladhanadāyakatvarūpasādṛśyaṃ pratyekaṃ vikalpenāśritāḥ ekacchāyāśritāḥ, teṣu yaṃ yācate dhanikaḥ sa sarvaṃ dadyād ity arthaḥ | dhanikaruṣyaviśeṣe tu "samaṃ syād śrutatvāt" iti nyāyenātrāpi svāṃśair dadyuḥ | ekacchāyāśritapratibhūsute tu viśeṣam āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	ekacchāyāśrite sarvaṃ dadyāt tu proṣite sutaḥ |

	mṛte pitari pitraṃśaṃ pararṇaṃ na bṛhaspatiḥ ||

sarvaṃ pararṇam api, na pitraṃśamātram ity arthaḥ | na tu sarvaṃ savṛddhikam iti vyākhyeyam,

	putreṇāpi samaṃ deyam ṛṇaṃ sarvaṃ tu paitṛkam |

iti bṛhaspatismaraṇāt | samaṃ mūlamātraṛṇaṃ prātibhāvyāgataṃ paitṛkam | etac ca dhanikecchāyām "proṣitasya putro mahyaṃ dadyāt" ity evaṃvidhāyāṃ satyāṃ sarvadānavidhānaṃ draṣṭavyam | asatyāṃ tu dhanikecchāyām "pitraṃśam apravṛddhikaṃ proṣitaputro dadyāt" it cāvagantavyam | pararṇaṃ parasya pitṛvyatiriktasya ekachāyāsritasya ṛṇāṃśaṃ pitari mṛte tatsutaḥ satyām api dhanikecchāyāṃ na dātum arhati, kiṃ tu pitraṃśam avṛddhikam eveti bṛhaspatir brūta ity arthaḥ | pratibhūdauṣṭyaviṣaye tv āha pitāmahaḥ |

	yo yasya pratibhūr bhūtvā mithyā caiva tu gacchati |

	dhanikasya dhanaṃ dāpyo rājñā daṇḍaṃ ca tatsamam ||

	kuryāc cet pratibhūr vādam ṛṇikārthe 'rthinā saha |

	sopasargas tadā daṇḍyo vivādād dviguṇaṃ dhanam || iti |

sopasargo viplavakārī ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ pratibhūputrādīnāṃ vidhayaḥ **

**atha pratibhvādidattapratikriyāvidhayaḥ**

tatra kātyāyanaḥ |

	yasyārthe yena yad dattaṃ vivāde (dā) 'bhyarthitena tu |

	sākṣibhir bhāvitenaiva pratibhūs tam avāpnuyāt ||

yasya prātibhāvyaṃ kārayituḥ kṛte yena pratibhuvā dhanikādibhir yācitena sākṣyādibhiś cānyārtham arpitartho(?) 'yam ity avadhṛtena yat svakīyaṃ suvarṇapasudhānyavastrādikaṃ dhanikādibhyo dattaṃ tatsamam evārthaṃ prātibhāvyakārayituḥ sakāśāt sa samāpnuyād ity arthaḥ | yat tu yājñavalkyenoktam,

	pratibhūr dāpito yatra prakāśaṃ dhanine dhanam |

	dviguṇaṃ pratidātavyam ṛṇikais tasya tad bhavet ||

iti, tad dhanikapīḍitapratibhūviṣayam (?) | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	yaṃ cārthaṃ pratibhūr dadyād dhanikenopapīḍitaḥ |

	ṛṇikaṃ taṃ pratibhuve dviguṇaṃ pratidāpayet ||

etad api pratidānavilambaviṣayam | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	prātibhāvyaṃ tu yo dadyāt pīḍitaḥ pratibhāvitaḥ |

	tripakṣāt parataḥ so 'rthaṃ dviguṇaṃ labdhum arhati ||

pratibhāvitaḥ pratibhūtvena kāritaḥ | tripakṣāt prāk tu samam ev labdhum arhatīty artho 'pi gamyate | yady api prāyeṇa prītyaiva pratibhūr bhavati, na ca prītidattae vṛddhir asti na ca dvaiguṇayam, etāvati kāle dharmyaṃ bhavitum arhati | tathāpi vacanabalāt sarvaṃ bhaviṣyati | na hi vacanasyātibhāro 'stīty avagantavyam | evam ukto dviguṇalābho hiraṇyaviṣayaḥ | paśvādau tu,

	saṃtatiḥ strīpaśuṣv eva dhānyaṃ triguṇam eva ca |

	vastraṃ caturguṇam proktaṃ rasaś cāṣṭaguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

iti yājñavalkyena dvaiguṇyāpavādasmaraṇāt | 

	uktā pañcaguṇā śāke bījekṣau ṣaḍguṇā smṛtā |

ityāder upalakṣaṇārtham idam uktaṃ tadbhāṣyakṛdbhiḥ, tena śākādau pañcaguṇādi deyam | evam uktānekavidhasavṛddhikadānam ṛṇikājñayā dattaviṣayam, anyatra tu dattasamam (?) eva deyam | tathā cocathyaḥ (?) |

	pratibhvā pratidattaṃ yad apṛṣṭe ṛṇike dhanam |

	dviguṇaṃ na pratibhuve pradeyam ṛṇikena tat ||

praṣṭuṃyogyadeśakālastharṇikādiviṣayam etat | tenānyatrāpṛṣṭe 'pi ṛṇike nāyaṃ pratiṣedhaḥ, kiṃ tu pṛṣṭatulyataiva | lagnakālagnako pakṣayapratikriyāṃ sādhāraṇīm api lagnakopakṣayapratikriyāvidhiprasaṅgād atraivāha nāradaḥ |

	yasya doṣeṇa yat kiṃcid vinaśyeta hriyeta vā |

	voḍhavyaṃ tad bhavet tena yac cājñānavināśitam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ pratibhvādidattapratikriyāvidhayaḥ pratibhūprakaraṇam samāptam**

**atha vṛddhiviṣayāṇi kānicid vacanāni likhyante**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ|

	vṛddhiś caturvidhā proktā pañcadhānyaiḥ prakīrtitā |

	ṣaḍvidhāsmin samākhyātā tattvatas tān nibodhata ||

asmin asmadīye dharmaśāstre | kathaṃ ṣaḍvidhatvam ity apekṣite sa evāha |

	kāyikā kālikā caiva cakravṛddhir athāparā |

	kāritātha śikhāvṛddhir bhogalābhas tathaiva ca ||

kiṃ punaḥ kāyikādīnāṃ svarūpam ity apekṣite 'py āha sa eva |

	kāyikā karmasaṃyuktā māsagrāhyā tu kālikā |

	vṛddher vṛddhiś cakravṛddhiḥ kāritā ṛṇinā kṛtā ||

	pratyahaṃ gṛhyate yā tu śikhāvṛddhis tu sā smṛtā |

	gṛhāttoṣaś (?) sadaḥ kṣetrāt bhogalābhaḥ prakīrtitaḥ || iti |

godhoṭakāder ādhīkṛtasya dohanavāhanādikaḥ kāyiko vyāpāra eva yatra vṛddhitvena kalpitaḥ sā kāyikety arthaḥ | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

	dohyavāhyakriyāyuktā kāyikā samudāhṛtā | iti |

māsagrāhyā pratimasaṃ labhyā vṛddhiḥ kālikā,

	pratimāsaṃ sravantī yā sā vṛddhiḥ kālikeritā (?) ||

iti nāradasmaraṇāt | vṛddher api pratimāsaṃ mūlabhāvena punar vṛddhiś cakravṛddhiḥ | ṛṇikecchayā kṛtā vṛddhiḥ kāritā | "icchākṛtā kāritā syāt" iti smṛtyantare 'bhidhānāt | tena chāndaso 'yaṃ svārtha eva kāriteti ṇicpratyayo draṣṭavyaḥ | parapreraṇayā tu karitā vṛddhri niṣiddhaiva | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	ṛṇikena tu yā vṛddhir adhikā samprakalpitā |

	āpatkālakṛtā nityaṃ dātavyā kāritā tu sā ||

	anyathā kāritā vṛddhir na dātavyā kathaṃcana | iti |

śāstroktād adhikā dhanadātṛpratilobhanārthaṃ svayaṃ kalpitā kāritākhyā dātavyā, na punar anevaṃvidhā dhanikena kāritā dātavyety arthaḥ | pratidinaṃ labhyā tu śikhāsādṛśyāc chikhāvṛddhir iti vyapadiśyate | kiṃ punaḥ śikhāsādṛśyaṃ vṛddher ity apekṣite bṛhaspatir evāha |

	śikheva vardhate nityaṃ śiraḥ chedān nivartate |

	mūle datte tathaiveṣā śikhāvṛddhis tataḥ smṛtā ||

pratyahaṃ gṛhyata iti saṃpratipannadinasaṃkhyāviśiṣṭavṛddhigrahaṇopalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	ekāntenaiva vṛddhiṃ tu śodhayed yatra carṇikam |

	pratikālaṃ dadāty eva śikhāviṛddhis tu sā smṛtā ||

gṛhāt toṣa (?) ityāder ayam arthaḥ: nivāsanibandhanaḥ gṛhasakāśāt saṃtoṣaḥ | kṣetrāt saṃbhūtaṃ dhānyādiphalaṃ ca bhogalābhākhyo vṛddhibheda iti | gṛhakṣetragrahaṇaṃ sthāvarātmakabhogyādher apy upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	ādhibhogas tv aśeṣo yo vṛddhiṃ tu parikalpitaḥ |

	prayogo yatra caivaṃ syād ādhibhogaḥ sa ucyate ||

aśeṣaḥ sthāvaramātrasaṃbandhīty arthaḥ |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ vṛddhibhedāḥ**

**atha vṛddhiparimāṇaniyamāḥ**

tatra manuḥ |

	aśītibhāgaṃ gṛhṇīyān māsād vārdhuṣikaḥ śate | iti |

niṣkaśate prayukte māsasya sapādaniṣkaparimitāṃ vṛddhiṃ vārdhuṣiko (?) vṛddhyarthaṃ dhanaprayoktā gṛhṇīyād ity arthaḥ | etat sabandhakaviṣayam,

	aśītibhāgo vṛddhiḥ syān māsi māsi sabandhake |

iti, yājñavlkyasmaraṇāt | ādhigrahaṇapūrvake dhanaprayoge yāvad dhanaṃ prayuktaṃ tasyāśītitamo bhāgaḥ pratimāsaṃ vṛddhiḥ syād ity arthaḥ | yat tu manunā vikalpatvenoktam "dvikaṃ śataṃ vā gṛhṇīyāt" iti, tad vyavasthitavikalpatvenoktam | yata āha vyāsaḥ |

	sabandhe bhāga āśītaḥ ṣāṣṭo bhāgaḥ salagnake |

	nirādhāne dvikasataṃ māsalābha udāhṛtaḥ ||

aśītiṣaṣṭibhāgāv ādhipratibhūsahitayoḥ prayogayoḥ pratimasaṃ yathākrameṇa grāhyau, etadrahite tu prayoge pañcāśadbhāgaḥ pratimāsaṃ grāhya ity arthaḥ | dve dīyate vṛddhir asmin śata iti dvikaśatam | anena vacobhaṅgyā pañcāśadbhāga uktaḥ | brāhmaṇādhamarṇa evāyaṃ dvikaṃ śatam iti niyamaḥ, kṣatriyādyadhamarṇe anyathā niyamaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	dvikaṃ trikaṃ catuṣkaṃ ca pañcakaṃ ca satam eva vā |

	māsasya vṛddhiṃ gṛhṇīyād varṇānām anupūrvaśaḥ ||

abandhakālagnakaprayogaviṣayam etat, dvikaśatasthāne varṇāntare trikaśatādividhānāt | ata eva yājñavalkyaḥ |

	varṇakramāc chataṃ dvitricatuḥpañxakam anyathā | iti |

anyathā bandhakalagnakarāhitya ity arthaḥ | tathādhamarṇaviśeṣe pratimāsaṃ vṛddheḥ parimāṇāntaraṃ dvikaśatādisthāne sa evāha |

	kāntāragās tu daśakaṃ sāmudrā viṃśakaṃ śatam | iti |

vṛddhyā dhanaṃ gṛhītvā ye durgavartmagantāraḥ te pratimāsaṃ daśakaṃ śataṃ dadyuḥ | ye tu samudragantāraḥ(?) te 'pi viṃśakaṃ śataṃ dadyur ity arthaḥ | evamuktāśītibhāgādiśāstrīyavṛddhiparimāṇena saha vikalpam adhamarṇābhyupagatavṛddhiparimāṇasyāha sa eva |

	dadyur vā svakṛtāṃ vṛddhiṃ sarve sarvāsu jātiṣu | iti |

sarve brāhmaṇādayo 'dharmarṇāh svābhyupagatāṃ vṛddhiṃ sarvāsu jātiṣūttamarṇabhūtāsu dadyur vety arthaḥ | ayaṃ ca vikalpaḥ kāritāyāhm eva vṛddhau, anyatra tu śāstrataḥ parimāṇaniyamavidhir ity ayaṃ svakṛtapakṣa eva | paśvādidravyasya tu vṛddhyarthaṃ prayuktasya tadīyā santatir eva vṛddhir ity āha sa eva "santatis tu paśustrīṇām" iti | striyo dāsyaḥ | santatyabhāve tu prayuktasya paśvādeḥ puṣṭir avināśo vā lābha iti ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ vṛddhiparimāṇaniyamāḥ**

**athākṛtavṛddhividhayaḥ**

tatra viṣṇuḥ |

	yo gṛhītvā ṛṇaṃ pūrvaṃ śvo dāsyāmīti sāmakam |

	na dadyāl lobhataḥ paścāt tad adhnā vṛddhim āpnuyāt ||

samam eva sāmakam avṛddhikam iti yāvat | etad uktaṃ bhavati: pratidānakāvāvadhim aṅgīkṛtya gṛhītam avṛddhikam api ṛṇam avadher anantarakālād ārabhya vardata eveti | vayasyāder upabhogādyartham arpitaviṣaye tv āha nāradaḥ |

	na vṛddhiḥ prītidattānāṃ syād anākāritā kvacit |

	anākāritam apy ūrdhvaṃ vatsarārdhād vivardhate ||

anākāritā akṛtā | prītidattānāṃ pratiyācanapratidānadinanirdeśaśūnyānām iti śeṣaḥ | anākāritam apītyāder ayam arthaḥ: pratidānadinanirdeśe tu taddinam ārabhya saṣaṇmāsād ūrdhvaṃ vardhate prītidattam apīti | gṛhītapaṇyamūlyānarpaṇaviṣaye tu kātyāyanaḥ |

	paṇyaṃ gṛhītvā yo mūlyam adatvaiva disaṃ vrajet |

	ṛtutrayasyopariṣṭāt tad dhanaṃ vṛddhim āpnuyāt ||

apratiyācitaviṣayam etat | kim atra vṛddheḥ parimāṇam | ucyate: adharmarṇādyaṅgīkārāyattaparimāṇasyātrāsaṃbhavād anyasya ca puruṣabuddhikalpitasya śāstrabāhyasyāyuktatvāc chāstroktam eva parimāṇaṃ grāhyam, tac ca pūrvasmin prakaraṇe darśitam "aśītibhāgam" ityādinā | ata eva viṣṇunā "vṛddhiṃ dadyād akṛtām api saṃvatsarātikrame yathābhihitam" ity uktam | yathābhihitaṃ dharmaśāstra iti śeṣaḥ | na ca yathā pratyarthinā madhyasthenārthinā vābhihitā tathā dadyād iti yathābhihitam iti vacanārthaḥ kasmān na syād iti vācyam, yat āha manuḥ |

	kṛtānusārād adhikā vyatiriktā na sidhyati |

	kusīdapatham āhus taṃ pañcakaṃ śatam arhati || iti |

kusīdapatham āhur ity ucchāstravṛddhiṃ nindayati | śāstrakṛtavṛddhyanusāro hi yo vṛddhigrahaṇe laukikānāṃ samayācāraḥ sa kṛtānusāraḥ, tasmād adhikā vṛddhir uttamarṇāder akṛtavṛddhau na sidhyati, yataḥ sā vyatiriktā dharmaśāstrabāhyety arthaḥ | ata eva kusīdapatham āhuḥ tan na dharmapatham iti nindāpy upapannā | "pañcakaṃ śatam arhati" ity asya viṣayaviśeṣo vakṣyate | yatu vaiṣṇavavacane saṃvatsarātikrama ity uktam, tad yācitakaviṣayam | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	yo yācitakam ādāya tam adatvā diśaṃ vrajet |

	ūrdhvaṃ saṃvatsarāt tasya tad dhanaṃ vṛddhim āpnuyāt || iti |

kṛtoddhāraṃ yācitakam ādāyety arthaḥ | pravāsābhāve tu pratiyāvanakālād ārabhya yācitakasya vṛddhim āha sa eva |

	svadeśe 'pi sthito yas tu na dadyād yācitaṃ kvacit |

	tat tato 'kāritāṃ vṛddhim anicchantaṃ ca dāpayet ||

na dadyād yācitam iti prakṛtena saṃbandhaḥ | tataḥ pratiyācanakālād ārabhyety arthaḥ | prītidatte ca pratimācite yācanakālād ārabhya vṛddhiviśeṣaniyamārtham eva vacanāntaram ārabdhaṃ tenaiva |

	prītidattaṃ na vardheta yāvan na pratiyācitam |

	yācyamānam adattaṃ ced vardhate pañcakaṃ śatam ||

nikṣepādāv api yācyayānam (?) adattam eva vardhate ity āha sa eva |

	nikṣepaṃ vṛddhiśeṣaṃ ca krayaṃ vikrayam eva ca |

	yācyamānam adattaṃ ced vardhate pañcakaṃ śatam ||

krayavikrayaśabdena paṇyamūlyaṃ lakṣyate | yat tu pūrvapradarśite mānave vacane "pañcakaṃ śatam arhati" iti sāmānyenoktaṃ tatpratiyācitaprītidattādiviṣayaṃ mantavyam | 

**iti smṛticandrikāyām akṛtavṛddhividhayaḥ**

**atha akṛtavṛddhyapavādaḥ** 

tatra nāradaḥ |

	paṇyamūlyaṃ bhṛtir nyāso daṇḍo yaś ca prakalpitaḥ |

	vṛthādānākṣikapaṇā vardhante nāvivakṣitāḥ ||

paṇyasya vastrāder mūlyaṃ paṇyamūlyam | vṛthādānaṃ nartakayādibhyaḥ pratiśrutam | ākṣikapaṇo dyūtadravyam | ukteṣu satsu akṛtavṛddhir nāstīty arthaḥ | atra paṇyamūlyasya vṛddhiḥ pravāsapratiyācanābhāve | nyāsasya tv avṛddhiḥ pratiyācanābhāve yathāsthitasyaiva | ato na pūrvaprakaraṇoktavacanavirodhāpattiḥ | saṃvarto 'pi |

	na vṛddhiḥ strīdhane lābhe nikṣepe ca yathāsthite |

	saṃdigdhe prātibhāvye ca yadi na syāt svayaṃkṛtā ||

lābhe na vṛddhiḥ | yathāsthite iti vadan nikṣepe vyaktyanyatvādikaraṇe vṛddhiḥ bhavatīti darśayati | saṃdigdhe dhane kenacit saṃdehena dātum anucitatvena sthite | prātibhāvye ṛṇidravyārpaṇādau sākṣāt pratibhūviṣaye 'pi | pratiyācanadeḥ parastād api na vṛddhiḥ | "yadi na syāt svayaṃkṛtā" iti vadan strīdhanādāv api kṛtā ced vṛddhiḥ deyaiveti darsayati | kātyāyano 'pi |

	carmasasyāsavadyūtapaṇyamūlye ca sarvadā |

	strīśulke ca na vṛddhiḥ syāt prātibhāvyāgateṣu ca ||

sarvadeti vadan pratiyācanādeḥ parastād api nāsty akṛtā vṛddhir iti darsayati | paṇyamūlye vacanāntarāvirodhaḥ pūrvavad avaseyaḥ | yady api sarveti sarvaśeṣaḥ pratibhāti, tathāpy avirodhāya paṇyamūlyaśeṣatā mantavyā | vyāso 'pi |

	prātibhāvyām bhuktabandham gṛhītaṃ ca ditsavaḥ |

	na vardhate prapannasya damaḥ śulkaṃ praiśrutam ||

bhuktabandhagrahaṇam upabhuktagopyādhau (?) nikṣepopabhoga iva vṛddhir mā bhūd ity evam artham | arthas tu gautamena spaṣṭīkṛtaḥ: "bhuktādhir na vardheta vastrālaṅkārādiḥ" iti | agṛhītaṃ ca ditsava iti kṛtavṛddhyapavādo 'pi vṛddhyabhāvakathanaprasaṅgād akṛtavṛddhyapavādaiḥ sahoktaḥ | tasyārtho yājñavalkyena spaṣṭīkṛtaḥ |

	dīyamānaṃ na gṛhṇāti prayuktaṃ yaḥ svakaṃ dhanam |

	madhyasthasthāpitaṃ tat tu vardhate na tataḥ param ||

na gṛhṇāti rakṣaṇākṣamatvavṛddhlolupatvādihetuneti śeṣaḥ | madhyasthasthāpanābhāve sthāpitasyāpi yācyamānasyāprāptau pūrvavad vardhata eva, pratidānodyamasya kṛtatvāsaṃbhavāt ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām akṛtavṛddhyapavādaḥ **

**atha vṛddhigrahaṇapratiṣedhāḥ**

tatra manuḥ |

	nātisāmvatsarīṃ vṛddhiṃ na cādṛṣṭāṃ vinirharet |

	cakravṛddhiṃ kālavṛddhiṃ kāritā kāyikā ca yā ||

atrādyapādārthaṃ <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecid</span> evam āhuḥ: ā dvaiguṇyād vṛddhigrahaṇavidhānād vatsarād ūrdhvam api vṛddhigrahaṇe doṣābhāvād abhyudayārthī cet saṃvatsarād ūrdhvaṃ yā vṛddhiḥ tāṃ na vinirharet na gṛhṇīyād iti | ayaṃ tāvad artho grāhyaḥ, virodhābhāvāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye</span> tu saṃvatsarādhikāṃ vṛddhiṃ na gṛhṇīyāt, yad vṛddhimahattvena tāvad eva dvaiguṇyaṃ bhaved ity adhyāhṛtyārtham āhuḥ, te mandāḥ: "kusīdavṛddhir dvaiguṇān nātyeti"ity anena phalato gatārthatvāpatteḥ, vatsaramātreṇa dvaiguṇṇā(?)pādakavṛddhimahattvasya niṣiddhasyānupapatteś ca | apare punar evaṃ vyācakṣate: yatrādhamarṇe pratimāsaṃ pañcakaṃ śataṃ gṛhṇīyād iti yā viṛddhiḥ prāg uktā sā brāhmaṇādyadhamarṇake kathaṃcid aṅgīkāravaśāt gṛhyamāṇa saṃvatsaraṃ yāvad grahītavyā na tataḥ param iti | ayam apy artho 'stu, prāktanārthavad bahudoṣābhāvāt | "na cādṛṣṭāṃ vinirharet" ity asyayam arthaḥ: dharmaśāstreṣv adṛṣṭāṃ ca ṣaṭkaṃ satam ity evaṃbhūtāṃ svabuddhikalpitāṃ vṛddhiṃ na gṛhṇīyād iti |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span>

	kṛānusārād adhikā vyatiriktā na sidhyati |
