ity anena gatārtham idaṃ vākyam evaṃvyākhyāyamāne syāt | astu vyartho 'nuvādaḥ gatyantarābhāvād iti <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecid</span> ācakṣate | dārḍhyārtham uktasyaiva punar abhidhānam ity <span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye</span> manyante | vastutas tu, anena niṣedhe kṛēte 'py akṛtavṛddhau vṛddhisaṃpratipattyabhāvāt śāstrokaiva vṛddhiḥ sidhyati, nānyā gaṃpratipattimātralabhyā vṛddhir it kathanārthaṃ tadvacanam ity agatārthataiva | "na vinirharet" iti padadvayam uttarārdhapadair anuṣaṅgāt saṃbadhyate | tataś cāyam arthaḥ: yā cakravṛddhyādibhedena caturvidhā vṛddhiḥ tām na gṛhṇīyād iti | etad uktaṃ bhavati: cakravṛddhyādayaḥ svarasato na grāhyā iti |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanv</span> aśītibhāgādivṛddhir api pratimāsaṃ grāhyā  kālikā bhavati, sā ca svarasato grāhyā, tathānatibhūriparimāṇā kāritāpi svarasato grāhyaiva | tathā kāyikāpy atipīḍārahitā | tena tāsāṃ kathaṃ pratiṣedhaḥ |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | kena voktaṃ tāsāṃ pratiṣedha iti | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kāsāṃ</span> tarhi pratiṣedhaḥ |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | yathā,

	pañacamāṣās tu viṃśatyā evaṃ dharmo na hīyate |

iti vāsiṣṭhavacanavihitā vṛddhiḥ, "vasiṣṭhavihitāṃ vṛddhim" iti mānavavacanāntare pratiṣdhyate | evaṃ "kusīdavṛddhir dharmyā viṃśateḥ pañcamāṣikī māsam" iti gautamena vihitā kālikātra pratiṣidhyate, kāyikāpy atipīḍāvatī tena na kaścid doṣaḥ | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> gautamoktā kālikā dharmyatvena tena vihitā kathaṃ pratiṣiḍhyate | yathā "evaṃ dharmo na hīyate" iti dharmyatvenāpi vasiṣṭhavihitā pratiṣiddhā tathaiva pratiṣidhyate | atyarthādhikaparimāṇatvenādharmyatvāt | adharmyatvaṃ coktaṃ manunā "vittavivardhinīm" iti vadatā | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kathaṃ</span> tarhi vasiṣṭhagautamayoḥ dharmyatvenābhidhānam |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">pañcakaśatavac</span> chūdrādhamarṇaviṣayatveneti brūmaḥ | evaṃ ca śūdretarādhamarṇaviṣayatve adharmyatvāt tatraiva kathaṃcid aṅgīkāravaśāt prāptā manunā pratiṣiddheti mantavyam |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecit</span> tu traivarṇikeṣv api dharmyatvam āpādayituṃ gautamādivacanam evaṃ vyācakṣate,

		māṣo viṃśatitamo bhāgaḥ paṇasya parikīrtitaḥ |

iti smṛtyukto māxaḥ kārṣāpaṇasya viṃśatitamo bhāgaḥ pañcamāṣikīty atra parigṛhyate | tathā ca sati kārṣāpaṇaviṃśateḥ prayuktā yā pañcamāṣikī vṛddhir aśītibhāgavṛddher īṣadadhiketi kutastyā vṛddher adharmyateti vyākhyādvayam apy ayuktam | vasiṣṭhavacane tāvad ubhayathā vyākhyāne 'pi "vasiṣṭhavihitām" ityādimanuvacanavirodho durvāraḥ | "dharmyatve vittavardhinīm utsṛjet" ity asyāghaṭanāt | gautamavacane tu "evaṃ ṣoṣasamāsair dviguṇā bhavatīti" iti svavākhyaśeṣavirodho duṣpariharaḥ (?) | tathā hi prathamavyākhyātṝṇāṃ vyākhyāne ṣoḍasamasaiḥ kārṣāpaṇacatuṣkaṃ bhavati | dvitīyavyākhyātṝṇāṃ tu suvarṇapañcakaṃ bhavati, tasmād vyākhyādvayam apy asaṃbaddham | matpakṣe punar na vākyaśeṣavirodhaḥ, vyāvahārikaniṣkaviṃśateḥ prasiddhamāṣapañcakavṛddhau ṣoḍaśamāsaiḥ dvaiguṇyasiddheḥ | kiṃ tu dharmyatvavirodhaḥ, sa cāsmābhiḥ parihṛtaḥ tena codyānavakāśaḥ | yata eva "svarasato na grāhyā" iti praiṣedho na punaḥ sarvathā na grāhyā iti, ata eva cakravṛddhau kathaṃcid aṅgīkṛtāyāṃ dhanikadoṣāt kvacit tasyālābham āha sa eva |

	cakravṛddhiṃ samārūḍho deśakālavyavasthitaḥ |

	atikrāman desakālau na tatphalam avāpnuyāt ||

atikrāman desakālau yadi paribhāṣitaṃ deśaṃ kālaṃ vātikrāmati na saṃnihitas tatra bhavati tataḥ svadoṣān na tatphalam avāpnuyāt na tāṃ vṛddhiṃ labhate ity arthaḥ | phalapratiṣedhān mūlaṃ labhate, yathoktapratiṣedhād anyāṃ vṛddhiṃ labheteti gamyate | anye 'pi "brāhmaṇasya na vārdhuṣam" ityādyā vṛddhigrahaṇapratiṣedhā nāradādyuktāḥ santi | te tv āhnikamadhya evāpadvṛttiprakaraṇe pradarśitā itīhāsmābhir (?) na pradarśitāḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ vṛddhigrahaṇapratiṣedhāḥ**

**atha vṛddhyuparamāvadhinirūpaṇam**

tatra nāradaḥ |

	ṛṇānāṃ sārvabhaumo 'yaṃ vidhir vṛddhikaraḥ smṛtaḥ |

	deśācārasthitis tv anyā yatrarṇam avatiṣṭhate ||

	āpadaṃ nistared vaiśyaḥ kāmaṃ vārdhuṣikarmaṇā ||

ityadinā smṛtaḥ ṛṇināṃ vṛddhikaro vidhiḥ sarvataḥ bhūmāv apīṣṭaḥ | yatra dvaiguṇyādāv ṛṇaṃ vardhamānam avatiṣṭhate tatra deśācārasthitiḥ deśāntarācārasthitito 'nyety arthaḥ | katham anyety apekṣite sa evāha |

	dviguṇaṃ triguṇaṃ caiva tathānyasmin caturguṇam |

	tathāṣṭaguṇam anyasmin deyaṃ deśe 'vatiṣṭhate ||

deyam ṛṇaṃ vardhamānaṃ kvacid dese dviguṇaṃ kvacit triguṇaṃ kvacic caturguṇaṃ vā yavad vardhata ity arthaḥ | evaṃ prayuktadravyabhedād api bhedavyavasthānam | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	hiraṇye dviguṇā vṛddhiḥ triguṇā vastrakupyayoḥ |

	dhānye caturguṇā proktā śadavāhyalaveṣu ca ||

	uktā pañcaguṇā śāke bījekṣau ṣaḍguṇā smṛtā |

	lavaṇasnehamadyeṣu vṛddhir aṣṭaguṇā matā ||

	guḍe madhuni caivoktā prayukte virakālike || iti |

kupyaṃ trapusīsakam | śadaḥ kṣetraphalam, tac ca gobalīvardanyāyād dhānyavyatiriktaṃ puṣpamūlaphalādikam | vāhyo balīvardaturagādiḥ | lavo meṣalomacamarīkeśādiḥ | sneho madhūcchiṣṭādiḥ | "prayukte cirakālike" it padadvayaṃ saptamyekavacanāntena hiraṇyādipadena sambadhyate | śadavāhyalaveṣu cirakālikeṣv ity adhyāharaḥ | evaṃ lavaṇasnehamadyeṣv ity atrāpy adhyāhāraḥ | dvaiguṇyahetubhūtaṃ pūrṇe dvaiguṇyam āpadyata ity āha sa eva |

	aśītibhāgo vardheta lābhe dviguṇatām iyāt |

	prayuktaṃ saptabhir varṣais tribhāgonair na saṃsayaḥ ||

lābhe pratimāsam aśītibhāgātmake saṃgṛhyamāṇe hiraṇyavad vajrādāv api dviguṇaiva vṛddhiḥ | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	vajraśuktipravālānāṃ hemnaś ca rajatasya ca |

	dviguṇā tv iṣyate vṛddhiḥ kṛtā kālānusariṇī ||

vajrasāhavaryāc chuktir iti muktāphalaṃ lakṣaṇayocyate | kātyāyanena tu "maṇimuktāpravālānām" iti vāvakaśabdenoktm, tad 'py atra lakṣaṇāniścaye kāraṇam | kupyavat tāmrādāv api triguṇaiva vṛddhiḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	tāmrāyaḥkāṃsyarītīnāṃ trapuṇaḥ sīsakasya ca |

	triguṇā tiṣṭhate vṛddhiḥ kālāc cirakṛtasya tu ||

bījavat kārpāse 'pi ṣaḍguṇaiva vṛddhiḥ | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

	śākakārpāsabījekṣau ṣaḍguṇā parikīrtitā | iti |

snehavad rasasyāpy aṣṭaguṇaiva vṛddhiḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	vadanty aṣṭaguṇān kāle madyasneharasāsavān | iti |

kātyāyano 'pi |

	tailānāṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ madyānām atha sarpiṣām |

	vṛddhir aṣṭaguṇā jñeyā guḍasya lavaṇasya ca ||

guḍavat tulāmeyasitādāv apy aṣṭaguṇaiva vṛddhiḥ | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ, "tulāghṛtam aṣṭaguṇam" iti | yat punas tenoktam: "triguṇaṃ dhānyaṃ dhānyenaiva rasā vyākhyātāḥ puṣpamūlaphalāni ca" iti, yat yatra deśe triguṇaṃ deyam avatiṣṭhate tadviṣayam, daridrādhamarṇaviṣayaṃ vā | yat tu manunoktam,

	dhānye śade lave vāhye nātikramati pañcatām |

iti, tat pratyarpaṇasamayasamṛddhādhamarṇaviṣayam | ye tu kambalādayo "hiraṇye dviguṇā vṛddhiḥ" ityadidharmaśāstreṣv anuktāḥ teṣāṃ dviguṇaiva vṛddhiḥ, "anuktānāṃ dviguṇā" iti viṣṇusmaraṇāt | cirakālam adānenādhamarṇopari vṛddhisthitāv eva prayuktadhanasya dvaiguṇyānatikramo nānyatrety arthaḥ | cirasthānābhāve tu prayuktaṃ vardhata eva, śataguṇatve 'pi "yāvat pratidānam" iti vyatirekād gamyate | cirasthāne 'pi skṛdāhitavṛddhāv eva dvaiguṇyānatikramo nānyatrety āha manuḥ |

	adhikaṃ grahīṣyāmīti yad alpaṃ dīyate tat kusīdam, tac ca dvaiguṇyasamabhivyāhārād atra hiraṇyam abhipretam | tasya vṛddhiḥ sakṛd āhitā | puruṣāntaram asaṃkrāmitā na vā mūlīkṛtā dvaiguṇyamūlena saha dviguṇatvaṃ natikrāmīty arthaḥ | atrāpi puruṣāntarasaṃkrāmitā punar vā mūlīkṛtā vṛddhir dvaiguṇyam astyetīti vyatirekād gamyate | yadā ṛṇikaḥ svayam eva ṛṇaṃ savṛddhikaṃ puruṣāntaradeyaṃ karoti, yadā vā mūlīkaroti, dhaniko vā dhanikānntare tv ādhiṃ kṛtvā svadhanaṃ gṛhṇāti, tadā taddinam ārabhya dvaiguṇyaparyantaṃ pratidānaparyantaṃ vā vardhate iti mantavyam | evaṃ traiguṇyādāv api sakṛd āhitā vṛddhir nātyeti, vastrādāv anyathā tv atyeti, nyāyasāmyāt | cirasthāna eva traiguṇyādau vṛddhyuparamo 'nyathā tu vardhata evety avagantavyam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ vṛddhyuparamāvadhinirūpaṇam**

**atha vṛddhyuparamāpavādāḥ** 

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	tṛṇakāṣṭheṣṭakāsūtrakiṇvacarmāsthivarmaṇām |

	hetipuṣpaphalānāṃ ca vṛddhis tu na nivartate ||

kiṇvaḥ surādravyopādānabhūto mūlaviśeṣaḥ | carma bāṇādinivārakaṃ phalakam | varva kavacam | hetiḥ āyudham | puṣpaphalayor vṛddhyanivṛttiḥ pratidānavelāyām atyantasamṛddhādhamarṇaviṣaye veditavyā, anyathā pūrvaprakaraṇoktatriguṇādipratipādakavacanavirodhāpatteḥ | viṣṇur api: "kiṇvakārpāsasūtracarmavarmāyudheṣṭakāṅgārāṇām akṣayā" iti | kārpāse tu pūrvaprakaraṇoktaṣaḍguṇābhidhāyakavacanāvirodhaḥ pūrvavad vijñeyaḥ | vasiṣṭho 'pi |

	dantacarmāsthiśṛṅgāṇāṃ mṛnmayānāṃ tathaiva ca |

	akṣayā vṛddhir eteṣāṃ puṣpamūlaphalasya ca ||

akṣayā mūlapratidānābhāve śataguṇāpi vardhata evety arthaḥ | bṛhaspatir api |

	śikhāvṛddhiṃ kāyikāṃ ca bhogalābhaṃ tathaiva ca |

	dhanī tāvat samādadyād yāvan mūlaṃ na śodhitam ||

śikhāvṛddhyādīnāṃ svarūpaṃ vṛddhibhedābhidhānaprakaraṇe darśitam | na śodhitaṃ na pratidattam ṛṇikenety arthaḥ | ata eva yājñavalkyaḥ |

	ādhis tu bhujyate tāvad yāvat tan na pradīyate | iti |

evam ukto vṛddhyuparamāpavādaḥ cirasthāne sakṛd āhitāyāṃ ca vṛddhau draṣṭavyaḥ, tatraivautsargikavṛddhyaparamaprāpteḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ vṛddhyuparamāpavādaḥ **

**samāptaṃ ca dhanadānādhamarṇaprakaraṇam**

**atha ṛṇapratidānavidhiḥ**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	yācamānāya dātavyam alpakālam ṛṇaṃ kṛtam |

	pūrṇe 'vadhau śāntalābham abhāve ca pituḥ sutaiḥ ||

alpakālam adīrthakālam iti yāvat | kṛtaṃ dīpotsavādau pratideyam ity evaṃ sāvadhitvena kṛtam | śāntalābham uparatavṛddhikam | etad uktaṃ bhavati: adīrghakālikam ṛṇaṃ yācñānantaraṃ dātavyam sāvadhikatvena kṛtaṃ tu pūrṇe 'vadhau | śāntalābhaṃ tu lābhaśāntyanantaram | ṛṇikābhāve ca tatsutair apy evam eva dātavyam iti | etac ca yācñādeḥ samanantaraṃ pratidānavidhānam, na tataḥ prāk pratidānavyudāsakam, sati saṃbhave śīghram apākaraṇīyatvād ṛṇasya | yas tu ṛṇaṃ nāpākaroti tasyādṛṣṭahāniḥ purāṇe darśitā |

	tapasvī cāgnihotrī ca ṛṇavān mriyate yadi |

	tapaś caivāgnotraṃ ca sarvaṃ tad dhanino bhavet ||

tenāvaśyam ṛṇam apākaraṇīyam ity arthaḥ | anenaivābhiprāyeṇa kātyāyanenāpy uktam |

	uddhārādikam ādāya svāmine na dadāti yaḥ|

	sa tasya dāso bhṛtyaḥ strī paśur vā jāyate ṛṇī (gṛhe) || iti |

uddhārādikaṃ pratideyatayaivāvasthitaṃ prītidattādikam | dāsabhṛtyayor bhedo vakṣyate | yat tu nāradenoktam,

	yācyamānaṃ na dadyād yad ṛṇaṃ vādhipratigraham |

	tad dravyaṃ vardhate tāvad yāvat koṭiśataṃ bhavet ||

	tataḥ koṭiśate pūrṇe veṣṭitas tena karmaṇā |

	aśvaḥ kharo vṛṣo dāso bhavej janmani janmani ||

iti, tatra yācyamānagrahaṇaṃ yācyamānasya ṛṇāder apratidāne kleśātiśayapratipādanārtham, na tu yācyamānasyaivāpratidāne kleśo nānyasyety abhidhānārtham it mantavyam | lekhyārūḍharṇapratidānānantaraṃ pratidātuḥ kartavyam āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	datvarṇaṃ pāṭayel lekhyaṃ śuddhyai vānyat tu kārayet | iti |

anṛṇatvaprakhyāpanārthaṃ pratidattapatraṃ vottamarṇād gṛhṇīyād iti dvitīyapādārthaḥ | ṛṇalekhyasya sthāpanāparijñānādinā pāṭhanāsaṃbhave tv ayaṃ pakṣa ity uktaṃ tadbhāṣye | asyāpi kathaṃcid asaṃbhave pakṣāntaraṃ nāradenoktam |

	lekhyaṃ dadyād ṛṇe śuddhe tadabhāve pratiśrayaḥ |

	dhanikarṇikayor evaṃ viśuddhiḥ syāt parasparam ||

pratiśravaḥ pratidattam ity asminn arthe sākṣyasiddhyai śrotriyādiśrāvaṇam | sākṣimad ṛṇapratidātāraṃ praty āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	sākṣimac ca bhaved yad vā tad dātavyaṃ sasākṣikam | iti |

sasākṣikam ṛṇaṃ pūrvasākṣisamakṣam eva dātavyam ity arthaḥ | pūrvasākṣiṇāṃ kathaṃcid asaṃbhave sākṣyantarasamakṣaṃ vā dātavyam, sasākxikam iti sāmānyonokteḥ pakṣadvayasamarthanārthatvāt | pūrvasākṣyantaraṃ tu pūrvasākṣibādhanakṣamatvāya saṃkhyāguṇādhikam eva kāryam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ ṛṇapratidānavidhiḥ**

**athāsamarthādhamarṇaviṣayāṇi **

tatra manuḥ |

	ṛṇaṃ dātum aśakto yaḥ kartum icchet punaḥkriyām |

	sa datvā nirjitāṃ vṛddhiṃ karaṇaṃ parivartayet ||

pramāṇamātravācako 'pi kriyāśabdo 'tra ṛṇaviṣayapramāṇaparatvāl lekhyasākṣiṣv evāvatiṣṭhate | evaṃ cāyam arthaḥ | pratidānakāle dhanāsaṃpattyādivaśāt savṛddhikamūladānāśakto yo 'dhamarṇaḥ ṛṇasya cirantanatvaparihārato dhanikasamādhānārthaṃ kriyāṃ lekhyādirūpāṃ punaḥ kartum icchet, sa niṣpannāṃ vṛddhiṃ datvā karaṇaṃ parivartayet, punar lekhyādikriyāṃ vartamānavatsarādicihnitāṃ kuryād iti | yadā tu nirjitāṃ vṛddhiṃ dātuṃ na śaknoti tadāpy āha sa eva |

	adarśayitvā tatraiva hiraṇyaṃ parivartayet |

	yāvatī saṃbhaved vṛddhis tāvatīṃ dātum arhati ||

asyārthaḥ: hiraṇyam adarśayitvā nirjitāṃ vṛddhim adatvā tatraiva pūrvakṛtakaraṇa (?) eva parivartayet nirjitāṃ vṛddhiṃ mūlatvenāropayet | tasyās tu vṛddhir na prayuktadhanavṛddhitulyā, kiṃ tu atyantālpaparimāṇenaivāropaṇīyeti | vṛddhāv apy aṃśamātradānaśaktena śakyāṃśaṃ datvā paścād aśakyāṃśāntaraṃ pūrvakaraṇa eva pūrvavad āropaṇīyam, nyāyasāmyāt | yas tu pratidānakāle savṛddhikaṃ mūlāṃśaṃ dātum aśaktaḥ taṃ praty āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	lekhyasya pṛṣṭe 'bhilikhet datvā datvarṇiko dhanam | iti |

kālāntare 'pi yāvan nikhilaṛṇāpākaraṇaṃ na bhavati tāvad evaṃ kṛtvānte pāṭanaṃ kuryād iti | atha vā yathāśakti stokaṃ datvā lekhyam upagatākhyam uttamarṇāt gṛhṇīyāt, uttamarṇena ca tad avaśyaṃ deyam,

	dhanī vopagataṃ dadyāt svahastaparicihnitam | 

iti pakṣāntaratayā tenaivānantaram abhidhānāt | etāvan mahyam anena dattam iti praveśapatraṃ vā dhanī pratidātre dadyād iti tasyārthaḥ | arthāntaraṃ ca tasyopariṣṭād dūre vakṣyāmaḥ | ayaṃ ca pakṣaḥ prācīnapakṣālābhe, tathā ca viṣṇuḥ: "asamagradāne lekhyāsaṃnidhāne cottamarṇaḥ svalikhitaṃ dadyāt" iti | ṛṇikāyeti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	gṛhītvopagataṃ dadyād ṛṇikāyodayaṃ dhanī | iti |

udayam ṛṇikenopārjitaṃ gṛhītvā dhanī ṛṇikāyopagataṃ dadyād ity anvayaḥ | udayaśabdenopārjitaṃ bruvan,

	brāhmaṇas tu parikṣīnaḥ śanair dāpyo yathodayam |

ity uktaviṣaye 'py ayaṃ pakṣovijñeya (?) iti darśayati | tena patrapṛṣṭhe lekhanapakṣo 'py anena vikalpitatvād asminn eva viṣaye vijñeyaḥ | evaṃ bhāgaśa ṛṇagrahaṇavidhibalād asminn eva viṣaye bhāgaśo grahaṇam, anyatra kṛtsnasyaivarṇasya grahaṇam iti mantavyam | tena yatra bhāgaśo grahaṇavidhiḥ tatraiva dattāṃśasya vṛddhinivṛttiḥ, anyatra tu yāvat kṛtsnaṃ na dadāti tāvad dīyamānam apy akṛtsnaṃ pratyākhyeyam, dattāṃśasyāpi vā vṛddhir grāhyaiva, tatrākṛtsnādānasya nikṣepamātratulyatvāt | na ca parikṣīṇaviṣaye stokaṃ dīyamānaṃ vṛddhibhaṅgabhayāt pratyākhyeyam, parikṣīṇasyānusanaṇīyatvāt, śanair dāpyatvavidhānāc ca | parikṣīṇaviṣaye 'py ādhimocanaṃ kṛtsnarṇāpākaraṇānantraṃ sakṛd eva, na punar dattāṃśānusāreṇa bahuśaḥ, yāvad ṛṇaṃ tava na dadāmi tāvad ayam ādhir iti bahumūlyasyāpy ānṛṇyaparyatam ādhīkaraṇāt | na cādhīkṛtadhanasvāmitveṇāpy asāv apariṣīṇa iti vācyam, pratibaddhadhanasvāmitvena niḥsvatulyatvāt | ādhibhoge 'pi na vṛddhinyāyena dattāṃśānusāreṇa bhoganivṛttiḥ | pratiniṣkam aśītibhāgādivṛddhyaṅgīkāro hi dhāryamāṇadhanānusāreṇa kṛtaḥ, tena pratidattāṃśasya dhāryamāṇasya vṛddhinivṛttir yuktā | ādhibhogas tu bogyādhitvasthityanuyāyī, na dhāryamāṇadhanānuyāyī, svalpadhanaprayogaviṣaye 'pi bahumūlyasyāpy ādhitvena sthitasyāśeṣasyaiva bhogyatvadarśanāt | na cāṅgīkāravaśāt tatra tathā bhogyatvadarśanam iti vācyam, kṛtsnaṃ bhogyaṃ tvayaitad ity evam anukte 'pi darśanāt | bhogyādhitvena sthiteś cāvimocanāt | vimocanaṃ ca kṛtsnarṇāpākaraṇānantaraṃ sakṛd evety uktam | tena parikṣīṇaviṣaye 'pi na dattāṃśānusāreṇādhyaṃśavaśāt tatra bhoganivṛttiḥ | tathā kāyikavṛddhyā gavādikam ādhīkṛtya niṣke ṛṇinā gṛhṇāti, na punar dattāṃśānusāreṇa ekastanaṃ dvistanaṃ tristanaṃ vādharmarṇāyārpayati | aśve 'py ādhibhūte dhanī svayam evāśvam āruhya kṛtsnaṃ mārgaṃ gacchati tathehāpīty alam atibahunā prapañcena |

	yas tu daurātmyād yācyayāno 'py upagataṃ na dadāti, tasya hānim āha sa eva |

	na dadyād yācyamānas tu śeṣahānim avāpnuyāt | iti |

śeṣo dāsyamānatayā sthito bhāgaḥ | śeṣasya svalpatve saty etad draṣṭavyam | tasyānalpatve tv adhikahānitvāt tāṃ nāpnuyāt, api tu gṛhītabhāgasya vṛddhidānanibandhanāṃ hānim | ata eva bṛhaspatiḥ |

	ṛṇaṃ dharmādito grāhyaṃ yas tūpari na lekhayet |

	na caivopagataṃ dadyāt tasya tad vṛddhim āpnuyāt || \
asyārthakathanārtham ādau viṣayatātparye nirūpyete |

	dhanī vopagataṃ dadyāt svahastaparicihnitam |

iti yājñavalkyavacanasya dvāv arthau: tatraitāvad dravyaṃ mama prāptam iti dhanī ṛṇalekhyapṛṣṭe svahastaparicihnitam upagataṃ likhed ity eko 'rthaḥ| arthāntaraṃ ca tasya prāg darśitam | tayor anyataram artham akurvato dhanikasya hānir anena vacanenocyate | akṣarārthas tu dharmopadhibalāt, kārāgṛhasaṃrodhanādyupāyair adhamarṇād akṛtsnam ṛṇam upādāya yo dhanī ṛṇalekhyasyopari mayaitāvat prāptam iti na likhet, na ca praveśapatraṃ dadyāt, tasya tad dinam ārabhya yāvallekhanaṃ lekhyadānaṃ vā na karoti tāvad adhamarṇād upāttaṃ dhanaṃ vṛddhim āpnuyāt adhamarṇāya vardhata iti yāvat | kayā vṛddhyety apekṣite nāradaḥ |

	yadi vā nopari likhed ṛṇinā codito 'pi san |

	dhanikasyaiva vardheta tathaiva ṛṇikasya tat ||

yathaiva tad dravyam ṛṇikasyopari sthitaṃ dhanikāya vardhate tathaivarṇikāya dhanikasyopari sthitaṃ vardhata ity arthaḥ |

**iti smṛticandrikāyām asamarthādhamarṇaviṣayāṇi**

**atha pratidānaparāṅmukhad ṛṇikād ṛṇagrahaṇopāyāḥ**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	pratipanna ṛṇī dāpyaḥ sāmādibhir upakramaiḥ | iti |

pratipannaḥ ṛṇasattāyāṃ saṃpratipannaḥ dāpyaḥ pratidānonmukhaḥ kāryaḥ dhaninety arthaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	yair yair upāyair arthaṃ svaṃ prāpnuyād uttamarṇakaḥ |

	tais tair upāyaiḥ saṃgṛhya dāpayed adharmarṇikam ||

ke te upāyā ity apekṣite bṛhaspatiḥ |

	dharmopadhibalātkāraiḥ gṛhasaṃrodhanena ca | iti |

ācaritākhyopāya eva gṛhasaṃrodhanenety anenopadiṣṭaḥ | dharmādīn svayam eva vyācaṣṭe |

	suhṛtsaṃbandhisaṃdiṣṭaiḥ sāmoktyānugamena ca |

	prāyeṇa vā ṛṇī dāpyo dharma eṣa udāhṛtaḥ ||

	chadmanā yācitaṃ cārtham ānīya ṛṇikād dhanī |

	anvāhitādi vāhṛtya dāpyate tatra sopadhiḥ ||

	yadā svagṛham ānīya tāḍanādyair upakramaiḥ |

	ṛṇiko dāpyate yatra balātkāraḥ sa kīrtitaḥ ||

	dāraputrapaśūn badhvā kṛtvā dāropaveśanam |

	yatrarṇī dāpyate 'rthaṃ svaṃ tad ācaritam ucyate || iti |

suhṛtsaṃbandhisaṃdiṣṭaiḥ mānyajanādeśaiḥ | saṃokytā priyapūrvavākyena | anugamanena anuvrajanena | prāyeṇa prārthanābahulyena (?) | chadmanā utsavādicchalād ānītabhūṣaṇādinā | yācitaṃ yācitakam | anvāhitam anyasmai dātum arpitam | ādigrahaṇād anyad api yathā kathaṃcid ānītaṃ saṃgṛhyate | arthaṃ svaṃ svakīyam artham | dāpyate pratidānonmukhīkriyate | śeṣaṃ vyaktārtham | dharmādayaś copāyā na yathākāmaṃ pravoktavyāḥ | kiṃ tu yathāyogyaṃ prayojyāḥ | tathā ca katyāyanaḥ |

	rājānaṃ svāminaṃ vipraṃ sāntvenaiva pradāpayet |

	rikthinaṃ suhṛdaṃ vāpi chalenaiva pradāpayet ||

	vaṇijaḥ karṣakāś caiva śilpinaś cāvravīd bhṛguḥ |

	deśācāreṇa dāpyāḥ syur duṣṭān saṃpīḍya dapayet || iti |

sāntvena dharmākhyopāyena | saṃpīḍyaśabdena balātkārācaritākhyopāyayor grahaṇam | kaḥ punaḥ deśācāra ity apekṣite sa evāha |

	dhāryo 'varuddhas tv ṛṇikaḥ prakāśaṃ janasaṃsadi |

	yāvan na dadyād deyaṃ ca deśācārasthitir yathā ||

yatra deśe dhanī svayam evāvarudhya dhārayati, tatra tathaiva dhāryaḥ | yatra punar adhamarṇasakāśād vetanārthinā nirghṛṇena puruṣāntareṇāvarudhya dhriyate tatra tathā puruṣāntaradvārā dhārya iti "deśācārasthitir yathā" ity asyārthaḥ | evaṃ ca avarudhya dhāraṇam eva deśācārānurodhitvād deśācāra ity ucyate | avaruddhasyāvaśyakaraṇīyeṣu manāg anugrahaḥ kārya ity āha sa eva |

	viṇmūtraśaṅkā yasya syād dhāryamāṇasya dehinaḥ |

	pṛṣṭhato vānugantavyo nibaddhaṃ vā samutsṛjet ||

nibaddhaṃ śṛṅkhalādinā | adhamādharmarṇaviṣayo dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ taditaraviṣayas tv ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ ity aucityat vyavasthāvagantavyā | ubhayaviṣaye 'pi pakṣāntaram āha sa eva |

	sa kṛtapratibhūś caiva moktavyaḥ syād dine dine |

	āhārakāle rātrau ca nibandhe pratibhūḥ sthitaḥ ||

saḥ dhāryamāṇo vaṇigādiḥ | kṛtadarśanapratibhūr āvaśyakakṛtyakāle vimoktavyaḥ | palāyanapratibandhe pratibhūr yataḥ sthita ity arthaḥ | yadā tu pratibhūr na labhyate labdhaṃ vā pratibhuvaṃ na dadāti tadā adhmādhamarṇaviṣaye punaḥ pakṣāntarābhidhānārtham āha |

	yo darśanapratibhuvaṃ nādhigacchen na cāśrayet |

	sa cārake niroddhavyaḥ sthāpyo vāvedya rakṣiṇaḥ ||

cārake saṃcārake, saṃcaraṇa iti yāvat | sthāpyaḥ prasthāpyaḥ | ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ pratibhūlābhe 'pi yo na dadāti tadviṣayaḥ, tasyātidauṣṭyāt | alabdhapratibhūviṣayo dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ, tasyātidauṣṭyābhāvāt | adhametaraviṣaye tv etatpakṣadvayasthāne 'nyapakṣadvayam āha sa eva |

	na cārake niroddhavyaḥ āryaḥ prātyayikaḥ śuciḥ |

	so 'nibaddhaḥ pramoktavyo nibaddhaḥ sapathena vā ||

prātyayikaḥ apalāyitvena viśvāsī | anibaddhaḥ rakṣakeṇa asaṃbaddha ity arthaḥ | evaṃ ca rakṣiṇaḥ āvedya prasthāpya ity asya sthāne pakṣo 'yam iti gamyate | itaras tu pakṣaḥ pāriśeṣyāt "sa cārake niroddhavyaḥ " iti pakṣasya sthāne draṣṭavyaḥ | yady api vaṇigādiviṣayatā deśācārākhyopāyasyoktā, tathāpy āryādiyogyānugrahapakṣapratipādanād dharmākhyopāyasādhyaviprādāv api deśācārākhyopāyo yogyānugrahapakṣasahitaḥ prayoktavya iti mantavyam | evam uktavidhayā dharmādyupāyaprayoktā rājñā na nivāraṇīyaḥ, smṛtyācāramārgeṇa kriyamāṇadhrṣaṇasyānivāryatvāt | ata eva manuḥ |

	yaḥ svakaṃ sādhayed artham uttamarṇo 'dhamarṇikāt |

	sa rājñā nābhiyoktavyaḥ svakaṃ saṃsādhayan dhanam ||

nābhiyoktavyo na kim api vacanīyaḥ | tathā ca viṣṇuḥ: "prayuktam arthaṃ yathā kathaṃcit sādhayamāno na rājñā vācyaḥ syāt" iti | yathā kathaṃcit smṛtyācāramārgāvirodheneti śeṣaḥ | tadvirodhena sādhayamāno rājñā nivāraṇīya eva, duṣṭatvāt | yac ca tenaivoktam: "sāthyamānaś (?) ced rājānam abhigacchet tatsamaṃ daṇḍyaḥ" iti, tatrāpi smṛtyācāramārgāvirodheneti śeṣo draṣṭavyaḥ, anyathā daṇḍyatvānupapatteḥ | tatsamaṃ sādhyamānarṇasamam | na kevalaṃ daṇḍyaḥ, ṛṇaṃ ca dāpyaḥ | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	prapannaṃ sādhayann arthaṃ na vācyo nṛpater bhavet |

	sādhyamāno nṛpaṃ gacchan daṇḍyo dāpayaś ca taddhanam ||

daṇḍya iti sāmānyābhidhānam asamarthaviṣaye svalpo 'pi daṇḍo yathā syād ity evamartham | ata eva manunā svalpadaṇḍo darśitaḥ |

	yaḥ sādhayantaṃ chandena vedayed dhanikaṃ nṛpe |

	sa rājñarṇacaturbhāgaṃ dāpyas tasya ca tad dhanam ||

chandena svābhiprāyeṇa, rājany anāvedyaiveti (?) yāvat | atra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	pratipannasya dharmo 'yaṃ vyapalāpī tu saṃsadi |

	lekhyena sākṣibhir vāpi bhāvayitvā pradāpyate ||

ayaṃ pūrvokto dharmagaṇaḥ ṛṇasattāyāṃ sampratipannasya ṛṇikasya | yas tu vyapalāpī ṛṇam apahnotuṃ tatsattāyāṃ vipratipannaḥ, saṃsadi pramāṇenarṇaṃ prasādhya pratipādanonmukhīkarya ity arthaḥ | evaṃ ca yad uktaṃ manunā,

	dharmeṇa vyavahāreṇa chadmanā caritena ca |

	prayuktaṃ sādhayed arthaṃ pañcamena balena ca ||

tatra vyavahāreṇeti vyapalāpiviṣayam, anyat saṃpratipannaviṣayam iti mantavyam | ata evāsaṃpratipanne vyavahārātiriktopāyaniṣedham āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	na roddhavyaḥ kriyāvādī saṃdigdhe 'rthe kathaṃcana |

	āsedhayaṃs tv anāsedhyaṃ daṇḍyo bhavati dharmataḥ ||

na roddhavya iti chalādipratiṣedhapradarśanārtham | kriyāvādisaṃdigdhapadayor arthaṃ svayam eva kathayati |

	pradātavyaṃ yad bhavati nyāyataḥ pradadāmi tat |

	evaṃ yatrarṇiko brūte kriyāvādī sa ucyate ||

	rūpasaṅghyādilābheṣu (?) yatra bhrāntir dvayor bhavet |

	deyānādeyayor vāpi saṃdigdho 'rthaḥ sa kīrtitaḥ || iti |

saṃdigdhe 'rthe pratipannadharmataḥ kurvato 'rthahānir daṇḍaś cety āha sa eva |

	anāvedya tu rājñe yaḥ saṃdigdhe 'rthe pravartate |

	prasahya sa vineyaḥ syāt sa cāpy artho na sidhyati ||

prasahya balātkāreṇety arthaḥ | kātyāyano 'pi |

	pīḍayet tu dhanī yatra ṛṇikaṃ nyāyavādinam |

	tasmād arthāt sa hīyeta tatsamaṃ cāpnuyād damam ||

tena vipratipanne 'pi vipratipattinivṛttaye vyavahārākhya evopāye pravṛttiḥ kāryety abhiprāyaḥ | sa copāyaḥ pratijñādaṇḍāntaḥ prathamaparicchede nirūpita ity uparamyate |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ pratidānaparāṅmukhād ṛṇikād ṛṇagrahaṇopāyāḥ **

**athānyāny api duḥsādhādhamarṇaviṣayāṇi vacanāni**

tatra yamaḥ |

	ṛṇikaḥ sadhano yas tu daurātmyān na prayacchati |

	rājñā dāpayitavyaḥ syāt gṛhītvā dviguṇaṃ tataḥ||

tataḥ durātmarṇikasakāśād ity arthaḥ | dviguṇam iti savṛddhikamūlyapradarśanārtham | dhanino durātmanaḥ sakāśād ṛṇaṃ balacchalādyupāyena gṛhṇīyāt | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	pūrṇe 'vadhau śāntalābham ṛṇam udgrāhayed dhanī | iti |

udgrāhaṇaṃ ca balādyupāyena sādhanam | pūrṇe 'vadhau sāvadhikatvena kṛtarṇasya udgraṇaṃ lābhaśāntyantaraṃ lābhasya niravadhikatvena kṛtaśāntalābhasya ca duḥsādhatvaśaṅkayā udgrāhaṇaṃ kāryam, anyathā tv anucitatvāt | ṛṇikaṃ tu pratipādanāt pakṣāntaram āha sa eva |

	kāreyed vā ṛṇī lekhyaṃ cakravṛddhivyavasthayā | iti |

vṛddher api punar vṛddhiś cakravṛddhiḥ | mūle 'pi viśeṣam āha sa eva |

	dvituṇasyopari yadā cakravṛddhiḥ pragṛhyate |

	bhogalābhas tadā tatra mūlaṃ syāt sodayaṃ nṛṇām ||

anenaiva vacanena dvguṇadravyānurūpabhogasamarthādhir vā cakravṛddhisthāne bhavatīty avagamyate | dviguṇagrahaṇāc chāntalābha eva pūrvoktalekhyāntarakaraṇapakṣo na punaḥ pūrṇāvadhyādāv iti gamyate | tena tatra yathāsaṃprapatti lekhyāntaram ṛṇinā kāryam, na cakravṛddhyādiniyamena dviguṇagrahaṇādi | prāguditapakṣatraye dhanikecchāto vyavasthā | yas tv ṛṇiko nirdhanatvenaiva na prayacchati so 'pi stokaṃ stokaṃ dāpya ity aha nāradaḥ |

	atha śaktivihīnaḥ syād ṛṇī kālaviparyayāt |

	śaktyapekṣam ṛṇaṃ dāpyaḥ kāle kāle yathodayam ||

dāpyo brāhmaṇa iti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	hīnajātiṃ parikṣīṇam ṛṇārthaṃ karma kāryet |

	brāhmaṇas tu parikṣīṇaḥ śanair dāpyo yathodayam ||

kārayed balātkāreṇāpīti seṣaḥ,

	dhanadānāsaṃ badhvā svādhīnaṃ karma kārayet |

iti kātyāyanasmaraṇāt | karmakaraṇāsahaṃ tu bandhanāgāre vāsayet,

	aśakto bandhanāgāre preveśyo brāhmaṇād ṛte |

iti tenaivoktatvā | praveśanaphalaṃ sāmarthyotpattau kathaṃcid ṛṇaprāptiḥ | yat punas tenaivoktam,

	karṣakān kṣatraviṭśūdrān samīhānāṃs tu dāpayet |

iti, tad yathodayaṃ dhanadānasahiṣṇuviṣayam | "dhanadānāsahaṃ vadhvā" iti sarvathā dhanadānāsahaviṣayam iti na kaścid virodhaḥ | yas tv anekarṇasamavāyād yugapad anekadhanikair duḥsādhaḥ sa kathaṃ dapya ity apekṣite yājñavalkyaḥ |

	gṛhītānukramād dāpyo dhaninām adhamarṇikaḥ |

	datvā tu brāhmaṇāyaiva nṛpates tadanantaram ||

nṛpateḥ kṣatriyasyety arthaḥ | vacanārthas tu kātyāyanena vivṛtaḥ |

	nānarṇasamavāye tu yad yat pūrvakṛtaṃ bhavet |

	tat tad evāgrato deyaṃ rājñaḥ syāc chrotriyād anu ||

śrotriyo 'tra brāhmaṇajātimātraśālī, na tu śrutādhyayanaśālī traivarṇikaḥ, rājajātyapekṣayotkṛṣṭajātiparatvenātra śrotriyapadaprayogāt | grahītṛjātikramayor virodhe jātikramo grāhyaḥ, brāhmaṇasya pūjyatayānugrāhyatvāt | evaṃ kṣatriyavaiśyayor vaiśyaśūdrayor vā yugapadupasthāne varṇakrameṇa dātavyam, pūrvapūrvasya śreṣṭhatvenānugrāhyatvāt | evaṃ krameṇa ṛṇāpākaraṇe kriyamāṇe yasya ṛṇāpākaraṇād arvāg alpadhana ṛṇikaḥ parikṣīṇo jātaḥ tasya "hīnajātiṃ parikṣīṇam" ityādinoktamārgānusaraṇam eva śaraṇam | ekadinakṛtanānarṇasamavāye tu na pūrvokto dāpanakramaḥ, kiṃ tu yugapad eva pratipādanam ṛṇikasya dhanabāhulye, dhanālpatve tu tattadṛṇānusāreṇa vibhajya yugapadaṃśadāpanam | tad āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	ekāhe likhitaṃ yatra tatra kuryād ṛṇaṃ samam |

	grahaṇaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ lābham anyathā tu yathākramam ||

grahaṇam ādhidhanam, rakṣaṇaṃ tasyaiva pālanam, lābhaṃ bhogarūpalābhaṃ ca samam eva kuryāt | anyathāharbhede likhitakrameṇa varṇabhedakrameṇa vā ṛṇapratipādanam | ādhyādau tv ādhi vivādāpanodaviṣayavacanasaṃgrahaṇaprakaraṇoktam anusaṃdheyam | "tatra kuryād ṛṇaṃ samam" ityādeḥ kvacid apavādam āha sa eva |

	yasya dravyeṇa yat paṇyaṃ sādhitaṃ yo vibhāvayet |

	tad dravyam ṛṇikenaiva dātavyaṃ tasya nanyathā ||

yasya uttamarṇasya dhanād yat paṇyam adhamarṇena vāṇijārthaṃ gṛhītaṃ tat paṇyavikrayāvāptaṃ dhanaṃ nānarṇasamavāye 'pi ṛṇikena tasyaivottamarṇasya ṛṇāpākaraṇārthaṃ dātavyam, nānyathā pūrvoktaprakāreṇa dātavyam ity arthaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ duḥsādhādhamarṇaviṣayāṇi**

**samāptaṃ ca prayuktadhanagrahaṇadharmasaṃgrāhakaṃ mahāprakaraṇam**

**atharṇapratidātṛnirṇayaḥ**

tatra brhaspatiḥ |

	yācamānāya dātavyam alpakālam ṛṇaṃ kṛtam |

	pūrṇe 'vadhau śāntalābham abhāve ca pituḥ sutaiḥ ||

dātavyaṃ dhanagrāhiṇeti śeṣaḥ, sati saṃbhave ṛṇasya grāhakeṇaivāpākaraṇīyatvāt | abhāve ca pituḥ sutair iti | asyāyam arthaḥ | ṛṇagrastāvasthasya pitur abhāve śarīratyāge sutair avaśyaṃ pitṛkṛtam ṛṇaṃ dhanine dātavyam iti | pitṛkṛtarṇasyāpākaraṇam āvaśyakam ity atra hetum āha nāradaḥ |

	icchanti pitaraḥ putrān svārthahetor yatas tataḥ |

	uttamarṇādhamarṇābhyāṃ mām ayaṃ mokṣayiṣyati ||

	ataḥ putreṇa jātena svārtham utsṛjya yatnataḥ |

	ṛṇāt pitā mocanīyo sa yathā narake 'patet ||

yatas tato bhāryopagamanaputrikākaraṇaputraparigrahādyupāyānāṃ madhye yena kenacid upāyenety arthaḥ | uttamam ṛṇam "jāyamāno vai brāhmaṇas tribhir ṛṇavā jayate" ityādiśrutyuktam | adhamam ṛṇaṃ parahastāt kusīdavidhinā gṛhītam | atha vā, uttamarṇādhamarṇaśabdato lakṣaṇayā kusīdavidhinā gṛhītam evarṇam avagantavyam | yad āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	pitṝṇāṃ sūnubhir jātair dānenaivādhamād ṛṇāt |

	vimokṣas tu yatas tasmād icchanti pitaraḥ sutān || iti |

dānena ṛṇapratidānena svārtham upabhogādirūpam utsṛjyety arthaḥ, dharmarūpasvārthotsargānupapatteḥ | vākyārthas tu: yata evam icchanti ataḥ ṛṇād avaśyaṃ pitā mocanīya iti | na ca jātair ity abhidhānāj jātamātrasya ṛṇamocane 'dhikāra iti vācyam, svārtham utsṛjyetyādeḥ śaiśavadaśāyām aghaṭanāt | tena vyavahārābhijñatayā jāteneti jātapadasyādhyāhārasāpekṣo 'rtho boddhavyaḥ | ata eva,

	aprāptavyavahāraś cet svatantro 'pīha narṇabhāk |

iti tenaivoktam | prāptavyavahāraś ca ṣoḍaśavārṣiko bhavati | tasyāṃ daśāyāṃ heyopādeyaparijñānaparipākāt | svatantras tu bālyadaśāyām api pitṛmaraṇāt bhavati | tena svatantro 'pīhety uktam | evaṃ ca, pitary uparate 'py aprāptavyavahārair na deyam, adāne 'pi doṣābhāvāt | kiṃ tu prabuddhakāle sarvaśaktyā deyam, adāne doṣasadbhāvāt | tad āha katyāyanaḥ |

	nāprāptavyavahārais tu pitary uparate kvacit |

	kāle tu vidhinā deyaṃ vaseyur narake 'nyathā ||

kvacid ity atra deyam ity anuṣajyate | vidhinā ṛṇapratidānaprakaraṇapratipāditena vidhinā | anuparate 'pi pitari sutaiḥ pitṛkṛtam ṛṇaṃ pitari pratidānāsamarthe deyam ity āha sa eva |

	vidyamāne 'pi rogārte svadeśāt proṣite tathā |

	vimśāt saṃvatsarād deyam ṛṇaṃ pitṛkṛtaṃ sutaiḥ ||

viṃśāt saṃvatsarāt pravāsam ārabhyeti śeṣaḥ | kutra gata ity ajñātaviṣaye sutair deyam, anyatra prasthāpanādināpi pitraiva dātuṃ śakyatvāt | rogārte tu svarūpasaṃkhyādivipratipattau nirṇayāt paścād eva deyam | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	sāṃnidhye 'pi pituḥ putrai ṛṇaṃ deyaṃ vibhāvitam |

	jātyandhapatitonmattakṣayaśvitrādirogiṇaḥ ||

avipratipattau tu, "yācamānāya dātavyam" ityādinoktayācanānantarakāla eva dātavyam, kālāntarasmṛteḥ | kṣaśvitrāītyādiśabdena kṣaśvitrādisadṛkṣaduścikitsā eva rogā gṛhante, na punar jvarādayaḥ | jātyandhādibhiś ca putraiḥ pitary uparate proṣite vyādhyādinā pīḍite 'samarthe 'pi na deyam, pitṛdravyabhāgānarhatvāt, kṣayādirogiṇām atyantopadrutatvāt | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	ṛṇaṃ tu dāpayet putraṃ yadi syān nirupadravaḥ |

	draviṇārhaś ca dhuryaś ca nānyathā dāpayet sutam ||

draviṇārhaḥ pitṛdravyabhāgārhaḥ | dhuryaḥ pitur dhuryāyā voḍhā | arha iti vadan pitṛdravyāgrahaṇe 'pi arhatve sati putro dāpya iti darśayati | duścikitsarogādinopadrutaḥ pitṛdravyānarhaś ca andhādiḥ adhuryaś ca pitṛkṛtarṇāpākaraṇāndhikārīti "nānyathā dāpayet sutam" ity anenoktam | dhuryās cety etat guṇapradhānabhāvena vartamānanānāputraviṣayam, tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	pitary uparate putrā ṛṇaṃ dadyur yathāṃśataḥ |

	vibhaktā vāvibhaktā vā yo vā tāmudvahed dhuram ||

yathāṃśata iti viṣamāṃśavibhāgavidhāyakaśāstrānusāreṇa vibhaktaputraviṣayam | samabhāgāvibhaktās tu samānam eva dhanaṃ dadyuḥ | avibhaktās tu samapradhānatayā vartamānāḥ saṃbhūyasamutthānena dadyuḥ | guṇapradhānatayā vartamāneṣv avibhaktkeṣu pradhānabhūta eva sarvaṃ dadyāt, guṇabhūtasyānadhikaraṇāt | yatra punaḥ pitrā saha vibhaktā avibhaktāś ca putrāḥ santi, tatra yeṣāṃ vibhāgād ūrdhvaṃ pitrā yad ṛṇaṃ kṛtaṃ tat tair na deyam, avibhakteṣu suteṣu satsu vibhaktānāṃ vibhāgataḥ pitṛdravyārhatvasyāpagatatvena mṛte pitari punaḥ pitṛdravyāgrahaṇāt | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	pitrarṇe vidyamāne tu na ca putro dhanaṃ haret |

	deyaṃ tad dhanine dravyaṃ mṛte gṛhṇaṃs tu dāpyate || \
mrte pitari tad dravyaṃ gṛhṇann eva putro dāpya ity arthaḥ | pitṛkṛtasvakṛtarṇasamavāye tu pitṛkṛtam ādau deyam "paścād ātmīyam eva ca" iti bṛhaspatismaraṇāt, ātmīyavad eva ca pitryaṃ deyam,

	ṛṇam ātmīyavat pitryaṃ putrair deyaṃ vibhāvitam |

iti tenaivoktatvāt | ātmīyavat yathātmīyaṃ savṛddhikaṃ deyaṃ tathety arthaḥ | na vayaṃ vidma iti yatra putrair nihnavaḥ kriyate tatra pramāṇena vibhāvitaṃ ced deyam, no cen na deyam iti vibhāvitapadasyārthaḥ | sarvathā kānicid ṛṇāni pitryāṇi putrair na deyānīty āha sa eva |

	saurākṣikaṃ vṛthādānaṃ kāmakrodhapratiśrutam |

	prātibhāvyaṃ daṇḍaśulkaśeṣaṃ putrair na dāpayet ||

sauraṃ surāsaṃpādananimittam, ākṣikaṃ dyūtaparājayanimittakaṃ ceti yāvat | vṛthādānaṃ smṛtyantare 'bhihitam |

	dhūrte vandini malle ca kuvaidye kitave śaṭhe |

	cāṭuvāraṇacoreṣu dattaṃ bhavati niṣphalam ||

kāmapratiśrutaṃ krodhapratiśrutaṃ ca kātyāyanenoktam |

	likhitaṃ muktakaṃ vāpi deyaṃ yat tu pratiśrutam |

	parapūrvastriyai tat tu vidyāt kāmakṛtaṃ nṛṇām ||

	yatra hiṃsāṃ samutpādya krodhād dravyaṃ vināśya vā |

	uktaṃ tuṣṭikaraṃ yat tu vidyāt krodhakṛtaṃ tu tat || iti |

muktakaṃ lekharahitam (?) | parapūrvastriyai parabhāryāyai | yatra hiṃsām ityāder ayam arthaḥ, parasya hiṃsāṃ dhanavināśaṃ vā krodhāt kṛtvā tattuṣṭaye dravyaṃ dāsyāmīti pratiśrutaṃ tad ṛṇaṃ krodhajam iti | prātibhāvyaṃ darśanapratibhūdeyam atra vivakṣitam | tathā ca manuḥ |

	prātibhāvyaṃ vṛthādānam ākṣikaṃ saurikaṃ ca yat |

	daṇḍaśulkāvaśiṣṭaṃ ca na putro dātum arhati ||

	darśanaprātibhāvye tu vidhiḥ syāt pūrvacoditaḥ || iti |

pūrvacoditavidhiḥ "prātibhāvyaṃ na putro dātum arhati" iti vidhiḥ" | putrais tu dātavyaṃ yat prātibhāvyaṃ yena ca prakārreṇa dātavyam, tat sarvaṃ pratibhūprakaraṇa eva darśitam | daṇḍaśulkaśeṣam iti padadvayasyārthaḥ uśanasā spaṣṭīkṛtaḥ |

	daṇḍaṃ vā daṇḍaśeṣaṃ vā śulkaṃ taccheṣam eva vā |

	na dātavyaṃ tu putreṇa yac ca na vyāvahārikam ||

vyāvahārikam saurikam ity arthaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām ṛṇapratidātṛnirṇaye putraviṣayāṇi**

**atha pautraviṣayāṇi kānicid vacanāni likhyante**

tatra kātyāyanaḥ |

	pitrā dṛṣṭam ṛṇaṃ yat tu kramāyātaṃ pitāmahāt |

	nidoṣaṃ noddhṛtaṃ putraiḥ deyaṃ pautrais tu tad bhṛguḥ ||

pitrā dṛṣṭaṃ svapitṛkṛtatvena pitrā niḥsaṃdigdham avagatam | pitāmahāt kramaprāptaṃ pūrvapūrvapuruṣābhāvādinā prāptam | nidoṣam adeyatvāpādakadoṣarahitam | putrair noddhṛtaṃ putrair duścikitsarogādivaśād anapākṛtam | tathā ca sa eva |

	paitāmahaṃ tu yat putrair na dattaṃ rogibhiḥ sthitaiḥ |

	tasmād evaṃvidhaṃ paurair deyaṃ paitāmahaṃ samam ||

samaṃ vṛddhirahitaṃ mūlamātram iti yāvat | putrair ekadeśāpākaraṇe tu anapākṛtāṃśāntaraṃ deyam,

	yad ṛṇaṃ dattaśeṣaṃ vā deyaṃ paitāmahaṃ tu tat |

iti tenaivoktatvāt | anevaṃvidham adeyam iti sa evāha |

	sadoṣaṃ vyāhataṃ pitrā naiva deyam ṛṇaṃ kvacit | iti |

sadoṣaṃ surādinimittatvena doṣayuktam | pitrā vyāhataṃ nirākṛtam, pitrā tv adṛṣṭam apahnutaṃ vā pramāṇasādhitaṃ deyam,

	putrapautrai ṛṇaṃ deyaṃ nihnave sākṣibhāvitam |

iti yājñavalkyenokteḥ | adeyopalakṣaṇārthaṃ sadopagrahaṇaṃ tenānyad apy adeyaṃ putreṣūktaṃ pautreṣv api śulkādyavagantavyam | prātibhāvyaṃ punaḥ sarvaprakāram api pautrair na deyam iti praibhūprakaraṇe darśitam | pautrair api prāptavyavahārair eva deyam, aprāptavyavahārāṇāṃ putreṣūktanyāyenānadhikārāt | proṣitaviṣaye ca purāṇāṃ yaḥ pratidānakālaḥ sa eva paurāṇām api, tathā ca viṣṇuḥ: "dhanagrāhiṇi prete pravrajite dvidaśāḥ samāḥ | proṣite vā tatputrapautrair dhanaṃ deyam | nātaḥ param anīpsubhiḥ" iti | pravrajite saṃnyasta ity arthaḥ | dvidaśāḥ samāḥ proṣite vā viṃśativarṣavyāpitayā vā pravāse dhanagrāhiṇā kṛta ity arthaḥ | nātaḥ param anīpsubhir ity asya viṃśativarṣād ūrdhvaṃ na vilambaḥ kāryaḥ ṛṇapratidānānīpsubhir apīty arthaḥ | atha vāyam arthaḥ: ataḥ putrapautrebhyaḥ param ūrdhvaṃ ye jātās taiḥ prapautrādibhir anīpsubhir na deyam iti | etad uktaṃ bhavati: putrapautrāṇām eva jātyandhādivyatiriktānāṃ nirupādhikariktārhatvam, nānyeṣāṃ prapautrādīnām iti | rikthagrahaṇābhāve prapautrādibhir avaśyaṃ putrapautravan na deyam iti | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	kramād avyāhataṃ prāptaṃ putrair yan narṇam uddhṛtam |

	dadyuḥ paitāmahaṃ pautrās tac caturthān nivartate ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	putrābhāve 'pi dātavyam ṛṇaṃ pautreṇa yatnataḥ |

	caturthena na dātavyaṃ tasmāt tad dhi nivartate ||

evaṃ ca prapitāmahādikṛtarṇāpākaraṇānadhikāraś caturthāder agṛhītarikthasyaiva na punar gṛhītarikthasyety avagantavyam | pitrātmīyarṇadānāt pūrvam eva paitāmaharṇaṃ pautreṇātmapitṛpitāmahakṛtarṇatrayasamavāye deyam,

	tayoḥ paitāmahaṃ pūrvaṃ deyam eva ṛṇaṃ sadā |

iti bṛhaspatismaraṇāt | tayos tābhyāṃ pitrātmīyābhyām ity arthaḥ | evaṃ pautreṇa rikthārhatvena ṛṇadānaṃ dhuryapautrāntarasyābhāve dhuryasya vā pitṛvyasya, dhuryasya sadbhāve tv adhuryasyānadhikārāt | samapradhānabhūteṣu pautrādiṣu vibhakteṣu yathāṃśataḥ ṛṇāpākaraṇam, vibhakteṣu tu saṃbhūyasamuttānenetyādy atrāpy avagantavyam | pautraviṣayavacanānāṃ viśeṣamātrapradarśanaparāṇāṃ pradarśitaviśeṣād anyat putraiḥ samānam ity ābhiprāyikārthāvagamāt | gṛhītariktānāṃ tu pautrāṇām adhikāro vṛddhisahitarṇāpākaraṇe "deyaṃ paitāmahaṃ samam" ity asyāgṛhītarikthaviṣayatvāt |

	tayoḥ paitāmahaṃ pūrvaṃ deyam eva ṛṇaṃ sadā |

ity uktas tu kramātmako viśeṣaḥ agṛhītarikthānām api pautrānām, sadetyabhidhānāt ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām ṛṇapraidātṛnirṇaye pautraviṣayāṇi**

**atha rikthagrāhāiviṣayāṇi**

tatra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	ṛṇagrāha ṛṇaṃ dāpyo yoṣidgrāhas tathaiva ca |

	putro 'nanyāśritadravyaḥ putrahīnasya rikthinaḥ ||

atra padārthas tāvad ucyate | vibhāgakrameṇa yo dravyaṃ gṛhṇāti sa rikthagrāhaḥ | rāgādivaśāt parabhāryāṃ yo bhāryātvena svīkaroti sa yoṣigrāhaḥ, na punaḥ putrotpādakatayā niyukto jāro vā, tayor upabhogamātrakāritvena grāhakatvābhāvāt | yo dāyānarhatayā paṅgvādir mātāpitrāśritadravyavān na bhavati so 'nanyāśritadravyaḥ | ye rikthagrāhās ta eva punaś ca rikthipadenoktāḥ | atha pādārthā ucyante, tatrādyantapādayor ayam arthaḥ: dāyānarhaputrasadbhāve 'py asadbhāve 'pi rikthagrāhī ṛṇaṃ dadyād iti | tathā ca viṣṇuḥ: "saputrasya vāputrasya vā rikthagrāhī dhanaṃ dadyāt" iti | etad uktaṃ bhavati: yathā putrapautrayor dāyabhāgārhayor bhāve ṛṇabhāk na tadvyatiriktaḥ, tathātreti | yathaiva paṅgvādilakṣaṇaputrasadbhāve cāsadbhāve ca rikthagrāhābhāve sati yoṣidgrāho ṛṇaṃ dadyād iti dvitīyapādasyārthaḥ | tathā ca viṣṇur eva: "vidhanasya strīgrāhī" iti | saputrasya vāpy aputrasya cety anuvartate | vidhanasyeti vadan dhanahārirahitasyeti darśayati | bṛhaspatinā tu spaṣṭam uktam |

	strīhārī ca tathaiva syād abhāve dhanahāriṇaḥ | iti |

tathaiva dhanahārī ṛṇabhāk tathaiva dhanahāry abhāve strīhārī syād ity arthaḥ | dhanahāristrīhāriṇor abhāve dāyānarhaḥ putro dadyād iti tṛtīyapādasyārthaḥ | tathā ca nāradena,

	dhanastrīhāriputrāṇām ṛṇabhāg yo dhanaṃ haret |

ity uktvā uktam: "putro 'satoḥ strīdhaninoḥ" iti | ṛṇabhāg ity anuvartate | strīgrāhadhanagrāhayor abhāve dāyānarhaḥ putra ṛṇabhāg ity arthaḥ | yat punas tenaivānantaram uktam "strīhārī dhaniputrayoḥ" iti, tad ayuktam iva pratibhāti | dhanahāriputrābhāve strīhārī ṛṇabhāg iti vacanāntareṇa prākpratipāditārthavirodhāt, putrasya strīhārirāhitye ṛṇabhāgitvam iti svoktena virodhāc ca | satyam asti virodhaḥ | tathāpi viṣayabhedād asāv apagacchati | tathā hi "vidhanasya strīgrāhī" iti viṣṇuvacanena pakṣadvayam uktam: saputrasya dhanahārirahitasya strīhārī dadyāt, aputrasya vā dhanahārirahitasyeti | tatra dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ "strīhārī dhaniputrayoḥ" ity anenoktaḥ | dhanahāriputrayor asatoḥ strīhārī ṛṇabhāg iti dvitīyapakṣasamānatvāt | vacanāntareṇa prākpratipādito 'rthaḥ prathamapakṣa eva | ato na tena saha dvitīyapakṣasyevāsyāpi virodhaḥ, vikalpitatvāt | "putro 'satoḥ strīdhaninoḥ" ity anena saputrasya strīhāridhanahārirahitasya ṛṇaṃ dāyānarhaḥ putro dadyād ity uktam | "putro 'nanyāśritadravyaḥ" iti vacanena tulyārthatvāt | evaṃ ca na prākpratipāditena svoktena vā virodha iti yuktam uktaṃ nāradena | yat tu kātyāyanenoktam,

	vyasanābhiplute putre bālo vā yatra dṛśyate |

	dravyahṛd dāpyate tatra tasyābhāve purandhrihṛt ||

iti, tat tasyāṃ daśāyāṃ dayārhaputrasyānadhikārapradarśanārtham, na tu dāyānarhaputrasya vyasanopaplutyādyavasthāyām eva dhanagrāhādir uktakrmeṇarṇabhāk, anyatra tu dāyānarhaḥ putra eva prathamataḥ paścād dhanagrāhādir iti kramāntaravidhānārtham, tasyātrāśrutatvāt, ādau dāyānarhaputradānāsāmañjasyāc ca | yat punas tenaivoktam,

	pūrvaṃ dadyād dhanagrāhaḥ putras tasmād anantaram |

	yoṣidgrāhaḥ sutābhāve putro vātyantanirdhanaḥ ||

iti tad yoṣidgrāhāpekṣayātyantabahudhano yaḥ putras tasya dhanagrāhānantaryārtham iti sarvam aviruddham | na ca yoṣidgrāhadānādhikāraśāstrāny athānupapattyā yoṣidgrahaṇam api pūrvapatikṛtarṇadātuḥ śāstrīyam iti śaṅkanīyam | yato rāgaprāpayoṣidgrahaṇasya saṃbhavān na śāstrasyānupapattiḥ | ata evāha saṃgrahakāraḥ |

	yatra dadyād ṛṇaṃ voḍhuḥ punarbhūsvairiṇīpatiḥ |

	na tena tad upādānaṃ śāstreṇa vihitaṃ bhavet ||

tadupādānaṃ punarbhuvāṃ svairiṇīnāṃ saṃgrahaṇam | tās tu nāradena nirūpitāḥ |

	parapūrvāḥ striyas tv anyāḥ sapta proktā yathākramam |

	punarbhūs trividhā tāsāṃ svairiṇī tu caturvidhā ||

	kanyaivākṣatayonir yā pāṇigrahaṇadūṣitā |

	punarbhūḥ prathamā proktā punaḥsaṃskārakarmaṇā ||

	deśadharmān avekṣya strī gurubhir yā pradīyate |

	utpannasāhasānyasmai sā dvitīyā prakīrtitā ||

	asatsu devareṣu strī bāndhavair yā pradīyate |

	savarṇāya sapiṇḍāya sā tṛtīyā prakīrtitā ||

	strī prasūtāprasūtā vā patyāv eva tu jīvati |

	kāmāt samāśrayed anyaṃ prathamā svairiṇī tu sā ||

	kaumāraṃ patim utsṛjya yā tv anyaṃ puruṣaṃ śritā |

	punaḥ patyur gṛhaṃ yāyāt sā dvitīyā prakīrtitā ||

	mṛte bhartari tu prāptā devarādīn apāsya vā |

	upagacchet paraṃ kāmāt sā tṛtīyā prakīrtitā ||

	prāptā deśād dhanakrītā kṣutpipāsāturā ca yā |

	tavāham ity upagatā sā caturthī prakīrtitā || iti |

utpannasāhasā kṣatayoniḥ prauḍheti yāvat | anyasmai devarāyety arthaḥ | devarāyety abhiprāyeṇātrānyaśabdaprayogāt, sa cābhiprāyaḥ "asatsu devareṣu" iti uttaratroktyā gamyate | samāśrayet suratārtham iti śeṣaḥ | evaṃ śritety atrāpi śeṣo 'dhyavaseyaḥ | punaḥ patyur gṛhaṃ yāyāt nivāsārtham iti śeṣaḥ | evaṃ ca yaḥ prathametarapunarbhuvam upagacchati sa niyuktamātro na yoṣidgrāha iti na punarbhūbhartṛkṛtarṇadānādhikārīty avagantavyam | evaṃ yaḥ svairiṇīṃ caturthīvyatiriktām upagacchati so 'pi jāramātro na yoṣidgrāha iti svairiṇīpatikṛtarṇānadhikārīty avagantavyam | ādyapunarbhvās tu yaḥ pāṇiṃ gṛhṇāti sa yoṣidgrāhī bhavaty eva bhāryātvenaiva svīkārāt | caturthyā api svairiṇyā bhāryātvenaiva svīkāra iti svīkartā yoṣidgrāha eva | tena tābhyāṃ punarbhvāḥ prathamāyāḥ patyā kṛtam ṛṇaṃ svairiṇyāś caturthyāḥ patyā kṛtaṃ ca ṛṇaṃ deyam | tathā ca tenaivoktam |

	animā svairiṇīnāṃ ya prathamā ca punarbhuvām |

	ṛṇaṃ tayoḥ patikṛtaṃ dadyād yas te upāśnute ||

patitveneti śexaḥ | ata eva,

	yas tu dadyād ṛṇaṃ voḍhuḥ punarbhūsvairiṇīpatiḥ |

iti saṃgrahakāreṇoktam | yat tu nāradenoktam,

	adhanasya hy aputrasya mṛtasyopaiti yaḥ striyam |

	ṛṇaṃ voḍhuḥ sa bhajate saivāsya ca dhanaṃ smṛtam ||

iti, tatra striyam upaitīty asya yathāśrutārthaparatve niyuktajārayor api ṛṇabhāgitvam iti prāguktavirodhaḥ | strīgrāhaparatve paunaruktyam iti saṅkaṭam iti | ucyate: dhanagrāhaputrayoṣidgrāhavihīnasya yoṣidupabhoktāpi ṛṇabhāg iti pratipādanārtham idaṃ vacanam ārabdham iti na saṅkaṭaṃ kiṃcit | yad api tenaivoktam,

	yā punaḥ sadhanaiva strī sāpatyā vānyam āśrayet |

	so 'syā dadyād ṛṇaṃ bhartur utsṛjed vā tathaiva tām |

iti, tasyāyam arthaḥ: yā strī sadhanā sabālatanayā ca rakṣārthaṃ mātulādikam āśrayet, sa cāśrayabhūto mātulādiḥ bhartṛkṛtarṇaṃ dāpayet | yadi tu sā dātuṃ necchati tadā sadhanāṃ satanayāṃ tyajed iti | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	bālaputrādhikārthā ca trātāraṃ yānyam āśritā |

	āśritas tadṛṇaṃ dadyād bālaputrāvidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ||

dadyāt dāpayed ity arthaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām ṛṇapratidātṛnirṇaye rikthagrāhādiviṣayāṇi**

**atha kuṭumbaviṣayāṇi**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	pitṛvyabhrātṛputrastrīdāsaśiṣyānujīvibhiḥ |

	yad gṛhītaṃ kuṭumbārthe tad gṛhī dātum arthati ||

śiṣyagrahaṇenāntevāsy api saṃgṛhītaḥ, chātramātrasya vivakṣitatvāt | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	śiṣyāntevāsidāsastrīpreṣyakṛtyakaraiś ca yat |

	kuṭumbahetor utkṣiptaṃ dātavyaṃ tatukuṭumbinā ||

śiṣyo vedavidyārthī | śilpavidhyārthī tv antevāsī | kuṭumbahetoḥ kuṭumbārtham utkṣiptaṃ asaṃnidhānādinā svānujñāṃ vināpi kṛtam ṛṇam | kuṭumbinaiva ṛṇakartuḥ pravāsavyasanādyabhāve 'pi deyam, kuṭumbabharaṇasya svakāryatvād ity arthaḥ | kātyāyano 'py amum evārtham āha |

	proṣitasyāmatenāpi kuṭumbārtham ṛṇaṃ kṛtam |

	dāsastrīmātṛśiṣyair vā dadyāt putreṇa vā bhṛguḥ ||

striyā mātrā vā kṛtam kuṭumbārtham api kiṃcid ṛṇaṃ deyam ity āha sa eva |

	deyaṃ bhāryākṛtam ṛṇaṃ bhartrā putreṇa mātṛkam |

	bhartur arthe kṛtaṃ yat syād abhidhāya gate diśam ||

nārado 'pi |

	putriṇī tu samutsṛjya putraṃ strī yānyam āśrayet |

	tasyā ṛṇaṃ haret sarvaṃ niḥsvāyāḥ putra eva tu ||

anyaṃ mātulādikam | anujñayā tu yasya kasyacid arthe kṛtam api sadā kuṭumbinaiva deyam, "prākpratipannaṃ deyaṃ yasya kasyacit kuṭumbārthaṃ vā" iti viṣṇusmaraṇāt | pratipannapadasyārthaḥ kātyāyanena prapañcitaḥ |

	deyaṃ putrakṛtaṃ tat syād yac ca syād anuvarṇitam |

	kṛtāsaṃvāditaṃ yac ca śrutvā caivānucoditam ||

kṛtam akṛchra iti śeṣaḥ | kṛchrakṛtaṃ tv apratipannam api deyam | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	pitur eva niyogād vā kuṭumbabharaṇāya vā |

	kṛtaṃ vā yad ṛṇaṃ kṛchre dadyāt putrasya tatpitā ||

atra ca pūrvatra ca putragrahaṇaṃ kuṭumbopalakṣaṇārtham, pitṛgrahaṇaṃ ceha gṛhaprabhor upalakṣaṇārtham | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	kuṭumbārtham aśakte tu gṛhītaṃ vyādhite 'tha vā |

	upaplavanimittaṃ ca vidyād āpatkṛtaṃ ca tat ||

	kanyāvaivāhikaṃ caiva pretakārye ca yatkṛtam |

	etat sarvaṃ pradātavyaṃ kuṭumbena kṛtaṃ prabhoḥ || iti |

aśakte kuṭumbabharaṇāsamarthe kuṭumbinīty arthaḥ | kanyāvaivāhikaṃ kanyāvivāhanimittakam | yatkṛtaṃ yena kṛtam | prabhoḥ prabhuṇā kuṭumbineti yāvat | yathā putrapitṛśabdayor upalakṣaṇārthatvaṃ nāradīye, tathā,

	ṛṇaṃ putrakṛtaṃ pitrā śodhyaṃ yad anumoditam |

	sutasnehena vā dadyāt nānyathā dātum arhati ||

iti bārhaspatyavacane 'py avagantavyam | śodhyam apākaraṇīyam | anumoditagrahaṇaṃ pratiśutasyāpy upalakṣaṇārtham,

	deyaṃ pratiśrutaṃ yat syāt yac ca syād anumoditam |

iti kātyāyanasmaraṇāt | snehād dānaṃ prāṅnirūpitanānāvidhadeyarṇavyatiriktarṇaviṣayam | bhāryākṛtarṇaviṣaye 'pi samānam, sutagrahaṇasya snehamātrodāharaṇatayā kṛtatvāt | evaṃ ca yad uktaṃ kātyāyenena,

	ṛṇaṃ putrakṛtaṃ pitrā na deyam iti dharmataḥ |

iti, tad uktanānāvidhadeyarṇetararṇaviṣayam ity avagantavyam | dharmata iti vadan snehato deyam iti darśayati | yad api nāradenoktam,

	na bhāryayā kṛtam ṛṇaṃ kathaṃcit patyur āvahet |

iti, tad api nirūpitadeyarṇavyatiriktaviṣayam | evaṃbhūtavixayatvapradarśanārtham evānantaram uktaṃ tenaiva |

	āpatkṛtād ṛte puṃsā kuṭumbartho hi dustaraḥ | iti |

bhāryayāpy āpadi kṛtaṃ kuṭumbārthaṃ ca kṛtaṃ patyur apākaraṇīyaṃ bhaved ity arthaḥ | pūrvokto yo niṣedhaḥ sa rajakādistrībhyo 'nyatrety āha sa eva |

	anyatra rajakavyādhagopaśauṇḍikayoṣitām |

	teṣāṃ tatpratyayā vṛttiḥ kuṭumbaṃ ca tadāśrayam ||

teṣāṃ rajakādīnām | tatpratyayā vṛttiḥ yoṣidadhīnaṃ vartanam ity arthaḥ | tenānāpadi kuṭumbārthaṃ kṛtam api patibhir deyam ity abhiprāyaḥ | rajakādigrahaṇaṃ yoṣidadhīnavṛttīnāṃ tailakaśailūṣādīnām upalakṣaṇārtham | yājñavalkyo 'pi hetukathanenopalakṣaṇārthatvaṃ darśayan nāradābhiprāyaviṣayatvenoktam evārtham āha |

	gopaśauṇḍikaśailūṣarajakavyādhayoṣitām |

	ṛṇaṃ dadyāt patis tāsāṃ yasmād vṛttis tadāśrayā ||

śaulūṣo naṭaḥ | evaṃ ca yad uktaṃ viṣṇunā "na strīkṛtaṃ patiputrau" iti, tad uktadeyabhūtavyatiriktaviṣayam iti mantavyam | manus tu kuṭumbārthe bhṛtyādikṛtakriyādir api kuṭumbināṅgīkaraṇīya ity āha |

	kuṭumbārthe tv adhīno 'pi vyavahāraṃ yam ācaret |

	svadeśe vā videśe vā tan nyāyān na vicālayet ||

kiṃ tu svīkuryād iti śeṣaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām ṛṇapratidātṛnirṇaye **

**atha kuṭumbajanaviṣayāṇi**

tatra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	avibhaktaiḥ kuṭumbārthe yad ṛṇaṃ tu kṛtaṃ bhavet |

	dadyus tad rikthinaḥ prete proṣite vā kuṭumbini ||

avibhaktadhanair bhrātrādibhiḥ samapradhānaiḥ kuṭumbavyayāya yad ṛṇaṃ kṛtaṃ tat taiḥ sadā na deyam, kiṃ tu taddānādhikāriṇi kuṭumbini prete proṣite vā dātavyam ity arthaḥ | tatrāpi keṣāṃcid abhāve yas tiṣṭhati sa dadyāt "avibhaktaiḥ kṛtam ṛṇaṃ yas tiṣṭhet sa dadyāt" iti viṣṇusmaraṇāt | avibhaktair iti bahuvacanaṃ pūrvatrātra cāvivakṣitam | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	pitṛvyeṇāvibhaktena bhrātrā vā yad ṛṇaṃ kṛtam |

	mātrā vā yat kuṛumbārthe dadyus tat sarvarikthinaḥ ||

ṛṇasya grahītā pitṛvyādir yadi naṣṭaḥ proṣito vā mṛto vā syāt tadā rikthibhir vibhaktais tatkuṭumbavyayāya kṛtam ṛṇaṃ dātavyaṃ savataḥ kim utāvibhaktair ity arthaḥ | evaṃ vṛttikāreṇa vyākhyātam | asmin vyākhyāne vacanānantare vā vṛthaivāvibhaktagrahaṇaṃ syād iti matvā bhāṣyakāreṇa pravibhaktadhanaiḥ pitṛvyādibhiḥ svataḥ svadhanād dātavyam ity artha iti vacanārtham uktvā madhyagād eva dhanād avibhaktair datvāvaśiṣṭavibhāgaḥ kāryo nādatveti vacanāntarārtho darśitaḥ | yadā pravibhaktadhanā ṛṇaṃ prayacchanti tadā dāyānurūpam aṃśaṃ dadyuḥ, "vibhaktāś ca dāyānurūpam aṃśam" iti viṣṇusmaraṇāt ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām ṛṇapratidātṛkuṭumbajanaviṣayāṇi**

**atha paratantrastrīviṣayāṇi**

tatra kātyāyanaḥ |

	bhartrā putreṇa vā sārdhaṃ kevalaṃ vātmanā kṛtam |

	ṛṇam evaṃvidhaṃ deyaṃ nānyathā tatkṛtaṃ striyā ||

anyathā tatkṛtaṃ kevalaṃ bhartrā putreṇa vā kṛtaṃ striyā tayor abhāve 'pi na deyam, kiṃ tu bhartrā putreṇa vā sārdhaṃ saṃbhūya gṛhītam ṛṇaṃ tayor abhāve deyam | svayam eva gṛhītaṃ tu tayor abhāve 'pīty arthaḥ | evaṃvidham iti vadan anyad apy asti striyā deyam iti darśayati | kiṃ tad ity apekṣite yājñavalkyaḥ: "pratipannaṃ striyā deyam" iti | pratipannaṃ patikṛtaṃ putrakṛtaṃ vā ṛṇam ahaṃ dāsyāmīty abhyupetam ity arthaḥ,

	na strī patikṛtaṃ dadyāt ṛṇaṃ putrakṛtaṃ tathā |

	abhyupetad ṛte .......................||

iti nāradasmaraṇāt | evaṃ ca patiputretarakṛtaṃ pratipannam api striyā na deyam iti parisaṃkhyārthatayā yājñavalkyavacanam iti mantavyam, spaṣṭatvena vidhyārthatvāsaṃbhavāt (?) | apratipannam api patikṛtaṃ kvacid viṣaye striyā deyam ity āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	martukāmena yā bhartrā uktā deyam ṛṇaṃ tvayā |

	aprapannāpi sā dāpyā dhanaṃ yady āśritaṃ striyā ||

atrārthād anāśritabhartṛdhanā strī aprapannā cen na deyam iti gamyate | yat tu nāradenoktam,

	dadyāc cāputravidhavā niyuktā vā mumūrṣuṇā |

	yo vā tadriktham ādadyād yato riktham ṛṇaṃ tataḥ ||

iti, tat āśritabhartṛdhanavidhavābhiprāyeṇoktam iti na pūrvoktena viruddham | yat tu viṣṇunoktam: "na strīpatiputrakṛtam" iti, tat sāmānyena pratiṣedhabodhakaṃ viśeṣeṇa vidhāyakaprāguktavacanaviṣayavyatiriktaviṣaye 'vatiṣṭhata ity aviruddham | deyādeyanirṇayāḥ pṛthak pṛthak kartum asukarā iti pratidātṛnirṇayāntaḥpātitayāsmābhiḥ kṛtāḥ pratyetavyāḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ pratikātṛnirṇaye paratantrastrīviṣayāṇi **

**samāptaṃ ca pratidātṛnirṇayaprakaraṇam**

**athātītottamarṇaṛṇāpākaraṇaviṣayāṇi**

tatra nāradaḥ |

	brāhmaṇasya tu yad deyaṃ sānvayasya na cāsti saḥ |

	nivapet tatsakulyeṣu tadabhāve 'sya bandhuṣu ||

brāhmaṇagrahaṇam uttamarṇopalakṣaṇārtham | evaṃ cāyam arthaḥ: uttamarṇasy deyaṃ yad ṛṇaṃ tat tadabhāve tatsantānasya tanyādes taddravyagrāhiṇaḥ ṛṇapratidātrā deyam | sasantānasyottamarṇasyābhāve tatsakulyeṣv antaraṅgānatikrameṇa deyam | sakulyānām apy abhāve mātulādiṣu bandhuṣv antaraṅgānatikrameṇa deyam iti | yadā tu pūrvoktānām abhāvaḥ tadāpy āha sa eva |

	yadā tu na sakulyāḥ syur na ca saṃbandhibāndhavāḥ |

	tadā dadyād dvijebhyas tu teṣv asatsv apsu nikṣipet ||

prajāpatir api |

	bandhvabhāve tu viprebhyo deyaṃ kṣepyaṃ jale 'pi vā |

	jale kṣiptaṃ tathāgnau ca dhanaṃ syāt pāralaukikam ||

ānṛṇyāpādanena paralokahitaṃ jalādau prakṣiptaṃ dhanaṃ bhavatīty uttarārdhasyārthaḥ | agnau cety atra hutam iti śeṣo 'dhyāhāryaḥ, na punaḥ kṣiptam ity asyānuṣaṅgaḥ kāryaḥ | yad āha gobhilaḥ: "ṛṇeṣv ajñāyamāneṣu golakāmadhyamaparṇena juhuyāt yat kusīdam" iti | māntravarṇikī ca agnir atra devatā | ānṛṇyārthaṃ cāyaṃ homaḥ | anṛṇo bhavāmīti mantraliṅgāt | golakā palāśaḥ | tathā ca saṃgrahakāraḥ |

	dravyaṃ yat tv adhamarṇasthaṃ kvacid brāhmaṇagaṃ bhavet |

	sutādibrāhmaṇāntānāṃ rikthabhājām asaṃbhave ||

	palāśasya palāśena juhuyān madhyamen tu |

	yat kusīdam iti prāsyed atha vāpsv eva tad dhanam || iti |

kvacit uttamarṇādibandhvantānām abhāvaviṣaya ity arthaḥ | yat kusīdam iti pūrveṇaiva saṃbadhyate, mūlasmṛtau jalapakṣepaṇamantrāsmaraṇāt | nikṣiptādidhane 'py eṣa eva vidhir nikṣepādisvāminy atīte draṣṭavyaḥ, samānakāraṇatvād ity uktaṃ devasvāminā ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām atītottamarṇaṛṇāpākaraṇaviṣayāṇi**

**iti sakalavidyāviśārada-śrīkeśvādityabhaṭṭopādhyāyasūnu-yājñikadevaṇabhattopādhyāyasomayājiviracitāyāṃ smṛticandrikāyām ṛṇādānākhyasya padasya vidhivitānaḥ samāptaḥ**

**atha dvitīyasya padasya nikṣepopanidhyādibhedenānekavidhasya vidhir ucyate **

tata manuḥ |

	kulaje vṛttasaṃpanne darmajñe satyavādini |

	mahāpakṣe dhaniny āpte nikṣepaṃ nikṣiped budhaḥ ||

mahāpakṣe bandhuśālini | kaḥ punar nikṣepa ity apekṣite vyāsaḥ |

	sthānatyāgād rājabhayād dāyādānāṃ ca vañcanāt |

	svadravyam arpyate 'nyasya haste nikṣepam āha tam ||

svadravyaṃ svakīyadravyaṃ vastraniṣkādikam anyasya kūlajatvādiguṇavato haste samarpyate grāhakasamakṣam evārpyate kṣemārthaṃ yat tatra nikṣepaśabdo vartata ity arthaḥ | tac cārpaṇaṃ grāhakasya purato gaṇanaṃ kṛtvā kāryam, "nikṣepaṃ gaṇitaṃ viduḥ" it nāradasmaraṇāt | upanidhisthāpanavidhim āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	sthānaṃ gṛhaṃ gṛhasthaṃ ca tadvarṇaṃ vividhān guṇān |

	satyaṃ śaucaṃ bandhujanaṃ parīkṣya sthapayen nidhim ||

nidhim upanidhim ity arthaḥ | tasya svarūpam api tenaivoktam |

	anākhyātaṃ vyavahitam asaṃkhyātam adarśitam |

	mudrāṅkitaṃ ca yad dattaṃ tad aupanidhikaṃ smṛtam ||

vyavahitaṃ karaṇḍakādau prakṣipya nihitam, nāsya samarpāṇe (?) grāhakasamakṣāsamakṣalakṣaṇo niyamaḥ, dattam iti sāmānyenokteḥ | nyāsasya tu svarūpanirūpaṇamukhenaiva sthāpanaprakāram āha sa eva |

	rājacorārātibhayād dāyādānāṃ ca vañcanāt |

	sthāpyate 'nyagṛhe dravyaṃ nyāsas tat parikīrtitam ||

dravyaṃ balīvardakāṃsyādikam | gṛha iti vadatā gṛhasvāminaḥ parasthānagatasya asamakṣe tasminn āgate samarpaṇīyam iti kathayitvā sthāpito nyāsaḥ, na punaḥ tatsamakṣe samarpita iti darśitam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ nikṣepādisthāpanavidhiḥ**

**atha nikṣepādipālanavidhiḥ**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	sasākṣikaṃ raho dattaṃ dvividhaṃ samudāhṛtam |

	putravat paripālyaṃ tad vinaśyaty anavekṣayā ||

pālayituḥ phalaṃ cāha sa eva |

	dadato yad bhavet puṇyaṃ hemakupyāmbarādikam |

	tat syāt pālayato nyāsaṃ tathaiva śaraṇāgatam ||

kupyaṃ trapusīsādikam | bhakṣakāder doṣo 'pi tenaiva darśitaḥ |

	bhartṛdrohe yathā nāryāḥ puṃsaḥ putrasuhṛdvadhe |

	doṣo bhavet tathā nyāse bhakṣitopekṣite nṛṇām ||

	nyāsadravyaṃ na gṛhṇīyāt tannāśas tv ayaśaḥkaraḥ || iti |

nyāsagrahaṇaṃ prācīnavacanatraye 'py upalakṣaṇārtham, tena phalaśrutyādikaṃ nikṣepāditrayasādhāraṇam it mantavyam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ nikṣepādipālanavidhiḥ**

**atha sabhyabhūtagrahītṛviṣayāṇi**

atha sabhyabhūtagrahītṛviṣayāṇi kānicid vacanāni likhyante | tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	daivarājopaghātena yadi tannāśam āpnuyāt |

	grahītṛdravyasahitaṃ tatra doṣo na vidyate ||

grahītur iti śeṣaḥ | upakṣādyabhāvād ity abhiprāyaḥ | grahītṛdravyasahitam ity etad upekṣādyabhāvaniścāyakatvenoktam | nikṣiptamātrasyāpi kāraṇāntareṇopakṣādyabhāve niścite grahītur doṣo na vidyata ity avagantavyam | daivarājagrahaṇaṃ grahītṛsamādheyanimittopalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	arājadaivikenāpi nikṣiptaṃ yatra nāśitam |

	grahītuḥ saha bhāṇḍena dātur naṣṭaṃ tad ucyate ||

bhāṇḍena arthenety arthaḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	grahītuḥ saha yo 'rthena naṣṭo naṣṭaḥ sa dāyinaḥ |

	daivarājakṛte tadvan na cet tat jihmakāritam ||

tat graḥtrarthena saha pradhvaṃsanaṃ kūṭakāritaṃ na ced ity antyapādasyārthaḥ | dāyinaḥ sa naṣṭa iti vadatā vacanabhaṅgyā grahītā mūlyadvāreṇa na dāpyo naṣṭaṃ dhanam ity uktam | uktaṃ ca yājñavalkyena |

	na dāpyo 'pahṛtaṃ tat tu rājadaivikataskaraiḥ | iti |

daivikapadasyārtho manunā spaṣṭatvenoktaḥ |

	corair hṛtaṃ jalenoḍham agninā dagdham eva ca |

	na dadyād yadi tasmāt sa na saṃharati kiṃcana ||

tasmād dhanād yadi stokam api na gṛhṇātīty arthaḥ | upanidhigrahītary apy uktaṃ tenaiva |

	samudrān nāpnuyāt kiṃcit yadi tasmān na saṃharet | iti | (MDh 8.188)

evaṃ nyāsagrahītary apy upekṣādyabhāve draṣṭavyam, asabhyatvābhāvāt | "samudrān nāpnuyāt" iti vacanāntareṇa pṛthagupanidhāv abhidhānaṃ prapañcarucitveneti mantavyam | kvacid yena kenacid dhetunā naṣṭam api grahītā mūlyadvāreṇa na dāpya ity āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	jñātvā dravyaviyogaṃ tu dātā yatra vinikṣipet |

	sarvvopāyavināśe 'pi grahītā naiva dapyate ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ sabhyabhūtagrahītṛviṣayāṇi**

**atha sabhyābhāsabhūtagrahītṛviṣayāṇi**

tatra kātyāyanaḥ |

	nikṣiptaṃ yasya yat kiṃcit tat prayatnena pālayet |

	daivarājakṛtād anyo vināśas tasya kīrtyate ||

yasya pārśve yat sthāpitaṃ tat tenāvahitena pālanīyam, yato daivarājakṛtād anyo vināśādis tasya grāhakasya doṣeṇa kṛtatvena kīrtyata ity arthaḥ na kevalaṃ duṣkīrtir eva kiṃ tu vastuvṛttyā svadoṣād vināśādau jāte bahvarthahāniś cety āha sa eva |

	yasya doṣeṇa yat kiṃcid vināśyeta hriyeta vā |

	tad dravyaṃ sodayaṃ dāpyo daivarājakṛtād vinā ||

upakṣādilakṣaṇo 'tra doṣo 'bhimataḥ | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	bhedenopekṣayā nyāsaṃ grahītā yadi nāśayet |

	yācyamāno na dadyād vā dāpyas tat sodayaṃ bhavet ||

nāśe mūlyadvāreṇa dāpyaḥ | anāśe tu svarūpata eva | akṛtavṛddhiprakaraṇe sāmānyenoktaṃ vṛddhiparimāṇaṃ nāśe grāhyam, adāne tu,

	yācyamāno na ced dadyād vardhate pañcakaṃ śatam |

iti viśeṣeṇa tatraivoktaṃ (?) grāhyam | bhedenopekṣayeti vadan svīyadravyeṇa sahaivopekṣayā nāśe tu sodayavidhir neti darśayati | tena "tatra samaṃ dāpya upekṣitaḥ" iti smṛtyantravihitaṃ mūlamātram eva deyam | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	yācitānantaraṃ nāśe daivarājakṛte 'pi saḥ |

	grahītā pratidāpyaḥ syāt ............ || iti |

mūlamātram iti śeṣaḥ | pratyarpaṇavilambamātrāparādhe savṛddhikadāpanāyogāt | rājñe ca tatsamo deyaḥ, tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	yācamānas tu yo dātuṃ nikṣepaṃ na prayacchati |

	daṇḍyaḥ sa rājño bhavati naṣṭe dāpyaś ca tatsamam ||

naṣṭa ity atra daivād rājato veti śeṣo 'dhyāhāryaḥ | yaḥ punaḥ sthāpitadhād vyayaṃ kurute, upabhogaṃ vā, lābhārthaṃ prayogaṃ vā | tatrāpy āha sa eva |

	yatrārthaṃ sādhayet tena nikṣeptur ananujñayā |

	tatrāpi daṇḍyaḥ sa bhavet taṃ ca sodayam āvahet ||

sādhitārthānusāreṇa daṇḍyaḥ | yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	ājīvan svecchayā daṇḍyo dāpyas tac cāpi sodayam | iti |

ājīvan upajīvan | svecchayā upanidhātrananujñayā | tacchabdenopanidhir atra parāmṛśyate, prakṛtatvāt | bṛhaspatir api |

	nyāsadravyeṇa yaḥ kaścit sādhayet kāryam ātmanaḥ |

	daṇḍyaḥ sa rājño bhavati dāpyas tac cāpi sodayam ||

sādhayet svāmyananujñayeti śeṣaḥ | svāmyanujñayā tu sādhayato na doṣa iti prācīnavacaneṣv evārthād avagamyate | kātyāyano 'pi |

	nyāsādikaṃ paradravyaṃ prabhakṣitam upekṣitam |

	ajñānanāśitaṃ caiva yena dāpyaḥ sa eva tat ||

atra viśeṣam āha vyāsaḥ |

	bhakṣite sodayaṃ dāpyaḥ samaṃ dāpya upekṣite |

	kiṃcin nyūnaṃ pradāpyaḥ syād dravyam ajñānanāśitam ||

kiṃcin nyūnam ity asya pādāṃśahīnam ity artho grāhya iti kaiścid uktam | bhakṣītavad apahṛtaṃ dapyaḥ, "nikṣepāpahārī vṛddhisahitaṃ dhanaṃ dhanikasya dāpyaḥ" iti viṣṇusmaraṇāt | atra daṇḍam api dāpyaḥ,

	nikṣepasyāpahartāraṃ tatsamaṃ dāpayed dhamam |

	tathopanidhihartāraṃ viśeṣeṇaiva pārthivaḥ ||

iti manusmaraṇāt | apahnave tv avṛddhikam eva sādhitaṃ dāpya ity āha vyāsaḥ |

	nikṣepaṃ nihnute yas tu naro bandhubalānvitaḥ |

	sākṣibhir vātha divyena vibhāvya pratidāpyate ||

bṛhaspatis tu daṇḍadāpanam apy āha |

	gṛhītvāpahnute yatra sākṣibhiḥ śapathena vā |

	vibhāvya dāpayen nyāsaṃ tatsamaṃ vinayaṃ tathā ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ sabhyābhāsabhūtahratītṛviṣayāṇi**

**atha grhītṛsthāpakādikṛtyaviṣayāṇi**

atra grahītāraṃ praty āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	sthāpitaṃ yena vidhinā yena yac ca yathāvidhi |

	tathaiva tasya tad deyaṃ na deyaṃ pratyanantare ||

sthāpaketarasya yasya sthāpitadravye svāmyam asti saḥ iha pratyanantara ity ucyate | sthāpakaṃ praty āha manuḥ |

	yo yathā nikṣiped dhaste yam arthaṃ yasya mānavaḥ |

	sa tathaiva grahītavyo yathā dāyas tathā grahaḥ ||

dāyo dānaṃ sthāpanam iti yāvat | graho grahaṇam | etad uktaṃ bhavati: sasākṣikatvena sthāpitaṃ sākṣisamakṣaṃ grahītavyam | rahasi sthāpitaṃ rahasy eva grāhyam iti | kadā grāhyam ity apekṣite kātyāyanaḥ |

	grāhyas tūpanidhiḥ kāle kālahīnaṃ tu varjayet |

	kālahīnaṃ dadad daṇḍaṃ dviguṇaṃ ca pradāpayet ||

yadbhayād upanidhir anyahaste nyastaḥ, tadbhayātīte kāle sa grāhya ity arthaḥ | tadbhayātīte kāle 'pi svayam eva nāyācitam arpaṇīyaṃ "sakṛd yācitam arpayet" iti bṛhaspatismaraṇāt | tadbhaye vartamāne svayam ayācitaṃ dīyamānaṃ kālahīnaṃ tasya dānaṃ dauṣṭyenaiveti dadato daṇḍo yuktaḥ | sthāpakasya dauṣṭye daṇḍam āha manuḥ |

	nikṣepo yaḥ kṛto yena yāvāṃś ca kulasaṃnidhau |

	tāvān eva sa vijñeyo vibruvan daṇḍam arhati ||

kulaṃ sākṣibhūtam | etad uktaṃ bhavati: sasākṣike sākṣivacanaṃ viruddhaṃ bruvan daṇḍya iti | asākṣike tv āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	raho datte nidhau yatra visaṃvādaḥ prajāyate |

	vibhāvakaṃ tatra divyam ubhayor api ca smṛtam ||

nidhāv upanidhau | ubhayor madhya ekasyety arthaḥ | ubhayor grahaṇam "rucyā vānyataraḥ kuryāt" ity ayam eva pakṣo yathā syād iti | pārthivaṃ praty āha manuḥ |

	nikṣepasyāpahartāram anikṣeptāram eva ca |

	sarvair upāyair anvicchec chapathaiś caiva vaidikaiḥ||

	yo nikṣepaṃ nārpayati yaś cānikṣipya yācate |

	tāv ubhau covac chasyau prāpyau tatsamaṃ damam || iti |

coravac chāsyau coradaṇḍena daṇḍyau | coradaṇḍaś ca prathamasāhasa ity uktaṃ manuvṛttau | prādvivākaṃ ca praty āha sa eva |

	teṣāṃ na dadyād yadi tu tad dhiraṇyaṃ yathāvidhi |

	dvayaṃ nigṛhya dāpyaṃ syād iti dharmasya dhāraṇā ||

	nikṣiptasya dhanasaivaṃ prītyopanihitasya ca |

	rājā vinirṇayaṃ kuryād akṣiṇvan nyāsadhāraṇam || iti |

teṣām abhiyoktṝṇām | tad dhiraṇyaṃ tanmūlyahiraṇyam abhiyoktṛbhyo dāpyam | dvayām api dviguṇaṃ nigṛhya daṇdayitvā | akṣiṇvan atāḍayan ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ grahītṛsthāpakādikṛtyaviṣayāṇi**

**atha pratyantare pratyarpaṇapratiṣedhasyāpavādaḥ**

tatra manuḥ |

	svayam eva tu yo dadyān mṛtasya pratyantare |

	na sa rājñābhiyoktavyo na nikṣeptuś ca bandhubhiḥ ||

pācīne prakaraṇe yā pratyantarapadasya vyākhyā kṛtā, sātrāpi draṣṭavyā | anena vacanena vacobhaṅgyā sthāpake mṛte pratyanantare pratyarpaṇaṃ grāhakeṇa kāryam ity uktam | ayācitenārpaṇam apy atra bhāvadoṣaparihārārthatvāt bhūṣaṇaṃ na tu dūṣaṇam ity abhisaṃdhāyoktam "svayam eva tu yo dadyāt" iti | pratyanantare  'pi kālahīnam ayācitena na deyam, bhāvadoṣāpatteḥ | pratyanantarabahutve tu naikasmin pratyanantare deyaṃ sarvaprayanantarasaṃnidhau deyam, tathā sati nikṣeptuḥ bandhubhiḥ pratyanantarabhūtair abhiyoktavyo na bhavati | yadā tu svayam eva na dadāti tadā prayanantaraṃ praty āha sa eva |

	acchalenaiva cānvicchet tam arthaṃ prītipūrvakam |

	vicārya tasya vā vṛttaṃ sāmnaiva parisādhayet ||

anveṣaṇaṃ nikṣepādir asmiñ jane 'stīty avadhāraṇam | svataḥ tad achalenaiva bhūtānusāreṇaiva kāryaṃ na chalānusāreṇa | parisādhanaṃ grāhakasakāśād ādānam | vṛttagrāhakaviṣaye sāmnaiva priyapūrvavacasaiva kāryaṃ na bhayadarśanādinā | vṛttaṃ vicārya durvṛttagrāhakaviṣaye tu chalānusāreṇa vānvicchet | bhayadarśanādyupāyāntareṇa chalādinā vā ṛṇādānaprakaraṇoktena parisādhayed ity asmād eva vacanād avagamyate yathā sadvṛtte chalādiprayogavac chapathena śodhanasyāpy anucitatvam | grāhake tu mṛte paścād yadadhīnam upanidhyādi jātaṃ tenaiva sthāpake pratyanantare vā pratyarpaṇīyam ity etad atisthūlatvāt smṛtikārair upekṣitam ity asmaraṇakāraṇam unneyam | yadi grāhakavad asau svayaṃ na dadāti tadā sthāpakaḥ pratyanantaro vā pūrvoktamārgeṇānvicchet | saṃpratipannaṃ pūrvoktaprakāreṇa parisādhayet | etad api smṛtikārair anuktam ūhenāpi jñātuṃ śakyatvāt ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ pratyanantare pratyarpaṇasya pratiṣedhāpavādaḥ**

**atha yācitānvāhitaviṣayāṇi kānicid vacanāni likhyanta**

tatra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	yācitānvāhitanyāsanikṣepādiṣv ayaṃ vidhiḥ | iti |

yācitam utsavādiṣu parakīyam alaṃkārādyarthaṃ yācitvā svasamīpam ānītam | anvāhitaṃ svasmin sthitaṃ paradhanam anyāntikasthitayā kṛtam | nyāsanikṣepayoḥ svarūpaṃ nikṣepādisthāpanavidhiprakaraṇe darśitam | yady api smṛtyantare nyāsanikṣepayoḥ sthāpanādidharmā upadiṣṭāḥ, tathāpy asyāṃ smṛtau nopadiṣṭā ity upadiṣṭopanidhidharmāṇām atideśo 'yaṃ yuktaḥ | bṛhaspatyādināpy anupadiṣṭadharmakeṣv evānvāhitādiṣv atidiṣṭam |

	anvāhite yācitake śilpanyāse sabandhake |

	eṣa evodito dharmas tathā ca śaraṇāgate || iti |

śilpanyāse kaṅkaṇādikaraṇāya svarṇakārādihastanyastahiraṇyādāv ity arthaḥ | anenāpratiyācitasya śilpanyāsasya daivādinā nāśe svarṇakāraprabhṛtir na dāpya ityādidharmo 'tidiṣṭa iti mantavyam | atra kvacid apavādam āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	yaiś ca saṃskriyate nyāso divasaiḥ pariniścitaiḥ |

	tadūrdhvaṃ sthāpayec chilpī dāpyo daivahate 'pi tam ||

yatra jīrṇāny eva vastrādīni nairmalyādyarthaṃ rajakādau nyastāni nūtanāny eva vā, tannāśaś ca śilpikṛtābhighātādyupetajīrṇatvādidoṣād abhighātādimātrād vā jātaḥ, tatra "yasya doṣeṇa" ityādinoktasodayadāpanam atideśāt prāptam iti vadanti | vastutas tu, jīrṇādau na śilpidoṣaḥ, nairmālyādyarthatvād abhidhātasya (?) | nūtanādau naivam iti śilpī doṣavān | tena jīrṇādau na kiṃcid dāpyaḥ, nūtanādau tu mūlyamātraṃ dāpyam, nairmālyārthād abhighātād adhikāṃśasyaiva doṣatvena svalpadoṣatvāt | etat sarvam abhisaṃdhāyāha sa eva |

	nyāsadoṣād vināśaḥ syāc chilpinaṃ tan na dāpayet |

	dāpayec chilpidoṣāt tat saṃskārārthaṃ yad arpitam ||

śilpidoṣād ity atra vināśaḥ syād ity anuṣajyate | yatra tantvādikaṃ vastrādyarthaṃ kuvindādau nyastaṃ khaṇḍapaṭādidaśāyāṃ naṣṭaṃ paripūrṇadaśāyāṃ vā kuvindādinā dīyamānaṃ svāminā na gṛhītaṃ naṣṭaṃ ca, tatrāpy āha sa eva |

	svalpenāpi ca yat karma naṣṭaṃ ced bhṛtakasya tat |

	paryāptaṃ ditsatas tasya vinaśyet tad agṛhṇataḥ ||

yat karma vastranirmāṇādi svalpenāpi prāntavānādinā vikalaṃ naṣṭaṃ cet bhṛtakasya śilpina eva naṣṭaṃ punar vetanagrahaṇam antareṇaiva vānādikriyāṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | yadi svāmī punas tantvādikaṃ nārpayati tadā punar vānādyabhāve 'pi vetanaṃ śilpine dattaṃ na labhate | paryāptaṃ paripūrṇaṃ vastrādikaṃ ditsato bhṛtasya yaḥ svāmī tasya dīyamānam agṛhṇatas tat paryāptaṃ vinaśyed ity uttarārdhasyārthaḥ | evaṃ cātra bhṛtako naṣṭaṃ na dāpya iti vacobhaṅgyā bhaṇitam ity avagantavyam | evaṃ śilpinyāsaviṣaye viśeṣam uktvā yācitaviṣaye 'py āha sa eva |

	yadi tat kāryam uddiśya kālaṃ pariniyamya vā |

	yācito 'rdhakṛte tasminn aprāpte na tu dāpyate ||

tātparyaṃ tāvad ucyate |

	yācyamāno na dadyād vā dāpyas tat sodayaṃ bhavet |

ity ayaṃ dharmo 'tideśād yācitake prāpto 'nena kvacit pratiṣidhyate | pratiṣedhavacanasyāyam arthaḥ: yat kāryaṃ dīrghakālasādhyaṃ tat kāryamadhye yadi yācitaḥ yadi vā saṃvatsaraparyantaṃ dīyatām ity evaṃ kālaṃ pariniyamya yācitaḥ, tasmin kāryamadhye pariniyatakālamadhye vā pratiyācyamāno yācitakaṃ yo na dadāti, asau na sodayaṃ dāpya iti | yācitakamātram evāsau kṛte kārye pariniyatakālātyaye vā dadyāt | yadi tadāpi na dadāti tadā daivādito vināśe haraṇe vā jāte mūlyaṃ deyam ity āha sa eva |

	prāptakāle kṛte kārye na dadyād yācito 'pi san |

	tasmin naṣṭe hṛte vāpi grahītā mūlyam āharet ||

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span>,

	yācitānantaraṃ nāśe daivarājakṛte 'pi saḥ |

	grahītā pratidāpyaḥ syāt ......... ||

ityādismṛtyā mūlyamātradāpanam upadiṣṭam ihātideśenaiva prāptam, kim artham iha punar upadiśyate | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span>, smṛtyantarād daṇḍo py evaṃ prāptas tannivṛttyartham ihāpy uktam | kvacid aprāpte 'pi kāle kāryamadhye 'pi yācitakaṃ dāpya ity āha sa eva |

	atha kāryavipattis tu tasyaiva svāmino bhavet |

	aprāpte vai sa kāle tu dāpyas tv ardhakṛte 'pi tat ||

yācitakasvāmikāryavipattir apratidāne cen madhye 'pi pratiyācito yācitakaṃ dāpya ity arthaḥ | yadi madhye na dadāti tadātra sodayaṃ dapyaḥ, ātideśikasyāpi pratiṣedhakopadeśābhāve grāhyatvāt | sthāpakapārthivayoḥ kṛtyam atideśād yācitake prāptam api sāmādyupāyaprayoganivṛttyartham āha sa eva |

	yo yācitakam ādāya na dadyāt pratiyācitaḥ |

	sa nigṛhya balād dāpyo daṇḍyaś ca na dadāti yaḥ ||

nigṛhya balād upavāsādi kārayitvā sthāpakena dāpyo dānonmukhaṃ kṛtvā grāhyaḥ | evam api yadi na dadāti, sa rājñā dāpyo daṇḍyaś cety arthaḥ | sthāpake mṛte svayam eva pratiyācanābhāve 'pi bhāvadoṣaparihārārthaṃ pratyanantare dadyād ity etad yācitake 'py atidiṣṭadharmavargāntargatatvena prāptam apy avaśyānuṣṭheyaṃ na bhavatīty āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	yācitaṃ svāmyanujñātaṃ pradadan nāparādhnuyāt | iti |

yācanād ūrdhvam apīti śeṣaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ yācitānvāhitaviṣayāṇi **

**samāptaṃ ca nikṣepākhyapadasya vidhivitānam**

**atha saṃbhūyasamutthānākhyasya padasya vidhir ucyate**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	kulīnadakṣānalasaiḥ prājñair nāṇakavedibhiḥ |

	āyavyayajñaiḥ śucibhiḥ śūraiḥ kuryāt saha kriyām ||

vāṇijyakṛṣiśikpakratusaṅgītastainyātmikām ity arthaḥ | tatra vāṇijyakriyā nāṇakavedibhir āyavyayajñaiḥ saṃbhūya kāryā, kṛṣikriyā tv āyavyayajñaiḥ, śilpakriyā saṅgītakriyā ca prājñaiḥ, kratukriyā kulīnaiḥ prājñaḥ śucibhiḥ, stainyakriyā śūraiḥ, vāṇijyādiṣaḍvidhāpi kriyā dakṣaiḥ analasaiś cety avagantavyam | dakṣānalasagrahaṇaṃ bhāgyādhikavyādhyapīḍitānāṃ pradarśanārtham | nāṇakavedigrahaṇaṃ cāḍhyānām | ata evādakṣālasapratiṣedhaṃ kurvan mandabhāgyādīn api sa eva pratiṣedhayati |

	aśaktālasarogārtamandabhāgyanirāśrayaiḥ |

	vāṇijyādyāḥ sahaitais tu na kartavyā budhaiḥ kriyāḥ || iti |

āśrayo mūladhanam | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	phalahetor upāyena karma saṃbhūya kurvatām |

	ādhārabhūtaḥ prakṣepa uttiṣṭheraṃs tato 'ṃśataḥ ||

ādhārabhūta āśrayabhūtaḥ | prakṣepo mūladhanaprakṣepaḥ | tato mūladhanaprakṣepānusārād uttiṣṭheran lābhabhājo bhaveyur ity arthaḥ | hānyādikam apy evam evety āha sa eva |

	samo 'tirikto hīno vā yatrāṃśo yasya yādṛśaḥ |

	kṣayavyayau tathā viṛddhiḥ tatra tasya tathāvidhāḥ ||

kṣayavyayau vṛddhir ity ete prakṣiptāṃśānusāreṇa veditavyā ity arthaḥ | bṛhaspatir api |

	prayogaṃ kurvate ye tu hemadhānyarasādinā |

	samanyūnādhikair aṃśair lābhas teṣāṃ tathāvidhaḥ ||

lābhavad eva karmavyayāv apīty āha sa eva |

	samo nyūnādhiko vāṃśo yena kṣiptas tathaiva saḥ |

	vyayaṃ dadyāt karma kuryāl lābhaṃ gṛhṇīta caiva hi ||

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	samavāyena vaṇijāṃ lābhārthaṃ karma kurvatām |

	lābhālābau yathādravyaṃ yathā vā saṃvidā kṛtau ||

samavāyena mūlyadravyasaṃsargeṇa yathādravyaṃ saṃsṛṣṭadravyavartitattadaṃśabhūtadravyānusāreṇa lābhālābhau jñeyāv ity arthaḥ | saṃvidā samayena kṛtau kalpitau, puruṣānusāreṇa kalpitau lābhālābhau jñeyāv iti yāvat | vyāsas tu saṃbhūtakāriṇāṃ kāryam āha |

	samakṣam asamakṣaṃ vāvañcayantaḥ parasparam |

	nānāpuṇyānusārāt te prakuryuḥ krayavikrayau ||

	agopayanto bhāṇḍāni śulkaṃ dadyuś ca te 'dhvani |

	anyathā dviguṇaṃ dāpyāḥ śulkasthānād bahiḥsthitāḥ || iti |

nārado 'pi |

	bhāṇḍapiṇḍavyayoddhārabhārasārānvekṣaṇam |

	kuryus te 'vyabhicāreṇa samaye sve vyavasthitāḥ 

atha vā sarvānujñayā sarveṣāṃ kāryam eka eva kuryāt | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	bahūnāṃ saṃmato yas tu dadyād eko dhanaṃ rahaḥ |

	karaṇaṃ kārayed vāpi sarvair eva kṛtaṃ bhavet ||

karaṇaṃ lekhyādikam | saṃbhūyakāriṇāṃ mitho vivāde 'py āha sa eva |

	parīkṣakāḥ sākṣiṇaś ca te evoktāḥ parasparam |

	saṃdigdhe 'rthe vañcanāyāṃ no ced vidveṣasaṃyutāḥ ||

yadā tu vidveṣasaṃyuktās tadāpy āha sa eva |

	yaḥ kaścid vañcakas teṣāṃ vijñātaḥ krayavikraye |

	śapathaiḥ sa viśodhyaḥ syāt sarvavāde 'py ayaṃ vidhiḥ ||

viśodhyaḥ sabhyair iti śeṣaḥ | sarvavāde 'pi vañcanetaravivāde 'pīty arthaḥ | vañcakatve siddhe sati kiṃ kāryam ity apekṣite yājñavalkyaḥ: "jihmaṃ tyajeyur nirlābham" iti | jihmaṃ vañcakaṃ nirlābhaṃ lābhahīnaṃ kṛtvā tyajeyuḥ | bahiḥsthitāḥ itare saṃbhūyakāriṇa ity arthaḥ | saṃbhūyakāriṣv asamarthaṃ praty āha sa eva: "aśakto 'nyena kārayet" iti | svāṃśaānurūpaṃ karmeti śeṣaḥ | bṛhaspatis tu sarvān praty āha |

	kṣayahānir yadā tatra daivarājakṛtā bhavet |

	sarveṣām eva sā proktā kalpanīyā yathāṃśataḥ ||

saṃbhūyakāribhiḥ sarvair iti śeṣaḥ | kṣayāyaiva hāniḥ upacayārthavyatiriktā hānir iti yāvat | daivarājagrahaṇaṃ prātisvikadoṣetaranimittopalakṣaṇārtham | prātisvikadoṣād dhānau tv āha sa eva |

	anirdiṣṭo vāryamāṇāḥ pramādād yas tu nāśayet |

	tenaiva tad bhaved deyaṃ sarveṣāṃ samavāyinām ||

anirdiṣṭaḥ samavāyānanujñātaḥ svabuddhyaiva kurvan samavāyidravyaṃ yo nāśayet, nivāryamāṇo vā samavāyibhiḥ ity ādyapadārthaḥ | pramādaḥ prajñāhīnatā sā prātisvikadoṣopalakṣaṇārthatayātroktā | tena kāmakrodhalobhādy api samutthānanāśanimittabhūtaṃ sarvam evātroktam iti mantavyam | yas tv ityādivacanaśeṣaṃ sugamam | pālane 'py āha sa eva |

	devarājabhayād yas tu svaśaktyā paripālayet |

	tasyāṃśaṃ daśamaṃ datvā gṛhṇīyas te 'ntataḥ pare ||

tasya tasmai daśamam aṃśaṃ dadyuḥ | te samavāyinaḥ | pālayet samavāyidravyam iti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	corataḥ salilād agner dravyaṃ yas tu samāharet |

	tasyāṃśo daśamo deyaḥ sarvavādeṣv ayaṃ vidhiḥ ||

samāharet svaśaktyā pratyāhared ity arthaḥ | asamavāyidravyapālane 'py ayaṃ vidhir vijñeya ity antyapādārthaḥ | adhamarnādibhyo datte yas tu pratiyācanādinā samavāyidravyaṃ samavāyibhiḥ saha na sādhayati tasya lābhahānir ity āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	samavetais tu yad dattaṃ prārthanīyaṃ tathaiva tat |

	na yācate ca yaḥ kaścil lābhāt sa parihīyate ||

yācanagrahaṇm aṃśānusāreṇa karaṇīyakarmaṇaḥ pradarśanārtham | tena karmāntarākaraṇe 'py akaraṇānusāreṇa lābhahānir ity asmād eva vacanāt pratipattavyam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ saṃbhūyakāriṇāṃ viṇijāṃ vidhayaḥ**

**atha saṃbhūyakāriṇāṃ kṛṣikāṇāṃ vidhayaḥ**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	vāhyakarṣakabījādyaiḥ kṣetropakaraṇena ca |

	ye samānās tu taiḥ sārdhaṃ kṛṣiḥ kāryā vijānatā ||

vāhyā lāṅgalādivāhakāḥ balīvardāḥ | karṣakāḥ kṛṣyarthaṃ svīkṛtāḥ puruṣāḥ | ādyaśabdena kṛṣyarthasya dhanasya grahaṇam | vāhyeṣu varjanīyān āha sa eva |

	kṛśātivṛddhaṃ kṣudraṃ ca rogiṇaṃ prapalāyinam |

	kāṇaṃ khañjaṃ ca nādadyād vāhyaṃ prājñaḥ kṛṣīvalaḥ ||

kāṇa ekākṣaḥ | khañjo hīnacaraṇaḥ | kṣetreṣu varjanīyam āha sa eva |

	parvate nagarābhyāśe tathā rājapathasya ca |

	ūṣaraṃ mūṣikāvyāptaṃ kṣetraṃ yatnena varjayet ||

parvate parvatānte | nagarābhyāśe nagarasamīpe | rājapathasya ca samīpa iti śeṣaḥ | etad uktaṃ bhavati: parvatādyāsannam, anāsannam py ūṣaraṃ mūṣikāvyāptaṃ ca kṣetraṃ varjayed iti | lābhavibhāgadikaṃ yat saṃbhūyavāṇijyakṛṣyādikarmaṇām asādhāraṇaṃ pūrvasmin prakaraṇe darśitaṃ tad apy atrāpy anusaṃdheyam | pūrvatra darśitāt prātisvikadoṣād doṣāntarenāpy ekasyāhānim āha sa eva |

	vāhyabījātyayād yasya kṣetrahāniḥ prajāyate |

	tenaiva sā pradātavyā sarveṣāṃ kṛṣijīvinām ||

saṃbhūyakāriṇām iti śeṣaḥ | vāhyabījagrahaṇaṃ kṛṣisādhanānām upalakṣaṇārtham iti mantavyam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ saṃbhūyakāriṇāṃ kṛṣikāṇāṃ vidhayaḥ**

**atha saṃbhūyakāriṇāṃ śilpināṃ vidhayaḥ**

śilpisvarūpanirūpaṇārtham āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	hiraṇyakupyasūtrāṇāṃ kāṣṭhapāṣāṇacarmaṇām |

	saṃskartā ca kalābhijñaḥ śilpī prokto manīṣibhiḥ ||

kupyaṃ hemarūpyavyatiriktaṃ trapusīsādikam | hemarūpye prakṛtya "tābhyāṃ yad anyat tat kupyam" ity amarasiṃhenoktam | śilpināṃ lābhasya vibhāgam āha sa eva |

	hemakārādayo yatra śilpaṃ saṃbhūya kurvate |

	karmānurūpaṃ nirveśaṃ labheraṃs te yathāṃśataḥ ||

nirveśo bhṛtiḥ | kātyāyano 'pi |

	śikṣakābhijñakuśalā ācāryaś ceti śilpinaḥ |

	ekadvitricaturbhāgān hareyus te yathottaram ||

kāṣṭhādimayaharmyādinirmātṝṇāṃ mukhyasya bhāgam āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	harmyaṃ devagṛhaṃ cāpi cārmikopaskarāṇi ca |

	saṃbhūya kurvatāṃ caiṣāṃ pramukho dvyaṃśam arhati ||

avañcakatvena karmakaraṇādidharmajātaṃ yat pūrvataraprakaraṇe darśitaṃ tad apy atrāpy anusaṃdheyam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ saṃbhūyakāriṇāṃ śilpināṃ vidhayaḥ**

**atha saṃbhūyakāriṇām ṛtvijāṃ vidhayaḥ**

tatra manuḥ |

	ṛtvijaḥ samavetās tu yathā satre nimantritāḥ |

	kuryur yathārhataḥ karma gṛhṇīyur dakṣiṇāṃ tathā ||

atra satraśabdo yajñamātravivakṣayā prayukto na punaḥ satrākhyayajñaviśeṣavivakṣayā, tatra yajamānānām eva kartṛtvena ṛtvijām asaṃbhavāt | tena somayāgādāv anena vacanena vyāpāralābhāv uktau | tatraiva lābhavibhāgābhidhānārtham āha sa eva |

	saṃbhūya svāni karmāṇi kurvadbhir iha mānavaiḥ |

	anena karmayogena kartavyāṃśaprakalpanā ||

svāni karmāṇi yājamānavyatiriktānīti śeṣaḥ | aṃśaprakalpanā ca "tasya dvādaśaśataṃ dakṣiṇā" ity evam ṛtusaṃbandhimātratayā vihitāyāṃ dakṣiṇāyām eva na tu "ratham adhvaryave, nividāṃ varam aśvaṃ hotram, brahmaṇe 'śvam ādhāne, subrahmaṇyāya somakraye śakaṭam" ity evam ṛtvigviśeṣasaṃbandhitvena vihitāyām, śrutivirodhāpatteḥ | ata evoktaṃ tenaiva |

	rathaṃ hareta cādhvaryuḥ brahmādhāne ca vājinam |

	hotā nividvaraṃ cāśvam udgātā cāpy anaḥ kraye ||

ṛtvigviśeṣollekhena vihitāṃśaṃ sa eva gṛhṇīyād ity arthaḥ | pūrṇāhutau hutāyāṃ varaṃ dadyād ity aṅgakarmollekhena yā dakṣiṇā vihitāḥ, tāḥ pray āha sa eva |

	yasya karmaṇi yās tu syur uktāḥ pratyaṅgadakṣiṇāḥ |

	sa eva tā ādadīta bhajeran sarva eva vā ||

yasya karmaṇi yatkartṛke karmaṇi yā dakṣiṇā uktāḥ sa eva tatkarmaṇi tā ādadītety arthaḥ | evaṃ ca pūrṇāhutāv adhvaryur varaṃ gṛhṇīyāt, tatra tasya kartṛtvāt | "bhajeran sarva eva vā" iti pakṣāntaram anekakartṛkāṅgadakṣiṇāviṣayam, tena stotradakṣiṇāḥ stotrakāriṇa eva chandogā bhajeran | pradhānadakṣiṇāsv aṃśaprakalpanāyāḥ prakāram āha sa eva |

	sarveṣām ardhino mukhyās tadardhenārdhino 'pare |

	tṛtīyinas tṛtīyāṃśāś caturthāṃśās tu pādinaḥ ||

mukhyā gaṇādyā brahmādayaḥ | apare gaṇināṃ dvitīyāḥ pratiprathātrādayaḥ | tṛtīyinaḥ gaṇināṃ tṛtīyāḥ pratihartrādayaḥ | pādino gaṇināṃ caturthāḥ grāvastudādayaḥ pratyetavyāḥ | tataś cāyam arthaḥ: sarveṣām ṛtvijāṃ madhye ardhino vihitadakṣiṇārdhavanto mukhyāḥ | ardhaśabdo 'tra kiṃcinnyūnadakṣiṇārdhe vartate | tadardhena kiṃcinnyūnadakṣiṇārdhasyārdhenāpare gaṇino dvitīyāḥ ardhino 'rdhavantaḥ | tṛtīyinas tṛtīyāṃśāḥ kiṃcinnyūnadikṣiṇārdhasya tṛtīyāṃśabhāginaḥ | pādinas tu kiṃcinnyūnadakṣiṇārdhasya caturthāṃśabhāginaḥ | evaṃ ca śatadakṣiṇāpakṣe caturṇāṃ mukhyānām aṣṭacatvāriṃśat gāvo bhavanti, tadanantarāṇāṃ caturṇāṃ caturviṃśatigāvaḥ, tadanantarāṇāṃ caturṇāṃ ṣodaśa gāvaḥ, tadanantarāṇāṃ dvādaśa gāva iti mantavyam | mukhyānāṃ caturṇāṃ mitho vibhāgaḥ samatvenaiva | evam eva tadanantarādīnām api mitho vibhāgaḥ | tathā ca kātyāyanasūtram: "dvādaśadvādaśādyebhyaḥ, ṣaṭ ṣaṭ dvitīyebhyaḥ, catasraś cataras tṛtīyebhyaḥ, tisras tisra itarebhyaḥ" iti | paśubandhādau viṣamavibhāgānabhidhānāt samatvenaiva vibhāgo jñeyaḥ | svakīyakarmakalāpāṃśakartuḥ kṛtānusāreṇa bhāgo deya ity āha manuḥ |

	ṛtvig yadi vṛto yajñe svakarma paribhāvayet |

	tasya karmānusāreṇa deyo 'ṃśaḥ saha kartṛbhiḥ ||

kartṛbhiḥ saṃbhūyakāribhir ity arthaḥ | yad vā kartṛbhiḥ saha deyo dakṣiṇādānakāle deyo yajamānenety arthaḥ | atha vā karmaṇi ṛtvikparityaktāṃśakartṛbhiḥ saha deya ity arthaḥ | etad uktaṃ bhavati: svakarmaikadeśakartur yā dakṣiṇā tāṃ tasya caikadeśāntarakartuś ca dakṣiṇākāle saṃbhūyakārisaṅgho yajamāno vā tatkṛtakarmānuśareṇārpayed iti | asya kvacid apavādam āha sa eva |

	dakṣiṇāsu ca dattāsu svakarma paribhāvayet |

	kṛtsnam eva labhetāṃśam anyenaiva ca kāreyet ||

anyena svagaṇavartināṃ madhye pratyāsannena | yena kenacid anyena vā kāryamāṇe tv ādhvaryavādisamākhyāvādhāpatteḥ | evam ṛtviji mṛte 'py ūhyam | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	ṛtvijāṃ vyasane 'py evam anyas tatkarma nistaret |

	labheta dakṣiṇābhāgaṃ sa tasmāt saṃprakalpitam ||

anyaśabdārthaḥ pūrvavad ihāpi draṣṭavyaḥ | yat tu bṛhaspatinoktam,

	evaṃ kriyāpravṛttānāṃ yadā kaścid vipadyate |

	tadbandhunā kriyā kāryā sarvair vā sahakāribhiḥ || iti |

yac ca śaṅkhena, "tatra ced anuprāpte savanam ṛtviṅ mriyeta tasya gotro 'sya śiṣyo vā tatkāryam anupūrayed atha ced abāndhavas tato 'nyam ṛtvijaṃ vṛṇuyāt" iti, tat sarvam avāntaragaṇaśūnyaṛtvikkartṛkayajñaviṣayam iti mantavyam | jīvaty eva ṛtviji yajamānena ṛtvigantarakaraṇe kasya dakṣiṇeti vivādāpanodārtham āha sa eva: "atha ṛtviji vṛte paścād anyaṃ vṛṇuyāt pūrvāhūtasyaiva dakṣiṇā paścād āhūtaḥ kiṃcil labheta" iti ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ saṃbhūyakāriṇām ṛtvijāṃ vidhayaḥ**

**atha saṃbhūyakāriṇāṃ nartakādīnāṃ stenādīnāṃ ca vidhayaḥ**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	nartakānām eṣa eva dharmaḥ sadbhir udāhṛtaḥ |

	tālajño labhate 'dhardhaṃ gāyanās tu samāṃśinaḥ ||

eṣa dharmaḥ śilpimukhyasyokto dharmaḥ | tenāyam arthaḥ: "pramukho dvyaṃsam arhati" it iyo 'yaṃ saṃbhūya harmyādikaṃ karvatāṃ śilpināṃ mikhyasyoktaḥ sa eva dharmo dvyaṃśabhagitvarūpo nartakā dīnāṃ saṃbhūya nṛttādikaṃ kurvatāṃ mukhyasya sadbhir udāhṛta iti | adhyardham ardhādhikaṃ bhāgaṃ tālajño labhate | stenān api praty āha sa eva |

	svāmyājñayā tu yac coraiḥ paradeśāt samāhṛtam |

	rājñe datvā tu ṣaḍbhāgaṃ bhajeyus te yathāṃśataḥ ||

	caturo'ṃśān bahen mukhyaḥ śūras tryaṃśam avāpnuyāt |

	samarthas tu hared dvyaṃśaṃ śeṣāt tv anye samāṃśinaḥ ||

paradeśāt vairideśād ity arthaḥ | pravalataravairideśād āhṛtaviṣayam etat | durbalavairideśāhṛtaviṣaye tv āh kātyāyanaḥ |

	pararāṣṭrād dhanaṃ yat syāc coraiḥ svāmyājñayā hṛtam |

	rājño daśāṃśam uddhṛtya vibhajeran anyathāvidhi ||

	corāṇāṃ mukhyabhūtas tu caturo'ṃśāṃs tato haret |

	śūro 'ṃśāṃs trīn samartho dvau śeṣās tv ekaikam eva ca ||

samarthaḥ śaktaḥ | eteṣāṃ hānir apy evam evety āha sa eva |
