	teṣāṃ cet prasṛtānāṃ yo grahaṇaṃ samavāpnuyāt |

	tanmokṣaṇārthaṃ yad dattaṃ vaheyus te yathāṃśataḥ ||

nanu saṃbhūyakāriṇāṃ samayānusārata evāṃśakalpanayā lābhahānyor vibhāgo bhaviṣyatīti vyarthā vibhāgavidhaya ity āśaṅkyāha sa eva |

	vaṇijāṃ karṣakāṇāṃ ca corāṇāṃ śilpināṃ tathā |

	aniyamyāṃśakartṝṇāṃ sarveṣām eṣa nirṇayaḥ ||

lābhahānyoḥ samayena pratipuruṣam aṃśam aniyamya vāṇijyaādikartṝṇām ity arthaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandriyāyāṃ saṃbhūyakāriṇāṃ nartakādīnāṃ stenādīnāṃ ca vidhayaḥ**

**samāptaṃ ca saṃbhūyasamutthānākhyapadasya vidhivitānam**

**atha dattāpradānikākhyasya padasya vidhir ucyate**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	eṣākhilenābhihitā saṃbhūyotthānaniṣkṛtiḥ |

	adeyadeyadattānām adattasya ca kathyate ||

adeyādīnāṃ svarūpam adhunā kathyata ity arthaḥ | tatra tāvad adeyasya svarūpabhedau kathayati |

	sāmānyaṃ putradārādhisarvasvanyāsayācitam |

	pratiśrutaṃ tathānyasya na deyaṃ tv aṣṭadhā smṛtam ||

sāmānyaṃ svam anekasvāmikaṃ rathyādy atra vivakṣitam, an tv avibhaktakuṭumbasvāmikaṃ kanakādikam, tasya deyatvena vakṣyamāṇatvāt | yady api anekasvāmikatvena rathyādikam api kuṭumbadhanatulyam, tathāpi svatantrānekasvāmikatvād adeyam | tathā hi: na tāvat svāmyantarānumatim antareṇa kenacit svāminā tad dātuṃ śakyate | svatantrabahusvāmike rathyādāv anumatir durghaṭaiva | kuṭumbadhane tu svatantrakatipayasvāmike 'numatiḥ sulabhaiveti bhedaḥ | nanu putradārasarvasveṣu pitrādisvāmikeṣu dānārheṣu katham adeyatvam | ucyate, yathā yajamānadhanānām api māṣāṇām "ayajñiyā vai māṣāḥ" iti niṣedhaśruter ayajñiyatvam, tathā putradārasarvasvāni svabhūtāny api "deyaṃ dārasutād ṛte | nānvaye sati sarvasvaṃ" ityādidānaniṣedhakasmṛtibalāt adeyāni | ādhinyāsayācitakeṣu tu adeyatvaṃ svatvābhāvād iti mantavyam | anyasmai pratiśrutamanyasmai vācā dattam | yady api vāgdāne svatvaṃ nāpaiti, tathāpi "nānvaye sati sarvasvaṃ yac canyasmai pratiśrutam" it niṣedhasmṛtibalāt sarvasvavad adeyaṃ pratiśrutam apīti mantavyam | sarvasvasyāpy adeyatvam avibhaktānvayadravyasaṃyuktasyaiva, dātuḥ tasyaiva dānaniṣedhāt | tena svasantānavihīnasya svasantānāya dattadāyasya vā sarvasvaṃ deyam | nāradenāpy adeyatvam evam evānvāhitādīnām uktam |

	anvāhitaṃ yācitakam ādiḥ sādhāraṇaṃ ca yat |

	nikṣepaḥ putradāraṃ ca sarvasvaṃ cānvaye sati ||

	āpatsv api hi kaṣṭāsu vartamānena dehinā |

	adeyāny āhur ācāryāḥ yac cānyasmai pratiśrutam || iti |

anvāhitam anyasmai dātum arpitam | anvāhitavat strīdhanam apy adeyam, svatvābhāvāt | ata eva dakṣaḥ |

	sāmānyaṃ yācitaṃ nyāsaḥ ādhir dārāś ca taddhanam |

	anvāhitaṃ nikṣepaḥ sarvasvaṃ cānvaye sati ||

	āpatsv api na deyāni nava vastūni paṇḍitaiḥ |

	yo dadāti sa mūḍhātmā prāyaścittīyate naraḥ || iti |

mūḍhātmā dānānirvartakasāmānyadravyādau tannivartakatvabuddhyā pravartamānatvāt | prāyaścittīyate putradārādidāne 'tikrāntaniṣedhatvāt | evaṃ ca atra pratigrahītāpy asādhur eva, ayuktakāritvāt | ata evobhayor api daṇḍam āha nāradaḥ |

	gṛhṇāty adattaṃ yo mohād yaś cādeyaṃ prayacchati |

	daṇḍanīyāv ubhāv etau dharmajñena mahīkṣitā ||

adattagrahaṇam adeyasyāpy upalakṣaṇārtham | tenādeyapratigrahītur adattapratigrahītuś ca daṇḍo 'nena vacanenokta iti mantavyam | gṛhītasya ca parāvartanam api mahīkṣitā kāryam ity adattādeyagrahaṇād gamyate, adattenādeyena ca dānasiddhyabhāvāt parasvatvānutpatteḥ ||

**iti smṛticandriyāyām adeyaviṣayāṇi**

**atha deyaviṣayāṇi**

atra nāradaḥ |

	kuṭumbabharaṇād dravyaṃ yat kiṃcid atiricyate |

	tad deyam upahatyānyaṃ dadad doṣam avāpnuyāt ||

anyam upahatya bhartavyakuṭumbam uparudhyety arthaḥ | uparodhaś ca niḥsvatayā bhojanācchādanocchedananibandhano 'trābhimato na tu tāmbūlādibhogasādhanavaikalyanibandhanaḥ | yad āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	kuṭumbabhaktavasanād deyaṃ yad atiricyate | iti |

bhaktaṃ bhojanam | vasanam ācchādanam | dhanadhānyādidravyam atra yatpadenoktam | upavanādidravyaṃ tu praty āha sa eva |

	saptārāmagṛhakṣetrād yad yat kṣetraṃ pracīyate |

	pitryaṃ vātha svayaṃ prāptaṃ tad dātavyaṃ vivakṣitam ||

saptabhya ārāmādibhyo yat pracīyate adhikaṃ syāt tad dātavyam iti smṛtiśāstre vivakṣitam ity arthaḥ | yat tu kātyāyanenoktam,

	sarvasvagṛhavarjaṃ tu kuṭumbabharaṇādhikam |

	yad dravyaṃ tat svakaṃ deyam ............. ||

iti, tat saptānadhikagṛhaviṣayam | svakaṃ svakīyaṃ yatheṣṭaviniyogārhadravyam iti yāvat | kathaṃ tarhi putradānam | svasvāmilakṣaṇasaṃbandhābhāvāt kevalaṃ janyajanakalakṣaṇa eva tatra saṃbandha ity āśaṅkyāha vasiṣṭhaḥ: "śuklaśoṇitasaṃbhavaḥ puruṣaḥ mātāpitṛnimittakaḥ, tasya pradānavikrayaparityāgeṣu mātāpitarau prabhavataḥ" iti | utpādanamātreṇa pitṛbhyām ārjitatvāt yatheṣṭaviniyogārhatvaṃ putrasyāpy astīti matvā prabhavata ity uktam | tena putro 'pi deyabhūto bhavatīty abhiprāyaḥ | yat tu smṛtyantaram,

	sutasya sutadārāṇāṃ vaśitvaṃ cānuśāsane |

	vikraye caiva dāne ca vaśitvaṃ na sute pituḥ ||

iti, yac ca yājñavalkyenoktam,

	svakuṭumbāvirodhena deyaṃ dārasutād ṛte |

iti, tad vacanadvayam anekasutaśūnyaviṣayam | tatra hi putradāne kṛte santānavicchedāpatteḥ | ata āha vasiṣṭhaḥ: "na tv ekaṃ putraṃ dadyāt pratigṛhṇīyād vā sa hi santānāya pūrveṣām" iti | anekaputreṣv api mātāpitṛviyogasahanakṣama eva deyaḥ |

	vikrayaṃ caiva dānaṃ ca na neyāḥ syur anicchavaḥ |

	dārāḥ putraś ca ............................ ||

iti kātyāyanasmaraṇāt | yathā dārāḥ vikrayaṃ dānaṃ vā bhartrā na neyās tathā mātṛpitṛbhyāṃ putrā api mātṛpitṛviyogānicchavo na neyāḥ syur ity arthaḥ | "na neyāḥ syur anicchavaḥ" ity etad anāpadviṣayam | 

	āpatkāle tu kartavyaṃ dānaṃ vikraya eva vā |

	anyathā na pravartanta iti śāstraviniścayaḥ ||

iti tān evādhikṛtya tenaivānantaram uktatvāt | yas tu nāradenoktam,

	nikṣepaḥ putradāraṃ ca sarvasvaṃ cānvaye sati |

	āpatsv api hi kaṣṭāsu vartamānena dehinā ||

	adeyāny āhur ācāryāḥ ................. |

iti, tad apy ekaputraviṣayam, anyathā pūrvoktavacanavirodhasya duṣpariharatvāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> mātuḥ prabhutve 'pi putradānam ayuktam, asvatantratvāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span>, svatantrapuruṣānujñayā tu yuktam eva | ata eva vasiṣṭhaḥ: "na strī putraṃ dadyāt pratigṛhṇīyād vānyatrānujñānāt bhartuḥ" iti | kiṃcid bhartrāpi bhāryānujñātam eva deyam, kiṃcin mukhyenāpi bhrātranujñātam eva deyam, kiṃcit svārjitam api dāsena svāmyanujñātam eva deyam | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	saudāyikaṃ kramāyātaṃ śauryaprāptaṃ ca yad bhavet |

	strījñātisvāmyanujñātaṃ dattaṃ siddhim avāpnuyāt ||

saudāyikaṃ vivāhalabdham, tad yasyā vivāhe labdhaṃ tayā bhāryayānujñātam eva deyam, pitāmahādikramāyātaṃ tv avibhaktadhanair jñātibhir anujātam eva deyam, bhṛtyena yuddhalabdhaṃ svāmyanujñātam eva deyam ity arthaḥ | strījñātyanujñātaṃ sāvaśeṣaṃ deyam,

	vaivāhike kramāyāte sarvadānaṃ na vidyate |

iti tenaivoktatvāt | svārjitaṃ tv avibhaktadhanair ananujñātam api deyam, "svayaṃ prāptam" iti tenaivabhihitatvāt | evaṃ ca svārjitaṃ sthāvaram api saptādhikaṃ jñātyananujñātaṃ deyam | yat punas tenaivoktam,

	vibhaktā vāvibhaktā vā dāyādāḥ sthāvare samāḥ |

	eko hy anīśaḥ sarvatra dānādhamanavikraye ||

iti, tat saptānadhikāvibhaktasthāvaraviṣayam | vibhiktā api samāḥ, kiṃ punar avibhaktā iti vyākhyeyam | anyathā vibhāgo 'narthakaḥ syāt | evaṃ ca yad uktaṃ smṛtyantre,

	eko 'pi sthāvare kuryād dānādhamanavikrayam |

	āpatkāle kuṭumbārthe dharmārthe 'pi viśeṣataḥ ||

iti, tat kramāyātavibhaktasthāvaraviṣayaṃ saptānadhikasthāvaraviṣayaṃ ceti mantavyam, apeḥ kākākṣivad ubhayatra saṃbandhāt | yadā pareṇa saṃbandhas tadāyam arthaḥ: sthāvare 'pi sthāvarabahutvābhāve 'pi eko dānādikaṃ kuryād iti | ādhir api dānam, tena rūpeṇa svatvāvagateḥ "bandhācāreṇa bandhakam" iti śravaṇāc ca deyam ity anuṣajyate | evaṃ cādher adeyatvaṃ pūrvasmin prakaraṇe 'bhihitam ādhirūpād rūpāntareṇeti mantavyam | deyoktiprasaṅgād deyasya pratigraḥīṣyataḥ pratigrahaprakāraviśeṣo yājñavalkyena darśitaḥ |

	pratigrahaḥ prakāśaḥ syāt sthāvarasya viseṣataḥ | iti |

prakāśaḥ prakaṭaḥ sasākṣika iti yāvat | putrasya pratigrahe prakāraviśeṣo vasiṣṭhena darśitaḥ: "putraṃ pratigrahīṣyan bandhūn āhūya rājani cāvedya niveśanasya madhye vyāhṛtibhir hutvādūrebāndhavam asaṃnikṛṣṭam eva gṛhṇīyāt" iti | adūrebāndhavaṃ saṃnihitamātulādibandhavam | asaṃnikṛṣṭaṃ saṃnikṛṣṭabhrātṛputrādivyatiriktam eva pratigṛhṇīyād ity arthaḥ | prāsaṅgikam uktvā prakṛtam api yājñavalkyenoktam |

	deyaṃ pratiśrutaṃ caiva datvā nāpaharet punaḥ | iti |

idaṃ te dāsyāmīti vācā yat pratiśrutaṃ tad avaśyaṃ tasmai dātavyam, dattaṃ ca na sarvathā punar apahartavyam ity arthaḥ | yaḥ punaḥ pratiśrutaṃ na dadāti, dattaṃ vāpaharati tasya doṣam āha hārītaḥ |

	pratiśrutārthādānena dattasyocchedanena ca |

	vividhān narakān yāti tiryagyonau ca jāyate ||

pratiśrutārthas tu vinā dānena ṛṇavan nāpaitīty āha sa eva |

	vācaiva yat pratijñātaṃ karmaṇā nopapāditam |

	ṛṇavad dharmasaṃyuktam iha loke paratra ca ||

yad vittaṃ dharmasaṃyuktaṃ pratigrahītṛpravṛttadharmasaṃpattyarthaṃ vācā pratijñānaṃ na paścāt samarpitam, tad iha paratra ca ṛṇavan nāpaitīty arthaḥ | ṛṇavad ity abhidhānenārthād apradāyako dāpyo daṇḍyaś cety uktam | uktaṃ ca kātyāyanena |

	svecchayā yaḥ pratiśrutya brāhmaṇāya pratigraham |

	na dadyād ṛṇavad dāpyaḥ prāpnuyāt pūrvasāhasam ||

brāhmaṇāya pravṛtadharmaparityāgarahitāyeti (?) śeṣaḥ | "pratiśrutyāpy adharmasaṃyukte na dadyāt" iti gautamasmaraṇāt ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ deyaviṣayāṇi**

**atha dattaviṣayāṇi**

tatra nāradaḥ |

	paṇyamūlyaṃ bhṛtis tuṣṭyā snehāt pratyupakārataḥ |

	strīśulkānugrahārthaṃ ca dattaṃ dānavido viduḥ ||

paṇyasya krītadravyasya mūlyam | bhṛtis tu kātyāyanena darśitā |

	avijñātopalabdhyarthaṃ dānaṃ yatra nirūpitam |

	upalabdhakriyālabdhaṃ sā bhṛtiḥ parikīrtitā ||

saprayojanakriyāsaṃpādanārthaṃ dattaṃ bhṛtir ucyata ity arthaḥ | tuṣṭyety anena vandijanādibhyo dattaṃ lakṣyate | snehād ity anena ca duhitrādibhyo dattam | pratyupakārataḥ pratyupakārārtham upakṛtasakāśāl labdham | tatpradarśanārtham āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	bhayatrāṇāya rakṣārthaṃ tathā kāryaprasādhanāt |

	anena vidhinā labdhaṃ vidyāt pratyupakārataḥ ||

bhayatrāṇāya bhayād rakṣaṇāya | rakṣārthaṃ bāladhanādirakṣārtham | kāryaprasādhanāt vivāhādisaṃpādanāt | anena vidhinā labdhaṃ bhayatrāṇādilakṣaṇopakaraṇāl labdham iti yāvat | strīśulkaṃ pariṇayanārthaṃ kanyājñātibhyo dattam | anugrahārthaṃ paropakāraḥ kartavya iti vidhibalād dattam | tatra satpātre 'nugrahād dattaṃ saphalaṃ bhavatīty āha nāradaḥ |

	mātāpitror gurau mitre vinīte copakāriṇi |

	dīnānāthaviśiṣṭebhyo dattaṃ tu saphalaṃ bhavet ||

upakāriṇi paropakārapare | saphalaṃ phalātiśayopetam ity arthaḥ | dattaṃ dānavido viduḥ tad etat paṇyamūlyādi saptavidhaṃ dattam eva dānavido viduḥ, aparāvartanīyaṃ vidur ity arthaḥ | bṛhaspatir api |

	bhṛtyā tuṣṭyā paṇyamūlyaṃ strīśulkam upakāriṇe |

	śraddhānugrāhasaṃprītyā dattam aṣṭavidhaṃ viduḥ ||

upakāriṇe yadi sarvasvam arpyate tadā dattaṃ na bhavatīty āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	prāṇasaṃśayam āpannaṃ yo mām uttārayed itaḥ |

	sarvasvaṃ tasya dāsyāmīty ukte 'pi na tathā bhavet ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ dattaviṣayāṇi**

**athādattaviṣayāṇi**

	adattaṃ tu bhayakrodhaśokavegaruganvitaiḥ |

	tathotkocaparīhāsavyatyāsacchalayogataḥ ||

	bālamūḍhāsvatantrārtamattonmattāpavarjitam |

	kartā mamāyaṃ karmeti pratilābhecchayā ca yat ||

	apātre pātram ity ukte kārye cādharmasaṃhite |

	yad dattaṃ syād avijñānād adattaṃ tad api smṛtam || iti |

etad uktaṃ bhavati: bhayoptaptena bandigrahādibhyo dattam, krodhopataptena krodhaviṣayabhūtānām avibhaktadhanānāṃ dhanavyayaṃ kartum itarebhyo dattam, śokavegādyupataptena kiṃ sthitena dhaneneti tātkalikayā buddhyā dattam, utkocena rājakīyādibhyo dattam, upahāsena dattam, vyatyāsacchalayogataḥ pracchannatayā grahītuṃ parapratāraṇārthaṃ janasamakṣaṃ dattam, aprāptavyavahāreṇa dattam, mūḍhena manasi sthitād anyasmai dattam, asvatantreṇa dāsādinā dattam, ārtena rogopahataprakṛtinā dattam, mattena dhuttūrādibhakṣaṇaskhalitadhiyā dattam, unmattena pittodrekādinā skhalitadhiyā dattam, karmakaraṇārthaṃ satkārarūpeṇākarmakarāya dattam, pratilābhecchayā pratilābham akurvāṇāya dattam, ayogyāya yogyoktimātreṇa dattam, asadviniyogakāriṇe sadviniyogakṛd ity uktimātreṇa dattam ity evaṃ ṣoḍaśaprakāram api punaḥpratyāharaṇīyatvād adattam ity ucyata iti | punaḥpratyāharaṇīyatvam evaṃvidheṣv āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	kāmakrodhāsvatantrārtaklībonmattapramohitaiḥ |

	vyatyāsaparihāsāc ca yad dattaṃ tat punar haret ||

	yā tu kāryasya siddhyartham utkocā syāt pratiśrutā |

	tasminn api prasiddhe 'rthe na deyā syāt kathaṃcana ||

	atha prāg eva dattā syāt pratidāpyas tathā balāt |

	daṇḍaṃ caikādaśaguṇam āhur gārgīyamānavāḥ || iti |

utkocāyāḥ svarūpam api tenaiva darśitam |

	stenasāhasikodvṛttapārajāyikaśaṃsanāt |

	darśanād vṛttanaṣṭasya tathāsatyapravartanāt ||

	prāptam etais tu yat kiṃcit tad utkocākhyam ucyate |

	na dātā tatra daṇḍyaḥ syān madhyasthaś caiva doṣabhāk || iti |

etad uktaṃ bhavati: yadi mahyaṃ na prayacchati tadā tvatkṛtaṃ kathayāmīti bhītim utpādya stenādisakāśād yat kiṃcid dhanam ādatte, tathā yadi mahyaṃ na prayacchasi tadā tvāṃ vārakasya darśayāmīti bhītim utpādya palāyitasakāśād yat kiṃcid ādatte, tathā yadi mahyaṃ prayacchasi tadā satyaṃ kṛtam iti svāminaḥ purastād asatyatayā vacmīty anukūlam uktvā dāsādisakāśāt yat kiṃcid ādatte, tat sarvam utkocākhyam | tad rājñā dātre dāpyam, utkocāpādakagrāhakau ca daṇḍanīyāv iti | bṛhaspatiḥ punaḥpratyāharaṇīyam ity āha |

	pratilābhecchayā dattam apātre pātraśaṅkayā |

	kārye vādharmasaṃyukte svāmī tat punar āpnuyāt ||

manur api |

	dharmārthaṃ yena dattaṃ svāt kasmaicid yācate dhanam |

	paścāc cen na tathā tat syād ādeyaṃ tena tad bhavet ||

yajñādidharmaṃ kartuṃ yācamānāya yad dattaṃ tena dhanena yady asau yajñādidharmaṃ na kuryāt tadā dattadhanaṃ punar ādeyam ity arthaḥ | yadi punar evaṃvidhasyānapahāryatāṃ sādhayitum icched yācakas tadāsau rājñā tad dhanaṃ suvarṇādikaṃ dāpyaḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	yadi saṃsādhayet tat tu darpāl lohena vā punaḥ |

	rājñā dāpyaḥ suvarṇaṃ syāt tasya steyasya niṣkṛtiḥ ||

bṛhaspatir apy adattāni kānicid darśayati |

	kruddhabhraṣṭapramattārtabālonmattabhayāturaiḥ |

	mattātivṛddhanirdhūtaiḥ saṃmūdhaiḥ śokavegibhiḥ ||

	narmadattaṃ tathaitair yat tad adattaṃ prakīrtitam || iti |

pramattena durgrahagṛhītena | nirdhūto 'vadhūtaḥ | narmadattaṃ parihāsena dattam | ārtadattasyādattatvaṃ dharmakāryavyatiriktaviṣayam,

	svasthenārtena vā dattaṃ śrāvitaṃ dharmakāraṇāt |

	adatvā tu mṛte dāpyas tatsuto nātra saṃśayaḥ ||

iti kātyāyanasmaraṇāt | tathedam aparaṃ sarvavivādapadasādhāraṇaṃ manunoktam |

	yogādhamanavikrītaṃ yogadānapratigraham |

	yatra vāpy upadhiṃ paśyet tat sarvaṃ vinivartayet ||

yogaḥ upāyaḥ | evaṃ cāyam arthaḥ: yenāgāminopādhiviśeṣeṇādhikrayadānapratigrahādyāḥ kṛtās tadupādhivigame te sarve vinivartanīyā iti | atra nāradaḥ |

	gṛṇāty adattaṃ yo mohād yaś cādeyaṃ prayacchati |

	daṇḍanīyāv ubhāv etau dharmajñena mahīkṣitā || iti |

atra saṃpradānakārakībhūto nirdiśyate | kartṛkārakībhūtanarasya tv adeyādattayoḥ pratipādanam aparahaṇaṃ vā na daṇḍyatvāpādakaṃ smṛtyācāramārgānusāritvāt | nāpi pratyavāyāpādakam,

	dattasyaiṣoditā dharmyā yathāvad anapakriyā |

iti manunā dharmyety abhidhānāt ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām adattaviṣayāṇi**

**samāptaṃ ca dattāpradānikākhyasya padasa vidhivitānam**

**athābhyupetyāśuśrūṣākhyasya padasya vidhir ucyate**

tatra nāradaḥ |

	śiṣyāntevāsibhṛtakāś caturthas tv adhikarmakṛt |

	ete karmakarā jñeyā dāsās tu gṛhajātayaḥ ||

	sāmānyam asvatantratvam eṣām āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ |

	jātikarmakṛtas tūkto viśeṣo vṛttitas tathā || iti |

ete śiṣyādayaś caturvidhāḥ śuśrūṣakāḥ karmakarā jñeyāḥ | gṛhajātayas tu pañcadaśavidhāḥ śuśrūṣakāḥ dāsāḥ jñeyāḥ | eṣāṃ karmakarāṇāṃ dāsānāṃ cāsvatantratvalakṣaṇaṃ dharmaṃ sādhāraṇam āhur manīṣiṇo manvādayaḥ | jātikṛtaḥ karmakṛto vṛttikṛtaś ca viśeṣaḥ śiṣyāntevāsidāsānām evokta ity arthaḥ | tatra śiṣyāṇāṃ traivarṇikānyatamatvalakṣaṇaḥ jātikṛto viśeṣaḥ "vasante brāhmaṇam upanayīta" ityādiśāstrasiddho 'dhyavaseyaḥ | karmakṛtas tu teṣāṃ viśeṣo bṛhaspatinoktaḥ |

	vidyā trayī samākhyātā ṛgyajuḥsāmalakṣaṇā |

	tadarthaṃ guruśuśrūṣāṃ prakuryāc chāstracoditām ||

śiṣya iti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	ā vidyāgrahaṇāc chiṣyaḥ śuśrūṣet prayato gurum | iti |

evaṃ gurudārādāv api śuśrūṣā kāryā |

	tadvṛttir gurudāreṣu guruputre tathaiva ca |

iti tenaivoktam | bhikṣādānādivṛttito viśeṣaḥ saṃskārakāṇḍe śiṣyāṇām ukta iti punaruktibhayān nehocyate | vṛttito viśeṣaṃ kaṃcid abhidhāyāha sa eva |

	samāvṛttas tu gurave pradāya gurudakṣiṇām |

	pratīyāt svagṛhān eṣā śiṣyavṛttir udāhṛtā ||

svagṛhān pratīyāt svamandiraṃ prati yāyād ity arthaḥ | kaḥ punar antevāsināṃ jātikarmakṛto viśeṣa ity apekṣite bṛhaspatiḥ |

	vijñānam ucyate śilpaṃ hemakupyādisaṃskṛtiḥ |

	nṛttādikaṃ ca yat prāptuṃ karma kuryād guror gṛhe ||

kaṅkaṇakaṭakādinirmāṇaviṣayaṃ nṛttagītādikaraṇaviṣayaṃ ca cakārāt stambhakumbhādiracanāviṣayaṃ ca vijñānaṃ śilpavijñānam ucyate, tatprāptyartham antevāsī guror gṛhe karma kaṅkaṇakaṭakādikaṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | anena hemakārādijātikṛtaḥ kaṅkaṇakaṭakādikarmakṛtaś ca viśeṣo 'ntevāsināṃ darśitaḥ | nāradas tv antevāsināṃ karmābhyāsopakramakāle kartavyam āha |

	svaśilpam icchann āhartuṃ bāndhavānām anujñayā |

	ācāryasya vased ante kālaṃ kṛtvā suniścitam ||

ante samīpe kālaṃ kṛtvā suniścitam etāvantaṃ kālaṃ matsamīpe sthātavyam ity ācāryoktakālaparimāṇaṃ suniścitaṃ kṛtvety arthaḥ | ācāryasyāpi kartavyam āha sa eva |

	ācāryaḥ śikṣayed enaṃ svagṛhe dattabhojanam |

	na cānyat kārayet karma putravac cainam ācaret ||

anyat karma svaśilpavyatiriktaṃ karma | evaṃ cāntevāsinā kaṅkaṇādikarmaphalārpaṇamātreṇa guruśuśrūṣā kāryety avaseyam | svagṛhe dattabojanam iti vadatā vṛttito viśeṣo 'ntevāsināṃ darśitaḥ | yas tv anevaṃvidha ācāryas tasya daṇḍam āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	yas tu na grāhayec chilpaṃ karmāṇy anyāni kārayet |

	prāpnuyāt sāhasaṃ pūrvaṃ tasmāc chiṣyo nivartate ||

śiṣyadauṣṭye 'py āha nāradaḥ |

	śikṣayantam aduṣṭaṃ ca yas tv ācāryaṃ parityajet |

	balād vāsayitavyaḥ syād vadhabandhau ca yo 'rhati ||

vāsayitavyaḥ syād ācāryasya pārśva iti śeṣaḥ | vadho 'tra tāḍanaṃ na prāṇacchedaḥ, aparādhasyālpatvāt | kṛtavidyasya kṛtyam āha sa eva |

	śikṣito 'pi kṛtaṃ kālam antevāsī samāpayet |

	tatra karma ca yat kuryād ācāryasyaiva tatphalam ||

kṛtaṃ kālam ācāryasamīpasthiter avadhitvena paribhāṣitaṃ kālam | tatra samāpanīye kālaśeṣe pratidinam abhāsoparame 'py ācāryasyārthalābhārtham avaśyam abhyastaṃ karma kāryam | kālaśeṣe 'pi gurugṛha eva bhojanam | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	kṛtaśilpo 'pi nivaset kṛtaṃ kālaṃ guror gṛhe |

	antevāsī guruprāptabhojanas tatphalapradaḥ ||

vidyāprāptiśuśrūṣāsamāptyanantaram antevāsinaḥ kṛtyam āha nāradaḥ |

	gṛhītaśilpaḥ samaye kṛtvācāryapradakṣiṇam |

	śaktitaś cānumānyainam antevāsī nivartayet ||

bhṛtakānāṃ tu nāntevāsivaj jātikṛto vṛttikṛto vā viśeṣaḥ, kiṃ tu bhṛtikṛtaḥ karmakṛtaḥ kālakṛtaś ca viśeṣaḥ | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	yo bhuṅkte paradāsīṃ tu sa jñeyo vanitābhṛtaḥ |

	karma tatsvāminaḥ kuryād yathānyo 'rthabhṛto naraḥ ||

	bahudhārthabhṛtaḥ proktas tathā bhāgabhṛto 'paraḥ |

	hīnamadhyottamatvaṃ ca sarveṣām eva coditam ||

	dinamāsārdhaṣaṇmāsatrimāsābdabhṛtas tathā || 

	karma kuryāt pratijñātaṃ labheta paribhāṣitam || iti |

tatsvāmino dāsīsvāmina ity arthaḥ | arthabhṛtasya bahuvidhatvam arthālpatvamahatvatāratamyena jñeyam | tattāratamyaṃ ca bhṛtyaśaktyanusārataḥ pratyetavyam,

	bhṛtyaśaktyanurūpā syād eṣāṃ karmaśrayā bhṛtiḥ |

iti nāradasmaraṇāt | svayam eva bhāgabhṛtasya vibhāgam āha |

	dviprakārā bhāgabhṛtāḥ kṛṣigojīvinaḥ smṛtāḥ |

	jātasasyāt tathā kṣīrāt sa labheta na saṃśayaḥ ||

hīnamadhyamottamatvalakṣaṇaḥ karmakṛto bhedo rakṣaṇādikarmanibandhanaḥ ity āha sa eva |

	āyudhīyottamas teṣāṃ madhyamaḥ sīravāhakaḥ |

	bhāravāho 'dhamaḥ proktas tathaiva gṛhakarmakṛt ||

sīravāhakaḥ karṣakaḥ | yathaiva bhāravāho 'dhamaḥ proktas tathaiva pākakaraṇādyakhilagṛhavyāpārakṛd adhamaḥ prokta ity arthaḥ | kālakṛtas tu bhṛtyānāṃ viśeṣaḥ kālālpatvamahattvanibandhanaḥ | adhikarmakṛtas tu svarūpam āha nāradaḥ |

	sarveṣv adhikṛto yaḥ syāt kuṭumbasya tathopari |

	so 'dhikarmakṛto jñeyaḥ sa ca kauṭumbakaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

sarveṣu bhṛtakeṣu adhikṛta uparikṛto 'dhiṣṭhāyaka iti yāvat | artheṣv adhikṛta iti kecit paṭhanti | tathāyam arthaḥ: artheṣu kṣetrahiraṇyādiṣv adhikṛtaḥ pālakatvena niyukta iti | kuṭumbasyoparīty atra kṛta ity adhyāhāryaḥ | kuṭumbasyoparikaraṇam āyavyayakartṛtvena niyoga eva | evaṃ nirūpitāḥ śiṣyāntevāsibhṛtakādhikarmakarāḥ śubhakarmakarā ity āha sa eva |

	śubhakarmakarā hy ete catvāraḥ samudāhṛtāḥ | iti |

śubhakarma ca jugupsitakarmetarad vijñeyam iti sa evāha |

	gṛhadvārāśucisthānarathyāvaskaraśodhanam |

	guhyāṅgasparśanocchiṣṭaviṇmūtragrahaṇojjhanam ||

	iṣṭataḥ svāminaś cāṅgair upasthānam athāntataḥ |

	aśubhaṃ karma vijñeyaṃ śubhaṃ tu yad ataḥ param || iti |

avaskaraḥ saṃmārjitareṇurāśiḥ | śodhanaśabdaḥ pratyekaṃ gṛhadvārādicaturṣv abhisaṃbadhyate | ujjhanaṃ tyāgaḥ | antato mūtrapurīṣavirāme lepanirmārjanārthaṃ svāmīcchayā svahastādyarpaṇam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ karmakaraviṣayāṇi**

**atha dāsanirūpaṇam**

tatra nāradaḥ |

	jaghanyakarmabhājas tu śeṣā dāsās tripañcakāḥ | iti |

śeṣāḥ śiṣyāntevāsibhṛtakādhikarmakṛdbhyo 'vaśiṣṭāḥ | jaghanyakarmabhājaḥ gṛhadvārāśucisthānaśodhanādyaśubhakarmabhājaḥ | anena dāsānāṃ karmato bheda uktaḥ | tripañcakāḥ pañcadaśasaṅkhyākāḥ | dāsaśabdavyutpattipradarśanamukhena dāsānāṃ karmakarebhyo bhedam āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	svatantrasyātmano dānād dāsatvaṃ dāravad bhṛguḥ | iti |

yathā bhartuḥ saṃbhogārthaṃ svaśarīradānād dvāratvaṃ tathā svatantrasyātmanaḥ parārthatvena dānād dāsatvam iti bhṛgur ācāryo manyata ity arthaḥ | anenātyantapārārthyam āsādya śuśrūṣakā dāsāḥ, pārārthyamātram āsādya śuśrūṣakā karmakarā iti bhedo 'py ukta ity avagantavyam | atyantapārārthyaṃ tu teṣāṃ bhavati, yais tu svapuruṣārthavṛttinirodhena pārārthyam āśritam | evaṃbhūtaṃ dāsatvaṃ brāhmaṇe tareṣv eva triṣu varṇeṣu vijñeyam "dāsyaṃ viprasya na kvacit" iti tenaivābhidhānāt | anena dāsānāṃ jātito bheda uktaḥ | vipretareṣv api dāsyam ānulomyenaiva |

	varṇakramānulomyena dāsyaṃ na pratilomataḥ |

	rājanyavaiśyaśūdrāṇāṃ tyajatāṃ hi svatantarām ||

svatantratāṃ tyajatām atyantapārārthyaṃ bhajatām ity arthaḥ | pratilomata ity etat svadharmaparityāgibhyo yatibhyo 'nyatra draṣṭavyam,

	varṇānāṃ prātilomyena dāsatvaṃ na vidhīyate |

	svadharmatyāgino 'nyatra dāravad dāsatā matā ||

iti nāradasmaraṇāt | yathottamavarṇaṃ prati hīnavarṇā savarṇā vā bhāryā bhavati na punar hīnavarṇaṃ praty uttamavarṇā, tathaiva dāso 'pi bhaved ity arthaḥ | dāravad dāsatetivacanād viprasya savarṇaṃ prati dāsatvam āpadi prāptam ivābhātīti buddhyā tanniṣedhārtham āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	samavarṇe 'pi vipraṃ tu dāsatvaṃ naiva kārayet | iti |

yat punaḥ punaruktam iva tenaivoktam |

	brāhmaṇasya hi dāsatvān nṛpatejo vihanyate |

	kṣatraviṭchūdradharmas tu samavarṇe kadācana ||

	kārayed dāsakarmāṇi brāhmaṇaṃ na bṛhaspatiḥ || iti |

atra vākyatrayam: tatrādyavākyasya prātilomyena dāsatve kārite kārayitus tejohānir jāyata ity arthaḥ | dāsatvaṃ tu na saṃkarajātidharma iti dvitīyavākyasyārthaḥ | dāsavad dāsakarmāṇy api sarvathā brāhmaṇaṃ na kārayet savarṇo 'pīti tṛtīyavākyasyārtha iti na kiṃcit punaruktam iva | svakīyecchāyā viśiṣṭapuruṣopakārārthaṃ tat karma kurvann api brāhmaṇo nāśubhaṃ karma kuryād ity āha sa eva |

	śīlādhyayanasaṃpanne tadūnaṃ karma kāmataḥ |

	tatrāpi nāśubhaṃ kiṃcit prakurvīta dvijottamaḥ ||

yasmāt paropakāraḥ kartavyaḥ tasmāt tadūnaṃ karma madhyamottamakarmavyatiriktam api karma kāmato vetanam antareṇa svecchayā parahitārtham aparaḥ kuryād iti pūrvārthasyārthaḥ | svāminaṃ praty āha manuḥ |

	kṣatriyaṃ caiva vaiśyaṃ ca brāhmaṇo vṛttikarśitau |

	bibhṛyād ānṛśaṃsyena svāni karmāṇi kārayet ||

vṛttikarśitāv ity atra dvitīyā pāśamantrasthadvitīyāvat karmatvamātravivakṣayā prayuktā | evaṃ cāyam arthaḥ: vṛttikarśitaṃ kṣatriyaṃ vaiśyaṃ ca dāsabhūtam akrauryeṇa karmāṇi kārayat svāmī poṣayed iti | vṛttikarśitāv iti vadann agatyaiva kṣatriyavaiśyayor dāsatvāṅgīkāraḥ kāryo na punaḥ sati saṃbhava iti darśayati | svānīti vadan na saṃbandhijanakarmāṇi kārayed ity āha | karmāṇīti sāmānyābhidhānena jaghanyakarmāṇy eva kārayitavyānīti nasti niyama iti sūcayati | vṛttikarśitau bibhṛyād iti vadann ākāṅkṣānusāreṇa kṣatriyavaiśyayor dāsyaṃ kārayitavyam, na prabhutvamāteṇety etad api jñāpayati | ata eva yaḥ prabhutvamātreṇa kārayati tasya jñāpitārthājñatvanibandhanam aparādhitvam anūdya daṇḍaṃ āha sa eva |

	dāsyaṃ tu kārayen mohāt brāhmaṇaḥ saṃskṛtān dvijān |

	anicchataḥ prābhavatyād rājñā dāpyaḥ śatāni ṣaṭ ||

prabhavato bhāvaḥ prābhavatyaṃ tasmāt prābhavatyāt prabhutvād eveti yāvat | dvijān iti vadan na daṇḍaḥ śūdraviṣaya iti darśayati | ata eva śūdraṃ yathā kathaṃcid api dāsyaṃ karayed ity āha sa eva |

	śūdraṃ tu kārayed dāsyaṃ krītam akrītam eva vā |

	dāsyāyaiva hi sṛṣṭo 'sau svayam eva svayaṃbhuvā ||

viṣṇus tu prātilomyena dāsyaṃ kārayitur daṇḍam āha: "yas tūttamavarṇaṃ dāsye niyojayati tasyottamasāhaso daṇḍaḥ" iti ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ dāsanirūpaṇam**

**athānyāni dāsaviṣayāṇi kānicid vacanāni likhyante**

tatra nāradaḥ |

	gṛhajātas tathā krīto labdho dāyād upāgataḥ |

	anākālabhṛtas tadvad āhitaḥ svāminā ca yaḥ ||

	mokṣito mahataś carṇād yuddhe prāptaḥ paṇe jitaḥ |

	tavāham ity upagataḥ pravrajyāvasitaḥ kṛtaḥ ||

	bhaktadāsaś ca vijñeyas tathaiva vaḍavāhṛtaḥ |

	vikretā cātmanaḥ śāstre dāsāḥ pañcadaśa smṛtāḥ || iti |

gṛhajātaḥ svagṛhadāsyāṃ jātaḥ | krīto mūlyena svāmyantarāt prāptaḥ | labdhas tata eva pratigrahādinā prāptaḥ | labdhas tata eva pratigrahādinā prāptaḥ | dāyād upāgataḥ rikthagrāhitvena labdhaḥ | anākālabhṛtaḥ durbhikṣe poṣitaḥ | āhitaḥ svāmina ṛṇadātary ādhitvaṃ nītaḥ | ṛṇān mokṣitaḥ ṛṇamocanapratyupakāratayā dāsatvam abhyupagataḥ | yuddhe prāptaḥ samare vijitya gṛhītaḥ | paṇe jito dāsatvapaṇake dyūtādau jitaḥ | tavāham ity upagataḥ tava dāso 'smīti svayam evābhyupagataḥ | pravrajyāvasitaḥ prabhraṣṭasaṃnyāsī | kṛtaḥ etāvantaṃ kālaṃ tavāhaṃ dāso bhavāmīty upagataḥ | bhaktadāsaḥ, bhakṣitaṃ bhaktam, mūlyadvāreṇa yāvat te dadāmi tāvad ahaṃ te dāsa ity upagataḥ | vaḍavāhṛtaḥ, vaḍavā gṛhadāsī tām udvāhya tatsvāmyanumatyarthaṃ dāsatvena praviṣṭaḥ | ātmano vikretā svayam evātmano vikrayam arthādyarthaṃ kṛtavān | ity evaṃ dharmaśāstre dāsāḥ pañcadaśaprakārāḥ smṛtāḥ ity arthaḥ | atrādyānāṃ gṛhajātakrītalabdhadāyāgatānāṃ caturṇāṃ dāsatvāpagamaḥ svāmiprasādavaśād eva nānyathety āha sa eva |

	tatra pūrvaś caturvargo dāsatvān na vimucyate |

	prasādāt svāmino 'nyatra dāsyam eṣāṃ kramāgatam ||

evam anyasyāpy ātmavikretur dāsatvaṃ svāmiprasādād anyato na vimucyata ity āha sa eva |

	vikrīṇīte svatantraḥ san ya ātmānaṃ narādhamaḥ |

	sa jaghanyatams teṣāṃ so 'pi dāsyān na mucyate ||

prasādāt svāmino 'nyatrety atrānuṣajyate | tataś cāyam arthaḥ: ātmavikretāpi gṛhajātādivat svāmiprasādād anyato dāsyān na vimucyata iti | evaṃ ca gṛhajātādayo 'py ātmavikretṛpañcamāḥ svāmiprasādād anākālabhṛtādaya iva dāsyān mucyanta iti vacobhaṅgyā darśitam iti mantavyam | svāmiprāṇarakṣaṇād api gṛhajātādayo 'nākālabhṛtādayaś ca sarve dāsyād vimucyanta ity āha sa eva |

	yo vaiṣāṃ svāmināṃ kaścin mocayet prāṇasaṃśayāt |

	dāsatvāt sa vimucyeta putrabhāgaṃ labheta ca ||

eṣāṃ pañcadaśavidhadāsānāṃ madhya ity arthaḥ | etac ca svāminaḥ prasādāt prāṇarakṣaṇād vā dāsyāpagamanaṃ pravrajyāvasitetaraviṣayam,

	pravrajāvasito rājño dāsa āmaraṇāntikaḥ |

iti yājñavalkyasmaraṇāt | rājño dāsaḥ pārthivasyaiva dāsaḥ nānyasyety arthaḥ | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	rājña eva tu dāsaḥ syāt pravrajyāvasito naraḥ |

	na tasya pratimokṣo 'sti nātra śuddhiḥ kathaṃcana ||

naro vipretaro 'bhipretaḥ, viprasya dāsyapratiṣedhāt | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	pravrajyāvasitā yatra trayo varṇā dvijātayaḥ |

	nirvāsaṃ kārayed vipraṃ dāsatvaṃ kṣatraviḍ bhṛguḥ || iti |

nirvāsaṃ kārayed rājeti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	pārivrājyaṃ gṛhītvā tu yaḥ svadharmaṃ na tiṣṭhati |

	śvapādenāṅkayitvā tu rājā śīghraṃ pravāsayet ||

śvapādena śunaḥ pādasadṛśataptāyasena rājñā dāsyam akurvatoḥ kṣatriyavaiśyayor api nirvāsm uktavidhinā kāryam, svadharme na tiṣṭhatīti sāmānyenābhidhānāt | yat tu tenaivoktam,

	dvāv etau karmacaṇḍālau loke dūrabahiṣkṛtau |

	pravrajyopanivṛttaś ca vṛthāpravrajitaś ca yaḥ ||

iti, tat rājadāsetaraviṣayam, rājadāsasya bahiṣkārānupapatteḥ | evaṃ ca pravrajyāvasitetaradāsavimokṣaḥ svāminaḥ prasādaprāṇarakṣaṇābhyāṃ bhavatīty avagantavyam | anākālabhṛtādīnāṃ tu pravrajyāvasitātmavikretṛvyatirikānāṃ navānāṃ pratyekam ekaikenāpi goyugadānādinā dāsyam apanīyata ity āha sa eva |

	anākālabhṛto dāsyān mucyate goyugaṃ dadat |

	āhito 'pi dhanaṃ datvā svāmī yady enam uddharet ||

	ṛṇaṃ tu sodayaṃ datvā ṛṇī dāsyāt pramucyate |

	tavāham ity upagato yuddhe prāptaḥ paṇr jitaḥ ||

	pratiśīrṣapradānena mucyeran tulyakarmaṇā |

	kṛtakālavyapagamāt kṛtako 'pi vimucyate ||

	bhaktasyotkṣepaṇāt sadyo bhaktadāsaḥ pramucyate |

	nigrahād vaḍavāyās tu mucyate vaḍvāhṛtaḥ || iti |

etad uktaṃ bhavati: durbhikṣe poṣaṇena kārito dāso godvayārpaṇād vimucyate | āhitadāsas tv ādātrā svagṛhīte ṛṇe pratyarpite saty uttamarṇadāsyād vimucyate | ṛṇadāsas tu svakṛtam ṛṇaṃ yena yāvad dhanaṃ datvāpākṛtaṃ tasmai tāvad dhanaṃ savṛddhikaṃ dadad vimucyate | tavāham ity upagatādayas trayo dāsaviśeṣās tu svābhinirvartyākhilavyāpāranirvartakadāsāntarapradānād vimucyante | kṛtas tu dāsaviśeṣo dāsyāvadhitvena paribhāṣitakālasyātyayād vimucyate | gṛhadāsīlobhena dāsatvam āpannas tu tatsaṃbhogatyāgād vimucyata iti | yājñavalkyas tu dāsābhāsānāṃ visarjanam āha |

	balād dāsīkṛtaś coraiḥ vikrītaś cāpi mucyate | iti |

yo balātkāreṇādāso 'pi kenacit prabhuṇā dāsaḥ kṛtaḥ, yaś ca corair apahṛtya dāsatvena vikrītaḥ, āhito datto vā sa yasya pārśve dāsabhāvena tiṣṭhati tena prabhunā mocanahetum antareṇaiva (?) śīghram evāsau mocanīya ity arthaḥ | yati tena lobhādivaśād asau na muktas tadā rājñā mocayitavyaḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	coropahatavikrītā ye ca dāsīkṛtā balāt |

	rājñā mocayitavyās te dāsatvaṃ teṣu neṣyate ||

yas tu pūrvam ekasya dāsaḥ sann aparasya dāsyam aṅgīkaroti asāv apareṇa visarjanīya iti vacobhaṅgyā sa evāha |

	tavāham iti cātmānaṃ yo 'svatantraḥ prayacchati |

	na samaṃ nāpnuyāt kāmaṃ pūrvasvāmī labheta tam ||

asvatantraḥ paradāsatvenāsvatantraḥ kāmaṃ nūtanasvāmini dāsyam, purātanasvāmini dāsena kāmyamānatvāt | evaṃ yad etad dāsam adhikṛtyoktaṃ tat sarvaṃ yathāyogyaṃ dāsyām api draṣṭavyam | dāsīsvāminam adhikṛtya viśeṣam āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	svadāsīṃ yas tu saṃgacchet prasūtā ca bhavet tataḥ |

	avekṣya bījaṃ kāryā syān na dāsī sānvayā tu sā ||

svakṛtagarbhādhānam anusaṃdhāya svāminā svadāsī santānasahitā dāsatvavimocakavidhinā svakṛtagarbhādhānāder dāsatvaparihārārtham adāsītvena kāryā syād ity arthaḥ | kaḥ punar dāsatvavimocako vidhir ity apeśite (?) nāradaḥ |

	svadāsam icched yaḥ kartum adāsaṃ prītimānasaḥ |

	skandhād ādāya tasyāsau (?) bhindyāt kumbhaṃ sahāmbhasā ||

	sākṣatābhiḥ sapuṣpābhiḥ mūrdhany adbhir avākiret |

	adāsa iti coktvā triḥ prāṅmukhas tam athotsṛjet ||

evaṃ samutsarge sati dāsatvakṛtam ayogyatvam apaitīty āha sa eva |

	tataḥ prabhṛti kartavyaḥ svāmy anugrahapālitaḥ |

	bhojyānno 'tha pratigrāhyo bhavaty abhimataḥ satām ||

svāmyanugraheṇa kaṣṭataradaśāpākaraṇarūpeṇa pālitaḥ nijasvarūpaṃ nītaḥ saṃbhāṣaṇādiyogyo bhavati tadānīm evety arthaḥ | dāsīm adāsīṃ kartum icchato 'pi samānam etad vidhānam, dāsam ity atra liṅgavacanayor uddeśyaviśeṣaṇayor avivakṣitatvāt | svāmyanujñayā pālito rakṣitaḥ bhojyānnaḥ pratigrāhyaḥ, satāṃ saṃmataś ca bhavatīty arthaḥ | ata eva,

	dāsasya tu dhanaṃ yat syāt svāmī tasya prabhuḥ smṛtaḥ |

iti kātyāyanena dāsadhanprabhutve smṛte 'pi dāsīdhane 'pi svāminaḥ prabhutvaṃ smṛtam iti mantavyam | tathā ca sa eva dāsena yā pariṇītā sāpi dāsītvam apadyata ity āha |

	dāsenoḍhā tv adāsī yā sāpi dāsītvam āpnuyāt |

	yasmād bhartā prabhus tasyāḥ svāmyadhīnaḥ prabhur yataḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ dāsaviṣayāṇi**

**samāptam abhyupetyāśuśrūṣākhyasya padasya vidhivitānam**

**atha vetanānapākarmākhyasya padasya vidhir ucyate**

tatra manuḥ |

	ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi vetanasyānpakriyām || iti |

vetanaṃ karmamūlyam, tasyānapakriyā bhṛtyāyāsamarpaṇam, samarpitasya vā parāvartanam | tatra samarpaṇe viśeṣam āha nāradaḥ |

	bhṛtyāya vetanaṃ dadyāt karmasvāmī yathākramam |

	ādau madhye 'vasāne ca karmaṇo yad viniścitam ||

tubhyam iyad dāsyāmīti yad vetanaṃ parimāṇato viniścitaṃ tridhā vibhajya karmaṇa ādimadhyāvasāneṣu dādyād ity arthaḥ | etat sakṛdādau deyam ityādiviśeṣaparibhāṣābhāve veditavyam | iyad dāsyāmīti paribhāṣāyā abhāve viśeṣam āha sa eva |

	bhṛtāv aniścitāyāṃ tu daśabhāgam avāpnuyuḥ |

	lābhagovīryasasyānāṃ vaṇiggopakṛṣīvalāḥ ||

daśabhāgaṃ daśamaṃ bhāgam ity arthaḥ | govīryaṃ pālyamānagavādipaśuprabhavaṃ payaḥprabhṛti avāpnuyuḥ, yathākrameneti śeṣaḥ | yadi karmasvāmī prāguktabhāgāvāptipratibandhako bhavati tadā tv āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	dāpyas tu daśamaṃ bhāgaṃ vāṇijyapaśusasyataḥ |

	aniścitya bhṛtiṃ yas tu kārayet sa mahīkṣitā ||

sasyadaśamabhāgabhṛtir iyam alpaprayāsasādhyakṛṣṭakṣetrakartṛviṣaye draṣṭavyam | bahvāyāsasādhyakṛṣṭakṣetrakartṛviṣaye tv āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	tribhāgaṃ pañcabhāgaṃ vā gṛhṇīyāt sīravāhakaḥ | iti |

vyavasthitavikalpaś cāyam | katham atra vyavasthety apekṣite sa evāha |

	bhaktācchādabhṛtaḥ sīrāt bhāgaṃ gṛhṇīta pañcamam |

	jātasasyāt tribhāgaṃ tu pragṛhṇīyād athābhṛtaḥ (?) ||

aśanācchādanābhyāṃ bhṛtaḥ kṛṣīvalaḥ lāṅgalavikṛṣṭakṣetrajātasa (?) syāt | pañcamabhāgaṃ gṛhṇīyāt | tābhyām abhṛtas tu tṛtīyabhāgam ity arthaḥ | atha vā yatra iyad dāsyāmīti paribhāṣāyā abhāvas tatra manūktaṃ draṣṭavyam |

	samudrayānakuśalā deśakālārthadarśinaḥ |

	niyaccheyuḥ bhṛtiṃ yāṃ tu sā syāt prāg akṛtā yadi ||

iyad dāsyāmīti paribhāṣite 'pi kvacit tato nyūnaṃ svāmibuddhimātraparikalpitaṃ vetanaṃ deyam, kvacit tato 'py adhikaṃ deyam ity āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	deśaṃ kālaṃ ca yo 'tīyāl lābhaṃ kuryāc ca yo 'nyathā |

	tatra syāt svāminaś chando 'dhike deyaṃ kṛte 'dhike ||

yo bhṛtyaḥ svāmyājñāṃ vinā svātantryeṇa vāṇijyādikarmaṇaḥ phalasādhakatvāpādakaṃ deśaṃ kālaṃ vātikrāmati, lābhaṃ vā bahutaravyayakaraṇena svalpaṃ karoti, tasmai pūrvaparibhāṣitabhṛtimadhye svāmī svecchānusāreṇa kiṃcid dadyāt | yas tu svātantryeṇa bahulābhaṃ karoti, tasmai paribhāṣitamūlyādhikaṃ kiṃcid deyaṃ svāminā pāritoṣakam ity arthaḥ | anekanirvartye karmaṇi paribhāṣitabhṛter arpaṇaprakāram āha sa eva |

	yo yāvat kurute karma tāvat tasya tu vetanam |

	ubhayor apy asādhyaṃ cet sādhye kuryād yathāśrutam ||

ayam arthaḥ: kūpe kṛte tatkartṝṇām iyad dāsyāmīti vetane pratiśrute dvibahukartṛbhir ārabdhe vighnavaśād asamāptau tattatkṛtakarmānusāreṇa pratikartṛ kiṃcid deyam | athāvighnena samāpte yāvat paribhāṣitam eva deyam iti ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ vetanasamarpaṇaviṣayāṇi**

**atha bhṛtyaviṣayāṇi**

tatra nāradaḥ |

	karmopakaraṇaṃ caiṣāṃ kriyāṃ prati yad āhitam |

	āptabhāvena tad rakṣyaṃ na jaihmena kadācana ||

eṣāṃ karmasvāmināṃ karmopakaraṇaṃ lāṅgalādikaṃ kṛṣyādikriyām uddiśya yad bhṛtyapārśve nihitaṃ tat tena sadā niḥśāṭhyena rakṣyam ity arthaḥ | bṛhaspatir api |

	bhṛtakas tu na kurvīta svāminaḥ śāṭhyam aṇv api |

	bhṛtihānim avāpnoti tato vādaḥ pravartate ||

tataḥ śāṭhyakaraṇāt vivādaḥ svāminā saha svasya pravartate, tatra parājito bhṛtakaḥ śāṭhyānusārāt bhṛtihātim avāpnotīty arthaḥ | karmaṇo 'karaṇe 'py āha sa eva |

	gṛhītavetanaḥ karma na karoti yadā bhṛtaḥ |

	samarthaś ced damaṃ dāpyo dviguṇaṃ tac ca vetanam ||

damaṃ śaktyaparādhānusāreṇa rājñe dadyāt | gṛhītaṃ ca vetanaṃ dvaiguṇyena svāmine dadyād ity arthaḥ | asminn eva viṣaye vetanāgrahaṇr tv āha yājñavalkyaḥ: "agṛhīte samaṃ dāpyaḥ" iti | yāvatā vetanena bhṛtyatvam aṅgīkṛtaṃ tāvad eva svāmine dadyān na tu rājñe daṇḍam ity arthaḥ | atha vāṅgīkṛtāṃ bhṛtiṃ datvā svāminā bhṛtyo balātkāreṇa kārayitavyaḥ | yad āha nāradaḥ |

	karma kurvan pratiśrutya kāryo datvā bhṛtiṃ balāt | iti |

pratiśrutyetat prārambhasyopalakṣaṇārtham | yad āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	karmārambhaṃ tu yat kṛtvā siddhaṃ naiva tu kārayet |

	balātkārayitavyo 'sāv akurvan daṇḍam arhati ||

kārṣāpaṇadviśatam iti śeṣaḥ | yad āha vṛddhamanuḥ |

	pratiśrutya na kuryād yaḥ sa kāryaḥ syāt balād api |

	sa cen na kuryāt tat karma prāpnuyād dviśataṃ damam || iti |

yat tu manunoktam,

	bhṛto 'nārto na kuryād yo darpāt karma yathoditam |

	sa daṇḍyaḥ kṛṣṇalān aṣṭau na deyaṃ cāsya vetanam ||

iti, tad alpadaṇḍatvāt bhāgāsiddhiviṣayam, dānapratiṣedhād dattam apy adattaprāyatvāt pratyāharaṇīyam | kiṃcin mātrāsiddhau tu pūrvoktam eva daṇḍavarjaṃ bhavatīty āha sa eva |

	yathoktam ārtaḥ svastho vā yas tat karma na kārayet |

	na tasya vetanaṃ deyam alponasyāpi karmaṇaḥ ||

svastho na kārayed iti vadann asvasthe 'pi svayaṃ kartṛtvaniyamo nāstīti darśayati | yas tv ārtaḥ svārtisamaye dhanādyabhāvena na kārayati, kiṃ tv ārtyapagamānantaraṃ svayaṃ karoti tatrārteḥ dīrghakālatayā kālakṣepe 'pi bhṛtyadoṣābhāvād vetanam asau nirvivādaṃ labhate ity āha sa eva |

	ārtas tu kuryāt svasthaḥ san yathābhāṣitam āditaḥ |

	sudīrghasyāpi kālasya labhetaiva ca vetanam ||

yas tu kālaviśeṣāvadhikaṃ karma pratijñāya pratijñātakālāpūrvāv eva karma tyajati taṃ praty āha nāradaḥ |

	 kāle 'pūrṇe tyajan karma bhṛter nāśam avāpnuyāt |

atra daṇḍam apy āha viṣṇuḥ: "paṇaśataṃ ca rājñe dadyāt" iti | asminn eva viṣaye mahāpāruṣyakaraṇādisvāmidoṣatas tyajan bhṛtyo yāvati kāle karma tatkālānusāreṇa kalpitaṃ vetanaṃ labhata ity āha nāradaḥ |

	svāmidoṣād apakrāman yāvatkṛtam avāpnuyāt | iti |

yas tu pramādādinā svadoṣeṇa svāmidravyaṃ balīvardādikaṃ nāśayati taṃ praty āha viṣṇuḥ: "taddoṣeṇa ca yad vinaśyet tat svāmine deyam anyatra rājadaivopaghātāt" iti | naṣṭasya yan mūlyaṃ yogyaṃ tad deyam ity arthaḥ | atra doṣaviśeṣād viśeṣam āha vṛddhamanuḥ |

	pramādān nāśitaṃ dāpyaṃ samaṃ dvir drohanāśitam | iti |

pramādān nāśitam anavadhānān nāśitaṃ samam eva dadyāt, drohanāśitaṃ tīvraprahārādinā nāśitaṃ tad dvir dāpyo dviguṇaṃ dadyād ity arthaḥ | bhṛtyadoṣābhāve yad anyata eva naṣṭaṃ tan na deyam ity āha sa eva |

	na tu dāpyo hṛtaṃ corair dagdhd ūḍhaṃ jalena vā | iti |

ūḍhaṃ nītam | yas tu vāhako vāhyadravyaṃ prajñāhīnatvādinā svadoṣeṇa vināśyati taṃ praty āha nāradaḥ |

	bhāṇḍavyasanam āgacched yadi vāhakadoṣataḥ |

	dāpyo yat tatra naśyet tu daivarājakṛtād ṛte ||

bhāṇḍaṃ goṇyādiṣu nyupya prāpaṇīyaṃ kramukādikam | vyasanam āgacchet doṣādikam prāpnuyāt | atrāpi,

	pramādān nāśitaṃ dāpyaḥ samaṃ dvir drohanāśitam |

iti vṛddhamanūkto viśeṣo draṣṭavyaḥ | yas tu vāhakaḥ svadoṣeṇa prasthānvighnaṃ karoti taṃ praty āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	vighnayan vāhako dāpyaḥ prasthāne dviguṇaṃ smṛtam | iti |

vāhaka ity udāharaṇamātram eva, na tu vivakṣitam, tenāyudhīyādibhṛtye 'pi vighnakāriṇi vacanam etad iti mantavyam | ata eva nāradena,

	dviguṇāṃ tu bhṛtiṃ dāpya prasthāne vighanm ācaran |

iti sāmānyenoktam | vighnācaraṇam aṅgīkṛtakarmākaraṇam evātra vivakṣitaṃ na punar āsedhādikam | aṅgīkṛtakarmākaraṇasyāpi yadā sahāyāntaralābhena prathānavighnānāpādakatvaṃ tadā tv āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	prakrānte saptamaṃ bhāgaṃ caturthaṃ pathi saṃtyajan |

	bhṛtim ardhapathe sarvāṃ pradāpyaḥ || iti |

prakrānte prasthānakarmaṇi svāṅgīkṛtaṃ karma tyajan bhṛtiḥ saptamaṃ bhāgaṃ dāpyaḥ | pathi gantavyabhāgādhikye tyajan bhṛteś caturthaṃ bhāgam ardhapathe tyajan sarvāṃ bhṛtim ity arthaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ bhṛtyaviṣayāṇi**

**atha svāmiviṣayāṇi**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	prabhuṇā viniyuktaḥ san bhṛtako vidadhāti yaḥ |

	tadartham aśubhaṃ karma svāmī tatrāparādhnuyāt ||

aśubhaṃ karma sīmollaṅghanādy anyāyena kṣetrakarṣaṇādikam | svāmyanujñayā bhṛtyenāśubhakarmakaraṇe svāmino daṇḍa iti vaktum idam uktam | kātyāyano 'pi |

	tyajet pathi sahāyaṃ yaḥ śrāntaṃ rogārtam eva vā |

	prāpnuyāt sāhasaṃ pūrvaṃ grāme tryaham apālayan ||

sahāyaṃ bhṛtyam | bṛhaspatir api |

	kṛte karmaṇi yaḥ svāmī na dadyād vetanaṃ bhṛte |

	rājñā dāpayitavyaḥ syād vinayaṃ cānurūpataḥ ||

bhṛte bhṛtye | viṣṇur api: "svāmī ced bhṛtam apūrṇakāle jahyāt tasya sarvam eva mūlyaṃ dadyāt, paṇaśataṃ ca rājñe, anyatra bhṛtadoṣāt" iti | tasyeti caturthyarthe ṣaṣṭhī, śeṣa ity anuvṛttau "caturthyarthe bahulaṃ chandasi" iti pāṇinismaraṇāt | doṣo 'tra cauryādir abhipretaḥ, na punar bahvāśitvādiḥ | yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	prakrānte saptamaṃ bhāgaṃ caturthaṃ pathi saṃtyajan |

	bhṛtim ardhapathe sarvāṃ pradāpyas tyājako 'pi ca ||

prasthānakarmaṇi prakrānte, gantavyabhāgādhike pathi arthapathe vā yo bhṛtyaṃ karma kurvāṇaṃ sāmī (?) tyāpayati, so 'tra tyājako mataḥ | so 'pi pūrvoktapradeśeṣu bhṛtyaṃ tyajan bhṛtyāya saptamabhāgaṃ dāpya ity arthaḥ | pathi caturthabhāgadāpanam avikrītabhāṇḍasvāmiviṣayam | vikrītabhāṇḍasvāmiviṣaye tv āha vṛddhamanuḥ |

	pathi vikrīya tad bhāṇḍaṃ vaṇig bhṛtyaṃ tyajed yadi |

	atha tasyāpi deyaṃ syād bhṛter ardhaṃ labheta saḥ ||

pathi gantavyabhāgādhika iti śeṣaḥ | śauḷkikādīnām āsedhena pratibaddhabhāṇḍasvāmiviṣaye rājādyapahṛtabhāṇḍasvāmiviṣaye cāha kātyāyanaḥ |

	yadā tu pathi tat bhāṇḍam āsidheta hriyeta vā |

	yāvān adhvā gatas tena prāpnuyāt tāvatīṃ bhṛtim ||

gatasaraṇyanusāreṇa svāmī bhṛtiṃ prāg adattāṃ dadyāt | prāg dattāyās tu bhṛter abhikam ādadītety arthaḥ | bhāṭakagṛhītena yānādinā bhāṇḍanetāraṃ praty āha nāradaḥ |

	anayan bhāṭayitvā tu bhāṇḍavān yānavāhane |

	dāpyo bhṛticaturbhāgaṃ sarvām ardhapathe tyajan ||

yānaṃ śakaṭādi | vāhanam aśvādi | te bhāṭayitvā prāpaṇādikāryopādhikaparikrayaṃ kṛtvā sahāyārthaṃ parikrītaṃ yady api na gṛhṇāti, tathāpi bhṛticaturbhāgaṃ mūlyacaturthāṃśaṃ dāpya ity arthaḥ | ardhapathe ca sarvadāpanavacanāt tato nyūnapathe bhāṭakāhṛtayānāni tyajan tribhāgadvibhāgakalpanayā dāpya ity ūhyam | yas tu śakaṭādikaṃ bhāṭayitvā tam evopakāraśūnya ādāya deśāntaraṃ gacchati, bhāṭakaṃ tu na prayacchati taṃ praty āha vṛddhamanuḥ |

	yo bhāṭayitvā śakaṭaṃ nītvā cānyatra gacchati |

	bhāṭaṃ na dadyād dāpyaḥ syād arūḍhasyāpi bhāṭakam ||

kāryopādhikaparikrayamūlyam iti yāvat | arūḍhasyāpi akṛtopakārasyāpi śakaṭāder bhāṭakaṃ dāpya ity arthaḥ | kātyāyanas tu kṛte kṛtye samanantaram asamarpitasya vāhanādeḥ samarpaṇaparyantaṃ bhāṭakānivṛtttir ity āha |

	hastyaśvagokharoṣṭrādīn gṛhītvā bhāṭakena yaḥ |

	nārpayet kṛtakṛtyārthaḥ sa tu dāpyaḥ sabhāṭakam ||

evaṃ gṛhāder apīty āha sa eva |

	gṛhavāryāpaṇādīni gṛhītvā bhāṭakena yaḥ |

	svāmine nārpayed yāvat tāvad dāpyaḥ sa bhāṭakam ||

vāriśabdenātra tadādhārapātraṃ maṇikādikaṃ lakṣyate | nārpayet kṛtakṛtyaḥ sann iti śeṣaḥ | maṇikādipātrasya kṛtsnabhraṃśaviṣaye tv āha nāradaḥ |

	stomavāhīni bhāṇḍāni pūrṇakālāny upānayet |

	grahītur ābhavet bhagnaṃ naṣṭaṃ cānyatra saṃplavāt ||

stomena bhāṭakena bhāṇḍāni dravadravyaprāpaṇārthaṃ gṛhītāni stomavāhīni, tāni pūrṇabhāṭakakālāni tatsvāminaṃ prāpayed ity arthaḥ | siddham uktvā grahītur ābhaved ityādy uktam | tasyāyam arthaḥ: samplavaḥ parasparam anyena vā dravyeṇa saṃghaṭṭanam, tatra leśataḥ kārtsnyena vā bhinnaṃ pūrvavat kṛtaṃ tulyarūpam āpannaṃ vā bhāṇḍasvāmine deyam | saṃplavād anyatra tu tathābhūtaṃ bhāṭakagrahītur ābhavet ātmasaṃbandhi bhavet bhāṭakadātrā na samādheyam iti yāvat | gṛhādhāradeśāya bhāṭakadātāraṃ ca praty āha sa eva |

	parabhūmau gṛhaṃ kṛtvā stomaṃ datvā vaset tu yaḥ |

	sa tad gṛhītvā nirgacchet tṛṇakāṣṭheṣṭakādikam || iti |

stomāpradāne 'py āha sa eva |

	stomād vinā vasitvā tu parabhūmāv aniścitaḥ |

	nirgacchaṃs tṛṇakāṣṭhādi na gṛhṇīyāt kathaṃcana ||

	yāny eva tṛṇakāṣṭhāni tv iṣṭakā viniveśitā |

	sa nirgacchaṃs tu tat sarvaṃ bhūmisvāmini vedayet || iti |

svāmini svāmine | vedayet nirvedayed ity arthaḥ | aniścita iti vacan tṛṇakāṣṭhādigrahaṇāgrahaṇaparibhāṣāvihīnaviṣayam etad iti darśayati | paribhāṣitaviṣaye tu yathā paribhāṣā kṛtā tathaiva | "sa tat gṛhītvā nigacchet" it mūlagrahaṇavyatiriktaviṣayam ity ācāravirodhāya kalpanīyam | śambhus tu "tat gṛhītvā" ity asya "gṛhaṃ gṛhītvā gṛhopakaraṇaṃ gṛhītveti yāvat" iti vyākhyānaṃ kṛtavān, tat "tṛṇakāṣṭheṣṭakādikam" ityādinā viruddham ity upekṣaṇīyam | vyāso 'pi mandiradravyasyaiva saṃbandham āha |

	snehena tu ciraṃ kālaṃ mandiraṃ kurute tu yaḥ |

	nirgacchatas tasya dāru dattastomasya nānyathā ||

tasya parabhūmau mandirādi kartuḥ | nirgacchataḥ tat sthānaṃ parityajya gacchataḥ | yad dārvādikaṃ mandirarūpeṇa sthitaṃ tad bhāṭake datte taddātur eva, no ced bhūmisvāmina evety arthaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ svāmiviṣayāṇi**

**atha paṇyastrītadupabhoktṛviṣayāṇi**

tatra nāradaḥ |

	śulkaṃ gṛhītvā paṇyastrī necchantī dviguṇaṃ vahet |

	anicchan śulkadātāpi śulkahānim avāpnuyāt ||

"necchantī dviguṇaṃ vahet" ity asya kvacid apavādaḥ smṛtyantare darśitaḥ |

	vyādhitā saṃbhramā vyagrā rājadharmaparāyaṇā |

	āmantritā ca nāgacched avācyā vaḍavā smṛtā ||

atyantāvaśyakeṣu kāryeṣu jātasambhramā tadupabhoktṛviṭaviṣate saṃbhramāpadenoktā | tatraiva vyākulā vyagrāpadenoktā | vaḍavā dāsī, tadgrahaṇam atra paṇyastrīpradarśanārtham, vyādhyādyanvayanibandhanasyāvācyatvasyānyatrāpi tulyatvāt | upabhoktāraṃ tu praty āha nāradaḥ |

	aprayacchaṃs tathā śulkam anubhūya pumān striyam |

	akrameṇa tu saṃgacchet ghātadantanakhādibhiḥ ||

	ayonau yaḥ samākrāmet bahubhir vāpi sādhanaiḥ |

	śulkaṃ so 'ṣṭaguṇaṃ dāpyo vinayaṃ tāvad eva tu || iti |

paṇyastriyās tv aparādhe daṇḍādikaṃ matsyapurāṇe darśitam |

	gṛhītvā vetanaṃ veśyā lobhād anyatra gacchati |

	tāṃ damaṃ dāpayed dadyād itarasyāpi bhāṭakam ||

vivādāntaranirṇetṝn vinā nirṇetrṝn āha nāradaḥ |

	veśyāpradhānā ye tatra kāmukās tadgṛhopitāḥ |

	tatsamuttheṣu kāryeṣu nirṇayaṃ saṃśaye viduḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ paṇyastrītadupabhoktṛviṣayāṇi**

**samāptaś ca vetanānapākarmākhyasya padasya vidhivitānaḥ**

**atha nāradābhiprāyataḥ prācīnapadaśeṣabhūtasya svāmipālavivādākhyasa padasya vidhir ucyate**

manor matyā tu krayavikrayānuśayākhyapadāntaraṃ svatantatayāsya padasyoktatvād anantaram evoddeśakramād vaktavyam | nāradīyoddeśakramānusāriṇaś ca vayam ity anavadyam ihābhidhānam | abhidhānapratijñā ca manunā svātantryaprakaṭanārtham kṛtā |

	paśuṣu svāmināṃ caiva pālānāṃ ca vyatikrame |

	vivādaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi yathāvad dharmatattvataḥ ||

vivādaṃ vivādāpanodakaṃ vidhim ity arthaḥ | paśuṣv iti pratijñāviṣayaniyamārtham uktam | tena paśuviṣaye tatsvāmipālayor vyatikrame bhṛtikalpanādividhir asmin pade pratipādyatayā pratijñātaḥ, na punaḥ sasyādiṣu paśūnāṃ svāmiṇāṃ pālānāṃ ca vyatikrame nivāraṇadaṇḍatāḍanādividhiḥ | ato 'tra nivāraṇādividhiḥ prāsāṅgika eveti mantavyam | ato 'smin pade 'smabhiḥ pratijñātabhṛtikalpanādividhipratipādakāni yāni vacanāni tāny eva likhyante | tatra nāradaḥ |

	gavāṃ śatād vatsatarī dhenuḥ syād dviśate bhṛtiḥ |

	pratisaṃvatsaraṃ gope saṃdhohaś cāṣṭame 'hani ||

pratisaṃvatsaraṃ vatsatarī samatikrāntavatsatvāvasthā gaur bhṛtiḥ | pālake pālyamānagośatavaśād deyā bhavati śatād adhike tu vatsatarīsthāne savatsā gaur aṣṭame 'hani saṃdohaś ca bhavatīty arthaḥ | saṃdohaḥ sarvadohaḥ | yathāha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	tathā dhenubhṛtaḥ kṣīraṃ labhetāsyāṣṭame 'khilam | iti |

etena śambhūktaṃ dhenusaṃdohayor nairapekṣyeṇa bhṛtitvaṃ nirastam ity upakṣaṇīyam | anayā diśā śatadviśatasaṃkhyāto nyūnādhikasaṃkhyākānāṃ gavāṃ mahiṣyādipaśvantarāṇāṃ ca bhṛtīyattā kalpanīyā | paribhāvitabhṛtiviśeṣābhāvaviṣayam etat, tatsadbhāvaviṣaye 'pīyattāparibhāṣābhāve tv āha manuḥ |

	gopaḥ kṣīrabhṛto yas tu sa duhyād daśato varām |

	gosvāmyanumato bhṛtyaḥ .......... || iti |

duhyāt svabhṛtyartham iti śeṣaḥ | etad uktaṃ bhavati: daśato daśadogdhīṇāṃ madhye varām utkṛṣṭāṃ svīkṛtya tatkṣīraṃ kṣīrabhṛto bhṛtyo gṛhṇīyād iti | daśadogdhrīpālanārthā bhṛtir iyam | anayā diśā daśasaṃkhyāto nyūnādhikasaṃkhyākānāṃ gavāṃ pālanārthā mahiṣyādipālanārthāpi bhṛtiḥ kalpanīyā | akṣīrapaśūnāṃ tu bhṛtiḥ kīramūlyataḥ kalpanīyā | dravyāntareṇābhṛtapālakaviṣaye kṣīrabhṛto yā proktā bhṛtiḥ saiva bhavatīty āha sa eva: "sā syāt pāle 'bhṛte bhṛtiḥ" | nāradas tu svāmipālayoḥ kartavyam āha |

	upānayed gāṃ gopāya pratyahaṃ rajanīkṣaye |

	samarpitāś ca tā gopaḥ sāyāhne pratyupānayet ||

gograhaṇaṃ paśūpalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva yājñāvalkyaḥ |

	yathārpitān paśūn gopaḥ sāyaṃ pratyarpayet tathā | iti |

kṛtavetanaḥ pālaka ity arthaḥ | pramādagrahaṇaṃ pālakadoṣopalakṣaṇārtham | tena maraṇādau nirdoṣaḥ pālako na dāpyaḥ | na punaḥ pramādamātrarahitaḥ, ata eva manuḥ |

	vighuṣya tu hṛtaṃ corair na pālo dātum arhati |

	yadi deśe ca kāle ca svāminaḥ svasya śaṃsati ||

vighuṣya paśūnām anudhāvanārthaṃ śṛṅgakalahaveṇvādibhir ghoṣaṃ kṛtvety arthaḥ | deśo yatra svāmī sthitaḥ so 'bhimataḥ, kālo 'py āharaṇakālād anativilambito 'bhimataḥ | evaṃbhūtaṃ deśaṃ kālaṃ vā yadā svadoṣeṇātikramya deśāntare kālāntare vā śaṃsati tadā tv aparādhitatvāt tadanusāreṇa dātum arhatīti gamyate | vyāsas tv adāpyatvaṃ nidoṣatvābhidhānād abhihitaṃ bhavatīty abhisaṃdhāya nirdoṣatvam eva pālakasya kvacid āha |

	pālagrahe grāmaghāte tathā rāṣṭrasya vibhrame |

	yat praṇaṣṭaṃ hṛtaṃ vā syān na pālas tatra kilbiṣī ||

puruṣakārākaraṇe 'pīti śeṣaḥ | anyatra tu puruṣakārākaraṇe bhavaty eva kilbiṣī | ata eva manuḥ |

	naṣṭaṃ vinaṣṭaṃ krimibhiḥ śvahataṃ viṣame mṛtam |

	hīnaṃ puruṣakāreṇa pradadyāt pāla eva tu ||

naṣṭaṃ kutrety aviditam | krimibhir vinaṣṭaṃ pradhvastam | śvahataṃ śunā hatam | viṣame hataṃ kandararandhrapradeśādau mṛtam | puruṣakāras tu nāradena darśitaḥ |

	krimicoravyāghrabhayād darīśvabhrāc ca pālayet |

	vyāyacche chaktitaḥ krośet svāmine vā nivedayet ||

vyāyacchet vyasananirāsāya yatetety arthaḥ | svāmine nivedanam aśaktapālakaviṣayam | yad āha sa eva |

	syāc ced govyasanaṃ gopo vyāyacchet tatra śaktitaḥ |

	aśaktas tūrṇam āgatya svāmine vā nivedayet ||

puruṣakāram akurvāṇaḥ prāguktavināśakair vinaṣṭāṃ vyaktiṃ daṇḍaṃ ca yathākramaṃ svāmini dātum arhatīty āha sa eva |

	avyāyacchann avikrośan svāmine vānivedayan |

	voḍhum arhati gopas tāṃ vinayaṃ caiva rājani ||

vinayapramāṇam āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	pāladoṣād vināśe tu pāle daṇḍo vidhīyate |

	ardhatrayodaśapaṇaḥ svāmine dravyam eva ca ||

ardhatrayodaśapaṇaḥ sārdhatrayodaśakārṣāpaṇaḥ, saḥ pāle vidheyo daṇḍa ity arthaḥ | "dravyaṃ vinaṣṭadravyaṃ mūlyaṃ vinaṣṭapaśumūlyaṃ ca svāmine dadyāt" iti viṣṇusmaraṇāt | pāladoṣapradarśaṇārthaṃ tenaiva kaścit pāladoṣo 'pi darśitaḥ: "divā paśūnāṃ vṛkādyupaghāte pāle tv anāyati pāladoṣaḥ" iti | anāyāti upaghātanivāraṇāyānāgacchatīty arthaḥ | upaghātaś cātra prāṇāṇtiko vighāto vivakṣito na punar upadravaleśaḥ | yad āha manuḥ |

	ajāvike tu saṃruddhe vṛkaiḥ pāle tv anāyati |

	yāṃ prasahya vṛko hanyāt pāle tat kilbiṣaṃ bhavet ||

yām ajāvikajātīyāṃ vyaktim ity arthaḥ | vṛkagrahaṇaṃ tādṛśahiṃsrapradarśanārtham | sugamasthalasthitaviṣayam etat | durgamasthalasthitaviṣaye tu śakyapuruṣakārasyāpi pālakasya niṣkilbiṣatvam ity āha sa eva |

	tāsāṃ ced avaruddhānāṃ carantīnāṃ mitho vane |

	yām upetya vṛko hanyān na pālas tatra kilbiṣī ||

vane durgamāraṇye 'varuddhānāṃ pālakena sthāpitānām | nāradena tu manūktavacanadvayasamānārthavacanatrayānantaram ajāviketarapaśupālakeṣu svavacanatrayārthātideśaḥ kṛtaḥ |

	anena sarvapālānāṃ vivādaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ | iti |

tathā pālake viśuddhisiddhyupāyam āha sa eva |

	mṛteṣu ca viśuddhiḥ syād vālaśṛṅgādidarśanāt | iti |

kālavaśād apy araṇye mṛteṣu paśuṣu paśvapahāraśaṅkānivṛttyarthaṃ vālaśṛṅgādi paśvavayavabhūtaṃ pālako darśayed ity arthaḥ | ādiśabdārtho manunā prapañcitaḥ |

	karṇau carma ca vāḷāṃś ca bastiṃ snāyuṃ ca rocanām |

	paśuṣu svāmināṃ dadyāt mṛteṣv aṅgāni darśayet ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ svāmipālākhyasya padasya vidhivitānam**

**atha prāsaṅgikāni paśvādivyatiriktaviṣaye yāni vivādāpanodakavacanāni tāni likhyante**

tatra kātyāyanaḥ |

	kṣetrārāmavivīteṣu gṛheṣu paśupādiṣu |

	grahaṇaṃ tatpraviṣṭānāṃ tāḍanaṃ vā bṛhaspatiḥ ||

ārāmaḥ upavanam | vivītaśabdena tṛṇakāṣṭhasamṛddhaḥ parapartigṛhītaḥ pradeśa ucyate | paśupādiḥ goṣṭhādiḥ | grahaṇaṃ nivāraṇārthaṃ karṇādyavayavagrahaṇaṃ tāḍanaṃ vā kṣetrādiṣu praviṣṭānāṃ parapaśūnāṃ kartavyam iti bṛhaspatiḥ brūta ity arthaḥ | grahaṇaṃ vatsādīnām, sthūlavṛṣādīnāṃ tu tāḍanam iti vyavasthā tu yogyatayādhyavaseyā | tāḍanam api nivāraṇārthād adhikaṃ na kāryam, yad āha sa eva |

	adhamottamamadhyānāṃ paśūnāṃ caiva tāḍane |

	svāmī tu vivaded yatra daṇḍaṃ tatra prakalpayet ||

yatra svāmī smṛtyācāramārgavyapetād adhikatāḍane vivadeta tatra tāḍanādhikyānusāreṇa daṇḍaprakalpanam | paśunivāraṇopāyāntaraṃ cāha sa eva |

	ajāteṣv eva sasyeṣu kuryād āvaraṇaṃ mahat |

	duḥkheneha nivaryante labdhasvādurasā mṛgāḥ ||

aṭavīnikaṭavartikṣetraviṣayam etad iti mṛgagrahaṇāt gamyate | mārgāsannakṣetraviṣaye tv āha nāradaḥ |

	pathi kṣetre vṛtiḥ kāryā yām uṣṭtro nāvalokayet |

	na laṅghayet paśur nāśvo na ca bhindyāc ca sūkaraḥ ||

vṛtiḥ varaṇaṃ kaṇṭakitaśākhābhiḥ prāntataḥ pariśrayaṇam iti yāvat | pathigrahaṇaṃ saṃbādhasthānopalakṣaṇārtham | saṃcārapathagrahaṇopadhyantaram āha |

	pathi grāmavivītānte na doṣo hy alpakālakam | iti |

dīrghakālacāre tu daṇḍam arhatīti vyatirekād gamyate, pālakasya tatra doṣasaṃbhavāt | tathā ca doṣa ity anuvṛttau gautamaḥ: "pathi kṣetre 'nāvṛte pālakṣetrikayoḥ" iti | dīrghakālaṃ paśutaḥ sasyapīḍana iti śeṣaḥ | kṣetrikaḥ kṣetrakārī, tasya vṛtim akurvato rājabhāgavināśanibandhano doṣaḥ, tataś ca so 'pi doṣānusāreṇa daṇḍya ity abhiprāyaḥ | sapālapaśusvāminas tu doṣas tadabhāve pālaksyaiva vijñeyo bhṛtyāparādhanibandhanatvāt svāmyaparādhasya | evaṃ ca yatra pālasya doṣo na vidyate tatra sapālapaśusvāmino 'pi doṣābhāvād vinaṣṭadhānyādimūlyaṃ kṣetrikāya svāmina ca deyam iti mantavyam | vipālapaśusvāmināpi na deyam, paśor vyatikrame 'pi sapālasyeva tasyāpy aparihāryatayā vyatikramābhāvāt | ata evādaṇḍyatvam api pālavat tasyāsmin viṣaye veditavyam | ata evāsya kṣetrikeṇāpi śado na dāpyaḥ | doṣasmaraṇāc ca, tathā ca uśanāḥ |

	gobhir vināśitaṃ dānyaṃ yo naraḥ pratiyācate |

	pitaras tasya nāśnanti nāśnanti tridivaukasaḥ || iti |

evaṃ ca yad uktaṃ manunā,

	sarvatra tu śado deyaḥ kṣetrikāyeti dhāraṇā |

iti, tat nidoṣaviṣayād anyatreti mantavyam | sarvatragrahaṇaṃ tu vipāle 

pi paśau kṣetrikasya śadalābho yathā syād ity evamartham | śadaḥ kṣetrapālam iti dhāraṇā eṣa niścaya ity arthaḥ | daṇḍas tu nirdoṣaviṣayād anyatreti sa evāha |

	kṣetreṣv anyeṣu tu paśuḥ sapādaṃ paṇam arhati | iti |

paśur arhati paśoḥ svāmī pālo vārhatīty arthaḥ | paśumukhena tatsvāminaḥ pālakasya vābhidhānaṃ paśubahutve pratipaśu sapādapaṇavidhānārtham | tena grāmādisamīpavṛttikṣetrādāv api vṛtiḥ kāryaiva | vṛtau śvādibhiḥ kṛtaṃ chidraṃ kaṇṭkādibhiḥ punar niśchidraṃ kuryād ity āha manuḥ |

	chidraṃ ca pūrayet sarvaṃ śvasūkaramukhānugam | iti |

evaṃ paśunivāraṇopāye kṛte 'pi tam atikramya sasyanāśe sa evāha |

	pathi kṣetre parivṛte grāmāntīye 'tha vā punaḥ |

	sapālaḥ śatadaṇḍārho vipālaṃ vārayet paśum ||

grāmāntīye grāmārāmādisamīpavartikṣetre | parivṛta iti viśeṣaṇam ihānvīyate | evaṃ cāyam arthaḥ: vṛtim atikramya grāsād adhikasasyaghātī sapālaḥ paśuḥ kārṣāpaṇaśatadāṇḍārhaḥ, tatpaśupālakaḥ śatadaṇḍanaṃ daṇḍanīya iti yāvat | vipālaṃ paśuṃ punaḥ kṣetriko laguḍādinā nivārayed iti | kṣetrikāyātra sapālasya paśoḥ svāminā vinaṣṭadhānyaṃ deyam, asminn arthe mūlaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ | vṛtim utkrāmataḥ paśor yathāśakty anivāraṇa evāyaṃ daṇḍaḥ | tatra nāradaḥ |

	utkramya tu vṛtiṃ yaḥ syāt sasyaghāto gavādibhiḥ |

	pālaḥ śāsyo bhavet tatra na cec chaktyā nivārayet ||

vṛtirāhityenāparihāryasasyaghātaviṣaye 'py āha sa eva |

	grāmopānte ca yat kṣetraṃ vivītānte mahāpathe |

	anāvṛtaṃ cet tannāśe na pālasya vyatikramaḥ ||

mahāpatha iti vadann aparihāryamārgagāmino vyatikramābhāvaṃ darśayati | atrārthād daṇḍābhāvo 'py uktaḥ | mānave tu sākṣād evoktaḥ |

	tatrāparivṛtaṃ dhānyaṃ vihiṃsyuḥ paśavo yadi |

	na tatra praṇayed daṇḍaṃ nṛpatiḥ paśurakṣiṇām ||

nivāraṇe 'nicchūnām iti śeṣaḥ | yad āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	pathi gṛāme vivītānte kṣetre doṣo na vidyate |

	akāmataḥ kāmacāre coravad daṇḍam arhati ||

antaśabdo 'tra samīve vartate, sa ca pathyādiṣi pratyekam abhisaṃbadhyate | atra daṇḍavyavasthām āha gautamaḥ: "paśupīḍane svāmidoṣaḥ pālasaṃyukta tu tasmin" iti | paśupīḍane paśuvaśāt sasyapīḍana iti yāvat | vipālapaśupīḍane svāmina eva doṣaḥ, pālasaṃyukte tu pāle 'pīty arthaḥ | tatra svāmina eva doṣe tasya śadadaṇḍau, dvayor doṣe tu svāminaḥ śadaḥ pālasya daṇḍa eva, na punaḥ śadopīti mantavyam | yat tu nāradenoktam,

	yā naṣṭā pāladoṣeṇa gauḥ kṣetraṃ tu vināśayet |

	na tatra svāmino doṣaḥ pālas taṃ daṇḍam arhati ||

iti, tatra svāmino daṇḍaprāpakadoṣābhāva ukto na punaḥ śadadānaprāpakadoṣābhāvo 'pīty avirodhaḥ | naṣṭā aviditasthānā | yat tu bṛhaspatinoktam,

	sasyān nivārayed gās tu vīrṇadoṣo dvayor bhavet |

	svāmī śadadamaṃ dāpyaḥ pālas tāḍanam arhati ||

iti, śadaś ca damaś ceti śadadamam ity asya vigrahaḥ | yac ca yājñavalkyenoktam,

	gopyas tāḍyas tu gomī tu pūrvoktaṃ daṇḍam arhati |

iti, gopaḥ paśupālaḥ, gomī paśusvāmī | tad idaṃ dvayam api samulasasyanāśaviṣayaṃ, tatra punaḥ prarohābhāvenāparādhādhikyāt, svāmino 'pi daṇḍārhatāc ca | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	samūlasasyanāśe tu tatsvāmī prāpnuyāc chadam |

	vadhena gopo mucyeta daṇḍaṃ svāmini pātayet ||

tatsvāmī sasyasvāmī | śado 'tra atyantavināśānusāreṇa śadakalpakaiḥ kalpitaḥ | śadakalpakāś ca bādhitakṣetrasya samantato yāni kṣetrāṇi tatkāriṇo vijñeyāḥ,

	gobhis tu bhakṣitaṃ sasyaṃ yo naraḥ pratiyācate |

	sāmantānumataṃ deyaṃ dhānyaṃ vā tatra vāpitam ||

iti tenaivoktatvāt | vadho 'tra kaśādinā tāḍanam | daṇḍo 'tra sa eva veditavyo yo yājñavalkyena pūrvam uktaḥ | kaḥ punar asau | ucyate |

	māṣān aṣṭau tu mahiṣī sasyaghātasya kāriṇī |

	daṇḍanīyā tadardhaṃ tu gaus tadardham ajāvikam ||

	bhakṣayitvopaviṣṭhānāṃ yathokād dviguṇo damaḥ |

	samam eṣāṃ vivītasthe kharoṣṭraṃ mahiṣīsamam || iti |

ayam arthaḥ: parasasyaghātakāriṇyā bāletaramahiṣyāḥ svāmī pratimahiṣy aṣṭau māṣān daṇḍanīyaḥ | uktaviśeṣaṇadvayayuktagosvāmī caturo māṣān | tathāvidhacchāgameṣasvāmī ca dvau dvau māṣau | eṣām eva paśūnāṃ sasyabhakṣaṇād ārabhya yāvacchayanam anivāritānāṃ svāmī tathoktadaṇḍād dviguṇaṃ pūrvavad daṇḍanīyaḥ | vivītasthatṛṇādyupaghāte 'pi pūrvoktapaśusvāmī sasyakṣetropaghātavad daṇḍanīyaḥ | kharoṣṭtrasvāmī mahiṣīsvāmivad daṇḍanīya iti | vācakapadena mahiṣīsvāmītyādinā daṇḍe vaktavye mahiṣītyādyavācakapadena daṇḍoktiḥ pratipaśv evaṃ daṇḍanīyaṃ ity abhidhānārtheti mantavyam | atrāparādhānusāreṇa daṇḍanārthaṃ tāmrikamāṣo grāhyaḥ, na punaḥ sovarṇo rājato vā | tāmrikaś ca māṣaḥ kārṣāpaṇasya ṣoḍaśo bhāgo bhavati | yais tv anurūpadaṇḍanārtham,

	māṣo viṃśatitamo bhāgaḥ paṇasya parikīrtitaḥ |

iti nāradenoktamāṣaḥ svīkṛtaḥ, teṣām,

	saṃkhyā raśmirajomūlā manunā samudāhṛtā |

	kārṣāpaṇonā sā divye niyojyā vinaye tathā ||

iti bārhaspatyavacanavirodho durvāraḥ, manunodāhṛtamāṣāsvīkārāt | tāmrikamāṣasya tu manunoktasya svīkāre na kenāpi virodha ity alaṃ parapakṣayutkāyuktacintayā | yat tu manunoktam "sapādapaṇam arhati " iti, tat svāmimatipūrvapaśuvyatikramaviṣayam | yājñavalkyavacanaṃ tv abuddhipūrvaviṣayam iti na tayor virodhaḥ | yat tu viṣṇunoktam "mahiṣī cet sasyaghātaṃ kuryāt pālas tv aṣṭau māṣān daṇḍyaḥ apālāyāṃ svāmī" iti, tad asamūlasasyanāśaviṣayam, anyataradaṇḍasyālpāparādha eva yuktatvāt | yat tu śaṅkhalikhitābhyām uktam "mahiṣī daśa" iti, tan nāradoktamāṣābhiprāyam, tathātve phalatas tāmrikāṣṭamāṣātmaka eva daṇḍo bhaviṣyati, tena na "māṣān aṣṭau" iti yājñavalkyavacanena virodhaḥ, na ca "saṃkhyā raśmi" ityādibārhaspatyavacanena | tac ca tābhyām evoktam "kharoṣṭraṃ ṣoḍaśa ajāvikaṃ caturaḥ" iti, tat bhakṣayitvopaviṣṭakharādiviṣayam | yat tu kātyāyanenoktam,

	dāpayet paṇapādaṃ gāṃ dvau pādau māhaṣīṃ tathā |

iti, yac ca nāradena,

	gāvaḥ pādaṃ pradaṇḍyās tu mahiṣyo dviguṇaṃ tataḥ |

iti, tat tāmrikamāṣasvīkārapakṣe phalataḥ samānatvād aviruddham eva | nāradoktamāṣasvīkārapakṣe tu paraṃ virodhaḥ | ata eva cāsau pakṣo nāsmākam iti sarvam aviruddham | yat tu smṛtyantaram,

	paṇasya pādau dvau gāṃ tad dviguṇāṃ mahaṣīṃ tathā|

	tathājāvikavatsānāṃ pādau daṇḍaḥ prakīrtitaḥ |

iti, tat bhakṣayitvopaviṣṭaviṣayam, vacobhaṅgyā tadviṣayadaṇḍasyaivābhidhānāt | yat punar nāradenoktam,

	māṣaṃ gāṃ dāpayed daṇḍaṃ dvau māṣau mahiṣīṃ tathā |

	tathājāvikavatsānāṃ daṇḍaḥ syād ardhamāṣakaḥ || 

iti, atra rājatasya māṣasya māṣaśabdenābhidhānaṃ bhakṣayitvopaviṣṭavatsaviṣayaṃ mantavyam |

	vasatāṃ dviguṇaḥ proktaḥ savatsānāṃ caturguṇaḥ |

iti smṛteḥ samānārthatvam evāsya vacanasya bhaviṣyati | dakṣiṇāpathe ṣodaśa tāmrikamāṣāṇām ekasya rājatamāṣasya tulyamūlatvāt | atha vātrāpi tāmrikamāṣasyaivābhidhānam astu, tathāpi muhūrtamātrabhakṣaṇaviṣayatvād avirodhaḥ | tathā ca "daṇḍaṃ prāpnuyāt" ity anuvṛttāv āhatuḥ śaṅkhalikhitau "rātrau carantī gauḥ pañca māṣān divā trīn muhūrte māṣaṃ grāse tv adaṇḍaḥ" iti | etad apratyakṣacārakaviṣayam,

	pratyakṣacārakāṇāṃ tu coradaṇḍaḥ smṛto budhaiḥ |

iti nāradasmaraṇāt | grāse tv adṇḍa ity asyāyam arthaḥ: mahiṣyādibhiḥ parasasyādiṣu kavalamātrabhakṣaṇe kathaṃcit kṛte pālasya svāmino vā svalpo 'pi daṇḍo nāstīti | āturapaśuviṣaye tu bahusasyanāśe 'py evam evādaṇḍa iti doṣābhāvābhidhānamukhenāha nāradaḥ |

	rājagrahagṛhīto vā vajrāśanihato 'pi vā |

	atha sarpeṇa vā daṣṭo vṛkṣād vā patito bhuvi ||

	vyāghrād abhihato vāpi vyādhibhir vāpy upadrutaḥ |

	na tatra doṣaḥ pālasya na ca doṣo 'sti gominām || iti |

āturāṇām anivāryatvād iti śeṣaḥ | nivāryāṇām api keṣāṃcit paśūnāṃ vyatikrame daṇḍo nāstīty āha sa eva |

	gauḥ prasūtā daśāhāntaṃ mahokṣo vājikuñjarāḥ |

	nivāryās tu prayatnena teṣāṃ svāmī na daṇḍabhāk ||

daśdinaparyantaṃ prasūtāyāḥ niroddhum aśakyāyāḥ tatsvāmī na daṇḍabhāk | mahokṣasy sarvāsāṃ garbhādhānārthaṃ sarvadā bandhanāyogāt tatsvāmī na daṇḍabhāk | vājikuñjarāṇāṃ svāmino 'daṇḍabhāktve hetur uṣanasā darśitaḥ |

	adaṇḍyā hastino hy aśvā prajāpālahitāḥ smṛtāḥ | iti |

evaṃ ca rājakīyānām uktavadbhāvād adaṇḍyatvam eva | svāmigrahaṇaṃ pālasyāpy upalakṣaṇārtham | yad āha manuḥ |

	anirdaśāhām gāṃ sūtāṃ vṛṣān devapaśūṃs tathā |

	apālān vā sapālān vā na daṇḍyān manur abravīt ||

vṛṣāḥ mahokṣāḥ, atha vā vṛṣotsargavidhānena utsṛṣṭāḥ,

	adaṇḍyāḥ kāṇakūṭāś ca vṛṣaś ca kṛtalakṣaṇaḥ |

ity uśanasoktatvāt | kāṇaḥ ekākṣaḥ | kūṭaḥ ekaśṛṅgaḥ | kṛtalakṣaṇaḥ pratapāyasena kṛtalāñchanaḥ, asya asvāmikatvāt svāmidaṇḍābhāve 'pi sasyarakṣaṇārthaṃ kadācit kṛtalakṣaṇānāṃ pāle kṛte na tasya daṇḍabhāgitvam, teṣāṃ durnivāratvād iti vaktuṃ "vṛṣaś ca kṛtalakṣaṇaḥ" ity uktam | evam eva vaktuṃ mānave "devapaśūṃs tathā" ity uktam | devapaśavo hi devatāpratimādīnāṃ kṣīrasnānādyarthaṃ taduddeśena dattāḥ, na ca tatra vastutaḥ svasvāmibhāvo 'stīti kṛtalakṣaṇavṛṣavat pāladaṇḍāpavādārtham eva devapaśugrahaṇam | prasūtagovad ubhayadaṇḍābhāva eva uśanasā goviśeṣe darśitaḥ |

	adaṇḍyāgantukī gauś ca prasūtā hy abhicāriṇī |

āgantukī anabhyastasthānā | abhicāriṇī pracuratāḍanāt pracyutā punaḥ svayūdhābhigāminī | evaṃ kālaviśeṣe tenaiva gomātraviṣaye daṇḍābhāvo darśitaḥ |

	adaṇḍyāś cotsave gāvaḥ śrāddhakāle tathaiva ca | iti |

atra vyāsaḥ |

	ākramya yad dvijair bhuktaṃ parikṣīṇaiś ca bāndhavaiḥ |

	gobhiś ca naraśārdūla vājimedhād viśiṣyate ||

atra manuḥ |

	etad vidhānam ātiṣṭhed dhārmikaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ |

	svāmināṃ ca paśūnāṃ ca pālānāṃ ca vyatikrame ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ paśvādivyatikramaviṣayāṇi**

**atha pratipannāsvāmivikrayaviṣayāṇi**

evaṃ vetanānapākarmākhyapadaśeṣabhūtaṃ svāmipālavivādākhyaṃ padam, tatprasaktāni ca paśvādivyatikramaviṣayāṇy uktvā idānīm uddeśakramaprāptāsvāmivikrayākhyasya padasya vidhir ucyate |

tatra nāradaḥ |

	dravyam asvāmivikrītaṃ prāptuḥ svāmī tad āpnuyāt | iti|

asvāminā vikrītaṃ svakīyaṃ dravyaṃ yasya pārśve dṛṣṭaṃ tasya sakāśāt svāmī tat gṛhṇīyād ity arthaḥ | etat svāmyananumatyā vikrītadravyaviṣayam,

	vkrīṇīte parasya svaṃ yo 'svāmī svāmyasaṃmataḥ |

iti manunā viśeṣitatvāt | parasya svam ity asyārtho bṛhaspatinā prapañcitaḥ |

	nikṣepānvāhitanyāsshṛtayācitabandhakam |

	upāṃśu yena vikrītam asvāmī so 'bhidhīyate ||

hṛtaṃ apahṛtam | itarāṇi pūrvārdhavartīni padāni bahudhā vyākhyātāni | upāṃśu aprakāśam | prapañco 'yaṃ paradravyatayā prasiddhānāṃ pradarśanārthaḥ | prāyikābhiprāyeṇopāṃśugrahaṇam | tena praṇaṣṭādhigatādikam api paradravyaṃ yen vikrītam, prakāśam api yena nikṣepādikaṃ vikrītam, so 'py asvāmī | asvāmivikrayanirūpaṇasya kiṃ prayojanam ity apekṣite nāradaḥ |

	asvāminā kṛto yas tu krayo vikraya eva ca |

	akṛtaḥ sa tu vijñeyo vyavahāreṣu nityaśaḥ ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	asvāmivikrayaṃ dānam ādhiṃ ca vinivartayet | iti |

evaṃ ca vikrayāditaḥ prāg evāsvāmihaste dṛṣṭaṃ naṣṭam apahṛtaṃ vā svakīyadravyam asvāminaḥ sakāśāt svāmī gṛhṇīyād iti daṇḍāpūpanyāyasiddhaṃ boddhavyam iti | yat tu yājñavalkyenoktam,

	hṛtaṃ praṇāṣṭaṃ yo dravyaṃ parahastād avāpnuyāt |

	anivedya nṛpe daṇḍyāḥ sa tu ṣaṇṇavatiṃ paṇān || iti |

atra na parahastād avāptiḥ daṇḍyatve hetuḥ nyāyyatvāt tasyāḥ, kiṃ tv anivedanam, tasya taskarapracchadanaphalakatvenānyāyyatvāt | yadā punaḥ parahastād avāptum asamarthaḥ svāmī tadā tv āha sa eva |

	naṣṭāpahṛtam āsādya hartāraṃ grāhayan naram |

	deśakālātipattau vā gṛhītvā svayam arpayet ||

ayam arthaḥ: vinaṣṭam apahṛtaṃ vā svakīyaṃ dravyam āsādya adhigantur apahartur vā haste dṛṣṭvā adhigantāram apahartāraṃ vā grāhayed rājapuruṣādibhiḥ sāmādyupāyaiḥ | deśakālātipattau puruṣādyānayanārthaṃ deśāntaragamane kālakṣepe ca kriyamāṇe palāyanasaṅkāryāṃ svayam eva vā gṛhītvā rājapuruṣebhyo rājñe vā samarpayed iti | tato rājapuruṣādibhiḥ sāmādyupāyaiḥ svāmine tad dhanaṃ dāpayitvā daṇḍayitvā cotsraṣṭavya iti grāhaṇagṛhītvārpaṇavidhyor dṛṣṭārthatvabalād gamyamānam iha boddhavyam | yadā tu vikrayād ūrdhvam eva kretur haste krītaṃ paśyati tadāpy āha sa eva: "svaṃ labhetānyavikrītam" iti | anyavikrītaṃ svāmyanumatim antareṇāsvāminā vikrītam ātmīyadravyaṃ kretuḥ sakāśāt svāmī gṛhṇīyād ity arthaḥ viṣṇur api: "ajñānataḥ prakāśaṃ yaḥ paradravyaṃ krīnīyāt tatra tasyādoṣaḥ, svāmī dravyam avāpnuyāt" iti | ajñānataḥ vikretur asvāmitvājñānataḥ | tatra paradravyakratye | tasya kretuḥ | adoṣaḥ tasya tatkaradoṣo nāstīty arthaḥ | vikretus tadoṣo 'sty eva, tenātra vikretaiva taskaravad daṇḍyaḥ na punaḥ kretāpi | yatra punar vikretur asvāmitvaṃ rahasi hīnamūlyena vā vikrayakaraṇādinā jñātvaiva lobhādinā paradravyaṃ krīṇāti tatra kretur api taskaradoṣo 'stīti so 'pi taskaravad daṇḍyaḥ | tathā ca sa eva: "yady aprakāśaṃ hīnamūlyaṃ vā vikrīṇīyāt tadā kretā ca coravac chasyaḥ" iti | bṛhaspatir api jñānato 'jñānataś ca kraye yathākameṇa stenatā nirdoṣatā ca kretur bhavatīti darśayati |

	yena krītaṃ tu mūlyena prāg rājñe viniveditam |

	na tatra vidyate doṣaḥ stenaḥ syād upavikrayāt ||

mūlyena ahīnamūlyena | prāg rājñe viniveditaṃ krayāt prāg eva prakāsitam ity arthaḥ | upavikrayapadaṃ tu svayam eva vyācaṣṭe |

	antargṛhe bahir grāmān niśāyām asato janāt |

	hīnamūlyaṃ ca yat krītaṃ jñeyo 'sāv upavikrayaḥ ||

asato janāt caṇḍālādijanād ity arthaḥ | asadgrahaṇam asvāmitvajñāpakadāsatvādivikretṛviśeṣaṇānām upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	asvāmyanumatād dāsād asataś ca janād rahaḥ |

	hīnamūlyam avelāyāṃ krīṇan taddoṣabhāg bhavet ||

asvāmyanumatāt asvāminaivānumatāt, svāmyanumatiśūnyād iti yāvat | dāsagrahaṇam asvatantropalakṣaṇārtham | taddoṣabhāk taskaradoṣabhāg ity arthaḥ | "kretuḥ steyaṃ rahaḥ krayāt" iti tenaivoktatvāt | evam "kretur doṣo 'prakāśite" iti yājñavalkyavacane 'pi steyadoṣa evokta ity avagantavyam | tathā ca tenaiva,

	hīnād raho hīnamūlye velāhīne ca taskaraḥ |

iti taskaraśabdaṃ prayuñjānena steyadoṣa eva doṣaśabdenokta iti sūcitam | hīnāt kreyadravyāgamopāyahīnād ity arthaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ pratipannāsvāmivikrayaviṣayāṇi**

**atha vipratipannāsvāvikrayaviṣayāni**

tatra kātyāyanaḥ |

	abhiyoktā dhanaṃ kuryāt prathamaṃ jñātibhiḥ svakam | iti |

abhiyoktā nāṣṭikaḥ, naṣṭadhanasyaivātrābhiyoktṛtvāt | so 'nyahaste dhanaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ jñātibhiḥ sākṣibhūtaiḥ svakaṃ svakīyaṃ yathā bhavati tathā tāvat sādhayed ity arthaḥ | kathaṃ nāṣṭikena svakīyatvasādhanam ity apekṣite yājñavalkyaḥ |

	āgamenopabhogena naṣṭhaṃ bhāvyam ............ | iti |

āgamas tu,

	labdhaṃ dānakrayaprāptaṃ śauryaṃ vaivāhikaṃ tathā |

	bāndhavād aprajāj jātaṃ ṣaḍvidhas tu dhanāgamaḥ ||

ityādivacanaiḥ bhuktiprakaraṇe nirūpito draṣṭavyaḥ | tena cāgamenopabhogasahitena jñātiprasiddhena naṣṭadhanasya svakīyatvaṃ sādhyam ity arthaḥ | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	nāṣṭikas tu prakurvīta tad dhanaṃ jñātibhiḥ svakam | iti |

tad dhanaṃ naṣṭadhanam | svakaṃ svakīyam | prakurvīta sādhayed ity arthaḥ | svakīyasya dhanasya svakīyatvāvagatir api dānādyabhāvena sādhanīyety āha sa eva |

	adattatyaktavikrītaṃ kṛtvā svaṃ labhate dhanam | iti |

dattaṃ ca tyaktaṃ ca vikrītaṃ ca dattatyaktavikrītam, tadviparītam adattatyaktavikrītaṃ tathābhūtaṃ bhavatīti pramāṇasiddhaṃ kṛtvā svaṃ svakīyaṃ dhanaṃ nāṣṭiko vikretrādisakāśāl labhata ity arthaḥ | kretāraṃ praty āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	pūrvasvāmī tu tad dravyaṃ yadāgatya vicāreyet |

	tatra mūlaṃ darśanīyaṃ kretuḥ śuddhis tato bhavet ||

mūlaṃ vikretrā | śuddhiḥ abhiyojyatvanivṛttiḥ | mūladarśanānantaraṃ vyāsaḥ |

	mūle samāhite kretā nābhiyojyaḥ kathaṃcana |

	mūlena saha vādas tu nāṣṭikasya tadā bhavet ||

nāṣṭikasya naṣṭadravyasvāminaḥ | tasmin vāde yadi mayāpy anyasmād vikretuḥ sakāśāt krītam ity abhiyojyo vadati tadā tatrāpy ayam eva mūladarśanādikramo 'nusaraṇīyaḥ | yadi tu naṣṭagrāhakatvenāpahārakatvena vā akiṃcitkaramūlatvena darśito dadāti tadāha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	vikretā darśito yatra hīyate vyavahārataḥ |

	kretre rājñe mūlyadaṇḍau pradadyāt svāmine dhanam ||

kretre mūlyaṃ rājñe daṇḍaṃ svāmine dhanaṃ pradadyād ity arthaḥ | nārado 'pi |

	vikretā svāmine 'rthaṃ svaṃ kretre mūlyaṃ ca tatkṛtam |

	dadyād daṇḍaṃ tathā rājñe vidhir asvāmivikraye ||

yadā tu mūlabhūto vikretā deśāntare sthitaḥ tadā tv āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	mūlānayanakālas tu deyo yojanasaṃkhyayā | iti |

yojansaṃkhyayā deśaviprakarṣāpekṣayety arthaḥ | yadā tu kālavilambenāpi mūladarśanaṃ na śakyaṃ tadāpy āha sa eva: "prakāśaṃ vā krayaṃ kuryāt" iti prākkṛtaṃ krayaṃ sākṣivacanāl lokaviditaṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	prakāśaṃ ca krayaṃ kuryāt sādhubhir jñā(tṛ)bhiḥ svakaiḥ |

	na tatrānyā kriyā proktā daivikī na ca mānuṣī ||

kraye prakāśite kretā na rājñā daṇḍya ity āha sa eva |

	viśodhite kraye rājñā vaktavyaḥ sa na kiṃcana | iti |

manur api |

	atha mūlam anāhāryaṃ prakāśakrayaśodhitam |

	adaṇḍyo mucyate rājñā nāṣṭiko labhate dhanam ||

prakāśakrayaśodhitaṃ dhanaṃ kretuḥ sakāśān nāṣṭiko labhate, kretā cādaṇḍyo bhūtvā rājakīyād avarodhān mucyata ity arthaḥ | "atha mūlam anāhāryam" ity anena sati saṃbhave mūlānayanapakṣa eva grāhya ity uktam | uktaṃ ca kātyāyanena |

	asamāhāryamūlas tu krayam eva viśodhayet | iti |

asamāhāryamūla eva krayaṃ viśodhayed ity arthaḥ | tatra,

	yadā kriyā(mūla)m upanyasya punar vādī krayaṃ vadet |

	āharen mūlam evāsau na krayeṇa prayojanam ||

vadet prakāśaṃ krayaṃ vaded ity arthaḥ | yadā mūlaṃ na darśayati kreyaprakāśanaṃ vā na karoti tadāpy āha sa eva |

	anupasthāpayan mūlaṃ krayaṃ vāpy aviśodhayan |

	yathābhiyogaṃ dhanine krayaṃ vāpy aviśodhayan ||

nāṣṭiko 'pi yadā naṣṭasya svakīyatvaṃ na sādhayet tadāpy āha sa eva |

	yadi svaṃ naiva kurute jñātibhir nāṣṭiko dhanam |

	prasaṅgavinivṛttyarthaṃ coravad daṇḍam arhati ||

prasaṅgaḥ atiprasaṅgaḥ | yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	āgamenopabhogena naṣṭaṃ bhāvyam ato 'nyathā |

	pañcabandho damas tatra rājñas tenāvibhāvite ||

vivādāspadasya dhanasya pañcabhāgasaṃmito yatra damo badhyate sa pañcabandhaḥ | alpāparādhaviṣayam etat | mahāparādhviṣaye tv āha vyāsaḥ |

	vādī cen mārgitaṃ dravyaṃ sākṣibhir na vibhāvayet |

	dāpyaḥ syād dviguṇaṃ daṇḍaṃ kretā tad dravyam arhati ||

kretuḥ dravyalābhaḥ pañcabandhaviṣaye 'pi bhavati | yadā ca nāṣṭikaḥ svakīyatvam anuvartamānaṃ ca vibhāvayati tatraiva kretuḥ krītadravyalābho nānyatrety anusaṃdheyam | evaṃ ca yan manunoktam,

	vikrayād yo dhanaṃ kiṃcit gṛhṇīyāt kulasaṃnidhau |

	krayeṇa sa viśuddhaṃ hi nyāyato labhate dhanam ||

iti, yac ca marīcinoktam,

	vaṇigvīdhīparigataṃ vijñātaṃ rājapūruṣaiḥ |

	divā gṛhītaṃ yat kretā sa śuddho labhate dhanam ||

iti, tad etanmārgitadravyāvibhāvanāviṣayam | mārgitadravyavibhāvanāsadbhāvaviṣaye 'pi manumarīcivacanabalāt prakāśakṛtakraye kretur dhanalābho 'stv iti cen, na; na hi vacanaśatenāpy asvāmivikrītaṃ kretuḥ saṃbhavatīti pramātuṃ śakyate | kiṃ ca sarvatra prakāśakrayakretuḥ dhanalābhe prāg uktena "atha mūlam anāhāryam" ityādivacanena saha virodho durvāraḥ syāt | tasmāt prakāśakraye 'pi mārgitadravyavibhāvanābhāva eva kretur dhanalābha ity avagantavyam | sambhunā tūktadoṣaparihārāya manumarīcivacanābhyāṃ kretur dhanayogyatāmātram ucyate, na tu vastutas tasyaiva dhanaṃ bhavatīty ucyata ity uktam; tad ayuktam, yogyatāmātrakathanasyopayogābhāvāt | yadā krayasyāpi sākṣibhir vibhāvanābhāvas tadā tv āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	pramāṇahīnavāde tu puruṣāpekṣayā nṛpaḥ |

	samanyūnādhikatvena svayaṃ kuryād vinirṇayam ||

yasmin vāse nāṣṭikasyānuvartamānasvatvasādhakapramāṇābhāvaḥ, kretuś ca prakāśakrayasādhakapramāṇābhāvas tasmin vāde nāṣṭikakretṛpuruṣayor asādhutvādyapekṣayā vivādāspadaṃ dhanaṃ samanyūnādhikatvena vibhajyaitāvat taveti svayam eva rājā vinirṇayaṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> pramāṇahīnavādo na kutrāpi saṃbhavati, kathaṃcin mānuṣābhāve 'pi divyābhāvasya sarvathā vaktum aśakyatvāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>, asvāmivikraye vāde divyābhāvas tāvad avagamyate,

	abhiyoktā dhanaṃ kuryāt prathamaṃ jñātibhiḥ svakam |

	paścād ātmaviśuddhyarthaṃ krayaṃ kretā svabandhubhiḥ ||

ityādivacanānāṃ sākṣiniyāmakānāṃ taditarapramāṇābhāvābhidhānaparatvāt | kiṃ ca,

	prakāśaṃ ca krayaṃ kuryāt sādhubhir jñātibhiḥ svakaiḥ |

	na tatrānyā kriyā proktā daivikī na ca mānuṣī ||

iti sākṣītarapramāṇaniṣedhād divyābhāvaḥ suvyaktaḥ | evaṃ ca yad uktaṃ kātyāyanena,

	alekhye 'sākṣike daivīṃ vyavahāre vinirdiśet |

iti, tad divyaniṣedhasmṛtyabhāvaviṣayam iti mantavyam | etenaitan nirastam, yat śambhunā mūlānayanakrayaprakāśanarūpam ubhayam adhikṛtyoktam: athobhayaṃ kartum asamarthaś cauryaṃ ca na manyate tadā dravyāpekṣayā divyaṃ deyam |

	alekhye 'sākṣike daivīṃ vyavahāre vinirdiśet |

iti kātyāyanenoktatvād iti | sapramāṇakavade 'pi kvacit samam eva dīyamānaṃ bhavatīti vacobhaṅgyā sa eva darśayati |

	vaṇigvīdhīparigataṃ vijñātaṃ rājapūruṣaiḥ |

	avijñātāśrayāt kretā vikretā yatra vā mṛtaḥ ||

	svāmī datvārdhamūlyaṃ tu pragṛhṇīta svakaṃ dhanam || iti |

avijñātāśrayād avijñātasthānakād vikretuḥ sakāśād ity arthaḥ | svoktaprakāreṇa grahaṇam upapādayitum uktaṃ tenaiva |

	ardhaṃ dvayor api hṛtaṃ tatra syād vyavahārataḥ | iti |

dvayoḥ kretṛnāṣṭikayoḥ vyavahārataḥ svakṛtāpacārataḥ svakīyadhanārdhaṃ hṛtaṃ gatam ity arthaḥ | kaḥ punaḥ svakṛtāpacāra ity apekṣite tenaivoktam |

	avijñātakrayo doṣaḥ tathā cāparipālanam |

	etad dvayaṃ samākhyātaṃ dravyahānikaraṃ budhaiḥ||

avijñātasthānakāt krayo 'vijñātakrayaḥ | atha vā paramārthato 'yaṃ svāmīty avijñātāt krayo 'vijñātakrayaḥ | sa eva kretur doṣo 'pacāraḥ | aparipālanam upekṣā, saiva nāṣṭikasyāpacāraḥ | etad dvayam avijñātakrayāparipālanātmakaṃ dvayaṃ kretṛnāṣṭikayor dravyahānikaratvena samākhyātam ity arthaḥ | marīcir api |

	avijñātaniveśatvād yatra mūlaṃ na labhyate |

	hānis tatra samā kalpyā kretṛnāṣṭikayor dvayoḥ ||

avijñātaniveśatvād avijñātasthānatvāt | mūlaṃ vikretā | bārhapatyavacanād abhinnārtham api asamagratayānyārtham iti etad vacanaṃ mā pratibhātv itīha samuccitaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ vipratipannāsvāmivikrayaviṣayāṇi**

**atha svāmyanarpitatadīyavastubhoktṛviṣayāṇi**

atha prasaṅgāt svāmyanarpitatadīyavastubhoktṛviṣayāṇi kānicin nāradīyāni vacanāni likhyante |

	uddiṣṭam eva bhoktavyaṃ strī paśur vasudhāpi vā |

	anarpitaṃ tu yo bhuṅkte bhuktabhogaṃ pradāpayet ||

	anirdiṣṭaṃ tu yad dravyaṃ vāsaḥ kṣetraṃ gavādikam |

	svabalenaiva bhuñjānaś coravad daṇḍam arhati ||

	anaḍvāhaṃ tathā dhenuṃ nāvaṃ dāsaṃ tathaiva ca |

	anidiṣṭaṃ tu bhuñjāno dadyāt paṇacatuṣṭayam ||

	dāsī naukā tathā dhuryo bandhakaṃ nopabhujyate |

	upabhoktā tu tad dravyaṃ paṇyenaiva viśodhayet ||

	divase dvipaṇaṃ dāsīṃ dhenum aṣṭapaṇaṃ tathā |

	trayodaśam anaḍvāham aśvaṃ bhūmiṃ ca ṣoḍaśa ||

	naukām aśvaṃ ca dhenuṃ ca lāṅgalaṃ kārṣikasya ca |

	balātkāreṇa yo bhuṅkte dāpyaś cāṣṭaguṇaṃ dine ||

	ulūkhale paṇārdhaṃ tu musalasya paṇadvayam |

	śūrpasya ca paṇārdhaṃ tu jaiminir munir abravīt ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ svāmyanarpitatadīyavastubhoktṛviṣayāṇi**

**samāptaś cāsvāmivikrayākhyasya padasya vidhivitānaḥ**

**atha vkrīyāsampradānākhyasya padasya vidhir ucyate**

tatra nāradaḥ |

	vikrīya paṇyaṃ mūlyena kretur yo na prayacchati |

	sthāvaraṃ sakṣayaṃ dāpyo jaṅgamaṃ sakriyāphalam ||

yo gṛhītatanmūlyo vikretā paṇyaṃ jātānuśayaḥ kretre prārthayamānāya nārpayati, tac ca paṇyaṃ yadi sthāvarātmakaṃ tadā kṣayeṇa sahitam asau dāpyaḥ | yadi tu jaṅgamātmakaṃ tadā kriyāphalena sahitam ity arthaḥ | kṣayaśabdena gatabhoga uktaḥ, kretṛsaṃbandhitvena pralīnatvāt | kriyāphalaṃ tu dhenvādeḥ paṇyasya kṣīrādikam, taddohanādikriyāphalatvāt | krayakālāpekṣayā dāpanakāle 'rghavṛddhāv etad draṣṭavyam, arghahrāse tv anyathābhidhānāt | tathā ca sa eva |

	arghaś ced apīheta sodayaṃ paṇyam āvahet | iti |

atra krayakālagṛhītena mūlyena yāvat paṇyam arpaṇakāle 'rghahrāsavaśāt sābyadhikaṃ labhyate tat sodayam, tad āvahet kretāraṃ prāpayet, kretre dadyād iti yāvat | krayakāle 'rpaṇakāle vārghasāmye tv āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	gṛhītamūlyaṃ yaḥ paṇyaṃ kretur naiva prayacchati |

	sodayaṃ tasya dāpyo 'sau .................. || iti |

arghasya hrāsavṛddhigrahaṇābhāvāt tatsāmyaviṣayam idaṃ vacanam iti gamyate | "sodayam" ityāder ayam arthaḥ | adīyamānapaṇyasya yāvatī vṛddhiḥ,

	nikṣepam vṛddhiśeṣaṃ ca krayavikrayam eva ca |

	yācyamānam adattaṃ ced vardhate pañcakaṃ śatam ||

ity akṛtavṛddhiprakaraṇoktaparimāṇataḥ kalpyate, tatsahitaṃ paṇyaṃ dāpya iti | arghasāmye paṇyopacayarūpodayāsaṃbhavād evaṃ vyākhyā kṛtā | tatra nāradaḥ: "sthāyinām eṣa niyamaḥ" iti | deśāntare hṛtvā vikretuṃ ye krīṇanti taditare kretāraḥ sthāyinaḥ, tadviṣayo 'yam "sthāvaraṃ sakṣayaṃ dāpyaḥ" ityādivacanokto niyama ity arthaḥ | kathaṃ tarhy asthāyināṃ niyama ity apekṣite sa evāha: "diglābhaṃ digvicāriṇām" iti | yat paṇyaṃ yasmin digantare vikretuṃ krītaṃ tat paṇyaṃ tasmin digantare vikrīnānasya yo lābhaḥ tena sahitaṃ deyam ity arthaḥ | viṣṇus tu vikretur daṇḍam apy āha: "gṛhītamūlyaṃ yaḥ paṇyaṃ kretur naiva dadyāt tasyāsau sodayaṃ dāpyo rājñā ca paṇaśataṃ daṇḍyaḥ" iti | gṛhītamūlyaṃ vikretrā yasya paṇyasya tad gṛhītammūlyam | tasya tasmai kretra iti yāvat | yas tu gṛhītamūlyasya paṇyasya vikrayānuśayābhāve 'py anarpakaḥ, yaś ca krayānuśayavaśād adattamūlyasya paṇyasyāgrāhakaḥ, tau praty āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	krītvā prāptaṃ na gṛhṇīyād yo na dadyād adūṣitam |

	sa mūlyād daśamaṃ bhāgaṃ datvā svadravyam āpnuyāt ||

	aprāpte 'rthakriyākāle kṛte naiva pradāpayet |

	evaṃ dharmo daśāhāt tu parato 'nuśayo na tu || iti |

adūṣitaṃ jalādineti śeṣaḥ | arthakriyākālo dohyavāhyādipaṇyasya dohanavāhanādikālaḥ | tasminn aprāpte sati agrahaṇe 'dāne vā kṛte 'pi naiva daśamaṃ mūlyabhāgaṃ pradāpayet, kiṃ tu tam adatvaiva svadravyam āpnuyāt | evam ukto dharmaḥ daśāhāt prāg arthakriyākālād ūrdhvaṃ veditavyaḥ | daśāhāt paratas tv anuśayo na kartavyaḥ, anuśayakālasyātītatvād ity abhiprāyaḥ | vāstavasyānuśayakāraṇasyābhāve prāg ukto dharmaḥ | tathā ca kretāram udāhṛtya tenaivoktam |

	krītvānuśayavān paṇyaṃ tyajed dohyādi yo naraḥ |

	aduṣṭam eva kāle tu samūlyād daśamaṃ vahet |

kāle anuśayakāle paramārthataḥ paṇyam aduṣṭam eva duṣṭavṛddhyā tyajet na gṛhṇīyād ity arthaḥ | gṛhītapaṇyatyāgaprakāro 'pi asmin viṣaye tenaiva darśitaḥ |

	krītvā gacchann anuśayaṃ krayī hastam upāgate |

	ṣaḍbhāgaṃ tatra mūlyasya datvā krītaṃ tyajed budhaḥ ||

anuśayakālād ūrdhvam anuśaye saty etad vacanam ity aparādityamatiḥ | sā tv ayuktā, "parato 'nuśayo na tu" ity uktatvāt, anavasthāprasaṅgāc ca | manunāpy anavasthāparihārārtham uktam |

	krītvā vikrīya vā kiṃcid yasyehānuśayo bhavet |

	so 'ntardaśāhāt tad dravyaṃ dadyāc caivādadīta ca ||

	pareṇa tu daśāhasya na dadyān nāpi dāpayet |

	ādadāno dadac caiva rājñā daṇḍyaḥ śatāni ṣaṭ || iti |

vāstavānuśayakāraṇasadbhāvaviṣayam etad dānādānam, mūlyadaśamāṃśadānānukteḥ | krayavikrayād anyatrāpy anuśaye karyavikrayānuśayoktam ūhyam ity āha sa eva |

	yasmin yasmin kṛte kārye yasyehānuśayo bhavet |

	tam anena vidhānena dharmye pathi niveśayet ||

vikrīyāsaṃprayacchato yad vikrītaṃ paṇyaṃ svapārśva eva sthitaṃ tasya daivādivaśān nāśe tat tulyaṃ paṇyaṃ kretre vikretrā deyam iti vacobhaṅgyā nārada āha |

	upahanyeta vā paṇyaṃ dahyetāpahriyeta vā |

	vikretur eva so 'nartho vikrīyāsaṃprayacchataḥ ||

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	rājadaivopaghātena paṇyadoṣa upāgate |

	hānir vikretur evāsau yācitasyāprayacchataḥ ||

yācitasyeti vacanād ayācitasya vikretur aprayacchato na hānir iti darśayati | evaṃ ca "sthāvaraṃ sakṣayaṃ dāpyaḥ" ityādikam api yācitaviṣayam iti mantavyam | paṇyād abhyadhikadāpanasya tatraivocitatvāt | tena kālāntare 'pi paṇyamātram evāyācitaviṣaye deyam | yathā paṇyadoṣa upāgate yācitasyāprayacchato vikretur eva hāniḥ, tathā dīyamānaṃ paṇyam agṛhṇataḥ kretur eva hānir ity āha nāradaḥ |

	dīyamānaṃ na gṛhṇāti krītaṃ paṇyaṃ ca yaḥ krayī |

	sa evāsya bhaved doṣo vikretur yo 'prayacchataḥ ||
