aprayacchato vikretur yo doṣaḥ sa evāsya bhaved ity anvayaḥ | kretur doṣābhidhānasya phalaṃ paṇyamūlyaṃ kretre vikretā na pratyarpaṇīyam iti | dīyamānam iti vadan adīyamānam agṛhṇato na mūlyahānir iti darśayati | yatra vikretrā na yācitam, na ca krayī dīyamānāgrāhakaḥ upāgataś ca paṇyadoṣaḥ, tatra dvayoḥ samā hāniḥ kalpyā, krayānantaram arpaṇagrahaṇaśaithilyena dvayor apy aparādhasāmyāt | yatra punar jātānuśayaḥ kretā vikretra dīyamānaṃ na gṛhṇāti tatrāpy āha sa eva |

	dīyamānaṃ na gṛhṇāti krītvā paṇyaṃ ca yaḥ krayī |

	vikrīṇānas tad anyatra vikretā nāparādhnuyāt ||

krayī jātānuśaya iti śeṣaḥ | yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	vikrītam api vikreyaṃ pūrvakretary agṛhṇati | iti |

agṛhṇati anuśayeneti śeṣaḥ | gṛhṇati tu na vikreyam ity arthād eva siddham | yo vikrīṇāti, yaś ca sadoṣaṃ paṇyaṃ pracchāditadoṣaṃ vikrīṇīte tayoḥ samāno daṇḍa ity āha sa eva |

	anyahaste ca vikrītaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ vā duṣṭavad yadi |

	vikrīṇīte damas tatra mūlyāt tu dviguṇaṃ bhavet ||

nāradas tv asyārthaṃ ślokadvayena vivicya vadan viśeṣam apy āha |

	nirdoṣaṃ darśayitvā tu sadoṣaṃ yaḥ prayacchati |

	mūlyaṃ taddviguṇaṃ dāpyo vinayaṃ tāvad eva tu ||

	tathānyahaste vikrīya yo 'nyasmai tat prayacchati |

	so 'pi taddviguṇaṃ dāpyo vinayaṃ tāvad eva tu || iti |

buddhipūrvakaviṣayam etat, daṇḍadāpyadravyayor atmahattvāt | ata eva bṛhaspatinā sadoṣam udāhṛtyoktam |

	jñātvā sadoṣaṃ yaḥ paṇyaṃ vikrīṇīte vicakṣaṇaḥ |

	tad eva dviguṇaṃ dāpyaḥ tatsamaṃ vinayaṃ tathā ||

abuddhipūrvake tu krayaparāvartanam eva | anyatrāpi kvacit parāvartyam ity āha sa eva |

	mattonmattena vikrītaṃ hīnamūlyaṃ bhayena vā |

	asvatantreṇa mūḍhena tyājyaṃ tasya punar bhavet ||

atra nāradaḥ |

	dattamūlyasya paṇyasya vidhir eṣa prakīrtitaḥ |

	adatte 'nyatra samayān na vikretur atikramaḥ ||

uttarārdhasyāyam arthaḥ |

	adattamūlye paṇye ca vāṅmātreṇa kraye kṛte |

	na parāvartitavyam .................... ||

ityevamādisamayābhāve sati pravṛttau vā nivṛttau vā na kaścid doṣa iti | yatra punaḥ vāṅmātrakrayaparihārārthaṃ vikretṛhaste kretrā kiṃcid dattaṃ tatra vikretṛdoṣavaśena krayāsiddhau kretṛdattadravyaṃ tasmai dviguṇaṃ dadyāt | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	satyaṃkārakṛtaṃ dravyaṃ dviguṇaṃ pratidāpayet | iti |

krayaṃ satyaṃ kartuṃ yat vikretṛhaste kṛtaṃ tat satyaṃkārakṛtam | kretṛdoṣavaśena krayāsiddhau tv āha vyāsaḥ |

	satyaṃkāraṃ ca yo datvā yathākālaṃ na dṛśyate |

	paṇyaṃ bhaven nisṛṣṭaṃ tat dīyamānam agṛhṇataḥ ||

nisṛṣṭaṃ bhaved utsṛṣṭaṃ bhaved ity arthaḥ | atra paṇasyotsargaḥ satyaṃkāradravyotsargānto 'bhimataḥ, anyathā vāṅmātrakrayakartṛtaulye vikretuḥ satyaṃkāragrāhakatā na syāt | atrāpi vikrītam api vikreyam ity uktam anusaṃdheyam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ vikrīyāsaṃpradānākhyasya padasya vidhivitānam**

**atha krītvānuśayākhyasya padasya vidhir ucyate**

tatra nāradaḥ |

	kretā paṇyaṃ parīkṣeta prāk svayaṃ guṇadoṣataḥ | iti |

krītvānuśayo mā bhūd iti svayaṃ kretā prāg eva krayāt paṇyaṃ guṇāḍhyaṃ duṣṭaṃ vety avadhāraṇārthaṃ parīkṣetety arthaḥ | bṛhaspatir api |

	parīkṣeta svayaṃ paṇyam anyeṣāṃ ca pradarśayet | iti |

anyeṣāṃ paṇyaguṇadoṣavidām iti śeṣaḥ | evaṃ ca tatkṣaṇa eva parīkṣaṇaṃ carmādipaṇyaviṣayam | yad āha vyāsaḥ |

	carmakāṣṭheṣṭakāsūtradhānyāsavarasasya tu |

	vasukupyahiraṇyānāṃ sadya eva parīkṣaṇam ||

vasuśabdo yady apy arthamātravācī, tathāpy atra gobalīvardanyāyāc carmādivyatiriktārthaparaḥ | kupyaṃ tu hemarūpyavyatiriktatrapusīsādikaṃ vijñeyam | tathā ca hemarūpye prastutya amarasiṃhenoktam: "tābhyāṃ yad anyat tat kupyam" iti | evaṃ carmādikam atyantāsthayā parīkṣyam | parīkṣya krītasya doṣadarśane 'pi tyāgāyogāt | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	parīkṣitaṃ bahumataṃ gṛhītvā na punas tyajet | iti |

bahumataṃ krītam iti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	parīkṣyābhimataṃ krītaṃ vikretur na bhavet punaḥ | iti |

doṣadarśane 'pīti śeṣaḥ | asyāpavādam āha sa eva |

	tryahād dohyaṃ parīkṣeta pañcāhād vāhyam eva tu |

	muktāvajrapravālānāṃ saptāhaṃ syāt parīkṣaṇam ||

	dvipadām ardhamāsaṃ tu puṃsāṃ tadviguṇaṃ striyāḥ |

	daśāhaṃ sarvabījānām ekāhaṃ lohavāsasām ||

	ato 'rvāk paṇyadoṣas tu yadi saṃjāyate kvacit |

	vikretuḥ pratideyaṃ tat kretā mūlyam avāpnuyāt || iti |

tryahāt krayadinam ārabheti śeṣaḥ | evaṃ pañcāhādāv api śeṣo draṣṭavyaḥ | atra vikretuḥ pratideyam ityādividhidarśanāt tryahād dohyam ityādiparīkṣaṇaṃ krītadohyādidravyaviṣayam iti gamyate | dvipadāṃ puṃsāṃ dāsānām ity arthaḥ | taddviguṇaṃ māsam iti yāvat | striyāḥ dāsījanasyety arthaḥ | ato 'rvāk tryahāder abhyantara ity arthaḥ | saṃjāyata ity anena jñānataḥ siddhir uktā na vastuni niṣpattiḥ | parīkṣāyā jñānataḥ siddhihetutvād ity uktam | jñānataḥ siddhyasiddhī ca kātyāyanena spaṣṭīkṛte |

	avijñātaṃ tu yat krītaṃ duṣṭaṃ paścād vibhāvitam |

	krītaṃ tat svāmine deyaṃ kāle ced anyathā na tu ||

avijñātaṃ parīkṣāśaithiyāt tattvato 'parijñātam | kāle yasya dravyasya yāvān parīkṣākāla uktas tasminn ity arthaḥ | anyathā tatkālātyaye duṣṭatvena vibhāvitam api krītaṃ na tat svāmine deyam, duṣṭagrahaṇasyānuśayahetumatparatvāt | nāradas tu krayānuśayānutpattyarthaṃ karyāt prāk jñātavyam āha |

	kṣayaṃ vṛddhiṃ ca jānīyāt paṇyānām āgamaṃ tathā | iti |

aśvādipaṇyānām ata ūrdhvam apacayo vṛddhir vā bhaviṣyatīti deśakālādivaśāj jānīyāt | kulīnatvādijñānārtham utpādakaṃ janmabhūmyādikaṃ ca jānīyād ity arthaḥ | yas tu na jānāti taṃ praty āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	kṣayaṃ vṛddhiṃ ca vaṇijā paṇyānām avijānatā |

	krītvā nānuśayaḥ kāryaḥ kurvan ṣaḍbhāgadaṇḍabhāk ||

anuśayaḥ paścāttāpaḥ | sa cāpacayādikam avijānatā vaṇijā krītvā vṛthā na kāryaḥ daurmatyāpatteḥ,

	krītvā nānuśayaṃ kuryāt vaṇik paṇyavicakṣaṇaḥ |

ityuktaniṣedhātikramāpatteś ca | ata evānuśayaṃ kurvann asau mūlyaṣaḍbhāgadaṇḍabhāk bhavatīty antyapādena daṇḍābhidhānam upapannam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> vijānatāpy anuśayo na kāryaḥ niṣedhasadbhāvāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span>, kiṃ tv apavādabalāt kriyate, sa cāpavādo 'nuśayāt tasya pratidānasya pratidānaṃ (?) kurvatā nāradenārthād darśitaḥ |

	krītvā mūlyena yat paṇyaṃ kuṣkrītaṃ manyate krayī |

	vikretuḥ pratideyaṃ tat tasminn evāhny avikṣatam ||

	dvitīye 'hni dadat kretā mūlyāt triṃśāṃśam āvahet |

	dviguṇaṃ tat tṛtīye 'hni parataḥ kretur eva tat || iti |

yo duṣkrītaṃ jātam iti kṣayādikaṃ jānan dṛḍhaṃ manyate tena duṣkrītaṃ pratideyam iti saṃbandhaḥ | avikṣatam avikṛtam | vikṛtaṃ ced vaikṛtyasamādhānārthaṃ madhyasthajanakalpitadravyasahitam eva krayadine 'pi pratideyam | dviguṇaṃ pañcadaśāṃśam | parataḥ tṛtīyasyāhṇaḥ parataḥ | kretur eva tat krītvānuśayaṃ kṣayādikaṃ jānann api na kuryād ity arthaḥ | apaśakunato 'nuśaye kṛte 'pi yadi kretā śakunābhijñaḥ tadā yājñavalkyenoktaṃ draṣṭavyam | yadā tu śakunānabhijñas tadā nāradoktaṃ kāryam, nyāyasāmyāt, duṣkrītaṃ manyata iti sāmānyenokteś ca | apaśakunato 'pi kretā duṣkrītaṃ manyata eva | yatra tu bahudoṣatvena jñātvāpi paṇyaṃ svapamūlyena krīṇāti na tatra duṣkrītaṃ manyata iti na krayaḥ parāvartate | tad etad udāharaṇamukhenāha sa eva |

	paribhuktaṃ tu yad vāsaḥ kliṣṭarūpaṃ malīmasam |

	sadoṣam api tat krītaṃ vkretur na bhavet punaḥ ||

parāvartyasamayam aṅgīkṛtya krītaṃ yadi sadoṣaṃ bhavati tad api vikretur na bhavati duṣkrītatve 'pi samayasya balīyastvāt | evam uktaviśeṣaśāstrāṣayakrītvānuśaye (?) krayaparāvṛttiprakāro 'pi vikrayānuśayaprasaṅgataḥ pūrvasmin pade 'smābhir darśitaḥ sa ihāpy anusaṃdheyaḥ | manus tu krītvānuśayānutpattyarthaṃ katipayapaṇyānāṃ vikrayānarhatvam āha |

	nānyad anyena saṃsṛṣṭarūpaṃ vikrayam arhati |

	na sāvadyaṃ na ca nyūnaṃ na dūre na tirohitam ||

dūre sthitam iti śeṣaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ krītvānuśayākhyasya padasya vidhivitānaḥ**

**atha samayānapākarmākhyasya padasya vidhir ucyate**

tatra tadupayoginam arthaṃ tāvad āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	vedavidyāvido viprān śrotriyān agnihotriṇaḥ |

	āhṛtya sthāpayet tatra teṣāṃ vṛttiṃ prakalpayet ||

tatra rājadhānyām, āryanivāsārhatayā kṛte sthāna ity arthaḥ | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	rājā kṛtvā pure sthānaṃ brāhmaṇān nyasya tatra tu | iti |

teṣāṃ vṛttiṃ prakalpayet ity etasyārthaḥ svenaiva vivṛtaḥ |

	anācchedyakarās tebhyaḥ pradadyāt gṛhabhūmayaḥ |

	muktabhāvyāś ca nṛpatiḥ lekhayitvā svaśāsane ||

anācchedyakarā agrāhyakarāḥ | agrāhyarājabhāgadeyakā iti yāvat | etad uktaṃ bhavati: āgāminṛpatibhir agrāhyakarāḥ svena visṛṣṭakarāś ca gṛhabhūmīḥ pradadyād iti | svaśāsanalekhanaprakāro lekhyaprakaraṇokto 'nusaṃdheyaḥ | evaṃ prakalpitavṛttiśālīnam āryavṛndaṃ svadharmānuṣṭhānaniṣṭhaṃ kartuṃ rājā prārthayet | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	traividyaṃ vṛttimad brūyāt svadharmaḥ pālyatām iti |

pauratraivarṇikakṛtyeṣv etair ārtvijyādikam api kāryam | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	nityaṃ naimittikaṃ kāryaṃ śāntikaṃ pauṣṭikaṃ tathā |

	paurāṇāṃ karma kuryus te saṃdigdhe nirṇayaṃ tathā ||

evaṃ samudāyaviśeṣasya kāryaviśeṣa uktaḥ | sarvasmudāyānāṃ ca kāryam āha sa eva |

	grāmaśreṇīgaṇānāṃ ca saṅketaḥ samayakriyā |

	bādhakāle tu sā kāryā dharmakārye tathaiva ca ||

gaṇānāṃ cety atra caśabdaḥ pāṣaṇḍanaigamādīnāṃ samuccayārthaḥ | evaṃ cāyam arthaḥ: grāmaśreṇīgaṇapāṣaṇḍanaigamādīnāṃ kṣudropadravakāle jīrṇoddhārādidharmakārye ca yāṃ pāribhāṣikīṃ samayakriyāṃ vinopadravo duṣpariharaḥ dharmakāryaṃ ca duḥsādham, sā pāribhāṣikī samayakriyā yena yenopādhinā  narāḥ grāmādiśabdābhilapyajātyā kṛtāḥ tattadupādhyupahitair narair bahubhir militaiḥ kāryeti | tathā coktaṃ tenaiva |

	cāṭacorabhaye bādhā sarvasādhāraṇī smṛtā |

	tatropaśamanaṃ kāryaṃ sarvair naikena kenacit ||

cāṭo vṛkaḥ | upaśamanam upaśamanādānam, samaya iti yāvat | samayasvarūpanirūpaṇārthaṃ dvitrāḥ samayāḥ pradarśyante: avarṣeṇopadrave pratikṣetraṃ pratigṛhaṃ vā etāvad dhanaṃ grahayajñādiśāntikasiddhaye deyam ity ekaḥ samayaḥ, tathā coropadrave pratigṛham ekaiko daśaḥ śatrapāṇir ekatrāgantavya iti, tathā rājopadrave rājadarśanārthaṃ pratigraham ekaikaḥ śreṣṭha āgantavya iti | dharmakārye tu samayas tenaiva nirūpitaḥ |

	sabhāprapādevagṛhataṭākārāmasaṃskṛtiḥ |

	tathānathadaridrāṇāṃ saṃskāro yajanakriyā ||

	kulāyanaṃ nirodhaś ca kāryam asmābhir aṃśataḥ |

	yatraital likhitaṃ patre dharmyā sā samayakriyā ||

	pālanīyā samastais tu ...................... || iti |

sabhā janāśrayo maṇṭapaḥ | prapā pānīyaśālikā | ārāmaḥ upavanam | saṃskṛtiḥ jīrṇoddhāraḥ | saṃskāra upanayanādikaḥ, pretadahanādiś ca | yajanakriyā somayāgādikartre dānam | kulāyanaṃ durbhikṣādipīṣāhatayūdhāgamanam | tasmin sati yat saṃvidhānaṃ vidheyaṃ tad eva tacchabdenoktam | nirodhaḥ nirodhanam, durbhikṣādyapagamaparyantaṃ kulāyanadhāraṇam iti yāvat | asmābhiḥ grāmādiśabdapravṛttinimittabhūtopādhiśālibhiḥ | aṃśataḥ gṛhakṣetrapuruṣādiprayuktyā saṃgrahītadhanena, madhyakatvena sthitena dhanena vā | samastaiḥ samudāyibhir iti śeṣaḥ | evaṃ kṛtā samayakriyā saṃpradāyaprāptā ca na kevalaṃ samudāyibhiḥ pālanīyā, kiṃ tu rājñāpi | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	pāṣaṇḍanaigamaśreṇīpūgavrātagaṇādiṣu |

	saṃrakṣet samayaṃ rājā durge janapade tathā ||

pāṣaṇḍāḥ vedoktaliṅgadhārivyatiriktāḥ sarve liṅginaḥ | teṣu maṭhādihitācaraṇādyāḥ samayāḥ santi | naigamāḥ sārthakavaṇikprabhṛtayaḥ, teṣu sakañcukasaṃdeśaharapuruṣatiraskāriṇo daṇḍyā ity evamādayo bahavaḥ samayā vidyante | śreṇayaḥ ekaśilpopajīvinaḥ kuvindādayaḥ, tāsv idam anayaiva śreṇyā vikreyam ityādikāḥ samayāḥ santi | pūgāḥ hastyaśvārohakādayaḥ | vrātagaṇaśabdau kātyāyanena vyākhyātau |

	nānāyudhadharāḥ vrātāḥ samavetās tu kīrtitāḥ |

	kulānāṃ hi samūhas tu gaṇaḥ sa parikīrtitaḥ || iti |

tatra pūge vrāte cānyonyam utsṛjya samare na gantavyam ityādayaḥ santi samayāḥ | gaṇe tu pañcame 'hni pañcame vābde karṇavedhaḥ kartavya ity evamādir asti samayaḥ | gaṇādiṣv ity atrādiśabdena brahmapurī mahājanaparigṛhītā, tatra gurudakṣiṇādyartham āgato mānanīya ityādiḥ samayo 'sti | durge tu dhānyādikaṃ gṛhītvānyatra yāsyato na tad vikreyam ityādir asti samayaḥ | janapade tu kvacid vikretṛhaste daśabandhagrahaṇaṃ grāhyam, kvacit kretṛhasta ityādiko 'sty anekavidhaḥ samayaḥ | janapade tathety atra tathāśabdo 'nuktagrāmaghoṣapurādīnāṃ pradarśanārthaḥ | tatra na gopracārasthāne sthātavyam ityādiko 'sti grāme samayaḥ | ābhīrastrīpuruṣavyabhicāre na daṇḍa ityādiko 'sti ghoṣe samayaḥ | pure tu vinaivārthārpaṇam āḍhyādīn yathāśakti paripālayadbhiḥ bandigrāhakādayo nihantavyā ityādayaḥ samayāḥ santi | tad etat samayajātaṃ yathā svayaṃ na bhraśyati na vyativartate tathā rājā kuryād ity arthaḥ | samudāyapuruṣān adhikṛtya bṛhaspatiḥ |

	kośena lekhyakriyayā madhyasthair vā parasparam |

	viśvāsaṃ prathamaṃ kṛtvā kuryuḥ kāryāṇy anantaram ||

lekhyakriyayā samayapatreṇa | madhyasthaiḥ pratibhūbhir ity arthaḥ | kāryāṇi samūhakāryāṇi | kātyāyano 'pi |

	samūhināṃ tu yo dharmas tena dharmeṇa te sadā |

	prakuryuḥ sarvakarmāṇi svadharmeṣu vyavasthitāḥ ||

sāmayikanijadharmānatikrameṇa samūhikāryāṇi samudāyinaḥ kuryur ity arthaḥ | yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	nijadharmāvirodhena yas tu sāmayiko bhavet |

	so 'pi yatnena saṃrakṣyo dharmo rājakṛtaś ca yaḥ ||

nijadharmo varṇāśramādidharmaḥ | sāmayikaḥ samayanirvartyo dharmaḥ | yaḥ punaḥ nijadharmavirodho sāmayiko dharmaḥ yatha: saṃdhyāvandanavelāyāṃ sarvair eva svatvavyāpāraparihāreṇa rājabhavanaṃ pratyāgantavyam, yo na gacchati tasya prathamasāhaso daṇḍa iti | nāsau rakṣya iti arthāt gamyate | asmadarātimaṇḍalam aśvādayaḥ prasthāpanīyāḥ, ityādiko yo nijadharmāvirodhena rājājñayā kṛto dharmaḥ so 'pi samūhenānusaraṇīya ity antyapādasyārthaḥ | kātyāyano 'pi |

	avirodhena dharmasya nirgataṃ rājaśāsanam |

	tasyaivācaraṇaṃ pūrvaṃ kartavyaṃ tu nṛpājñayā ||

dharmasya śrautasmārtādidharmamārgasya | nirgata niṣṭhitam ity arthaḥ | rājaśāsanaṃ rājñāniśiṣṭo dharmaḥ | tasyaiva śrautasmārtamārgāvirodhena vihitasyaiva | yaḥ punaḥ śrautasmārtamārgavirodhena rājājñānirmito dhramaḥ, yathā "asmābhir dattasya gṛhakṣetrāder ādhivikrayadānādikaṃ na kāryam" iti, tasyācaraṇaṃ na kartavyam ity evakārāt gamyate | katham atra śrautasmārtamārgavirodhaḥ | ucyate: dravyārjanavidhinārjitasya dravyasya yatheṣṭaṃ viniyogaḥ kārya ity ayam api śrautasmārtamārga eva, tadvirodhas tatrāsty evety alaṃ pratyudāharaṇasamarthananirbandhena | yat punar tenaivoktam,

	rājapravartitān dharmān yo naro nānupālayet |

	garhyaḥ sa pāpo daṇḍyaś ca lopayan rājaśāsanam ||

iti, tat śrautasmārtamārgāviruddharājapravartitadharmaviṣayam iti mantavyam | samudāyibhir vicitramatibhir aparimitaiś ca samyagasamyaktvaṃ aikamatyena kāryasya niścetum aśakyam iti matvā dvitrāḥ pañca vā kāryacintakāḥ kāryā ity āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	dvau trayḥ pañca vā kāryāḥ samūhahitavādinaḥ |

	kartavyaṃ vacanaṃ teṣāṃ grāmaśreṇīgaṇādibhiḥ || iti |

kāryacintakeṣu heyāḥ upādeyāś ca tenaiva darśitāḥ |

	vidveṣiṇo vyasaninaḥ śālīnālasabhīravaḥ |

	lubdhātivṛddhabālāś ca na kāryāḥ kāryacintakāḥ ||

	śucayo vedadharmajñāḥ dakṣāḥ śāntāḥ kulodbhavāḥ |

	sarvakāryapravīṇāś ca kartavyāś ca mahattamāḥ || iti |

śālīnāḥ lajjāśīlāḥ | kāryacintakāḥ samūhakāryasādhakabādhakavicārakāḥ | yājñavalkyas tv akāryacintakānām api samūhahitavādināṃ vacanaṃ sarvaiḥ samūhibhiḥ kāryam ity āha |

	kartavyaṃ vacanaṃ sarvaiḥ samūhahitavādinām | iti |

yas tu hitavādināṃ pratikūlaḥ syāt sa samūhena prathamasāhasaṃ daṇḍya ity āha sa eva |

	yas tatra viparītaḥ syāt sa dāpyaḥ prathamaṃ damam || iti |

kātyāyano 'pi |

	yuktiyuktaṃ ca yo hanyād vaktur yo 'navakāśadaḥ |

	ayuktaṃ caiva yo brūte sa dāpyaḥ pūrvasāhasam ||

bṛhaspatiḥ |

	yas tu sādhāraṇaṃ hiṃsyāt kṣipet traividyam eva vā |

	saṃdhikriyāṃ vihanyāc ca sa nirvāsyas tataḥ purāt ||

sādhāraṇaṃ daṇḍādidravyaṃ daṇḍyādeḥ sāhāyyakaraṇādinā nāśayed ity arthaḥ | kṣipet ākṣipet | tataḥ purāt samudāyasthānāt | atraividyākṣepe tu vākpāruṣyapade daṇḍo vakṣyate | samudāyimātrasya marmodghāṭakādau nirvāsanam eva daṇḍaḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	aruntudaḥ sūcakaś ca bhedakṛt sāhasī tathā |

	śreṇipūganṛpadviṣṭaḥ kṣipraṃ nirvāsyate tataḥ ||

aruntudo marmodghāṭakaḥ | sūcakaḥ piśunaḥ | bhedakṛt samūhiṣu vimatikṛt | tataḥ samūhasthānāt | nirvāsyate samūheneti śeṣaḥ | na ca vācyaṃ samūhasya daṇḍane 'nadhikārāt samūheneti śeṣa ity etad ayuktam iti | yata āha sa eva |

	kulaśreṇīgaṇādhyakṣāḥ puradurganivāsinaḥ |

	vāgdhigdamaṃ parityāgaṃ prakuryuḥ pāpakarmaṇām ||

	taiḥ kṛtaṃ yac ca dharmeṇa nigrahānugrahaṃ nṛṇām |

	tad rājñāpy anumantavyaṃ nisṛṣṭārthā hi te smṛtāḥ || iti |

vāgdamaḥ pāpiṣṭho 'sītyādibhartsanam | dhigdamo dhig iti kutsanam | parityāgaḥ aṅkakaraṇaṃ nirvāsanaṃ vā | etat arthadaṇḍāder apy upalakṣaṇārtham, nigrahānugraham iti sāmānyataḥ punar abhidhānāt | nisṛṣṭārthāḥ anujñātakāryāḥ | adharmeṇa taiḥ kṛte 'py āha sa eva |

	bādhāṃ kuryur yad ekasya saṃbhūtā dveṣasaṃyutāḥ |

	rājñā jñātvā nivāryās tu śāsyāś caivānubandhataḥ || iti |

anubandhataḥ nibandhānusāreṇa śāsyā daṇḍyā ity arthaḥ | nārado 'pi daṇḍyān āha |

	pṛthag gaṇāṃs tu ye bhindyuḥ te vineyā viśeṣataḥ |

	āvaheyur bhayaṃ ghoraṃ vyādhivat te hy upekṣitāḥ ||

gaṇagrahaṇam atra samūhamātraparam, na punaḥ kulasamūharūpaviśeṣaparam | tena pāṣaṇḍādāv api bhedakā ye te rājñā viśeṣato vineyāḥ | viśeṣagrahaṇāc chārīreṇāpi daṇḍena vineyāḥ | pāṣaṇḍyādisarvasamūhiṣu rājñā yathā vartitavyaṃ tathāpy āha sa eva |

	yo dharmaḥ karma yac caiṣāṃ upasthānavidhiś ca yaḥ |

	yac caiṣāṃ pratyupādānam anumanyeta tat tathā ||

dharmo jaṭādhāritvādikaḥ | karma vrataṃ paryuṣitabhikṣāṭanādikam | upasthānavidhiḥ samudāyikāryārthaṃ paṭahādidhvanim ākarṇya maṇṭapādau melanam | pratyupādānaṃ jīvanāya tāpasaveṣādiparigrahaḥ | eṣāṃ pāṣaṇḍādīnām ity arthaḥ | anyad api rājakṛtyam āha sa eva |

	pratikūlaṃ ca yad rājñaḥ prakṛtyāvamataṃ ca yat |

	bādhanaṃ ca yad arthānāṃ tat tebhyo vinivartayet ||

pratikūlaṃ yathā,

	yasya rājñas tu kurute śūdro dharmavivecanam |

	tasya prakṣubhyate rāṣṭraṃ balaṃ kośaś ca naśyati || iti |

evaṃ ca sārthakādiśūdrakartṛkaṃ traivarṇikapaurādīnāṃ vivāde dharmavivecanādikaṃ "pratikūlaṃ ca yad rājñaḥ" ity asyodāharaṇam iti mantavyam | prakṛtyā svabhāvata evāvamatam avajñātam, tad yathā: pāṣaṇḍādiṣu tāmbūlabhakṣaṇādikam | yac cārthānāṃ bādhanaṃ rasabādhādikaṃ tat tebhyaḥ sakāśād rājā vinivartayet | anyāny api nivartanīyāny āha sa eva |

	mithaḥ saṅghātakaraṇam ahite śastradhāraṇam |

	parasparopatāpaṃ ca teṣāṃ rājā nivartayet ||

mithāh saṅghātakaraṇam upasthānavidheḥ pūrvaṃ pṛthak pṛthag avāntarastomakaraṇam | ahite kulajādau | parasparopatāpo rājakīyāśrayeṇa anyonyam arthāharaṇādikam | anyad api nivartyam āha sa eva |

	doṣavatkāraṇaṃ yat syād adhunā ca prakalpitam |

	pravṛttam api tad rājā śreyaḥkāmo nivartayet ||

lobhdidoṣavakāraṇakaṃ śrutismṛtiviruddhaṃ vidhavādau veśyātvādikaṃ pāṣaṇḍādibhiḥ prakalpitaṃ bahukālaṃ pravṛttam api rājā nivartayed ity arthaḥ | samūhiṣu yat samūhena kartum aśakyaṃ mukhyānām auddhatyanivāraṇādikaṃ tad api rājā kuryāt | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	mukhyaiḥ saha samūhānāṃ visaṃvādo yadā bhavet |

	tadā vicāreyad rājā svamārge sthāpayec ca tān ||

yas tu mukhuaḥ svamārge rājñāpi sthāpayitum aśakyas tatroktaṃ yājñavalkyena |

	gaṇadravyaṃ hared yad tu saṃvidaṃ laṅghayec ca yaḥ |

	sarvasvaharaṇaṃ kṛtvā taṃ rāṣṭrād vipravāsayet ||

rājeti śeṣaḥ, evaṃvidhadaṇḍaprayoge tasyaiva sāmārthāt | yadā samūhasyāpi kathaṃcit sāmarthyam asti tadā prakṛtatvāt gaṇsyaiva daṇḍaprayogakartṛtvam avagantavyam | kātyāyenāpy uktam |

	sāhasī bhedakārī ca gaṇadravyavināśakaḥ | 

	ucchedyāḥ sarva evaite vikhyāpyaivaṃ nṛpair bhṛguḥ ||

kecin "nṛpe bhṛguḥ" iti paṭhanti | tadā ayam arthaḥ: sāhasikatvādikaṃ ṇṛpe vikhyāpya gaṇeṇocchedyā iti | yas tu mukhyaḥ śapathena svamārge sthāpayitum aśakyas tatroktaṃ manunā |

	yo grāmadeśasaṅgheṣu kṛtvā satyena saṃvidam |

	visaṃvaden naro lobhāt taṃ rāṣṭrād vipravasayet ||

	nigṛhya dāpayed enaṃ samayavyabhicāriṇam |

	catuḥsuvarṇaṃ ṣaṇṇiṣkaṃ śatamānaṃ ca rājatam ||

	evaṃ daṇḍavidhiṃ kuryād dhārmikaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ |

	grāmajātisamūheṣu samayavyabhicāriṇām || iti |

satyena śapathenety ārthaḥ | suvarṇaniṣkaśatamānaśabdāḥ prāg divyaprakaraṇe vyākhyātāḥ | tatra trayo 'rthadaṇḍāḥ daṇḍyānām arthasattānusāreṇa vyavasthāpanīyāḥ | nirvāsanaṃ tu nirbandhaviaṣaye vyavasthāpanīyam | dhārmikagrahaṇād adhārmikasya daṇḍavidhāv audhāsīnyam apy astīty avagamyate | yadā ca dhārmiko rājā daṇḍavidhāv udāsīnas tadā grāmādaya eva daṇḍavidhiṃ kuryuḥ, "nisṛṣṭārthā hi te smṛtāḥ" ity uktatvāt | amukhyānāṃ tu samayavyabhicāriṇām audhatyānusāreṇa daṇḍaḥ kalpanīyaḥ | teṣām api sāmarthyato mukhyatulyatve jāte bṛhaspatinoktam |

	.......................... yaḥ samartho visaṃvadet |

	sarvasvaharaṇaṃ daṇḍas tasya nirvāsanaṃ purāt || iti |

samarthaḥ samayaṃ pālayituṃ samartho mukhyatulya iti yāvat | visaṃvadet samayaṃ laṅghayet | aparān api daṇḍyān āha sa eva |

	saṃbhūyaikamatiṃ kṛtvā rājabhāvyaṃ haranti ye |

	te tadaṣṭaguṇaṃ dāpyāḥ vaṇijaś ca palāyinaḥ ||

"rājabhāvyaṃ haranti ye" iti caturthapāde 'nuṣañjanīyaḥ | samūhapūjārthaṃ yad rājñā samūhakāryārtham āgatāya dattaṃ tad yadi samūhapārśvam āgatyāsau samūhāya svayaṃ na dadāti, tadā rājñā dattam ekādaśaguṇaṃ dāpyaḥ | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	samūhakārya āyātān kṛtakāryān visarjayet |

	sadānamānasatkāraiḥ pūjayitvā mahīpatiḥ ||

	samūhakāryaprahito yal labheta tad arpayet |

	ekādaśaguṇaṃ dāpyo yady asau nārpayet svayam || iti |

yal labheta samūhamānyatvanimitteneti śeṣaḥ, svakīyasevādhyayanādinimittena tu labdhasya prātisvikatvena samudāye 'rpaṇavidhyayogāt | samūhakāryaprahitenārpitaṃ ca sarve samūhinaḥ samaṃ vibhāgena vibhajya gṛhṇīyuḥ,

	tato labhyeta yat kiṃcit sarveṣām eva tat samam |

iti bṛhaspatismaraṇāt | evaṃ vibhajya grahaṇam atucchadravyaviṣayam, tucchadravyaṃ tu labdhaṃ niḥsvādibhyaḥ samūhena deyam | yad āha sa eva |

	ṣāṇmāsikaṃ māsikaṃ vā vibhaktavyaṃ yathāṃśataḥ |

	deyaṃ vā niḥsvavṛddhārtastrībālāturarogiṣu ||

	sāntānikādiṣu tathā dharma eva sanātanaḥ | iti |

ekasya puruṣasya ṣaṇmāsanirvāhāyāparyāptaṃ kuṭumbasya vaikamāsanirvāyāyāparyāptaṃ labdhaṃ cen niḥsvādibhyo tātparyārthaḥ | yat punas tenaivokam,

	yat taiḥ prāptaṃ rakṣitaṃ vā gaṇārthe vā ṛṇaṃ kṛtam |

	rājaprasādalabdhaṃ vā sarveṣām eva tat samam ||

iti, tasyāyam arthaḥ: taiḥ samūhakāryārthaprahitair yat sīmāvivādādāv adhikaṃ kṣetrārāmādikaṃ dharmādhikaraṇe nyāyataḥ prāptaṃ parair apahriyamāṇaṃ vā rakṣitam, tathā samūhaprayojanārtham upāttam ṛṇaṃ samūhakṛtānukūlyādijanitarājaprasādalabdhaṃ vā yat tad etat sarvaṃ sarveṣāṃ samūhināṃ samaṃ jñeyam iti | gaṇārthe kṛtam ṛṇaṃ sarveṣāṃ samam ity kvacid apavādam āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	gaṇam uddiśya yat kiṃcit kṛtvarṇaṃ bhakṣitaṃ bhavet |

	ātmārthaṃ viniyuktaṃvā deyaṃ tair eva tad bhavet ||

tair eva samūhakāryaprahitair eva pratideyaṃ tad ṛṇaṃ bhavatīty arthaḥ | paribhāṣitapātheyānarpaṇe 'pi taiḥ kṛtam ṛṇaṃ gaṇena na deyam, evakārakaraṇāt | kiṃ tu pātheyam eva deyam | ye punaḥ samudāyaṃ prasādya tadantarbhāvam āpannāḥ, ye ca samudāyakṣobhādinā tato bahir bhūtāḥ tān praty āha sa eva |

	gaṇināṃ śilpivargāṇāṃ gatāḥ syur ye tu madhyatām |

	prāktanasya dhanarṇasya samāṃśāḥ sarva eva te ||

	tathaiva bhojyavaibhāvyadānadharmakriyāsu ca |

	samūhastho 'ṃśabhāgī syāt pragatas tv aṃśabhāṅ na tu || iti ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ samayānapākarmākhyasya padasya vidhivitānaḥ**

**atha kṣetrajavivādākhyasya padasya vidhir ucyate**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	niveśakāle kartavyaḥ sīmābandhaviniścayaḥ |

	prakāśopāṃśucihnaiś ca lakṣitaḥ saṃśayāpahaḥ ||

niveśakālaḥ grāmādipraveśakālaḥ | sīmāyā bandho nibandho niyāmaka iti yāvat | viniścīyate sīmābandho yena sa viniścayaḥ pāṣāṇādimayaḥ sthūlaguḍakaḥ | sīmābandhaś cāsau viniścayaś ceti sīmābandhaviniścayaḥ, sīmāniyāmakasthūlaguḍaka ity arthaḥ | etad uktaṃ bhavati: grāmādipraveśakāle tatsīmāniyāmakaḥ sthūlaguḍakaḥ prakāśaguptaliṅgopetaḥ sīmāsaṃdhau sthāpanīya iti | prakāśaguptaliṅgāny api tenaiva darśitāni |

	vāpīkūpataṭākāni caityārāmasurālayāḥ |

	sthalanimnanadīsrotaḥśaragulmanagādayaḥ ||

	prakāśacihnāny etāni sīmāyāṃ kāreyet sadā |

	karīṣāsthituṣāṅgāraśarkarāśmakapālikāḥ ||

	sikateṣṭakagovālakārpāsāsthīni bhasma ca |

	prakṣipya kumbheṣv etāni sīmānteṣu nidhāpayet || iti |

vāpī puṣkariṇī | caityam iṣṭakādyair viracitaṃ sthaṇḍilam | sthalam unnato bhūpradeśaḥ | nimnaṃ parighā | śarāḥ tṛṇaviśeṣāḥ | gulmāḥ kandaśūnyāḥ karavīraprakārāḥ | nagāḥ vṛkṣāḥ | te tu manunā viśeṣitāḥ |

	sīmāvṛkṣāṃs tu kurvīta nyagrodhāśvatthakiṃśukān |

	śalmalīn sālatālāṃś ca kṣīriṇaś caiva pādapān ||

nyagrodho vaṭaḥ | kiṃśukaḥ palāśaḥ | nagādaya ity atrādiśabdena veṇuvallīvalmīkavartmapurātanasetvādīnāṃ smṛtyantaroktānāṃ grahaṇam | karīṣaṃ śuṣkagomayam | asthīni paśvādīnām | tuṣāḥ vrīhyāditvacaḥ | aṅgārā dagdhakāṣṭhāvayavāḥ śāntāgnayaḥ | śarkarāḥ pāṣāṇavat kaṭhinā mṛdaḥ | kapālikāḥ pakvaghaṭāvayavānām avayavāḥ | kārpāsāsthīni kārpāsabījāni | nidhāpayet gartābhyantareṣu kumbhīḥ nidhāya mṛdbhiḥ pracchādayet | tathā ca manuḥ |

	upacchannāni cānyāni sīmāliṅgāni kārayet |

	sīmājñāne nṛṇāṃ vīkṣya loke nityaṃ viparyayam ||

upacchannāni pracchāditāni anyāni prakāśacihnebhyo 'nyāni tāni cādhastād evoktāni | tatra kārpāsāsthivarjāni sarvāṇi mānave 'py anukīrtitāni | liṅgānām anukīrtanam upalakṣaṇārtham iti darśayituṃ kārpāsāsthikīrtane manor anāsthā | ata eva upāṃśuliṅgāny abhidhāyābhihitaṃ manunā |

	yāni caivaṃprakārāṇi kālāt bhūmir na bhakṣayet |

	tāni saṃdhiṣu sīmāyām aprakāśāni kārayet ||

tāni śuktiśaṅkhagairikakhadirasāraprabhṛtīni | evamuktaliṅgānāṃ madhye vṛkṣaliṅgānvitā sīmā dvajinīty ucyate | jalaliṅgānvitā matsinī | tuṣāṅgārādiguptaliṅgānvitā naidhānīty ucyate | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

	grāmayor ubhayoḥ sīmni vṛkṣā yatra samunnatāḥ |

	samucchritā dhvajākārā dhvajinī sā prakīrtitā ||

	svacchandagā bahujalā matsyakūrmasamanvitā |

	nityapravāhiṇī yatra sīmā sā matsinī matā ||

	tuṣāṅgārakapālais tu kumbhair āyatanais tathā |

	sīmā pracihnitā kāryā naidhānī sā nigadyate || iti |

samunnatāḥ kauṭilyavikalāḥ | samucchritāḥ uccāḥ | sīmāliṅgāni yatnasiddhāni svataḥsiddhāni vā prathamavayasāṃ galitavayaskair jñāpanīyāni | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	tataḥ paugaṇḍabālānāṃ prayatnena pradarśayet |

	vārdhakye ca śiśūnāṃ te darśayeyus tathaiva ca ||

	evaṃ paramparājñāne sīmābhrāntir na jāyate || iti |

paugaṇḍabālāḥ kiṃcitprabuddhabālāḥ | te 'pi ca paugaṇḍabālāḥ kālena vārdhakyam āpannāḥ śiśūnāṃ kiṃcitprabuddhānāṃ svajñātijñāpitāni sīmāliṅgāni prayatnena darśayeyuḥ | evam avicchinnā jñātṛparamparā bahutarakālātyaye 'pi sīmābhrāntyanutpattyarthaṃ kāryety arthaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ sīmāliṅganirūpaṇam**

**atha sīmāvivādanirṇayaḥ**

tatra manuḥ |

	etair liṅgair nayet sīmāṃ rājā vivadamānayoḥ || iti |

etaiḥ prāṅnirūpitaiḥ sīmāliṅgair arthipradarśitaiḥ sīmāṃ nayet nirṇayed ity arthaḥ | athārthiny aviśvāsaḥ tadā sākṣipratyayād eva nirṇayet | tad āha sa eva |

	yadi saṃśaya eva syāl liṅgānām api darśane |

	sākṣipratyaya eva syāt sīmāvādaviniścaye ||

liṅgaviṣayakaḥ sīmāviṣayako vā sākṣipratyayaḥ sīmāvivādaniścayahetuḥ syād ity arthaḥ | tatra liṅgaviṣayakapratyayaśālināṃ sākṣiṇāṃ sākṣiprakaraṇoktalakṣaṇam evānusaṃdheyam | sīmāviṣayakapratyayaśālināṃ tu sākṣiṇāṃ lakṣaṇādhikyam iha bṛhaspatinā darśitam |

	āgamaṃ ca pramāṇaṃ ca bhogaṃ kālaṃ ca nāma ca |

	bhūbhāgalakṣaṇaṃ caiva ye vidus te 'tra sākṣiṇaḥ ||

āgamaḥ svatvāpādakaḥ krayādiḥ | pramāṇaṃ daṇḍādinā parikalpitaṃ parimāṇam | yadā tūktavidhasākṣyabhāvaḥ tadā sāmantapradarśitair liṅgair nirṇayet | etad api vacobhaṅgyāha manuḥ |

	sākṣyabhāve tu catvāro grāmasīmāntavāsinaḥ |

	sīmāvinirṇayaṃ kuryuḥ prayatā rājasaṃnidhau ||

kātyāyano 'pi: "teṣām abhāve sāmantāḥ" iti | teṣāṃ dvividhasākṣiṇām | ke punaḥ sāmantā ity apekṣite sa evāha: "saṃsaktakās tu sāmantāḥ" iti | vipratipannasīmakasya grāmādeś catasṛṣu dikṣv anantaragrāmādibhoktāraḥ saṃsaktakāḥ, ta eva sāmantā jñeyā ity arthaḥ | evamuktānāṃ sāmantānāṃ yadā rāgadveṣādiprakaṭadoṣasadbhāvas tadāpy āha sa eva |

	svārthasiddhau praduṣṭeṣu sāmanteṣv arthagauravāt |

	tatsaṃsakteṣu kartavyaḥ uddhāro nātra saṃśayaḥ ||

tatsaṃsakteṣu sāmantasaṃsakteṣu | uddhāraḥ sīmāyā uddhāraḥ sīmānirṇaya iti yāvat | etad uktaṃ bhavati: catasṛṣu dikṣu sthitasāmantagrāmādibhyo 'nantaratvena tattaddiśi sthitagrāmādibhoktāraḥ tatsaṃsaktāḥ, taiḥ pradarśitasīmāliṅgair grāmādeḥ sīmāṃ nirṇayed iti | yadā teṣām api prakaṭadoṣasadbhāvaḥ tadāpy āha sa eva |

	saṃsaktasaktadoṣe tu tatsaṃsaktāḥ prakīrtitāḥ | iti |

tatsaṃsaktāḥ saṃsaktasaktasaṃsaktāḥ | etad uktaṃ bhavati: catasṛṣu dikṣu sthitasaṃsaktasaktagrāmādibhyo 'nantaratvena tattaddiśi sthitagrāmādibhoktāraḥ saṃsaktasaktasaṃsaktāḥ, taiḥ pradarśitasīmāliṅgaiḥ grāmādisīmāṃ nirṇayed iti | yadā tu teṣām api prakaṭadoṣasadbhāvaḥ tadāpy āha sa eva |

	tyaktvā duṣṭāṃs tu sāmantān anyān maulādibhiḥ saha |

	saṃmarśya kārayet sīmām evaṃ dharmavido viduḥ ||

saṃsaktasaktasaṃsaktā api sāmantakoṭiniviṣṭāḥ, tena eteṣāṃ sāmantaśabdena nirdeśo nānupapannaḥ | tataś cāyam arthaḥ: duṣṭān saṃsaktasaktasaṃsaktān tyaktvā sākṣisāmantatatkoṭibhyo 'nyān sīmāliṅgābhijñān maulavṛddhoddhṛtasahitān sīmāntapratinirṇāyakān kārayed iti | ke punaḥ sākṣisāmantatatkoṭibhyo 'nya ity apekṣite nāradaḥ |

	nagaragrāmagaṇino ye ca vṛddhatamā narāḥ | iti |

sīmāliṅgajñā iti śeṣaḥ | maulavṛddhoddhṛtās tu kātyāyanena darśitāḥ |

	ye tatra pūrvasāmantāḥ paścād deśāntaraṃ gatāḥ |

	tanmūlatvāt tu te maulā ṛṣibhiḥ samprakīrtitāḥ ||

	niṣpādyamānaṃ yair dṛṣṭaṃ tat kāryaṃ nṛguṇānvitaiḥ |

	vṛddhā vā yadi vāvṛddhās te vṛddhāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ||

	upaśravaṇasaṃbhogakāryākhyānopacihnitāḥ |

	uddharanti tato yasmād uddhṛtās te tataḥ smṛtāḥ || iti |

nṛguṇānvitaiḥ puruṣaguṇānvitaiḥ | vayovṛddhatvaṃ na tantram iti vikalpoktyā darśitam | kāryajñātṛtvaṃ yeṣāṃ pāramparyeṇa te uddhṛtā iti tṛtīyaślokasya tātparyārthaḥ | evaṃ ca prakaṭadoṣeṇa saṃsaktasaktasaṃsakteṣu duṣṭeṣu pūrvasāmantādyupetanāgaragrāmyajanaśreṇīvayovṛddhadarśitaiḥ sīmāliṅgaiḥ sīmānirṇayaḥ kārya ity avaboddhavyam | guptadoṣeṣu sāmanteṣu viśeṣam āha sa eva |

	sāmantāḥ sādhanaṃ pūrvam aniṣṭoktau guṇānvitāḥ |

	dviguṇās tūttarā jñeyās tato 'nye triguṇā matāḥ ||

aniṣṭoktau prativādinā guptadoṣodbhāvane kṛte ity arthaḥ | uttarāḥ tatsaṃsaktādayo 'ntaraṅgāḥ sāmantakoṭayo dviguṇā jñeyāḥ | tataḥ sāmantatatkoṭibhyo 'nye bahiraṅgā nāgarādayo maulavṛddhoddhṛtasahitās triguṇā matāḥ | evaṃ tatsaṃsaktakādiṣv api guptadoṣodbhāvane saty uttareṣāṃ dvaiguṇyādikam ūhyam | sākṣiprabhṛtyuddhṛtaparyantānām abhāve tu manur āha |

	sāmantānām abhāve tu maulānāṃ sīmasākṣiṇām |

	imān apy anuyuñjīta puruṣān vanagocarān ||

sāmantādīnām anugrāhakamaulādīnāṃ sīmāsākṣiṇāṃ cābhāve imān asabhyān api vakṣyamāṇān puruṣān anuyuñjīta sīmāliṅgāni pṛcched ity arthaḥ | tān eva darśayati |

	vyādhān śākunikān gopān kaivartān mūlakhānakān |

	vyālagrāhān ucchavṛttīn anyāṃś ca vanagocarān || (MDh 8.260)

vyādhādīnāṃ dvitīyāntatayā nirdeśaḥ pūrvaślokasthenānuyuñjītetipadenānvayārthaḥ | kaivartāḥ taṭākādikhananopajīvinaḥ | nāradas tu maulādisahitānyeṣām abhāve sīmāntikapradeśakarṣakāḥ teṣām abhāve vanagocarā iti darśayituṃ vanagocarebhyaḥ prāksīmākarṣakān darśayati |

	grāmasīmāsu ca bahiḥ ye syus tat kṛṣijīvinaḥ |

	gopāḥ śākunikā vyādhā ye cānye vanagocarāḥ || (NSm 11.3)

evaṃ sāmantādyuddhṛtaparyanteṣv apy utkṛṣṭānām abhāve nikṛṣṭānām anuyojanam ūhyam | anuyojanaṃ satyānṛtajanyapuṇyapāpapratipādakamanvādivacanair yathārthakathanaparān kṛtvā prastutārthapraśnakaraṇam | tāni ca vacanāni sākṣyanuyojanavidhiprakaraṇoktāny anusaṃdheyāni | sākṣipraśnavidhiprakaraṇoktaśapathaiḥ śāpitā eva sāmantādayo vinirṇayaṃ brūyuḥ | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	śapathaiḥ śāpitāḥ svaiḥ svaiḥ brūyuḥ sīmāvinirṇayam |

	darśayeyuś ca liṅgāni tat pramāṇam iti sthitam ||

śapathaiḥ svaiḥ svaiḥ,

	satyena śāpayed vipraṃ kṣatriyaṃ vāhanāyudhaiḥ |

ityādinoktavyavasthān atikrameṇety arthaḥ | manunāpi,

	grāmeyakakulānāṃ tu samakṣaṃ sīmasākṣiṇaḥ |

	praṣṭavyāḥ sīmaliṅgāni tayoś caiva vivādinoḥ ||

ity uktvoktam,

	te pṛṣṭās tu yathā brūyuḥ sīmāsaṃdhiṣu lakṣaṇam |

	tat tathā sthāpayed rājā dharmeṇa grāmayor dvayoḥ || iti |

grāmīṇapuruṣasamūhasya vivādinoś ca samakṣaṃ sīmāliṅgāni tatsākṣiprabhṛtayaḥ praṣṭavyā iti prathamaślokasyārthaḥ | dvitīyaślokārthas tu suvyaktaḥ | sīmāyā eva ye sākṣiṇas te sīmārtham eva praṣṭavyāḥ, pṛṣṭāś ca yathā sīmāṃ brūyuḥ tathā jñāpayed ity uhyam | yadā tu sīmāliṅgasākṣiṇo lakṣaṇāni kathaṃcit pradarśayituṃ na śaknuvanti kevalaṃ sīmāṃ vadanti tadā tān praty āha sa eva |

	śirobhiḥ svaiḥ gṛhītvorvīṃ sragviṇo raktavāsasaḥ |

	sukṛtaiḥ śāpitāḥ svaiḥ svaiḥ nayeyus tān samañjasam ||

yāvantaḥ sīmāliṅgasākṣiṇaḥ te sarve lohitakusumasragviṇo lohitavasanāḥ loṣṭaṃ śirasi dhārayantaḥ sīmānuyāyinā caṅkrameṇa sīmāntaṃ pradarśayantas tāṃ sīmāṃ samañjasaṃ samyak nirṇayeyur ity arthaḥ | yājñavalkyas tu sāmantādīn pray āha |

	sāmantā va samagrāmāś catvāro 'ṣṭau daśāpi vā |

	raktasragvasanāḥ sīmāṃ nayeyuḥ kṣitidhāriṇaḥ ||

vāśabdāt tatsaṃsaktakādayo 'py evam eva liṅgapradarśanāsaṃbhave sīmāṃ nayeyur iti gamyate, liṅgapradarśakeṣu vikalpārthatvāt | samagrāmāḥ samasaṅkhyātāḥ samudāyabhāvam āpannāś catvāra ityādiviśeṣopādānam anyasamasaṃkhyānirāsārtham | samagrāmā ity atra samagrahaṇaṃ viṣamasaṃkhyānivṛttyartham | tatrāpy atyartham ekasaṃkhyānivṛttyartham āha nāradaḥ |

	naikaḥ samunnayet sīmāṃ naraḥ pratyayavān api |

	gurutvād asya kāryasya kriyaiṣā bahuṣu sthitā ||

asya pratiṣedhasya kvacit pratiprasavam āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	jñātṛcihnair vinā sādhur eko 'py ubhayasaṃmataḥ |

	raktamālyāmbaradharo mṛdam ādāya mūrdhani ||

	satyavrataḥ sopavāsaḥ sīmāntaṃ darśayen naraḥ || iti |

jñātṛcihnair vinā jñātṝṇāṃ cihnānāṃ cābhāva ity arthaḥ | etad uktaṃ bhavati: sākṣyādivanagocarāntānāṃ sīmājñātṛṇāṃ pra(?)prakāśopāṃśuliṅgānām abhāve yaḥ kaścid uktaviśeṣaṇaviśiṣṭo naraḥ sīmāvit sīmāntam uktavidhinā caṅkramamāṇo darśayed iti | yady apy atra manvādivacanāc caṅkramaṇānantaram eva nirṇayaḥ saṃpadyata iti pratibhāti, tathāpi caṅkramaṇadinam ārabhya sārdhamāsānte nirṇayo na tato 'rvāg ity avagantavyam | yad āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	sīmācaṅgramaṇe krośe pādasparśe tathaiva ca |

	tripakṣapakṣasaptāhaṃ daivarājakam iṣyate || iti |

yathāsaṃkhyam iti śeṣaḥ | yadāpy uktalakṣaṇasya (narasyā) pramāṇasyābhāvaḥ tadāpi na divyena nirṇayaḥ,

	vākpāruṣye mahīvāde divyāni parivarjayet |

ityādyanekavacanena bhūvivāde divyaniṣedhāt | sīmāvivādaś ca bhūvivāda eva | yad āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	ādhikyaṃ nyūnatā cāṃśe astināstitvam eva ca |

	abhogabhuktiḥ sīmā ca ṣaṭ bhūvādasya hetavaḥ || iti |

kathaṃ tarhy atra nirṇaya ity apekṣite nāradaḥ |

	yadā tu na syur jñātāraḥ sīmāyā na ca lakṣaṇam |

	tadā rājā dvayoḥ sīmām unnayed iṣṭataḥ svayam ||

iṣṭataḥ icchāta ity arthaḥ | iṣṭata ity asya kvacid apavādam āha manuḥ |

	sīmāyām aviṣahyāyāṃ svayaṃ rājaiva dharmavit |

	praviśed bhūmim ekeṣām upakārād iti sthitiḥ ||

aviṣahyā jñātṛjñāpakaśūnyā | etad uktaṃ bhavati: yatra vivādaviṣayo bhūr ekasya niravakāśasya grāmakṣetrāder atyantopakārikā anyasya tu sāvakāśasya na tathā tatra mahopakārārthaṃ niravakāśagrāmādiśeṣatayā tāṃ bhūmiṃ praveśayed iti | evam uktaividhinā sīmānirṇayo nāvedanānantaram eva ṛṇādinirṇayavat kartuṃ sarvadā sukaraḥ, prāvṛḍādikāle sasyādibhis tirohiteṣu setvādisīmāliṅgeṣu duṣkaratvāt | tena yadā setvādisīmāliṅgānāṃ tirodhāyakasasyādyabhāvaḥ tadā nirṇayaḥ kāryaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	sīmāṃ prati samutpanne vivāde grāmayor dvayoḥ |

	jyeṣṭhamāsi nayet sīmāṃ suprakāśeṣu setuṣu ||

dvayor grāmādhipayor vivāde sīmāṃ prati samutpanne jyeṣṭamāsi māsāntare vā setuprabhṛtiṣu sīmāliṅgeṣu suvyakteṣu vivādādhyāsitāṃ sīmāṃ nirṇayed ity arthaḥ | grāmagrahaṇaṃ kṣetrādīnām upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva bṛhaspatinā,

	grāmakṣetragṛhādīnāṃ sīmāvādaṃ nibodhata |

ity upakrāntam | gṛhādīnām ityādiśabdena nagaradeśau svīkriyete, tatrāpi sīmāvādasadbhāvāt | ata eva kātyāyanena,

	sāmantabhāve sāmantaiḥ kuryāt kṣetrādinirṇayam |

	grāme sīmāsu ca tathā tadvan nagaradeśayoḥ ||

ity uktam | kṣetrādinirṇayaṃ kṣetragṛhayoḥ sīmānirṇayam ity arthaḥ | na caivaṃ grāmakṣetragṛhādiṣv anyonyasāmantair anyonyanirṇayaḥ kāryaḥ, grāmasāmantānāṃ kṣetragṛhasīmāsv aparicitatvāt, evaṃ kṣetrasāmantānāṃ grāmagṛhasīmāsu aparicitatvāt | ata evāha sa eva |

	grāmo grāmasya sāmantaḥ kṣetraṃ kṣetrasya kīrtitam |

	gṛhaṃ gṛhasya nirdiṣṭaṃ sāmantān paribhāvayet ||

atra grāmādiśabdena prathamāntena lakṣaṇayā grāmādibhoktā kathitaḥ | tataś cāyam arthaḥ: vivādaviṣayasya grāmādeḥ samantataḥ pūrvadakṣiṇapaścimottaradikṣu sthitagrāmādibhoktṛjanas tasya sāmantaḥ tataḥ sakāśād vivādaviṣayagrāmādisīmāliṅgāni paribhāvayet niścinuyāt nirṇetā rājādir iti | evaṃ nagaradeśayor api tattatsāmantāt paribhāvayed iti vidhir udāharaṇamukhenāsmin vacane sūcita ity avagantavyam | evam eva kedārārāmodyānadevālayakūpataṭākapravarṣaṇodbhūtajalapravāhasthānādisīmāvivāde sākṣitattatsāmantādito nirṇetā nirṇayet | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ|

	sarvasmin sthāvare vāde vidhir eṣa prakīrtitaḥ | iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ sīmāvivādanirṇayaḥ**

**atha sīmāsākṣyādyaparādhaviṣayāṇi kānicid vacanāni likhyante**

tatra kātyāyanaḥ |

	bahūnāṃ tu gṛhītānāṃ na sarve nirṇayaṃ yadi |

	kuryur bhayād vā lobhād vā dāpyas tūttamasāhasam ||

sīmāsākṣitvena prakīrtitānām aśeṣāṇāṃ sākṣyavādārthaṃ melane kṛte te sarve yadi bhayādinā sākṣyavādaṃ na brūyuḥ tadā te pratyekam uttamasāhasaṃ dāpyā ity arthaḥ | pratyekam ity anuktāv api ekaikasyaiva sākṣitvāt tad atra labhyate | yadā tu te bhayādinā sarve saṃśayam utpādayitvānaikamatyena brūyus tadāpy evam eva dāpyā ity āha sa eva |

	kīrtite yadi bhedaḥ syāt dāpyās tūttamasāhasam | iti |

yadā tv anṛtaṃ brūyus tadā tv āha viṣṇuḥ: "kūṭasākṣiṇāṃ sarvasvāpahāraḥ" iti | sāmānyenābhidhāne 'pi daṇḍagauravāt bhūvādaviṣayam etad avaseyam | sāmantānām anṛtavāditve tv āha nāradaḥ |

	atha ced anṛtaṃ brūyuḥ sāmantāḥ sīmanirṇaye |

	sarve pṛthak pṛthag daṇḍyā rājñā madhyamasāhasam ||

anṛtaṃ brūyuḥ sākṣyavāde sīmāliṅgāni vañcayitvā brūyur ity arthaḥ | ajñānoktau tv āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	nājñānena hi mucyante sāmantā nirṇayaṃ prati |

	ajñānoktau daṇḍayitvā punaḥ sīmāṃ vicārayet ||

ajñānoktāv iti nirṇayābhāvopalakṣaṇārtham, tena bhedenoktāv api nirṇayābhāvāt punaḥ sīmāṃ vicārayet | kas tatra nirṇāyaka ity apekṣite śaṅkhalikhitau: "sāmantavirodhe lekhyapratyayo lekhyavirodhe grāmanagaravṛddhaśreṇīpryayo grāmanagaravṛddhaśreṇīvirodhe daśavarṣā bhuktir anyatra rājaviplavāt" iti | lekhyapratyayo nirṇāyaka iti śeṣaḥ | evam uttaratrāpi śeṣo draṣṭavyaḥ | tatsaṃsaktādivanagocarāntānām anṛtavāditve tu nārada āha |

	śeṣāś ced anṛtaṃ brūyuḥ niyuktā bhūmikarmaṇi |

	pratyekaṃ tu jaghanyās te vineyāḥ pūrvasāhasam ||

	gaṇavṛddhādayas tv anye daṇḍanīyāḥ pṛthak pṛthak |

	vineyāḥ prathamenaiva sāhasenānṛte sthitāḥ || iti |

śeṣāḥ sāmantebhyo 'vaśiṣṭāḥ tatsaṃsaktāḥ | tebhyo jaghanyāḥ saṃsaktasaṃsaktāḥ | gaṇavṛddhādaya ity atrādiśabdena grāmanagaramaulavṛddhoddhṛtasīmākarṣakavanagocarāḥ saṃgṛhītāḥ | manus tu sīmācaṅkramaṇakartṝṇām anṛte sthitānāṃ daṇḍam āha |

	yathoktena nayantas te pūyante satyasākṣiṇaḥ |

	viparītaṃ nayantas tu dāpyās tu dviśataṃ damam ||

yathoktena "śirobhis te gṛhītvorvīm" ityādinoktamārgānatikrameṇa nayantaḥ sīmācaṅkramaṇaṃ kurvāṇāḥ satyasākṣiṇaḥ satyabhūtasīmānubhavaśālinaḥ pūyante pāpena na saṃbadhyante | viparītaṃ nayantaḥ pūrvasīmātikrameṇa caṅkramaṇaṃ kurvāṇāḥ kārṣāpaṇānāṃ dviśataṃ dāpyā ity arthaḥ | viparītanayanaṃ tu caṅkramaṇānantarakṣaṇam ārabhya sārdhamāsābhyantare daivarājakṛtavyasanadarśane veditavyam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ sīmāsākṣyādyaparādhaviṣayāṇi**

**atha nadyādivaśāt prāptabhūviṣayāṇi**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	anyagrāmāt samāhṛtya dattānyasya yadā mahī |

	mahānadyātha vā rājñā kathaṃ tatra vicāraṇā ||

	nadyotsṛṣṭā rājadattā yasya tasyaiva sā mahī |

	anyathā na bhavel lābho narāṇāṃ rājadaivikaḥ ||

	kṣayodayau jīvanaṃ ca daivarājavaśān nṛṇām |

	tasmāt sarveṣu kāryeṣu tatkṛtaṃ na vicālayet || iti |

tatkṛtaṃ daivarājakṛtam | yady api daivaśabdo bhāgyam ācaṣṭe tathāpi nadīkṛte daivakṛtam ity ucyate, bhāgyasyaiva mūlakāraṇatvāt | tathā ca sa eva |

	grāmayor ubhayor yatra maryādā kalpitā nadī |

	kurute dānaharaṇaṃ bhāgyābhāgyavaśān nṛṇām ||

	ekatra kūlapātaṃ tu bhūmer anyatra saṃsthitim |

	nadī tīre prakurute tasya tāṃ na vicālayet || iti |

tīre nadī prakurute ity anvayaḥ | tasya nadīvaśāl labdhabhūmikasya tāṃ nadīkṛtabhūmisaṃsthitiṃ pūrvasvāmī na vicālayed ity arthaḥ | etad anuptasasyatīraviṣayam | uptasasyatīraviṣaye 'py āha sa eva |

	kṣetraṃ sasasyam ullaṅghya bhūmiś chinnā yadā bhavet |

	nadīsrotaḥpravāheṇa pūrvasvāmī labheta tām ||

tāṃ sasasyāṃ bhūmim | chedanād ūrdhvam api pūrvasvāmī yāvad uptasasyaphalaprāptis tāval labhata ity arthaḥ | phalalābhād ūrdhvaṃ tu prācīnavacanaviṣayatulyataiva | rājadattabhūmiviṣaye 'pi kvacit pūrvasvāmī vicālayet kvacin na vicālayed ity āha sa eva |

	yā rājñā krodhalobhena chalanyāyena vā kṛtā |

	pradattānyasya tuṣṭena na sā siddhim avāpnuyāt ||

	pramāṇarahitāṃ bhūmiṃ bhuñjato yasya yā hṛtā |

	guṇādhikāya vā dattā tasya tāṃ na vicālayet || iti |

pramāṇarahitāṃ bhūmiṃ bhuñjataḥ svatve likhitādipramāṇarahitāṃ bhūmiṃ bhuñjata ity arthaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ nadyādivaśāt prāptabhūviṣayāṇi**

**atha gṛhādiviṣayāṇi**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	niveśakālād ārabhya gṛhavāryāpaṇādikam |

	yena yāvad yathā bhyuktaṃ tasya tan na vicālayet ||

grāmādipraveśakālād ārabhya gṛhādikaṃ tatsvāminā yena yāvat pracārabhūmyādyupetaṃ tathā yasyāṃ diśi dvārādimad bhuktaṃ tasya tan na vicālayet prātiveśyadir jana ity arthaḥ | "nirveśakālād ārabhya" iti vadan kālāntarād ārabhya bhuktaṃ vipratipannaṃ cet vicālayed iti darśayati | evaṃ niveśakāle kalpitaṃ gavākṣādikaṃ prātiveśyādyaniṣṭakāry api na kenacic cālanīyam ity āha sa eva |

	vātāyanaṃ praṇālīṃ ca tathā niryūhavedikāḥ |

	catuḥśālasyandanikāḥ prāṅniviṣṭā na cālayet ||

vātāyanaṃ gavākṣaḥ | praṇālī kāṣṭhādimayo jalanirgamopāyaḥ | niryūhaḥ gṛhaghoṇā | vedikā dārupariṣkṛtā caturaśrā viśrāntibhūmiḥ | catasṝṇāṃ śālānāṃ samāhāraś catuḥśālam | etac ca tṛṇamayagṛhopalakṣaṇārtham uktam | tasmād vṛṣṭyudakanipātasyandanikāḥ | atrāpi madhye niviṣṭānāṃ vicālanaṃ pūrvavad arthād uktam | ata eva gavākṣādikaṃ parāniṣṭakāritayā na kāryam ity āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	niveśasamayād ūrdhvaṃ naite yojyāḥ kadācana | iti |

parāniṣṭakāritayeti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	dṛṣṭiprāsaṃ praṇālīṃ ca na kuryāt paraveśmasu | iti |

dṛṣṭiprāso gavākṣaḥ | paraveśmasu paraveśmābhimukhyenety arthaḥ | evaṃ kṛte parāniṣṭaṃ bhavatīty abhiprāyaḥ | anenaivābhiprāyeṇa bṛhaspatināpy uktam |

	varcaḥsthānaṃ vahnicayaṃ gartocchiṣṭāmbusecanam |

	atyārāt parakuḍyasya na kartavyaṃ kadācana ||

varcaḥsthānaṃ viṣṭhāsthānam | atyārāt aratnidvayam avivihāyety arthaḥ | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	viṇmūtrodakavapraṃ ca vahniśvabhraniveśanam |

	aratnidvayam utsṛjya parakuḍyān niveśayet ||

bṛhaspatis tu śakaṭādikaṃ saṃkaṭahetubhūtaṃ saṃsaraṇe na ciraṃ dharyam ity āha |

	yānty āyānti janā yena paśavaś cānivāritāḥ |

	tad ucyate saṃsaraṇaṃ na roddhayaṃ tu kenacit ||

evaṃ catuṣpathādāv apy avarodhanaṃ na kāryam | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	catuṣpathasurasthānarājamārgān na rodhayet | iti |

surasthānaṃ devakulādikam | catuṣpatharājamārgayoḥ svarūpam āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	sarve janāḥ sadā yena prayānti sa catuṣpathaḥ |

	aniruddhā yathākalaṃ rājamārgaḥ sa ucyate ||

avelāyāṃ yatra mārge rājakīyaiś caṅkramaṇaṃ niṣidhyate sa rājamārga ity arthaḥ | yasya kṣetrasyāntike madhye vā mārgo 'sti taṃ pray āhatuḥ śaṅkhalikhitau: "mārgakṣetre pathivisargaḥ" iti | kārya iti śeṣaḥ | yas tu saṃsaraṇādāv avarodhaṃ karoti tasya daṇḍam āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	yas tatra saṃkaraṃ śvabhraṃ vṛkṣāropaṇam eva ca |

	kāmāt purīṣaṃ kuryād yas tasya daṇḍas tu māṣakaḥ ||

saṃkaraḥ saṃkīrṇatā avarodha iti yāvat | vṛkṣagrahaṇaṃ sasyāder upalakṣaṇārtham | yady api pañcakṛṣṇalako māṣo 'trāpi grāhyatayā pratibhāti, tathāpy aparādhānurūpatvāya kārṣāpaṇasya viṃśo bhāgo grāhyaḥ, tatrāpi māṣavyavahārāt | rājamārge purīṣakartur daṇḍādhikyam āha manuḥ |

	samutsṛjed rājamārge yas tv amedhyam anāpadi |

	sa dvau kārṣāpaṇau dadyād amedhyaṃ cāśu śodhayet ||

mārgavaiśiṣṭyād atrāparādhādhikyam abhisaṃdhāya daṇḍādhikyābhidhānaṃ manor iti mantavyam | āpadi tu nārthadaṇḍaḥ kiṃ tu vāgdaṇḍa ity āha sa eva |

	āpadgatas tathā vṛddhaḥ garbhiṇī bāla eva vā |

	paribhāṣaṇam arhanti tac ca śodhyam iti sthitiḥ ||

taṭākādāv amedhyakartur atyantāparādhitvād daṇḍe 'py atyantādhikyam āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	taṭākodyānatīrthāni yo 'medhyena vināśayet |

	amedhyaṃ śodhayitvā tu daṇḍayet pūrvasāhasam ||

kaśmalacelanirṇejanādinā tīrthadūṣakasyāpy ayam eva daṇḍa ity āha sa eva |

	dūṣayet siddhatīrthāni sthāpitāni mahātmabhiḥ |

	puṇyāni pāvanīyāni prāpnuyāt pūrvasāhasam ||

aparādhāntareṣu daṇḍān āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	maryādāyāḥ prabhede tu sīmātikramaṇe tathā |

	kṣetrasya haraṇe daṇḍā adhamottamamadhyamāḥ ||

sīmāliṅgavināśakasya prathamasāhaso daṇḍaḥ, kṣetrasyāpaharaṇe 'pahartur madhyamasāhaso daṇḍa ity arthaḥ | yat tu viṣṇunoktam: "sīmābhettāram uttamasāhasaṃ daṇḍayitvā punaḥ sīmāṃ kārayet" iti, tatra sīmābhettāram ity asya sīmām ullaṅghya karṣakam ity artho 'dhyavaseyaḥ | sīmāpradeśe punaḥkarṣaṇādyakaraṇam eva punaḥ sīmākaraṇam, tad yathā bhavati tathā rājā yateteti punaḥ sīmāṃ kārayed ity asyārthaḥ | uttamasāhasābhidhānam ardhasīmātikramaviṣayam | samagrasīmātikramaviṣaye tv āhatuḥ śaṅkhalikhitau: "sīmātikrameṣv aṣṭasahasram" iti | daṇḍa iti śeṣaḥ | daṇḍādhikyāt samagrasīmātikramaviṣayatvam asya vacanasya nyāyyam | svalpasīmātikramaviṣaye tv āha vṛddhamanuḥ |

	sthāpitāṃ caiva marydām ubhayor grāmayos tathā |

	atikrāmanti ye darpāt te daṇḍyāḥ dviśataṃ damam ||

daṇḍālpatvād alpātikramaviṣayam etad iti nyāyyam | yas tu yājñavalkīye sīmāliṅgavināśe prathamasāhasa uktaḥ sa gṛhasīmāliṅgavināśaviṣayaḥ daṇḍasyālpatvāt | kṣetrasīmāliṅgavināśaviṣaye tv aparādhādhikyād daṇḍādhikyam āhatuḥ śaṅkhalikhitau: "kṣetramaryādābhede tv aṣṭaśatam" iti | daṇḍa iti śeṣaḥ | evaṃ grāmādisīmāliṅgavināśe daṇḍādhikyam ūhyam | uktavidhinā daṇḍayitvā punar gṛhādīnāṃ sīmāliṅgāni kārayed iti cohyam | yas tu yājñavalkīye kṣetrāpaharaṇe madhyamasāhasa uktaḥ sa tu balād apahāraviṣayaḥ | catvāriṃśadadhikapañcaśatakārṣāpaṇātmakasya madhyamasāhasasya gurudaṇḍatvāt | bhayapradarśanenājñānena vāpaharaṇe kṛte tu manur āha |

	gṛhaṃ taṭākam ārāmaṃ kṣetraṃ vā bhīṣayā haran |

	śatāni pañca daṇḍyāḥ syād ajñānād dviśato damaḥ ||

yat tu śaṅkhalikhitābhyām uktam: "kṣetrodakāpaharaṇe aṣṭaśatam" iti, daṇḍa iti śeṣaḥ | tad etad balātkāreṇa sodakaśālyādikṣetrāpaharaṇe draṣṭavyam | evam apahriyamāṇakṣetrādibhūstvāpekṣayā daṇḍādhikyam ūhyam | sīmotpannavṛkṣādiphalapuṣpāpahāradaṇḍaprāptiparihāropayoginam artham āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	sīmāmadhye tu jātānāṃ vṛkṣāṇāṃ kṣetrayor dvayoḥ |

	phalaṃ puṣpaṃ ca sāmānyaṃ kṣetrasvāmiṣu nirdiśet ||

sāmānyaṃ sādhāraṇam | kṣetrasvāmiṣu savṛkṣasīmakṣetrayoḥ svāmiṣu | yady ekakṣetrasvāmy eva sarvaphalam āharet tadā tasminn arthaphalāpahāradaṇḍaprāptiḥ | yeṣāṃ tu vṛkṣādīnām ekasya kṣetre mūlapradeśā vartante anyakṣetrasyopari śākhās tadviṣaye 'py āha sa eva |

	anyakṣetre tu jātānāṃ śākhā yatrānysaṃśritāḥ |

	svāminaṃ taṃ vijānīyād yasya kṣetreṣu saṃśritāḥ ||

saṃśritā āśritāḥ jātā iti yāvat ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ gṛhādiviṣayāṇi**

**atha setvādiviṣayāṇi**

tatra nāradaḥ |

	setus tu dvividho jñeyaḥ khanyo bandhyas tathaiva ca |

	toyapravartane khanyo bandhyaḥ syād vinivartane ||

kṣetrasthitādhikodakanirgamanārthaṃ khātvā yaḥ kriyate setuḥ sa khanyaḥ, āgatodakadhāraṇārthaṃ mṛdādibhiḥ yatra jalapravāho badhyate sa setuḥ bandhya ity arthaḥ | tatra nātinimnatayā khanyaḥ kāryaḥ, nātyuccatayā bandhya iti darśayitum anudakātyudakanindām āha sa eva |

	nāntareṇodakaṃ sasyaṃ nāśaś cātyudake sati |

	ya evātyudake doṣaḥ sa evānudake bhavet ||

ato yathā na sarvodakahānis tathā khanyaḥ kāryaḥ, yathā ca nātibahūdakasthitiḥ tathā bandhyaḥ kāryaḥ ity abhiprāyaḥ | setubandhapratibandhakam api praty āha sa eva |

	parakṣetrasya madhye tu setur na pratiṣidhyate |

	mahāguṇo 'lpadoṣaś ced vṛddhir iṣṭā kṣaye sati ||

asyārthaḥ: svakṣetre pareṇa kriyamāṇaḥ setuḥ svakṣetre 'py apekṣitodakasthāpakatvādimahāguṇavān, svakṣetralavanāśakaratayālpadoṣavān kṣetrasvāminā na pratiṣedhyo yasmāt alpakṣetrakṣaye saty api sasyasamṛddhir iṣṭeti | cecchabdāt kutracit uktavaiparītye pratiṣedhya iti darśayati | yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	na niṣedhyo 'lpavādhas tu setuḥ kalyāṇakārakaḥ |

	parabhūmiṃ haran kūpaḥ svalpakṣetro bahūdakaḥ ||

na niṣedhya ity anuṣaṅgāt kūpapadenāpi saṃbadhyate | svalpakṣetraḥ svalpakṣetravartī | evaṃ cāyam arthaḥ: parabhūmiṃ svalpāṃ haran bahūdakaḥ kūpaḥ pareṇa bhūsvāminā na pratiṣedhya iti | viparītas tv atrāpi niṣedhya eva | yat punas tenoktam,

	svāmine yo 'nivedyaiva kṣetre setuṃ pravartayet |

	utpanne svāmino bhogas tadabhāve mahīpateḥ ||

iti, tasya sati saṃbhave kṣetrasvāminaṃ tadabhāve rājānaṃ vānujñāpyaiva pareṇa parakṣetre setvādikaḥ pravartanīya ity atra tātparyam, na punar anivedane setvādivaśād utpannaparakṣetraphalabhoktṛnirūpaṇe, vacanavaiyarthyaprasaṅgāt | na hi setvādipravartanamātreṇa paraḥ parakṣetrotpannaphalabhoktṛtāṃ pratipadyate, yena tannivāraṇārthaṃ vacanam arthavat bhavet | kecit tu setvādinirmāṇotpannadṛṣṭādṛṣṭaphalabhoktṛnirūpaṇārthaṃ vacanam etad iti vadanti | yad atra yuktaṃ tad grāhyam | evam evānivedya jīrṇoddhāre kṛte 'pi boddhavyam | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	pūrvapravṛttam utpannam apṛṣṭvā svāminaṃ tu yaḥ |

	setuṃ pravartayet kaścin na sa tatphalabhāg bhavet ||

	mṛte tu svāmini punaḥ tadvaṃśye vāpi mānave |

	rājānam āmantrya tataḥ kuryāt setupravartanam ||

	ato 'nyathā kleśabhāk syāt mṛgavyādhāvamarśanāt |

	iṣavas tasya naśyanti yo viddham anuvidhyati || iti |

avamarśanaṃ nidarśanam | tasya mṛgavyādhasya | kātyāyano 'pi |

	asvāmyanumatenaiva saṃskāraṃ kurute tu yaḥ |

	gṛhodyānataṭākānāṃ saṃskartā labhate na tu ||

	vyayaṃ svāmini cāyāte na nivedya nṛpe yadi |

	athāvedya prayuktas tu tadgataṃ labhate vyayam || iti |

āvedya nṛpe tatprayuktaḥ saṃskartā saṃskārakṛtaṃ vyayaṃ labhate ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ setvādiviṣayāṇi**

**atha kṣetrakartṛviṣayāṇi**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ: "gṛhītvā bāhayet kāle" iti | kṣetrādiviṣaye kṣetrādisvāmipārśve aham idaṃ kariṣyāmīti kṛṣīvalaḥ kṣetraṃ gṛhītvā grīṣmādikāle lāṅgalādikaṃ balīvardādibhir vāhayed ity arthaḥ | vāhanagrahaṇaṃ tadādiphalasaṃgrahaṇāntavyāpārasyopalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva kṛṣimātraṃ kurvan kṛṣīvalo vyāpāraikadeśakaratayā duṣṭatvāt kṣetraphalamūlyatayā kalpitaṃ kṣetrasvāmine rājñā dāpya ity āha sa eva: "vāpagopansaṃgrahān | akurvan svāmine dāpyaḥ" iti | vāpo bīnānām āvāpaḥ | gopanaṃ sasyādirakṣaṇam | saṃgrahaḥ phalasaṃgrahaṇam | vākyārthas tu yājñavalkyena vivṛtaḥ |

	phālāhatam api kṣetraṃ yo na kuryān na kārayet |

	taṃ pradāpyākṛṣṭaśadaṃ kṣetram anyena kārayet ||

phālāhataṃ phālena vidāritaṃ kṛṣṭam iti yāvat | na bījāvāpayogyaṃ mārdavādikaṃ kuryāt | akṛṣṭaśadam akṛṣṭatvena sthitakṣetrād yat tṛṇādi phalaṃ labhyate tad akṛṣṭaśadam | anyena kṛṣīvalāntareṇa | yas tu kṣetraṃ gṛhītvā kṣetrakaraṇakālārdhe gate karṣaṇaṃ kurute sa kālātyayāparādhānurūpaṃ damaṃ dāpya ity āha bṛhaspatiḥ: "madhye kṛṣṭe damaṃ tu saḥ" iti | dāpya ity anuṣajyate | yas tu kṣetraṃ gṛhītvā tatkaraṇakālāntaparyantaṃ na kiṃcit karoti kārayati ca, tam api praty āha sa eva |

	kṣetraṃ gṛhītvā yaḥ kaścin na kuryān na ca kārayet |

	svāmine sa śadaṃ dāpyo rājñā daṇḍaṃ ca tatsamam ||

śadaṃ kṣetraphalam, tatsamaṃ svāmigrāhyaśadasamam | svāmigrāhyaśado 'pi kiyān ity apekṣite sa evāha |

	cirāvasanne daśamaṃ kṛṣyamāṇe tathāṣṭamam |

	svasaṃskṛte tu ṣaṣṭhaṃ syāt parikalpya yathāsthitam ||

cirāvasanne cirakālam akṛṣṭakṣetraṃ kariṣyāmīti svīkṛtya upekṣite, yāvatphalam anupekṣite labhyate tasya daśamaṃ bhāgaṃ mūlyadvāreṇa dāpyaḥ | kṛṣyamāṇe acirāvasanne kṣetre svīkṛtyopekṣite tv aṣṭamaṃ bhāgaṃ dāpyaḥ | svasaṃskṛte tu kṣetre svīkṛtyopekṣite ṣaṣṭhaṃ bhāgaṃ dāpya ity arthaḥ | yat tu kṣetraṃ svāminaḥ sāmarthyavaikalyādinā khilatvādyavasthayā sthitaṃ gṛhītvā tad yena kṛṣīvalena svāmyanivāritena kṛtaṃ tat praty āha nāradaḥ |

	aśaktapretanaṣṭeṣu kṣetrikeṣv anivāritaḥ |

	kṣetraṃ ced vikṛṣet kaścid aśnuvīta sa tatphalam ||

aśaktāḥ kṣetrakaraṇasāmarthyavikalāḥ | pretāḥ svaryātāḥ | naṣṭāḥ kutra gatā iti cirakālam avijñātāḥ | kṣetrikāḥ kṣetrasvāminaḥ | etad uktaṃ bhavati: parakṣetratve 'pi khilabhūtabhūviṣaye kartuḥ phalabhogo na jātu phaladaṇḍadāpanam iti | prasaṅgāt kṣetrasvāminam āgatam api praty āha sa eva |

	vikṛṣyamāṇe kṣetre tu kṣetrikaḥ punar āvrajet |

	khilopacāraṃ tat sarvaṃ datvā svaṃ kṣetram āpnuyāt ||

khilopacāraḥ kilhabhañjanārtho vyayaḥ  | tasyeyattāvadhāraṇaṃ khilabhūtakṣetrakāṭhinyatāratamyāyattam iti tat tāratamyam āha sa eva |

	saṃvatsareṇārdhakhilaṃ khilaṃ syād vatsarais tribhiḥ |

	pañcavarṣāvasannaṃ tu kṣetraṃ syād aṭavīsamam ||

saṃvatsaropekṣitaṃ kṣetram ardhakhilam īṣadduṣkarṣaṃ bhavati, trivatsaropekṣitaṃ tu khilaṃ syād duṣkarṣaṃ bhavet | pañcavarṣopekṣitaṃ punar aṭavīsamaṃ syāt atyantaduṣkarṣaṃ bhaved ity arthaḥ | yadā khilabhañjanārthaṃ vyayaṃ svāmī na dātum utsahate tadā tv āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	aśaktito na dadyāc cet khilārthe yat kṛto vyayaḥ |

	tad aṣṭabhāgahīnaṃ tu karṣakaḥ phalam āpnuyāt ||

	varṣāṇy aṣṭau sa bhoktā syāt parataḥ svāmine tu tat | iti |

khilārthe yaḥ kṛto vyayaḥ tatpratidānāsamarthaḥ svāmī karṣakāya yadi khilavyayaṃ na dadyāt tadā karṣakaḥ kṣetraphalsyāṣṭamaṃ bhāgam aṣṭau varṣāṇi yāvat svāmine datvā avaśiṣṭaṃ gṛhṇīyāt tadūrdhvaṃ svāmine tat kṣetraṃ samarpayed ity arthaḥ | yad etat "vikṛṣyamāṇe kṣetre" ityādinā "parataḥ svāmine tu tat" ityantenoktaṃ tat sarvaṃ pretakṣetraviṣaye tatputrādyāgamane 'pi kāryam, aśaktanaṣṭakṣetraviṣaye tu teṣām āgamane tatputrādīnām āgamane vā kāryam iti mantavyam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ kṣetrakartṛviṣayāṇi**

**samāptaś ca kṣetrajavivādākhyasya padasya vidhivitānaḥ **

**atha strīpuṃsaṃbandhākhyasya padasya vidhir ucyate**

tatra manuḥ |

	puruṣasya striyāś caiva dharmye vartmani tiṣṭhatoḥ |

	saṃyoge viprayoge ca dharmān vakṣyāmi śāśvatān ||

dharmye vartmani śāstrīye mārge | saṃyoge anyonyasaṃnidhāne | viprayoge deśataḥ kālato vā vyavadhāne | śāśvatān nityān avaśyānuṣṭheyān iti yāvat | etad uktaṃ bhavati: anucchṛṅkhalayoḥ jāyāpatyoḥ anyonyam avipratipattisiddhyartham avaśyaṃ ye dharmāḥ parasparasaṃnidhāv asaṃnidhau cānuṣṭheyāḥ tān vakṣyāmīti | ke punas te dharmā ity apekṣite sa evāha |

	asvatantrāḥ striyaḥ kāryāḥ puruṣaiḥ svaiḥ divāniśam |

	viṣaye sajjamānāś ca saṃsthāpyā hy ātmano vaśe ||

svaiḥ puruṣaiḥ bhartrādipuruṣaiḥ | viṣaye vināśahetubhūtaśītādiviṣaye | nārado 'pi |

	svātantyād vipraṇaśyanti kule jātā api striyaḥ |

	asvātantryam atas tāsāṃ prajāpatir akalpayat ||

ato 'nyair api svastrīṇāṃ yathā bhavaty asvātantryaṃ tathaiva kalpayitavyam iti śeṣaḥ | duṣprasaṅgād api rakṣaṇaṃ kartavyam | tathā ca hārītaḥ: "jāyānāśe kulanāśaḥ kulanāśe tantunāśaḥ tantunāśe devapitṛnāśo yajñanāśo dharmanāśo dharmanāśe ātmanāśaḥ ātmanāśe sarvanāśaḥ tasmād enāṃ dharmaśīlāṃ suguptāṃ patnīṃ rakṣet" iti | manur api |

	sūkṣmebhyo 'pi prasaṅgebhyaḥ striyo rakṣyā viśeṣataḥ |

	dvayor hi kulayoḥ śokam āvaheyur arakṣitāḥ ||

	imaṃ hi sarvavarṇānāṃ paśyanto dharmam anuttamam |

	yatante rakṣituṃ bhāryāṃ bhartāro durbalā api ||

	svāṃ prasūtiṃ caritraṃ ca kulam ātmānam eva ca |

	svaṃ ca dharmaṃ prayatnena jāyāṃ rakṣan sa rakṣati || iti |

arakṣitāḥ striyo duścaritena dvayoḥ kulayoḥ bhartṛpitṛkulayoḥ śokam āvaheyuḥ kuryur ity arthaḥ | anena kuladvayavṛddhair api rakṣyā iti tatkleśakathanam upadarśitam | darśitaṃ cāsāṃ rakṣaṇaṃ bṛhaspatinā |

	sūkṣmebhyo 'pi prasaṅgebhyo nivāryā strī svabandhubhiḥ |

	svastrādibhiḥ gurustrībhiḥ pālanīyā divāniśam ||

manus tv ātmanaiva puruṣavat striyo 'pi guptā bhaviṣyantīti buddhyā strīrakṣaṇe puruṣeṇānāsthā na kāryeti pratipādanārtham āha |

	naitā rūpaṃ pratīkṣante nāsāṃ vayasi saṃsthitiḥ |

	surūpaṃ vā virūpaṃ vā pumān ity eva bhuñjate ||

	pauṃścalyāc calacittatvān naiḥsnehyāc ca svabhāvataḥ |

	rakṣitā yatnato 'pīha bhartṛṣv etā vikurvate ||

	śayyāsanam alaṃkāraṃ kāmaṃ krodham anārthatām |

	drohabhāvaṃ kucaryāṃ ca strībhyo manur akalpayan ||

	evaṃ svabhāvaṃ jñātvāsāṃ prajāpatinisargajam |

	paramaṃ yatnam ātiṣṭhet puruṣo rakṣaṇaṃ prati || iti | \
drohabhāvo dakṣeṇa prapañcitaḥ |

	jalūkāvat striyaḥ sarvā bhūṣaṇācchādanāśanaiḥ |

	saṃbhṛtāpi kṛtā nityaṃ puruṣaṃ hy apakarṣati ||

	jalūkā raktam ādatte kevalaṃ sā tapasvinī |

	itarā tu dhanaṃ vittaṃ māṃsaṃ vīryaṃ balaṃ sukham ||

	sāśaṅkā bālabhāve tu yauvane vimukhī bhavet |

	tṛṇavan manyate nārī vṛddhabhāve punaḥ patim || iti |

bhūṣaṇābhiḥ saṃbhṛtā kṛtāpi puruṣaṃ nityam apakarṣati satatam avajñāpātraṃ karotīty arthaḥ | itarā strīty arthaḥ | dhanam ityādau pratipadam ādatta ity anuṣajyate | evaṃ drohabhāvam atiśayena vadato dakṣasyāyam abhiprāyaḥ: bhāryāyāṃ bahudhā bahuvidhadauṣṭyadarśane 'pi jātisvabhāvanibandhane kim atra citram ity udvegam utsṛjya pālane yatnānuvṛttiḥ kāryeti | bharyāyā bharaṇe 'pi ca puruṣeṇa yauvane yatitavyam | tathā ca manuḥ |

	pitā rakṣati kaumāre bhartā rakṣati yauvane |

	rakṣanti sthāvire putrā na strī svātantryam arhati ||

patiputravihīnāyās tūbhayavidharakṣaṇaṃ patipakṣāntargatena pratyāsannena kāryam | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	mṛte bhartary aputrāyāḥ patipakṣaḥ prabhuḥ striyāḥ |

	viniyogātmarakṣāsu bharaṇe ca sa īśvaraḥ ||

viniyogaḥ karmaṇi niyojanam | patipakṣasyāpy abhāve sa evāha |

	parikṣīṇe patikule nirmanuṣye nirāśraye |

	tatsapiṇḍeṣu cāsatsu pitṛpakṣaḥ prabhuḥ striyāḥ ||

viniyogādiṣv iti śeṣaḥ | pitṛpakṣasyāpy abhāve sa evāha |

	pakṣadvayāvasāne tu rājā bhartā smṛtaḥ striyāḥ |

	sa tasyā bharaṇaṃ kuryān nigṛhṇīyāt paticyutām ||

bhartā bharaṇakartā ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ strīrakṣaṇavidhiḥ**

**atha strīrakṣaṇaprakāraḥ**

tatra manuḥ |

	na kaścid yoṣitaḥ śaktaḥ prasahya parirakṣitum |

	etair upāyayogais tu śaktas tāḥ parirakṣitum ||

prasahya ākramya avarudhyeti yāvat | yady apy avarodhena śārīravyabhicārād rakṣaṇaṃ śakyam, tathāpi mānasavyabhicārād rakṣaṇam aśakyam iti manvānena manunā,

	na kaścid yośitaḥ śaktaḥ prashya parirakṣitum |

ityādy uktam | na ca māstu mānasavyabhicārād rakṣaṇam, anyajātyasaṃbhavena prajāśuddhivighātābhāvād iti vācyam | yata āha sa eva |

	yādṛśaṃ bhajate hi strī sutaṃ sūte tathāvidham |

	tasmāt prajāviśuddhyarthaṃ striyaṃ rakṣet prayatnataḥ ||

yādṛśaṃ puruṣam ṛtukāle strī manasā bhajate tatsamānaśīlaṃ putraṃ janayatīti pūrvārdhasyārthaḥ | tathā ca śaṅkhalikhitau: "yasmin bhāvo 'rpitaḥ strīṇām ārtave tacchīlaṃ putraṃ janayati" iti | ato mānasavyabhicārād api striyaḥ rakṣed iti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca manunā "tasmāt" ityādinā uttarārdhena ayam eva vidhir darśitaḥ | parirakṣaṇopāyā api manunā darśitāḥ |

	arthasya saṃgrahe caināṃ vyaye caiva niyojayet |

	śauce dharme 'nnapaktyāṃ ca pārīṇahyasya cekṣaṇe ||

saṃgrahe svena samānītārthasaṃvidhāne | vyaye svenoktavyaye | śauce gṛhādiśuddhikarasaṃmārjanānulepanādau | dharme agnihotrādyanukūlalaukikavyāpāre | annapaktyāṃ cullīsaṃmārjanādipākavyāpāre | pārīṇahyasyekṣaṇe piṭharādigṛhopakaraṇapratīkṣaṇe | etad uktaṃ bhavati: akutsitāvaśyakavyāpāravaiyagryavaśena puruṣāntaracintanādyavasararāhityaṃ bhāryāyā yathā bhavati tathā kuryād iti | bṛhaspatināpi pūrvoktā evopāyā uktāḥ |

	āyavyaye 'nnasaṃskāre gṛhopaskārarakṣaṇe |

	śauce 'gnikārye saṃyojyāḥ strīṇāṃ śuddhir iyaṃ smṛtā ||

iyam uktopāyaprabhavā strīṇāṃ śuddhiḥ sādhvī smṛtety arthaḥ | tathā ca manunā smaryate |

	ātmānam ātmanā yās tu rakṣeyus tāḥ surakṣitāḥ | iti |

ātmanā arthasaṃgrahādyāsaktacittenety arthaḥ | āptapuruṣais tu rakṣitāḥ striyo na samyag rakṣitā ity āha sa eva |

	arakṣitā gṛhe ruddhāḥ puruṣair āptakāribhiḥ | iti |

āptakāribhiḥ puruṣair gṛhe ruddhā ity anvayaḥ | arakṣitāḥ samyagrakṣāvihīnā ity arthaḥ | samyagrakṣāvihīnatvaṃ ca prāg evābhihitam | pānādinivāraṇam api nārīrakṣaṇaprakāra iti darśayitum āha sa eva |

	pānaṃ durjanasaṃsargaḥ patyā ca viraho 'ṭanam |

	svapno 'nyagehe vāsaś ca nārīṇāṃ dūṣaṇāni ṣaṭ || iti |

tenaitāny avahitena patiprabhṛtinā nārīṣu pratiṣeddhavyānīti śeṣaḥ | pānaṃ madyādīnām | patyā ca viraho deśāntare patim utsṛjyāvasthānam | aṭanaṃ vinā patyā tīrthayātrādikaraṇam | svapno yatra kutra vā śayanam | anyegehe vāsaḥ paragṛhe vasanam | patyuḥ śaiṣṭyam api strīrakṣaṇaprakāra iti darśayitum āha sa eva |

	yādṛgguṇena bhartrā strī saṃyujyeta yathāvidhi |

	tādṛgguṇā sā bhavati samudreṇeva nimnagā ||

avyabhicāravyabhicārayoḥ śubhāśubhaphalajñāpanam api strīrakṣaṇaprakāra iti darśayituṃ tayoḥ phalam āha sa eva |

	patiṃ yā nāticarati manovākkāyasaṃyatā |

	sā bhartṛlokān āpnoti sadbhiḥ sādhvīti cocyate ||

	vyabhicārāt tu bhartuḥ strī loke prāpnoti nindyatām |

	sṛgālayoniṃ prāpnoti pāparogaiś ca pīḍyate || iti |

bharaṇarūparakṣaṇasyāpi prakāraṃ darśayitum āha sa eva |

	devadattāṃ patir bhāryāṃ vindate necchayātmanaḥ |

	tāṃ sādhvīṃ bibhṛyān nityaṃ devānāṃ priyam ācaran ||

devair dattā devadattā devavaśāyāteti yāvat | tāṃ bhāryāṃ svayaṃvare patir vindate na punar ātmecchayā ātmavyāpāreṇa vindate | tatra svavyāpārābhāvāt tāṃ devavaśāyātāṃ sādhvīṃ śobhanāṃ nityaṃ bibhṛyāt poṣayed ity arthaḥ | na caivaṃ mānuṣavaśād āyātāyāṃ bhāryāyāṃ bharaṇam anāvaśyakam iti vācyam | daṇḍāpūpanyāyena tatrāpi nityaṃ bibhṛyād iti vidhir gamyate yataḥ | tathā hi, vareṇāvṛtāpy avaśyaṃ bhartavyety ukte varavṛtā tu sutarām iti gamyate | na ca sādhvīm ity asya pativratām ity arthāntaraparatvena na vyabhicāriṇīṃ bibhṛyād ity artho 'rthād gamyata iti vyabhicāriṇyāḥ bharaṇam anāvaśyakam iti vācyam, tasyā apy avaśyabharaṇīyatvāt | tatrānutkaṭavyabhicāriṇī satīva bharaṇīyā, asaṃvyavahāryaiva paramāprāyaścittakaraṇāt | utkaṭavyabhicāriṇy api paścāttāpākhyaprāyaścittādhikāraviśeṣeṇa siddhiparyantam avaśyaṃ bhartavyā, kiṃ tu kadannādinā | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	vyabhicāre striyā mauṇḍyam adhaḥśayanam eva ca |

	kadannaṃ ca kuvāsaś ca karma cāvaskaro 'nvaham ||

striyā atyantavyabhicāre jāte mauṇḍyam adhaḥśayanaṃ ca sādhayet, kadannaṃ kuvāsaś ca bharaṇārthaṃ dadyāt | amedhyaśodhanarūpaṃ ca karma kārayed ity arthaḥ | evaṃ ca manuvṛttau sādhvīm ity asya yad arthāntaram uktam: "yad vā sādhvīṃ pativratāṃ bibhṛyāt na vyabhicāriṇīm" iti, tat tu heyam | hārīto 'pi atyantavyabhicāriṇyāḥ bharaṇam āvaśyakam ity āha |

	bhāryāyā vyabhicāriṇyāḥ parityāgo na vidyate |

	dadyāt piṇḍaṃ kucelaṃ cāpy adhaḥśayyāṃ ca śodhayet ||

piṇḍaṃ kṣunnivāraṇamātrakṛt kadannam ity arthaḥ | adhaḥ śayyā yasyāḥ sā adhāḥśayyā tām | yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	hṛtādhikārāṃ malināṃ piṇḍamātropajīvinīm |

	paribhūtām adhaḥśayyāṃ vāsayed vyabhicāriṇīm ||

hṛtādhikārāṃ śrautasmārtādikarmaṇi nivṛttādhikārām | paribhūtām anadhikṛtām | vāsayet svagṛhaikadeśa iti śeṣaḥ,

	vipraduṣṭāṃ striyaṃ bhartā nirundhyād ekaveśmani |

iti manusmaraṇāt | vipraduṣṭāṃ kāyikavyabhicāreṇātyantaduṣṭām ity arthaḥ | tathā ca śaṅkhalikhitau: "kāmacāriṇīṃ malināṃ kucelāṃ piṇḍamātropajīvanīṃ nivṛttādhikārām adhaḥśayyāṃ niruddhāṃ nivāsayed atyarthavyabhicāriṇīm" iti | kāmacāriṇīṃ parapuruṣakāmanayā carantīm ity arthaḥ | svacchandacāriṇyās tyājyatvād evaṃ vyākhyātā kṛtā | tasyās tyājyatvam āha yamaḥ |

	svacchandagā ca yā nārī tasyās tyāgo vidhīyate | iti |

saṃvyavahāryatvāpādakaprāyaścittābhāvo yad gamane bhavati tam api yā gacchati sā svacchandagā | atyarthavyabhicārīṇī tu na tyājyā, prāyaścittena saṃvyavahāryatvasaṃbhavāt | yat tu yājñavalkyenoktam,

	somaḥ śaucaṃ dadau strīṇāṃ gandharvaś ca śubhāṃ giram |

	pāvakaḥ sarvamedhyatvaṃ medhyā vai yoṣito hy ataḥ ||

iti, sarvamedhyatvaṃ sarvayajñārhatvam ity arthaḥ | tad etat praśaṃsāmātram, tena vipraduṣṭatvaṃ hṛtādhikāratvaṃ ca vyabhicāriṇyā uktam aviruddham | yat punar manunoktam,

	prajanārthaṃ mahābhāgāḥ pūjārhā gṛhadīptayaḥ |

	striyaś śriyaś ca geheṣu na viśeṣo 'sti kaścana || 

iti, pūjārhāḥ pūjāspadībhūtā ity arthaḥ | tad etad avipraduṣṭastrīviṣayam | tena paribhāvāspadatvaṃ vyabhicāriṇyā uktam aviruddham | maṅgalārtham apy avipraduṣṭāḥ striyaḥ pitrādibhiḥ pūjyā ity āha sa eva |

	pitṛbhir bhrātṛbhiś caitāḥ patibhir devarais tathā |

	pūnyā bhūṣayitavyāś ca bahukalyāṇam īpsubhiḥ ||

devarāḥ patyuḥ bhrātaraḥ | yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	bhartṛbhrātṛpitṛjñātiśvaśrūśvaśuradevaraiḥ |

	bandhubhiś ca striyaḥ pūjyā bhūṣaṇācchādanāśanaiḥ ||

atra bhartṛvyatiriktaiḥ pūjanam utsavaviṣaye draṣṭavyam | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	bhartrā patnī samabhyarcyā vastrālaṃkārabhojanaiḥ |

	utsave tu pitṛbhrātṛśvaśurādyāiś ca bandhubhiḥ ||

tatra manuḥ |

	yatra nāryas tu pūjyante ramante tatra devatāḥ |

	yatra tās tu na pūjyante sarvās tatrāphalāḥ kriyāḥ ||

	śocanti yoṣito yatra vinaśyanty āśu tatkulam |

	na śocanti tu yatraitā vardhate tatra sarvadā || iti |

śocanti bharaṇapūjanayor abhāveneti śeṣaḥ | yatra kula ity arthaḥ | pravatsyatā tu pratyāgamanaparyantaṃ bharaṇārtham arthasaṃvidhānaṃ vidhātavyam | anyathā sanmārge sthitāpi vardhanarāhityād dhairyacyutā vṛttyarthaṃ vyabhicared ity āha sa eva |

	vidhāya vṛttiṃ bhāryāyāḥ pravaset kāryavān naraḥ |

	avṛttikarśitā hi strī praduṣyet sthitimaty api ||

dveṣānuvṛttimatyās tu bhāryāyāḥ dveṣānuvṛtteḥ prāk pūjanāya dattaṃ vastrābharaṇādikaṃ saṃvatsarād ūrdhvaṃ hṛtvā tām ṛtukāle 'pi na sevety āha sa eva |

	saṃvatsaram udīkṣeta dviṣantīṃ yoṣitaṃ patiḥ |

	ūrdhvaṃ saṃvatsarāt tv enāṃ hṛtvā na saṃvaset ||

udīkṣeta dveṣānuvṛttiṃ pratīkṣeta | ūrdhvaṃ saṃvatsarāt dveṣānuvṛttau satyām iti śeṣaḥ | dāyaṃ pūjanāya dattam | vṛttyarthaṃ tu kalpitam anāharyam, bhāryāyā dveṣānuvṛttiśālinyā api bharaṇasyāvaśyakatvāt | uktārthasya kvacid apavādam āha sa eva |

	unmattaṃ patitaṃ klībam abījaṃ vāpi rogiṇam |

	na pradviṣantyās tyāgo 'sti na ca dāyāpavartanam ||

klībaṃ nirutsāham | abījaṃ nirvīryam | etad uktaṃ bhavati: dṛṣṭādṛṣṭavaikalyanibandhanadveṣānuvṛttāv apy ayuktakāritvābhāvād ṛtugamanatyāgādir atra nāstīti | yājñavalkyas tv adhivinnāyā bharaṇam evāvaśyakaṃ na pūjanādikam ity āha |

	adhivinnā ca bhartavyā mahad eno 'nyathā bhavet |

bhartavyā pūrvavad eveti śeṣaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ strīrakṣaṇaprakāraḥ**

**athādhivedanaviṣayāṇi kānicid vacanāni likhyante**

tatra manuḥ |

	madyapāsabhyavṛttā ca pratikūlā ca yā bhavet |

	vyādhitā cādhivettavyā hiṃsrārthaghnī ca sarvadā ||

adhivedanamātrayogyapātivratyarahitā madyapātra vivakṣitā, na punar mahāpātakavaśāt tyāge 'pi yogyā surāpī | asabhyavṛttā vyabhicāraratā durācārā vā | pratikūlā nityam iṣṭaviparītakāriṇī | vyādhitā dīrgharogā | hiṃsrā atikrūrā | arthaghnī svātantryeṇārthavyayaśīlā | adhivettavyeti pañcasv anuṣajyate | adhivedanaṃ pūrvasthitabhāryopari pariṇayanam | arthaghnī ceti caśabdo 'nuktasamuccayārthaḥ | kāḥ punaś caśabdasamuccitā ity apekṣite śaṅkhalikhitau: "dhūrtāṃ vaināsikīṃ strījananīṃ vandhyām apriyavādinīm apriyaśīlāṃ puruṣadveṣiṇīm ananukūlāṃ cādhivindet" iti | dhūrtā pratārikā | vaināsikī vigatanāsā | strījananī stryapatyamātrajananī | etad uktaṃ bhavati: dharmakāryaputralābhayoḥ siddhir yayā saha na saṃbhavati tām atītya bhāryāntaraṃ vinded iti | kāmasiddhis tu yayā saha na saṃbhavati paripūrṇā vā na bhavati tām arthais toṣayitvā bhāryāntaram udvahed ity āha devalaḥ |

	ekām utkramya kāmārtham anyāṃ labdhuṃ ya icchati |

	samarthas toṣayitārthaiḥ pūrvoḍhām aparāṃ vahet ||

kvacit pūrvabhāryātaḥ vivāhāntare (?) 'nujñāṃ prāpyānyām udvahed ity āha manuḥ |

	yā rogiṇī syāt tu hitā saṃpannā caiva śīlataḥ |

	sānujñāpyādhivettavyā nāvamānyā ca karhicit ||

rogiṇī dīrgharogā | hitā bhartur abhyudayārthinī | kvacit kālakṣepeṇa kvacit taṃ vinaivādhivedanaṃ kāryam ity āha sa eva |

	vandhyāṣṭame 'dhivedyābde daśame tu mṛtaprajā |

	ekādaśe strījananī sadyas tv apriyavādinī ||

aṣṭame 'bde gate iti śeṣaḥ | "aprajāṃ navame varṣe" iti hārītasmaraṇāt | evam ekādaśe ity atrāpi śeṣo 'vagantavyaḥ,

	ākāṅkṣetāṣṭavarṣāṇi bhartātiprasavāṃ striyam |

	daśa vandhyāṃ ca nindyāṃ ca dvādaśe strīprasavinīm ||

iti devalasmaraṇāt | atiprasavā atikrāntaprasavā pratigarbhaṃ garbhasrāvavatīti yāvat | vandyā anapatyā | nindyā madyapāsabhyavṛttetyevamādikā | daśa vandhyām iti priyataravandhyāviṣayam | atra manuḥ |

	adhivinnā tu yā nārī nirgacchet ruṣitā gṛhāt |

	sā sadyaḥ saṃniroddhavyā tyājyā vā kulasaṃnidhau ||

upari yasyā abhūt pariṇayanaṃ sādhivinnocyate | kulasaṃnidhau adhivinnāyāḥ pitrādikulasaṃnidhāv ity arthaḥ | tatkulasaṃnidhau tyaktāyā api bharaṇaṃ patir eva saṃnidhānakaraṇena kuryāt,

	pitā rakṣati kaumāre bhartā rakṣati yauvane |

ity uktatvāt,

	adhivinnā tu bhartavyā mahad eno 'nyathā bhavet |

ity uktatvāc ca | yā tv adhyūḍhā nārī patyur aucityājñānadoṣāt kupitā tadgṛhān nirgatā bandhubhyo 'anyam anāśritā sā patigṛhe bandhubhir āśrayabhūtaiḥ praveśanīyā | bandhurahitā cet svayam eva vimṛśya patigṛham āśrayed ity āha nāradaḥ |

	ajñānadoṣād ūḍhā yā nirgatā nānyam āśritā |

	bandhubhiḥ sā niyoktavyā nirbandhuḥ svayam āśrayet ||

yājñavalkyas tu adhivinnastrībhyo 'dhivedananimittakaṃ bhartur deyam āha |

	adhivinnastriyai dadyād ādhivedanikaṃ samam |

	na dattaṃ strīdhanaṃ yasyai dattaṃ tv ardhaṃ prakīrtitam ||

adhivinnāyai striyai strīdhanarahitāyai yāvad adhivedanārthaṃ vyayīkṛtaṃ yavad vādhunā pariṇītayai dattaṃ tatsamam adhivedananimittakadhanaṃ bhartrā deyam | tadardhaṃ tu strīdhanasahitāyai deyatvena bhartuḥ prakīrtitam ity arthaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām adhivedanaviṣayāṇi**

**athātyājyastrīviṣayāṇi**

tatra devalaḥ |

	svadārān tyajato mohān narasyānyāyamocinaḥ |

	dharmavaṃśaparityaktur niṣkṛtir na vidhīyate ||

śāstroktatyāgahetūn vinaiva yo mohādinā svastriyaṃ tyajati tasyānyāyena svadāramocinaḥ tanmocanadvāreṇa tayā saha vihitaśrautasmārtādidharmasya tasyām utpādyamānasaṃtānasya ca tyaktur niṣkṛtir nastīty arthaḥ | iha loke 'pi tasya rājñā coravad daṇḍanaṃ kāryam | tathā ca "coravac chāsyaḥ" ity anuvṛttau viṣṇuḥ: "nirdoṣāṃ parityajan patnīṃ ca" iti | tyāgahetubhūtadoṣarahitāṃ bhāryāṃ parityjann api coravad daṇḍya ity arthaḥ | guṇavatīṃ punaḥ parityajan mahatā daṇḍena vaśīkṛtya tasyām eva bhāryāyām avasthāpyaḥ | tathā ca naradaḥ |

	anukūlām avāgduṣṭāṃ dakṣāṃ sādhvīṃ prajāvatīm |

	tyajan bhāryām avasthāpyo rājñā daṇḍena bhūyasā ||

yadā punar daṇḍena mahatā tasyām avasthāpayitum aśakyas tadā tv āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	ajñāsaṃpādinīṃ dakṣāṃ vīrasūṃ priyavādinīm |

	tyajan dāpyas tṛtīyāṃśam adravyo bharaṇaṃ striyāḥ ||

guṇavatīm api bhāryāṃ yo durāgraheṇa utsṛjati taddhanatṛtīyāṃśaṃ tyakṣyamāṇabhāryāyai rājñāsau dāpyaḥ | alpadhanś ced bharaṇamātraparyāptaṃ dhanaṃ dāpya ity arthaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām atyājyastrīviṣayāṇi**

**atha tyājyastrīviṣayāṇi**

tatra nāradaḥ |

	anyonyaṃ tyajator dharmaḥ syād anyonyaṃ vikurvatoḥ |

	strīpuṃsayor na coḍhāyā vyavacārād ṛte kriyāḥ ||

vivāhasaṃskāravihīnayoḥ hīnajātīyastrīpuṃsayor anyonyavirodhenānyonyaṃ tyajatoḥ dharmaḥ syād doṣo na syād ity arthaḥ | ūḍhā vivāhasaṃskṛtā | tasyās tu vyabhicārarūpanimittam antareṇa nāsti tyāgaḥ | anena vyabhicāre saty ūḍhāyā apy asty eva tyāga ity arthād uktam | tac ca svacchandavyabhicāriṇīviṣayam,

	svacchandagā ca yā nārī tasyās tyāgo vidhīyate |

iti yamasmaraṇāt | tyāgo 'tra vadhapratinidhitvena kāryaḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	svacchandavyabhicāriṇyā vivasvāṃs tyāgam abravīt |

	na vadhaṃ na ca vaikṛtyaṃ vadhaḥ strīṇāṃ visarjanam ||

strīṇāṃ mahāparādhe vadhaṃ kurvan visarjanam eva tāsāṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | vaikṛtyaṃ karṇanāsādyaṅgavikartanam | tad api bhartrā na kadācit kāryam ity arthaḥ,

	na caiva strīvadhaṃ kuryān na caivāṅgavikartanam |

iti tenaivoktatvāt | evam eva śiṣyagāpi nārī parityājyaiva | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	catasras tu parityājyāḥ śiṣyagā gurugā ca yā |

	patighnī ca viśeṣeṇa juṅgitopagatā ca yā ||

śiṣyo bhartṛśiṣyaḥ | guruḥ pitā | juṅgitaḥ patitaḥ, pratilomajo vā | patighnī tu jñātibhiḥ parityājyā | jñātiparityaktāyāḥ kadannapradānādikam api na kartavyam, viśeṣeṇety uktatvāt | catasra ity uktiḥ na tato 'dhikaparityājyayoṣidabhāvabodhanārthā, juṅgitopagatapadena patitopagatapratilomajopagatayor abhidhānāt pūrvāparavirodhāpatteḥ | kathaṃ tarhi catasra ity uktam | ucyate, patitapratilomajopagatayor juṅgitopagatapadārthatayaikyam upetya catasra iti saṃkalīkṛtā | yat eva catasya ity uktiḥ parityājyāntarābhāvaṃ na bodhayati ata eva parityājyāntarṇy āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	.......................... garbhe tyāgo vidhīyate |

	garbhabhartṛvadhe tāsāṃ tathā mahati pātake || iti |

yatra dvijastīṇāṃ śūdrāt garbhe sati prāyaścittena saṃvyavahāryatvābhāvāt tatraiva viṣaye garbhe sati tyāgo vidhīyata iti mantavyam | tathā ca vasiṣṭhenoktam |

	brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ striyaḥ śūdreṇa saṃgatāḥ |

	aprajātā viśudhyanti prāyaścittena netarāḥ || iti |

hārīto 'pi: "garbhaghnīm adhovarṇaśiṣyagurugāminīṃ pānavyāsaktāṃ dhanadhānyavikrayakāriṇīṃ ca varjayet" iti | atrāpi yatrādhovarṇagamane pānavyasane dhanadhānavikraye ca prāyaścittena śuddhir nāstīti śāsrād gamyate tataiva visarjanavidhānam iti mantavyam | visarjanaṃ vyavahāraparityāgaḥ | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	vyavāye tīrthagamane dharmebhyaś ca nivartate | iti |

vyavāyaḥ saṃbhogaḥ | tīrthagamanaśabdenātra smārtakarma pradarśitam | dharmaśabdena śrautam | caśabdena sparśanādi laukikam | tataś cāyam arthaḥ: bhogasahāyakārisaṃsparśasaṃbhāṣaṇādibhyo varjitā strī nivartata iti | anena vacobhaṅgyā saṃbhogāder ātyantikavarjanaṃ visarjanam ity uktam | evaṃ saṃbhogādau nivṛttāyā api striyāḥ kadannādi kalpayitavyam | gṛhasamīpe gṛhāntaraṃ cety āha manuḥ |

	evam eva vidhiṃ kuryād yoṣitsu patiāsv api |

	vastrānnam āsāṃ deyaṃ tu vaseyuś ca gṛhāntike ||

devalas tu vyādhyādinā tyājyāsu saṃbhogamātrasya tyāgo na sahādhikārādīnām ity āha |

	vyādhitāṃ strīprajāṃ vandhyām unmattāṃ vigatārtavām |

	aduṣṭāṃ labate tyaktuṃ tīrthān na tv eva karmaṇaḥ||

tīrtāt saṃbhogād ity arthaḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	vandhyāṃ strījananīṃ nindyāṃ pratikūlāṃ ca sarvadā |

	kāmato nābhinandeta kurvann etan na doṣabhāk ||

nindyāṃ maraṇaśīlāpatyaprasaveneti śeṣaḥ | sarvadā pratikūlāṃ nityam iṣṭaviparītakāriṇīm | kāmataḥ saṃbhogakaraṇenety arthaḥ | na doṣabhāg iti vadan pratiṣedhavidher anityatāṃ darśayati atra bodhāyanaḥ |

	aprajāṃ navame varṣe strīprajāṃ dvādaśe tyajet |

	mṛtaprajāṃ pañcadaśe sadyas tv apriyavādinīm ||

tyajet saṃbhogata iti śeṣaḥ | apriyavādinīṃ tu sahavāsato 'pi tyajet | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	anarthaśīlā satataṃ tathaivāpriyavādinī |

	pūrvāśanā ca yā bhartuḥ tāṃ strīṃ nirvāsayed gṛhāt ||

aparā api gṛhān nirvāsanīyāḥ striyas tenaiva darśitāḥ |

	strīdhanabhraṣṭasarvasvāṃ garbhavisraṃsinīṃ tathā |

	bhartuś ca vadham icchantīṃ striyaṃ nirvāsayed gṛhāt ||

strīdhanena saha bharṣṭaṃ sarvasvaṃ yasyāḥ sā tathoktā | garbhāvisraṃsinī auṣadhādisevanayā saṃpāditagarbhasrāvā | bhartur vadham icchantī viṣapradānādineti śeṣaḥ | bodhāyanenāpi nirvāsanīyāḥ striyo darśitāḥ |

	bhartuḥ pratiniveśena yā bhāryā skandayed ṛtum |

	tāṃ grāmamadhye vikhyāpya bhrūṇaghnīṃ tu nayed gṛhāt ||

	aśuśrūṣākarīṃ nārīṃ bandhakīṃ parihiṃsikām |

	tyajanti puruṣāḥ prājñāḥ kṣipram apriyavādinīm || iti |

bandhakī puṃścalī ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ tyājyastrīviṣayāṇi**

evaṃ saṃyoge viprayoge ca puruṣasya dharmā uktāḥ | adhunā saṃyoge eva dvayor jāyāpatyor dharmā ucyante | tatra manuḥ |

	saṃtuṣṭo bhāryayā bhartā bhartrā bhāryā tathaiva ca |

	yasminn etat kule nityaṃ kalyāṇaṃ tatra vai dhruvam ||

tathaiva bhartṛvad eva bhāryā bhartrā saṃtuṣṭeti vipariṇamya pūraṇīyam, yathāsthitasya puṃliṅgatvenātrānvayāsaṃbhavāt | yasmin kule nityam etad anyonyasaṃtuṣṭatvaṃ tatra kalyāṇam, suputrajanmalakṣaṇaṃ bhāryābandhuvarge prītimattvalakṣaṇaṃ parasparāvyabhicāritvādilakṣaṇaṃ cāvaśyaṃ bhavatīty ārthaḥ | tathā ca svayam eva vyatirekamukhenānvayamukhena ca kalyāṇaśabdasya vivakṣitārthaṃ vivṛṇoti |

	yadi hi strī na roceta pumāṃsaṃ na pramodayet |

	apramodāt punaḥ puṃsaḥ prajanaṃ na pravartate ||

	striyāṃ tu rocamānāyāṃ sarvaṃ tad rocate kulam |

	tasyām arocamānāyāṃ sarvam eva na rocate ||

	anyonyasyāvyabhīcāro bhaved āmaraṇāntikaḥ | iti |

puṃsaḥ prajanaṃ putrajananam ity arthaḥ | tatkulaṃ strīkulam | dampatyor dharmāntaram āha sa eva |

	tathā nityaṃ yateyātāṃ strīpuṃsau ca kṛtakriyau |

	yathā nāticareyātāṃ viyuktāv itaretaram ||

nāticareyātāṃ dharmārthakāmeṣv iti śeṣaḥ | dakṣo 'pi |

	svarge 'pi durlabhaṃ hy etad anurāgaḥ parasparam |

	raktam ekaṃ viraktaṃ vā tataḥ kaṣṭataraṃ nu kim ||

dampatyoḥ parasparam anurāga ity etat svarge 'pi durlabham | tathā tayor ekatarat svarūpam anuraktaṃ viraktaṃ vā syāt tataḥ kaṣṭataraṃ nu kiṃ na kim api, tad eva paramaṃ kaṣṭam ity arthaḥ | tena mitho 'nurāgo yathā bhavati tathā strīpuṃsau yateyātām iti śeṣaḥ | yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	yatrānukūlyaṃ dampatyos trivargas tatra vardhate | iti |

tena mitho 'nukūlatvaṃ yathā bhavati tathā strīpuṃsau yateyātām iti śeṣaḥ | trivargo dharmārthakāmāḥ | tathā ca dakṣaḥ |

	gṛhāśramāt paraṃ nāsti yadi bhāryā vaśānugā |

	tayā dharmārthakāmātmatrivargaphalam aśnute ||

tayā vaśavartinyā dharmārthakāmātmakaṃ trivargākhyaphalam aśnute gṛhīty arthaḥ | vaśānugeti guṇāntarāṇām upalakṣaṇārtham | tathā ca sa eva |

	gṛhe vāsaḥ sukhārtho hi patnīmūlaṃ ca tat sukham |

	sā patnī yā vinītā ca cittajñā vaśavartinī ||

	anukūlā tv avāgduṣṭā dakṣā sādhvī prajāvatī | iti |

patnī yajñādhikārasaṃpadyuktā bhāryā, tadvikalā tu stry eva na patnī | sāpi bhāryā prāguktavinītatvādiguṇānvitety āha sa eva |

	ebhir eva guṇair yuktā bhāryaiva strī na saṃśayaḥ | iti |

ebhir evety evakāro 'tryāyogavyavacchedārtho na punar anyayogavyavacchedārthaḥ, guṇāntarayogasyāpīṣṭatvāt | yā punar nirguṇā sā jarety āha sa eva |

	aduṣṭamānasā nityaṃ sthānamānavicakṣaṇā |

	bhartuḥ priyakarī yā tu sā bhāryā tv itarā jarā ||

itarā guṇarahitā jarā kleśakāriṇīty arthaḥ | patnyādāv eva patnyādiśabdaprayogo vinītatvādiguṇānvitāyām eva samagraṃ patnyādinirvartyakāryaṃ bhavati nānyasyām iti praśaṃsārthaḥ | yathā "paśavo goaśvāḥ" iti śrutau gavāśvapaśuṣv eva paśuśabdaprayogo gośveṣv eva samagraṃ paśunirvartyām kāryam, na punar ajādiṣv iti praśaṃsārthaḥtadvad atrāpīti sarvam anavadyam | suśikṣitā bhāryā tu bāhyābhyantaraśuddhimadbhrātrādisamety āha sa eva |

	śiṣṭā bhāryā śucibhrātṛmitradāsasamā smṛtā |

	yasyaitāni vinītāni tasya lokeṣu gauravam ||

mitradāso 'nukūladāsaḥ | etāni pūrvoktopasarjanāni | vyāsas tu strīdharmaiḥ pūrvoktaguṇaiś ca yuktā strī puṇyakarmaṇaḥ kasyacid eva saṃpadyata ity āha |

	pūrvotthānaparā dakṣā jaghanyāsanaśāyinī |

	avāgduṣṭānukūlā strī bhaved vai puṇyakarmaṇaḥ ||

uktalakṣaṇastrīkasya svargasaṃnibhaṃ sukhaṃ tayā labhyata ity āha dakṣaḥ |

	anukūlakalatrasya svargas tena na saṃśayaḥ | iti |

pratikūlakalatradvayaśālino duḥkhaviśeṣam āha sa eva |

	duḥkhāsikā kalir bhedaś chidrapīḍā parasparam |

	pratikūlakalatrasya dvidvārasya na saṃśayaḥ || iti |

duḥkhāsikā duḥkhena vasanam | kaliḥ kalahaḥ | bhedo vimatiḥ | chidrapīḍā chidrānveṣaṇanibandhanapīḍā | parasparaṃ kalatrayor mitha ity arthaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kathaṃ</span> tarhi pratikūladvikalatrasya kalahādijanyaduḥkhaviśeṣakathanam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span>: mithaḥ kalatrayor utpannaḥ kalahādiḥ tad bhartṛparyantatām āyātīty abhisaṃdhāyoktam, "pratikūlakalatrasya dvidvārasya" iti ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ jāyāpatyor dharmāḥ**

**atha strīdharmāḥ**

tatra manuḥ |

	bālayā vā yuvatyā vā vṛddhayā vāpi yoṣitā |

	na svātantryeṇa kartavyaṃ kāryaṃ kiṃcid gṛheṣv api || \
	bālye pitur vaśe tiṣṭhet pāṇigrāhasya yauvane |

	putrasya bhartari prete na bhajet svatantratām ||

	pitrā bhrātrā sutair vāpi necched viraham ātmanaḥ |

	eṣāṃ hi vraheṇa strī garhye kuryād ubhe kule || iti |

ubhe kule pitṛbhartṛkule | svayaṃ ca garhyā bhavatīti daṇḍāpūpanyāyena gamyate, yā kulasyāpi garhyatām āvahati sā sutarām ātmana iti | uktaṃ ca bṛhaspatinā |

	bhartrā pitrā sutair na strī viyuktānyagṛhe vaset |

	asatsaṅge viśeṣeṇa garhyatām eti sā dhruvam ||

yājñavalkyenāpy uktam |

	pitṛmātṛsutabhrātṛśvaśrūśvaśuramātulaiḥ |

	hīnā na syād vinā bhartrā garhaṇīyānyathā bhavet ||

vyāsas tu veśyāvvad ācaraṇapratiṣedhārtham āha |

	dvāropaveśanaṃ nityaṃ gavākṣāvekṣaṇaṃ tathā |

	asatpralāpo hasyaṃ ca dūṣaṇaṃ kulayoṣitām ||

nityam ity avekṣaṇādāv anuṣajyate | bṛhaspatis tu svairaṇīvad ācaraṇapratiṣedhārtham āha |

	pānāṭanadivāsvāpam akriyā dūṣaṇaṃ striyāḥ | iti |

akriyā akaraṇaṃ nirvyāpāratayā sthānam iti yāvat | śaṅkhalikhitau veśyāvad ācaraṇapratiṣedhārtham āhatuḥ: "strī nānuktvā bahir niṣkrāmen nānutsave gandhamālyābharaṇāni vikṛtāni vāsāṃsi bibhṛyān na parapuruṣam abhibhāṣetānyatra vaṇikpravrajitavṛddhebhyo na nābhiṃ darśayed ā gulphābhyāṃ vāsaḥ paridadhyān na stanau vivṛtau kuryān na hased anapāvṛtaṃ na mahājane" iti | vikṛtānīti purastāt parastāc ca saṃbadhyate | pravrajitaś caturthāśramī | anapāvṛtam asaṃvṛtam, kriyāviśeṣaṇaṃ caitat | mahājanasamīpe tu saṃvṛtasyāpi hasanasya pratiṣedhārthaṃ punar niṣedhaḥ kṛtaḥ | veśyādistrībhiḥ sahaikatrāvasthānapratiṣedho 'pi tābhyāṃ darśitaḥ: "na gaṇikādhūrtācāriṇīmāyāvinīkuhakaśīlāviplutābhiḥ sahaikatas tiṣṭhet | saṃsargeṇa hi cāritraṃ duṣyati" iti | kuhakaśīlā śaṭhasvabhāvā | viplutā jārādibhir naṣṭā | ekataḥsthitiniṣedho 'yaṃ punaḥ punaḥ kriyamāṇaviṣaya iti hetvabhidhānād avagamyate | na hi sakṛd ekatra sthityā kulavadhūnāṃ cāritraṃ duṣyati | evaṃ kāyaśuddhyupahatihetubhūtaparaśayanādisaṃsargaṃ (?) varjayet | tathā ca hārītaḥ: "paraśayanāsanavastrābharaṇāni manasāpi nādhyavasyet ā punaḥsaṃskārāt | tathaikapātre madyamāṃsādīny ucchiṣṭanirmālye cānyatra gurubhartṛsutebhyaḥ" iti | ā punaḥsaṃskārāt ā punarnirṇejanasaṃskārāt | ekapātragrahaṇam anyena saha bhojanopalakṣaṇārtham | madyamāṃsagrahaṇam apeyābhakṣyāṇām upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva surāpyātyarthopahatakāyayā saṃspṛṣṭaṃ duṣṭaṃ bhavatīty āha sa eva |

	daive vā yadi vā pitrye surāpy āyatanaṃ spṛśet |

	rajasvalā puṃścalī vā rakṣasāṃ gacchatīha tat ||
