ata eva madyamāṃsādīnītyādigrahaṇaṃ kṛtam | ucchiṣṭaṃ ca nirmālyaṃ cocchiṣṭanirmālye | guruḥ pitā anyatra gurubhartṛsutebhya iti vadan gurvādīnām ucchiṣṭanirmālyavarjane 'pi na doṣa iti darśayati | apeyādivarjanam avaśyaṃ kāryam, garbhasyāpi doṣahetutvāt | na hi duṣṭakāraṇajanyam aduṣṭaṃ bhavitum arhati | mātrā yat sevitaṃ duṣṭam aduṣṭaṃ vā tad api garbhakāraṇam | tad etad āhatuḥ śaṅkhalikhitau: "surālaśunapalāṇḍugṛñjanakalañjamāṃsādīny abhakṣyāṇi varjayen mātur aśitapītād dhi garbhaḥ saṃbhavati" iti | laśunādīnām avāntarajātibhedaḥ suśrute nirūpitaḥ | tena bhedena trayāṇāṃ grahaṇam arthavat | surā tu striyā viśeṣato varjanīyā, bhartur api doṣāvahatvāt | tathā ca hārītaḥ |

	pataty ardhaṃ śarīrasya yasya bhāryā surāṃ pibet |

	patitārdhaśarīrasya niṣkṛtir na vidhīyate ||

yamo 'pi |

	vāruṇīṃ yasya viprasya bhāryā seveta saṃnidhau |

	sa śūdravad bahiṣkāryaḥ sarvasmād dvijakarmaṇaḥ ||

saṃnidhāv iti vadan saṃsargiṇy eva bhartari bahiṣkāravidhir iti darsayati | tena surāpīparityāgino noktadoṣa ity avagantavyam | yājñavalkyo 'pi surā viśeṣato varjyā brāhmaṇyā iti darśayituṃ tatpānajanyapratyavāyasya phalam āha |

	patilokaṃ na sā yāti brāhmaṇī yā surāṃ pibet |

	ihaiva sā śunī ghṛdhrī sūkarī vopajāyate ||

tena surā prayatnato varjyety abhiprāyaḥ | viṣṇus tu dharmāntarāṇy āha: "atha strīdharmāḥ | kvacit samānavṛttacaritratvaṃ susaṃskṛtopaskaratā amuk tahastatā suguptatā mūlakriyāsv anabhiratir maṅgalācāratatparatā" iti | susaṃskṛtopaskaratā prakṣālanādibhiḥ saṃskṛtapīṭhādigṛhopakaraṇatā | amuktahastatā asadvyayaparāṅmukhatā | mūlakriyā mūlakarma, mantratantrādinā bhartur vaśīkaraṇam iti yāvat ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ strīdharmāḥ**

**atha strīkarmāṇi**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	pūrvotthānaṃ guruṣv arvāk bhojanavyañjanakriyā |

	jaghanyāsanaśāyitvaṃ karma strīṇām udāhṛtam ||

pūrvotthānaṃ bhartur utthānāpekṣayā | evaṃ jaghanyāsanādividhāv api bhartrāsanādyapekṣayā jaghanyatvam | mānyeṣv ādau bhojanapradānādivyāpāraḥ | devalo 'pi: "patiśuśrūṣā sahadharmacaryā tatpūjyamānapūjanaṃ taddveṣyadveṣaṇam" iti | śaṅkhalikhitāv api: "śvaḥpacanabhāṇḍānām upalepanaṃ susaṃmṛṣṭagṛhadvāropalepanaṃ dadhyakṣatadūrvāpravālapuṣpakṛtabalikarma śvaśurayor abhivādanaṃ mahāvaśyakāni kuryāt" iti | śvaḥpacanabhāṇḍānām upalepanaṃ pūrvedyur iti śeṣaḥ | ṛśyaśṛṅgo 'pi:

	gṛhamedhī bhaven nityaṃ bhūṣaṇāni ca bhūṣayet |

	nityaṃ snānakṛtāṃ veṇīm añcayet puṣpamālayā ||

	pūrvam eva raho gacchet yāvan nāryaḥ prabudhyate |

	devatārādhanaṃ kuryāt dhūpapuṣpākṣatādibhiḥ || iti |

gṛhamedhī gṛhadevatāpūjāparā | snānakṛtāṃ snānena saṃskṛtām | raho gacchet rahasi bhartuḥ sakāśāt gacchet | kātyāyano 'pi |

	patyā cāpy aviyoginyā śuśrūṣyo 'gnir vinītayā |

	saubhāgyavad avaidhavyakāmyayā bhartṛbhaktayā ||

agnir gārhapatyādiḥ, aupāsanākhyo vā | saubhāgyavad avaidhavyakāmyayā | saubhāgyopetam avaidhavyaṃ kāmayamānayā anena saubhāgyam avaidhavyaṃ cāgniparicaryāphalam ity uktam | ślokādāv ante ca uktaviśeṣaṇavaśād vinitayā patir api satataṃ śuśrūṣya iti gamyate | na kevalaṃ śuśrūṣyaḥ api tu durdaśāyām apy alaṅghyaḥ patir ity āha manuḥ |

	yasmai dadyāt pitā tv enāṃ bhrātā vānumate pituḥ |

	taṃ śuśrūṣeta jīvantaṃ duḥsthitaṃ ca na laṅghayet || iti |

na ca taṃ dviṣ¥ād iti caśabdārthaḥ | tathā ca śaṅkhalikhitau: "na bhartāraṃ dviṣyād aṣṭīvalaḥ syāt patito 'ṅgahīno vyādhito vā patir hi daivataṃ strīṇām" iti | aṣṭīvalaḥ syāt aṣṭīvalākhyarogī syād ity arthaḥ | patitasya tu pātityāpagamaparyantaṃ bhāryayāsau patiḥ śuśrūṣārthaṃ pratīkṣya ity āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	ā śuddheḥ saṃpratīkṣyo hi mahāpātakadūṣitaḥ | iti |

patitāvasthāyāṃ patiḥ na śuśrūṣya ity ārthiko 'rthaḥ pratyetavyaḥ | duḥśīlādis tu patir naiva dauḥśīlyādyapagamaparyantaṃ pratīkṣyaḥ | yad āha manuḥ |

	viśīlaḥ kāmavṛtto vā guṇair vā parivarjitaḥ |

	upacaryaḥ striyā sādhvyā satataṃ devavat patiḥ ||

kāmavṛttaḥ svacchandacārī | devavad upacaryaḥ devo yathā aihikāmuṣmikasukhasaṃpādakatvād upacaryaḥ tadvat patir apīty arthaḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	anṛtāv ṛtukāle ca mantrasaṃskārakṛt patiḥ |

	sukhaṃ nityaṃ dadātīha paraloke ca yoṣitaḥ ||

mantrasaṃskārakṛt mantrāpādyasaṃskārakṛt, vivāhādisaṃskārakṛd iti yāvat | yājñavalkyas tu patiśuśrūṣaṇātmakadharmānurodhenaiva anyo dharmaḥ kārya iti pratipādanārtham āha |

	strībhiḥ bhartṛvacaḥ kāryam eṣa dharmaḥ paraḥ striyāḥ | iti |

paraḥ utkṛṣṭa ity arthaḥ | evaṃ cotkṛṣṭānurodhenāpakṛṣṭānuṣṭhānam ity arthāt pratipāditam | manur apy arthād etad eva vaktum āha |

	nāsti strīṇāṃ pṛthagyajñaḥ na vrataṃ nāpy upoṣaṇam |

	patiḥ śuśrūṣyate yena tena svarge mahīyate ||

śaṅkho 'pi |

	na vratenopavāsena dharmeṇa vividhena ca |

	nārī svargam avāpnoti prāpnoti patipūjanāt ||

viṣṇus tu patiśuśrūṣaṇam akṛtvā upavāsavrataṃ na kāryam iti pratipādayitum āha |

	patyau jīvati yā yoṣit upavāsavrataṃ caret |

	āyur harati sā bhartuḥ narakaṃ caiva gacchati || iti |

yat tu śaṅkhalikhitābhyām uktam: "bhartur anujñayā vratopavāsaniyamejyādīnām ārambhaḥ strīdharmaḥ" iti, tat patiśuśrūṣaṇānupamardena saṃpāditavratādiviṣayam | yat tu paiṭhīnasinoktam: "striyo gṛhadevatās tāsāṃ nāśaucaṃ na vrataṃ nopavāsaḥ patiśuśrūṣayaiva gacchanti paramāṃ gatim" iti, tat patiśuśrūṣāyāḥ prāśastyamātraparaṃ na punaḥ śaucādinivāraṇaparam iti mantavyam | evaṃ kurvantyāḥ phalam āha manuḥ |

	anena nārī vṛttena manovāgdehasaṃyatā |

	ihāgryāṃ kīrtim āpnoti patilokaṃ paratra ca ||

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	patipriyahite yuktā svācārā vijitendriyā |

	iha kīrtim avāpnoti pretya cānuttamāṃ gatim || iti |

kātyāyano 'pi |

	patiśuśrūṣayaiva strī sarvān kāmān samaśnute |

	divaḥ punar ihāyātā sukhānāṃ śevadhir bhavet ||

divaḥ sakāśāt punar ihāgatā sukhānāṃ nidhir bhaved ity arthaḥ | pṛthivīṃ prati lakṣmīvākyam api |

	nārīṣu nityaṃ suvibhūṣitāsu pativratāsu priyavādinīṣu |

	amuktahastāsu śubhānvitāsu suguptabhāṇḍāsu balipriyāsu ||

	saṃmṛṣṭagehāsu jitendiryāsu kalivyapetāsu vilolupāsu |

	dharmavyapekṣāsu dayānvitāsu sthitā sadāhaṃ muitāsu dhātri || iti |

kalivyapetāsu kalaharahitāsu | hārītas tu apativratāyā doṣam āha |

	asādhvī yā patiṃ tyaktvā vartate kāmakārataḥ |

	na sā sukham avāpnoti kalpate narakāya ca ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ strīkarmāṇi**

**atha proṣitabhartṛkāyāḥ striyā dharmāḥ**

tatra manuḥ:

	vidhāya proṣite vṛttiṃ jīven niyamam āsthitā |

	proṣite tv avidhāyaiva jīvec chilpair agarhitaiḥ ||

jīvanārthaṃ vyayaṃ parikalpya proṣite bhartari tadbhāryā vakṣyamāṇaniyamasthā punar āgamanaparyantaṃ parikalpitaṃ vyayārthaṃ dravyam upajīvet | tatkṣaye tadakalpane vā kartanādiśilpaiḥ paragṛhapraveśanaduḥsaṅgatyādihetutvādirāhityenāgarhitair jīved ity arthaḥ | ke punar vakṣyamāṇā niyamā ity apekṣite viṣṇuḥ: "bhartari proṣite pratikarmākriyā paragṛheṣv anabhigamanaṃ dvāradeśagavākṣeṣv anavasthānam" iti | pratikarmākriyā alaṅkṛter akaraṇam | tathā ca hārītaḥ: "na proṣite 'laṃkuryān na veṇīṃ muñcet" iti | śaṅkhalikhitāv api niyamān āhatuḥ: "preṅkhātāṇḍavavihāracitradarśanāṅgarātodyānayānavivṛaśayotkṛṣṭapānabhojana-kantukakrīḍādhūpagandhamālyālaṃkāradantadhāvanāñjanādarśanaprasādhanādīnām asvatantrāṇāṃ proṣitabhartṛkāṇāṃ kulastrīṇām anārambhaḥ" iti | preṅkhā ḍolāvihāro rathyādau, na punar gṛhe 'pi | vivṛtaśayanaṃ niṣprāvaraṇatayā śayanam | preṅkhādiprasādhanāntānām anārambho 'svatantrāṇāṃ proṣitabhartṛkāṇāṃ kulastrīṇām ity anvayaḥ | prasādhanādīnām ityādigrahaṇalabdhān āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	prasādhanaṃ nṛttagītasamājotsavadarśanam |

	māṃsamdhābhiyogaṃ ca na kuryāt proṣite prabau ||

proṣitabhartṛkāṇāṃ duṣprasaṅgebhyo rakṣakajane vyavasthām āhatuḥ śaṅkhalikhitau: "sarvāsāṃ proṣite bhartari brāhmaṇī cāritraṃ rakṣet | itarāsāṃ mātāpitarau anantaro vā rājanyo vā" iti | sarvāsāṃ kṣatriyādistrīṇām | itarāsāṃ viprāstrīṇām | anantaraḥ pratyāsannabandhuḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ proṣitabhartṛkāyāḥ striyo dharmāḥ**

**atha mṛtabhartṛkā striyā dharmāḥ**

tatrāhitāgner bhāryāṃ praty āha hārītaḥ: "āhitāgniś cet pramīyeta aupāsanāvakṣāṇāgniṃ parigṛhya sarparājñībhir anusavanam indhānā vaset" iti | ardhādhānapakṣe mṛtasyāhitāgnes tretāgninā dahanam | aupāsanāgnis tu patyartham indhane dhriyate | ulmukāvasthendhanāny avakṣāṇāny ucyate | evaṃ cāyam arthaḥ: ulmukāvastham aupāsanāgniṃ parigṛhya "bhūmir bhūmnā" iti catasṛbhir anusavanam indhānā śvaśurādigṛhe vased iti | evam evānāhitāgner mṛtasya bhāryā vaset | iyaṃs tu viśeṣaḥ: aupāsanāgneḥ svagṛhyoktavidhinā punaḥ saṃdhānaṃ laukikāgner vā parigrahaṃ kuryāt | tathā ca sa eva: "anāhitāgniś ced anyam ādadhyāj janāgniṃ vā parigṛhya" iti | anāhitāgniś cet pramīyītety anuṣajyate | parigṛhya pūrvavat samindhnam ācared iti śeṣaḥ | anāhitāgner dahanakarmaṇi pūrvasthitasyaupāsanasya pratipattir jāteti punar utpattyartham anyam ādadhyād ity uktam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kathaṃ</span> punaḥ sarvādhānapakṣe mṛtabhartṛkāyā agniparicaryā, na cānāhitāgner bhāryāyām uktam atrāpy ūhyam, vacanabalenaiva mṛtabhartṛkāyā alaukikāgniniṣpatteḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span>: nirmathitāgniṃ parigṛhya pūrvavat samindhanam ācaret | "nirmanthyena patnīm" ity āpastambenaitasmin pakṣe nirmanthyena patnyāḥ pitṛmedhavidhānāt | evaṃ strīviśeṣe 'gniviśeṣasamindhanam uktvā sarvapramītabhartṛkāyāḥ sādhāraṇadharmam apy āha sa eva: "bhartuḥ pituḥ svajanasya vā gṛham āśritya saṃyatajihvāhastapādendriyā svācāravatī divārātraṃ bhartāram anuśocantī vratopavāsaiḥ kṛśātmā āyuṣo 'nte patilokaṃ jayati na bhūyaḥ pativiyogam āpnoti" iti | smṛtyantare 'pi phalam uktam |

	pativratā tu yā nārī niṣṭhāṃ yāti prabhau mṛte |

	sā hitvā sarvapāpāni patilokam āpnuyāt ||

bṛhaspatināpy uktam |

	vratopavāsaniratā brahmacarye vyavasthitā |

	dharmadānaparā nityam aputrāpi divaṃ vrajet ||

yat tu śrutāv uktam: nāputrasya loko 'sti" iti, tat yaḥ putrotpattau dharmyamārgeṇādhikāre jāte 'pi kiṃ putreṇety anāsthayā putrotpattiṃ na karoti tadviṣayam | ayam eva viṣayo 'syāḥ śruteḥ iti darśayituṃ manunā dṛṣṭānto 'pi darśitaḥ |

	anekāni sahasrāṇi kaumārabrahmacāriṇām |

	divaṃ gatāni viprāṇām akṛtvā kulasaṃtatim ||

	mṛte bhartari sādhvī strī brahmacarye vyavasthitā |

	svargaṃ gacchaty aputrāpi yathā te brahmacāriṇaḥ || iti |

putrapautrādisaṃtatim akṛtvā kaumārabrahmacāriṇāṃ viprāṇām anekāni sahasrāṇi svargaṃ gatānīty ādyaśokānvayaḥ | yā tu putrotpattyarthaṃ brahmacarye 'avasthitiṃ na karoti, tasyāḥ doṣam āha sa eva |

	apatyalobhād yā tu strī bhartāram ativartate |

	seha nindām avāpnoti patilokāc ca hīyate ||

yat tu yamenoktam,

	striyāḥ śrutau vā śāstre vā pravrajyā na vidhīyate |

	prajā hi tasyāḥ svo dharmaḥ savarṇād iti dhāraṇā || 

iti — śāstre dharmaśāstre, pravrajyā brahmacaryam ity arthaḥ, yady api striyā braahmacaryaṃ śrutyādau vihitaṃ tathāpi savarṇataḥ putraprāptilakṣaṇadharmapraśaṃsārthaṃ brahmacaryavidhir avidyamānaprāya iti nindānena kriyata ity avirodhaḥ — tad etat kaliyugād yugāntaradharmatvenoktam iti mantavyam | tathā ca saṃskārakāṇḍe vidhavāyā niyojanaprakaraṇe pratipāditam asmābhiḥ | tena kaliyuge brahmacarye vyavastitatvam eva dharmaḥ | yugāntare tu yamokto 'pi dharmo bhavatīty avagantavyam | tatrāpi brahmacarye vyavasthānam uttamo dharmo brahmalokaprāptikaratvāt | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	mṛte bhartari yā sādhvī brahmacarye vyavasthitā |

	sārundhatīsamācārā brahmaloke mahīyate ||

yat tu viṣṇunā dharmāntaram uktam: "mṛte bhartari brahmacaryaṃ tadanvārohaṇaṃ vā" iti — tadanvārohaṇaṃ bhartāram anu āhrohaṇam, agnyārohaṇam; tathā ca aṅgirāḥ:

	mṛte bhartari yā nārī samārohed dhutāśanam |

	sārundhatīsamācārā svargaloke mahīyate ||

— tad etad dharmāntaram api brahmacaryadharmāt jaghanyam, niṛṣṭaphalatvāt ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ mṛtabhartṛkā dharmāḥ**

**atha dāyavibhāgākhyasya padasya vidhir ucyate**

tatra manuḥ |

	eṣa strīpuṃsayor ukto dharmo vo ratisaṃhitaḥ |

	āpady apatyaprāptiś ca dāyadharmaṃ nibodhata ||

dāyākhyadravyaviṣayadharmaṃ mayocyamānaṃ yūyaṃ nibodhatety arthaḥ | kiṃ punar dāyākhyadravyam ity apekṣite nighaṇṭukāreṇoktam |

	vibhaktavyaṃ pitur dravyaṃ dāyam āhur manīṣiṇaḥ | iti |

vibhāgārhapitrādidvārāgate dravye vṛddhā dāyaśabdam āhur ity arthaḥ | ata eva dhāreśvareṇaivam evoktam: "dāyaśabdena pitṛdvārā mātṛdvārāgataṃ ca dravyam evocyate" iti | caśabdaḥ saṃbandhyantaradvārāgatadravyam api dāyaśabdenocyata iti sūcanārthaḥ | evaśabdas tv anāpannasvatvarūpam iti jñāpanārthaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">sa ca ayuktaḥ</span>, āpannasvatvarūpasyaiva dravyasya pitṛdvārā putrapautreṣv āgamanāt | evaṃ cānyasaṃbandhini dhane vibhāgārhadāyaśabdo vartata iti nighaṇṭukāreṇoktam iti mantavyam | dāyaviṣayadharmaś cātra vibhāgalakṣaṇo 'bhipretaḥ "strīpuṃdharmo vibhāgaś ca" iti padoddeśāvasare tasyaiva pūrvam uktatvāt | ata eva saṃgrahakāraḥ |

	pitṛdvārāgataṃ dravyaṃ mātṛdvārāgataṃ ca yat |

	kathitaṃ dāyaśabdena tadvibhāgo 'dhunocyate ||

pitṛdvārāgatam iti yad dravyaṃ dāyaśabdena dāyadharmam iti samāsāntargatena kathitaṃ tasya vibhāgo 'dhunā strīpuṃdharmākhyapadapratipādyajātasya sarvasya pratipādanānantaraṃ manunocyata iti saṃgrahaśokasyārthaḥ | katham ucyata ity apekṣite manuḥ |

	ūrdhvaṃ pituś ca mātuś ca sametya bhrātaraḥ samam |

	bhajeran paitṛkaṃ riktham anīśās te hi jīvatoḥ ||

asyāpi tātparyam āha saṃgrahakāraḥ |

	yasmin kāle yayā bhaṅgyā yair eva kriyate 'pi ca |

	yādṛśasya ca dāyasya yathāśāstraṃ pradarśyate ||

asyārthaḥ: yādṛśasya dāyasya paitṛkamātṛkāder yasmin kāle yayā samaviṣamādibhaṅgyā prakāreṇa yaiḥ pitṛmātṛbhaginyādibhiḥ kartṛbhir vibhāgaḥ kartavyaḥ tad etat sarvaṃ vṛddhamanvādiśāstrānatikrameṇa "ūradhvaṃ pituś ca" ityādinā pradarśyata iti | "ūrdhvaṃ pituś ca" iti pitṛdhanavibhāgakāla uktaḥ | "mātuś ca" iti mātṛdhanavibhāgakālaḥ | tena mātari jīvantyām api pitṛdhanavibhāgaḥ kāryaḥ | tathā mātur ūrdhvaṃ pitari jīvaty api mātṛdhanavibhāgaḥ kārya eva | anyataradhanavibhāge ubhayor ūrdhvakālapratīkṣaṇānupayogāt | tathā ca saṃgrahakāraḥ |

	pitṛdravyavibhāgaḥ syāj jīvantyām api mātari |

	na svatantratayā svāmyaṃ yasmān mātuḥ patiṃ vinā ||

	mātṛdravyavibhāgo 'pi tathā pitari jīvati |

	satsv apatyeṣu yasmān na strīdhanasya patiḥ patiḥ || iti |

bhāryāyāḥ patiṃ vinā patimaraṇe 'pi yasmāt patyur dhane svatantratvena na svāmitvam, yasmāc cāpatyeṣu vidyamāneṣu strīdhanasya bhāryādhanasya bhāryāmaraṇe 'pi patiḥ bhartā na patiḥ na svāmī | tasmāt tayor madhye jīvaty apy anyatarasmin anyataradhanavibhāgo yukta ity arthaḥ | anena pitari jīvati taddravyavibhāgo mātari ca jīvantyāṃ taddravyavibhāgaḥ putrādair na kārya ity arthād uktam | uktaṃ cāntyapādena mānave: "anīśās te jīvatoḥ" iti | anīśāḥ asvatantrāḥ | tathā ca śaṅkhalikhitau: "na jīvati pitari putrā rikthaṃ bhajeran yady api syāt paścād adhigataṃ tair anarhā eva putrā arthadharmayor asvātantryāt" iti | yady api taiḥ svakīyajanmanaḥ paścād anantaram eva pitṛdhane svāmyam adhigataṃ prāptaṃ tathāpi jīvati pitari pitṛdhanaṃ na vibhajeran | yato 'rthadharmayor asvātantryāt vibhāgaṃ kartum anarhāḥ putrā ity arthaḥ | arthāsvātantryaṃ arthādānapradānayor asvātantryam, tathā ca hārītaḥ: "jīvati pitari putrāṇām arthadānavisargākṣepeṣv asvātantryam" iti | arthadānaṃ arthopabhogaḥ | visargo vyayaḥ | ākṣepaḥ dāsādiparijanasyāparādheṣu śikṣārtham ākṣepaḥ | asvātantryaṃ pitur anujñām antareṇa svecchayārthādānādāv apravṛttiḥ | dharmāsvātantryam api evaṃ pṛthag iṣṭāpūrtādāv apravṛttiḥ | dharmāsvātantryam api evaṃ pṛthag iṣṭāpūrtādāv apravṛttiḥ | evaṃ ca pitrānujñātena putreṇa svakarmāgnihotrādi kāryaṃ nānanujāteneti mantavyam | yat tu devalenoktam,

	pitary uparate putrā vibhajeran pitur dhanam |

	asvāmyaṃ hi bhaved eṣāṃ nirdoṣe pitari sthite ||

iti, tatrāsvāmyavacanam asvātantryapratipādanārtham iti mantavyam | nirdoṣe pitari sthite 'pi pitṛdhane putrāṇāṃ janmanā svāmyasya lokasiddhatvāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanv</span> alokikaṃ svāmyaṃ na putrāṇāṃ lokasiddham iti vṛdhaiva (?) "asvāmyaṃ hi bhavet" iti vacanasvārasyabhaṅgaḥ kriyate | na ca vācyaṃ pratijñāmātram alaukikaṃ svāmyam iti, yato nyāyam āha saṃgrahakāraḥ |

	vartate yasya yad dhaste tasya svāmi sa eva na |

	anyasvam anyahasteṣu cauryād yaiḥ kiṃ na vartate ||

	tasmāc chāstrata eva syāt svāmyaṃ nānubhavād api || iti |

yasmād yasyāntike yad dhanaṃ vartamānaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tasya sa eva svāmīty avadhārayituṃ na śakyate | parakīyasyāpi cauryādinānyāntikasthasya darśane tasyaiva svāmitvāpatteḥ | tasmāc chāstraikasamadhigamyaṃ svāmyaṃ na punar mānāntaragamyam apīty arthaḥ | kiṃ ca yadi yad yasyāntike dṛṣṭaṃ tasya sa eva svāmī tarhy asya svam etenāpahṛtam iti na brūyāt, yadyaivāntike dṛṣṭaṃ tasyaiva svāmitvāt | api ca pramāṇāntaragamye svāmye "brāhmaṇasyādhikaṃ labdham, kṣatriyasya vijitam, nirviṣṭaṃ vaiśyaśūdrayoḥ" iti gautamapraṇīte dharmaśāstre yathākramaṃ varṇānatikrameṇa pṛthak pṛthag vibhinnaprakāreṇa vihito 'rthāgamo vyarthaḥ syāt, mānāntarasyaiva niyāmakatvāt, etad bādhakaṃ cāha sa eva |

	asyāpahṛtam etena na yuktaṃ vaktum anyathā |

	vihito 'rthāgamaḥ śāstre yathāvarṇaṃ pṛthak pṛthak ||

	pratigrahāstravāṇijyaśuśrūṣādyair yathākramam || iti |

"asya" ityādinā "vaktum" ityantenātra prathamaṃ bādhakam uktam, avaśiṣṭena vyarthaḥ syād ity adhyāhārasāpekṣeṇa dvitīyam iti mantavyam | evaṃ ca svatvam api svāmyavad eva śāstraikasamadhigamyaṃ vijñeyam | yasmāt svāmyatvatvayos tulyayogakṣemayor ekataram adhikṛtya sādhite 'pi śāstraikasamadhigamyatve dvayor eva sādhitaṃ bhavati | ata eva saṃprati svatvam adhikṛtyāpi śāstraikasamadhigamyatvaṃ dvayoḥ sādhayitum āha sa eva |

	na ca svam ucyate tadvat svecchayā viniyujyate |

	viniyogo 'pi sarvasya śāstreṇaiva niyamyate ||

asyāyam arthaḥ: na ca na brūmo 'ntike vartamanatayā paridṛṣṭaṃ svam iti, kiṃ tu yad vastu yena yatheṣṭaṃ viniyujyate tat tasya svam ity ucyate | tataś ca nātiprasaṅgādidūṣaṇam, apahṛtāder ayatheṣṭaviniyojyasya svavyavahārāprasaṅgād iti vācyam, yataḥ sarvasya svavyavahārāviṣayasyāpi dhanasya viniyogaḥ śāstreṇaiva gurubhṛtyādeḥ bharaṇādau niyamyata iti yatheṣṭaviniyojyaṃ kim api nāstīti | prapañcitaṃ caitat sarvaṃ dhāreśvarasūriṇā | tasmāt

	asvāmyaṃ hi bhaved eṣāṃ nirdoṣe pitari sthite | 

iti dharmaśāstrād asvāmye siddhe "yady api syāt paścād adhigataṃ taiḥ" iti śaṅkhavanasyaivānyathā vyākhyā nyāyyā |

	atrocyate: na brūmo yatheṣṭaṃ viniyojyaṃ svam iti, kiṃ tu yatheṣṭaviniyogārhaṃ svam iti brūmahe | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> śāstreṇa gurubhṛyāder bharaṇādau viniyoganiyamāt yathā yatheṣṭaviniyojyaṃ durnirūpaṃ tathā yatheṣṭaviniyogārhatvam api yatheṣṭaviniyogābhāvād eva durnirūpam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>, yatheṣṭaviniyogābhāve 'pi yad yenārjitaṃ tat tasya yatheṣṭaviniyogārham ity evaṃ nirūpyate | tathā ca nayaviveke bhavanāthenaivaṃ nirūpitam "tac ca tasya tad arhaṃ yad yenārjitam" iti granthena | tasyāyam arthaḥ: yad vastu yena puruṣeṇārjitaṃ tad vastu tasya puruṣasya tadarhaṃ yatheṣṭaviniyogārham iti | svatvanirūpaṇavad yatheṣṭaviniyogārhatvanirūpaṇaṃ cāsmin mate suśakam iti caśabdarthaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanv</span> evaṃ corasya cauryārjitaṃ yatheṣṭaviniyogārhaṃ syāt ity āśaṅkyāha sa eva: "lokasiddhaṃ cārjanaṃ janmādi" iti | janmakrayasaṃvibhāgaparigrahādhigamādy evānidaṃprathamalokasiddhaṃ (?) dhanārjanaṃ na punaś cauryādikam ity arthaḥ | atiprasaṅgapariharaṇam api suśakam iti caśabdārthaḥ |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanv</span> idam ārjanam anidaṃprathamalokasiddham idaṃ nety atra kiṃ niyāmakam ity āśaṅkyāha sa eva: "ata evānidaṃprathamalokadhīviṣayavyavasthitanibandhanārthā smṛtiḥ vyākaraṇādismṛtivat" iti | yata evānidaṃprathamalokasiddhārjanam eva svatvāpādakaṃ tataś ca tad eva laukikavaidikavyavahārasiddhyartham avaśyaṃ jñeyam | ata evānidaṃprathamalokadhīviṣayatayā vyavasthitārjanānāṃ svagranthe nibandhanārtha "svāmī rikthakrayasaṃvibhāgaparigrahādhigameṣu brāhmaṇasyādhikaṃ labdhaṃ kṣatriyasya vijitaṃ nirviṣṭaṃ vaiśyaśūdrayoḥ" ityādikā gautamādipraṇītā dharmasmṛtiḥ sādhuśabdanibandhanārthavyākaraṇādismṛtivat kṛtety arthaḥ | rikthaṃ rikthārjanaṃ pitrādidhane svāmitvāpādakaṃ gautamenaiva: "utpattyaivārthasvāmitvaṃ labhetety ācāryaḥ" iti | utpattyaiva mātur garbhe śarīrotpattyaivety arthaḥ | saṃvibhāgaḥ pitrādidhane viśeṣaniṣṭhasvāmitvasaṃpādako vibhāgaḥ | parigrahaḥ kānanādigatajalatṛṇakāṣṭāder anyenāsvīkṛtasya svīkāraḥ | adhigamo nidhyāder upalabdhiḥ | eteṣu nimitteṣu satsu putrādiḥ kretā saṃvibhaktā parigrahītādhigantā ca yathākrameṇa pitrādidhanasya krītasya saṃvibhakāṃśasya parigṛhītasyādhigatasya ca svāmī bhavati |

	tathā ca labdhaṃ parigṛhītaṃ brāhmaṇasyādhikaṃ prātisvikam ārjitam, evaṃ kṣatriyasa vijitaṃ vijayalabdham, evaṃ vaiśyasya nirviṣṭaṃ kṛṣṭādau bhṛtirūpeṇa labdham, śūdrasyāpi nirviṣṭaṃ dvijaśuśrūṣādau bhṛtirūpeṇa labdham, prātisvikam ārjitam ity evam ārjananibandhanārthāyā gautamasmṛter artho vijñeyaḥ | evaṃ ca yat saṃgrahakāreṇoktam: "vartate yasya yaddhaste" ityādinā, yac ca dhāreśvarasūriṇā prapañcitam, tat sarvam apāstaṃ veditavyam | tataś ca,

	asvāmyaṃ hi bhaved eṣāṃ nirdoṣe pitari sthite |

iti vacanānāñjasyena śaṅkhavacanavirodhaparihāro yukta evety alam atibahunā |

	prakṛtam ucyate: nirdoṣagrahaṇāt pitari sthite 'pi doṣe sati na putrāṇāṃ tatpāratantryam iti darśayati | yena pitari sthite 'py akṣamatvādidoṣe sati arthādānavisargādau jyeṣṭhasya svātantryam, anujānāṃ tu jyeṣṭhādhīnatvam avagantavyam | ata eva śaṅkhalikhitābhyām uktam: "pitary aśakte kuṭumbasya vyavahārān jyeṣṭhaḥ prakuryād anantaro vā kāryajñas tadanumatena" iti | tadanumatena jyeṣṭhānumatena, tadānīṃ tasyaiva svātantryāt | tadanantragrahaṇam anujopalakṣaṇārtham, kāryajñasyaivātra vivakṣitatvāt | aśaktagrahaṇaṃ ca dīnāder upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva hārītaḥ: "kāmaṃ dīne proṣite ārtiṃ gate vā jyeṣṭho 'rthāṃś cintayet" iti | dīne ityādau jīvati pitarīti padadvayam anuṣajyate | tasya pūrvavākye śravaṇād ihākāṅkṣitatvāc ca | kāmam iti vadan pitṛparatantratvaṃ tadānīṃ gatam iti darśayati | gate ca pitṛparatantratve purāṇāṃ pitṛdhanavibhāgakartṛtvārhatā jāteti pitṛdhanavibhāgo 'pi tadānīṃ putrāṇām evecchayā bhavitum arhati | ata eva śaṅkhalikhitau: "akāme pitari rikthavibhāgo vṛddhe viparītacetasi dīrgharogiṇi ca" iti | akāme pitari vibhāgecchāśūnye pitarīty arthaḥ | vṛddhe ativṛddhe | viparītacetasi aprakṛtisthe | etad uktaṃ bhavati: vārdhakādinā pitary asvatantratvam āpanne tadanicchyāpi taddhanavibhāgaḥ putrāṇām icchayaiva bhavatīti | dīrgharogigrahaṇaṃ dīrghakopāder apy upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	vyādhitaḥ kuptaś caiva viṣayāsaktamānasaḥ |

	anyathāśāstrakārī ca na vibhāge pitā prabhuḥ ||

api tu tatputra eva prabhavati iti śeṣaḥ | anyathāśāstrakārī smṛtyācāravyapetamārgavartī | nirdoṣe pitari sthite 'pi kvacid viṣaye putrakartṛkam eva vibhāgam āha sa eva |

	ata ūrdhvaṃ pituḥ putrā vibhajeran dhanaṃ samam |

	mātur nivṛtte rajasi prattāsu bhaginīṣu ca |

	nivṛtte cāpi ramaṇe pitary uparataspṛhe || iti |

ata ūrdhvam ityādi samamityantam ādyaṃ vākyaṃ jīvadvibhāgakālabodhakam, tathāpy uttaravākyapūraṇopayogārthaṃ paṭhitam | pitror apatyotpattisāmagryabhāvaniścaye stryapatyavivāhe ca kṛte pitur dhanaspṛhāyāṃ ca gatāyāṃ taddhanaṃ putrā eva vibhajerann iti dvitīyavākyasyārthaḥ | bodhāyanas tv atra pitur api kartṛtvam anumatidvāreṇāha: "pitur anumatyā dāyavibhāgaḥ" iti | kva tarhi pitṛkartṛko vibhāga ity apekṣite nāradaḥ |

	pitaiva vā svayaṃ putrān vibhajed vayasi sthitaḥ | iti |

vayasi sthita iti vadann apratihatasvātantryayuktapitṛviṣaya evāyaṃ niyama iti darśayati | evakāreṇa pitṛkartṛkaniyamalābhe 'pi svayaṃgrahaṇād asmin viṣaye putrāṇām anumatikartṛtvam api nirastam | vāśabdaḥ sahavāsena vikalpārthaḥ, na punaḥ pitrādikartrantareṇa, sahavāsasyaivātra pakṣāntaratvāt | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

	bhrātṝṇāṃ jīvatoḥ pitroḥ sahavaso vidhīyate | iti |

pitur ūrdhvam api bhrātṝṇām anyonyam arthopacayārthaṃ sahavāso 'sty eva | tathā ca śaṅkhalikhitau: "kāmaṃ sahavaseyur ekataḥ saṃhatā vṛddhim āpadyeran" iti | pṛthak pṛthak vyayābhāvad iti bhāvaḥ | vibhāge tu dharmavṛddhim āpadyerann ity āha gautamaḥ: "vibhāge tu dharmavṛddhiḥ" iti | katham ity apekṣite nāradaḥ |

	bhrātṝṇām avibhaktānām eko dharmaḥ pravartate |

	vibhāge sati dharmo 'pi bhavet teṣāṃ pṛthak pṛthak ||

dharmaḥ pitṛdevadvijārcanajanyaḥ | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	ekapākena vasatāṃ pitṛdevadvijārcanam |

	ekaṃ bhaved vibhaktānāṃ tad eva syād gṛhe gṛhe ||

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanv</span> agnihotrādijanyo 'pi dharmo vibhaktānāṃ vardhate nāvibhaktānāṃ svatvābhāvenāvibhaktānāṃ svasyāgnihotrādijanyadharmārjanāsaṃbhavāt | tenāgnihotrādiharmo vibhāgapakṣotkṛṣṭatve hetutayā vaktavyaḥ | uktaṃ ca tathaiva saṃgrahakāreṇa |

	kriyate svaṃ vibhāgena putrāṇāṃ paitṛkaṃ dhanam |

	svatve sati pravartante tasmād dharmyā pṛthakkriyā ||

pravartante svasādhyāgnihotrādīnīti śeṣaḥ | atrocyate: paitṛkadhanavibhāgena putrāṇāṃ svaṃ kriyata ity etad ayuktam, janmanaiva svaṃ kriyata iti prāg eva pratipāditatvāt | tataś cāvibhaktānām api svatvam astīti svasādhyāgnihotrādijanyo dharmaḥ saṃpadyata eveti na kaścid vibhāgapakṣasyāvibhāgapakṣād viśeṣa iti pūrvoktaprakāreṇaiva vibhāgapakṣe dharmavṛddhiḥ gautamādibhir ukteti dik ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ vibhāgakālakartṛpradarśanam**

**atha jīvadvibhāgaprakāraḥ**

tatra śaṅkhalikhitau: "jīvati pitari rikthavibhāgo 'numataḥ prakāśaṃ vā mitho vā dharmataḥ" iti | yo jīvadvibhāgapakṣo 'numataḥ sa tāvat prakāśaṃ bandhvādijanasamakṣaṃ yathā bhavati tathā mitho vā rahasi vā dharmato dharmānapetena prakāreṇa kārya ity arthaḥ | tam evaṃ prakāram āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	sakalaṃ dravyajātaṃ yad bhāgaiḥ gṛhṇanti tatsasamaiḥ |

	pitaro bhrātaraś caiva vibhāgo dharmya ucyate ||

yan madhyagaṃ dravyajātaṃ tat sarvaṃ pitrādayo yatra vibhāgaiḥ samair eva bhāgair gṛhṇanti sa vibhāgaḥ śāstrāvagatatvāt dharmād anapeta ity ucyata ity arthaḥ | jyeṣṭhabhrātṛbhāgādhikyena vidhāntarato dharmyaṃ vibhāgaṃ vaktuṃ bodhāyanenoktam: "manuḥ putrebhyo dāyaṃ vyabhajat, iti samo 'ṃśaḥ sarveṣām aviśeṣāt" iti | manuḥ putrebhyo dāyaṃ vyabhajad iti jīvadvibhāgābdhidāyake brāhmaṇe viśeṣānabhidhānāt "samaṃ syād aśrutatvāt" iti nyāyabalād asmād eva śāstrāt sarveṣāṃ pitṛputrāṇāṃ sama evāṃśo 'vagamyata ity arthaḥ | jyeṣṭhasya tv ādhikyaṃ śrutyantarasiddham ity āha sa eva: "dhanam ekaṃ cāru samuddharej jyeṣṭhas tasmāj jyeṣṭhaṃ putraṃ dhanena niravasāyayanti" iti śrutiḥ | dhanam ekam iti vadan dhanenety ekavacanaṃ śrutivākyagataṃ vivakṣitam iti darśayati | niravasāyayanti toṣayantīty arthaḥ | tathā ca āpastambaḥ: "ekadhanena jyaeṣṭhaṃ toṣayitvā jīvan putrebhyo dāyaṃ vibhajet samam" iti | jīvan pitā śreṣṭhenaikadhanena madhyakadravyād uddhṛtena jyeṣṭhaṃ prathamaputraṃ toṣayitvāvaśiṣṭam ātmasahitajyeṣṭhādiputrebhyaḥ samatvenaiva vibhajed ity arthaḥ | evaṃ ca prathamotpannatayā tadartham evodhāraḥ | sa caikasyaiva sarvadhanaśreṣṭhasya, uddhṛtāvaśiṣṭasya samatvenaiva vibhāga iti vidhāntaram uktam ity avagantavyam | evaṃ kātyāyanabodhāyanoktapakṣayor madhye yaṃ pakṣaṃ pitā kartum icchati tam eva pakṣaṃ kuryāt | pitṛkartṛke vibhāge tasyaiva prabhutvena tadicchāyā eva pakṣaviśeṣaparigrahakāraṇatvāt | tad etat sarvaṃ saṃkṣipya yājñavalkyenoktam |

	vibhāgaṃ cet pitā kuryād icchayā vibhajet sutān |

	jyeṣṭhaṃ vā śreṣṭhabhāgena sarve vā syuḥ samāṃśinaḥ ||

atrottarārdhena prāṅnirūpitapakṣadvayaṃ pūrvoktakramavyatyāsenoktam | tayor anyatarapakṣaparigrahe pitur icchaiva kāraṇaṃ na punaḥ putrāṇām apīcchā kāraṇam iti pūrvārdhenoktam iti mantavyam | evaṃ cātmecchayā yaḥ pakṣaḥ pitrā parigṛhītaḥ sa sutair anapekṣito 'pi anumantavyaḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	nyūnādhikavibhaktānāṃ dharmyaḥ pitṛkṛtaḥ smṛtaḥ | iti |

nyūnatayā vibhaktānāṃ jyeṣṭhetareṣāṃ śreṣṭhabhāgābhāvena tatsadbhāvāt, adhikatayā vibhakto jyeṣṭhas teṣāṃ pitur icchayā svīkṛto yady uddhārapūrvako vibhāgaḥ tadā so 'pi śāstramūlatvena dharmyatayā prāk smṛta iti tair apy anumantavya ity arthaḥ | nārado 'py amum evārtham āha |

	pitraiva tu vibhaktā ye samanyūnādhikair dhanaiḥ 

	teṣāṃ sa eva dharmyaḥ syāt sarvasya hi pitā prabhuḥ ||

samadhanaiḥ kṛto yo dhanavibhāgaprakāras tatra pitrā mahyam ekam adhikaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ dhanaṃ na dattam iti jyeṣṭhenanuśayo na kāryaḥ | tathā yaḥ pitrā kṛto nyūnādhikadhanair vibhāgas tatra pitrāsmabhyaṃ nyūnaṃ dattaṃ jyeṣṭhāyādhikam iti anujair anuśayo na kāryaḥ, pitur icchayā prāptasyaiva atra dharmyatvāt | kutas tasyaiva dharmyatvam ity apekṣite 'py uktam "sarvasya hi pitā prabhuḥ" iti | sarvavidhasya pitṛkartṛkavibhāgasya yataḥ pitaiva prabhur ity arthaḥ | ye punar dharmyaṃ vibhāgam atikrāmanti ye daṇḍyāḥ | yad āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	samanyūnādhikā bhāgāḥ pitrā yeṣāṃ prakalpitāḥ |

	tathaiva te palanīyā vineyās te syur anyathā ||

pitrā śāstrāvagataprakārānusāreṇeti śeṣaḥ, prakārāntareṇa kalpitānām adharmyatvenāpalanīyatvāt | na hi svecchayaiva svārjitadhane 'pi kasyacit putrasya niṣkasahasreṇa kasyacit putrasya kapardikāmātreṇa vibhāgaḥ kṛto dharmyo bhavitum arhati | anidaṃprathamasaṃvibhāgasyaiva svatvavyavasthāpakatvāt | na caicchiko viṣamavibhāgo 'nidaṃprathama eva "icchayā vibhajet sutān" iti smṛtinibaddhakatvād iti vācyam, asyāḥ smṛtes tathāvidhavibhāgānibandhakatvāt | tathā hi, svatas tāvad ayuktatve 'py aparārkeṇāsyāḥ smṛteḥ pāriśeṣyāt tathāvidhavibhāgapratipādanaparatvam āpāditam | tat prākpratipāditasamyagarthasadbhāve saty apāstam iti | svecchāmātreṇa pitrā svārjitadhane 'pi kṛto viṣamavibhāgaḥ putrair anuśaye saty apālanīya iti siddham | yat punar aparārkeṇoktam "śreṣṭhabhāgenety etad uddhārapradarśanārtham, tena 'jyeṣṭhasya viṃśa uddhāraḥ' ityādibhir manvādiśāstrair yāvanta uddhāraprakārā abhihitāḥ te sarve 'tropalakṣitāḥ" iti, tad apy apāstam, "dhanam ekaṃ cāru samuddharj jyeṣṭhaḥ" iti jīvadvibhāgoktoddhāraviśeṣaparatvasyaiva nyāyyatvāt | bṛhaspatis tu pitur bhāgādhikyena prakārāntaram āha |

	jīvadvibhāge tu pitā gṛhṇītāṃśadvayaṃ svakam | iti |

pitā vibhajann iti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	dvāv aṃśau pratipadyeta vibhajann ātmanaḥ pitā | iti |

vibhajann iti vadan pitṛkartṛke jīvadvibhāge bhāgadvayam ātmano na punaḥ putrakartṛke jīvadvibhāga iti darśayati | pitṛkartṛkavibhāge 'py ātmano bhāgadvayagrahaṇe viśeṣam āhatuḥ śaṅkhalikhitau: "sa yady ekaputraḥ syāt dvau bhāgāv ātmanaḥ kuryāt" iti | sa iti prakṛtaḥ pitā pratyavamṛśyate | ekaputraḥ syāt atikrāntaputrāntaralābhakālaḥ syāt, galitavayaskaḥ syād iti yāvat | ata eva bahuputrasadbhāvaviṣaye 'pi galitavayaskasya bhūyiṣṭhabhagagrahaṇe pitṛputrāṇāṃ bhāgavaiṣamyam āha hārītaḥ: "jīvann eva vā vibhajya vanam āśrayed vṛddhāśramaṃ vā gacchet svalpena vā saṃvibhajya bhūyiṣṭham ādāya vaset sa yady upadasyet punas tebhyo gṛhṇīyāt kṣīṇāṃś ca vibhajet" iti | svalpena bhāgenātmīyabhāgārthapramāṇakena bhāgena pitā putrān vibhajya dvaiguṇyena bhūyiṣṭhaṃ bhāgaṃ svayam ādāya gṛha eva vā vaset | evaṃ vasan yadi kathaṃcid upadasyed aśanādyabhāvena kṣīṇaḥ syāt pitā tadā tebhyaḥ putrebhyaḥ svadattabhāgavaśād upacitadravyebhyaḥ sakāśāt svakuṭumbabharaṇaparyāptaṃ dhanaṃ punar gṛhṇīyāt | ata putrā evāśanādyabhāvena kṣīṇāḥ tadā tān punaḥ pūrvavad vibhajed ity arthaḥ | vanam āśrayet vānaprasthaḥ syāt | vṛddhāśramaḥ caturthāśramaḥ | vṛddhāśramam iti vadan galitavayaskaviṣayam iti darśayati | evaṃ cāparavayasi putrāśrayārthitvāt "yathā pitā putraṃ kṣita upadhāvati tādṛg eva tat" iti śrutiviṣayatvaṃ pitur yuktam | svalpabhāgagrahaṇād yathā putraḥ pitaraṃ kṣita upadhāvati tādṛg eva tad iti śrutiviṣayatvaṃ putrasya yuktam ity abhisaṃdhāya "yady upadasyet" ityādinā "yathā pitā putram, yathā putraḥ pitaram" ityāditacchrutidvayārthaḥ ukta iti mantavyam | ata eva "punas tebhyo gṛhṇīyāt kṣīṇāṃś ca vibhajet" iti svakīyasmṛtyor evaṃvidhaśrutimūlatāṃ darśayitum etatsamānārthaśrutidvayaṃ pratīkena tenaiva darśitam: "athāpy atra grahopadāsopadāyikīṃ śrutim udāharanti — pitāgrayaṇaḥ putrā itare grahā yady āgrayaṇaḥ skandeyur iti vyākhyātām" iti | grahopadāsopadāyikīṃ somagrahaśoṣasamādhātrīm | āgrayaṇaḥ somagrahaviśeṣaḥ | itare āgrayaṇavyatiriktā grāhā aindravāyavādayaḥ | upa vā dasyet upadasyed vā śuṣyed veti yāvat | skandeyur itītikāro 'trāvaśiṣṭaśrutibhāgapratīkārthaḥ | vyākhyātām iti pratīkopadarśitaśrutibhāgasya vyākhyāsmābhiḥ "yady upadasyet punas tebhyo gṛhṇīyāt kṣīṇāṃś ca vibhajet" iti vākyadvayena kṛtety arthaḥ | atrāpi pitur icchayā samavibhāgapakṣo 'pi pakṣe kāryaḥ,

	sakalaṃ dravyajātaṃ yadbhāgair gṛhṇanti tatsamaiḥ |

	pitaro bhrātaraś caiva vibhāgo dharmya ucyate ||

iti jīvadvibhāgaṃ vadatā kātyāyanena samavibhāgapakṣasya sārvatrikatvenābhidhānāt | tenātra viṣaye yadi svakīyecchayā pitā samabhāgapakṣaṃ kuryāt tadā tv āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	yadi kuryāt samān aṃśān patnyaḥ kāryāḥ samāṃśikāḥ |

	na dattaṃ strīdhanaṃ yāsāṃ bhartrā vā śvaśureṇa vā ||

yadi vārdhake 'py ātmanā saha samavibhāgapakṣam icchayā pitā kuryāt tadā tv ātmabhāgena saha tatsamānaṃ bhāgaṃ pratipatni gṛhṇīyād ity arthaḥ | evaṃ ca "jāyāpatyor na vibhāgo vidyate" iti hārītavacanavirodhaśaṅkā parihṛteti sarvam anavadyam | yatra putraḥ pitṛdhane dhanārjanasamarthatayā svāṃśaṃ grahītuṃ necchati tadā yāvat svīkaroti tāvat tasmai datvā pṛthakkriyā kāryety āha sa eva |

	śaktasyānīhamānasya kiṃcid datvā pṛthakkriyā | iti |

yadā punar jīvati pitari putrakartṛko vibhāgaḥ kriyate tadā "sakalaṃ dravyajātam" iti kātyāyenenoktasamabhāgaprakāreṇa kāryaḥ, putrakartṛkajīvadvibhāge pramāṇāntarapratipādakaśāstrāntarābhāvāt, "pituḥ putrā vibhajeran dhanaṃ samam" ity anuvṛttau "mātur nivṛtte rajasi" ityādinā samavibhāganiyamasya nāradoktasya pūrvaprakaraṇe putrakartṛkajīvadvibhāgāvasare darśitatvāc ca ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ jīvadvibhāgaprakaraṇam**

**athājīvadvibhāge samavibhāgaprakārāḥ**

tatra pitarīty anuvṛttau hārītaḥ: "samenaiva mṛte rikthavibhāgaḥ" iti | mṛte pitari bhrātṛbhiḥ kriyamāṇo rikthavibhāgaḥ samāṃśenaiva kārya ity arthaḥ | paiṭhīnasir api: "paitṛke vibhājyamāne dāyādye bhrātṝṇāṃ samo vibhāgaḥ" iti | dāyādye dāyadhana ity arthaḥ | na ca bhrātṝṇām iti bahucavanabalāt dvayor bhrātror avibhāga eveti vācyam, madhyakadravyasvāmisamarpaṇamātrārthatvāt tasya | ata eva madhyakadravyasvāmina ekasyaiva dāyavibhāgaḥ devalena pratiṣidhyate |

	eka eva savarṇaḥ syād dāyo 'tra na vibhajyate | iti |

savarṇāsavarānekabhrātṛviṣaye tu kvacid deśe dāyo na vibhajyata iti darśayituṃ savarṇaḥ syād ity uktam | uktaṃ ca manunā |

	brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ śūdrāputro na rikthabhāk | iti |

etad uktaṃ bhavati: śūdrāśūdrabhrātror anekatve 'pi vivāhaśunyaśūdrāputro rikthānarha ity aśūdra eva sarvaṃ gṛhṇīyād iti | evaṃ vibhāgānadhikārisavarṇasāhityād anekatve 'pi eka eva gṛhṇīyāt | tathā ca samgrahakāraḥ |

	sarvam eva harej jyeṣṭho 'nujeṣv anadhikāriṣu |

	madhyamo vā kaniṣṭḥo vā jyāyasy anadhikāriṇi || iti |

na tv adhikārisavarṇānekabhrātṛviṣaye 'pi dāyo na vibhajyate | tatra manuḥ |

	jyeṣṭha eva tu gṛhṇīyāt pitryaṃ dhanam aśeṣataḥ |

	śeṣās tam upajīveyuḥ yathaiva pitaraṃ tathā ||

na caitad vacanaṃ sahavāsapakṣaśikṣārtham iti vācyam | yatas tadartham anyad eva vacanam "evaṃ sahavaseyur vā" iti tenaiva praṇītam āste | satyam āste, tathāpi pragalbhabhrātṛṣu sahavāsapakṣaśikṣārtham eva sahavaseyur ity atideśaḥ | apragalbhānujeṣu tu tatprāgalbhyaparyantaṃ sahavāsa eva kāryo 'nena prakāreṇeti darśayitum "jyeṣṭha eva tu gṛhṇīyāt" ity upadeśa iti nānena vacanena vacobhaṅgyā savarānekabhrātṛṣu dāyavibhāgaḥ pratiṣidhyata iti na kaścid virodhaḥ | yat tu nāradenoktam,

	bibhṛyād vecchataḥ sarvān jyeṣṭho bhrātā yathā pitā |

	bhrātā śaktaḥ kaniṣṭho vā śaktyapekṣā kule sthitiḥ ||

iti, tad aśaktākhilānujaviṣayam | yat tu gautamenoktam: "sarvaṃ vā pūrvajasya itarān bibhṛyāt pitṛvat" iti | na caitan mānavena samānārtham iti vācyam, vāśabdena pragalbhabhrātṛṣv anujānāṃ dayahartvasya pākṣikatvapratipādanārthatvāvagateḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> — na mānavena samānārtham, kiṃ tu pratyakṣaśrutiviruddhtvād anadartavyam | tathā ca āpastambaḥ: "jyeṣṭho dāyāda ity eke tac chāstrair vipratiṣiddhaṃ manuḥ putrebhyo dāyaṃ vyabhajad ity aviśeṣeṇa śrūyate" iti | jyeṣṭha eva bhrātṝṇāṃ madhye paitṛkadhanabhāg ity eke punar ācāryā manyante tanmataṃ pratyakṣaśrutiviruddham, yatas taittirīyakabrāhmaṇe: "manuḥ putrebhyo dāyaṃ vyabhajat" ity aviśeṣeṇa śrūyata ity arthaḥ | svamataṃ cānantaraṃ tenaivoktam: "sarve hi dharmayuktā dharmayuktā bhāginaḥ" iti | sarve putrā ity śeṣaḥ | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	pitṛrikthaharāḥ putrāḥ sarva eva samāṃśinaḥ | iti |

rikthe ṛṇe ca samāṃśina ity arthaḥ | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	vibhajeran sutāḥ pitror ūrdhvaṃ riktham ṛṇaṃ samam | iti |

ṛṇam atra paitṛkaṃ vivakṣitam | apaitṛkasya tadaivāpākaraṇaniyamāt | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	bhrātrā pitṛvyamātṛbhyāṃ kuṭumbārtham ṛṇaṃ kṛtam |

	vibhāgakāle deyaṃ tat rikthibhiḥ sarvam eva tu ||

nāradas tu vibhāgakāle paitṛkam ṛṇam api deyam ity āha |

	yac chiṣṭaṃ pitṛdāyebhyo datvarṇaṃ paitṛkaṃ ca tat |

	bhrātṛbhis tad vibhaktavyam ṛṇī syād anyathā pitā ||

"pitṛdāyāt nava śrāddhāni, navaśrāddhaṃ saha dadyuḥ" iti gautamabrāhmaṇāt,

	pitur ūrdhvaṃ vibhāgo ya ekoddiṣṭād anantaram |

iti saṃgrahakāravacanāc ca | evaṃ ca paitṛkaṃ dhanaṃ navaśrāddhapaitṛkādiṛṇāpākaraṇārthadhanād abhyadhikaṃ cen nāradoktam eva kāryam, no ced yājñavalkyenoktam everty avagantavyam | paitṛkam api kiṃcid ṛṇaṃ vibhāgakāle paitṛkadhanād anapākaraṇīyam, kiṃ tu vibhajanīyam evety āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	dharmārthaṃ prītidattaṃ ca yad ṛṇaṃ syān niyojitam |

	tad dṛśyamānaṃ vibhajen na dānaṃ paitṛkād dhanāt ||

yad dharmārthaṃ saṃkalpitam, yac ca pitrā prītena vācā dattam, yac ca svenaiva pitrā putrair apākaraṇīyam iti niyojitaṃ tad etat trividham ṛṇaṃ dṛśyamānaṃ jñayamānaṃ vibhajed evety arthaḥ | yaḥ punaḥ putraḥ svakartṛkadhanārjanakarmaṇā dhanaṃ prāptuṃ śaktaḥ san pitṛdvārāgataṃ dhanaṃ necchati tasya santānatas tadaṃśanimittakavivādaparihārārtham asāvitaraiḥ putrair vibhājyadhanāt kiṃcid dhanaṃ mūladhanārthaṃ datvā avaśyaṃ vibhājya ity āha |

	bhrātḍṇāṃ yas tu neheta dhanaṃ śaktaḥ svakarmaṇā |

	sa nirbhājyaḥ svakād aṃśāt kiṃcid datvopajīvanam ||

bhrātṛviśeṣasya "karmabhūyastvāt phalabhūyastvam" iti nyāyena samabhāgād abhyadhikena dhānyādinā vivardhanam itarair bhrātṛbhiḥ kāryam ity āha nāradaḥ |

	kuṭumbārtheṣu codyuktaṃ tat kāryaṃ kurute tu yaḥ |

	sa bhrātṛbhir bṛhaṇīyo grāsācchādanavahanaiḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām ajīvadvibhāge samavibhāgaprakāraḥ**

**atha viṣamavibhāgaprakāraḥ**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	pitṛrikthaharāḥ putrāḥ sarva eva samāṃśinaḥ |

	vidyākarmaratas teṣām adhikaṃ labdhum arhati ||

ye patitādivyatiriktāḥ pitṛrikthaharāḥ putrāḥ vidyāder asattayā sattayā vā sadṛśās te sarve samāṃśina eva syuḥ | ye punar vidyāder asattayā sattayā va visadṛśās teṣāṃ madhye yo vidyādyupetaḥ sa evoddhāreṇa vā viṣamavibhāgena vādhikaṃ dhanaṃ labdhum arhatīty arthaḥ | tatrāpi karmānuṣṭhātṛtvatāratamye labhyadhanaparimāṇaśreṣṭhyayos tāratamyaṃ bhavati | na punar vidvattātāratamyenety āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	yathā yathā vibhāgāptaṃ dhanaṃ yāgārthatām iyāt |

	tathā tathā vidhātavyaṃ vidvadbhir bhāgagauravam || iti |

dravyabāhulye satīti śeṣaḥ | ata eva manuḥ |

	uddhāro na daśasv asti saṃpannānāṃ svakarmasu |

	yat kiṃcid eva deyaṃ syāj jyāyase mānavardhanam || iti |

jyeṣṭhāder arpaṇārthaṃ vibhājyadravyarāśeḥ sakāśād yo 'rtha uddhriyate sa uddhāraḥ | daśasu katipayeṣu jīvanaparyāptadhaneṣv iti yāvat | svakarmasu svādhikārato 'nuṣṭheyakarmasu saṃpannānāṃ kartṛtvam āpannānām aśeṣabhrātṝṇāṃ dravyabāhulye saty api karmaniṣṭhatvasāmyād uddhāro mānavardhanārthadānaṃ ca nāsti | kiṃ tu svalpadhanaśāliṣu vidyādito visadṛśeṣu jīvanamātraparyāptadhanatvenānuddhāre 'pi saṃmānārthaṃ jyāyase kiṃcid vastramātraṃ deyamity arthaḥ | evaṃ ca yeṣāṃ bhrātṝṇāṃ prabhūtaṃ dhanaṃ vidyate, vidyādau ca tāratamyam asti teṣāṃ vibhāge uddhāra iti mantavyam | uddhāraprakāram apy āha manuḥ |

	jyeṣṭhasya viṃśa uddhāraḥ sarvadravyāc ca yad varam |

	tato 'rthaṃ madhyamasya syāt turīyaṃ tu yavīyasaḥ ||

jyeṣṭhasya agrajasya vidyādivaśād uttamasya vibhājyadravyarāśer viṃśatitamo bhāgaḥ, tasminn eva rāśau śreṣṭham ekaṃ ca dravyam uddhāraḥ | tato 'rthaṃ tasminn eva rāśau catvāriṃśattamo bhāgo madhyamam ekaṃ dravyaṃ janmato vidyādivaśataś ca madhyamasyoddhāraḥ | turīyaṃ tasminn eva rāśau aśītitamo bhāgaḥ kaṇiṣṭham ekaṃ darvyaṃ janmato vidyāvaśāc ca yavīyasa uddhāra syād ity arthaḥ | aviśiṣṭasya ca rāśer vibhāgaprakāram āha sa eva |

	evaṃ samuddhṛtoddhāre samānaṃśān prakalpayet | iti |

uddhṛtāvaśiṣṭam samaṃ nibhajed ity arthaḥ | atha vā tasminn eva viṣaye viṣamavibhāga eva syān noddhāra ity āh sa eva |

	uddhāre 'nuddhṛte tv eṣām iyaṃ syād aṃśakalpanā |

	ekādhikaṃ harj jyeṣṭhaḥ putro 'dhyarthaṃ tato 'nujaḥ ||

	aṃśam aṃśaṃ yavīyāṃsa iti dharma vyavasthitaḥ ||

ekādhikam aṃśaṃ dvyaṃśam it yavat, "dvyaṃśī vā pūrvajaḥ syāt" iti gautamasmaraṇāt | pūrvajo vidhyādināpi jyeṣṭha ity arthaḥ | ata eva bṛhaspatiḥ |

	janmavidyāguṇajyeṣṭho dvyaṃśaṃ dāyam avāpnuyāt | iti |

evaṃ ca na janmataḥ prāthamyādimātram uddhāre viṣamavibhāge vā kāraṇam, kiṃ tu vidyādinibandhanaśreṣṭhatvādyupetaṃ prāthamyādikam iti mantavyam | ayaṃ ca viṣamavibhāgaprakāraḥ kaliyuge tu na vartat ity āha saṃgrahakāraḥ |

	yathā niyogadharmo 'dya nānūbandhyāvadho 'pi vā |

	tathoddhāravibhāgo 'pi naiva saṃprati vartate ||

adya saṃpratīty etau śabdau kaliyugam abhisaṃdhāyoktau | ata eva purāṇam |

	ūḍhāyāḥ punar udvāhaṃ jyeṣṭhāṃśaṃ govadhaṃ tathā |

	kalau pañca na kurvīta bhrātṛjāyāṃ kamaṇḍalum ||

jyeṣṭhāṃśaṃ janmavidyādinibandhanaśreṣṭhāṃśam | govadham anūbandhyādikarmāṅgam | kamaṇḍaluṃ gṛhiṇaḥ kamaṇḍaludhāraṇam | etad eva dhāreśvareṇoktam: "jyeṣṭhasya viṃśa uddhāraḥ ityevamādīni vākyāni na vicāryante lokena atyantaṃ parityaktatvāt" iti | kalāv iti śeṣaḥ, dvāparādāv anuṣṭheyatvenātyantaṃ parityāgābhāvāt | yat punar viśvarūpeṇoktam, "yathā

	mahokṣaṃ vā mahājaṃ vā śrotriyāyopakalpayet |

ityasya śiṣṭācāreṇa bādhitatvād akaraṇam, evam evoddhārasyāpi" iti, tad ayuktam, smṛtiśiṣṭācārayor virodhe śiṣṭācārasyaiva durbalasya bādhyatvāt | durbalatvaṃ ca "śrutismṛtivihito dharmas tadalābhe śiṣṭācāraḥ pramāṇam" iti vasiṣṭhasmaraṇād avagamyate | kiṃ ca mahokṣāder anupakalpanaṃ śiṣṭācārābhāva evaṃ na punaḥ śiṣṭācāra iti śiṣṭācāreṇa badhitatvād ity ayuktam uktam, "śiṣṭācārābhāvād akaraṇam" iti śrīkaroktivad vaktavyam, na ca tathoktam | yat punar vijñāneśvareṇoktam: "satyam ayaṃ viṣamo vibhāgaḥ śāstradṛṣṭaḥ, tathāpi lokavidviṣṭatvān nānuṣṭheyaḥ" iti, etad api vāṅmātram | na hy uddhāravibhāgādau lokavidveśo 'sti, pratyuta vidyāguṇapuṇyakarmasaṃpannajyeṣṭhādau bhāgādhikye lokānurāgo dṛśyata iti yat kiṃcid etat | ye punaḥ smṛtisamuccayakārāḥ śambhuśrīkaradevasvāmyādayaḥ uddhāraviṣamavibhāgayoḥ śiṣṭācāraṃ kvāpi manyamānā uddhārādiviṣayāṇi bahūni smṛtivākyāni vicārayituṃ granthavistaraṃ cakrire | teṣāṃ dharmajñasamayapurāṇavacanābhyāṃ kalau sarvatra śiṣṭācārābhāvasya niścitatvād vṛthaiva prayāso granthavistaraś ca jāta ity asmābhir uddhārādiviṣaye diṅmātram eva pradarśitam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ viṣamavibhāgaprakāraḥ**

**athānyāny apy ajīvadvibhāgaviṣayāṇi kānicid vacanāni likhyante**

tatra vasiṣṭhaḥ: "atha bhrātṝṇāṃ dayavibhāgo yāś cānapatyāḥ striyas tāsāṃ cā putralābhāt" iti | yāḥ pitṛstriyo 'napatyā garbhāvasthāpatyās tāsām ā putralābhād ā prasavāt sahavāsena sthitānāṃ bhrātṝṇāṃ prasūtāpatyaliṅgānānantaraṃ dāyavibhāgo na punar evaṃvidhaviṣaye navaśrāddhānantaraṃ dāyavibhāgo na punar evaṃvidhaviṣaye navaśrāddhānantaraṃ dāyavibhāga ity arthaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanv</span> asya vacanasya navaśrāddhānantaraṃ bhrātṝṇām anapatyapitṛstrīṇāṃ ca dāyavibhāgo bhavatīti ṛjvarthaḥ kim iti parityajyate | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span>: anapatyastrīṇām ā putralābhād iti viruddhārthāvagates tatparihārāya parityajyate | strīṇām adāyānāṃ dāyavibhāgāsaṃbhavāc ca parityajyate | strīṇām adāyānāṃ dāyavibhāgāsaṃbhavāc ca parityajyate | tathā ca arhati strīty anuvṛttau bodhāyanaḥ: "na dāyaṃ nirindriyā hy adāyāś ca striyo matā iti śrutiḥ" iti | hiśabdo 'tra yasmādarthe | evaṃ cāyam arthaḥ: yasmān nirindriyā vyādhyādināpagatendriyāḥ striyaś cādāyā matā iti śrutis tasmān na strī dāyaṃ vibhaktavyā, anyadvārāgata taddravyam arhatīti | "nirindriyā adāyāś ca striyo matāḥ" ity anena "tasmāt striyo nirindriyā adāyādīḥ" iti taittirīyakaśrutir arthataḥ pradarśiteti mantavyam | yady adāyāḥ striyaḥ kathaṃ tarhi yājñavalkyenoktam,

	pitur ūrdhvaṃ vibhajatāṃ mātāpy aṃśaṃ samaṃ haret |

iti, kathitaṃ ca vyāsena,

	asutās tu pituḥ patnyaḥ samānāṃśāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |

	pitāmahyaś ca sarvās tā mātṛtulyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ||

iti, kathitaṃ ca viṣṇunā: "mātaraḥ putrabhāgānusāribhāgahāriṇya anūḍhāś ca duhitaraḥ" iti | na hi strīṇāṃ dāyānarhatve mātrādīnāṃ duhitrantānām aṃśabhāgitvoktir yujyate | bāḍhaṃ yujyate, dāyānarhāṇāṃ tu dāyarāhitvoktir virudhyate, na punar aṃśahāritvoktiḥ | aṃśaśabdo hi bhāgavacano na dāyavacanaḥ, gaṇadravyādāv apy aṃśo deya iti prayogadarśanāt | tena mātrādīnāṃ dāyadravyābhāve 'pi vibhājyarāśau svāmyasya patnyadhikaraṇasiddhasya vidyamānatvāt tatra yāvadartham arthaharaṇaṃ svakīyasvāmyavyavasthāpakaṃ mātrādibhir api kāryam iti yājñavalkyādibhir uktam iti mantavyam | na ca dāyaśabdo "yad dhanaṃ svāmisaṃbandhād eva nimittād anyasya svaṃ bhavati tad ucyate" iti dāyaśabdārthanirūpaṇārthaṃ mitākṣarāyām uktaṃ yuktam | evaṃ hi nityaṃ vibhāgārham eva tvanmate patnīsvaṃ bhavet dāyaśabdārthatvāt | loke dampatyor dhane vibhāgārhadravyam eva hi dāyaśabdena prayujyate | tvanmate patnīsvaṃ patisaṃbandhād eva bhavatīti tasyāpi dāyatvāpattiḥ | tataś ca "adāyāḥ striyaḥ" iti śrutivirodho durvāraḥ syāt | asmin mate tu vibhāgārhaṃ svasvāmisaṃbandhād eva nimittād anyasya svaṃ jātaṃ dāyaśabdārtha iti vibhāgānarhaṃ patnīsvaṃ na dāyaḥ | tathā hi, patidvārāgataṃ jāyādhanaṃ nityaṃ vibhāgānarham eva, loke dampatyor dhane vibhāgādarśanāt, "jāyāpatyor na vibhāgo vidyate," iti hārītasmaraṇāc ca | tenātra na mātuḥ svāmyavyavasthāpako dāyavibhāgaḥ, kiṃ tu yāvadartham evārthagrahaṇam iti mantavyam | ata eva smṛtyantare nirdhanamātṛviṣayam evāṃśaharaṇaṃ na mātṛmātraviṣayam eva jñāyate,

	janany asvadhanā putrair vibhāge 'ṃśaṃ samaṃ haret |

iti smaraṇāt | asvadhanā prātisvikastrīdhanaśūnyā jananī putrair ajīvadvibhāge kriyamāṇe putrāṃśasamam aṃśaṃ hared ity arthaḥ | jananīgrahaṇaṃ tatspatnyāder upalakṣaṇārtham, asvadhanetiviśeṣaṇopādānāt | svadhanād eva svakīyajīvanasya svānuṣṭheyasya ca dhanasādhyakarmaṇaḥ siddhisaṃbhave jananyādīnāṃ na bhāgagrahaṇam iti gamyate | tathā svadhanamātrāt tayoḥ siddhyasaṃbhave jananyādīnāṃ sadhanānām api na samabhāgaharaṇam, kiṃ tu yathopayogaṃ nyūnabhāgasyaiva grahaṇam iti ca gamyate, tathā vibhājyarāśer atibahutve nirdhanānām api jananyādīnāṃ na samāṃśagrahaṇam, kiṃ tu yathāsvopayogaṃ nyūnasyaiva haraṇam ity api gamyate, asvadhaneti viśeṣaṇasyopayogavaśād aṃśaharaṇam jananyāḥ na punaḥ bhrātṛvad dāyabhāgitvavaśād iti jñāpanārthatvāt | samam iti viśeṣaṇasya tūpayogavaśād asamāṃśasya haraṇe 'py avaiyarthyam, alpavibhājyarāśāv upayogavaśād adhikaharaṇasya prāptasya nivṛttyarthatvāt | yat punar viṣṇunā duhitṝṇāṃ putrabhāgānusāribhāgahāritvam uktam, tatrāpi janmanā labdhasvāmyasya pitṛmaraṇe 'py asvatantrāvasthasyāpy avibhājyasyādāyatvāt, anūḍhā iti viśeṣaṇopādānāc ca vivāhārthaṃ putrabhāgānusāribhagaharaṇaṃ na punaḥ bhrātṝṇām iva duhitṝṇāṃ dāyavibhāgārtham iti gamyate | yata eva na dāyavibhāgārtham aṃśaharaṇaṃ kiṃ tu vivāhasaṃskārārtham ata eva vibhājyadhanabāhulyābhāvaviṣayam etad iti vakṣyate | ata eva ca devalenoktam |

	kanyābhyaś ca pitṛdravye deyaṃ vaivāhikaṃ vasu |

vivāhaprayojakaṃ dhanam ity arthaḥ | ata eva ca saṃskāryā ity anuvṛttau yājñavalkyenoktam |

	bhaginyaś ca nijād aṃśād datvāṃśaṃ tu turīyakam | iti |

ekasya putrasya yāvān nijāṃśas taccaturthāṃśaṃ pratibhagini pradāya bhrātṛbhir bhaginyaḥ saṃskāryā vivāhayitavyā ity arthaḥ | smṛtyantare 'pi |

	bhrātṛbhyo 'ṃśacaturbhāgaṃ tatra kanyā hared dhanam | iti |

bhrātṛbhyaḥ sakāśād aṃśaṃ caturthāṃśaṃ dhanaṃ tatra ajīvadvibhāge ekaikā kanyā hared ity arthaḥ | analpavibhājyaviṣayam etat | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	kanyakānāṃ tv adattānāṃ caturtho bhāga iṣtate |

	putrāṇāṃ tu trayo bhāgāḥ sāmyaṃ tu alpadhane smṛtam ||

kanyakānāṃ pratyekam iti śeṣaḥ | evaṃ putrāṇām ity atrāpi śeṣo draṣṭavyaḥ | alpe vibhājyadhane putrabhāgasāmyaṃ tv ekaikakanyakābhāgasya viṣṇvādinā smṛtam iti turīyapādārthaḥ | evaṃ cānalpe vibhājyadhane caturtho bhāga iti pāriśeṣyād avagamyate | "putrāṇāṃ tu trayo bhāgāḥ" ity etat samasaṃkhyākabhrātṛbhaginīviṣayam | yatra tu bhaginyo nyūnasaṃkhyākās tatra putrāṇāṃ na trayo bhāgāḥ kiṃ tu kiṃcid abhyadhikāḥ | yat punar manunoktam,

	svebhyo 'ṃśebhyas tu kanyābhyaḥ pradadyur bhrātaraḥ pṛthak |

	svāt svād aṃśāc caturbhāgaṃ patitāḥ syur aditsavaḥ ||

iti, yady apy atra svāt svād iti vīpsayā yāvanto bhrātṝṇām aṃśās tāvanta eva caturthāṃśāḥ kanyābhyo bhrātṛbhiḥ pradeyā iti ṛñvarthaḥ pratibhāti | tathāpy adhikasaṃkhyākakanyāviṣayatvān na prācīnasmṛtivirodhaḥ | na cātraikaikasyāḥ svāt svād aṃśāc caturthāṃśadānam, yena prācīnasmṛtivirodhaḥ | kiṃ tu samudāyasyeti sutarām avirodhaḥ | dattaṃ ca kanyābhiḥ samatvena vibhajya grāhyam | yat punar viṣṇunoktam: "anūḍhānāṃ ca kanyānām aṃśavān svavittānusāreṇa saṃskāraṃ kuryāt" iti, tad ekaputratayā dāyavibhāgābhāvaviṣayam | yad vā bhrātṝṇāṃ sahavāsaviṣayam | kanyāgrahaṇam asaṃskṛtānāṃ pitur apatyānām upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva vyāsaḥ |

	asaṃskṛtās tu ye tatra paitṛkād eva te dhanāt |

	saṃskāryā bhrātṛbhir jyeṣṭhaiḥ kanyakāś ca yathāvidhi ||

bṛhaspatiḥ |

	asaṃskṛtā bhrātaras tu ye syus tatra yavīyasaḥ |

	saṃskaryāḥ pūrvajais te vai paitṛkān madhyakād dhanāt ||

tatra ajīvatpitṛkeṣu bhrātṛṣv ity arthaḥ | asaṃskṛtāḥ pitreti śeṣaḥ | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	yeṣāṃ vai na kṛtāḥ pitrā saṃskāravidhayaḥ kramāt |

	kartavyā bhrātṛbhis teṣāṃ paitṛkād eva te dhanāt ||

paitṛkadhanābhāve 'py āha sa eva |

	avidyamāne pitrye 'rthe svāṃśād uddhṛtya vā punaḥ |

	avaśyakāryāḥ saṃskārā bhrātṝṇāṃ pūrvasaṃskṛtaiḥ ||

saṃskārā jātakarmādyā upanayanāntā vivakṣitāḥ, avaśyakāryā ity abhidhānāt | vivāhādisaṃskārasya tu naiṣṭhikatvādipakṣāntaradarśanād avaśyakāryatābhāvāt saṃskāraśabdasya saṃkoco 'tra vivakṣita ity anavadyam | kanyakānāṃ tu vivāhāntāḥ saṃskārā upanayanarahitāḥ pitryārthābhāve svārthād uddhṛtya kāryāḥ, vivāhasyopanayanasthānatvenāvaśyakāryatvāt | vibhāgakāle 'nyad api dhanaṃ kanyakā svadhṛtālaṃkārādikaṃ labhata ity āha śaṅkhaḥ: "vibhajyamāne dāyādye kanyālaṃkāre vaivāhikaṃ strīdhanaṃ ca kanyā labhet" iti | dāyādye dāyadhane bhrātṛbhir vibhajyamāne kanyā svadhṛtālaṃkāraṃ vaivāhikaṃ turīyāṃśādidhanaṃ strīdhanaṃ ca pitrādinā dattaṃ labhed ity arthaḥ | bodhāyano 'pi: "mātur alaṃkāraṃ duhitaraḥ sāṃpradāyikaṃ labheran anyad vā" iti | sāṃpradāyikaṃ mātṛparaṃparāyātam | anyat tad itarad vā mātrā dhṛtam alaṃkāraṃ mātṛkaṃ tatra vibhayamāne duhitaraḥ kumāryo labherann ity arthaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām ajīvadvibhāgaviṣayāṇi**

**atha anyāny api dāyāṃśānarhaviṣayāṇi kānicid vacanāni likhyante**

tatra devalaḥ |

	mṛte na pitari klībakuṣṭhyunmattajaḍāndhakāḥ |

	patitaḥ patitāpatyaṃ liṅgī dāyāṃśabhāginaḥ ||

mṛte pitari klībādayo dhanāṃśabhāgino na bhavantīty arthaḥ | liṅgī naiṣṭhikavanasthādiḥ | kṣapaṇakapāśupatādiś cātra vivakṣitaḥ | mṛte pitarīti vibhāgakālapradarśanārtham uktam | tena pitari jīvaty api jīvadvibhāge klībādayo dāyabhāgino na bhavanti | ata eva jīvadvibhāge 'py abhāgitvam eteṣāṃ vaktum uktam āpastambena: "jīvan putrebhyo dāyaṃ vibhajet samaṃ klībam unmattaṃ patitaṃ ca parihāpya" iti | caśabdaḥ kuṣṭhijaḍāndhādīnāṃ saṃgrahārthaḥ | parihāpya varjayitvety arthaḥ | manur apy anaṃśabhāgina āha |

	anaṃśau klībapatitau jātyandhabadhirau tathā |

	unmattajaḍamūkāś ca ye ca kecin nirindriyāḥ ||

nirindriyāḥ vyādhyādinā vinaṣṭaghrāṇādīndriyāḥ | nārado 'pi |

	pitṛdviṭ patitaḥ ṣaṇḍo yaś ca syād apapātritaḥ |

	aurasā api naite 'ṃśaṃ labheran kṣetrajāḥ kutaḥ ||

apapātritaḥ apapātrīkṛtaḥ, "apapātritasya rikthapiṇḍodakāni vyāvartante" iti śaṅkhalikhitasmaraṇāt | apapātritasya mahāparādhena bandhubhir bahiṣkṛtasyety arthaḥ | vasiṣṭho 'p: "anaṃśās tv āśramāntaragatāḥ" iti | gṛhasthāśramam apekṣyeti śeṣaḥ | na caivam upakurvāṇasya brahmacāriviśeṣasyāpy aṃśaśūnyatvam āyātam iti vācyam, gṛhasthāśramānarhatvakāryāśramāntarasyātra vivakṣitatvāt | viṣṇur api: "patitaklībāciktsyarogavikalās tv abhāgaharāḥ" iti | vikalaḥ indriyavikalaḥ | acikitsyaroga iti vadan aciktsyaklaibyavaikalyādiśālino 'py abhāgaharā iti darśayati | tena vibhāgakālasthitaklaibyādiśālinām abhāgaharatvaṃ na punaḥ sahajabādhiryaklaibyādiśālinām eveti mantavyam | kātyāyanaḥ |

	akramoḍhāsutaś caiva sagotrādyas tu jāyate |

	pravrajyāvasitaś caiva na riktaṃ teṣu cārhati ||

akramoḍhāsuto varṇakramajanmakramātikrameṇa pariṇītāyāḥ suto yaḥ | tathā sagotrāt sagotrastrīpariṇetuḥ sakāśād yaḥ sutaḥ sagotrastriyāṃ jāyate | tathā pravrajyāvasitaḥ svīkṛtacaturthāśramatyāgī yo bhavet | teṣv akramoḍḥāsutādiṣu rikthaṃ prāptuṃ nārhati, te rikthānarhā ity arthaḥ | manur api |

	aniyuktāsutaś caiva pitriṇyāptaś ca devarāt |

	ubhau tau nārhato bhāgaṃ jārajātakakāmajau ||

aniyuktāyāṃ parastriyām apariṇetuḥ sakāśād utpannaḥ suto jārajātakaḥ, svārthe kapratyayaḥ | pariṇetrotpannaputravatyāṃ devarāt utpannaḥ kāmajaḥ | tāv ubhau bhāgaṃ nārhata ity arthaḥ | etad uktaṃ bhavati: jārajātaḥ niyogavidhyatikrameṇa jātaś ca kṣetriṇo dhanabhāgaṃ nārhatīti | bṛhaspatir api |

	savarṇajo 'py aguṇavān nārhaḥ syāt paitṛke dhane | iti |

aguṇavān pitṛdṛṣṭādṛṣṭakāryopayogiguṇarahitaḥ | tathā cānantaram uktaṃ tenaiva |

	uttamarṇādhamarṇābhyāṃ pitaraṃ trāyate sutaḥ |

	atas tu viparītena nāsti tena prayojanam ||

	tathā gavā kiṃ kriyate yā na dogdhrī na garbhiṇī |

	ko 'rthaḥ putreṇa jātena yo na vidvān na dhārmikaḥ ||

	śāsraśauryārtharahitas tapovijñānavarjitaḥ |

	ācārahīnaḥ putras tu mūtroccārasamaḥ smṛtaḥ || iti |

uttamam ṛṇam ṛṣidevapitṝṇām | adhamam ṛṇaṃ dhanikahastāt gṛhītam | yathā vidyādirahitaḥ sūnur auraso 'pi heyabhūta iti mūtroccārasama ity uktam | manur api |

	sarva eva vikarmasthā nārhanti bhrātaro dhanam | iti |

vikarmasthāḥ niṣiddhakarmaikaniratāḥ | dhanaṃ vibhājyadhanam | evaṃ nirūpitaniraṃśakāḥ sarve poṣaṇīyāḥ | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	klībo 'tha patitas tajjaḥ paṅgur unmattako jaḍaḥ |

	andho 'cikitsyarogādyā bhartavyāś tu niraṃśakāḥ ||

tajjaḥ patitotpannaḥ | ādyaśabdenānyeṣāṃ prākpratipāditānāṃ grahaṇam | bhartavyāḥ dāyaharair it śeṣaḥ, "rikthagrāhibhis te bhartavyāḥ" it viṣṇusmaraṇāt | kathaṃ bhartavyā ity apekṣite manuḥ |

	sarveṣām api tu nyāyyaṃ dātuṃ śakyaṃ manīṣiṇā |

	grāsācchādanam atyantaṃ patito hy adadad bhavet ||

atyantaṃ yāvajjīvam ity arthaḥ | kātyāyanaḥ |

	grāsācchādanam atyantaṃ deyaṃ tadbandhubhir matam |

	bandhūnām apy abhāve tu pitṛdravyaṃ tadāpnuyāt ||

	apitryaṃ draviṇaṃ prāptaṃ dāpanīyā na bāndhavāḥ || iti |

tadbandhubhiḥ niraṃśakabandhubhiḥ | tatpitṛdravyagrāhibhir grāsācchādanaṃ deyam iti manvādīnāṃ matam ity arthaḥ | apitryam ityāder ayam arthaḥ | niraṃśakapitṛdraviṇaṃ tadbandhubhir aprāptam, rājñā tadbandhavo bharaṇāya na dāpanīyā iti | etad uktaṃ bhavati | niraṃśakapitṛdhanāgrāhakabāndhavānām āvaśyakaṃ niraṃśakabharaṇam iti | evam aśeṣaniraṃśakānāṃ bharaṇaṃ prāptaṃ kasyacit paryudāsaṃ kurvann āha devalaḥ |

	teṣāṃ patitavarjyebhyo bhaktavastaṃ pradīyate | iti |

patitotpannasyāpi patitatvāt so 'pi varjyaḥ | ata eva bodhayanaḥ: "atītavyavahārān grāsācchādanaiḥ bibhṛyuḥ andhajaḍaklībavyasanivyādhitādīṃś cākarmiṇaḥ patitatajjātavarjyam" iti | atītavyavahārāḥ mūkādayaḥ | akarmiṇaḥ dharmārthavṛttyarthakarmasv akṣamāḥ | vasiṣṭhas tu tantrokyaiva caturṇāṃ bharaṇapratiṣedham āha: "anaṃśās tv āśramāntaragatāḥ klībonmattapatitāś ca bharaṇaṃ klībonmattānām" iti | atra viśeṣagrahaṇaṃ śeṣapratiṣedhārtham iti nyāyena patitāśramāntaragataviṣayasya bharaṇasya pratiṣedho gamyate | āśramāntaragatim antareṇa pravrajyāvasitatvāsaṃbhavāt pravrajyāvasitaviṣayabharaṇasyāpi pratiṣedho 'trāvagamyate | evaṃ ca patitatajjātāśramāntaragatapravrajyāvasitatajjātānāṃ niraṃśakānāṃ bharaṇam anāvaśyakam iti mantavyam | niraṃśakaputrāṇām aṃśagrahaṇavirodhiklaibyādyābhāve 'pi niraṃśakaputratvena paitāmahadhanānarhatve prāpte tadapavādam āha devalaḥ |

	tatputrāḥ pitṛdāyāṃśaṃ labheran doṣavarjitāḥ | iti |

tatputrāḥ niraṃśakaputrāḥ | aṃśagrahaṇavirodhiklaibyādidoṣavarjitāḥ pitṛdāyāṃśaṃ paitāmahadhanāṃśaṃ labherann ity arthaḥ | na cedaṃ vacanaṃ patitāpatyasyāpi paitāmahadhanabhāgitvaṃ prāpayati tatputrā iti sāmānyenābhidhānād iti śaṅkanīyam, doṣavarjitā ity anena vyadastatvāt  | patitasyāpi pumapatyaṃ patitam eva bhavati | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ: "patitotpannaḥ patito bhavatīty āhur anyatra striyāḥ sā hi paragāminī" iti | patitasya putravat pratilomāyāḥ striyāḥ putrasya putro 'pi paitāmahadhanānarhaḥ aṃśagrahaṇavirodhidoṣasadbhāvāt | ata eva viṣṇuḥ: "teṣām evaurasāḥ putrā bhāgahāriṇo na tu patitasya patanīye kṛte karmaṇy anantarotpannāḥ pratilomāsu strīṣūtpannāś cābhāginas tatputrāḥ paitāmahe 'py arthe" iti | anantarotpannāḥ paścād utpannāḥ, ānantaryasyāvivakṣitatvāt | te tu na bhāgahāriṇaḥ | evaṃ pravrajyāvasitādiputreṣu yatra yatra aṃśagrahaṇavirodhidoṣo 'sti tatra tatra paitāmahadhanābhāgitvaṃ vijñeyam | kṣetrajaputraviṣaye 'py uktaṃ yājñavalkyena,

	aurasakṣetrajās teṣāṃ nirdoṣā bhāgahāriṇaḥ |

iti, tat dvāparādiviṣayam iti mantavyam, kalau kṣetrajaputraniṣedhāt | sadoṣās tv aurasādayo bhartavyā ity etat

	andhociktsyarogādyā bhartavyās tu niraṃśakāḥ |

ity anenaivoktam itīha noktam, kiṃ tu pūrvaṃ yan noktaṃ tad āha sa eva |

	sutāś caiṣāṃ prabhartavyā yāvad vai bhartṛsātkṛtāḥ |

	aputrā yoṣitaś caiṣāṃ bhartavyāḥ sādhuvṛttayaḥ ||

	nirvāsyā vyabhicāriṇyaḥ pratikūlās tathaiva ca || iti |

sutāḥ kanyakāḥ eṣāṃ niraṃśakānām | bhartavyāḥ niraṃśakapitṛdravyagrāhibhir niraṃśakabharaṇaprakāreṇaiva | yā vajjīvam ity asyāpavādo "yāvad vai bhartṛsātkṛtāḥ" iti,yāvad vivāhasaṃskṛtā bhavanti tāvad evaty apavādabhāgasyārthaḥ | eṣāṃ niraṃśakānām aputrā yoṣitaḥ pariṇītāḥ striyaḥ sadācārā niraṃśakapitṛdravyagrāhibhir eva niraṃśakabharaṇaprakāreṇaiva bhartavyāḥ | vyabhicāriṇyaḥ bharaṇakartuḥ pratikūlāś ca gṛhād bahiḥ kāryāḥ | tatrāsādhuvṛttayo nirvāsitā na bhartavyāḥ | pratikūlās tu nirvāsitā na bhartavyāḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām aṃśānarhaviṣayāṇi**

**atha vibhājyanirūpaṇam**

tatra kātyāyanaḥ |

	paitāmahaṃ ca pitryaṃ ca yac cānyat svayam ārjitam |

	dāyādānāṃ vibhāge tu sarvam etad vibhajyate ||

svayam ārjitaṃ pitryādyavibhaktadravyopayogena svayam ārjitam, tadanupayogena svayam ārjitasyāvibhājyatvāt | evaṃ trividhaṃ dhanaṃ sarvaṃ vibhajyate | yadi nāsti pitāmahādikṛtam ṛṇādikam iti śeṣaḥ | asti cen na sarvam, api tu ṛṇādikaṃ datvāvaśiṣṭaṃ vibhajyate | tathā ca sa eva |

	ṛṇaṃ prītipradānaṃ tu datvā śeṣaṃ vibhājayet | iti |

prītipradānaṃ prītyā pradattaṃ śeṣaṃ vibhājayed iti vadan vibhājyabāhulyaviṣayam etad iti darśayati | tadbāhulyaviṣaye tu rikthavad ṛṇam api vibhājyam ity ajīvadvibhāgaprakaraṇe pradarśitam | vibhāgakāle yad ṛṇaṃ prītideyaṃ tasyākūṭatvaniścayārthaṃ bandhubhiḥ saha rikthagrāhibhis tadvicāryam ity āha sa eva |

	ṛṇam evaṃvidhaṃ śodhya vibhāge bandhubhiḥ saha | iti |

vañcanarhaṃ riktham api viśodhyam ity āha sa eva |

	gṛhopaskaravāhyāś ca dohyābharaṇakarmiṇaḥ |

	dṛśyamānā vibhajyante kośaṃ gūḍhe 'bravīd bhṛguḥ ||

karmiṇaḥ karmakarā dāsādayaḥ | gūḍhe dravye vañcanāśaṅkāyāṃ kośākhyaṃ divyaṃ bhṛgur abravīd ity arthaḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	gūḍhadravyābhiśaṅkāyāṃ pratyayas tatra kīrtitaḥ | iti |

prayayo divyam, tad api kośākhyam evety uktaṃ prāk | bṛhaspatir apy atra tad eva divyaṃ bhavatīty āha |

	gṛhopaskaravāhyādidohyābharaṇakarmiṇaḥ |

	dṛśyamānā vibhajyante gūḍhe kośo vidhīyate ||

na ca kośagrahaṇaṃ yathāprāptadivyopalakṣaṇārtham iti vācyam,

	śaṅkāviśvāsasaṃdhāne vibhāge rikthināṃ sadā |

	kriyāsamūhakartṛtve kośam eva pradāpayet ||

iti kātyāyanīye vibhāgaviṣaye 'bhihite 'pi kośe punar  iha viṣayābhidhānasya niyamārthatvāt | tena bārhaspatye 'pi kośagrahaṇaṃ niyamārtham eva ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ vibhājyanirūpaṇam**

**atha avibhājyanirūpaṇam**

tatra vyāsaḥ |

	vidyāprāptaṃ śauryadhanaṃ yac ca saudāyikaṃ bhavet |

	vibhāgakāle tat tasya nānveṣṭavyaṃ svarikthibhiḥ ||

vidyāprāptaśabdenātra na vidyāmātraprāptaṃ dhanam ucyate, kiṃ tu vidyāviśeṣaprāptam | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	parabhaktopayogena vidyā prāptānyatas tu yā |

	tayā prāptaṃ dhanaṃ yat tu vidyāprāptaṃ tad ucyate ||

parānyaśabdāv atrāvibhaktāpekṣayā yad vyaktyantaraṃ tatra prayuktau | bhaktasabdo 'tra dravyamātropalakṣakatayā prayuktaḥ | uktalakṣaṇayā vidyayā dhanaprāptau nimittatvam anekavidham iti nimittabhāvabhedena tatprāptaṃ dhanam apy anekavidham, tat sarvam avibhājyam iti saṃkṣepato vidyāprāptaśabdenaiva vyāsenābhihitam | tat svagranthe prapañcitum apy āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	upanyaste tu yal labdhaṃ vidyayā paṇapūrvakam |

	vidyādhanaṃ tu tad vidyād vibhāge na vibhajyate ||

	śiṣyād ārtvijyataḥ praśnāt saṃdigdhapraśnanirṇayāt |

	svajñānaśaṃsanad vādāl labdhaṃ prādhyayanāc ca yat ||

	vidhādhanaṃ tu tat prāhur vibhāge na vibhajyate |

	paraṃ nirasya yal labdhaṃ vidyāto dyūtapūrvakam ||

	vidyādhanaṃ tu tad vidyān na vibhājyaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ |

	vidyāpratijñayā labdhaṃ śiṣyād āptaṃ ca yad bhavet ||

	ṛtviṅnyāyena yal labdham etad vidyādhanaṃ bhṛguḥ |

	śilpiṣv api hi dharmo 'yaṃ mūlyād yac cādhikaṃ bhavet ||

	vidyābalakṛtaṃ caiva yājyataḥ śiṣyatas tathā |

	etad vidyādhanaṃ prāhuḥ sāmānyaṃ yad ato 'nyathā || iti |

upanyaste vargatyāgādivaicitryeṇopanyaste | śiṣyāt adhyāpanāt | ārtvijyataḥ ārtvijyakaraṇāt | praśnāt upapātakyādikṛtaprāyaścittārthapraśnāt | saṃdighapraśnanirṇayāt arthyādikṛtapraśnapratipraśnayor nirṇayāt | svajñānaśaṃsanāt agrapūjādau svajñānaprakhyāpanāt | vādāt jalpavitaṇḍādibhedāt | prādhyayanāt ghaṭikādhyayanāt |vidyātaḥ akṣahṛdayajñānādinā | vidyāpratijñayā bahuvidyāḍhyatvapratijñayā | śiṣyād āptaṃ gurupūjanārtham | ṛtviṅnyāyena labdham upadraṣṭṛtvādinā labdham | śilpiṣv api śilpividhyopajīviṣv api | ayaṃ vidyādhanavibhāgarūpo dharmo 'sti | mūlyāt bhṛteḥ yad dhanam adhikaṃ bhṛtakādhyayanādau bhavet | tathā vidyābalakṛtaṃ vidyādhikyakṛtaṃ yad viśiṣṭapūjādau bhavet | tathā vidyābalakṛtaṃ vidyādhikyakṛtaṃ yadviśiṣṭapūjādau bhavet | tathā yājyataḥ śiṣyataḥ satkārādau bhavet | tad etad vidhyādhanaṃ prātisvikaṃ prāhuḥ | ato vidyādhanād yadanyathābhūtaṃ vibhaktapitrādidravyopayogena prāptaṃ tadvibhaktānāṃ sāmānyaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ vibhājyam iti yāvat | śeṣaṃ vyaktārtham | nārado 'pi sāmānyaṃ vidyādhanam āha |

	kuṭumbaṃ bibhṛyād bhrātur yo vidyām adhigacchati |

	bhāgaṃ vidyādhanāt tasmāt sa labhetāśrito 'pi san ||

avibhaktadhanopayogena prāptavidyādhanasya vibhājyatvapradarśanārtham etat | āśrito 'pi avidyo 'īty arthaḥ | evam avibhaktapitrādigrāhitavidyālabdham api dhanaṃ vibhājyam | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	kule vinītavidyānāṃ bhrātṝṇāṃ pitṛto 'pi vā |

	śauryaprāptaṃ tu yad vittaṃ vibhājyaṃ tad bṛhaspatiḥ || iti |

avibhaktasvakule pitṛdravyādeḥ pitṛto 'pi vā śikṣitavidyānāṃ yad vittaṃ śauryādiprāptaṃ vidyayaiva prāptaṃ tat vidyādhanaṃ vibhājyaṃ bṛhaspatir abravīd ity arthaḥ | vibhājyavidyādhane bhāgādhikyam ārakasyāsti, "yena caiṣāṃ svayam ārjitaṃ syāt sa dvyaṃśam eva haret" iti vasiṣṭhasmaraṇāt | gautamas tv avibhājyavidyādhane 'pi aṃśadānam ārjakecchayāpi kvacid āha: "svayam ārjitaṃ vaidyebhyo vaidyāḥ kāmaṃ dadyāt" it | vaidyebhyaḥ vidyāvadbhyaḥ | nāradas tu icchāśūnyo na dadyād ity āha |

	vaidyo vaidyāya nākāmo dadyād aṃśaṃ svato dhanāt |

	pitṛdravyaṃ samāśritya na cet tena tad āhṛtam ||

pūrvārdhe yad dhanād iti sāmānyenoktaṃ tad avibhājyavidyādhanaviṣayam ity uttarārdhenāvagantavyam | avaidyāya sakāmo 'pi na dadyāt | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	avidyānāṃ tu vaidyena deyaṃ vidyādhanāt kvacit |

	samavidyādhikānāṃ tu deyaṃ vaidyena tad dhanam ||

avaidyānāṃ na kvacid deyam, sakāmenāpi na deyam ity arthaḥ | śauryadhanaṃ ca tenaiva nirūpitam |

	āruhya saṃśayaṃ yatra prasabhaṃ karma kurvate |

	tasmin karmaṇi tuṣṭena prasādaḥ svāminā kṛtaḥ ||

	tatra labdhaṃ tu yat kiṃcit dhanaṃ śauryeṇa tad bhavet || iti |

prasabho balātkāraḥ | anyad apy avibhājyam āha sa eva |

	dhvajāhṛtaṃ bhaved yat tu vibhājyaṃ naiva tat smṛtam | iti |

dhvajāhṛtapadapratipādyam apy uktaṃ tenaiva |

	saṃgrāmād āhṛtaṃ yat tu vidrāvya dviṣatāṃ balam |

	svāmyarthe jīvitaṃ tyaktvā tad dhvajāhṛtam ucyate ||

etad api śauryadhanaśabdenaiva vyāsenābhihitam, tadveiśeṣatvāt | kātyāyanena bhedena dhvajāhṛtasyābhidhānaṃ prapañcanārtham iti mantavyam | atrāpi vidyāprāptavad avibhājyatve pitrādyavibhaktadhanānupayogenārjanaṃ prayojakam ity avagantavyam | ata eva tadupayogenārjitaṃ viṣamavibhāgena vibhājyaṃ bhavatīty āha vyāsaḥ |

	sādhāraṇaṃ samāśritya yat kiṃcid vāhānāyudham |

	śauryādināpnoti dhanaṃ bhrātaras tatra bhāginaḥ ||

	tasya bhāgadvayaṃ deyaṃ śeṣās tu samabhāginaḥ || iti |

sādhāraṇaṃ vibhaktānāṃ dhanam | bhrātṛgrahaṇam avibhaktopalakṣaṇārtham | tasya sādhāraṇadhanāśrayād ārjitasyety arthaḥ | śauryādineti vadan anyatrāpi dhane kanyāgatavaivāhikādau sādhāraṇaṃ samāśritya vivāhena prāpte vibhājyatvaṃ darśayati | kanyāgatavaivahikayoḥ svarūpam āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	yal labdhaṃ dānakāle tu sajātyā kanyayā saha |

	kanyāgataṃ tu tad vittaṃ śuddhaṃ vṛddhikaraṃ smṛtam ||

	vaivāhikaṃ tu tad vidyāt bhāryayā yat sahāgatam |

	dhanam evaṃvidhaṃ sarvaṃ vijñeyaṃ dharmasadhakam || iti |

kanyāgataṃ kanyayā sahāgatam | strīdhanasya tu sarvavidhasyāpi avibhājyatvam āha sa eva |

	vivāhakāle yat kiṃcid varayoddiśya dīyate |

	kanyāyās tad dhanaṃ sarvam avibhājyaṃ ca bandhubhiḥ ||

	śauryaprāptaṃ vidyayā ca strīdhanaṃ caiva yat smṛtam |

	etat sarvaṃ vibhāge tu na ca vaibhājyam arthibhiḥ ||

bṛhaspatir apy avibhājyadhanam āha |

	pitāmahapitṛbhyāṃ ca dattaṃ mātrā ca yad bhavet |

	tasya tan nāpahartavyaṃ śauryabhāryādhanaṃ tathā ||

mātṛdatte tu viśeṣam āha nāradaḥ |

	mātrā ca yad dhanaṃ yasmai syāt prītipūrvakam |

	tasyāpy eṣa vidhir dṛṣṭo mātāpīṣṭe tathā pitā ||

svadhana iti śeṣaḥ | eṣa vidhiḥ pitṛdattaviṣayokto vidhiḥ | evaṃ mitradattādikam apy avibhājyam | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	pitṛdravyāvirodhena yad anyat svayam ārjitam |

	maitram audvāhikaṃ caiva mādhuparkikam eva ca || iti |

manunātra mādhuparkikasyāpy avibhājyatvam uktam | 

	pitṛdravyāvirodhena yad anyat svayam ārjitam |

ity asyārtho manunā spaṣṭīkṛtaḥ |

	anupaghnan pitṛdravyaṃ śrameṇa yad upārjayet | iti |

ubhayatra pitṛgrahaṇam avibhaktopalakṣaṇārtham | śrameṇa śramajanakena kṛṣyādineti yāvat | anupaghnan apīḍayan | vyāso 'pi |

	anāśritya pitṛdravyaṃ svaśaktyāpnoti yad dhanam |

	dāyādebhyo na tad dadyāt ................... ||

anāśritya ārjanasiddhyartham it śeṣaḥ | pitṛgrahaṇam avibhaktopalakṣaṇārtham atrāpi | prajāpatir api |

	vidyāśauryaśramair labdhaṃ strīdhanaṃ mādhuparkikam |

	maitram audvāhikaṃ bhrātuḥ bhrātṛbhir na vibhajyate ||

śramaḥ kṛṣyādiḥ | evaṃ pūrvapuruṣakramāyātaṃ parāpahṛtaṃ svaśaktyābhyuddhṛtaṃ dravyaṃ dāyādebhyo na dadyāt,

	kramād abhyāgatadravyaṃ hṛtam abhyuddharet tu yaḥ |

	dāyādebhyo na tad dadyāt .................. ||

iti yājñavalkyasmaraṇāt | dravyaṃ bhūvyatiriktam | bhūdravye 'py āha śaṅkhaḥ |

	pūrvanaṣṭāṃ tu yo bhūmim ekaś cābhyuddharet kramāt |

	yathābhāgaṃ labhante 'nye datvāṃśaṃ tu turīyakam ||

kramād abhyāgatāṃ putrapautrādīnāṃ madhye yaḥ pūrvaṃ naṣṭāṃ parāpahṛtāṃ bhūmiṃ svaśaktyābhyuddharet tasmai taccaturthāṃśaṃ datvā śeṣam uddhārakeṇa sahānye vibhajerann ity arthaḥ | kecit — abhyuddhṛtaṃ tvam eva gṛhāṇety anyānumatim antareṇābhyuddhṛtabhūmyādisarvadravyaviṣayam etad vacanam, yājñavalkyavacanaṃ tv anyānumatyābhyuddhṛtabhūmyādisarvadravyaviṣayam — iti vadanti | yad atra yuktaṃ tad grāhyam | pareṇāpahnutusya (?) tu bhūmyādidravyasyoddhāre vyāsenoktam |

	kṛte 'kṛte vā vibhāge rikthī yatra pravartate |

	sāmānyaṃ ced bhāvayati tatra bhāgaharas tu saḥ ||

parāpahnutaṃ vibhājyadhanaṃ yo rikthī sādhayati sa tatra sādhite dhane dvyaṃśī syād ity arthaḥ | anyad apy avibhājyam āha manuḥ |

	vastraṃ patram alaṃkāraṃ kṛtānnam udakaṃ striyaḥ |

	yogakṣemapracāraṃ ca na vibhājyaṃ pracakṣate ||

vastram avibhaktaprāvṛtaṃ vastram, "yac cāṅgayojitam" iti kātyāyanasmaraṇāt | patraṃ patrārūḍham ṛṇam, "dhanaṃ patraniviṣṭam" iti tenaivoktatvāt | striyo dāsyaḥ | udakaṃ svaniveśanasthakūpavāpyādyambhaḥ | yogakṣemaśabdau lokākṣiṇā vyākhyātau |

	kṣemaṃ pūrtaṃ yogam iṣṭam ity āhus tattvadarśinaḥ |

	avibhājye tu te prokte ....................... || iti |

atha vā yogakṣemārtham upāsiteśvarasakāśād yo rikthināṃ lābhaḥ sa evātra yogakṣemaśabdenocyate | pracāraśabdena gopracāra ucyate, kātyāyanena "gopracāraś ca" iti viśeṣitatvāt | atha vā pracāraśabdenāṅkaṇādikam ucyate | avibhājyaṃ pracakṣate vicārahīnāḥ kecana smṛtikārā iti śeṣaḥ | ata eva bṛhaspatiḥ |

	vastrādayo vibhājyā yair uktās tair na vicāritam |

	dhanaṃ bhavet samṛddhānāṃ patrālaṃkārasaṃśritam ||

	yuktyā vibhajanīyaṃ tad anyathānarthakaṃ bhavet || iti |

yady api vastrādāv ekasmin vastre dhāraṇāya vibhāge kriyamāṇe vastunāśaḥ | ṛṇalekhye tu tatprāmāṇyanāśaḥ | kṛtānne prabhūte vibhajyamāne svalpāśanabhoktṛviṣaye tannāśaḥ | kūpādau tu duṣkaro vibhāga iti avibhājyatvam eva bhāti, tathāpi yathā vastunāśādyanavatāraḥ tathā yuktyā vibhajanīyam, anyathā sādhāraṇatayāvasthite satyasūyayā parasparopabhogapratibandhe kasyacid apy upakārābhāvād anarthakaṃ bhaved ity arthaḥ | yuktyā vibhajanaprakāro 'pi tenaiva darśitaḥ |

	vikrīya vastrābharaṇam ṛṇam udgrāhya lekhitam |

	kṛtānnaṃ cākṛtānnena parivartya vibhajyate ||

	uddhṛtya kūpavāpyambhas tv anusāreṇa gṛhyate |

	ekāṃ strīṃ kārayet karma yathāṃśena gṛhe gṛhe ||

	bahvyaḥ samāṃśato deyā dāsānām apy ayaṃ vidhiḥ |

	yogakṣemavato lābhaḥ samatvena vibhajyate ||

	pracāraś ca yathāṃśena kartavyo rikthibhiḥ sadā || iti |

ṛṇam udgrāhya adhamarṇasakāśād ādāya | anusāreṇa svabhāgānusāreṇety arthaḥ | evaṃ ca yad uktam uśanasā |

	avibhājyaṃ sagotrāṇām ā sahasrakulād api |

	yājyañṃ kṣetraṃ ca patraṃ ca kṛtānnam udakaṃ striyaḥ || iti |

etad api anādṛtya yuktyā yājyaṃ ca kṣetraṃ ca vibhajanīyam | tathā hi — yājyasakāśād utpanno lābho vibhajanīyaḥ | kṣetraṃ tu akhiladāyādānumatyā vibhajanīyam,

	dāyādair nābhyanujñātaṃ yat kiṃcit sthāvare kṛtam |

	tat sarvam akṛtaṃ jñeyaṃ yady eko 'pi na manyate ||

iti prajāpatismaraṇāt | yat punas tenaivoktam,

	gṛhakṣetrāṇi yājyāś ca prasādo yaś ca paitṛkaḥ |

	mātṛkaś ca prasādo yaḥ tadvibhāgo na vidyate || iti |

tatra tāvad vibhāganiṣedham anādṛtyaiva yuktyā pūrvoktaprakāreṇa gṛhādikaṃ vibhajanīyam | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ,

	dṛśyamānaṃ vibhajyeta gṛhaṃ kṣetraṃ catuṣpadam |

iti gṛhāder api vibhāgam āha | pitṛprasādalabdhasya niṣedho 'pi sthāvare 'nādṛtya eva,

	pitṛprasādāt sidhyanti vastrāṇy ābharaṇāni ca |

	sthāvarāṇi na sidhyanti prasāde paitṛke sati ||

iti yājñavalkyasmaraṇāt | yat punas tenaiva smṛtam,

	loke rikthavibhāge 'pi na kaścit prabhutām iyāt |

	bhoga eva tu kartavyo na dānaṃ na ca vikrayaḥ || iti |

loke kulakramāyāte sthāvarādau na kaścit pitrādir api rikthavibhāge, apiśabdāt vikrayādāv api na prabhutām iyāt | tena tatra dāyādānumatim antareṇa na vibhāgavikrayadānāni kuryād iti tasyārthaḥ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām avibhājyanirūpaṇam **

**atha putrapautrādivibhāgviṣayāṇi kānicid vacanāni likhyante**

tatra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	pramītapitṛkāṇāṃ tu pitṛto bhāgakalpanā | iti |

pramītā avibhaktāḥ pitaro yeṣāṃ bhrātṝṇāṃ te pramītapitṛkāḥ | teṣāṃ pitṛto bhāgakalpanā | pitṛdvāreṇaiva pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahadravyavibhāgakalpanā, na punaḥ svarūpeṇety arthaḥ | pitṛto bhāgakalpanāyāṃ ko viśeṣa ity apekṣite bṛhaspatiḥ |

	tatputrā vixamasamāḥ pitṛbhāgaharāḥ smrtāḥ | iti |

tatputrāḥ pramītapitṛkāṇām ekaikasya putrā viṣamasamāḥ nyūnādhikasaṃkhyākāḥ svaṃ svaṃ paitṛkaṃ bhāgam eva labhanta ity arthaḥ | etad uktaṃ bhavati: kasyacit pramītasya pitur eka eva putraḥ, kasyacit dvau putrau, kascacid bahavaḥ tatra yathaikaḥ svapitṛbhāgaharaḥ tathaiva dvāv api svapitṛbhāgamātrahatau | tathaiva bahavo 'pi svapitṛbhāgamātraharāḥ smṛtā iti | yady api pitṛbhāgamātraharatve naikapitṛkāṇāṃ pitṛto bhāgakalpanā svāmyānanurūpā, tathāpi vācanikatvād anumantavyā | yadā sasutayor avibhaktayor bhrātroḥ madhye kaścid bhrātā mṛtaḥ tatsutas tu pitāmahād apy aprāptāṃśakaḥ, pitāmaho 'pi nasīt, tadā kātyāyana āha |

	avibhakte 'nuje prete tatsutaṃ rikthabhāginam |

	kurvīta jīvanaṃ yena labdhaṃ naiva pitāmahāt ||

	labhetāṃśaṃ sa pitryaṃ tu pitṛvyāt tasya vā sutāt || iti |

jīvanaṃ dāyadhanam | anujagrahaṇaṃ mṛtabhrātur upalakṣaṇārtham | asminn eva viṣaye yadā pramītasya sutā bahavaḥ tadāpy āha sa eva |

	sa evāṃśas tu sarveṣāṃ bhrātṝṇāṃ nyāyato bhavet | iti |

nyāyato bhavet, "samaṃ syād aśrutatvāt" iti nyāyena mithaḥ samabhāgatayā bhaved ity arthaḥ | yad aparaṃ sa evāha |

	labheta tatsuto vāpi nivṛttiḥ parato bhavet | iti |

tasyāyam arthaḥḹ tasya vibhājyadhanasvāmipautrasya suto 'pi vā svapitur abhāve tadbhāgaṃ labheta, atha tasyāpy abhāvaḥ kiṃ tu tatsutād eva vidyamānatvaṃ tadā tu mṛtabhrātṛsantatau vṛddhaprapitāmahadhanabhāgagrahaṇanivṛttir iti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> prapautrasya prapitāmahadhanagrahaṇam api na ghaṭate, janmanā pitṛpitāmahayor eva dhane putrapautrayor eva svatvasiddhiniyamāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span>, yathā putrāder mātṛdhane piṇḍaṃ datvā tadaiva mātur ūrdhvaṃ svatvasiddhiḥ jīvanakriyayā bhavatīti vakṣyate tathā prapitāmahadhane prapautrasyāpi svatvasiddhir iti yuktam uktam "labheta tatsuto vāpi" iti | evaṃ ca yo yasya dhanasvāminaḥ pramītasya pitṛtvena pitāmahatvena vā piṇḍadātā tasya taddhanabhāgitvaṃ dhanasvāminaḥ saṃtatyantare saty api vidyata ity avagantavyam | ata eva devalaḥ |

	samam icchanti piṇḍānāṃ dāyārthasya vibhājanam | iti |

ā caturthād dāyārthasya vibhāgaṃ piṇḍadātṛtvaṃ ca manvādaya icchantīty arthaḥ | tathā ca sa eva |

	avibhaktavibhaktānāṃ kulyānāṃ vasatāṃ saha |

	bhūyo dāyavibhāgaḥ syād ā caturthād iti sthitiḥ ||

	tāvat kulyāḥ sapiṇḍāḥ syuḥ piṇḍabhedas tataḥ param | iti |

avibhaktavibhaktānām avibhaktadhanānāṃ vibhinnasaṃtatijātānāṃ kūṭasthakulyānāṃ bhūyaś ciraṃ sahavasatām ā caturthāt kūṭasthaprapautraparyantaṃ dāyadhanavibhāgaḥ syād ity anekasaṃtatikadāyavibhāgamaryādeyam ity arthaḥ | jīvatpitṛkasya punaḥ pitrā saha kathaṃ paitāmahadhanavibhāga ity apekṣite kātyāyanaḥ |

	paitāmahaṃ samānaṃ syāt pituḥ putrasya cobhayoḥ | iti |

vyāso 'pi |

	kramāyāte gṛhakṣetre putrapautrāḥ samāṃśinaḥ | iti |

bṛhaspatir api |

	dravye pitāmahopātte jaṅgame sthāvare 'pi vā |

	samam aṃśitvam ākhyātaṃ pituḥ putrasya caiva hi ||

yājñavalkyaḥ |

	bhūr yā pitāmahopāttā nibandho dravyam eva vā |

	tatra syāt sadṛśaṃ svāmyaṃ pituḥ putrasya cobhayoḥ ||

nibandhaḥ karatayā yācakādibhiḥ paṇyadiṣu gṛhyamāṇo 'ṃśaḥ | sadṛśaṃ svāmyaṃ syād ity anayaiva vacobhaṅgyā samāṃśatvam evoktam iti mantavyam | anyathā pūrvoktavacanasamānārthatā svarasato yuktā na syāt | evaṃ ca jīvadvibhāge pitāmahādidhanaviṣaye viṣamavibhāgo na kadācid apīti mantavyam | svārjitadhanaviṣaye tu viṣamavibhāgo 'pi yugāntare kadācid astīti jīvadvibhāgaprakaraṇe 'bhihitam | kecid yathāśrutārthatām eva cāsya vacanasyāṅgīkkurvanti | tathā ca pautramātrecchayāpi pitāmahadhanavibhāgo bhavati | pitur icchāmātreṇa ca kramāyātadhanadānādikaṃ na bhavati, tatra pautrasyāpi svāmyābhidhānād ity āhuḥ | tad atrāpi grāhyam, āñjasatvāt, "arthe paitāmahe pitṛputryos tulyaṃ svāmyam" iti viṣṇunāpy uktatvāt | atrārthād atulyaṃ svāmyaṃ pitṛputrayoḥ pitṛdhana iti gamyate | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> paitāmahe paitṛke ca janmanaiva svāmyam iti kā tatra tulyātulyatā | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span>: paitāmahe dhane pitṛputrayoḥ svāmye svātantryam eva tulyatā | paitṛke tu jīvati pitari nirdoṣe tasyaiva svātantryam ity atulyatā | anenaiva bhedena svāmye tulyātylyoktiḥ | yat tu katyāyanenoktam,

	svayaṃ copārjite pitrā na putraḥ svāmyam arhati |

iti, etat putramātrecchayā paitṛkadhanavibhānarhatāṃ (?) vacobhaṅgyā vakti, na punar yathāśrutārthaparam ity anavadyam | vyāsena tu spaṣṭam evoktam |

	paitṛke na vibhāgarhāḥ putrāḥ pitur anicchataḥ | iti |

yat punar bṛhaspatinoktam,

	paitāmahaṃ hṛtaṃ pitrā svaśaktyā yad upārjitam |

	vidyāśauryādināvāptaṃ tatra svāmyaṃ pituḥ smṛtam ||

iti, tatrāpi svāmyam ity anena vacobhaṅgyā pituḥ svātantryam uktam iti mantavyam | svātantryābhidhānasya prayojanam apy āha sa eva |

	pradānaṃ svecchayā kuryād bhogaṃ kuryāt tato dhanāt |

	tadabhāve tu tanayāḥ samāṃśāḥ parikīrtitāḥ || iti |

sutānumatim antareṇāpi pituḥ svātantryabalād dānādikaṃ jīvadvibhāgoktaviṣayaviśeṣe viṣamavibhāgakalpanaṃ ca yujyata iti tātparyārthaḥ | svārjitaprāyaṃ yat kramāyātam, yac ca svārjitaṃ pitṛdhanaṃ tadvibhāge putrair balādkāro na kārya iti vacobhaṅgyāha kātyāyanaḥ |

	svaśaktyāpahṛtaṃ naṣṭaṃ svayam āptaṃ ca yad bhavet |

	etat sarvaṃ pitā putrair vibhāge naiva dāpyate ||

yat parair apahṛtaṃ kramāyātaṃ svaśaktyaivoddhṛtam, yad vinaṣṭaṃ vā kramāyātaṃ svenaiva labdham, yac ca vidyāśauryādinā svayam evārjitam etat sarvaṃ pitā vibhāge putrair na dāpya ity arthaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ putrapautrādivibhāgakalpanāviṣayāṇi**

**atha strīdhanavibhāgaviṣayāṇi**

tatrādau tāvat strīdhanabhedān āha manuḥ |

	adhyagnyadhyāvahanikaṃ dattaṃ ca prītikarmaṇi |

	bhrātṛmātṛpitṛprāptaṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ strīdhanaṃ smṛtam ||

atra pūrvārdhasyārthaḥ kātyāyanena vivṛtaḥ |

	vivāhakāle yat strībhyo dīyate hy agnisaṃnidhau |

	tad adhyagnikṛtaṃ sadbhiḥ strīdhanaṃ parikīrtitam ||

	yat punar labhate nārī nīyamānā pitur gṛhāt |

	adhyāvahanikaṃ caiva strīdhanaṃ tad udāhṛtam ||

	prītyā dattaṃ tu yat kiṃcit śvaśrvā va śvaśureṇa vā |

	pādavandanikaṃ caiva prītidattaṃ tad ucyate || iti |

pādavandanikaṃ pādavandanāvasare dattam | bhrātṛmātṛpitṛprāptaṃ yadā kadā vā jīvanartham iti śeṣaḥ | ṣaḍvidhagrahaṇam uttarārdhoktam eva strīdhanam iti bhramāpanuttyarthaṃ kṛtam, na punar avadhāraṇārtham | ata eva,

	mātāpitṛpatibhrātṛdattam adhyagnyupāgatam |

	ādhivedanikādyaṃ ca ............... ||

iti yājñavalkyenādyagrahaṇaṃ kṛtam | viṣṇunā tu ṣaḍvidhād adhikam uktam: "pitṛmātṛsutabhrātṛdattam adhyagnyupāgatam adhivedanikaṃ bandhudattaṃ śulkam anvādheyikaṃ strīdhanam" iti | ādhivedanikam adhivedananimittam | bandhudattam ity atra bandhuśabdaḥ pūrvoktapitrādivyatiriktabandhuṣu gobalīvardanyāyād vartate | śulkānvādheyikayoḥ svarūpaṃ kātyāyanenoktam |

	gṛhopaskāravāhyānāṃ dohyābharaṇakarmiṇām |

	mūlyaṃ labdhaṃ tu yat kiṃcic chulkaṃ tat parikīrtitam ||

	vivāhāt parato yat tu labdhaṃ bhartṛkulāt striyā |

	bhartuḥ pitroḥ sakāśād vā anvādheyaṃ tu tad bhṛguḥ || iti |

mūlyaṃ gṛhopaskarādimūlyam labdhaṃ kanyādhanatvena varādisakāśāt kanyārhaṇopādhitayeti śeṣaḥ | pitṛmātrādibhiḥ striyai jīvanārthadānaviṣaye viśeṣam āha sa eva |

	pitṛmātṛpatibhrātṛjñātibiḥ strīdhanaṃ striyai |

	yathāśaktyā dvisāhasrād dātavyaṃ sthāvarād ṛte ||

yathāśakti sthāvaravyatiriktadvisāhasrakārṣāpaṇaparyantaṃ dātavyam ity arthaḥ | vyāso 'pi |

	dvisāhasraḥ paṇo dāyaḥ striyai deyo dhanasya ca | iti |

dīyata iti dāyaḥ | paraḥ paramaḥ | evaṃ ca dvisahasrakārṣāpaṇādhikamūlyo dhanasya bhāgo jīvanārtham ṛddhenāpi na deya iti gamyate | striyai deya ity atra pratyabdam iti vidheyasaṃkhyā yogyatābalād gamyate | striyai deya ity atra pratyabdam iti vidheyasaṃkhyā yogyatābalād gamyate | pratyabdam asakṛdarpaṇe niyamo 'yam | anekābdeṣūpajīvanārthaṃ sakṛd eva dāne tu nayam avidhiniyamo nāpi sthāvaraparyudāsaḥ | yat tūtsavādāv eva dhāryam ity evamādyupādhinālaṃkārādikaṃ dattam, yac ca dāyādadivañcanārthaṃ dattam, tat strīdhanaṃ na bavatīty āha kātyayanaḥ |

	yat tu sopādhikaṃ dattaṃ yac ca yogavaśena vā |

	pitrā brātrātha vā patyā na tat strīdhanam iṣyate ||

yogavaśena vañcanādyupāyata evety arthaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanū</span>pādhiyogayor abhāve 'pi pitrādinā dattaṃ na strīdhanaṃ bhavitum arhati,

	bhāryā putraś ca dāsaś ca nirdhanāḥ sarva eva te |

	yat te samadhigacchanti yasyaite tasya tad dhanam ||

iti smaraṇāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>, putrādisāhacaryān nānena paramārthato nirdhanatvaṃ bhāryāyā gamyate, kiṃ tu dhanavyayādāv asvātantryamātram | tena yasya ete tasyānujñayā svadhanasyāpi viniyogaṃ bhāryādayaḥ kuryur iti smṛtivākyatātparyam avaseyam | ata eva coktaṃ manunā |

	na nirhāraṃ striyaḥ kuryuḥ kuṭumbād bahumadhyagāt |

	svakād api ca vittād dhi svasyā bhartur anājñayā ||

svatantrānanujñyā paratantrāḥ striyaḥ strīpuṃsasādhāraṇavittād ātmīyavittād vā tyāgabhogādikaṃ na kuryur ity arthaḥ | atha vā, nirdhanatvādhidhāyakasmṛtivākyasya śilpādiprāptadhanaviṣayatvaṃ vijñeyam | tad āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	prāptaṃ śiklpais tu yad vittaṃ prītyā caiva yad anyataḥ |

	bhartuḥ svāmyaṃ tadā tatra śeṣaṃ tu strīdhanaṃ smṛtam ||

anyataḥ sakhyāditaḥ, pitrāditaḥ prāptasya strīdhanatvena śeṣakoṭitvāt ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ strīdhanabhedāḥ **

**atha strīdhanakṛtyam**

tatra vyāsaḥ |

	yac ca bhartrā dhanaṃ dattaṃ sā yathākāmam aśnuyāt | iti |

caśabdāt "saudāyikaṃ yathākāmam" iti vadan bhartṛdāyādau svātantryaṃ darśayati | kātyāyano 'pi |

	saudāyikaṃ dhanaṃ yat tu strīṇāṃ svātantryam iṣyate |

	tasmāt tad ānṛśaṃsyārthaṃ tair dattam upajīvanam ||

	saudāyike sadā strīṇāṃ svātantryaṃ parikīrtitam |

	vikraye caiva dāne ca yatheṣṭaṃ sthāvareṣv api ||

	bhartṛdāyaṃ mṛte patyau vinyaset strī yatheṣṭataḥ |

	vidyamāne tu saṃrakṣet ...................... || iti |

dvitīyaślokena saudāyikākhyastrīdhane patyau vidyamāne 'py avidamāne 'pi svātantryam uktam, sadety abhidhānāt | bhartṛdāyo bhartṛdattam, tasmin dhane tu tadanantaroktapādatrayenāvidyamāne patyau svātantyam uktam | vidyamāne tu saṃrakṣet bhartṛdattaṃ bhartrājñayā vinyased ity arthaḥ | saudāyikapadaṃ tenaiva nirūpitam |

	ūḍhayā kanyayā vāpi patyuḥ pitṛgṛhe 'pi vā |
