	bhrātuḥ sakāśāt pitror vā labdhaṃ saudāyikaṃ smṛtam ||

labdha dhanam iti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca vyasaḥ |

	yat kanyayā vivāhe ca vivāhāt parataś ca yat |

	pitṛbhartṛgṛhāt prāptaṃ dhanaṃ sodāyikaṃ smṛtam || iti |

etadvacanadvayenaitad uktaṃ bhavati | vāgdānaprabhṛti patigṛhapraveśarūpotsavasamāptiparyantaṃ pitṛgṛhe patigṛhe vā pitṛmātṛpakxata eva striyā labdhaṃ yautakādi dhanaṃ saudāyikaśabdābhidheyam iti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> "yautakādi tu yad deyaṃ sudāyaḥ" iti nighaṇṭupāṭhāt kathaṃ saudāyikaśabdo 'tra prayuktaḥ | svārthataddhitāntatayety anavadyam | bhartṛdāye tu mṛte bhartari na sthāvare svātantryam | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	bhartrā prītena yad dattaṃ striyai tasmin mṛte 'pi tat |

	sā yathākāmam aśnīyād dadyād vā sthāvarād ṛte ||

bhartari mṛte 'pi na taddattasthāvare svātantryam ity arthaḥ | yathākāmam ity anena svātantryam uktam | evaṃ ca saudāyike sthāvaretaraprītidatte ca strīṇāṃ svātantryam anyatra tu strīdhane 'py asvātantryam iti mantavyam | puruṣāṇāṃ tu strīdhane sarvatrāsvātantryam eva | yad āha katyayanaḥ |

	na bhartā naiva ca suto na pitā bhrātaro na ca |

	ādāne ca visarge vā strīdhane parbhaviṣṇavaḥ ||

svāmitvābhāvād ity abhiprāyaḥ | ata evānantaram uktaṃ tenaiva |

	yadi hy ekataro 'py eṣāṃ strīdhanaṃ bhakṣayed balāt |

	savṛddhikaṃ pradāpyaḥ syād daṇḍaṃ caiva samāpnuyāt ||

	tad eva yady anujñāpya bhakṣayet prītipūrvakam |

	mūlyam eva pradāpyaḥ syāt yady asau dhanavān bhavet || iti |

dhanavān yadi bhaved ity abhidhānāt mūlyamātram api nirdhano na dāpya ity arthāt gamyate | anujñāpya bhakṣaṇe 'pi mūlyapradānābhidhānāt bhartrādīnām asvātantryam agagamyate, na punaḥ pāratantryamātram | evaṃ ca vivāhena bhāryāyā bhartṛdhane nityapāratantryaṃ svāmitvaṃ saṃpadyate, na punar bhartuḥ bhāryādhane tādṛśam apīty avagantavyam | ata eva bhartuḥ strīdhanabhoge 'py anarhatām āha devalaḥ |

	vṛttir ābharaṇaṃ śulkaṃ lābhaś ca strīdhanaṃ bhavet |

	bhoktrī tat svayam evedaṃ patir nārhaty anāpadi ||

	vṛthā mokṣe ca bhoge ca striyai dadyāt savṛddhikam | iti |

vṛttiḥ vartanārthaṃ pitrādinā dattam | labhyata iti lābhaḥ | etad uktaṃ bhavati: pārvatyādiprītyarthaṃ vratādau striyā yal labhyate tad api strīdhanam iti | svayam evety evakāraḥ svāpatyānāṃ vyudāsārthaḥ | bhartṛvyudāsasya patir nārhatīty anena siddhatvāt | bhartur vyudāse tato bahiraṅgabhrātrādivyudāsasya daṇḍāpūpanyāyasiddhatvāt | vṛthā āpadaṃ vinety arthaḥ | mokṣas tyāgaḥ | striyānanujñātabalātkārarahitatyāgabhogaviṣayam etat, savṛddhikapradānasya daṇḍāsahitasyābhidhānāt | patir nārhatīty anapadīti vadan āpadi tu patir evārhati strīdhanaṃ bhoktuṃ nānya iti darśayati | ata eva,

	putrārtiharaṇe vāpi strīdhanaṃ bhoktum arhati |

ity anantaravacane bhoktum arhatīty atra patir iti śeṣo draṣṭavyaḥ | putragrahaṇaṃ svakuṭumbopalakṣaṇārtham | ārtiḥ dhanālābhanimittato durapanodātra vivakṣitā | tasyāḥ haraṇe parihareṇe | vāśabdād anyatrāpi dhanālābhanimittato duṣparihare mahāsaṅkaṭe strīdhanam ananujñātam api patir bhoktuṃ tyaktuṃ vārhatītyuktam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> paradhanatyāgabhoge parasya svāmyanujñayā vinā katham arhatā | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span>: svāmyanujñābhāve 'pi pūrvoktaviṣaye svādhīnajanasvāmyake tu strīdhane yatheṣṭaviniyogānarhe 'py āpadapanodakatyāgabhogādāv arhatāstīty asmād eva vacanāt kalpyata ity adoṣaḥ | atra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	durbhikṣe dharmakārye ca vyādhau saṃpratirodhake |

	gṛhītaṃ strīdhanaṃ bhartā na striyai dātum arhati ||

dharmakārye nitye naimittike ca kāmye 'pi | kvacic chāntike grahayajñādau | saṃpratirodhake dhanadānaṃ vinā nivārayitum aśakye dhanikāsedhādau | gṛhītaṃ strīdhanam, gatyantarābhāveneti śeṣaḥ | bhartā pratidānasamarthadhanābhāvena daridraḥ iti śeṣaḥ, sati saṃbhave pratidānasyātrāvaśyakatāt | ata eva pratidānasya kvacid evāvaśyakatvam uktaṃ kātyāyanena |

	vyādhitaṃ vyasanasthaṃ ca dhanikair vopapīḍitam |

	jñātvā nisṛṣṭaṃ yat prītyā dadyād ātmecchayā tu saḥ ||

jñātvā striyeti śeṣaḥ | nisṛṣṭam anujñātam | yady apīdaṃ vacanaṃ "na bhartā naiva ca sutaḥ" ityādivacanatrayānantaryato bhartrādiviṣayam iti pratibhāti, tathāpi,

	atha cet sa dvibhāryaḥ syān na ca tām bhajate punaḥ |

	prītyā nisṛṣṭam api cet pratidāpyaḥ sa tadbalāt ||

	grāsācchādanavāsānām ācchedo yatra yoṣitaḥ |

	tatra svam ādadīta strī ............... ||

ity uparitanavacanaparyālocanayā bhartrekaviṣayam iti mantavyam | yā punar atiduṣṭā strī sā svadhanam api viniyoktuṃ nārhatīty āha sa eva |

	apakārakriyāyuktā nirmaryādārthanāśikā |

	vyabhicāraratā yā ca strīdhanaṃ na ca sārhati ||

svecchayā viniyoktum iti śeṣaḥ | bhartrāśrutaṃ strīdhanaṃ tv agṛhītam api deyam,

	bhartrā pratiśrutaṃ deyam ṛṇavat strīdhanaṃ sutaiḥ |

iti tenaivoktatvāt | sutagrahaṇaṃ pautrasyāpy upalakṣaṇam ṛṇavad ity abhidhānāt | anenāpi strīdhane sutādīnāṃ nāsti svāmyam iti gamyate | tataś ca strīdhane jīvadvibhāgo nasty eva stryekasvāmikatvāt | ata eva manuḥ |

	jīvantīnāṃ tu tāsāṃ ye tad dhareyuḥ svabāndhavāḥ |

	tān śiṣyāc coradaṇḍena dhārmikaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ ||

	patyau jīvati yaḥ strībhir alaṃkāro dhṛto bhavet |

	na taṃ bhajeran dāyādāḥ bhajamānāḥ patanty adhaḥ || iti |

ghṛtaḥ sātatyeneti śeṣaḥ | sātatyena dhṛte yogopādhirāhityena strīdhananiścayo bhavati | pūrvārdhasya ca niścitastrīdhanakathanārthatvāt sātatyeneti śeṣeṇa bhāvyam iti gamyate | dāyādā duhitrādayaḥ |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ strīdhanakṛtyam**

**atha strīdvārāgatadhanavibhāgaḥ**

tatra tāvad āgamanaprakāram āha manuḥ |

	anvādheyaṃ ca yad dattaṃ patyā prītena caiva yat |

	patyau jīvati vṛttāyāṃ prajāyās tad dhanaṃ bhavet ||

anvādheyaṃ vivāhād ūrdhvaṃ striyā bhartṛkulāt pitṛkulāc ca labdham,

	vivāhāt parato yat tu labdhaṃ bhartṛkulāt striyā |

	anvādheyaṃ tu tad dravyaṃ labdhaṃ pitṛkulāt tathā ||

iti kātyāyanasmaraṇāt | vivāhāt parata ity anenānvādheyapadasthānuśabdārtho vivṛtaḥ | labdham ity anena tatrasthādheyaśabdārtha iti mantavyam | yad anvadheyam, yac ca prītena patyaiva dattaṃ tad dvividhaṃ strīdhanaṃ dhanasvāminyāṃ mṛtāyām anantarakṣaṇavartinyāḥ strīpuṃsaprajāyāḥ svaṃ bhaved ity arthaḥ | etad uktaṃ bhavati: saprajastrīdhanaṃ dhanasvāmimaraṇānatarakṣaṇajīvanaśālitve 'pi na patyur bhavati, kiṃ tu tacchālinyāḥ prajāyā iti | evaṃ cāsmād idam avagamyate: dhanasvāmina ūrdhvaṃ dhanāgamane dhanasvāmimaraṇāntarakṣaṇajīvanakriyaiva dhanagrahaṇādhikāritayā dharmaśātrapratipāditajanasya svatvāpattikāraṇam iti | tena yatra yatra dhanasvāmina ūrdhvam eva dhanāgamanam aputrasvaryātadhanadau tatra tatra rikthagrāhiṇaḥ svatvāpattāv idam eva kāraṇaṃ kalpyam | prajāyā iti sāmānyenābhidhānād atra strīpuṃsaprajāyā uktadvividharikthagrahaṇādhikāraḥ samasamaya eva jñāyata iti | svatvāpattir api tathaiva, na punaḥ pūrvaṃ bhaginīnāṃ tadabhāve bhrātṝṇāṃ bhavatīti mantavyam | vibhāgo 'py atra bhrātṛbhaginīkartṛko vijñeyaḥ | evaṃ ca yad uktam,

	jananyāṃ saṃsthitāyāṃ tu sarvaṃ sarve sahodarāḥ |

	bhajeran mātṛkaṃ rikthaṃ bhaginyaś ca sanābhayaḥ ||

iti, tat svoktānvādheyādidvividharikthaviṣayam iti mantavyam | asminn eva viṣaye veśeṣam āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	strīdhanaṃ syād apatyānāṃ duhitā ca tadaṃśinī |

	aprattā cet samuḍhā tu labhate sā na mātṛkam ||

apatyānāṃ putrāpatyānām | vacanadvaye 'pītaretarayoge caśabdaḥ, tenātretaretarayuktānāṃ vibhāgakartṛtvaṃ vijñeyam | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	bhaginyo bāndhavaiḥ sārdhaṃ vibhajeran sabhartṛkāḥ | iti |

bāndhavaiḥ sahodarair bhrātṛbhir ity arthaḥ | sabhartṛkā iti viśeṣaṇaṃ vidhavānivṛttyartham | na punaḥ kanyānivṛttyartham, pūrvoktavacanavirodhāt | sahodarabhrātṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ bhāgaharā bhaginyo yās tāḥ prakṛtyāha manuḥ |

	yās tāsāṃ syur duhitaras tāsām api yathārhataḥ |

	mātāmahyā dhanāt kiṃcit pradeyaṃ prītipūrvakam ||

yathārhataḥ śīlopayogadāridryādyapekṣayety arthaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> duhitṛduhitṝṇāṃ bhrātṛbhaginīsadbhāve mātāmahīdhane svācitvābhāvāt kim iti kiṃcit pradīyate | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span>: yathā paitṛke dhane kanyānāṃ dāyārhatvābhāve 'pi vacanāt tābhyas turīyāṃśo bhrātṛbhir dīyate, tathātra svāmitvābhāve 'pi bhrātṛbhaginībhir vacanabalāt kiṃcid dīyate | iyāṃs tu bhedaḥ: tatra dāyānarhatve 'pi janmanā svāmyam astīty abhisaṃdhāya "patitāḥ syur aditsavaḥ" iti doṣakīrtanād avaśyaṃ dātavyam, iha tu svāmitvam api nāstīty abhisaṃdhāya prītipūrvakam iti svavacanāt prītau satyāṃ deyam, no cen na deyam iti | anyat kiṃcin mātṛkaṃ riktham aprattānām eva na punaḥ sarvāsāṃ duhitṛsodaraprajānāṃ bhavatīty āha sa eva |

	mātus tu yautakaṃ yat syāt kumārībhāga eva saḥ | iti |

yautakaṃ samānāsanopaveśanapratyāsannayor vadhūvarayor vivāhādau yena kenacit samarpitaṃ dhanam,

	tadvadhūvarayor deyaṃ yutayor yautakaṃ matam | 

iti nighaṇṭukāroktatvāt | anyonyānvitayor vadhūvarayor yad deyaṃ tad dhanaṃ yutayor idam iti vyutpattyā yautakaṃ matam ity arthaḥ | devasvāmī tu, "pitṛgṛhāl labdhaṃ bhartṛgṛhāl labdhāpekṣayā pṛthakdhanatayā mātur yautakaṃ mātṛdhanaṃ mātur eva" ity āha | tac cintyaṃ pakṣadvayasyāpi kalpanāmātratvāt | kumārīṇām anekatve "samaṃ syād aśrutatvāt" iti nyāyena yautakavibhāgaḥ kāryaḥ bhāgaviśeṣāsmṛteḥ | evam uktaṃ trividhavyatiriktaṃ mātṛkaṃ rikthaṃ kumārīṇām akumārīṇām apy apratiṣṭitānām eva, na punaḥ sarvāsāṃ duhitṝṇām ity āha gautamaḥ: "strīdhanaṃ duhitṝṇām aprattānām apratiṣṭhitānāṃ ca" iti | adhyagnyādi strīdhanaṃ kumārīṇām apratiṣṭhitānām anūḍhānāṃ ca duhitṝṇām evety arthaḥ | tataś ca tad dhanaṃ tā eva duhitaro vibhajerann ity abhiprāyaḥ | apratiṣṭhitā anapatyā nirdhanāḥ durbhagāḥ vidhavā vā | evam aparārkānusāreṇa gautamavacanaṃ vyākhyātam | asya vijñāneśvarakṛtā vyākhyā heyā, svabuddhimātreṇādhyāhārādikaraṇāt | asminn eva viṣaye viśeṣam āha yājñavalkyaḥ: "mātur duhitaraḥ śeṣam ṛṇāt" iti | mātṛṛṇāpākaraṇāvaśiṣṭaṃ mātṛkaṃ rikthaṃ mātur ūrdhvaṃ samam aprattāpratiṣṭhitaduhitaro vibhajerann ity arthaḥ | evaṃbhūtaduhitrabhāve 'py āha sa eva: "tābhya ṛte 'nvayaḥ" iti | etad eva nāradaḥ spaṣṭayati: "abhāve duhitṝṇāṃ tadanvayaḥ" iti | aprattaduhitṛṣv anvayāsaṃbhavāt prattaduhitranvaya iti pāriśeṣyād avagamyate | strīgāmidhanatvāt strīrūpānvaya iti ca gamyate | prattaduhitṝṇāṃ strīrūpānvayābhāve dauhitrāṇāṃ yathā syād iti sāmānyena tadanvaya ity uktam | dautrāṇām apy abhāve tu,

	vibhajeran sutāḥ pitror ūrdhvaṃ riktham ṛṇaṃ samam |

iti yājñavalkyavacanataḥ mātur ūrdhvaṃ mātṛkaṃ rikthaṃ mātṛkṛtaṃ ca ṛṇaṃ samaṃ sutā vibhajerann ity avagamāt sutānāṃ mātṛṛṇadhanavibhāgakartṛtvaṃ siddham, anyathā "vibhajeran sutāḥ pitroḥ" ity ekaśeṣoktir apārthikā syāt | sutānām apy abhāve pautrāṇāṃ pitāmahīṛṇadhanabhoktṛtvam "putrapaitrai ṛṇaṃ deyam" iti pautrāṇām api pitāmahīkṛtaṛṇāpākaraṇādhikārāt, "rikthabhājaḥ ṛṇaṃ prakuryuḥ" it smaraṇāc ca | bhinnapitṛkāṇāṃ viṣamasaṃkhyānāṃ pautrāṇāṃ samavāye pitāmahīṛṇadhanavibhāgaḥ pitāmahadhanavibhāgavat "pitṛto bhāgakalpanā", evam eva bhinnamātṛkāṇāṃ dauhitrāṇāṃ dauhitīṇāṃ ca viṣamasaṃkhyānāṃ samavāye mātṛto bhagakalpanā | atra "pratimātṛ svavarge bhāgaveśeṣaḥ" iti gautamasmaraṇāt | yat tu kātyāyanenoktam,

	duhitṛṇām abhāve tu rikthaṃ putreṣu tad bhavet |

iti, tad aprattaduhitṛviṣayam | tatra ṛtukālabhartror asaṃbhavenānvayāsaṃbhavāt | evaṃ ca kātyāyanenoktaṃ yautakaviṣayam iti mantavyam | bhāryāyā ūrdhvam anvayābhāve bhartari bhāryārikthaṃ bhavet,

	aprajaḥ strīdhanaṃ bhartuḥ brāhmādiṣu caturṣv api |

iti yājñavalkyasmaraṇāt | apiśabdāt gāndharve 'pi | ata eva manuḥ |

	brāhmadaivārṣagāndharvaprājāpatyeṣu yad dhanam |

	atītāyām aprajasi bhartur eva tad iṣyate ||

uktapañcavivāheṣu saṃskṛtāyāḥ bhāryāyā yad dhanaṃ tat tasyāḥ duhitrādipautrāntadhanahārisaṃtater abhāve saty atītāyāḥ bhartur eveṣyate, na punar mātrādīnāṃ bandhūnām ity arthaḥ | yat tu kātyāyanenoktam,

	bandhudattaṃ tu bandhūnām abhāve bhartṛgāmi tat |

iti, tat uktapañcavidhetaravivāhasaṃskṛtastrīdhanaviṣayam | tathā ca sa eva |

	āsurādiṣu yal labdhaṃ strīdhanaṃ paitṛkaṃ striyāḥ |

	abhāve tadapatyānāṃ mātāpitros tad iṣyate ||

paitṛkaṃ mātāpitṛsakāśād dānenāgatam | tadapatyānām abhāve āsurādiṣu saṃskṛtastriyām utpannāpatyānām abhāve | apatyagrahaṇaṃ pūrvoktadauhitrādipautrāntānāṃ strīdhanahāriṇām upalakṣaṇārtham | yat tu yamenoktam,

	āsurādiṣu yad dravyaṃ vivāheṣu pradīyate |

	aprajāyām atītāyāṃ pitaiva tu dhanaṃ haret ||

iti, tatra pradīyate pitreti śeṣo draṣṭavyaḥ | tataś ca na pūrvoktavacanavirodhaḥ | evaṃ pitṛvyabhrātṛmātulādibandhudattaṃ strīdhanaṃ sati saṃbhave pitṛvyādibandhūnām, anyathā bhartur evety āsurādiṣv avagantavyam | kiṃcid bandhudattaṃ na dātur bhavatīty āha gautamaḥ: "bhaginīśulkaḥ sodaryāṇām ūrdhvaṃ mātuḥ" iti, śulkākhyaṃ strīdhanaṃ pūrvataraprakaraṇe nirūpitam, taddātāro varādayaḥ, teṣāṃ dātṛtve 'pi taddhanaṃ na bhavati, kiṃ tu dhanasvāmitvaṃ sodarabhrātṝṇām, teṣām abhāve tanmātur bhavatīty arthaḥ | yat punar arhatīty anuvṛttau śaṅkhenoktam: "svaṃ ca śulkaṃ voḍhā" iti, tat aparisamāpte vivāhe sati mṛtāyāṃ vadhvāṃ draṣṭavyam | "mṛtāyāṃ dattam ādadyāt" iti yājñavalkyasmaraṇāt | dattaṃ śulkam alaṃkārādikaṃ vā ādadyāt voṣheti śeṣaḥ | kanyādhanaṃ pray āha bodhāyanaḥ |

	rikthaṃ mṛtāyāḥ kanyāyāḥ gṛhṇīyuḥ sodarāḥ svayam |

	tadabhāve bhaven mātus tadabhāve pitur bhavet ||

gauṇamātṛparigaṇanapūrvakaṃ dhanahartṝn āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	mātṛṣvasā mātulānī pitṛvyastrī pitṛṣvasā |

	śvaśrūḥ pūrvajapatnī ca matṛtulyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||

	yady āsām auraso na syāt suto dauhitra eva vā |

	tatsutā vā dhanaṃ tāsāṃ svastrīyādyāḥ samāpnuyuḥ || iti |

svasrīyo dhanasvāminyā bhāgineyaḥ svamātṛṣvsur dhanam avāpnuyāt | evamādyaśabdaparigṛhītāḥ yathākrameṇa svakīyamātṛtulyāyāḥ dhanaṃ samāpnuyuḥ | evam eva sapatnīsaṃtāno 'py upamātṛdhanaṃ tatsaṃtānatadbhartrādyabhāve saty avāpnuyāt | kvacid bhartrādisadbhāve saty avāpnuyāt | kvacid bhartrādisadbhāve 'pi sapatnīnāṃ saṃtānaviśeṣasyopamātṛdhanabhāktvam āha manuḥ |

	striyās tu yad bhaved dattaṃ pitrā dattaṃ kathaṃcana |

	brāhmaṇī tad dharet kanyā tadapatyasya vā bhavet ||

pitrā dattam iti vadan pūrvoktadhanahartṛbhartṛpitṛprabhṛtiṣu satsv apīti darśayati | bhartṛvijātīyastrīdhanaṃ tatsaṃtānābhāve sati bhartṛsajātīyastryantarakanyā tatsaṃtatir vā hared ity arthaḥ | evaṃ ca bhartṛsajātīyānekastrīṣu saṃtānaśūnyāyā mṛtāyā dhanaṃ stryantarakanyā tatsaṃtatir vā na haret | kiṃ tu brāhmādiṣu bhartaiva, śeṣeṣu dhanadātaivety anusaṃdheyam | uktārthopasaṃhāras tu kātyāyanena kṛtaḥ |

	strīdhanasyeti dharmo 'yaṃ vibhāgaś ca prakalpitaḥ |

ity evaṃ nirūpito dharmo 'yaṃ prakalpitaś ca vibhāgaḥ strīdhanasyādhyavaseya ity arthaḥ \\

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ strīdvārāgatadhanavibhāgaḥ**

**atha gauṇapitṛdvārāgatadhanavibhāgaḥ**

tatra manuḥ |

	na bhrātaro na pitaraḥ putrā rikthaharāḥ pituḥ | iti |

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span>,

	eka evaurasaḥ putraḥ pitryasya vasunaḥ prabhuḥ |

iti tenaivoktatvāt, pitṛriktha bhrātrādīnāṃ na prasaktir iti kathaṃ tatpratiṣedho 'vakalpate | na ca pranaṣṭaputraviṣaye 'vakalpata iti vācyam, putrā rikthaharā iti vidhānānavakalpanāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span>: "putrā rikthaharāḥ pituḥ" ity atra pitṛputraśabdau gauṇau | evaṃ cāyam arthaḹ kṣetrajādiputrāḥ kṣetrasvāmyādipitṛrikthaharā na tadbhrātrādaya iti | kṣetrajādiputrā api tena darśitāḥ |

	yas talpajaḥ pramītasya klībasya patitasya vā |

	svadharmeṇa niyuktāyāṃ sa putraḥ kṣetrajaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

	mātā pitā vā dadyātāṃ yad adbhiḥ putram āpadi |

	sadṛśaṃ prītisaṃyuktaṃ sa jñeyo dattrimaḥ sutaḥ ||

	sadṛśaṃ tu prakuryād yaṃ guṇadoṣavicakṣaṇam |

	putraṃ putraguṇair yuktaṃ sa vijñeyas tu kṛtrimaḥ ||

	utpadyate gṛhe yas tu na vijñāyeta kasyacit |

	sa gṛhe gūḍha utpannas tasya syād yasya talpajaḥ ||

	mātāpitṛbhyām utsṛṣṭaṃ tayor anyatareṇa vā |

	yaṃ putraṃ parigṛhṇīyād apaviddhas tu sa smṛtaḥ ||

	pitṛveśmani yaṃ putraṃ janayet kanyakā rahaḥ |

	taṃ kānīnaṃ vaden nāmnā voḍhuḥ kanyāsamudbhavam ||

	yā garbhiṇī saṃskriyate jñātājñātāpi vā satī |

	voḍhuḥ sa garbho bhavati sahoḍha iti cocyate ||

	krīṇīyād yas tv apatyārthaṃ mātāpitror yam antikāt |

	sa krītakaḥ sutas tasya sadṛśo 'sadṛśo 'pi vā ||

	yā patyā vā parityaktā vidhavā vecchayātmanaḥ |

	utpādayet punarbhūtvā sa paunarbhava ucyate ||

	mātāpitṛvihīno yas tyakto vā syād akāraṇāt |

	ātmānaṃ sparśayed yasmai svayaṃ dattas tu sa smṛtaḥ ||

	yaṃ brāhmaṇas tu śūdrāyāṃ kāmād utpādayet sutam |

	sa pārayann eva śavas tasmāt pāraśavaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

	kṣetrajādīn sutān etān ekādaśa yathoditān |

	putrapratinidhīn āhuḥ kriyālopān manīṣiṇaḥ || iti |

adbhir iti putradānavidhānasyopalakṣaṇārtham | tadvidhānaṃ cāsmābhir dattāpradānikapade darśitam | āpadi durbhikṣādau, atha vā grahītur āpadi putrābhāve | sadṛśaṃ dātuḥ pratigrahītuś ca savarṇam | prītisaṃyuktaṃ na lobhādisaṃyutam | prakuryāt anāthaṃ putratvena svīkuryāt | "sadṛśo 'sadṛśo 'pi vā" ity atra guṇāpekṣayeti śeṣaḥ | gṛhe bhāryayā utsṛṣṭaṃ duṣṭamuhūrtajatvādihetuto na pātityataḥ | pārayann eva śavaḥ jīvann eva śavaḥ | putrapratinidhīn gauṇaputrān | kriyālopāt aurasābhāve tatkartṛkaśrāddhādikriyālopāt bibhyato manīṣiṇa āhur iti saṃbandhaḥ | evaṃ nirūpitagauṇaputrāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ yugāntare putratvena parigrahaḥ, kalau tu dattasyaiva,

	dattaurasetareṣāṃ tu putratvena parigrahaḥ |

iti kaler ādau dharmaguptyarthaṃ mahātmabhiḥ dattakaurasetareṣāṃ putratvena parigrahanivāraṇāt | putrikākaraṇam apy asmād eva vākyāt kalau nivāritam, dattaurasetaratvāt putrikāyāḥ | evaṃ ca kalāv aurasaputrapautrayor abhāve dattaka eva putro gauṇo bhavati nānya ity anusaṃdheyam | mukhyo 'pi putraḥ kalāv asavarṇabhāryābhavo nāsti, asavarṇakanyāvivāhaniṣedhāt | tathā ca dharmavākyam |

	kanyānām asavarṇānāṃ vivāhaś ca dvijanmabhiḥ | iti |

atrāpi kaler ādau dharmaguptyarthaṃ mahātmabhiḥ nivārita iti vākyaseṣo draṣṭavyaḥ | ata evāsmābhir asavarṇāputrāṇāṃ dattaketaragauṇaputrāṇāṃ putrikāyās tatputrasya ca vibhāgavidhayo na nibadhyante, saṃpraty ananuṣṭheyatayā vṛthā granthavistarāpatteḥ | yat punar manunoktam,

	bhrātṝṇām ekajātānām ekaś cet putravān bhavet |

	sarve te tena putreṇa putriṇo manur abravīt ||

iti, tan na paramārthato bhrātrantarsyāpi tenaiva putreṇa putravattvam ācaṣṭe, bhrātṛputrasadbhāve 'pi bhrātrantarasyāputratvāvagamāt | ata eva yājñavalkyena "patnī duhitaraḥ" ityādinā bhrātṛputrasadbhāve 'pi "svaryātasya hy aputrasya" ity uktam | bhrātṛputrasya ca patnīduhitṛpitṛbhāve saty aputradhanabhāgitvaṃ ca ata eva tatroktam | evaṃ tarhi manuvacanasya kā gatiḥ | uktam asmābhiḥ śrāddhādhikāranirūpaṇaprakaraṇe bhrātrantarāṇāṃ putratvoktiḥ grāmasya tāta itivad aurasapraśaṃsārtheti | yat tu saṃgrahakāreṇoktam,

	yady ekajātā bahavo bhrātaras tu sahodarāḥ | 

	ekasyāpi sute jāte sarve te putriṇaḥ smṛtāḥ ||

	bahvīnām ekapatnīnām eṣa eva vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ |

	ekā cet putriṇī tāsāṃ sarvāsāṃ piṇḍadas tu saḥ ||

iti, tasya pūrvoktena sahāvirodhāya devasvāminā tātparyārtha uktaḥ, "ubhayatra nānyaḥ pratinidhiḥ kāryaḥ" ity anena granthena | ubhayatrāpi "yady ekajātāḥ" ityādivacanadvaye 'pi bhrātṛsute sapatnīsute putrapratinidhitayā kathaṃcit kartuṃ śakye sati tadanyo na pratinidhiḥ kārya iti tātparyārtho boddhavya ity arthaḥ | evaṃ ca gauṇapitṛdvārā dhanāgamanaṃ kalau dattakākhyaṃ putraṃ praty eva | atra manuḥ |

	upapanno guṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ putro yasya tu dattrimaḥ |

	sa haretaiva tad rikthaṃ saṃprāpto 'py anyagotrataḥ ||

apiśabdāt sagotrataḥ saṃprāpto 'pi | atra tṛtīyapādārtho devasvāminā vivṛtaḥ: "tadīyaṃ sarvaṃ rikthaṃ gotraṃ ca haretaiva" iti | evaṃ ca putratvāpādakakriyayaiva dattrimasya pratigrahītur dhane svatvaṃ tatsagotratvaṃ ca bhavatīti mantavyam | dātur dhane tu dānād eva putratvanivṛttidvārā dattrimasya svatvanivṛttir dātur gotranivṛttiś ca bhavatīti cāvagantavyam | anenaivābhiprāyeṇoktam |

	gotrarikthe janayitur na hared datrimaḥ sutaḥ | iti |

pratigrahītṛrikthagrahaṇe 'pi sarvaṃ kvacid viṣaye na haret | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ: "tasmiṃs cet pratigṛhīta aurasaputra utpadyeta caturthabhāgī syāt" iti | viṣṇuḥ |

	anekapitṛkāṇāṃ tu pitṛto 'ṃśasya kalpanā |

	yad yasya paitṛkaṃ rikthaṃ sa tad gṛhṇīta netaraḥ ||

yatra bhrātṝṇām ekasyaurasaḥ putra itareṣāṃ kṣetrajādayaḥ yadā te avibhaktadhanā mṛtāḥ tadā teṣām aurasādīnāṃ mukhyagauṇapitṛdvārā paitāmahadravyavibhāgakalpanā kartavyā | tatāpy aurasotpattau caturthāṃśabhāgitvam eva, itareṣāṃ pūrvanyāyānapāyāt | yatra bhrātaraḥ kecij jīvanti kecin naṣṭāḥ tatrāpy ayam eva nyāya iti ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ gauṇapitṛdvārāgatadhanavibhāgaḥ**

**atha putradvārāgatadhanavibhāgaḥ**

tatra manuḥ |

	pitā hared aputrasya rikthaṃ bhrātara eva vā | iti |

akṣarārtho vyaktas tātparyārthas tv avyaktaḥ saṃgrahakāreṇa darśitaḥ |

	aśeṣātmajahīnasya mṛtasya dhanino dhanam |

	kenedānīṃ grahītavyam ity etad adhunocyate ||

asyāyam arthaḥ: mukhyagauṇaputravihīnasya dhanavato mṛtasya dhanam idānīṃ tanmaraṇānantaraṃ kena janena hartavyam ity ākāṅkṣāyāṃ pitrādinā hartavyam ity etat adhunā pitrādyapekṣayeha bahuvidhopakārakāsannajanābhāve manunocyata iti | ata eva pitrādibhyo gauṇaputrāṇām āsannataratvaṃ jñātvā saṃgrahakāreṇa "pitā hared aputrasya" ity asya aśeṣātmajahīnasyeti tātparyam uktam, tad anavadyam eva | kiṃ tu yathā gauṇaputrāṇāṃ dṛṣṭādṛṣṭopakārakatvena pitrādyapekṣayāgresaratvāt tadapekṣayāsannataratvam, tathā patnyā api dṛṣṭādṛṣṭopakārakaraṇe śrutismṛtyādiparyālocanayā pitrādyapekṣayāgresaratvāt tadapekṣayāsannataratvam astīti patnyā apy abhāve "pitā hared aputrasya" ity etan manunocyata ity evaṃ tātparyam ūhyate | ata eva dṛṣṭādṛṣṭopakārakatvala(kṣa?)ṇasaṃbandhenānyāpekṣayā patnyāḥ pratyāsannatvam abhidhāya bṛhaspatinā gauṇaputrābhāve tiṣṭhatsv api pitrādiṣu sakulānteṣu patnyā eva patidhanabhāgitvaṃ darśitam |

	āmnāye smṛtitantre ca lokācāre ca sūribhiḥ |

	śarīrārdhaṃ smṛtā bhāryā puṇyāpuṇyaphale samā ||

	yasya noparatā bhāryā dehārdhaṃ tasya jīvati |

	jīvaty ardhaśarīre 'rthaṃ katham anyaḥ samāpnuyāt ||

	kulyeṣu vidyamāneṣu pitṛbhrātṛsanābhiṣu |

	asutasya pramītasya patnī tadbhāgahāriṇī ||

atra dvitīyārdhena dṛṣṭādṛṣṭopakārasaṃpadane putrādibhyaḥ patnyāḥ pratyāsannatvam uktam | avayavārthas tu — āmnāye vede "ardho vā eṣa ātmanaḥ yat patnī" ityevamādau | ātmano dehasyety arthaḥ | etad uktaṃ bhavati: dehārdhaṃ yathā arthāt ardhaṃ dṛṣṭādṛṣṭopakāri tathā jāyāpīti | smṛtitantre dharmaśāstre |

	pataty ardhaṃ śarīrasya yasya bhāryā surāṃ pibet |

	patitārdhaśarīrasya niṣkṛtir na vidhīyate ||

ityevamādau | lokācāre lokānusāryarthaśāstre |

	śarīrārdhamayīṃ bhāryāṃ ko vihāsyati paṇḍitaḥ |

ityevamādau | puṇyāpuṇyaphale smārtakarmaṇi sahādhikārāt | asutasya mukhyagauṇasutahīnasya | patnī yajñādhikārāpādakapraśastabrāhmādivivāhasaṃskṛtā, "patyur no yajñasaṃyoge" iti pāṇinismaraṇāt | netarā, patnīpadena vyāvartitāyāḥ tasyāḥ patnītvāyogāt | tathā ca smṛtyantaram |

	krayakrītā tu yā nārī na sā patny abhidhīyate |

	na sā daive na sā pitrye dāsīṃ tāṃ kavayo viduḥ ||

patnītvābhāve kevaladṛṣṭopakāratvaṃ striyā iti darśayituṃ dāsīṃ vidur ity uktam | evaṃ ca pitryādikarmaṇy arhatāpi patibhāgahāritve prayojiketi patnīgrahaṇena jñāpitam | ata eva śrautasmārtādikarmaṇi pātivratyena parirakṣitāyā adhikārārhāyā eva patnyāḥ patidhanalābha ity āha prajāpatiḥ |

	pūrvaṃ pramītāgnihotraṃ mṛte bhartari taddhanam |

	labhet pativratā nārī dharma eṣa sanātanaḥ ||

agnihotraśabdena tatsādhanāgnir lakṣyate | pativratā susaṃyatā, svataḥ prāyaścittena vā śrautasmārtakarmādhikārārhatayā vā bhartrā sahavāsena sthiteti yāvat | nārī patnī, agnihotralābhokteḥ patnītvāvagamārthatvāt | karmārhāyāḥ pitrye karmaṇi bhrātrādyapekṣayāgresaratvaṃ bṛhaspatinā darśitam |

	putrābhāve tu patnī syāt patnyabhāve tu sodaraḥ | iti |

atra vṛddhamanuḥ |

	aputrā śayanaṃ bhartuḥ pālayantī vrate sthitā |

	patny eva dadyāt tatpiṇḍaṃ kṛtsnam aṃśaṃ labheta ca ||

uttarārdhe tv arthakrameṇa pāṭhakramabādho draṣṭavyaḥ | tataś cāyam arthaḥ: uktalakṣaṇā patny eva kṛtsnaṃ bhartraṃśaṃ pūrvaṃ labheta paścāt patipiṇḍaṃ dadyāt | na punas tasyāṃ satyāṃ bhrātrādir iti | bhartuḥ śayanaṃ pālayantī susaṃyatety arthaḥ, varte sthitā patyau jīvaty api bhartur ajujñayā vratādiparā "kāmaṃ bhartur anujñayā vratopavāsaniyamejyādīnām ārambhaḥ strīdharmaḥ" iti śaṅkhalikhitasmaraṇāt | anenāstikatāpi patyaṃśalābhe prayojiketi vacobhaṅgyā jñāpitam iti mantavyam | yady api vivāhād eva patidhane kṛtsne patnyā api svāmyam ājīvanāt paratantratayā siddham, tathāpi svatantratayā svāmitvāntaraṃ labhyata ity evamarthaṃ labheta cety uktam | tatpiṇḍakṛtsnapadayor arthaḥ prajāpatinā prapañcitaḥ |

	jaṅgamaṃ sthāvaraṃ hema kupyaṃ dhānyarasāmbaram |

	ādāya dāpayec chrāddhaṃ māsaṣāṇmāsikādikam ||

	pitṛvyagurudauhitrān bhartuḥ svasrīyamātulān |

	pūjayet kavyapūrtābhyāṃ vṛddhānāthātithīṃs tathā || iti |

kupyaṃ trapusīdādi | kavyaṃ pitrarthaṃ saṃkalpitam annam | pūrtaṃ pūrtākhyakātādikarmāṅgabhūtaṃ dakṣiṇādikam | etad uktaṃ bhavati: sthāvareṇāpi sahitaṃ kṛtsnam aṃśam ādāya dhanasādhyaṃ stryadhikāraśrāddhapūrtādikaṃ dānādikaṃ ca patyur ātmanaś ca śreyaḥsādhanaṃ karmajātaṃ patipakṣīyaṛtvigācāryādipuraḥsaraṃ patnyā gṛhītadhanānusāreṇa kāryam iti | evaṃ ca yat kaiścid uktam: patnīgṛhītaṃ dhanaṃ yogyapatipakṣābhogyaṃ dhanikānupakārakaṃ vṛthā yāsyatīti na patnī patidhanabhāginīti, tat asiddhahetukatvād dheyam | etac ca patnīsvāmitvaṃ vibhakte patyau draṣṭavyam | yad āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	yad vibhakte dhanaṃ kiṃcid ādhyādi vividhaṃ smṛtam |

	tajjāyā sthāvaraṃ muktvā labheta mṛtabhartṛkā ||

yat kiṃcid ādhyādi vividhaṃ dhanaṃ sthāvarajaṅgamātmakaṃ bhartṛsvāmikātmakaṃ smṛtam, tat sarvaṃ vibhaktaviṣaye labhetety arthaḥ | vibhaktagrahaṇād avibhaktaviṣaye tu sahavāsina eva pitṛbhrātrādayā mṛtāputradhanaṃ labherann iti gamyate | jāyā patnī | sthāvaraṃ muktvety etad duhitṛrahitapatnīviṣayam | patnīmātraviṣayate tu,

	jaṅgamaṃ sthāvaraṃ hema kupyaṃ dhānyarasāmbaram |

	ādāya (dāpayec chrāddhaṃ māsaṣāṇmāsikādikam) ||

iti pūrvoktavacanavirodhaḥ syāt | na ca tadvirodhaparihārāyāvibhaktapatyaṃśaviṣayaṃ vṛttahīnapatnīviṣayaṃ vedaṃ vacanam astv iti vācyam | yata evaṃprakārāṃ vyavasthāṃ nirākartum āha sa eva |

	vṛttasthāpi kṛte 'py aṃśe strī sthāvaram arhati |

iti | saṃtānavṛttibhūtasthāvaralabdhyarhatā tu saṃtānaśālitāyatteti tacchūnyā strī vṛttasthāpi vibhaktaviṣaye 'pi sthāvaraṃ nārhatīty arthaḥ | yad aparam uktaṃ tenaiva,

	mṛte bhartari bhartraṃśaṃ labheta kulapālikā | 

	yāvajjīvaṃ hīnasvāmyaṃ dānādhamanavikraye ||

iti, kulapālikā vaṃśapālikā vṛttastheti yāvat | tat vṛddhānāthādyupajīvanāyādṛṣṭārthadānavidhānāt taditaradṛṣṭārthanartakādīnāṃ dānādāv asvātantryapratipādanārtham iti mantavyam | evaṃ ca dharmārthadāne svātantryam asty eva | ata eva dharmārthadānam aniśam āvartanīyam ity āha sa eva |

	vratopavāsaniratā brahmacarye vyavasthitā |

	dharmadānaratā nityam aputrāpi divaṃ vrajet ||

na hi pāratantrye nityadānakriyā yujyate | evaṃ cādṛṣṭasādhakadravyasaṃpādanārthayor ādhivikrayayor api svātantryam apratiṣiddham iti mantavyam | yad aparam uktaṃ kātyāyanena,

	aputrā śayanaṃ bhartuḥ pālayantī gurau sthitā |

	bhuñjītāmaraṇāt kṣāntā dāyādā ūrdhvam āpnuyuḥ ||

iti — kṣāntā dāyādakāritadhanaviniyogapratibandhaṃ sahamānety arthaḥ — tat avibhaktadaśāyāṃ rakṣaṇabharaṇāsamartheṣu kāryāntaravyagreṣu vā śvaśurādiṣu patnyā svayam eva jīvanārtham upāttāvibhaktadravyaviṣayam | vibhaktadravyaviṣayatve vṛddhamanvādivacanapariniścitārthavirodhapatteḥ | rakṣaṇādisamartheṣu śvaśurādiṣv avibhaktamṛtadhanagrāhiṣu satsu tair eva gṛhītadhanair bharaṇaṃ karyam | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	yāvatyo vidhavāḥ sādhavyo jyeṣṭhena śvaśureṇa vā |

	gotrajenāpi vānyena bhartavyāś chādanāśanaiḥ ||

dhanagrāhiṇeti sarvatra jyeṣṭhādau śeṣo draṣṭavyaḥ | dhanagrahaṇanimittatvāt bharaṇasya | atra veśeṣam āha kātyayanaḥ |

	svaryāte svāmini strī tu grāsācchadanabhaginī |

	avibhakte dhanāṃśaṃ tu prāpnoty āmaraṇāntikam ||

dhanāṃśaṃ yāvatā dhanenākliṣṭajīvanaṃ dhanasādhyaṃ ca nityanaimittikaṃ karma stryadhikārakaṃ kāmyavratādikaṃ ca sidhyati tāvantam ity arthaḥ | tuśabdo vāśabdārthe, dhanāṃśaṃ vā prāpnotīty arthaḥ | etāvad dhanasaṃpādakaṃ kṣetrāṃśaṃ vā prapnoti, dhanagrahaṇasya vartanādyupāyopalakṣaṇārthatvāt | atrādyapakṣaḥ patnīvyatiriktabhāryāviṣayaḥ, jīvanamātrasādhanasvalpārthabhāgitvābhidhānāt | jīvanamātrasādhanasya svalpām iyattām āha nāradaḥ |

	āḍhakāṃs tu caturviṃśat catvāriṃśat paṇāṃs tathā |

	pratisaṃvatsaraṃ sādhvī labheta mṛtabhartṛkā ||

āḍhako 'ṣṭonadviśataprasṛtiparimito dhānyacayaḥ | paṇaḥ kārṣāpaṇaḥ | sa ca vyāvahārikaniṣkāśītitamabhagasya sthāne kvacid deśe pravartate | tena yatra deśe paṇo na pravartate tatra tatsthāne vyāvahārikaniṣāśītitamabhāgaḥ labhyate | kṛte 'py aṃśa ity anuvṛttau bṛhaspatiḥ |

	pradadyāt tv eva piṇḍaṃ vā kṣetrāṃśaṃ vā yadṛcchayā | iti |

piṇḍagrahaṇam aśanācchādanopalakṣaṇārtham | evaṃ cāyam arthaḥ: aśanācchādanaṃ pūrvoktaparimāṇakaṃ pūrvoktadhanāṃśasaṃpādakakṣetrāṃśaṃ vā | sa ca rucyā bhartraṃśarhapatnīvyatiriktavidhavāyai avibhaktaviṣaye jīvanārthaṃ pradadyād iti | evakāraḥ pradānasyāvaśyakatvajñāpanārthaḥ | śvaśrvādyaśuśrūṣakastrīviṣayo 'trādyaḥ pakṣaḥ | tatra jñāpakam upariṣṭāt bhaviṣyati | dattaṃ ca dāyaketarair api pālanīyam ity āha sa eva |

	sthāvarāj jīvanaṃ strībhyo yad dattaṃ śvaśureṇa tu |

	na tac chakyam apāhartum itaraiḥ śvaśure mṛte ||

śvaśuragrahaṇaṃ bharaṇakāriṇa upalakṣaṇārtham | sthāvaragrahaṇaṃ ca dhanasyopalakṣanārtham | tena dhanādy api jīvanārthaṃ strībhyo dattam apāhartum aśakyam itarair ity avagantavyam | kvacid apahartavyam ity āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	bhoktum arhati kḷptāṃśaṃ guruśuśrūṣaṇe ratā |

	na kuryād yadi śuśrūṣāṃ celapiṇḍe niyojayet ||

kḷptāṃśam apahṛtyeti śeṣaḥ | evam akāryakāriṇyādāv api kḷptāṃśāpaharaṇaṃ kāryam ity āha sa eva |

	apacārakriyāyuktā nirlajjā cārthanāśikā |

	vyabhicāraratā yā ca strī dhanaṃ na ca sārhati || iti |

dhanaṃ jīvanārtham upakḷptadhanāṃśam, kṣetrāṃśaṃ vā jīvanādyartham upakḷptam uktā caturvidhā strī nārhatīty arthaḥ | dhanagrahaṇam aśanācchādanādyupalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	bharaṇaṃ cāpi kurvīran strīṇām ā jīvanakṣayāt |

	rakṣanti śayyāṃ bhartuś cet ācchindyur itarāsu tat ||

itarāsu vyabhicāraratāsu | bharaṇam aśanācchādanāya kalpitaṃ dhānyavastramūlyadravyam ācchindyuḥ apahareyur ity arthaḥ | yad atra manunoktam,

	evam eva vidhiṃ kuryād yoṣitsu patitāsv api |

	vastrānnam āsāṃ deyaṃ tu vaseyuś ca gṛhāntike ||

iti, tat bhartṛkartṛkabharaṇaviṣayam iti pūrvārdhata evāvagamyata ity avirodhaḥ | yā punaḥ śaṅkitavyabhicārā tasyās tu vibhaktaviṣaye patnītve 'pi hārītoktam kāryam |

	vidhavā yauvanasthā cet nārī bhavati karkaśā |

	āyuṣaḥ kṣapaṇārthaṃ tu dātavyaṃ jīvanaṃ tadā || iti |

karkaśā krūrā sāhasārhā saṃbhāvitavyabhicāreti yāvat | yat punar manunā "patny eva kṛtsnam aṃśaṃ labheta ca" iti vṛddhamanūktaviruddham uktam,

	yeṣāṃ jyeṣṭhaḥ kaniṣṭho vā hīyetāṃśapradānataḥ |

	mriyetānyataro vāpi tasya bhago na lupyate ||

	sodaryā vibhajeraṃs taṃ sametya sahitāḥ samam |

	bhrātaro ye ca saṃsṛṣṭā bhaginyaś ca sanābhayaḥ ||

iti — hīyate pātityādinimitteneti śeṣaḥ — yad api nāradena,

	saṃsṛṣṭānāṃ tu yo bhāgas teṣām eva sa iṣyate |

ity uktvoktam,

	bhrātṝṇām aprajāḥ preyāt kaścic cet pravrajeta vā |

	vibhajeyur dhanaṃ tasya śeṣās te strīdhanaṃ vinā ||

iti, tad etad vayam api saṃsṛṣṭadravyaviṣayam iti spaṣṭam eva | tena nasti virodhaḥ | evaṃ ca "patny eva samastam aṃśaṃ labheta" iti vibhaktāsaṃsṛṣṭaviṣayam it mantavyam | tathā ca saṃgrahakāraḥ |

	bhrātṛṣu pravibhakteṣu saṃsṛṣṭeṣv apy asatsu ca |

	gurvādeśān niyogasthā patnī dhanam avāpnuyāt ||

"gurvādeśān niyogasthā" iti dhāreśvaramataṃ viśvarūpādibhiḥ samyag dūṣitatvād upekṣaṇīyam | tataś ca saṃgrahakāroktaviṣaye vṛddhamanūktaguṇaviśiṣṭā patnī bhartṛdhanam akhilam avāpnuyād ity etad eva matam ādartavyam | yat tu śrutāv uktam: "tasmāt striyo nirindriyā adāyādīḥ" ity, tad api na vṛddhamanvādivacanabādhakam, nirindriyaputrasāhacaryād apatyabhūtastrīviṣayatvāvagateḥ | bhavatu vā sarvastrīviṣayatvāvagatiḥ, tathāpi dāyādatayā śṛṅgagrāhikoktapatnyādistrīvyatiriktaviṣayārthavādaśrutir iti sarvaṃ sustham | patnībahutve samaṃ vibhaya aputrabhartṛdhanagrahaṇaṃ sarvāsāṃ yuktam | evaṃ sarvasmṛtyekavākyatayā niścitaṃ patnīdhanaṃ ye pratibadhnanti te rājñā niyantavyā ity āha prajāpatiḥ |

	tatsapiṇḍā bāndhavāś ca ye tasyāḥ paripanthinaḥ |

	hiṃsyur dhanāni tān rājā coradaṇḍena śāsayet ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ putradvārāgatadhanavibhāge patnīviṣayāṇi**

**atha duhitrādiviṣayāṇi kānicid vacanāni likhyante**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	bhartur dhanaharī patnī tāṃ vinā duhitā smṛtā || iti |

tāṃ vinā tasyā abhāva ity arthaḥ | ata eva viṣṇuḥ: "aputrasya dhanaṃ patnyabhigāmi tadabhāve duhitṛgāmi" iti | asmin krame nyāyam āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	aṅgād aṅgāt saṃbhavati putravad duhitā nṛṇām |

	tasmāt pitṛdhanaṃ tv anyaḥ kathaṃ gṛhṇīta mānavaḥ ||

śarīrāvayavasaṃbandhena duhitā putrasamā, putre hi pitravayavānāṃ bāhulyena saṃkrāntiḥ, duhitari tv alpatayā,

	pumān puṃso 'dhike śukle strī bhavaty adhike striyāḥ |

iti smaraṇāt | tena kiṃcitsāmānyāt putravad ity uktam | anyaḥ putrapatnīvyatiriktaḥ pitrādir mānavaḥ tṣṭhantyām duhitari putradhanaṃ kathaṃ gṛhṇītety arthaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	yathaivātmā tathā putraḥ putreṇa duhitā samā |

	tasyām ātmani tiṣṭhantyāṃ katham anyo dhanaṃ haret ||

ātmani ātmatulyaputrasamāyām ity arthaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanv</span> evam api gauṇaputrapatnyor abhāve duhitetikrame nyāyo noktaḥ, aurasābhāvamātre duhitety etāvanmātrasādhakatvād uktanyāyasya | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span>, kiṃ tv idam eva gauṇaputrapatnyor abhāve duhitety atrāpi krame nyāya ūhanīya ity abhiprāyeṇoktam | ata eva nāradena tayor apy abhāve duhiteti kramānusārī nyāyaḥ svayam ūhito mandānugrahāya pradarśitaḥ |

	putrābhāve tu duhitā tulyasaṃtānadarśanāt | iti |

svayam eva nyāyaṃ vivṛṇoti |

	putraś ca duhitā cobhau tulyasaṃtānakārakau | iti |

ubhau svapitṛśreyaḥkarasaṃtānakārakāv ity arthaḥ | tathā hi pautradauhitrayoḥ putraduhitṛsaṃtānayoḥ svarūpatas tulyatvābhāvāt kāryato 'tra tulyatvam abhipretam | na ca ṛṇāpākaraṇakāryatas tulyatvaṃ saṃbhavati "putrapautraiḥ ṛṇaṃ deyam" iti smaraṇāt | tathā pitāmahadravyam adhikṛtya,

	tatra syāt sadṛśaṃ svāmyaṃ pituḥ putrasya cobhayoḥ |

iti smaraṇataś ca pautrasyādhikyapratīteḥ, tenātrādṛṣṭakāryatas tulyatvam abhipretam | tac ca, śrāddhadātṛtvam

	pūrveṣāṃ tu svadhākāre pautrā dauhitrakā matāḥ |

iti viṣṇusmaraṇāt | evaṃ ca duhituḥ svasaṃtānamukhenādṛṣṭopakārakasaṃbandhenāsannatā ca | etāvatā nimittena "putrābhāve tu duhitā" ity atra putragrahaṇaṃ patnyā api pradarśanārtham iti mantavyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> pitā śrāddhadāne svayam evādṛṣṭopakāraka iti duhitur apekṣayāsannatvāt patnyabhāve "pitā hared aputrasya" ity asyāyam avasara iti kathaṃ duhitur arthagrahaṇam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>,

	tasyām ātmani tiṣṭhantyāṃ katham anyo dhanaṃ haret |

ityanenaivoktatvāt | tathā hi, yady apy adṛṣṭopakārasaṃbandhena vyavahitā, tathāpi śārīrasambandhenāvyavahitety ubhayathāsaṃbandhād duhitaivāgresarī | evaṃ tarhi duhitrabhāve "pitā haret" ity asyāvasaraḥ syāt | nādhunāpi tasyāvasaraḥ, duhitrabhāve 'pi dauhitrasya tatkoṭitvena pitrādyapekṣayāsannatvāt,

	aputrapautrasaṃtāne dauhitrā dhanam āpnuyuḥ |

	pūrveṣāṃ tu svadhākāre pautrā dauhitrakā matāḥ ||

iti viṣṇusmaraṇāc ca | evaṃ sopapattikāṃ patnyabhāve duhitṛgāmitāṃ bruvatā bṛhaspatyādinaiva dauhitragāmi dhanam iti vidhāyakaṃ yad vacanajātaṃ tat putrikāviṣayam eva, na punar aputrikāduhitṛviṣayam iti dhāreśvaradevasvāmidevarātamataṃ smṛtitantrābhijñatvābhimānonmādakalpitaṃ nirastaṃ veditavyam | tathā hi, "tṛtīyāh putraḥ putrikā vijñāyate" iti vasiṣṭhasmṛtyā gauṇaputrakoṭiniviṣṭāyāḥ putrikāyāḥ patnyāṃ satyām api kṣetrajāder iva,

	na bhrātaro na pitaraḥ putrā rikthaharāḥ pituḥ |

ityādivacanāntarair eva aurasābhāve rikthagrāhiṇyāḥ patnyāḥ prāg eva daṇḍāpūpanyāyenaiva dhanabhāgitve siddhe punaḥ kiṃ sopapattikaṃ dhanabhāgitvaṃ smartuṃ bṛhaspatyādīnāṃ vacanāntarārambheṇa | tena tair eva tanmataṃ nirastam ity alaṃ dhāreśvarādimatāntaranirākaraṇayatnenāsmadīyena | yat tu nāradena putrahīnapatnīm adhikṛtyoktam,

	syāt tu ced duhitā tasyāḥ pitryo 'ṃśo bharaṇe mataḥ |

	ā saṃskārād dhared bhāgaṃ parato bibhṛyāt patiḥ ||

iti, tasyārthaḥ: tasyāḥ patnyāḥ putrarahitāyāḥ yadi duhitā vidyate tadā duhitur bharaṇe bhraṇāya pitryo 'ṃśo 'bhimataḥ | tasmād ā vivāhasaṃskārāt bharaṇārtham eva duhitā pitṛbhāgaṃ haret | na punar yatheṣṭaviniyogārtham iti | evaṃ ca sarvāsām eva kanyānāṃ pitṛdhanaprāptir utsarga iti gamyate | tataś cāsyāpavādakāni duhituḥ pitṛdhanaprāptipratipādakāni vacanāni sarvāṇi putrikāviṣāṇy eveti vācyam, duhitṛmātraviṣayatve tūtsargavat sāmānyatayā tadapavādākṣamatvād anarthakāni bhaveyuḥ | tasmād dhāreśvarādīnām eva matam anusartavyaḥ (?) syād eva yadi nāradavacanaṃ vibhaktaviṣayaṃ syāt | saṃsṛṣṭiviṣayaṃ tu tad iti tasyaiva pūrvāparaparyālocanayā sphuṭam avagamyate | tataś ca vibhaktaviṣaye yāni duhitṛdāyapratipādakavacanāni teṣāṃ tatprāpakatvam eva nāpavādakatvam iti na putrikāviṣayatvakalpane kiṃcin mūlam upalabhāmahe ity alam atibahunā | evam api na duhitṛmātraviṣayāṇi tāni vacanāni, yat āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	patnī bhartur dhanaharī yā syād avyabhicāriṇī |

	tadabhāve tu duhitā yady anūḍhāpratiṣṭhitā || iti |

evaṃ ca kātyāyanavacanāny anūḍhāduhitṛviṣayāṇi, atha vā nirdhanoḍhāduhitṛviṣayāṇīti mantavyam | nirdhanatvenaivāpratiṣṭhitātra vivakṣitā, na punar vandhyātvādinā saṃtānarāhityenāpratiṣṭhitā, tasyāḥ saṃtānamukhenādṛṣṭopakārakasaṃbandhābhāvena dhanahāritvāyogāt | tadabhāve ity anena pūrvoktāyāḥ avyabhicāriṇyāḥ patnyā abhāvaḥ pratyavamṛśyate, na patnīsvarūpamātrasya, na kevalaṃ patnyā svarūpābhāve duhitā dhanahāriṇī kiṃ tv avyabhicāritvalakṣaṇaviśeṣaṇābhāve 'pīti mantavyam | ata eva saṃgrahakāreṇa,

	tādṛkpatnyā abhāve 'pi putrikā dhanam arhati |

ity uktam | na paraṃ patnīsvarūpābhāve, kiṃ tu dhanabhāginīti nirūpaṇārtham uktaviśeṣaṇaviśiṣṭapatnyabhāve 'pi putrikā dhanam arhatīty arthaḥ | putrikā dhanam arhatīti tu prāg eva nirastatvād upekṣaṇīyam | tena patnyāḥ svarūpābhāve duhitṛgāmi dravyam, viśeṣaṇābhāve tu pitā hared ityādivacanoktapitrādigāmīti kaiścit kṛtā viṣayavyavasthāpy upekṣaṇīyā | bṛhaspatis tu patnyā ūrdhvam arthagrāhṇīnāṃ mukhyaputrād ūrdhvam arthagrāhiṇīnāṃ ca duhitṝṇāṃ viśeṣaṇāny āha |

	sadṛśī sadṛśenoḍhā sādhvī śuśrūṣaṇe ratā |

	kṛtākṛtā vāputrasya pitur dhanaharī tu sā ||

sadṛśī pitṛsavarṇā | atrādyāni catvāri viśeṣaṇāni patnyā ūrdhvaṃ dhanagrāhiduhitṛviṣayāṇi | prāgdhanagrāhiṇyā duhitur viśeṣaṇe tv avaśiṣṭe | kṛtākṛtety atra putriketi viśeṣyasyādhyāhāraḥ kartavyaḥ | itaratra duhiteti viśeṣyasyādhyāhāraḥ kāryaḥ | vāśabdo vyavasthitavikalpābhidhānārthaḥ | evaṃ cāyam arthaḥ: aurasaputravihīnasya pitur dhanaṃ dvividhāpi putrikā patyāḥ pūrvaṃ gṛhṇīyāt, savarṇādiviśeṣaṇopetāpratiṣṭhitānūḍhānāṃ duhitṝṇāṃ samavāye 'nūḍhaiva gṛhṇāti, pitrā bhartavyatvāt | tadabhāve 'pratiṣṭhitā, bhartrā bhartavyate 'pi bharutr bharaṇasāmarthyābhāvenāpratiṣṭhitatvāt | tadabhāve savarṇādiviśeṣaṇopetā pratiṣṭhitā, pratiṣṭhitatve 'pi dhanagrahaṇayogyatvāt | tadabhāve dauhitraḥ, tatkoṭitvād ity anusaṃdheyam | dauhitrasyābhāve tu pitrapekṣayānyasyāsannatarasyābhāvāt | "pitā hared aputrasya riktham" ityuktasyāvasaratvāt pitṛgāmi dhanaṃ bhavati | asminn evāvasare mātrapekṣayāpy anyasyāsannatarasyābhāt,

	anapatyasya putrasya mātā dāyam avāpnuyāt |

ity uktasyāvasaratvān mātṛgāmi dhanaṃ bhavati | ata eva yājñavalkyena "patnī duhitaraś caiva pitarau" ity uktam | caśabdena sūcitasya dauhitrasyānantaram eva mātāpitarau samasamaye dhanabhājau | tayor avāntarakrame nyāyābhāvād ity abhiprāyo yājñavalkyasyāvagantavyaḥ | abhiprāyam abudhvātrāpi kaiścit paṇḍitaṃmanyaiḥ kaścin nyāya utprekṣitaḥ, mātur garbhadhāraṇapoṣaṇadvāreṇātyantopakāritvāt,

	sahasraṃ tu pitur mātā gauraveṇātiricyate |

iti smaraṇāc ca, pitari vidyamāne 'pi mātur eva dhanagrahaṇe 'dhikāra iti | nāyaṃ nyāyo mātur ādau aṃśagrahaṇādhikārāpādanāyālam, pitur api bahudhā saṃvidhātṛtvāt, vidyāpradatvāt, 

	tayor api pitā śreyān bījaprādhānyadarśanāt |

iti smaraṇāc ca | anyaiḥ punar anyathā utprekṣitaḥ: "pitā sapatnīputreṣv api sādhāraṇaḥ mātā tu na sādhāraṇīti pratyāsattyatiśayo 'sti" iti | vipralambhasadṛkṣam idam, na hi jananījanakayor janyaṃ prati saṃnikarṣe tāratamyam asti | na ca bahusaṃbandhataḥ sākṣātsaṃbandhanibandhanāyāḥ pratyāsatter atiśayo 'py apaiti | yad api tair evoktam: "ekaśeṣaśravaṇe 'pi kathaṃcin matuḥ prāthamyam avagamyate" iti, tad api mandam, "sārasvatau bhavataḥ" ity utpattivākye kramāvagatyabhāvena yājyākrameṇa pradhānayoḥ kramaḥ pañcame darśito na punaḥ sārasvatāv ity ekaśeṣata eva kathaṃcit kramāvagatir upapāditeti nirnibandhanam eva mātuḥ prāthamyasamarthanam | ata eva śrīkareṇa pitror vibhajyadhanagrahaṇam uktam | tad apy ayuktam, "pitā hared aputrasya riktham," "svaryātasya hy aputrasya mātā dāyam avāpnuyāt" ity etābhyāṃ vrīhiyavayor nirapekṣasādhanatvavan nirapekṣasvāmyapratīteḥ | apare punar anyathā mātuḥ pratyāsattim unnayanti: "sodarasya tu sodaraḥ" ity atra mātṛdvāreṇa sodare dāyavacanān mātuḥ pratyāsattir gamyata iti, tad etat kāśakuśāvalambanamātram, tathā hi bhrātur bhinnodarād ekodarayor ekamātṛkatvena pratyāsattau viśeṣo 'sti janakāt punar jananyāḥ putraṃ prati pratyāsattau viśeṣaḥ kiṃnibandhano bhaviṣyatīti na vidmaḥ | tasmād atra pitroḥ sadbhāve kaḥ krama ity apekṣāyāṃ vaktavya viśeṣaḥ | yat tūktaṃ śambhunā: "madhyakadhanatvāt dampatyor yena kenacit gṛhyamāṇam ubhayārtham iti na viśeṣo vaktavyaḥ" iti, tad ayuktam | mātrā gṛhyamāṇaṃ mātrartham evādhyagnyādistrīdhanavan nobhayārtham iti viśeṣo vaktavya eva | so 'bhidhīyate: nyāyābhāvād atra atra krame vacanam eva śaraṇam, vacane ca pitur eva prathamaṃ dhanagrahaṇe 'dhikāraḥ pratipādyate | tathā ca "aputrasya dhanaṃ patnyabhigāmi, tadabhāve duhitrṛgāmi" ity anuvṛttau bṛhadviṣṇuḥ: "tadabhāve pitṛgāmi tadabhāve mātṛgāmi" iti | yady apy aputradhanasya duhitrabhāve pitṛgāmitvam uktam | tathāpi duhitrabhāve dauhitragāmitvasya nyāyavacanābhyām uktatvāt | dauhitrasyābhāve tu pitṛgāmitvam avagantavyam, dauhitrasyāpi duhitṛkoṭitvāt pṛthak dauhitragāmitvānabhidhānaṃ bṛhadviṣṇor iti ca mantavyam | mātrabhāve tu sodarabhrātṛgāmitvam ekamātṛkatvena mṛtabhrātṛpratyāsattyatiśayalakṣaṇanyāyāt prāptam, tadabhāve bhinnodarabhrātṛgāmitvaṃ ca, tat yājñavalkyena nyāyamūlakramam evābhidadhatābhihitam: "pitarau bhrātaras tathā" iti | bhrātaraḥ sodarā evātra bhinnodarāpekṣayā dhaninaṃ prati patyāsannatvād abhipretāḥ | tataś ca mātrabhāve sodarabhrātṛgāmy aputradhanam ity utsargo yājñavalkyena darśitaḥ | tathā sodaratvarūpaviśeṣavivakṣāyām api bhrātara iti sāmānyaśabdaprayogeṇa sodarābhāve bhinnodarā iti cotsargas tenaiva darśitaḥ | utsargasya vakṣyamāṇaviṣayadvaye 'pavādam āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	vibhakte saṃsthite dravyaṃ putrābhāve pitā haret |

	bhrātā vā jananī vātha mātā vā tatpituḥ kramāt ||

tatpitur mātā vibhaktamṛtāputrasya pitur mātā, pitāmahīti yāvat | putragrahaṇam āsannataropalakṣaṇārtham | tena putrādidauhitrāntānāṃ pitrapekṣayā dṛṣṭādṛṣṭopakārakādisaṃbandhenāsannatarāṇām abhāve prathamaṃ pitā hared ity arthaḥ | vāśabdās trayo 'py atrābhāvavikalpārthāḥ | svāmyākhye siddharūpe vastuni "na hi vastu vikalpyate" iti nyāyena tulyavad vikalpāsaṃbhavāt | evaṃ caitad uktaṃ bhavati: pitrabhāve bhrātā haret tadabhāve jananī tadabhāve pitāmahīti | kramāt uktapāṭhakramenety arthaḥ | anenaiva ca krameṇa vibhaktasaṃsthitaviṣaye manur api putrapatnīduhitṛdauhitrāṇām āsannatarāṇām abhāvam aputrasyety upalakṣakaśabdena aputrasyety uktvā pitṛbhrātṛmātṛpitāmahīnāṃ dhanagrahaṇaṃ sārdhaślokenāha |

	pitā hared aputrasya rikthaṃ bhrātara eva vā |

	anapatyasya putrasya mātā dāyam avāpnuyāt ||

	mātary api ca vṛttāyāṃ pitur mātā dhanaṃ haret | iti |

aputrasya putrapatnīduhitṛdauhitraśūnyasyety arthaḥ | evaṃ ca kātyāyanamanupratipāditaḥ pitrādipitāmahyantānāṃ dhanagrahaṇakramo vacanaikanibandhanaḥ svaviruddhanaiyāyikakramabādhaka iti nyāyavirodhaśaṅkātra na kāryā | yājñavalkīyam eva vacanaṃ kramaparam, tatpartvasya tatra "pūrvābhāve paraḥ paraḥ" iti kaṇṭhoktyā vyaktatvāt | tena tadviruddhāni vacanāni "pitā hared aputrasya" ityevamādīni tv adhikāramātraparāṇy eveti vyākhyāpy upekṣaṇīyā | "mātā vā tatpituḥ kramāt" iti, "mātary api ca vṛttāyām" iti kātyāyanavacanayor api kaṇṭhoktyā kramasmṛteḥ | mātuḥ pūrvaṃ bhrātā dhanahārīty atra viśeṣam āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	bhāryāsutavihīnasya vibhaktasya mṛtasya tu |

	mātā riktahārī jñeyā bhrātā vā tadanujñayā || iti |

tasya mṛtasya | bhāryāgrahaṇaṃ nyāyato baddhakramāṇāṃ duhitṛdauhitrapitṝṇām upalakṣaṇārtham | tena sutabhāryāduhitṛdauhitrapitṛvihīnasyety artho vijñeyaḥ | evaṃ ca "pitarau bhrātaras tathā" ity uktakramasya mātur anujñāviṣaye vidyamānapitāmahīviṣaye ca kātyāyanādyuktakrameṇāpavādo 'nusaṃdheyaḥ | etenedaṃ nirastam, yat kaiścid uktam: "mātṛpitṛbhrātṛsutānāṃ 'pitarau bhrātaras tathā tatsutāḥ' iti vacanena baddhakramatvān madhye 'nupraveśābhāvāt bhrātṛsaṃtānānantaraṃ pitāmahī gṛhṇāti, tasyāḥ kramaviśeṣoktyabhāvenāvirodhāt" iti | na hi pitāmahyāḥ kramaviśeṣoktyabhāvaḥ, kātyāyanavacane pāṭhatas tadgatāthaśabdena, mānavīye "mātari vṛttāyām" iti padadvayena ca pitāmahyāḥ kramaviśeṣokteḥ prākpradarśitatvāt | baddhakramasyāpi tasya nyāyamūlasya madhye vacanamūlakam aviśeṣasaṃbhavāc ca | yat tu śaṅkhalikhitoktam: "svaryātasya hy aputrasya bhrātṛgami dravyam, tadabhāve pitarau hareyātām" iti, tat sāmānyaviśeṣanyāyena vibhaktasaṃsthitaviṣayād anyatra saṃsṛṣṭasvaryātaviṣaye 'vatiṣṭhata ity avirodhaḥ | yat tu bṛhaspatinoktam,

	putrābhāve tu patnī syāt patnyabhāve tu sodaraḥ |

	tadabhāve tu dāyādaḥ paścād dauhitrakaṃ dhanam ||

iti, tat patnyāḥ pūrvaṃ sodaranivṛttyartham, na punar dāyādaśabdanirdiṣṭaduhitṛbhyaḥ pūrvaṃ sodaraprāptyartham | tathātve "aṅgād aṅgāt saṃbhavati putravad duhitā" ityādisvavacanavirodhāpatteḥ | yat tu devalenoktam,

	tato dāyam aputrasya vibhajeran sahodarāḥ |

	tulyā duhitaro vātha dhriyamāṇaḥ pitātha vā |

	sarvarṇā bhrātaro mātā bhāryā veti yathākramam || iti |

yady apy atra vyavahitānvayo vacanaracanāñjasyenāvagamyate, tathāpi pūrvoktasarvavacananyāyāvirodhāya vyavahitānvayenaivārtho 'vagantavyaḥ | tathā hi, aputrasya dāyaṃ bhāryā patnī vāpnuyāt atha vā tulyāḥ savarṇāḥ duhitaro vibhajeran api vā dhriyamāṇo vidyamānaḥ pitā haret, anarthakadhriyamāṇaśabdād adhyamāṇe pitari mātety anvayāvagamāt pitur abhāve mātāvāpnuyāt, tataḥ sahodarāḥ savarṇāś ca bhrātaro yathākramaṃ pūrvaṃ sahodarās tattadabhāve savarṇā iti kramānatikrameṇa vibhajerann iti | mātranujñāyāḥ pitāmahyāś cābhāvaviṣaya etad draṣṭavyam | asminn api viṣaye kātyāyanena subodhāya kramo darśitaḥ |

	aputrasyātha kulajā patnī duhitaro 'pi vā |

	tadabhāve pitā mātā bhrātā putrāś ca kīrtitāḥ ||

putraśabdaḥ saṃandhiśabdatvāt padanyāyena bhrātṛputreṣv eva vartate | ata eva yājñavalkyena "bhrātaras tathā tatsutāḥ" ity uktam | yat tu saṃgrahakāreṇoktam,

	tādṛgduhitrabhāve 'pi mātā dhanam avāpnuyāt |

	vidyamāne 'pi pitari sapatnīsutasaṃtatau ||

	tādṛṅmātur abhāve 'pi pitur mātā hared dhanam |

	vidyamāne 'pi pitari kṣatriyāsutasaṃtatau ||

	pitāmahyā abhāve 'pi pitā dhanam avāpnuyāt ||

iti —sutasaṃtatāv ity atra vidyamānāyām ity adhyāhāre kṛte saty asyārthaḥ sugamaḥ — tad etad dhāreśvarotprekṣitanyāyamūlatvād viśvarūpādibhis tannyāyanirākaraṇān mūlabhūtanyāye asaty anādṛtyam eva | yat punas tenaivoktam,

	sodaryāḥ santy asodaryā bhrātaro dvividhā yadi |

	vidyamāne 'py asodarye sodaryā eva bhāginaḥ ||

iti, tat samyaṅnyāyamūlatvād ādaraṇīyam | bhrātṛsuteṣv apy ayaṃ viseṣaḥ sodarāsodarabhrātṛsutasamavāye grāhyaḥ | tataś c sodarabhrātṛsutābhāve sapatnibhrātṛsutā dhanabhājaḥ | teṣām abhāve ke dhanabhāja ity apekṣite yājñavalkyaḥ "gotrajāḥ" iti | dhanabhāja iti śeṣaḥ | gotrajaśabdo 'tra gobalīvardanyāyāt pūrvoktapitṛbhrātṛtatsutavyatiriktapitāmahatatsutādigotrajeṣu vartate | tatrāpi sarūpaikaśeṣasya svato 'vagateḥ pitāmahaduhitrādistrīvyatirikteṣu vartate | kāraṇāntarād eva hi "kukkuṭāvanaya (?) mithunīkariṣāmahe" ityādau virūpaikaśeṣāvagatiḥ | na ceha tathāstikāraṇāntaram, pratyuta bhrātṛtatsutasāhacaryāt pumāṃsa eva gotrajā gamyante | kiṃ ca patnīduhitrādīnāṃ śṛṅgagrāheṇa dāyādatvasmṛter agatyā "tasmāt striyo nirindriyā adāyādīḥ" iti śrutes tadvyatiriktaviṣayatoktā | teneha sarūpaikaśeṣatayā smṛteḥ satyāṃ saṃgatau śrutivirodhinī virupaikaśeṣatā dūrotsāritā | ata eva "jīvan putrebhyo dāyaṃ vibhajet" ity āpastambasūtraṃ vyācakṣāṇena tadbhāṣyakāreṇa putrebhya eva dāyaṃ vibhajen na strībhyo duhitṛbhya ity uktam | yady api "bhrātṛputro svasṛduhitṛbhyām" iti śabdasmṛtyā putrebhya ity atra virūpaikaśeṣaṃ kṛtvā duhitṝṇām apy anupraveśaḥ sūtre kartuṃ śakyate, tathāpi pumāṃso dāyādā na striyaḥ "tasmāt striyo nirindriyā adāyādīḥ" iti śruter iti | etenaitan nirastam, yat kaiścid uktam, gotrajā pitāmahī tatsapiṇḍāḥ samānodakāś ca, tatra pitāmahī prathamṃ dhanabhāk "mātary api ca vṛttāyāṃ pitur mātā dhanaṃ haret" iti mātrantaraṃ pitāmahyā dhanagrahaṇe prāpte putrādīnāṃ bhrātṛsutaparyantānāṃ baddhakramatvena madhye 'nupraveśābhāvād utkarṣe tatsutānantaram api pitāmahī gṛhṇāti avirodhād iti | bhrātṛsutānantaram api teṣāṃ gotrajānāṃ ca baddhakravatvāviśeṣāt pitāmahyā sahaivātra kramo bādhyata ity asaṃbandhasarūpaikaśeṣatvena puṃsām eva gotrajānāṃ bhrātṛsutaiḥ saha kramabandhanāt, na cānyagotrajā pitāmahī mṛtagotrajāpīty alaṃ bahunā | gotrajā ity ekaśeṣakaraṇam api pitarāv itivan nyāyāmūlāvāntarakramābhāvād eva yājñavalkyasyeti mantavyam | na hi bhrātṛsutābhāve pitāmahasuto dhanabhāg ity evamādyavāntarakrame kaścin nyāyo 'sti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> pitāmaham atikramya tatsuto dhanabhāg iti kenocyate | bhrātaras tatsutā ity abhidhāya gotrajā ity abhidadhatā yājñavalkyenocyate | gotrajaśabdenaiva bhrātṛtatsutayor nirdeśe labhyamāne 'pi pṛthak tayor abhidhānasya gotrajeṣu pitāmahādiṣu tasya tasya saṃtatau pitṛsaṃtānāv iv dvayor eva putrapautrayor dhanabhāgitvajñāpanārthatvāt | manunāpy ayam evārthaḥ sūcyate |

	yo yo hy anantaraḥ piṇḍāt tasya tasya dhanaṃ bhavet |

	ata ūrdhvaṃ sakulyāḥ syur ācāryaḥ śiṣya eva vā ||

tad etad dhāreśvaro vyācaṣṭe: yo yo hy anantaraḥ piṇḍād ity atra piṇḍād iti padaṃ sapiṇḍād ity arthe draṣṭavyam | kaḥ punar ayam avadhibhūtaḥ sapiṇḍaḥ | pitā hared ity adhikṛtatvāt pitaiva | nanu pitur antaras tatpitā bhavati tatputraś ca | tatrobhayor vidyamānatve kasyānantaryaṃ yuktam | tatputrāṇām iti brūmaḥ | kuta etat | 'pitā hared putrasya rikthaṃ bhrātara eva vā' ity atra evakāreṇa pitāmahe rikthabhāgitvābhāvasūcanāt | tataś ca vacanād eva tulye 'py ānantarye saṃtatidvāram evānantaryam iṣyate | evaṃ ca 'yo yo hy anantaraḥ piṇḍāt' ity anena pitṛsaṃtater abhāve pitāmahasaṃtatir abhidhīyate, tasyāpy abhāve prapitāmahasaṃtatir ity evamādyāt sapiṇḍād ity anusaṃdheyam | sapiṇḍānām abhāve tu sakulyāḥ samānodakāś cātra sakulayaśabdenocyate | teṣām apy āsannasaṃtater abhāve pūrvavad viprakṛṣṭasaṃtatī rikthārheti | evaṃ ca ye — bhrātṛsutānantaraṃ pitāmaho dhanabhāk tadabhāve tatsaṃtatiḥ, evaṃ prapitāmahāder apīty āhuḥ, te nyāyasiddhakramabādhakakramāntaraparavacanasūkṣmārthajñā na bhavanti | atrāyaṃ dāyaprāptikramaḥ — bhrātṛsutābhāve pitāmahasutasya dāyaprāptiḥ, tasyābhāve prapitāmahasutasya, tasyābhāve vṛddhaprapitāmahasutasya, tasyābhāve vṛddhaprapitāmahapitṛsutasya, tasyābhāve sapiṇḍāntimapuruṣasya, tasyabhāve tatsutasya, tasyābhāve samānodakādyapuruṣasya, tasyābhāve tatsutasya, evam evoparitanaṣaṭsamānodakasaṃtatāv apy anusaṃdheyam | tad etat sarvam abhisaṃdhyāha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	bahavo jñātayo yatra sakulyā bāndhavās tathā |

	yas tv āsannataras teṣāṃ so 'napatyadhanaṃ haret ||

jñātayaḥ sapiṇḍāḥ sakulyāḥ samānodakāḥ | bāndhavās tv āsannatarāḥ krameṇaiva smṛtyantare pradarśitāḥ |

	ātampitṛṣvasuḥ putrā ātmamātṛṣvasuḥ sutāḥ |

	ātamamātulaputrāś ca vijñeyā ātmabāndhavāḥ ||

	pituḥ pitṛṣvasuḥ putrāḥ pitur mātṛṣavasuḥ sutāḥ |

	pitur mātulaputrāś ca vijñeyāḥ pitṛbāndhavāḥ ||

	mātuḥ pitṛṣvasuḥ putrāḥ mātur mātṛṣvasuḥ sutāḥ |

	mātur mātulaputrāś ca vijñeyā mātṛbāndhavāḥ || iti |

jñātisakulyabandhuṣu vācanikāsannatarābhāve yathā kathaṃcid apy āsannatarā mṛgyāḥ, "piṇḍagotraṛṣisaṃbandhā rikthaṃ bhajeran" iti sāmānyena gautamasmaraṇāt | bandhūnām abhāve ke dhanabhāja ity apekṣite yājñavalkyaḥ: "śiṣyasabrahmacāriṇaḥ" iti | dhanabhāja iti śeṣaḥ | upanīya vedam adhyāpitaḥ śiṣyaḥ, ekācāryaḥ sabrahmacārī | śiṣyopādhyāyasaṃbandhena dhanasaṃbandhe guṇabūtasya śiṣyasya kathite pradhānabhūtācāryasya daṇḍāpūpanyāyāt bandhvabhāve prathamaṃ dhanasaṃbandho jñāyate iti matvācāryasyātrānabhidhānam iti mantavyam | sabrahmacāryabhāve ke dhanabhāgina ity apekṣite manuḥ |

	sarveṣām apy abhāve tu brāhmaṇā rikthabhāginaḥ |

	traividyāḥ śucayo dāntāḥ tathā dharmo na hīyate ||

	ahāryaṃ brāhmaṇadravyaṃ rājñā nityam iti sthitiḥ || iti |

manūktalakṣaṇabrāhmaṇābhāve rājānaṃ praty āha nāradaḥ |

	brāhmaṇārthasya tannāśe dāyādaś cen na kaścana |

	brāhmaṇāyaiva dātavyam enasvī syān nṛpo 'nyathā ||

tannāśe arthasvāmināśe | brāhmanetarārthasya tannāśe tv āha manuḥ |

	itareṣāṃ tu varṇānāṃ sarvābhāve haren nṛpaḥ | iti |

nṛpo janapadapuraparipālanādikartā | sarveṣām abhāve rājagāmi dhanam ity anuvṛttau nāradaḥ |

	anyatra brāhmaṇāt kiṃ tu rājā dharmaparāyaṇaḥ |

	tatstrīṇāṃ jīvanaṃ dadyād eṣa dāyavidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ||

tatstrīṇāṃ brāhmaṇetaradhanasvāmistrīṇāṃ dhanabhāgitvānarhāṇām ity arthaḥ | sarveṣām abhāve ity atra varṇabhedanibandhanaviśeṣam āha saṃgrahakāraḥ |

	pitary avidyamāne 'pi dhanaṃ tatpitṛsaṃtateḥ |

	tasyām avidyamānāyāṃ tatpitāmahasaṃtateḥ ||

	asatyām api tasyāṃ tu prapitāmahasaṃtateḥ |

	evam evoparitanāḥ sapiṇḍā rikthabhāginaḥ ||

	tadabhāve sakulyāḥ syur ācāryaḥ śiṣya eva vā |

	sabrahmacārī sadviprāḥ purvābhāve paraḥ paraḥ ||

	śūdrasyaikodarābhāve rājā dhanam avāpnuyāt |

	ācāryasyāpy abhāve tu tathā kṣatriyavaiśyayoḥ || 

iti saṃgrahakārasya dhāreśvaramatānusāritvāt pitary avidyamāne 'pi dhanaṃ tatpitṛsaṃtateḥ ity abhidhānānam | asmin mate tu pitary avidyamāne tu mātur dhanam, tadabhāve pitāmahyāḥ, tadabhāve dhanikapitṛsaṃtateḥ bhrātṛtatsutarūpāyā ity anusaṃdheyam | evam uktam aputradhanaviṣayaṃ sarvaṃ yathāyogyam anupanītopakurvāṇabrahmacārisamāvṛttagṛhasthāśramāntarabahirbhūtasnātakasvāmiviṣayam, naiṣṭhikavanasthayatisvāmikadhanaviṣaye tu grāhakāntarasmaraṇāt | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	vānaprasthayatibrahmacāriṇāṃ rikthabhāginaḥ |

	krameṇācāryasacchiṣyadharmabhrātrekatīrthinaḥ ||

brahmacāry atra yatisāhacaryān naiṣṭhiko 'vagamyate | dharmabhrātā samānācāryakaḥ | ekatīrthaḥ samānaśāstrakaḥ krameṇa pūrvapūrvābhāve paraḥ para ity arthaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ duhitrādiviṣayāṇi**

**atha saṃsṛṣṭabhrātrādiviṣayāṇi kānicid vacanāni likhyante**

atra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	vibhakto yaḥ punaḥ pitrā bhrātrā vaikatra saṃsthitaḥ |

	pitṛvyeṇātha vā prītyā tatsaṃsṛṣṭaḥ sa ucyate ||

yaḥ putrādiḥ pitradinā saha vibhaktaḥ san punaḥ prītyādinimittena vibhaktenaiva yena pitrādinā sahavāsam āpannaḥ sa tena saṃsṛṣṭa ity ucyata ity arthaḥ | idaṃ cātrārthād avagamyate — pitṛbhrātṛpitṛvyavyatiriktena bhrātṛpitṛvyaputrādinā saha saṃsargo na vidyata iti | sahavāse puruṣāṇām āhatya saṃsargābhāvāt dhanadvāreṇa saṃsargo vācya itīdaṃtāvyavahāranimittabhūtāvacchedakāpanodena vibhaktānāṃ pūrvavad ekarāśīkaraṇaparyantaḥ saṃsargo na punaḥ sahavāsamātram iti mantavyam | ata eva punaḥ kriyamāṇadhanavibhāgam anūdya tatra prakāraviśeṣam āha manuḥ |

	vibhaktāḥ sahajīvanto vibhajeran punar yadi |

	samas tatra vibhāgaḥ syāj jyaiṣṭhyaṃ tatra na vidyate ||

sahajīvantaḥ sahavāsena jīvantaḥ | vibhajeran saṃsṛṣṭadhanam iti śeṣaḥ | tatra saṃsṛṣṭadhanavibhāge samavibhāgavidhānād eva siddhe jyaiṣṭhyanimittakāṃśāgrahaṇe punar jyaiṣṭhyanimittakabhāgavaiṣamyaniṣedho 'yaṃ svalpadhanasaṃsarganimittakabhāgavaiṣamyānujñānārthaḥ | tena saṃsargasamaye yadīyaṃ yāvatsaṃsṛṣṭaṃ tadanusāreṇa saṃsṛṣṭavibhāgavaiṣamyaṃ kalpanīyam | evaṃ ca dhanasyedaṃtāpanodāya saṃsargo na punar iyattāpanodāyeti mantavyam | anyad api bhāgavaiṣamyaṃ nimittāntarakṛtam āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	saṃsṛṣṭānāṃ tu yaḥ kaścid vidyāśauryādinādhikam |

	prāpnoti tasya dātavyo dvyaṃśaḥ śeṣāḥ samāṃśinaḥ ||

tasmin prāptādhikadhana iti śeṣaḥ | saṃsṛṣṭavyānuparodhenārjite 'pi vibhājyatvavidhānārtham etat | saṃsṛṣṭānāṃ madhye punar vibhāgakaraṇād arvāk pramītasya putrādisadbhāve,

	pramītapitṛkāṇāṃ tu pitṛto bhāgakalpanā |

iti vidhinā vibhāgaḥ kartavyaḥ, vidhānāntarāsmaraṇāt, putrādyabhāve tu na patnīduhitṛnyāyaḥ, vidhānāntarasmaraṇāt | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	vibhaktā bhrātaro ye tu saṃprītyaikatra saṃsthitāḥ |

	punar vibhāgakaraṇe teṣāṃ jyaiṣṭhyaṃ na vidyate ||

	yadā kaścit pramīyeta pravrajed vā kathaṃcana |

	na lupyate tasya bhāgaḥ sodarasya vidhīyate || iti |

yathā prathamavibhāgakaraṇāt pūrvaṃ mṛtasyāputrasya pravrajitasya vā bhāgo lupyate, vibhāgābhāvena taddhetukāyā iyattāyā abhāvāt, tena sarvaṃ rikthaṃ sahavāsina eva tatra sarve gṛhṇanti, na tathātra vibhāgahetukāyā iyattāyāḥ abhāvaḥ, prathamavibhāgenaiveyattāyāḥ kṛtatvāt | na ca saṃsargāt sā apaiti, tasyedantāmātrāpanodakatvāt | tena na sarvaṃ rikthaṃ saṃsṛṣṭina eva sarve gṛhṇīyuḥ, kiṃ tu vibhāgakāle tattadbhāgaḥ pṛthaguddharaṇīyaḥ | sa ca vibhaktapatibhāgaviṣaya ivādau na patnyāḥ, kiṃ tu saṃsṛṣṭisodarasya bhrātur vacanena vidhīyate | sodarasyety ekavacanam avivakṣitam | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	bhrātṝṇām aprajāḥ preyāt kaścic cet pravrajeta vā |

	vibhajeyur dhanaṃ tasya śeṣās te strīdhanaṃ vinā ||

śeṣāḥ saṃsṛṣṭinaḥ sodarabhrātaraḥ,

	saṃsṛṣṭinas tu saṃsṛṣṭī sodarasya tu sodaraḥ |

iti yājñavalkyasmaraṇāt | saṃsṛṣṭino bhrātur dhanaṃ saṃsṛṣṭy eva bhrātā haret na patnyādiḥ, tatrāpi sodara evety arthaḥ | evaṃ tarhy atra mṛtasya patnīnām aprattaduhitṝṇāṃ ca kā gatir ity apekṣite 'py āha nāradaḥ |

	bharaṇaṃ cāsya kurvīran strīṇām ā jīvitakṣayāt |

	rakṣanti śayyāṃ bhartuś ced ācchindyur itarāsu tat ||

	yā tasya duhitā tasyāḥ pitryo 'ṃśo bharaṇe mataḥ |

	ā saṃskārād dhared bhāgaṃ parato bibhṛyāt patiḥ || iti |

tasya mṛtasya pravrajitasya vā yā duhitā tasyāḥ pariṇayanam, tataḥ pūrvaṃ bharaṇaṃ ca śeṣā eva kurvīrann iti dvitīyaślokasya tātparyārthaḥ pretyetavyaḥ | yatra punaḥ śeṣeṣu bhrātṛṣv asaṃsṛṣṭā api sodarāḥ kecit santi tatra ye saṃsṛṣṭāḥ sodarās ta eva vibhajeyuḥ |

	saṃsṛṣṭānāṃ tu yo bhāgas teṣām eva sa iṣyate |

iti prastutya bhrātṝṇām aprajā ity uktam | yatra tv asaṃsṛṣṭāḥ sarve sodarāḥ bhinnodarās tu saṃsṛṣṭāḥ tatra sodarā eva asaṃsṛṣṭā api tasya dhanaṃ vibhajeran na tu bhinoodarāḥ saṃsṛṣṭāḥ,

	saṃsṛṣṭy api cādadyāt saṃsṛṣṭo nānyamātṛjaḥ |

iti yājñavalkyasmaraṇāt | asaṃsṛṣṭy apīty apiśabdāt anyamātṛjasya saṃsṛṣṭitvaviśiṣṭasya ādānapratiṣedhaḥ avagamyate | yadā tu śeṣeṣu sodarābhāvaḥ tadā bhinnodarāṃs saṃsṛṣṭā vibhajeyuḥ,

	saṃsṛṣṭau yau punaḥ prītyā tau parasparabhāginau |

iti bṛhaspatismaraṇāt | atra bhinnamātṛkāv iti paunaruktyaparihārāya gamyate | yat tu yājñavalkyoktam,

	anyodaryas tu saṃsṛṣṭī nānyodaryo dhanaṃ haret |

iti, tat sodaryasadbhāvaviṣayam ity aviruddham | yady asaṃsṛṣṭānām ekodarāṇām abhāva eva saṃsṛṣṭabhinnodarāṇāṃ dhanagrahaṇaṃ tarhi,

	yeṣāṃ jyeṣṭhaḥ kaniṣṭho vā hīyetāṃśapradānataḥ |

	mriyetānyataro vāpi tasya bhāgo na lupyate ||

	sodaryā vibhajeraṃs taṃ sametya sahitāḥ samam |

	bhrātaro ye ca saṃsṛṣṭā bhaginyaś ca sanābhayaḥ ||

iti manuvacanavirodhaḥ syāt | caśabdadvayena sarveṣāṃ ślokoktānāṃ sodarabhrātṛbhaginyasodarabhrātṝṇām itaretarayuktānāṃ vibhāgāvagateḥ | kiṃ ca saṃsṛṣṭā bhinnodarabhrātaras taiḥ sahitāḥ sodaryāḥ sanābhayo bhaginyaḥ sametya tam aluptabhāgaṃ samaṃ vibhajerann ity evānvayān militānām eva kartṛtā sahitasarvaśabdābhyāṃ suvyakteti vyakto nirodhaḥ | kecid virodhaparihārārtham idaṃ vacanam evaṃ vyācakṣire: "tam aluptabhāgaṃ sodarā yadā saṃsṛṣṭinaḥ tadā ta eva gṛhṇīyuḥ, nāsaṃsṛṣṭinaḥ sodarā api | saṃsṛṣṭīnāṃ sodarāṇām abhāve sarve sodarāḥ sametya militāh sahitāḥ samapradhānabhāvena samaṃ anyūnādhikaṃ vibhajeran | sodarāṇām abhāve bhaginyaḥ sanābhayo vibhajeran | tāsām apy abhāve anyodaryā bhrātaraḥ" iti | tad etat anekādhyāhārakaraṇād atyantāsamañjastvāc copekṣaṇīyam | anye punar virodhaparihārārtham,

	anyodaryas tu saṃsṛṣṭī nānyodaryo dhanaṃ haret |

	asaṃsṛṣṭy api cādadyāt saṃsṛṣṭo nānyamātṛjaḥ ||

iti yājñavalkyavacanaṃ paṭhitvā tadvacanaṃ yathā pratīyamānamānavavacanasamānārthatayā vyākurvate | tatra tāvat "anyodaryas tu saṃsṛṣṭī nānyodaryo dhanaṃ haret | asaṃsṛṣṭī" ity etāvato bhāgasyākṣarārthatātparyārthau vyākhyātau | anyodaryo yaḥ sāpatno bhrātā saṃsṛṣṭidhanaṃ haret na punar anyodaryo dhanaṃ haret asaṃsṛṣṭī | anenānvayavyatirekābhyām anyodaryasya saṃsṛṣṭitvaṃ dhanagrahaṇe kāraṇam uktam iti | api cādadyāt asaṃsṛṣṭī" (?) ity etāvatā madhyamabhāgena saha saṃbandham asaṃsṛṣṭīti pūrvabhāgasyābhidhāyākṣarārthasahitaḥ tātparyārtho vyākhyātaḥ | asaṃsṛṣṭīty etad uttareṇāpi saṃbadhyate | tataś cāsaṃsṛṣṭy api saṃsṛṣṭino dhanam ādadīta | ko 'sāv ity ata āha "saṃsṛṣṭaḥ" iti | saṃsṛṣṭaḥ ekodarasaṃsṛṣṭaḥ sodarya iti yāvat | anenāsaṃsṛṣṭasyāpi sodaryadhanagrahaṇe sodaratvaṃ kāraṇam uktam iti | nānyamātṛja iti bhāgasyāpy evakārādhyāhāraṃ kṛtvā tena saha saṃbandhaṃ saṃsṛṣṭa iti madhyamabhāgāntargatasya padasyābhidhāyākṣarārtho vyākhyātaḥ | saṃsṛṣṭa ity uttareṇāpi saṃbadhyate | tatra ca saṃsṛṣṭaḥ saṃsṛṣṭīty arthaḥ | nānyamātṛja ity atra evaśabdādhyāhāreṇa vyākhyānaṃ kāryam | saṃsṛṣṭy apy anyamātṛja eva sodarasahitaḥ saṃsṛṣṭino dhanaṃ nādadīteti kṛtsnaślokasya ca tātparyartho mānavavacanasamānārthatayā darśitaḥ | evaṃ ca "asaṃsṛṣṭy api cādadyāt" ity apiśabdaśravaṇāt "saṃsṛṣṭo nānyamātṛjaḥ" ity avadhāraṇaniṣedhād asaṃsṛṣṭasodarasya saṃsṛṣṭabhinnodarasya ca vibhajyagrahaṇaṃ kartavyam ity uktaṃ bhavati | dvayor api dhanagrahaṇakāraṇasyaivaikasya sadbhāvād iti | tad etat evaṃ vyākhyātṛbhyaḥ tebhya eva rocate, na punaḥ pratipattṛbhyaḥ, vacanato 'tyantāpratīyamānasyaiva svaprajñābalād vacanārthakaraṇāt | tasmād atra manuvacanayājñavalkyavacanayor yathāpratīyamānārthaparayor viṣayavyavasthayaivāvirodho vācyo na punar arthaikyābhidhānakleśād iti saivocyate | manuvacanaṃ tāvat sthāvarataditaradhanasadbhāvaviṣayam, prajāpatinā tatraiva saṃsṛṣṭāsaṃsṛṣṭānāṃ vibhajyadhanagrahaṇavidhānāt |

	antardhanaṃ ca yad dravyaṃ saṃsṛṣṭānāṃ ca tad bhavet |

	bhūmiṃ gṛhaṃ cāsaṃsṛṣṭāḥ pragṛhṇīyur yathāṃśataḥ || iti |

saṃsṛṣṭānāṃ bhinnodarabhrātṝṇāṃ yathāṃśato gūḍhadhanaṃ jaṅgamaṃ ca dvipadacatuṣpadādirūpaṃ bhavet | asaṃsṛṣṭāḥ sodarabhrātṛbhaginyas tu gṛhakṣetraṃ yathāṃśataḥ pragṛhṇīyur ity arthaḥ | evaṃ ca pāriśeṣyāt kevalasthāvarasadbhāvaviṣaye kevalasthāvaretarasadbhāvaviṣaye vā yājñavalkyavacanaṃ draṣṭavyam | yadā tu śeṣabhūtasaṃsṛṣṭabhinnodarā eva tadā pitā pitṛvyo vā yaḥ saṃsṛṣṭaḥ sa eva gṛhṇīyāt, "saṃsṛṣṭini prete saṃsṛṣṭo rikthabhāk" iti gautamasmaraṇāt | yadā tu pitā pitṛvyo vā saṃsṛṣṭo na vidyate tadā tv asaṃsṛṣṭabhinnodaro bhrātā gṛhṇīyāt | tadabhāve tv asaṃsṛṣṭaḥ pitā, tadabhāve mātā, tadabhāve patnī | tathā ca śaṅkhaḥ: "svaryātasya hy aputrasya bhrātṛgāmi dravyaṃ tadabhāve pitarau hareyātāṃ jyeṣṭhā vā patnī" iti | svaryātasya hy aputrasya pitrā pitṛvyeṇa va saṃsṛṣṭasya saṃsṛṣṭyabhāve bhinnodarāsaṃsarge bhrātṛgāmi dravyam ity arthaḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	saṃsṛṣṭānāṃ tu yo bhāgas teṣām eva sa iṣyate |

	ato 'nyathāṃśato bhājo nirbījeṣv itarān iyāt ||

ato 'nyathā saṃsṛṣṭeṣu satsu bhinnodarabhrātrādyasaṃsṛṣṭino nāṃśabhājaḥ | yadā tu sarve saṃsṛṣṭāḥ nirbījāḥ prajārahitā bhavanti tadā cetarān bhinnodarabhrātrādīn asaṃsṛṣṭān iyāt saṃsṛṣṭānāṃ bhāgaṃ prāpnuyād ity arthaḥ | tatra cāyam "bhrātṛgāmi dravyam" ityādiśaṅkhavacanoktakramo draṣṭavyaḥ | jyeṣṭhāgrahaṇaṃ susaṃyatatvādiguṇavatyāḥ kathanārtham, na punar madhyamādinivṛttyartham | punar api tadabhāva iti vaktavye vāśabdaḥ prayuktaḥ, phalasāmyāt | tathā hi, vāśabdād vikalpo gamyate | na cātra svāmyarūpe vastuni tulyavikalpaḥ saṃbhavati, "na hi vastuni vikalpaḥ" iti nyāyaśāstre siddhatvāt | tadmād atra vāśabdād abhāvavikalpāvagateḥ phalasāmyam asty eva | evaṃ cāyaṃ kramaḥ: bhrātrabhāve pita haret tadabhāve mātā tadabhāve patnīti | tataś ca vibhaktaviṣayoktapatnīduhitrādikramaviruddhatvāt tadavirodhāyaitat saṃsṛṣṭāṃśaviṣayam iti kalpyate | vibhaktaviṣayoktanaiyāyikapatnīduhitrādikramo 'smin viṣaye śaṅkhoktavācanikakrameṇa bādhyate | vācanika evāyaṃ kramaḥ, asmin krame kasycin nyāyasyābhāvāt | anena vyutkrameṇa yadā patnīnām āgataṃ dhanaṃ bhrātṛputrādayaś ca sapiṇḍā vidyante tadā tv āha nāradaḥ |

	mṛte patyau tu bhāryāḥ syur abhrātṛpitṛmātṛkāḥ |

	sarve sapiṇḍāḥ svadhanaṃ vibhajeyur yathāṃśataḥ ||

bhāryāḥ patnyāḥ | abhrātṛpitṛmātṛkāḥ yāḥ patyur bhrātṛpitṛmātaraḥ sāsām abhāvaviśiṣṭā ity arthaḥ | anena dvandvasamāse bhrātrapekṣayābhyarhitaṃ pitṛpadasya pūrvanipātanaṃ parityajya vaiparītyena samāsaracanāṃ kurvatā nāradena saṃsṛṣṭāputradhanaṃ prathamato bhrātṛgāmi tadabhāve pitṛgāmi tadabhāve mātṛgāmi tadabhāve sarvavṛttasthapatnyabhigāmīti darśitam | saṃsṭṣṭaviṣaye patnīnāṃ na gauṇaputrābhāve dāyaharatvam, kiṃ tu bhinnodarāsaṃsṛṣṭabhrātṛpitṛmātṝṇām apy abhāv it mantavyam | sarve sapiṇḍā ityāder ayam arthaḥ: saṃsṛṣṭāputrasya ye bhrātṛpitṛmātṛvyatiriktāḥ sapiṇḍāḥ bhrātṛputrādayas te svadhanaṃ pūrvam aputradhanena saha svapitrādisaṃsṛṣṭaṃ tadūrdhvaṃ tatpatnībhiḥ saha yathāṃśato bhrātṛputrāṇāṃ bhrātraṃśo bhāryāṇāṃ bhartraṃśa ity aṃśānatikrameṇa vibhajeyur iti | patnīnām abhāve tu saṃsṛṣṭāputrāṃśaṃ tadbhaginī labhate | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	yā tasya bhaginī sā tu tato 'ṃśāl labdhum arhati |

	anapatyasya dharmo 'yam abhāryāpitṛkasya ca ||

	sā ca dattā tv adattā vā sodare tu mṛte sati |

	tasyāṃśaṃ tu haret saiva dvayor vyaktaṃ hi kāraṇam ||

abhrātṛmātṛkasya ceti caśabdārthaḥ | bhaginyabhāve tu kevalāḥ sapiṇḍāḥ saṃsṛṣṭāṃśam,

	anantaraḥ sapiṇḍād yas tasya dhanaṃ bhavet |

ityuktakrameṇa vibhajeran, pratipadoktānām abhāvāt | tathā ca sa eva |

	mṛto 'napatyo 'bhāryaś ced abhrātṛpitṛmātṛkaḥ |

	sarve sapiṇḍās taddāyaṃ vibhajeran yathāṃśataḥ ||

taddāyaṃ saṃsṛṣṭadāyam | mṛto 'napatyo bhinnamātṛko bhrātrādipratipadoktadhanagrāhitvarahitaś ced iti pūrvārdhasya tātparyārthaḥ | sapiṇḍābhāve tu vibhaktasaṃsthitadravyavad eva saṃsṛṣṭasvaryātadravyam api samānodakādigāmīty anusaṃdheyam | saṃsṛṣṭadravyam adhikṛtya sapiṇḍebhyaḥ ūrdhvaṃ viśeṣāsmṛteḥ | 

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ saṃsṛṣṭabhrātrādiviṣayāṇi**

**atha vibhaktaputrādivibhāgaḥ**

atra jīvadvibhāgottarakālajātaṃ putraṃ praty āha viṣṇuḥ: "pitṛvibhāgānantarotpannasya bhāgaṃ dadyuḥ" iti | asyārthaḥ: avispaṣṭagarbhāyāṃ pitṛbharyāyāṃ ye putrāḥ pitrā vibhaktās te svavibhāgottarakālajasya putrasya tatsaṃbhājñānataḥ svabhāgapraviṣṭatadbhāgam uddhṛtya dadyur iti | pitā tu svabhāgapraviṣṭatadbhāgāṃśaṃ na dadyāt, kiṃ tu pūrvajair dattān aṃśān gṛhītvā vibhaktajena saha vaset | tasyāprāptavyavahārasya sahavāsena pālanīyatvāt | ata eva "pitṛvibhaktāḥ bhāgaṃ dadyuḥ" ity uktam, na punaḥ pitā pitṛvibhaktāś ca bhāgaṃ dadyur iti | yat tu gautamenoktam: "vibhaktajaḥ pitryam eva" iti, bhāgaṃ gṛhṇīyād iti śeṣaḥ | tad etat pitṛvibhaktaputrair vibhaktajasya bhāgadānāt prāg eva mṛte pitari draṣṭavyam | tathā ca pūrvajair bhāgo na deyaḥ, pityam evety evakārakaraṇāt | yat tu bṛhaspatinoktam,

	pitrā saha vibhaktā ye sāpatnā vā sahodarāḥ |

	jaghanyajās tu ye teṣāṃ pitṛbhāgaharās tu te ||

iti, tatra pitṛbhāgaharā ity asya pitṛbhāga eva bhāgaharā ity artho 'vagantavyaḥ | tad etat vibhād ūrdhvam eva ye garbhasthā bhūtvā jātās tadviṣayam | jaghanyajānāṃ pitṛbhāgād eva bhāgaharatve kāraṇam apy āha sa eva |

	anīśaḥ pūrvajaḥ pitrye bhrātṛbhāge vibhaktajaḥ |

anīśaḥ asvāmī | anīśaḥ pūrvajaḥ pitrya ity atra pitrā saha vibhaktatvād ity abhiprāyaḥ pratyetavyaḥ | bhrātṛbhāge vibhaktaja ity atra tu bhrātṛbhāge vibhaktajadhanasaṃkramaṇābhāvād ity abhiprāyo 'dhyavaseyaḥ | prathamoktābhiprāyeṇa vibhaktāgrajānām anīśatāṃ pitrye prasādhya tadbalād anyad apy āha sa eva |

	putraiḥ saha vibhaktena pitrā yat svayam ārjitam |

	vibhaktajasya tat sarvam anīśāḥ pūrvajāḥ smṛtāḥ ||

sarvagrahaṇaṃ vibhāgāt paścād ārjite pitrye pūrvajānāṃ sutānām agṛhītāṃśatvenāṃśo 'stīti śaṅkānivṛttyartham | evaṃ ca pūrvajās taditarāś cānyonyam asaṃbandhijanavad asvāminaḥ parasparadhane, kiṃ tv īṣad atra bhedo 'stīty āha sa eva |

	yathā dhane tathā carṇe dānādhānakrayeṣu ca |

	parasparam anīśās te muktvāśaucodakakriyāḥ ||

kevalam āśaucodakakriyādau parasparam īśā na dhanādāv ity arthaḥ | ādhānam ādhiḥ | uktam ṛṇādāv anīśatvaṃ saṃsargābhāve satīty āha sa eva |

	saṃsṛṣṭau yau punaḥ prītyā tau parasparabhāginau | iti |

yat punar manunoktam,

	ūrdhvaṃ vibhāgāj jātas tu pitryam eva hared dhanam |

	saṃsṛṣṭās tena vā ye syuḥ vibhajeta sa taiḥ saha ||

iti, tatra pitryam evety uttarārdhe 'pi saṃbadhyate | ato na prāguktena viruddham | tad etad vibhaktajena pituḥ sahavāsadaśāyāṃ mṛte pitari draṣṭavyam | ajīvadvibhāgottarakālajātaṃ tu putraṃ praty āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	vibhakteṣu suto jātaḥ savarṇāyāṃ vibhāgabhāk |

	dṛśyād vā tadvibhāgaḥ syād āyavyayaviśodhitāt ||

pitur ūrdhvam avispaṣṭagarbhāyāṃ pitṛbhāryāyāṃ bhrātṛṣu parasparaṃ vibhakteṣu paścāt suto yo jātaḥ sa vibhāgabhāk, bhāga eva vibhāgaḥ taṃ labhata iti yāvat | sarvasmād vibhaktatadhanād uddhṛtya bhāgabhāg iti yāvat | yad vā, dṛśyāt dṛśyamānagṛhopaskaravāhyadohyābharaṇabhṛtyādeḥ sakāśād evāyavyayaviśodhitāt upacayāpacayābhyām avadhāriteyattādikād vibhaktād uddhṛto bhāgas tasya vibhaktajasya syād ity arthaḥ | dṛśyagrahaṇaṃ gūḍhadravyajātād vibhaktād ūddhṛtyāṃśakalpanānivṛttyartham | vibhaktajasya sutatvāviśeṣe 'pi vibhāgakāle durvijñeyasadbhāvaśālitvāt tatra bhāge hāsakaraṇaṃ nyāyyam iti manvānena pakṣāntaram uktam iti mantavyam | durvijñeyatatsadbhāvatā na taddoṣakṛteti prathamapakṣo 'pi nātyantānucita iti mantavyam | yatra punar vibhaktāgatasya hrāsapakṣa eva na samānabhāgapakṣāntaronmeṣaḥ | ata eva tatra hrāsabhāgam evāha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	gotrasādhāraṇaṃ tyaktvā yo 'nyaṃ deśaṃ samāśritaḥ |

	ardhatas tv āgatasyāṃśaḥ pradātavyo na saṃśayaḥ ||

gotrasādhāraṇaṃ tyaktvā sarvasahavāsanivāsadeśam utsṛjya yo 'tyantadūradeśanivāsī svasadbhāvājñānataḥ śeṣair eva vibhajya sarvasmin dhane gṛhīte paścād āgatasyāṃśo 'rdhato vibhaktadravyārdhād uddhṛtya dātavya ity arthaḥ | atretareṣāṃ vibhaktāgatasadbhāvājñānaṃ taddoṣanibandhanam iti na pakṣāntaronmeṣaḥ | ata eva na saṃśaya ity uktam | evam atidīrghakalaproṣitasya sadbhāvājñānataḥ kṛte vibhāge saty āgatasyāpīty āha sa eva |

	ṛṇaṃ lekhyaṃ gṛhaṃ kṣetraṃ yasya paitāmahaṃ bhavet |

	cirakālaproṣito 'pi bhāgabhāg āgatas tu saḥ ||

bhāgabhāk ardhabāg ity arthaḥ | āgato vibhāgād ūrdhvam āgataḥ | pautrādis tu vibhaktāgataḥ kramāyātadravyamātre 'ṃśabhāg ity āha sa eva |

	tṛtīyaḥ pañcamaś caiva saptamo yo 'pi vā bhavet |

	janmanām aparijñāne labhetāṃśaṃ kramāgate ||

kasyacid vibhaktāgatasya kramāgateṣv api bhūmātre 'ṃśo deya ity āha sa eva |

	yaṃ paramparayā maulāḥ samastāḥ svāminaṃ viduḥ |

	tadanvayasyāgatasya dātavyā gotrajair mahī ||

āgatasya vibhāgād ūrdhvam iti śeṣaḥ | vibhāgād ūrdhvam āgatasya pūrvam āgatasya vā svabhāgaṃ grahītuṃ pravṛttasya dṛṣṭādṛṣṭapramāṇenādau tāvad ātmanaḥ parāyatte dravye svāmyaṃ sādhayato bhāgaharaṇe 'dhikāro bhavati nānyathety āha sa eva |

	kṛte 'kṛte vā vibhāge rikthī yatra pravartate |

	sāmānyaṃ ced bhāvayati tatra bhāgaharas tu saḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ vibhaktajaputrādivibhāgaḥ**

**athāvaluptavibhāgaḥ**

tatra manuḥ |

	ṛṇe dhane ca sarvasmin pravibhakte yathāvidhi |

	paścād dṛśyeta yat kiṃcit tat sarvaṃ samatāṃ nayet ||

vibhāgakāle yad dṛśyate ṛṇaṃ dhanaṃ vā sarvasmin tasmin yathāvidhi,

	pitṛrikthaharāḥ putrāḥ sarva eva samāṃśinaḥ |

	vidyākarmayutas teṣām adhikaṃ labdhum arhati ||

ityādividhyanatikrameṇa vibhakte paścāt kālāntare yat kiṃcid ṛṇaṃ proṣitottamarṇasya yat kiṃcid dhanaṃ proṣitanikṣepadhārakādisamīpasthaṃ tayoḥ samāgamādivaśād dṛśyate tat sarvaṃ samatāṃ nayet | na punar vidhyākarmayute 'dhikatām ity arthaḥ | paścād dṛṣṭe ṛṇe samatāni yamāt pūrvadṛṣṭe ṛṇe dhanavad viṣamatāstīti gamyate | evaṃ vibhāgakāle yad vastu yena kenacid vañcakena parakīyabuddhyutpādanādinā pracchāditaṃ vibhāgottarakāle vicāryamāṇe svakīyam eva jñātaṃ cet tatsamatāṃ nayed ity āha kātyayanaḥ |

	pracchāditaṃ yadi dhanaṃ punar āsādya tatsamam |

	bhajeran bhrātṛbhiḥ sārdham abhāve hi pituḥ sutāḥ ||

pitur abhāve sarve sutā eva tadāsāditaṃ vibhajerann ity arthaḥ | evaṃ sahavāsiṣu kenacit kiṃcid dhanam apahṛtaṃ kathaṃcid vibhāgād ūrdhvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ cet samatāṃ nayet | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	anyonyāpahṛtaṃ dravyaṃ vibhakte yat tu dṛśyate |

	tat punas te samair aṃśair vibhajerann iti sthitiḥ ||

te sarve vibhaktā ity arthaḥ | apahṛtavad durvibhaktam api samatāṃ nayet | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	anyonyāpahṛtaṃ dravyaṃ durvibhaktaṃ ca tad bhavet |

	paścāt prāptaṃ vibhajyeta samabhāgena tad bhṛguḥ ||

durvibhaktam aśāstroktaprakāreṇa viṣamatayā vibhaktaṃ mitho 'pahṛtadurvibhaktavad anyāpahṛtaṃ naṣṭalabdhaṃ ca samatāṃ nayet | tathā vibhaktenārjitaṃ dhanaṃ tv ārjakasyaiva bhavati na dāyādasyety āha sa eva |

	vibhaktenaiva yat prāptaṃ dhanaṃ tasyaiva tad bhavet |

	hṛtaṃ naṣṭaṃ ca yal labdhaṃ prāguktaṃ ca punar bhajet ||

prāguktaṃ mitho 'pahṛtaṃ durvibhaktaṃ ca, dṛṣṭāntārtham atra punar anayor upādānam | evaṃ ca prāguktavat vibhajerann ity arthaḥ | tena parāpahṛtasya naṣṭalabdhasya ca samam eva vibhajanam anenoktam iti mantavyam | evaṃ manvādibhir vibhāgāt paścād dṛśyamānamātrasyaiva sādhāraṇadravyasya vibhāgavidhānāt, pūrvakṛtavibhāgaḥ samyak jāta iti gamyate | tena vibhāgād ūrdhvaṃ kiṃcit sāmānyadravyadarśane 'pi puruṣāṇāṃ vibhaktatvaṃ pūrvam eva saṃpannam iti mantavyam | yat punar manunoktam,

	vibhāge tu kṛte kiṃcit sāmānyaṃ yatra dṛśyate |

	nāsau vibhāgo vijñeyaḥ kartavyaḥ punar eva hi ||

iti, tat vibhaktair vibhaktadravyeṣv āyavyayādikaraṇāt prāg eva dṛṣṭaviṣaye draṣṭavyam | anyathā pūrvoktasarvavacanavirodhāpatteḥ | punarvibhāgavidhānasya prayojanaṃ paścād dṛṣṭāṃśe 'py uddhārādikaraṇam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ avaluptavibhāgaḥ **

**atha vibhaktakṛtyam**

tatra nāradaḥ |

	yady ekajātā bahavaḥ pṛthagdharmāḥ pṛthakkriyāḥ |

	pṛthakkarmaguṇopetā na cet kāryeṣu saṃmatāḥ ||

	svabhāgān yadi dadyus te vikrīṇīrann athāpi vā |

	kuryur yatheṣṭaṃ tat sarvam īśās te svadhanasya vai ||

asyārthaḥ: ekasmāj jātā yadi bahavo 'nekadhā vibhaktāḥ tathā pṛthak pṛthak parasparānumatim antareṇa dhanasādhyāgnihotrādikarmakāriṇaḥ syuḥ, tathaiva vibhaktavyayāyattakṛṣyādilaukikakriyākāriṇo bhaveyuḥ, tathā vibhinnabhāṇḍādikarmāṅgadravyopetāḥ syuḥ, tathā svakaryeṣu bhrātaro na cet saṃmatāḥ tadā tān anādṛtya svakāryaṃ kuryuḥ | tathā te vibhaktā yadi svabhāgāt dadyur vikrīnīyur athāpi vā tat sarvaṃ yatheṣṭaṃ kuryuḥ yatas te vibhaktāḥ svatantrāḥ svāmina iti yāvat | yat tu bṛhaspatinoktam,

	vibhaktā vāvibhaktā vā dāyādāḥ sthāvare samāḥ |

	eko hy anīśaḥ sarvatra dānādhamanavikraye ||

iti, ādhamanam ādhīkaraṇam | tad etad yatra samatayā sthāvaravibhāgam atiduṣkaraṃ matvā tatphalam eva phalakāle vibhajya grahīṣyāma ity abhisaṃdhinā taditaradhanavibhāgato dāyādā vibhaktā bhavanti tadviṣayam, tatra sthāvare tv ekaikasya svatantrasvāmitvābhāvāt | vibhaktasya kṛtyāntaram apy āha sa eva |

	yenāṃśo yādṛśo bhuktaḥ tasya tan na vicālayet | iti |

tathā rājānaṃ praty āha |

	sa rājñāṃśe svake sthāpyaḥ śāsanīyo 'nubandhakṛt |

anubandho nibandhaḥ āgraha iti yāvat ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ vibhaktakṛtyaviṣayāṇi**

**atha vibhāgataddharmasadbhāvanirṇayahetavaḥ kathyante**

tatra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	vibhāganihnave jñātibandhusākṣyabhilekhitaiḥ |

	vibhāgabhāvanā jñeyā gṛhakṣetraiś ca yautakaiḥ ||

yautakaiḥ pṛthakkṛtaiḥ | vibhāgagrahaṇaṃ taddharmāṇām api pradarśaṇārtham | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	vibhāgadharmasaṃdehe dāyādānāṃ vinirṇayaḥ |

	jñātibhir bhāgalekhyena pṛthakkāryapravartanāt ||

nāsīdāvayor vibhāga iti svarūpāpalāpādinā sarvasmād vibhājyānnāvayor vibhāga iti dharmāpalāpādinā vibhāgataddharmasadbhāvasaṃdehe dāyādānāṃ jñātyādisākṣibhir vibhāgalekhyena vā pṛthakkāryapravartanādiyuktibhir vā nirṇayo jñeya ity arthaḥ | pṛthakkāryapravartanaṃ dāyādānāṃ pṛthak pṛthag vaiśvadevabhikṣādānātithipūjanādidharmapravartanam | kathaṃ tasya yuktitvam ity apkeṣite anantaram uktaṃ tenaiva |

	bhrātṝṇām avibhaktānām eko dharmaḥ pravartate |

	vibhāge sati dharmo 'pi bhavet teṣāṃ pṛthak pṛthak ||

dharmo vaiśvadevādiḥ | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	ekapākena vasatāṃ pitṛdevadvijārcanam |

	ekaṃ bhaved vibhaktānāṃ tad eva syād gṛhe gṛhe ||

evaṃ ca pṛthak pṛthag vaiśvadevādikārthapravartanam avibhakeṣv avidyamānaṃ vibhaktatvam avagamayatīti vibhāgasaṃdehe sati nirṇāyakayuktitayoktir yuktety anavadyam | yuktyantarāṇi vaktuṃ parasparasākṣitvādikaṃ tāvad vibhaktānāṃ vidhāsyan tatpratiṣedham avibhakteṣu sa evāha | 

	sākṣitvaṃ prātibhāvyaṃ ca dānaṃ grahaṇam eva ca |

	vibhaktā bhrātaraḥ kuryuḥ nāvibhaktāḥ parasparam ||

grahaṇaṃ pratigrahaḥ | evaṃ ca parasparasākṣitvādiyuktibhyo 'pi vibhāgasadbhāvāvagatiḥ sidhyaty eva | ata evānantaram uktam tenaiva |

	yeṣām etāḥ kriyā loke pravartante svarikthiṣu |

	vibhaktān avagaccheyuḥ lekhyam apy antareṇa tān ||

pravartante vyastāḥ samastā veti śeṣaḥ | evam ṛṇagrahaṇam api rikthiṣu pravartamānaṃ vibhaktāvagamakam, avibhakteṣv apravartanāt | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	bhrātṝṇām atha dampatyoḥ pituḥ putrasya caiva hi |

	prātibhāvyam ṛṇaṃ sākṣyam avibhakte na tu smṛtam ||

tataś ca ṛṇadātur api ṛṇagrahītuḥ sakāśāt vibhaktatvaṃ siddham | ata eva bṛhaspatiḥ |

	pṛthag āyavyayadhanāḥ kusīdaṃ ca parasparam |

	vaṇikpathaṃ ca ye kuryuḥ vibhaktās te na saṃśayaḥ ||

kusīdaṃ vṛddhyarthaṃ dhanaprayogaḥ | vaṇikpatho vāṇijyam | parasparam ity ubhayatra saṃbadhyate | evaṃ hetuto nirṇayaḥ svataḥ śreṣṭhanirṇāyakapramāṇābhāve kārya ity āha sa eva |

	sāhasaṃ sthāvaraṃ svāmyaṃ prāgvibhāgaś ca rikthinām |

	anumānena vijñeyo na syur yatra ca sākṣiṇaḥ ||

prāgvibhāgo vibhāgavivādāt prāg jāto vibhāgaḥ | anumānaṃ yuktiḥ | sāhasādisādhakayuktipradarśanārthaṃ kāṃścit sādhakān āha sa eva |

	kulānubandhavyāghātahoḍhaṃ sāhasasādhakam |

	svasya bhogaḥ sthāvarasya vibhāgasya pṛthag dhanam ||

kulānubandhaḥ pūrvapuruṣavairānubandhaḥ | vyāghātaḥ parasparaṃ spardhā | hoḍhaṃ balād apahṛtaleśadarśanam | svasya bhogaḥ ātmano bhogaḥ atra kātyāyanaḥ |

	vaseyur daśa varṣāṇi pṛthag dharmāḥ pṛthak kriyāḥ |

	bhrātaras te 'pi vijñeyāḥ vibhaktāḥ paitṛkād dhanāt ||

bhrātṛśabdo 'tra rikthasaṃbandhyupalakṣaṇārthaḥ | paitṛkagrahaṇaṃ dāyadhanopalakṣaṇārtham | paramārthato dāyagrahanābhāve 'pi,

	paśyato 'bruvato bhūmer hānir viṃśativārṣikī |

	pareṇa bhujyamānāyāḥ dhanasya dasavārṣikī ||

iti vanānusāreṇa vibhaktā eveti vijñeyā ity arthaḥ | daśavarṣād arvāk punaḥ prāguktayuktibhir eva nirṇayaḥ | tāsām anyathā siddhisaṃbhāvanayā nirṇayābhāve tu,

	yuktiṣv apy asamarthāsu śapathair eva nirṇayet |

iti vacanād yady api śapathaḥ prāpitaḥ, tathāpi śapathe nirṇayo na kāryaḥ | yata āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	vibhāgdharmasaṃdehe bandhusākṣyabhilekhitaiḥ |

	vibhāgabhāvanā kāryā na bhaved daivikī kriyā || iti |

kathaṃ tarhi yuktiṣv asamarthāsu nirṇaya ity apekṣite manuḥ |

	vibhāge yatra saṃdeho dāyādānāṃ parasparam |

	punar vibhāgaḥ kartavyaḥ pṛthaksthānasthitair api |

yatra saṃdeho yuktibhir asamarthābhir nāpaitīti śeṣaḥ | yat punas tenaivoktam,

	sakṛd aṃśo nipatati sakṛt kanyā pradīyate |

	sakṛd āha dadānīti trīṇy etāni sakṛt sakṛt ||

iti, tat yuktyādibhir apagatasaṃdehavibhāgaviṣayam iti sarvam anavadyam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ vibhāgatadharmasadbhāvanirṇayahetavaḥ**

**samāptaṃ ca dāyavibhāgākhyapadasya vidhivitānam**

atreyaṃ prakaraṇānupūrvī — vibhāgakālakartṛpradarśanam, jīvadvibhāgaprakāraḥ, viṣamavibhāgaprakāraḥ, jīvadvibhāgaprakāraviṣayāṇi, dāyānarhaviṣayāṇi, vibhājyanirūpaṇam, avibhājyanirūpaṇam, putrapautrādivibhāgakalpanāviṣayāṇi, strīdhanabhedāḥ, strīdhanakṛtyam, strīdvārāgatadhanavibhāgaḥ, gauṇapitṛdvārāgatadhanavibhāgaḥ, putradvārāgatadhanavibhāgaḥ, aputradvārāgatadhanavibhāge patnīviṣayāṇi, duhitrādiviṣayāṇi, saṃsṛṣṭabhrātrādiviṣayāṇi, vibhaktajaputrādivibhāgaḥ avaluptadhanavibhāgaḥ, vibhaktakṛtyam, vibhāgataddharmasadbhāvanirṇayahetavaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ dāyavibhāgākhyapadasya prakaraṇānupūrvī**

**iti dāyabhāgaprakaraṇaṃ samāptam**

**atha sāhasākhyapadasya vidhir ucyate **

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	manuṣyamāraṇaṃ cauryaṃ paradārābhimarśanam |

	pāruṣyam ubhayaṃ ceti sāhasaṃ syāc caturvidham ||

atra ādye dvividhe sāhase sāhasikajñānārtham āha sa eva |

	hatas tu dṛśyate yatra ghātakas tu na dṛśyate |

	pūrvavairānumānena jñātavyaḥ sa mahībhujā ||

	vijñeyo 'sādhusaṃsargāc cihnāt hoḍhena taskaraḥ |

	eṣoditā ghātakānāṃ taskarāṇāṃ ca bhāvanā ||

cihnaṃ śoṇitalepādi | hoḍhena hṛtahastasthadhanādinā | uditabhāvanāsaṃbhave tu kātyāyanaḥ |

	vinā cihnais tu yat kāryaṃ sāhasākhyaṃ pravartate |

	śapathaiḥ sa viśodhyaḥ syāt sarvavādeṣv ayaṃ vidhiḥ || iti |

sa iti sāhasakartṛtvenābhiyuktaḥ pratyavamṛśyate | tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	divyair viśuddho mānyaḥ syād aśuddho vadham arhati | iti |

nārado 'pi |

	tatkāriṇo nārthadamaiḥ śāsyā vadhyāḥ prayatnataḥ | iti |

tatkāriṇaḥ sāhasalakṣaṇavadhakāriṇaḥ | teṣāṃ vadhe viśeṣam āha vyāsaḥ |

	jñātvā tu ghātakaṃ samyag asahāyaṃ sabāndhavam |

	hanyāc citravadhopāyair udvejanakarair nṛpaḥ ||

	bandigrāhāṃs tathā vājikuñjarāṇām ca hāriṇaḥ |

	prasahya ghātinaś caiva śūlān āropayen narān ||

yat tu bṛhaspatinoktam,

	prakāśavadhakārāś ca tathā copāṃśughātakāḥ |

	jñātvā samyag dhanaṃ hṛtvā hantavyā vividhair vadhaiḥ||

iti, tat brahmaghnakṣatriyādiviṣayam | yad āha bodhāyanaḥ: "kṣatriyādīnāṃ brāhmaṇasya vadhe vadhaḥ sarvasvaharaṇaṃ ca, teṣām eva tulyāpakṛṣṭavadhe yathābalam anurūpān daṇḍān prakalpayet" iti | bahūnām ekaghātakatve doṣānurūpadaṇḍābhidhānārtham āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	ekaṃ ced bahavo hanyuḥ saṃrabdhāḥ puruṣaṃ narāḥ |

	marmaghātī tu yas teṣāṃ sa ghātaka iti smṛtaḥ ||
