tena (?) sa eva vadhāparādhadaṇḍabhāk | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	marmaghātī tu tas teṣāṃ yathoktaṃ dāpayed damam | iti |

tam iti śeṣaḥ | yattador nityābhisaṃbandhāt | marmahantṛvyatiriktānām api daṇḍo 'nantaram uktaḥ |

	ārambhakṛt sahāyaś ca tathā mārgānudeśakaḥ |

	āśrayaḥ śastradātā ca bhaktadātā vikarmiṇām ||

	yuddhopadeśakaś caiva tadvināśapradarśakaḥ |

	upekṣī kāryayuktaś ca doṣavaktānumodakaḥ ||

smṛtyantare 'pi |

	aniṣeddhā kṣamo yaḥ syāt sarve tatkāryakāriṇaḥ |

	yathāśaktyanurūpaṃ tu daṇḍam eṣāṃ prakalpayet || iti |

anurūpaṃ doṣānurūpam | ata eva marmahantṛdoṣārthabhāgitvaṃ dvayor darśayati manuḥ |

	ārambhakṛt sahāyaś ca doṣabhājau tadardhataḥ | iti |

evaṃ mārgānudeśakāder api doṣalāghavam ūhyam | yājñavalkyas tu sāhasaprayojakatvatāratamyād doṣamahattvatāratamyaṃ daṇḍātirekakathanamukhenāha |

	yaḥ sāhasaṃ kārayati sa dāpyo dviguṇaṃ damam |

	yaś caivam uktvāhaṃ dātā kāreyet sa caturguṇam ||

yad idaṃ sāhasaṃ bhavān kuryāt tadaitāvad dhanaṃ bhavate dāsyāmīty evam uktvā sāhasaṃ kārayati sa caturguṇaṃ dāpya ity arthaḥ | dviguṇaṃ caturguṇam ity atra sāhasakartur uktadaṇḍāt dviguṇaṃ caturguṇam ity artho 'vaseyaḥ | manus tu krodhād itaḥ preritānāṃ sāhasikānām ukto yo daṇḍas tasyābhāvaṃ doṣābhāvakathanamukhena vidhitaḥ preritānāṃ sāhasikānāṃ kathayati:

	śastraṃ dvijātibhir grāhyaṃ dharmo yatroparudhyate |

	dvijātīnāṃ ca varṇānāṃ viplave kālakārite ||

	ātmanaś ca paritrāṇe dakṣiṇānāṃ ca saṃgare |

	strīviprābhyavapattau ca ghnan dharmeṇa na duṣyati ||

dharmaḥ taṭākārāmādikaḥ bhedanacchedanādisāhasikaiḥ yatra deśe kāle coparudhyate, tathā śūdretaravarṇasaṃkare paradārākramaṇādirūpe rājābhāvakālakārite, tathātmanaḥ parataḥ prāṇasaṃśaye, tathā dakṣiṇānāṃ gavāṃ saṃgare grahaṇanimittakayuddhe, tathā strīviprābhyavapattau durbalahiṃsānivāraṇe, dvijātibhiḥ kṣatradharmāśrayaṇarahitair asamarthaiḥ śastraṃ grāhyam iti saṃbandhaḥ | kṣatriyasya prajāmātrarakṣaṇārthaṃ śastragrahaṇaṃ prāptam iti tadvyatiriktavipravaiśyaviṣayaṃ dvijātigrahaṇam | tathā ca bodhāyanaḥ |

	brāhmaṇārthe gavārthe vā varṇānāṃ vāpi saṃkare |

	gṛhṇīyātāṃ vipraviśau śastraṃ dharmavyatikrame ||

gautamo 'pi: "prāṇasaṃśaye brāhmaṇo 'pi śastram ādadīta durbalahiṃsāyāṃ vimocane śaktaś cet" iti | brāḥmaṇagrahaṇaṃ vaiśyasyāpi pradarśanārtham | ata eva viṣṇuḥ: "ātmatrāṇe varṇasaṃkare vā brāhmaṇavaiśyau śastram ādadīyātām" iti | yat tu bodhāyanenoktam: "bhayārtham api brāhmaṇa āyudhaṃ nādadīta" iti, yad apy āpastambena: "parīkṣārtho 'pi brāhmaṇa āyudhaṃ nādadīta" iti, ubhayatrāpy apiśabdena bibhīṣikāryaṃ hiṃśārthaṃ vā brāhmaṇasya śastragrahaṇaṃ dūrotsāritam iti gamyate | tena bibhīṣikārthaṃ brāhmaṇasya śatragrahaṇavidhānaṃ pūrvoktaṃ virudhyate | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span>, ata eva pūrvoktadharmoparodhādiśastragrahaṇavidhiviṣayād anyatra pratiṣedho 'vatiṣṭhate iti vyavasthāpanīyam | "ghnan dharmeṇa na duṣyati" iti vadatā manunā hiṃsāparyanto 'yaṃ śastragrahaṇopadeśo na bibhīṣikāmātrasaṃjananāyeti darśitam | "ghnan dharmeṇa na duṣyati" ity asya yady api kṣātrayuddhadharmeṇa ghnan na duṣyatīty artho bhavati | tathāpi dharmoparodhakādihiṃsāyā avaśyakartavyatvāt tatra kṣātrayuddhadharmeṇa ghnann ity arthāyogād dharmeṇa hiṃśādividhinā prerito būtvā ghnan na duṣyatīty artho 'vagantavyaḥ | etad uktaṃ bhavati: dharmoparodhakādihiṃsāyāś coditatvāt tatkartā na duṣyatīti | tathā ca manuvṛttāv uktam: "stenādīnāṃ vadhaḥ kṣātradharmeṇety ayuktam, tadghananasyāvaśyakartavyatvāt | tasmād dharmeṇa śāstā na duṣyatīti draṣṭavyam" iti | dharmoparodhakādihananacodanā smṛtyanumeyā na pratyakṣaśruter iti darśayitum upakramasmṛtivāyam āha manuḥ |

	guruṃ vā bālavṛddhau vā brāhmaṇaṃ vā bahuśrutam |

	ātatāyinam āyāntaṃ hanyād evāvicārayan ||

atra gurvādipadāny anyaparatayā prayuktānīti darśayituṃ teṣāṃ tātparyārtho vṛttikāreṇa darśitaḥ: "guruṃ vā mānyatamaṃ vety arthaḥ | bālavṛddhau vā kṛpāviṣayam apīty arthaḥ | brāhmaṇaṃ vā bahuśrutaṃ samastapātraguṇayuktam ity arthaḥ" | uttarārdhārtho 'pi tenaiva darśitaḥ: "vadhārtham adhikāravicchedārtham avaśyam etīty ātatayinam āyāntaṃ pravṛttaṃ prāṇādyapahāre hanyād eva, avicāraynn ity atra dhāraṇeti niyamaḥ paraḥ" iti | kātyāyano 'pi |

	vināśahetum āyāntaṃ hanyād evāvicārayan |

vināśahetum udāsīnaṃ jalabhedādivināśahetum ātatāyinam iti yāvat | kvacid api vicārayann iti pāṭhādarśanāt | etad uktaṃ bhavati: ātatāyivadhaḥ sadoṣo nirdoṣo veti vicāro na kāryaḥ vaidhatvād iti | vasiṣṭho 'pi vaidhatvaṃ darśayati |

	ātatāyinam āyāntam api vedāntagaṃ raṇe |

	jighāṃsantaṃ jighāṃsīyān na tena brūṇahā bhavet || iti |

atra <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecid</span> āhuḥ | ātatāyivadhavidhivākyatraye 'py āyāntam iti vacanād āttaśastro hantum unmukho 'bhidhāvan dārādīn vā jihīrṣan hantavyaḥ | kṛte tv anarthe kim anyat kariṣyatīty upekṣya eveti | atra kṛte tv anartha ityādy ayuktam ity <span style="text-decoration:underline;">apare</span> dūṣayanti | kariṣyan kṛtavāṃś ca dvāv api dauṣṭhyena samau vadhārhāv eva | tasmād āyāntam iti padaṃ kṛtvāgatasyāpy ātatāyina upalakṣaṇārtham uktam iti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye</span> punar evam āhuḥ: vartamānārthajighāṃsantam iti vidhivākyasthapadaparyālocanayā vartamānaviṣadānādivyāpārā evātatāyina ucyante | tadvyāpāranivāraṇaṃ ca yatrātatāyivadham antareṇa na saṃbhavati tatraiva tadvadhābhyanujñā, satyāṃ gatau vadhasyānucitatvāt | tena viṣopādānādau vyāpriyamāṇaḥ praharaṇādimātreṇa anivāryaḥ, na hantavyaḥ | viṣadānādau vyāpṛtasya grahaṇādimātreṇa nivārayituṃ śakyasya vā vadho doṣanimittam eveti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">tad api na</span> | na hi viṣadānādivyāpāreṣu vyāpṛtānāṃ vyāpāranivṛttāv api pūrvasiddhaṃ paraśarīrādivināśahetutvalakṣaṇam ātatayitvam apaiti | tad uktaṃ medhātithinā (on MDh 8.351): "ātatāyitvāc cāsau hanyate na hi kṛtavataḥ śtatāyitvam apaiti" iti | tena viṣadānādau vyāpṛto 'py ātatāyitvād ghantavya iti medhātither abhiprāyaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca dārādirakṣaṇārtho vadha iti kṛte dārādiviplave paścād vadho vyartha ity upekṣya eva kṛtavān ātatāyī, na hantavyaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>, na dārādirakṣaṇārtho vadhavidhiḥ, kiṃ tu dārādyupadravādinimitte vadho vidhīyate | rakṣaṇārthas tu vadhavidhir ātmanaś ca paritrāṇa ityādau kvacid eva | tasmāt kṛtavān ity ātatāyī nopekṣyaḥ | ata eva manuḥ |

	nātatāyivadhe doṣo hantur bhavati kaścana |

	prakāśaṃ vāprakāśaṃ vā manus taṃ manum ṛcchati ||

etadbhāṣyakāro medhātithir vyācaṣṭe: "na kaścaneti nehādharmo na daṇḍo na prāyaścittam | prakāśam ābhāṣya janasamakṣam | aprakāśaṃ viṣadānādinā yena kenacid upāyena | manuḥ krodhābhimāninī devatā | sa manyum ṛcchati | nātra hatṛhantavyabhāvo 'sti puruṣayoḥ | ātatāyikrodhaḥ itareṇa krodhena hantavya ity arthavādo 'yam" ityādigranthena | atrāprakāśavadhe 'pi doṣābhāvaṃ vadan manur apy upaplavaṃ kṛtvā gate 'py ātatāyini viṣadānādinā vadho na doṣāyeti darśayati, upaplavakaraṇasamaye viṣadānāsaṃbhavāt | bṛhaspatir api |

	nātatāyivadhe hantā kilbiṣaṃ prāpnuyāt kvacit |

	vināśārthinam āyāntaṃ ghātayan nāparādhnuyāt ||

atra kariṣyadātatāyiviṣayam uttaravākyaṃ vināśārthinam iti viśeṣaśrutyaiva pratipannam iti pūrvavākyaṃ kṛtvāgatātatāyiviṣayam iti gamyate | kariṣyadātatāyino 'pi yathākathaṃcid vināśārthitvāpagamāt nivṛttodyamāḥ tadā tān ghātayan aparādhnuyād iti darśayitum "vināśārthinam āyāntam" ity uktam | ata evāsmin viṣaye vadhasthāne grahaṇam āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	udyatānāṃ tu pāpānāṃ hantur doṣo na vidyate |

	nivṛttās tu yadārambhāt grahaṇaṃ na vadhaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

ātatāyitvāniṣpatter ity abhiprāyaḥ | ātatāyitvaniṣpattāv api kvacid viṣaye na vadha ity āha sumantuḥ: "ātatāyivadhe na doṣo 'nyatra gobrāhmaṇād yadā hataḥ prāyaścittaṃ syāt" iti | gauḥ brāhmaṇo vā ātatāyī yadā hataḥ tadā prāyaścittaṃ syād doṣaḥ syād ity arthaḥ | ātmaparitrāṇavyatiriktaviṣayam etat | yad āha devalaḥ |

	ātmatyāgaḥ paratyāgāt pāpīyān pātakād api |

	pātake niṣkṛtiḥ proktā katham ātmaghnaniṣkṛtiḥ ||

	ātmānaṃ buddhisaṃpannaṃ yogyaṃ sarvārthasiddhiṣu |

	śramaduḥkhabhaye tyaktvā raurave paripacyate ||

	udyamya śastram āyāntaṃ bhrūṇam apy ātatayinam |

	nihatya bhrūṇahā na syād ahatvā bhūṇahā bhavet || iti |

paravadhārhapātakād ātmatrāṇānāsthānād ātmatyāgaḥ pāpīyān ity uktadoṣam apaitya bhrūṇam api brāhmaṇam api daṇḍāpūpanyāyāt gām apy ātatāyinam ātmaparitrāṇāyāvaśyaṃ hanyād ity arthaḥ | yat tu uśanasā brāhmaṇasya brāhmaṇasya rudhirotpādananimittadoṣam abhidhāyābhihitam: "gṛhītaśastram ātatāyinaṃ hatvā na doṣaḥ syāt" iti, tad api pūrvoktātmaparitrāṇaviṣaye draṣṭavyam | yat tu kātyāyanenoktam,

	ātatāyini cotkṛṣṭe tapaḥsvādhyāyajanmataḥ |

	vadhas tatra tu naiva syāt pāpe hīne vadho bhṛguḥ || 

iti — tapaḥsvādhyāyajanmata utkṛṣṭe brāhmaṇe na vadha ity arthaḥ —, yac ca bṛhaspatinoktam,

	ātatyinam utkṛṣṭaṃ vṛttasvādhyāyasaṃyutam |

	yo na hanyād vadhaprāptaṃ so 'śvamedhaphalaṃ labhet ||

— utkṛṣṭaṃ brāhmaṇam ity arthaḥ, vadhaprāptaj,

	svādhyāyinaṃ kule jātaṃ yo hanyād ātatāyinam |

	na tena bhrūṇahā bhavati manyus taṃ manyum ṛcchati |

ityādivacanāpātamātrād vadham aprāptam ity arthaḥ —, tad etad vacanadvayaṃ pūrvoktātmatrāṇavyatiriktaviṣaye brāhmaṇātatāyini draṣṭavyam | yat tu bodhāyanenoktam: "ṣaṭsv apy anabhicaran patati" iti, ṣaṭsu ātatāyiṣv iti śeṣaḥ | ke punas ta ity apekṣite vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	agnido garadaś caiva śastrapāṇir dhanāpahaḥ |

	kṣetradāraharaś caiva ṣaḍ ete hy ātatāyinaḥ ||

udāharaṇabhūtānām atyantaprasiddhānāṃ ṣaḍvidhtvād ubhayatra ṣaḍgrahaṇam, na punaḥ parisaṃkhyārtham, vidhāntareṇātatayināṃ loke vidyamānatvāt | ata eva,

	udyatāsiviṣāgniś ca cāpodyatakaras tathā |

	ātharvaṇena hantā ca piśunaś caiva rājani ||

	bhāryātikramakārī ca randhrānveṣaṇatatparaḥ |

	evamādyān vijānīyāt sarvān evātatayinaḥ ||

iti kātyāyanenaiva evamādyān ity uktam | evamādyān evaṃprakārān ity arthaḥ | ata evātatāyina ity anuvṛttau tenaivoktam |

	yaśovṛttaharān pāpān āhur dharmārthahārakān |

	anākṣāritapūrvo yas tv aparādhe pravartate ||

	prāṇadravyāpahāre ca taṃ vidyād ātatāyinam ||

prāṇadravyāpahāre 'nyasminn api tattulyāparādhe ca yas tv anākṣāritapūrvo 'bhādhitapūrvaḥ pravartate tam ātatāyinaṃ vidyād ity arthaḥ | anenārthād ākṣāritapūrvo yaḥ pūrvoktaviṣadānādyaparādhe pravartate nāsāv ātatāyīty uktam | evaṃ ca "ātatāyī vadhodyataḥ" ity amarasiṃhakṛto 'rthanirdeśaḥ kṣetradārāpahartrādīnām arthānāṃ pradarśanārtham iti mantavyam | evaṃ ca "ṣaṭsv apy anabhicaran patati" ity ātatāyivadhamātram akurvan patito bhavatīty artho 'vagantavyaḥ | tad etad bodhāyanavacanam ātmatyāgaviṣaye tadvyatiriktadharmādyuparodhaviṣaye 'pi gobrāhmaṇetaraśeṣātatāyiviṣaye draṣṭavyam | gavāṃ paryudāsavacanāt taditarapaśvāditiryagjātīnām apy ātatāyināṃ vadho vihita ity avagamyate | ata eva kātyāyanena ātatāyipasvādivadhe 'pi doṣābhāvo darśitaḥ |

	nakhināṃ śṛṅgiṇāṃ caiva daṃṣṭriṇāṃ cātatāyinām |

	hastyaśvānāṃ tathānyeṣāṃ vadhe hante na doṣabhāk ||

anyeṣāṃ cañcvādiśālināṃ pakṣyādīnām | evaṃ cātatāyināṃ vadhe yatra doṣābhāva uktaḥ tatra ghātakānāṃ vadhanibandhanadaṇḍābhāvaḥ pratyetavyaḥ, asmin sāhasākhyavadhe doṣābhāvakathanasya daṇḍābhāvapratipattyarthatvāt ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ vadhalakṣaṇasāhasaviṣayāṇi vacanāni nirūpitāni**

**atha sāhasasteyaviṣayāṇi kānicid vacanāni likhyante**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	sāṃprataṃ sāhasaṃ steyaṃ śrūyatāṃ krodhalobhajam | iti |

sāhasalakṣaṇakaṃ steyam ity arthaḥ | kiṃ tad ity apekṣite yājñavalkyaḥ |

	sāmānyadravyaprasabhaharaṇaṃ sāhasaṃ smṛtam | iti |

sāmanyadravyaṃ bahujanaiḥ praharādikālakrameṇa rakṣyamāṇaṃ dravyam | etat chalena hartuṃ na śakyate, rakṣaṇe pramādāsaṃbhavāt | tenāsya prāyeṇa balād apaharaṇam, tad etad abhisaṃdhāyoktam: "sāmānyadravyaprasabhaharaṇam" iti | sāhasaṃ smṛtaṃ sāhasalakṣaṇaṃ steyam ity arthaḥ | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

	sānvayas tv apahāro yaḥ prasahya haraṇaṃ ca yat |

	sāhasaṃ ca bhaved evaṃ steyam uktaṃ vinihnavaḥ ||

anvayo rakṣaṇakālakramaprāptapālakanaranairantaryam, tasmin sati yo 'pahāraḥ saḥ sānvayo 'pahāraḥ | sa ca prasahya kriyamāṇaḥ sāhasaṃ ca steyaṃ ca ity evaṃ dvirūpam āpadyate | uktaprakāraviparīto 'pi nihnavo dravyāpahāraḥ steyarūpam evāpadyata iti smṛtāv uktam ity arthaḥ,

	niranvayaṃ bhavet steyaṃ kṛtvāpavyayate ca yat |

iti manusmaraṇāt | asyārtho medhātithinā spaṣṭīkṛtaḥ: "niranvayam ārakṣakapuruṣavarjitam avasaram abhijñāya kriyate yac cauryam, prasahya kṛtaṃ nihnute kṛtam idaṃ na mayeti, tad api steyam" iti | evaṃ sāhasasteyakevalasteyayor bhedakathanaṃ tatkartṛṣu daṇḍabhedakathanārtham | tatra tāvat sāhasasteyakartṛviṣaye daṇḍān āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	kṣetropakaraṇaṃ setumūlapuṣpaphalāni ca |

	vināśayan haran daṇḍaḥ śatādyam anurūpataḥ ||

	paśuvastrānnapānāni gṛhopakaraṇaṃ tathā |

	hiṃsayan corayan dāpyo dviśatādyaṃ damas tathā ||

	strīpuṃgohemaratnāni devavipradhanaṃ tathā |

	kauseyaṃ cottamaṃ dravyam eṣāṃ mūlyasamo damaḥ ||

	dviguṇo vā kalpanīyaḥ puruṣāpekṣayā nṛpaiḥ |

	hantā vā ghātanīyaḥ syāt prasaṅgavinivṛttaye || iti |

atra vināśayan haran hiṃsayan corayan hantā veti ca vadan idaṃ daṇḍaśāstraṃ sāhasasteyakartṛviṣayam iti darśayati, tasya krodhalobhavattvena hananopetasteyakāritvāt | hantā vā ghātanīya ity brāhmaṇaviṣayam | tathā ca sāhasasteyaṃ prakṛtya yamaḥ |

	na śārīro brāhmaṇasya daṇḍo bhavati karhicit |

	gupte tu bandhane baddhvā rājā bhaktaṃ pradāpayet ||

	atha vāpy adhanaṃ rakṣākarma vā kārayen nṛpaḥ |

	māsārdhamāsaṃ kurvīta kāryaṃ vijñāya tattvataḥ ||

	yathāparādhaṃ vipraṃ tu vikarmāṇy api kārayet |

	abadhyā brāhmaṇā gāvo loke 'smin vaidikī śrutiḥ || iti |

rakṣākarma paśvādipālanarūpaṃ garhitam | yat tu yājñavalkyena sāhasasteyaṃ prastutyānantaram uktam |

	tanmūlyād dviguṇo daṇḍo nihnave tu caturguṇaḥ | iti |

tanmūlyāt sāhasasteyaprāptavastrādimūlyād ity arthaḥ | tadvacanaṃ vastrādyuttamaharaṇe dṛṣṭasāhasakṛte draṣṭavyam,

	dviguṇo vā kalpanīyaḥ puruṣāpekṣayā nṛpaiḥ |

iti vastrādyuttamadravyaharaṇe bṛhahaspatinoktatvāt | nihnave tu na mayedam uttamadravyaprasabhaharaṇaṃ kṛtam ity apalāpe tu kṛte ity arthaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandriyāyāṃ sāhasasteyaviṣayāṇi**

atha prasaṅgād asminn eva pade kevalasteyaviṣayāny api kānicid vacanāni likhyante, nāradīye padoddeśakavacane steyasaṃgrahayor anuddeśād uddeśakramaprāptāvasarābhāvāt | tatra manuḥ |

	dvividhāṃs taskarān vidyāt paradravyāpahāriṇaḥ |

	prakāśāṃś cāprakāśāṃś ca cāracakṣur mahīpatiḥ ||

bṛhaspatir api |

	prakāśāś cāprakāśāś ca dvividhās taskarāḥ smṛtāḥ |

	prajñāsāmarthyamāyābhiḥ prabhinnās te sahasradhā ||

ke punaḥ prakāśās taskarā ity apekṣite svayam evāha |

	naigamā vaidyakitavā sabhyotkocakavañcakāḥ |

	daivotpātavido bhadrāḥ śilpajñāḥ pratirūpakāḥ ||

	akriyākāriṇaś caiva madhyasthāḥ kūṭasākṣiṇaḥ |

	prakāśās taskarā hy ete tathā kuhakajīvanāḥ || iti |

pratirūpakāḥ pratirūpakarāḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	prakāśavañcakās tatra kūṭamānatulāḥ smṛtāḥ |

	utkocakāḥ sopadhikāḥ kitavāḥ paṇyayoṣitaḥ ||

	pratirūpakarāś caiva maṅgalādeśavṛttayaḥ |

	ity evamādayo jñeyāḥ prakāśās taskarā bhuvi || iti |

naigamādicchadmanā paradravyāpahāriṇaś cet prakāśataskarā na svarūpata ity avagantavyam | naigamādivyājena paradravyapahartṛtve siddhe daṇḍam āha vyāsaḥ |

	strīpuṃsau pañcayantīha maṅgalādeśavṛttayaḥ |

	gṛhṇanti chadmanā cārtham anāryās tv āryaliṅginaḥ ||

	naigamādyā bhūridhanā daṇḍyā doṣānurūpataḥ |

	yathā te nātivartante tiṣṭhanti samaye tathā ||

doṣānurūpato daṇḍyā na punar dhanānurūpata ity arthaḥ | te ca vidhayo vistārabhayān na darśitāḥ granthāntare draṣṭavyāḥ | eam aprakāśataskarāṇāṃ daṇḍam abhidhātuṃ teṣāṃ svarūpam āha sa eva |

	sādhanādyanvitā rātrau vicaranty avibhāvitāḥ |

	avijñātanivāsāś ca jñeyāḥ pracchannavañcakāḥ ||

rātrāv iti prāyikābhiprāyeṇoktam | divāpy araṇyādāv avibhāvitānāṃ vicaratāṃ saṃbhavāt | eteṣām avāntarabhedam āha sa eva |

	utkṣepakaḥ saṃdhibhettā pāntamuṭ granthibhedakaḥ |

	strīpuṃgo'śvapaśusteyī coro navavidhaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

utkṣepako dhaninām anavadhānam avadhāryāntikasthaṃ dhanam uddhṛtya grāhakaḥ | saṃdhibhettā gṛhāṇāṃ vicchedāya kṛtasaṃcarasthāne pṛṣṭhasaṃdhāv avasthāya tatratyabhittibhettā | pānthamuṭ utkaṭakāntarādau patikānāṃ dhanāpahārakaḥ | granthibhedakaḥ paridhānādigranthidhanaṃ grahītuṃ tadgrantivimocakaḥ | strīpuṃgo'śvapaśusteyī dvandvānteśrūyamāṇaḥ śabdaḥ pratyekam abhisaṃbadhyate | ata eva navavidha ity uktam | atra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	grāhakair gṛhyate coro loptreṇātha padena vā | iti |

bṛhaspatir api |

	saṃsargaiś cihnaloptraiś ca vijñāto rājapūruṣaiḥ |

	pradāpyo 'pahṛtaṃ śāsyo damaiḥ śāstrapracoditaiḥ ||

saṃsargaiḥ kutsitasaṃsargaiḥ | cihnaṃ cauryasādhanasaṃgrahavattvādikam | loptraṃ steyāvaptaṃ dhanam | pradāpyaḥ svāmina iti śeṣaḥ | ata eva viṣṇuḥ: "stenāḥ sarva evāpahrtaṃ dhanikasya dāpyāḥ, tatas teṣām abhihitadaṇḍaprayogaḥ" iti | kasya stenasya kaḥ punar abhihito daṇḍa ity apekṣite bṛhaspatiḥ |

	utkṣepakasya saṃdaṃśaḥ chettavyo rājapūruṣaiḥ | iti |

saṃdaṃśo 'trāṅgulyaṅguṣṭhātmakaḥ paravastrādānahetur vivakṣitaḥ | manur api |

	saṃdhiṃ bhitvā tu ye cauryaṃ rātrau kurvanti taskarāḥ |

	teṣāṃ chitvā nṛpo hastau tīkṣṇe śūle niveśayet ||

tān iti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

	saṃdhiṃ bhitvānekavidhaṃ dhanaṃ prāpnoti vai gṛhāt |

	pradāpya svāmine sarvaṃ tīkṣṇaśūle niveśayet ||

yaḥ prāpnoti taṃ pradāpya paścāc chūle niveśayed ity arthaḥ | anyasya stenasya daṇḍam āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	ekasmin yatra nidhanaṃ prāpite duṣṭacāriṇi |

	bahūnāṃ bhavati kṣemaḥ tasya puṇyaprado vadhaḥ ||

	tathā pānthamuṣo vṛkṣe gale badhvāvalambayet || iti |

aparasya manur daṇḍam āha |

	aṅgulī granthibhedasya chedayet prathame grahe |

	dvitīye hastacaraṇau tṛtīye vadham arhati ||

aṅgulī tarjanyaṅguṣṭhau, granthibhedane tayoḥ sādhakatamatvāt,

	prathame granthibhedānām aṅgulyaṅguṣṭhayor vadhaḥ |

iti bṛhaspatismaraṇāc ca | strīpuṃstenayor daṇḍam āha vyāsaḥ |

	strīhartā lohaśayane dagdhavyo vai kaṭāgninā |

	narahartā hastapādau chitvā sthāpyaś catuṣpathe ||

gostenasya daṇḍam āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	gohartur nāsikāṃ chitvā badhvāmbhasi nimajjayet |

aśvapaśustenayor daṇḍam āha vyāsaḥ |

	aśvāpaharaṇe pādau kaṭiṃ chitvā pramāpyate |

	paśuhartus tv ardhapādaṃ tīkṣṇaśastreṇa kartayet ||

paśuhartur arthadaṇḍaḥ paśvanusāreṇa kārya ity āha nāradaḥ |

	mahāpaśūn stenayato daṇḍa uttamasāhasam |

	madhyamaṃ madhyamapaśūn pūrvaṃ kṣudrapaśau hṛte ||

madhyamaṃ madhyamasāhasam | pūrvaṃ prathamasāhasam | suvarṇādikaṃ stenayato daṇḍam āha manuḥ |

	suvarṇarajatādīnām uttamānāṃ ca vāsasām |

	pañcāśatas tv abhyadhike hastacchedanam iṣyate ||

	śeṣeṣv ekādaśaguṇaṃ mūlyād daṇḍaṃ prakalpayet |

	dhānyaṃ daśabhyaḥ kumbhebhyo harato 'bhyadhikaṃ vadhaḥ ||

	śeṣe 'py ekādaśaguṇaṃ dāpyas tasya ca tad dhanam || iti |

svarṇarajatādīnāṃ tulayā meyānāṃ pañcāśatsaṃkhyāḥ deśavyavahārānusāreṇa karpādinā veditavyāḥ | "tathā gaṇimameyānāṃ śatād abhyadhike vadhaḥ" ity atrāpi evam eva śatasaṃkhyāvagantavyā | śeṣaśabdo yady apy uktasaṅkhyātirikte nyūnādhikasaṃkhyāke vartitum arhati, tathāpi laghudaṇḍābhidhānān nyūnasaṃkhyāka eva vartata iti mantavyam | kumbhaśabdaḥ khārīparyāyaḥ, tatra kvacid deśe kumbhaśabdaprayogāt | khāryāḥ punar iyattā smṛtyantare darśitā |

	aṅgulyagratragrāhyā śāṇam ity abhidhīyate |

	śāṇaṃ pāṇitalaṃ muṣṭiḥ prasṛtiś ca tathāñjaliḥ ||

	kuṭupaś ca tathā prasthaḥ āḍhako droṇa eva ca |

	mānī khārī ca vijñeyāḥ saṃkhyāyāś caturuttarāḥ || iti |

"dāpyas tasya ca tad dhanam" ity anena yady api prakṛtadhānyātmakam eva dhanaṃ tatsvāmine stenāpahṛtaṃ dāpya iti bhāti, tathāpi "stenāḥ sarva evāpahṛtaṃ dāpyāḥ" iti viṣṇusmaraṇāt sarvatra kṛte steye yojyam | anyāny api bahūni steyaviṣayāṇi vidyante vacanāni vistarabhayād iha na likhitāni mānavādau draṣṭavyāni ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ kevalasteyaviṣayāṇi**

**atha sāhasatrīsaṃgrahaviṣayāṇi**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	anicchayā yat kriyate suptonmattapramattayā |

	pralapantyā vā rahasi balātkārakṛtaṃ tu tat ||

saṃvarto 'pi |

	necchantyā yāni cihnāni blātkārakṛtāni ca |

	puṃsaḥ prasaṅgeṣu nārīṇāṃ tāni śṛṇvataḥ ||

	nakhadantakṣatakṣāmā kucagrahaṇavikṣatā |

	sadyo vidhvaṃsitā nārī balātkāreṇa dūṣitā ||

	uccair vikrosayantī ca rudantī lokasaṃnidhau |

	tasya nāmnā vadantī ca yāthāhaṃ tena dūṣitā ||

	śoced evaṃvidhair liṅgaiḥ kṣāmīkṛtapayodharā |

	chinnālaṅkārakeśaiś ca vyākulīkṛtalocanā ||

	rājñā sabhaiḥ sabhāṃ nītvā svayam anviṣya tatkṣaṇāt |

	yad brūyāt sahajaṃ vākyaṃ tat kartavyaṃ prayatnataḥ ||

	vivāde sākṣiṇām atra na kurvīta parigraham |

	prārthanād abhiśastasya na divyaṃ dātum arhati || iti |

balātkāreṇa sadyo vidhvaṃsitā dūṣitā nārī yā nakhadantakṣatādyanvitā vidhvaṃsakasya nāmnā tatkṛtavidhvaṃsanaprakāraṃ vadantī śocet tāṃ tatkṣaṇād rājā svayam anviṣya sabhyaiḥ saha sabhāṃ prāpya kā tava pīḍeti pṛcchet | tatas tadā tayāveditaṃ tad ākarṇya cihnair evātra rājñā nirṇetavyam ity arthaḥ | tatrāparadhino daṇḍam āha manuḥ |

	sahasraṃ brāhmaṇo daṇḍyo viprāṃ guptāṃ balād vrajan | iti |

guptāṃ svaniyamena rakṣitām | brāhmaṇetarasavarṇāviṣaye tu bṛhaspatir aparādhino daṇḍam āha |

	sahasā kāmayed yas tu dhanaṃ tasyākhilaṃ haret |

	utkṛtya liṅgavṛṣaṇau bhrāmayed gardabhena tu ||

kāmayet parastriyaṃ vrajed ity arthaḥ | uktadaṇḍasya viṣayaṃ viṣayāntare daṇḍāntaraṃ cāha sa eva | 

	damo neyaḥ samāyāṃ tu hīnāyām ardhikas tataḥ |

	puṃsaḥ kāryo 'dhikāyāṃ tu gamane sa pramāpaṇam ||

damaḥ "sahasā kāmayet" ityādivākyokto damaḥ | samāyāṃ jārasavarṇaparabhāryāviṣaye neyo jāraṃ prāpaṇīyaḥ | jārato hīnāviṣaye tūktadamād adhiko damo jāraṃ neyaḥ | jārato 'dhikāviṣaye tu sa evokto damaḥ puṃsaḥ kāryaḥ pramāpaṇam api puṃsaḥ karyam ity arthaḥ | yat tu kātyāyanena prāpaṇamātram uktam,

	strīṣu vṛttopabhogaḥ syāt prashya puruṣo yadā |

	vadhe tatra pravarteta kāryātikramaṇaṃ hi tat ||

iti, tad aguṇavato jāyāyāṃ draṣṭavyam | atra manvādibhiḥ puruṣasyaiva daṇḍābhidhānaṃ daṇḍaprapakastrīgataparādhābhāvād iti mantavyam | tathāpītarapuruṣasaṃsargajaṃ pāpaṃ nāryāḥ saṃpadyate | tataś cāsaṃvyavaharyatatrāpi daṇḍyāyām iva samānā | sā prāyaścittena kvacid apaiti kvacin nety āha bṛhaspatiḥ | 

	anicchantī tu yā bhuktā guptāṃ tāṃ vāsayed gṛhe |

	malināṅgīm adhaḥśayyāṃ piṇḍamātropajīvinīm ||

	kārayen niṣkṛtiṃ kṛcchraṃ parākaṃ vā same gatām |

	hīnavarṇāopabuktā yā tyājyā vadhyātha vā bhavet || iti |

guptāṃ punaḥ saṃbhogarahitām | vāsayed viśuddhiparyantam iti śeṣaḥ | same gatāṃ same varṇe puṃsi saṃgatām ity arthaḥ | hīnavarṇopabhuktāviṣaye vacanāntaraparyālocanayā yad vaktavyaṃ tad vistarabhayād iha noktam | svāvasare prāyaścittakāṇḍe vakṣyate |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ sāhasastrīsaṃgrahaviṣayāṇi**

**atha prasaṅgād evāsmin pade kevalastrīsaṃgrahaviṣayāṇy api **

**kānicid vacanāni likhyante**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	chadmanā kāmayed yas tu tasya sarvaharo damaḥ |

	aṅkayitvā bhagāṅkena purān nirvāsayet tataḥ ||

chadmanā kāmayed vañcanayā saṃgacchet | sarvaharaḥ sarvasvaharaṇam | tataḥ bhagāṅkakaraṇāntaram ity arthaḥ | sahasā kāmayed ityādivākyasyevāsyāpi,

	damo neyaḥ samāyāṃ tu hīnāyām ardhikas tataḥ |

	puṃsaḥ kāryo 'dhikāyāṃ tu gamane sa pramāpaṇam ||

iti viśeṣo draṣṭavyaḥ | tasyāyam arthaḥ: samāyāṃ jārasavarṇaparabhāryāgamanaviṣaye "chadmanā kāmayet" ityādivākyokto damo neyaḥ pumāṃsaṃ jārabhūtaṃ prāpaṇīyaḥ | hīnāyāṃ jārato hīnavarṇāyāṃ gamane tataḥ chadmanā gamananimittakād damād ardhiko 'rdhaḥ damaḥ puṃsaḥ kāryaḥ | adhikāyāṃ jārato 'dhikavarṇāyāṃ gamane sapramāpaṇam api puṃsaḥ kāryam sarvasvaharaṇaṃ kṛtvā pramāpayed ity arthaḥ | atrāpi puṃsa evāparādhitvāt tasyaiva daṇḍābhidhānam iti mantavyam | tenātrāpi striyā nasti daṇḍaḥ, tathāpi parapuruṣasaṃparkajanmadoṣasadbhāvād asaṃvyavahārayatāsti | tataś cātrāpi |

	anicchantī tu yā bhuktā suptāṃ tāṃ vāsayed gṛhe |

	malināṅgīm adhaḥśayyāṃ piṇḍamātropajīvinīm ||

	kārayen niṣkṛtiṃ kṛcchraṃ parākaṃ vā same gatām |

	hīnavarṇopabhuktā yā tyājyā vadhyātha vā bhavet ||

ityuktam anusaṃdheyam | strīpuṃsayoḥ parasparānurāgajopagamane tu daṇḍam āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	sajātāv uttamo daṇḍaḥ ānulomye tu madhyamaḥ |

	prātilomye vadhaḥ puṃsāṃ strīṇāṃ nāsādikartanam ||

atra nāryā api daṇḍābhidhānād anyonyānurāgajopabhogaviṣayam idaṃ vacanam iti gamyate, gurudaṇḍābhidhānāt saṃbandhibhiḥ prasahya paripālitacaritaśālinīviṣayam iti ca gamyate | madhyamo daṇḍaḥ catvāriṃśatsahitapañcaśatakārṣāpaṇātmakaḥ | evaṃ ca pañcaśatādhikatvād ayam api gurudaṇḍaḥ,

	ṛṇaṃ vā yadi vā daṇḍaḥ prāyaścittam athāpi vā |

	yatra pañcaśatādhi syāt tat kāryaṃ guru kīrtitam ||

iti smaraṇāt | tena gurutvān madhaymo 'pi pūrvoktaguptāviṣaya eva | karṇādikartanaṃ tu prātilomya eva, tadanantarābhidhānād vadhārdhatulyatvāc ca | evaṃ ca svajātāv ānulomye ca nāryāḥ puṃso 'bhihitārthadaṇḍārdhadaṇḍaḥ kalpanīya iti vadhārdhatulyakarṇādikartanābhidhānād evādhigantavyam | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	sarveṣu cāparādheṣu puṃso yo 'rthadamaḥ smṛtaḥ |

	tadardhaṃ yoṣito dadyuḥ . . . || iti |

puruṣavad aparādhaka**trya iti śeṣaḥ | yat tu manunā sānurāgayā brāhmaṇyā saha saṃgatasya madhyamasāhasam uktam,

	śatāni pañca daṇḍyaḥ syād icchantyā saha saṃgataḥ |

iti, tad arakṣitacaritaśālinīviṣayam | yat punar ānulomye 'py evam eva tenoktam |

	agupte vaiśyarājanye śūdrāṃ vā brāhmaṇo vrajet |

	śatāni pañca daṇḍyaḥ syāt sahasraṃ cāntyaje smṛtam || iti |

antyajaḥ prasiddhaś carmakarādiḥ | agupte mānasavyabhicārād arakṣite vṛhe 'varuddhe iti yāvat,

	arakṣitā gṛhe ruddhā puruṣair āptakāribhiḥ |

iti tenaivoktatvāt | evaṃ ca ruddhām ity atra gṛhe ruddhām ity adhyāhartavyam | evaṃ caitad āptakāribhiḥ prasahya rakṣitacaritaśālinīviṣayam ity avaseyam | yat tu brāhmaṇasya śūdratarānulomye tenoktam,

	sahasraṃ brāhmaṇo daṇḍaṃ dāpyo 'gupte tu te vrajan |

iti, te kṣatriyāvaiśye agupte mānasavyabhicārānavakāśāya gṛhavyāpārāvasaktacittatayā surakṣite vivakṣite, na tu svagṛhe 'varuddhe gurutaradaṇḍatvāt | dvividhaguptāvyatiriktaviṣaye tu vyāsa āha |

	guptāyāṃ saṃgrahe daṇḍo yathoktaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ |

	icchantyām āgatāyāṃ tu gacchato 'rdhadamaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

guptāṃ gacchato yāvān daṇḍa uktas taditarāṃ gacchatas tadardho daṇḍaḥ smṛtaḥ ity arthaḥ | evaṃ ca guptāyāḥ saṃgrahe yatra vadha uktaḥ tatra taditarasyāḥ saṃgrahe madhyamasāhasaḥ | yatra punaḥ madhyamasāhasa uktas tatra prathamasāhasa ity anusaṃdheyam | prātilomye tu jātiviśeṣato daṇḍaviśeṣān āha manuḥ |

	śūdro guptam aguptaṃ vā dvaijātaṃ varṇam āvasan |

	aguptam aṅgasarvasvī guptaṃ sarveṇa hīyate ||

asyārthaḥ: śūdraḥ svetaravarṇajāṃ parastriyaṃ gacchan mahāparādhī bhavati | tatra guptāyāṃ saṃgrahe tāvad aṅgasarvasvī tābhyāṃ hīyate, liṅgena dhanena ca hīyata iti yāvat | aguptāyāṃ saṃgrahe tu sarveṇa liṅgena śarīreṇa hīyata iti | tathā ca śūdrasyety anuvṛttau gautamaḥ: "āryastryabhigamane liṅgoddhāraḥ sarvasvaharaṇaṃ ca goptā ced vadho 'dhikaḥ" iti | āryastryabhigamane taivarṇikastryabhigamana ity arthaḥ | guptaṃ dvaijātaṃ varṇam āvasann ity anuvṛttau manuḥ |

	vaiśaḥ sarvasvadaṇḍaḥ syāt saṃvatsaranirodhitaḥ |

	sahasraṃ kṣatriyo daṇḍyo mauṇḍyaṃ mūtreṇa cārhati ||

saṃvatsaranirodhitaḥ bandhanāgāra iti śeṣaḥ | mūtreṇa gardabhasya gor vety śeṣaḥ | etayor evāguptāṃ brāhmaṇīṃ gacchatoḥ daṇḍam āha sa eva |

	brāḥmaṇīṃ tu yadāguptāṃ gacchetāṃ vaiśyapārthivau |

	vaiśyaṃ pañcaśataṃ kuryāt kṣatriyaṃ tu sahasriṇam ||

pañcaśataṃ kuryāt pañcaśatakārṣāpaṇadaṇḍena daṇḍayed ity arthaḥ | etayor eva guptāyāṃ brāhmaṇyāṃ daṇḍādhikyam āha sa eva |

	ubhāv api tu tāv eva brāhmaṇyā guptayā saha |

	viplutau śūdravad daṇḍyau dagdhavyau vā kaṭāgninā ||

śūdravad daṇḍyau liṅgena dhanena śarīreṇa ca hīnau kāryāv ity arthaḥ | viṣyāntare 'py etayor eva daṇḍāntaram āha sa eva |

	vaiśyas cet kṣatriyāṃ guptāṃ vaiśyāṃ vā kṣatriyo vrajan |

	yo brāhmaṇyām aguptāyāṃ tāv ubhau daṇḍam arhataḥ ||

"vaiśyaṃ pañcaśataṃ kuryāt kṣatriyaṃ tu sahasriṇam" itiuktadaṇḍam arhata ity arthaḥ | prātilome 'py alpadaṇḍārhatvāyātyantanirguṇapatipatnīviṣaya eva vaisyadaṇḍo 'yam draṣṭavyaḥ | ānulomye tu gurudaṇḍārhatvāyātyantasaguṇapatipatnīviṣaya evāyaṃ kṣatriyadaṇḍo draṣṭavyaḥ | evaṃ ca pāriśeṣyāt "vaiśyaḥ sarvasvadaṇḍaḥ syāt" ityādinokto gurudaṇḍaḥ svajatāv evatyantasaguṇapatipanīviṣaya evāvatiṣṭhata ity avagantavyam | svajātāv api kvacic chārīradaṇḍam aparādhādhikyaṃ pradarśayann āha naradaḥ |

	mātā mātṛṣvasā śvaśrūr mātulānī pitṛṣvasā |

	pitṛvyasakhiśiṣyastrī bhaginī tatsakhī snuṣā ||

	duhitācāryabhāryā ca sagotrā śaraṇāgatā |

	rājñī pravrajitā dhātrī sādhvī varṇottamā ca yā ||

	āsām anyatamāṃ gatvā gurutalpaga ucyate |

	śiśnasya kartanaṃ tatra nānyo daṇḍo vidhīyate || iti |

anyo 'smān nyūna iti śeṣaḥ, adhikasya vidhānāt | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	pituḥ svasāraṃ matuś ca matulānīṃ snuṣām api |

	mātuḥ sapatnīṃ bhaginīm ācāryatanayāṃ tathā ||

	ācāryapatnīṃ svasutāṃ gacchaṃs tu gurutalpagaḥ |

	chitvā liṅgaṃ vadhas tasya sakāmāyāḥ striyās tathā || iti |

brāhmaṇavyatiriktaviṣayam etat, vadhasyāpi vidhānāt | asminn eva viṣaye striyā api vadhaḥ, "sakāmāyāḥ striyās tathā" iti vacanāt | anyatrāpi kvacit striyā vadham āha manuḥ |

	bhartāraṃ laṅghayed yāt tu jātistrīguṇadarpitā |

	tāṃ śvabhiḥ khādayed rājā saṃsthāne bahusaṃsthite ||

laṅghayet kim anenātyantānanurūpeṇa patyeti upapatiṃ saṃāśrayed ity arthaḥ | yamo 'pi |

	vṛṣalaṃ sevate yā tu brāhmaṇī madamohitā |

	tāṃ śvabhiḥ khādayed rājā saṃsthāne vadhyaghātinām |

	vaiśyaṃ vā kṣatriyaṃ vāpi brāhmaṇī sevate tu yā |

	śiroso muṇḍanaṃ tasyāḥ prayāṇaṃ gardabhena tu || iti |

madamohiteti vadan vadhadaṇḍasyāsārvatrikatvaṃ darśayati | tena nāryāḥ karṇādikartanam iti prāgukto daṇḍo rāgād atyantāsaktāviṣaya iti mantavyam | atyantāsaktirahitāviṣaye tu na śārīro daṇḍaḥ, saṃvyavahārārtham,

	yat puṃsaḥ paradāreṣu tac caināṃ cārayed vratam |

iti prāyascittavidhānāt | evaṃ ca yat kātyāyanenoktam,

	nāsvatantrāḥ striyo grāhyāḥ pumāṃs tatrāparādhyati |

	prabhunā śāsanīyās tā rājā tu puruṣaṃ nayet ||

	proṣitasvāmikā nārī prāpitā yady api grahe (?) |

	tāvat sā bandhane sthāpyā yāvat pratyāgataḥ prabhuḥ || 

iti, tad vratacāraṇārhāsvatantrāsu draṣṭavyam | yoṣīd utthāpitānurāgajasaṃgrahe tu bṛhaspatir āha |

	gṛham āgatya yā nārī pralobhya sparśanādinā |

	kāmayet tatra sā daṇḍyā narasyārdhadamaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

daṇḍyā yoṣito 'bhihitadaṇḍeneti śeṣaḥ | ardhadamo yoṣiddamād ardhadamaḥ | yat tu yamenoktam,

	paradārasavarṇāsu daṇḍyāḥ syuḥ pañcakṛṣṇalān |

	asavarṇāḥ svānulomye daṇḍo dvādaśako mataḥ ||

iti — dvādaśakaḥ dvādaśakārṣāpaṇa ity arthaḥ — tad etad badhakīviṣayam, bandhakyadhikāre tenasy daṇḍasya vidhānāt | veśyāviṣaye tu vyāsa āha |

	paroparuddhāgamane pañcāśatpaṇako damaḥ |

	prashya veśyāgamane daṇḍo daśapaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ kevalastrīsaṃgrahaviṣayāṇi**

**atha sāhasapadāntargatobhayapāruṣyaviṣayāṇi**

tatra nāradaḥ |

	phalamūlodakādīnāṃ kṣetropakaraṇasya ca |

	bhaṅgākṣepāvamardādyaiḥ prathamaṃ sāhasaṃ smṛtam ||

	vāsaḥpraśvannapānānāṃ gṛhopakaraṇasya ca |

	etenaiva prakāreṇa madhyamaṃ sāhasaṃ smṛtam ||

	vyāpādo viṣaśastrādyaiḥ paradārābhimarśanam |

	prāṇoarodhi yac cānyad uktam uttamasāhasam ||

	tasya daṇḍaḥ kriyāpekṣaḥ prathamasya śatavaraḥ |

	madhyamasya tu śāstrajñaiḥ dṛṣṭaḥ pañcaśatāvaraḥ ||

	vadhaḥ sarvasvaharaṇaṃ puryā nirvāsanāṅkane |

	tadaṅgaccheda ity ukto daṇḍa uttamasāhase ||

	syātāṃ saṃvyavahāryau dvau ghṛtadaṇḍau tu pūrvayoḥ |

	dhṛtadaṇḍo 'py asaṃbhāṣyo jñeya uttamasāhase || iti |

etenaiva prakāreṇety anena bhaṅgākṣepāvamardādyaḥ prakāra uktaḥ | bhaṅgaḥ phalādirūpasya | ākṣepaḥ ākrośaḥ phalamūlāder vācā nyagbhāvakaraṇam iti yāvat | avamardaḥ svarūpāvaśeṣeṇa pīḍanam | ādyaśabdenāmedhyādinā upaghātādi gṛhyate | atrākṣepaśabdena vākpāruṣyam uktam | bhaṅgāvamardādyair ity anena daṇḍapāruṣyam | tayoḥ prathamamadhyamādisāhasabhedoktyā tu sahaśākṛtaviṣayatāpi jñāpitā | evaṃ ca phalamūlādiṣu sahasā kṛtaṃ vākpāruṣyaṃ daṇḍapāruṣyaṃ vā prathamasāhasam | vāsaḥpaśvādiṣu kṛtaṃ tu madhyamasāhasam | prāṇiṣu prāṇoparodhitayā kṛtaṃ punar uttamasāhasam iti mantavyam | tasya sāhasavākpāruṣyasya sāhasadaṇḍapāruṣyasya vāparādhasya daṇḍaḥ kriyāpekṣaḥ aparādhakriyāpekṣaḥ kalpanīya iti śeṣaḥ | tatra prathamasya daṇḍaḥ śatāvaraḥ | śatakārṣāpaṇād ūno nāstīty arthaḥ | evam uttaravākyasyāpy artho vyākhyeyaḥ | prathamasāhasadaṇḍasya kriyāpekṣayā ādhikyaṃ madhyamasāhasadaṇḍāt kalpyam | vadhādyuttamasāhasadaṇḍapañcake 'pi kriyāpekṣayā vyavasthā kalpyā, "tasya daṇḍaḥ kriyāpekṣaḥ" ity asya prathamamadhyamottamasāhasādhārasyehābhidhānāt | kriyāpekṣaḥ sahasākṛtaḥ pāruṣyatāratamyāpekṣa ity arthaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ sāhasapadāntargatobhayapāruṣyaviṣayāṇi **

**atha prasaṅgāt sāhasakalpāparādhadaṇḍaviṣayāṇi **

**kānicid vacanāni likhyante**

tatra manuḥ |

	kūṭaśāsanakartṝṃś ca prakṛtīnāṃ ca dūṣakān |

	strībālabrāhmaṇaghnāṃś ca hanyād dviṭsevinas tathā ||

dviṭsevinaḥ śatrusevakān | dvitīyapādas tu "svāmyamātyadurgakośadaṇḍarāṣṛramitrāṇi prakṛtayas taddūṣakāṃś ca hanyāt" iti viṣṇuvacanād eva vyākhyātaḥ | daṇḍaśabdo 'tra senāmātram ācaṣṭte, "rāṣṭradurgabalāni ca" ity amarasiṃhenābhidhānāt | mānave brāhmaṇagrahaṇaṃ manuṣyopalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva rājā hanyād ity anuvṛttau viṣṇuḥ: "strībālapuruxaghātinaś ca" iti | atha vā brāhmaṇaghnagrahaṇaṃ mahāpātikinām upalakṣaṇārtham | tathā ca tatraivoktam:

	brahmahā ca surāpaś ca taskaro gurutalpagaḥ |

	ete sarve pṛthag vadhyā mahāpātakino narāḥ ||

yasya pratiṣiddhā surā sa iha surāpo vivakṣitaḥ | taskaro 'py atra suvarṇasteyī vivikṣitaḥ, "mahāpātakinaḥ" ity abhidhānāt | vipretaramahāpātakiviṣayam etat | vipraviṣaye tv āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	mahāpātakayukto 'pi na vipro vadham arhati |

	nirvāsanāṅkane mauṇḍyaṃ tasya kuryān narādhipaḥ ||

kāmakṛtaviṣayam etat | nivāsanādidaṇḍe kṛte 'py atra doṣo nāpaiti, uttamasāhasakalpāparādhatvāt,

	dhṛtadaṇḍo 'py asaṃbhāṣyo jñeya uttamasāhase |

ity asya tatkalpāparādhe 'py atidiṣṭatvāt |

	dhṛtadaṇḍo 'py asaṃbhāṣyo jñeya uttamasāhase |

ity asya tatkalpāparādhe 'py atidiṣṭatvāt |

	ata eva nirvāsitānām aṅkitānām apy asaṃvyavahāryatāṃ prapañcitavān manuḥ |

	asaṃbhojyā hy asaṃyājyā apāṭhyāś cāvivāhinaḥ |

	careyuḥ pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ sarvadharmabahiṣkṛtāḥ ||

	jñātisaṃbandhibhiś caite kartavyāḥ kṛtalakṣaṇāḥ |

	nirvācyā nirnamaskārās tan manor anuśāsanam || iti |

sarvadharmabahiṣkṛtāḥ śrautasmārtakarmaparibhraṣṭā ity arthaḥ | kṛtalakṣaṇāḥ lalāṭe kṛtāṅkāḥ | jñātyādibhiḥ nirvācyāḥ nirnamaskārāḥ kartavyā ity anvayaḥ | yat tu tenaivoktam,

	āgaḥsu brāhmaṇasyaiva kāryo madhyamasāhasaḥ |

	vivāsyo vā bhaved rāṣṭrāt sadravyaḥ saparicchadaḥ || iti |

āgaḥsu mahāpātakeṣv ity arthaḥ | tad akāmakṛtaviṣayam | tatrāpi prāyaścittam akurvato madhayamasāhaso daṇḍaḥ kāryaḥ | tad apy akurvato vivāsa iti vyavasthā jñeyā | brāhmaṇetaramahāpātakiviṣaye tv akāmakṛte sravasvaharaṇaṃ kāmakṛte vadha ity aha sa eva,

	itare kṛtavantas tu pāpāny etāny akāmataḥ |

	sarvasvahāram arhanti kāmatas tu pramāpaṇam ||

	ete sarve pṛthag vadhyā mahāpātakino narāḥ ||

ity anena vipretareṣu niṣkāraṇaṃ vadhyasoktatvāt,

	brāhmaṇān bādhamānaṃ tu kāmād avaravarṇajam |

	hanyac citravadhopāyair udvejanakarair nṛpaḥ ||

ity tenaiva brahmaghavadhe viśeṣasmaraṇāc ca | avaravarṇajaṃ brāhmaṇetaravarṇajam | sarvasvahāram arhanti prāyaścittam akurvanta iti śeṣaḥ | kurvantas tu karma hantīty (?) apekṣite sa evāha |

	prāyaścittaṃ tu kurvāṇāḥ pūrve varṇā yathoditam |

	nāṅkyā rājñā lalāṭe tu dāpyas tūttamasāhasam ||

nāṅkyāḥ nāpi sarvasvadaṇḍārhāḥ kiṃ tūttamasāhasaṃ dāpyā ity arthaḥ | yat tu bodhāyanenoktam: "kṣatriyādīnāṃ brāhmaṇavadhe vadhaḥ sarvasvaharaṇaṃ ca" iti, tat sāhasarūpavadhaviṣayam | yat tv anantaram uktam: "teṣām eva tulyāpakṛṣṭavadhe yathābalam anurūpaṃ daṇḍaṃ prakalpayet" iti, teṣāṃ kṣatriyādīnāṃ tulyāpakṛṣṭavadhe balānurūpaṃ daṇḍaṃ prakalpayed ity arthaḥ | tat kaṇṭhoktyaiva spaṣṭaviṣayam | daṇḍaprakalpanaprakāraś cānantaram uktam: "kṣatriyavadhe gosahasram ṛṣabhaikādhikaṃ rājña utsṛjed vairaniryātanārthaṃ śataṃ vaiśye daśa śūdre vṛṣabhaś cātrādhikaḥ śūdravadhena strīvadho govadhaś ca vyākhyātaḥ" iti | utsṛjet dadyād ity arthaḥ | vaiśyasya vadhe śataṃ gośatam | śūdre śūdravadhe daśa gāḥ tāsu vṛṣabho 'dhikaḥ | vairaniryātanārthaṃ rājña utsṛjed ity ubhayatrānuṣajyate | vairaniryātanārtham ity anenāyaṃ daṇḍo na doṣaniryātanārtham ity uktam | tenātra dhṛtadaṇḍasyāpy asaṃbhāṣyatvādikaṃ nāpaitīti darśitam | evaṃ ca jaḍādhikṛtakṣatriyādivadhe kāmakṛte pādono gosahasrādiko daṇḍaḥ kalpanīyaḥ | akāmakṛte tv ardhona iti jñeyam | praṇāḍyā kṛtvākāmataś cet tripādonaḥ kalpanīyaḥ, doṣānusāritvād daṇḍasya | doṣābhāvaṃ kvacit praṇāḍyā vadhe tv āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	amanuṣyakṛto doṣo nāpaihīti prajalpataḥ |

	kāṣṭhaloṣṭeṣupāṣāṇabāhāyudhakṛtas (?) tathā |

asyārthaḥ: amanuṣyaiḥ paśupakṣyādibhiḥ svata eva kṛto hiṃsādidoṣaḥ tatsvāmināṃ teṣu balavardhanaghāsādidāyitve 'pi na bhavati | tathānyapreṣitakāṣṭhaloṣṭapāṣāṇapṛṣṭhayānavāhādikṛto hiṃsādidoṣaḥ prerakasyāpasareti punaḥ punar uccair uccarituḥ na bhavatīti | tato 'tra daṇḍo nāstīty abhiprāyaḥ | daṇḍābhāvasyātrābhipretasya kvacid apavādam aha sa eva |

	śakto hy amokṣayan svāmī daṃṣṭriṇāṃ śṛṅgiṇāṃ tathā |

	prathamaṃ sāhasaṃ dadyād vikruṣṭe dviguṇaṃ tathā ||

vikruṣṭe mocaya mocayet pīḍyamānena ākrandite 'py amokṣayan prathamasāhasadvayaṃ dadyād ity arthaḥ | bṛhaspatir api sāhasakalpāparādhe daṇḍam āha |

	daṇḍājinādinā yuktam ātmānaṃ darśayanti ye |

	hiṃsanti chadmanā śūnye vadhyās te rājapūruṣaiḥ ||

yājñavalkyas tu saṃbandhivadhe daṇḍam āha |

	viṣāgnidāṃ patigurunijapatyapramāpaṇīm |

	vikarṇakaranāsoṣṭhīṃ kṛtvā gobhiḥ pramāpayet ||

asaṃbandhipuruṣe tu viṣāgnidānādau sāhasikavadhavat sahāyāder vadho na kāryaḥ, kiṃ tu tasyaiva kārya ity āha yamaḥ |

	viṣāgnidāyakāś corāḥ ghātakāś copaghātakāḥ |

	svaśarīreṇa daṇḍyāḥ syuḥ manur āha prajāpatiḥ ||

upaghatakāḥ anyadvārā ghātakāḥ | gurvādighātakasyāpi strīvad daṇḍaḥ, viśeṣāsmṛteḥ daṇḍāpūpanyāyasiddhatvāc ca | tathā hi, yatra striyā api gurudaṇḍas tatra sutarāṃ puṃśa iti gamyate | vividhavadho vā, strīdaṇḍāpekṣayā puruṣasyānyatra daṇḍādhikyadarśanāt | saṃbandhivadhanimittadaṇḍo 'yaṃ kāmakṛte draṣṭavyaḥ, kāmakṛtamahāpatakadaṇḍādhikyasya akāmakṛtaviṣaye kalpanāyogāt | akāmakṛtasaṃbandhivadhaviṣaye tu akāmakṛtamahāpātakadaṇḍādhikadaṇḍatvāya purān nirvāsanāntaṃ sarvasvaharaṇaṃ prāyaścittam akurvato daṇḍaḥ kalpanīyaḥ | kurvatas tūttamasāhasadvayam ity ūhyam | manur api sāhasakalpāparādhe daṇḍam āha |

	taṭākabhedakaṃ hanyād apsu suddhavadhena vā |

	tac cāpi pratisaṃskuryād dadyād vottamasāhasam ||

taṭākamahattvālpatvānusāreṇātra daṇḍavikalpe vyavasthā kāryā | tathā,

	yas tu pūrvaniviṣṭasya taṭākasyodakaṃ haret |

	āgamaṃ vāpy upārundhyāt sa dāpyaḥ pūrvasāhasam ||

āgamam udakasya taṭākaṃ praty āgamanam | haret svataṭākādipūraṇāyeti śeṣaḥ | evam upārundhyād ity atrāpi śeṣo draṣṭavyaḥ | kātyāyano 'pi |

	hared bhindyād dahed vāpi devānāṃ pratimā yadi |

	tadgṛhaṃ caiva yo bhindyāt prāpnuyāt pūrvasāhasam || \
	pramāṇena tu kūṭena mudrayā vāpi kūṭayā |

	kāryaṃ tu sādhayed yo vai sa dāpyo damam uttamam || iti |

pramāṇaṃ likhitādi | bṛhaspatir api |

	mantrauṣadhibalāt kiṃcit saṃbhrāntiṃ darśayanti ye |

	mūlakarma ca kurvanti nirvāyās te mahībhujā ||

mūlakarma vaśikriyāviśeṣo mūladyauṣadhasādhyaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ sāhasakalpaparādhadaṇḍaviṣayāṇi **

**samāptaṃ ca sāhasākhyapadasya prāsaṅgikasya vidhivitānam**

**atha vākpāruṣyasya padaya vidhir ucyate **

tatra brhaspatiḥ |

	samajātiguṇānāṃ tu vākparuṣye parasparam |

	vinayo 'bhihitaḥ śāstre paṇā ardhatrayodaśāḥ ||

ardhaṃ trayodaśaṃ yeṣāṃ dvādaśānāṃ te tathoktāḥ | kevalajātisāmye tu manur āha |

	samavarṇe tu sarveśāṃ dvādaśaiva vyatikrame | iti |

parasparaṃ vācaiveti śeṣaḥ | vācā vyatikramasya paurvāparyādikṛtaveśeṣābhave dvayoḥ samadoṣayor dvādaśa paṇā eva daṇḍo bhavati na punar anyatarasya nyūlo 'dhiko vety arthaḥ | ata eva smṛtyantaram |

	pāruṣyadoṣānṛtayoḥ yugapatsaṃpravṛttayoḥ |

	viśeṣaś cen na dṛśyeta vinayaḥ syāt samastayoḥ ||

viśeṣadarśane tu tadanusāreṇa viṣama eva damaḥ syād ity abhiprāyaḥ | ata eva bṛhaspatiḥ |

	smānayoḥ samo daṇḍao nyūnasya dviguṇas tataḥ |

	uttamasyārdhikaḥ prokto vākpāruṣye parasparam || \
ayugapat saṃpravṛttayoḥ samānayor api viṣamo daṇḍaḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	pūrvam ākṣārayed yas tu niyataṃ syāt sa doṣabhāk |

	paścād yaḥ so 'py asatkārī pūrve tu vinayo guruḥ ||

pūrve tv ākṣāraṇe tannimittako vinayaḥ paścād ākṣāraṇanimittakavinayād abhyadhiko bhaved ity arthaḥ | varṇāditaḥ samayor nibandhe tu viśeṣadarśane tannimittam api vinayagauravaṃ bhavatīty āha sa eva |

	dvayor āpannayos tulyam anubadhnāti yaḥ pumān |

	tayor daṇḍam avāpnoti pūrvo vā yadi vottaraḥ ||

tulyam āpannayoḥ samatvenaiva ākṣepakarayor iti yāvat | tayor daṇḍam avāpnoti tulyam āpannayor dvayoḥ | daṇḍo militayor yāvān tāvantam āpnotīty arthaḥ | yaḥ punar anutāpān nibandhaṃ tyajati tasya daṇḍahrāsakalpanasya prakāram āha uśanā |

	mohāt pramādāt saṃgharṣāt prītyā voktaṃ mayeti yaḥ |

	nāham evaṃ punar vakṣye daṇḍārdhaṃ tasya kalpayet ||

evaṃ jātiguṇavayovidyāviśeṣadarśane, tathā prathamamadhyamottamabhāvena tridhābhihitavākpāruṣyāntargatabhedadarśane tathā niṣṭhurāślīlatīvratvādivākpāruṣyaviśeṣadarśane, tathā śrutābhijanadeśakarmaśarīrapitṛmātṛgurvādyadhikṣepaviśeṣadarśane tattannibandhnoccāvacadaṇḍavidhāyikāḥ smṛtayo yady api vacaḥsamuccayakāraiḥ samuccitāḥ | asmābhis tu saṃprati tadarthānuṣṭhānaniṣṭhaprajāśikṣakābhāvāt vṛthāgranthavistarāpattir mā bhūd iti na samuccitāḥ | kvacid vākpāruṣyadaṇḍasyāpavādam āha vacobhaṅgyā bṛhaspatiḥ |

	guṇahīnasya pāruṣye brāhmaṇo nāparādhnuyāt | iti |

satyavāditve 'pi vākpāruṣyadaṇḍo nāpaitīty āha vacobhaṅgyā nāradaḥ |

	patitaṃ patitery uktvā coraṃ coreti va punaḥ |

	vacanāt tulyadoṣaḥ syān mithyā dvirdoṣatāṃ vrajet ||

vacanāt tathyavacanāt | tathā ca sa eva |

	duṣṭasyaiva tu yo doṣān kīrtayet krodhakāraṇāt |

	anyāpadesavādī ca vāgduṣṭaṃ taṃ naraṃ viduḥ ||

krodhakāraṇād iti vadan duṣṭapariharaṇakāraṇād doṣakīrtanaṃ na doṣakārīti darśayati | darśitaṃ ca katyāyanena |

	yatra syāt parihārārthaṃ patitas tena kīrtanam |

	vacanāt tatra na syāt tu doṣo yatra vibhāvayet ||

vacanāt patitādikīrtanād ity arthaḥ | yatrābhiyogādau pātityādikaṃ sādhayet tatrāpi vacanād doṣo na syād ity arthaḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ vākpāruṣyasya padasya vidhivitānam**

**atha daṇḍapāruṣyākhyasya padasya vidhir ucyate**

atra manuḥ |

	eṣa daṇḍavidhiḥ prokto vākpāruṣyasya tattvataḥ |

	ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi daṇḍapāruṣyanirṇayam ||

daṇḍapāruṣyasya prativyakti daṇḍanirṇayam ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmīty arthaḥ | daṇḍapāruṣyavyaktayas tu diṅmātrataḥ pariśiṣṭakāreṇa pradarśitāḥ |

	duḥkhaṃ raktaṃ vraṇaṃ bhaṅgaṃ chedanaṃ bhedanaṃ tathā |

	kuryad yaḥ prāṇināṃ tad dhi daṇḍaparuṣyam ucyate ||

sthāvarajaṅgamaprāṇināṃ prāṇyantarakṛtaṃ nakhādinā tvagbhedādibhavaṃ duḥkhaṃ raktavraṇādikaṃ ca daṇḍapāruṣyam ucyata ity arthaḥ | vyāsenāpi diṅmātreṇa pradarśitāḥ |

	bhasmādinā prakṣipaṇaṃ (?) tāḍanaṃ ca karādinā |

	āveṣṭanaṃ cāṃśukādyair daṇḍapāruṣyam ucyate || iti |

ādigrahaṇenopari prakṣepaṇād duḥkhakaraṃ kardamapāṃsumalādi dravyaṃ gṛhyate | karādinety anenadiśabdena laguḍapāṣāṇeṣṭakāyudhādi dravyam, ādyagrahaṇena rajjuśṛṅkhalādi dravyam | pradarśitavyaktīnāṃ madhye kāsucid vyaktiṣu daṇḍe nirṇayam aha manuḥ |

	tvagbhedakaḥ śataṃ daṇḍyo lohitasya ca darśakaḥ |

	māṃsabhettā tu ṣaṇṇiṣkān pravāsyas tv asthibhedakaḥ ||

māṃsabhettā vraṇakartā | asthibhedako 'sthibhañjakaḥ | kātyāyano 'pi |

	karṇōṣṭhaghrāṇapādākṣijihvāśiśnakarasya ca |

	chedane cottamo daṇḍo bhedane madhyamo bhṛguḥ ||

bṛhaspatir api |

	bhasmādinā prakṣipaṇaṃ tāḍanaṃ ca karādinā |

	prathamaṃ daṇḍapāruṣyaṃ damaḥ kāryo 'tra māṣakaḥ |

	iṣṭakopalakāṣṭhaiś ca tāḍane tu dvimāṣakaḥ |

	kāryaḥ kṛtanurūpas tu lagne ghāte damo budhaiḥ ||

	eṣa daṇḍaḥ sameṣūktaḥ parastrīṣv adhikeṣu ca |

	dviguṇās triguṇo jñeyaḥ prādhānyāpekṣayā budhaiḥ || iti |

yājñavalkyas tv apradarśitāsv api daṇḍapāruṣyavyaktiṣu daṇḍam āha |

	pādakeśāṃśukakarolluñchaneṣu pāṇān dasa |

	pīṣākarṣāṃśukāveṣṭapādādhyāse śataṃ damaḥ ||

atra aṃśukāveṣṭanaṃ ca aṃśukādair iti pradarśitam | śeṣās tv apradarśitā vyaktatyaḥ | evam anyāsv apy apradarśitavyaktiṣu prativyaktidaṇḍanirṇayasmṛtayo yady api samuccayakāraiḥ samuccitāḥ | asmābhis tu vistarabhayān samuccitāḥ | kātyāyanas tu vākpāruṣyoktaprativyaktidaṇḍanirṇaya ihānuktadaṇḍaviṣaye kvacid anusaṃdheya iti darśayati |

	vākpāruṣye yathaivoktāḥ prātilomyānulomyataḥ |

	tathaiva daṇḍapāruṣye pātyā (?) daṇḍā yathākramam ||

evaṃ cātra prativyakti daṇḍanirṇayaḥ prātilomyādāv api kātyāyanena smṛta iti na kvacid asmṛtāḥ daṇḍāh pātyāḥ | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanv</span> evam api kvacid atrāparādhānusāreṇa kalpitā daṇḍā pātyāḥ, anantavyaktiṣu prativyakti daṇḍanirṇayasmaraṇayogāt | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | ata evoktam uśanasā |

	yatra nokto damaḥ sarvair ānantyāt tu mahātmabhiḥ |

	tatra kāryaṃ parijñāya kartavyaṃ daṇḍadhāraṇam ||

ānantyāt pāruṣyavyaktīnām iti śeṣaḥ | kāryaṃ prāṇiṣu prāṇyantarair utpāditaṃ duḥkham | ata eva manuḥ |

	manuṣyāṇāṃ paśūnāṃ ca duḥkhāya prahṛte sati |

	yathā yathā mahad duḥkhaṃ daṇḍaṃ kuryāt tathā tathā ||

kenacit kasyacid duḥkhyāya prahṛte sati svalpaṃ duḥkhaṃ mahad vā bhavatu, daṇḍas tu mahān evety aha sa eva |

	yena kenacid aṅgena hiṃsyāc chreyāṃsam antyajaḥ |

	chettavyaṃ tat tad evāsya tan manor anuśāsanam ||

hiṃsyāt praharet | śreyāṃsaṃ dvijam | antyajaḥ śūdraḥ | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	yenāṅgena dvijātīnāṃ śūdraḥ praharate ruṣā |

	chettavyaṃ tad bhavet tasya manunā samudāhṛtam ||

yena kenacid aṅgeneti sāmānyenoktiṃ svayam eva manur viśeṣaniṣṭhāṃ kartum āha |

	pāṇim udyamya daṇḍaṃ vā pāṇicchedanam arhati |

	pādena praharan kopāt pādacchedanam arhati ||

	avaniṣṭhīvato darpād dvāv oṣṭhau chedayen nṛpaḥ |

	avamūtrayato meḍhram avaśardhayato gudam |

	keśeṣu gṛhṇato hastau chedayed avicārayan |

	pādayor dāḍhikāyāṃ ca grīvāyāṃ vṛṣaṇeṣu ca || iti |

pāṇiṃ daṇḍaṃ vā udyamyety atra praharann ity anuṣajyate | keśeṣv ekena hastena gṛhṇato 'py ubhayahastacchedanavidhiḥ dvivacanād gamyate | dāḍhikā puruṣasya pradhānaṃ liṅgam ucyate | kopād darpād iti ca vadan mohapramādadinā prahārāvaṣṭhīvanādikaṃ kurvan na daṇḍya iti darśayati | darśitaṃ ca yājñavalkyena |

	hīneṣv ardhadamo mohamadādibhir adaṇḍanam | iti |

hīneṣu pāruṣyakṛdapekṣayā jātyādinā hīneṣu puruṣeṣu pāruṣye kṛte tatkartur ardhadamaḥ sameṣūktadamapekṣayā bhavatīty arthaḥ | parasparapāruṣyakāriṣu damam āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	dvayoḥ praharator daṇḍaḥ samayos tu samaḥ smṛtaḥ |

	ārambhako 'nubandhī ca dāpyaḥ syād adhikaṃ damam ||

saṃkhyayā samabhāvābhāve tv āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	ekaṃ ghnatāṃ bahūnāṃ tu yathokād dviguṇo damaḥ | iti |

bahūnāṃ pratyekaṃ dviguṇo damo na punaḥ samudāyasya prahārakasya, pratyekam evāparādhadhikyāt | ata eva viṣṇuḥ: "ekaṃ ghnatāṃ bahūnāṃ pratyakesyoktadaṇḍo dviguṇaḥ" iti | pratyekasya pratyekam ity arthaḥ | vraṇādiduḥkheṣv atiduḥsaheṣu jāteṣv āha katyāyanaḥ |

	dehendriyavināśe tu yathā daṇḍaṃ prakalpayet |

	tathā tuṣṭikaraṃ deyaṃ samutthānaṃ ca paṇḍitaiḥ ||

tuṣṭikaraṃ duḥsahavraṇatuṣṭikaraṃ deyaṃ duḥsahavraṇādikāriṇā deyam | samutthānaṃ vyayaṃ paṇḍitaiḥ vraṇagurutvānusāreṇa kalpitam iti śeṣaḥ | samutthānaṃ ca ā vraṇaropaṇād deyam,

	samutthānavyayaṃ casau dadyād ā vraṇaropaṇāt |

iti tenaivoktatvāt | samutthānavyayaṃ bhiṣagbheṣajapathyapānādyarthaṃ kriyamāṇaṃ vyayam | bṛhaspatir api |

	aṅgāvapīḍane caiva chedane bhedane tathā |

	samutthānavyayaṃ dapyaḥ kalahāpahṛtaṃ ca yat ||

samutthānavyayam aṅgādipīḍanadiduḥkhotpādako dāpya ity āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	duḥkham utpādayed yas tu sa samutthānaṃ vyayam |

	dāpyaḥ . . . || iti |

duḥkham utpādayen manuṣyagrāmyapaśūnām iti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca viṣṇuḥ: "sarve ca puruṣapīḍākarās tadutthaṃ vyayaṃ dāpyāḥ grāmyapaśupīḍākarāś ca" iti | grāmyapaśupīḍātiśayena paśumaraṇe tv āha sa eva: "grāmyapaśughātī kārṣāpaṇaśataṃ daṇḍyaḥ paśusvāminaś ca tanmūlyaṃ dadyāt" iti | prāṇighātanibandho daṇḍaḥ kvacit kvacid aśakyapratīkāraviṣaya doṣābhāvān nety āha manuḥ |

	chinne nasye yuge bhagne tiryakpratimukhāgat |

	akṣabhaṅge ca yānasya cakrabhaṅge tathaiva ca ||

	chedane caiva yantrāṇāṃ yoktraraśmes tathaiva ca |

	ākrande cāpy apaihīti na daṇḍaṃ manur abravīt || iti |

chinne nasye balīvarān nāsikāstharajjvādau truṭite | yuge śakaṭādiyugakāṣṭhe bhagne | tiryakpratimukhāgate kathaṃcid bhūvaiṣamyadinā tiryagabhimukhaṃ vā parāvṛtte yāne | yantrāṇi śakaṭādikāṣṭānāṃ bandhanārthaṃ rajjvādīni | balīvardādiniyantṛkapāśapragrahayor yoktraraśmiśabdābhyāṃ pṛthag abhidhānād yantraśabdena na grahaṇam | apaihīty ākrande apaihīty uccair uccārite | apaihītiśabdo 'pasaretyāditatsamānārthākhilaśabdānāṃ pradarśanārtham | tenāpabhraṃśabhāṣayāpy ākrande kṛte na daṇḍaḥ | śakyapratīkāre 'tropekṣakasya daṇḍam aha sa eva |

	yatrāpavartate yugyaṃ vaivuṇyāt prājakasya tu |

	tatra svāmī bhaved daṇḍyo hiṃsāyāṃ dviśataṃ damam ||

prājakasya nodakasya, śakaṭādinetur iti yāvat | dviśatagrahaṇaṃ tattatprāṇihiṃsāyāṃ viśeṣavihitadaṇḍopalakṣaṇārtham | prājakasya vaiguṇyād ekahastatvādikāt svāminā vetanalāghavārthamanumatāt | praguṇaprājakapramādādinā pravṛtte yugye na svāmī daṇḍyaḥ, kiṃ tu prājaka ity aha sa eva |

	prājakaś ced bhaved āptaḥ prājako daṇḍam arhati | iti |

āptaḥ praguṇa ity arthaḥ | nārado 'pi kvacid daṇḍyaḥ prabhur ity āha |

	putrāparādhe na pitā na svāmī śuni daṇḍabhāk |

	na markaṭe ca tatsvāmī tair eva prahito na cet ||

sthāvaraprāṇipīḍākarāṇāṃ tu daṇḍam āha manuḥ |

	vanaspatīnāṃ sarveṣām upabhogo yathā yathā |

	tathā tathā damaḥ kāryo hiṃsāyām iti dhāraṇā ||

sthāvaraprāṇijātopalakṣaṇārthaṃ vanaspatigrahaṇam | phalabogārtheṣu panasādimahābhogakāraṇeṣu uttamasahasadaṇḍaḥ, puṣpabogārtheṣu campakādiṣu pakvāpakvaphalabhogāpekṣayālpabogakāraṇeṣu madhyamasāhasadaṇḍaḥ, patrabhogārtheṣu puṣpabogāpekṣayā svalpabogakāraṇeṣu vallīgulmalatādisthāvaraprāṇiṣu kārṣāpaṇaśatam, atyalpabhogārtheṣu tṛṇeṣv ekaḥ kārṣāpaṇa ity upabhogānusāreṇa damo 'vagantavyaḥ | tathā ca daṇḍa ity anuvṛttau viṣṇuḥ: "phalopabhogadrumacchedī tūttamasāhasam, puṣpopabhogacchedī madhyamasāhasam, vallīgulyalatācchedī kārṣāpaṇaśatam, tṛṇacchedy ekam, sarve ca tatsvāmināṃ tadutpattim" iti | sarve phalopabhogadrumacchedakādayaḥ tatsvāmināṃ chinnadrumādisvāmināṃ tadutpattiṃ phalopabhogadrumādyutpattiṃ punaḥ praropitadrumādibhogakālaparyantaṃ dāpyā iti śeṣaḥ ||'

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ daṇḍapāruṣyākhyasya padasya vidhivitānam**

**atha dyūtasamāhvayākhyasya padasya vidhir ucyate**

tatra nṛpatiṃ praty āha manuḥ |

	prakāśam etat tāskaryaṃ yad devanasamāhvayau |

	tayor nityaṃ pratīghāte nṛpatir yatnavān bhavet ||

tāskaryaṃ taskaratvam | yatnavān bhavet yatnavān bhūtvā tau nivārayet | tathā cāha sa eva |

	dyūtaṃ samāhvayaṃ caiva rājā rāṣṭre nivārayet | iti |

dyūtasamāhvyayoḥ ko bheda ity apekṣite sa evāha |

	aprāṇibhir yat kriyate tal loke dyūtam ucyate |

	prāṇibhiḥ kriyate yas tu sa vijñeyaḥ samāhvayaḥ ||

aprāṇibhiḥ akṣādibhiḥ | prāṇibhiḥ meṣādibhiḥ | nivāraṇam atra nirvāsanādidaṇḍena, daṇḍasyaiva nīcanivāraṇatvāt | ata eva nivāraṇāya nirvāsanam āha sa eva |

	kuśīlavāṃś ca kitavān pāṣaṇḍasthāṃś ca mānavān |

	vikarmasthān śauṇḍikāṃś ca kṣipraṃ nirvāsayet purāt ||

kitavānāṃ nīcakāritvaprakhyāpanāyātra kuśīlavādyanekanīcasāhacaryakaraṇam iti mantavyam | duḥsaṅgena kumārgitvam avilambena prajānām apadyata iti kṣipragrahaṇaṃ kṛtam | kṣipragrahaṇasyaetad eva prayojanam uktaṃ tenaiva |

	ete rāṣṭre vartamānāḥ rājñaḥ pracchannataskarāḥ |

	vikarmakriyayā nityaṃ bādhante bhadrikāḥ prajāḥ ||

ete kuśīlavādayaḥ | bṛhaspatis tu manor matam anyeṣāṃ mataṃ cāha |

	dyūtaṃ niṣiddhaṃ manunā satyaśaucadhanāpaham |

	abhyanujñātam anyais tu rājabhagasamanvitam ||

	sabhikādhiṣṭhitaṃ kāryaṃ taskarajñānahetunā | iti |

sabhāṃ kṛtvā dyūtakārakaḥ sabhikaḥ | kathaṃ punaḥ sabhikasya dyūtakārakatvam ity apekṣite sa evāha |

	sabhiko grāhako dravyaṃ dadyāj jetre nṛpāya ca | iti |

dyūtaparājitakitavānāṃ tu bandhanādinā paṇagrāhako bhavet | paṇagrahaṇāt prāg eva svadravyaṃ jetre nṛpāya ca yathābhāgaṃ dadyāt sabhika ity arthaḥ | tathā ca katyayanaḥ |

	jetur dadyāt svakaṃ dravyaṃ jitād grāhyaṃ tripakṣakam |

	sadyo vā sabhikenaiva kitavāt tu na saṃśayaḥ ||

tripakṣakam ity anena yathāsāmarthyam ā tripakṣāt paṇadānakālo deya iti darśitam | jetre rājñe ca dattasya svadravyasya paṇapratinidheḥ vṛddhiḥ paṇagrahaṇakāle paṇena saha sabhikena grāhyā,

	daśakaṃ tu śate vṛddhiṃ gṛhṇīyāt tu parājayāt |

iti tenaivoktatvāt | parājayāt parājitād ity arthaḥ | sabhikādhiṣṭhitam ity asyānityatvam āha sa eva |

	atha vā kitavo rājñe datvā bhāgaṃ yathoditam |

	prakāśaṃ devanaṃ kuryād evaṃ doṣo na vidyate ||

doṣo rājavañcanalakṣaṇo dyūtakāritvalakṣaṇo vā | samāhvayaṃ prastutyāha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	dvaṃdvayuddhena yaḥ kaścid avasādam avāpnuyāt |

	tatsvāminā paṇo deyo yas tatra parikalpitaḥ ||

kvacit paṇaparikalpanaṃ kṛtākṛtam ity āha nāradaḥ |

	parihāsakṛtaṃ yac ca yac cāpy aviditaṃ bhavet |

	tatrāpi nāpnuyāt kāmam atha vānumataṃ tayoḥ ||

kāmyata iti kāmaḥ paṇaḥ, nāpnuyād dyūtasya tatrālasyāpanodanārthatvād ity abhiprāyaḥ | tayor jetṛjitayor devanāt prāg anumataṃ kāmaṃ parihāsakṛtādāv api jetā prāpnuyād iti śeṣaḥ | tatra prāptapaṇāpāditabhakṣyādibhakṣaṇādāv āvṛttipratiṣedhārtham āha sa eva |

	bhakṣyabhojyānnapānāni svalpāny anyāni kānicit |

	prītyā tu sakṛd ājīvet prasaṅgaṃ tu vivarjayet ||

vivādanirṇayas tatra sabhikādisamayānusāreṇa prasiddha iti tadviṣayāṇi vacanāny anasthayā nāsmābhiḥ samuccitāni ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ dyūtasamāhvayākhyasya padasya vidhivitānam**

**atha prakīrṇakākhyasya padasya vidhir ucyate**

tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	eṣa vādikṛtaḥ prokto vyavahāraḥ samāsataḥ |

	nṛpāśrayaṃ pravakṣyāmi vyavahāraṃ prakīrṇakam ||

vādikṛtaḥ arthipratyarthibhyāṃ rājani mitho visaṃvādam āvedya kṛtaḥ | sa ca ṛṇādānādidyūtāntaviṣayo na dyūtamātraviṣaya iti | eṣaśabdo 'tra prāguktasaptadaśapadāntargatāśeṣagaṇe vartate, na punar anantaroktadyūtasamāhvayāntargataviśeṣeṣv evāvatiṣṭhet | samāsata ity ubhayatra sambadhyate | nṛpāśrayaṃ duṣṭaceṣṭopetāśrayāntarasāpekṣanṛpāśrayam | ekāśrayavyavahārābhāvāt prakīrṇakaṃ prakīrṇakavyapadeśayoginam, tadyogaś ca viprakīrṇānāṃ nṛpāśrayāṇām ekatra saṃniveśāt | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

	rājñām ājñāpratīghātaḥ tatkarmakaraṇaṃ tathā |

	purapramāṇaṃ sambhedaḥ prakṛtīnāṃ tathaiva ca ||

	pāṣaṇḍanaigamaśreṇigaṇadharmaviparyayaḥ |

	pitāputravivādaś ca prāyaścittavyatikramaḥ ||

	pratigrahavilopaś ca kopa āśramiṇām api |

	varṇasaṃkaradoṣaś ca tadvṛttiniyamas tathā ||

	na dṛṣṭaṃ yac ca pūrveṣu sarvaṃ tat syāt prakīrṇakam || iti |

pratīghāto bhaṅgaḥ | tatkarma siṃhāsanārohanādirājakarma | purapramāṇaṃ pauracaritalekhyapramāṇam | sambhedaḥ prakṛtīnāṃ rājyāṅgānāṃ marmodbhedo dūṣaṇaiḥ prasiddhaiḥ | pāṣaṇḍādayaḥ prāg anekadhā vyākhyātāḥ | paradharmāṇāṃ karaṇaṃ dharmaviparyayaḥ | pitāputravivādo 'tra ṛṇādānādyanantarbhūto 'bhihitaḥ | na dṛṣṭaṃ yac ca pūrveṣv iti prāguktasarvaśeṣatayābhidhānāt | rājājñāpratīghātaviśeṣe kenacit kṛte rājñā svayam anviṣya bhāvite daṇḍam āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	ūnaṃ vābhyadhikaṃ vāpi likhed yo rājaśāsanam |

	pāradārikacorau vā muñcato daṇḍa uttamaḥ ||

anyūnānatirekeṇa lekhanasyāduṣṭalakṣaṇasya ca rājñādiṣṭasyātikrame tadājñāpratighātakatvenātidauṣṭyād uttamasāhasadaṇḍo 'tra grāhya ity arthaḥ | ājñākāriṇāṃ satkāram anyathākāriṇām atyantāpakāram ācared ity āha sa eva |

	ye rāṣṭre 'dhikṛtās teṣāṃ cārair jñātvā viceṣṭitam |

	sādhūn saṃmānayed rājā viparītāṃś ca ghātayet ||

adhikṛtasthānānusāreṇa vartamānāḥ sādhavaḥ | rāṣṭra ity upalakṣaṇam | ata eva vyāsaḥ |

	nyāyasthāne ye 'dhikṛtā gṛhītvārthaṃ vinirṇayam |

	kurvanty utkocakās te tu rājadravyavināśakāḥ ||

	utkocajīvino dravyahīnān kṛtvā vivāsayet | iti |

kātyāyano 'pi |

	rājakrīḍāsu ye saktāḥ rājavṛttyupajīvinaḥ |

	apriyasya ca yo vaktā vadhaṃ teṣāṃ pravartayet ||

purapramāṇaprakṛtisaṃbhedādau rājñā yat kartavyaṃ tad asmābhiḥ prāg eva prasaṅgād asmin kāṇḍe sadācārakāṇḍe cābhihitam ity uparamyate | tena prakīrṇakākhyapadapratipādyaṃ kiṃcid eveha pratipāditam | avaśiṣṭam iha tatra tatra prasaṅgād uktam anusaṃdheyam ||

**iti sakalavidyāviśāradaśrīkeśavādityabhaṭṭopādhyayasūnu-**

**yājñikadevaṇabhaṭṭopādhyāyasomayājiviracitāyāṃ**

**smṛticandrikāyāṃ vyavahārakāṇḍe dvitīyaparicchedaḥ **

**kāṇḍaś ca samāptaḥ**
